# THE HORARY TEXTBOOK

# 作者：John Frawley

# THE HORARY TEXTBOOK

# Revised Edition

# 作者：John Frawley

翻译：乾坤 校正：绿窗小语

# 首版序言

自从 2009 年接触到占星学后，就被这门学科迷住了，不断的寻找资料，不 断的做着心得笔记（网上应该都能搜索到），一直到今天。

和大部分接触占星的朋友一样，我是从现代占星的心理占星入门，不过当研 究过一段时间后，觉得心理占星虽然能对一个人的性格做出分析，但是并不能论 断准确的事件，纵然是给人进行心理解析的时候，心里总是有个声音在对我说： 不够，不够，这一点都不够。

是的，光是进行心理解析，其实对别人一点帮助都没有，如果一个成年的人， 对自己都没有了解，还需要通过外界的帮助来了解自己，那不是可笑之极么？何 况，从心理学角度来说，一个人的性格极为不容易改变，除非经历过极大的磨难， 而这个磨难，不正是事件么？？？连佛祖都做不到说过一番话就能让人做出改变， 何况是一名占星师？？你自问自己能强于佛祖吗？？？只有在做出精确的事件 预测后，人才会对你的话深信不疑，这个时候再通过各种宗教里面的真理来对其 进行善导，才可能让其在日后的所作所为中存一丝的善念，这才是功德。

于是我寻找各类可以找到的书籍，期望能够找到预测事件的方法，只是可惜， 国内这方面的资料实在是太少，而且都是片面的，只能通过自己的理解和基础来 摸索，可惜进展实在是太小。

某次接触到卜卦占星（还是在占星网上面找到的资料），就开始研究，但是 零碎的资料根本就难以整个的了解这个系统。这个时候，有人出现，跟我聊卜卦， 然后说理论，我问为什么这么说，对方就说《The Horary Textbook》（当时我已 经知道了 Lilly 的基督占星，但是中文资料实在是少，全部都是片面的翻译，古 英语又不懂，就放弃了）说的，然后我问，那你发给我看看，告之没有，问在哪 儿买？不回答。再问是否有中文版，回答没有，并说里面的英语都很简单，你自 己看就会了（我的英语水平为 0）。你看，就是如此蛋疼，我就一怒之下不研究 卜卦了。继续研究推运。

后来，又了解到古典占星，各种闻所未闻的术语都出现了，我就问学习古占 的人术语的意思，对方都是以一种高姿态爱答不理的有一句没一句的回答，当我 再次问，这个术语的理论应该怎么使用？？？这就没有回答了。再看到那帮学习 古占的人之间的讨论，神马三分啊，互溶啊，接纳啊之类的，完全不懂，然后这 个分数那个分数加来加去的，觉得真的很蛋疼，再加上那帮学习古占那种高人一 等的姿态，我再次一怒之下，放弃研究古占。

心想，中国的命理也博大精深，我既然学不了卜卦和古占，就转为学习八字， 入门后兼学六爻，期间也是如学习占星般那样学习，好在对文言文毫无压力，相

关方面书籍和视频又足，又幸运的碰到高手指点，自是喜然然。占星反而是放下 了。

在一个偶然的机会，找到了全本的《The Horary Textbook》的全本，又正巧 在研究六爻，想着自己没事就对着翻译机和自己那点可怜的英语基础来翻译，结 果被里面的内容深深的吸引，立志将这本好书整本翻译出来，经过一年的时间， 总算是初步翻译完毕，其中经过也不必多说。因为水平问题其中有很多胡乱的翻 译，准备在日后不断的整理和找人帮忙校正。

这本书绝对是一本好书，深入浅出的全面的讲解了卜卦占星，并且也是让网 上充斥的那些古占术语有个详尽的解释，以这本书进行古占入门是再好也不过的 了；作者还以自己的经验和观点对古占中的理论进行了增删，看到这些的时候需 要自己懂脑子推敲。

至于这本书是否应该分享出来，我纠结过一段时间。但是看现在网上，骗子 占星师那么多，某些人自持有英文水平或者有相关全部资料而不分享，有些地方 只是翻译一些只言片语而不提用法又没有系统的讲解，某些人不见有何自己著作 问世就靠着不知道哪儿来的名气在不断圈钱的等等不可胜数的原因，我觉得在国 内占星水平还处于初级阶段下，还是免费分享给那些真正的占星爱好者，让他们 能够免费的学习到知识；何况这也谈不上收费，知识是作者的，我只是翻译了而 已，何况还有很多可能是翻译错了的，但求没有误导人就心下大慰了。

这本书放出去后会有什么后果我不知道，如果被那些骗钱的大神们拿去学了 一点后继续骗人，我只能说出来混迟早会还的，自有因果报应；可能会有人说我 侵犯了作者著作权，就我找过的法律条款来看，我这么做并没有侵犯版权，就算 是有侵犯，请你扪心自问一下，你是否看过了？

这本书的前几章，有一位微博账号叫“千叶 Anita”的朋友帮我校正，那几 章应该看起来比较通顺，在此对她表示由衷的感谢！也希望有精通英语并热爱占 星的朋友能和我联系，帮我对本书进行校正，不断的完善这本书，我的微博账号 是“真乾坤”。

乾坤

二零一三年五月二十五日

# 2.0 版序言

这个版本首先要感谢数位帮我进行校正的朋友，我只记得饭饭了，但是依然 要感谢帮我进行校正的朋友。

这个版本里面，我修订了数个翻译不合理的地方，还有逻辑和语法说不通的 地方；对字体格式进行了统一；对于文中提到的哪一页的例子，也根据翻译后的 实际情况进行了修改，不过插入本页后，可能又不对了，不过也就在附近 1,2 页， 不会离太远，我实在是懒得再修正了，等下个版本吧。

这个版本也可能会有许多不对的地方，欢迎大家指正。

关于下个版本，我的想法是自己多收集案例来印证，自己针对原文进行批注， 增加案例来弥补本书案例较少的缺憾，不过时间就真的不知道会有多久了，希望 十年内能出来吧。

乾坤

二零一四年二月二十五日

# 3.0 版序言

本来以为要等很久我才会去增加案例做一个 3.0 版，还专门卖了 2010 年出 版的《The Horary Textbook》作为纪念。没有想到作者居然出了个 2014 增订版， 让我不得不掏钱又买了这本。

里面增加一些作者新的经验、心得和要注意的地方，很值得一读。

虽然作者信誓旦旦的说《卜卦案例》这本书肯定会出的，但是我持保留意见， 谁知道他什么时候出来。我还是自己慢慢积累案例吧。

这个版本将过去版本我漏掉的段落补上了，翻译难免有错，大家凑合看吧。

乾坤

二零一五年六月二十一日

# 4.0 版序言

这个版本是对 3.0 版本的修正，在此特别感谢同窗：绿窗小语。凭借她 出色的英语功底，对本书所有的内容和语法上进行了大幅度的修正，真是难 为她校正我那漏洞百出的翻译了，相信你在这个过程中吃了不少苦，再次表 达我的谢意！我个人也将此版本中的一些字体或说法上进行了改正，希望 5.0 版本能有我的案例出现把。

乾坤

二零一五年六月二十一日

# 6.0 版序言

因为 AI 的迅猛发展，对翻译校正起到了极大的帮助，因此采用 Deepseek 在 5.0 版本的基础上进行校正。同时还加入了 John Frawley 个人网站中一些 卜卦占星的答疑内容。在文中用【】标识。

乾坤

二零二五年十一月二十日

# Introduction

# 导言

My aim in The Horary Textbook is to present a clear and comprehensive guide to the craft of horary astrology. Part 1 teaches the techniques that are used. Part 2 shows how these techniques are applied to find answers to all the more common questions that the astrologer is called upon to judge. 在《The Horary Textbook》中，我的目标是清晰而全面地介绍卜卦占星学的技艺。 书的第一部分将讲解相关的技法，第二部分则演示如何运用这些技法，为占星师 日常需要判断的各类常见问题寻找答案。

The endless variety of questions asked makes it impossible to give a method for tackling each one of them. If ever you wonder how rich life’s tapestry really is, set yourself up as a horary astrologer! Whenever I think that I have heard absolutely everything, I can be sure that something yet more bizarre is waiting just around the corner. But the careful study of what is given here will enable you to make a sound judgement on anyting that is not. 问题层出不穷，无法为每个问题都提供一套固定的解决方法。若你想知道生活之 布究竟能编织得多绚丽，那就成为一名卜卦占星师吧！每当我以为自己已听闻世 间所有奇事，总会有更光怪陆离的事情接踵而至。但只要你认真研习本书所授之 法，即便面对任何前所未见的问题，也能做出可靠的判断。

A companion to this book, Horary Practice, is due for publication in the autumn of
2005. That will present a long series of charts on questions of every kind, walking the student through the process of judgement one step at a time – as close as can be to the experience of standing at the elbow of master astrologer as he works. These volumes will guide any reader prepared to make the necessary efforts to proficiency in this most rewarding of crafts. 本书的姊妹篇《Horary Practice》预计将于 2005 年秋季出版。该书将通过大量各 类问题的星盘案例，逐步引导学习者掌握判读流程——宛若亲临占星大师身侧观 摩其推演过程。对于愿意潜心修习的读者，这两部著作必将指引您精通这门回报 丰厚的占星技艺。

# Introduction to the

# Revised edition

# 修订版导言

I have learned a lot in the years since I wrote this book. It is time to incorporate what I have learned in an enlarged and amended second edition. There are passages that my students have shown me need clarification. There are topics omitted that could usefully be included, and others of which the treatment should be longer. There are passages where what I wrote is wrong and demands correction. 自本书初版问世以来，我已积累了许多新的认知。现在正是时候将这些心得融入 这本经过扩充与修订的第二版中。书中有些章节内容——经学生们反馈——需要 进一步阐释；有些主题在初版中未能涉及，本次将予以增补；另有些议题的论述 值得进一步展开。当然，也存在个别论述存在谬误，必须予以修正。

Rather than rewriting the book to incorporate the corrections and additions, I have thought it better to leave the original text intact, giving the updates separately. This for two reasons. One, that the hook, in English and in its various translations, is widely used as a teaching tool. It is important that students can easily find the passages to which their teacher is pointing them. To this end, the page numbers of the first edition are given here in the margins. Second, it is generally more educational to raise points of error and discuss them than to silently air-brush them away as if they were Stalinist politicians who had strayed from the party line. It is no bad thing to show the development of understanding. This knowledge is not something that drops onto our shoulders, ready-made and perfectly fitted, but is bought piece by piece with the coin of time and effort. 我决定不直接修订原书内容以纳入修改和补充，而是保留原文不动，单独列出更 新内容。这主要基于两点考量：其一，本书英文版及各种译本已被广泛用作教学 资料，学生需要能快速定位教师指定的章节，因此本版在页边空白处标注了初版 页码；其二，指出谬误并进行探讨比悄然修正更具教育意义——正如我们不应像 处理偏离路线的斯大林派政客那样将其从历史中抹除。展现认知发展的过程并非 坏事，因为知识并非浑然天成地降临，而是需要我们用时间和努力逐一换取。

This being so, I will doubtless soon find cause to amend and amplify what is in this new edition. Such further corrections will appear on my website as I make them. In astrology, as in any branch of knowledge more complicated than the multiplication tables, there is always more to learn. Joy that this is so! For where would the fun be if we could know it all? 正因如此，我无疑很快又会发现需要修订和补充这本新版的内容。后续的修正将 随时发布在我的网站上。占星学如同任何比九九乘法表更复杂的学问，永远有更 多需要探索的空间。这何等令人欣喜！倘若我们能够穷尽所有知识，人生的乐趣

又将何在？

As you read these additions and corrections you will see that my approach has become increasingly simplified. In horary, indeed in all astrological judgement, less really is almost always more. The things I learn are rarely arcane titbits of complexity, but things so obvious in their simplicity that I have walked right past them. Concision and economy are the very heart of horary. 在阅读这些增补与修正时，您会发现我的方法已趋于化繁为简。在卜卦占星—— 乃至所有占星判断中，少即是多的原则几乎总是成立的。我所领悟的往往不是晦 涩难懂的复杂细节，而是因其过于简明而被我屡屡忽略的真谛。精炼与简约正是 卜卦占星的精髓所在。

You will also notice that many of the errors I have identified came from too great a reverence for the writings of our illustrious forebears. Our relationship with these authorities must be one of questioning dialogue, not thoughtless obedience. It is unfortunately common in the world of traditional astrology to think that citing an authority closes any discussion. It is more often a sign that the one doing the citing doesn’t understand what is being discussed. The one statement that can confidently be cited is Nicky Culpeper’s wise advice to keep our brains in our heads, not in our books, because that’s the place God ordained for them. 您还会注意到，我所指出的诸多谬误，往往源于对前辈著作的过度尊崇。我们与 这些权威典籍的关系应当是充满质疑的对话，而非盲从。在传统占星学界，常见 这样一种现象：认为引用权威就能终结讨论。但更多时候，这恰恰暴露了引用者 并未真正理解所讨论的议题。唯一值得引用的，是 Nicky Culpeper（尼古拉斯·库 尔佩珀）的睿智箴言：务必将头脑放在自己的头颅里，而非书本中——因为上帝 为我们安排的安放之处就在于此。

Horary Practice, the companion volume to this, advertised in the original Textbook for publication in 2005, will eventually follow. In the meantime, I would direct those eager to learn to my Sports Astrology. Two of the four main chapters in that are devoted to horary, walking the reader step by step through a long series of chart judgement. My aim there was to answer all the questions a student would like to ask a teacher but cannot usually ask a book. Insofar as I may have succeeded, the book is a useful tool regardless of whether the reader has any interest in sport. 作为本书姊妹篇的《Horary Practice》，虽在原版教材中预告于 2005 年出版，终 将面世。在此期间，我建议渴求知识的读者先参阅我的《Sports Astrology》。该 书四个主要章节中有两章专门探讨卜卦占星，通过一系列星盘判读的循序渐进解 析，旨在解答学生在课堂上想向老师提出却通常无法在书中找到答案的所有疑问。 若拙作在这方面有所成就，那么无论读者是否对体育感兴趣，这本书都将成为有 益的学习工具。

These additions have been read and thoughtfully commented upon by Fotini Christodoulou, Anne Coralie, Gabrielle Dunn and Kathryn Silvestre. The erros and infelicities that remain are mine alone.

Fotini Christodoulou（福蒂尼·克里斯托杜卢）、Anne Coralie（安妮·科拉莉）、 Gabrielle Dunn（加布里埃尔·邓恩）与 Kathryn Silvestre（凯瑟琳·西尔维斯特） 已审阅了这些增补内容并提出宝贵意见。文中若仍有错漏不当之处，责任完全在 于本人。

### The new additions are enclosed between✷✷. Internal references in the original text

have been silently changed to fit the new pagination. The matter of tradition and the authority of books, on which I touch briefly above, is dealt with at more length on my website: www.johnfrawley.com.

### 新增内容均置于✷✷之内。原文中的内部参照已作隐性调整以适配新版页码。

上文提及的传统与典籍权威之议题，在我的网站 www.johnfrawley.com 上有更详 尽的论述。

The charts in this edition are cast using the Mercurius software, written by Bernhard Bergbauer. 本版所载星盘均采用 Bernhard Bergbaue（r伯恩哈德·伯格鲍尔）编写的 Mercurius 软件绘制。（译者：本译本依然采用第一版的星盘，因为这一版的星盘我觉得难 看。）

# Acknowledgements

# 致谢

In writing The Horary Textbook, my greatest debt is to Wililiam Lilly, master astrologer, magister meo, who has taught and continues to teach me so much. 在撰写《The Horary Textbook》过程中，我受惠最深者当属 Wililiam Lilly（威廉·利 利）——他是中世纪时期伟大的占星师，始终予我无尽启迪。

Everyone studying traditional astrology is indebted to Olivia Barclay, who worked so hard to restore Lilly’s Christian Astrology to its rightful place at the heart of the astrological canon. I was fortunate to study horary with Olivia, and it was she who encouraged me to write, speak and teach on the subject. 所有研习传统占星学的学者都受惠于 Olivia Barclay（奥利维娅·巴克利）—— 她以不懈努力使 Lilly 的《Christian Astrology》重归占星经典核心地位。我有幸 曾师从 Olivia 研习卜卦占星，正是她鼓励我就此课题进行写作、演讲与教学。

Teaching others has taught me even more than being taught myself. How true it is that one does not teach a subject, one teaches people. It is the years of reframing knowledge to make it intelligible to the eager mind of each of these people that gives this book whatever virtue it may possess. To my students, my thanks. 教导他人让我收获远胜于独自求学。诚哉斯言：传授之道不在授业，而在育人。 正是多年来为满足每位求知者心灵而不断重组知识体系的过程，才赋予了本书可 能存在的价值——谨以此书向我的学生们致以谢忱。

My gratitude, as ever, goes to Victor Laude and Despina Giannokopulou, without whom the road might have petered out long before reaching this point. 谨向 Victor Laude（维克多·劳德）与 Despina Giannokopulou（德斯皮娜·詹 诺科波卢）致以一如既往的谢忱——若非二位，这条道路或许早已半途而废。

Branka Stamenkovic and Tijana Marinkovic have been the most effective of cheerleaders, encouraging me forward whenever the task seemed too daunting. Branka, Yasmin Bolland, Nina Holly, Dolores Quiddington, Richard Redmond and Carol Walsh read the manuscript and provided invaluable suggestions and corrections. What errors remain are mine alone. Branka Stamenkovic（布兰卡·斯塔门科维奇）与 Tijana Marinkovic（蒂贾娜·马 林科维奇）始终是最得力的支持者，每当我感到任务艰巨时，她们总会给予前进 的勇气。Branka（布兰卡）、Yasmin Bolland（亚斯明·博兰）、Nina Holly（妮 娜·霍莉）、Dolores Quiddington（多洛雷斯·奎丁顿）、Richard Redmond（理 查德·雷德蒙）和 Carol Walsh（卡罗尔·沃尔什）审阅了本书手稿，提出了宝 贵的修改建议。书中若仍有疏漏之处，责任全在于我。

Many times I have been asked the horary question, ‘Will I make a living as a horary astrologer?’ and that the answer to this question is usually ‘No’ is less because of the skills involved, which can be learned, but because of the sacrifices that must be made. In my case, most of these sacrifices have been made by my wife, Anna, who has stood by me resolutely, never failing in her support and understanding as I have built my career. Were she any less remarkable I would not be in the position to write this book. My thanks to her are endless. 常有人通过卜卦占星向我询问：“我能以卜卦占星师为生吗？”这个问题的答案 多为否定——这并非因为所需技艺难以掌握（这些都可以通过学习获得），而是 因为从业者必须做出巨大牺牲。就我而言，这些牺牲大多由我的妻子 Anna（安 娜）承担。在我开拓事业的岁月里，她始终如磐石般坚定不移地支持我，从未缺 席过任何一次理解与扶持。若她没有这般非凡的品格，我绝无可能完成本书的写 作。对她的感激永无止境。

# Introduction to Horary

# 卜卦占星学简介

Horary is the art of drawing specific answers to specific questions from an astrological chart set for the time the question is asked. It is quick, simple and effective, providing concrete, verifiable answers. 卜卦占星是一门通过建立提问时刻的星盘，为具体问题推演具体答案的占卜艺术。 它快速、简明而高效，能提供明确且可验证的解答。

“How quick?How simple?” “有多快？有多简单？”

Follow this example. You may not yet understand many of the technical terms I use, but the principle of the judgements should be clear. Next door’s cat had been gradually moving into my house. When he didn’t appear for a couple of days, I was concerned for his safety, so asked the question ‘Where is the cat?’ 请看这个例子。你可能还不理解我使用的许多专业术语，但判断原则应当清晰明 了。邻居家的猫渐渐把我家当自己家。当它连续几天不见踪影时，我开始担心它 的安全，于是提出疑问：“这只猫在哪儿？”

I set an astrological chart for the time I asked this question and for my location at that time. Printing the chart here, I have left out everthing not needed for judgement. 我根据提问的时间和所在位置绘制了星盘。此处列出的星盘已省略所有与判断无 关的元素。

Where is the cat? August 30th 1998,9.20 am BST, London. 猫在何处？1998年 8月 30日，上午 9点 20分 英国夏令时，伦敦

I am asking about a cat.This is a small animal, and so is represented by the sixth house of the chart. The planet that rules the sign on the cusp of that house will signify the cat. Pisces is on the 6th cusp, so its ruler, Jupiter, signifies the cat. 我正在询问关于一只猫的情况。作为小型动物，它由星盘中的 6 宫代表。该宫位 宫头所在星座的守护星将象征这只猫。双鱼座位于 6 宫头，因此其守护星木星便 代表了这只猫。

Where is Jupiter? In the 6th house: the house of the cat. So where is the cat? In his own house: at home. 木星在何处？位于 6 宫——即代表猫的宫位。那么猫在何处？就在它自己的宫位 内：在家中。

Is he OK? Jupiter, the most benefic of planets, is in its own sign, so has lots of essential dignity. Signified by a strongly dignified benefic, the cat is doing just fine. 它安然无恙吗？木星作为最吉利的行星，正位于其自身守护的星座，因此具备强 大的先天尊贵力量。由能量旺盛的吉星作为象征，这只猫一切安好。

Jupiter (the cat) is in a water sign, so he may be somewhere wet. But water signs also

show places that are comfortable, which, considering the nature of the beast and that he is clearly happy where he is (strongly dignified benefic), must be the more likely choice. So he is probably curled up on the sofa or bed. 木星（代表猫）位于水象星座，因此它可能身处潮湿之地。但水象星座也象征着 舒适之所，考虑到这只猫的天性以及它当前状态显然很愉悦（由能量旺盛的吉星 象征），更可能是在安逸环境中。所以它大概率正蜷缩在沙发或床上。

Will he come back? Jupiter is retrograde: it is going back where it has been before.So yes, he will come back. 它会回来吗？木星正处于逆行状态：这意味着它正在退回它曾经过的地方。因此， 它一定会回来。

The chart has given a specific, verifiable answer to the question. It has done this using only one planet! Horary is quick; horary simple. 星盘为问题给出了具体且可验证的答案，而这一切仅凭一颗行星就实现了！卜卦 占星既快捷又简明。

We can refine this answer by predicting the time of the cat’s return. For this there must be a connection between the cat’s significator and something that represents either me or my home. Jupiter is making no such contact in this chart, so we must introduce a second planet. The Moon is natural ruler of all lost objects, especially animate ones. 我们可以通过预测猫咪的回归时间来完善这个答案。这需要猫的征象星与代表我 或我家的行星之间建立联系。木星在此星盘中未形成此类相位，因此我们需要引 入第二颗行星。月亮是所有失物的先天守护星，尤其对活物更是如此。

The person asking the question is shown by the Ascendant and its ruler. The Moon applies to sextile the Ascendant. Just as the 6th can be taken literally as the cat’s house, the first is literally my house. The Moon must travel almost exactly 1 degree to perfect this aspect. So the cat will return in almost exactly 1 unit of time. The sign and house the Moon is in as it makes this aspect tell us which unit of time this is. With the Moon in a mutable sign and a cadent house, the unit must be a day.So the cat will returen almost exactly 24 hours after time for which the chart was cast. And so it proved. 提问者由上升点及其守护星代表。月亮即将与上升点形成六合相位。正如 6 宫可 直译为猫的居所，1 宫直译便是我的住所。月亮需运行将近 1 度才能完全形成这 个相位。因此猫咪将在几乎恰好 1 个时间单位后归来。当月亮形成此相位时所在 的星座与宫位，揭示了该时间单位的具体量纲——月亮位于变动星座与变动宫， 故时间单位必为“天”。这意味着在星盘绘制后几乎整整 24 小时，猫咪将会归 来。而事实果真如此。

Even now, we have only two planets in the chart. Yet we have a precise, timed,

accurate prediction. Horary is simple. 即便此刻，我们星盘中仍仅有两颗行星参与推演，却已得出一个精确且能推算应 期的准确预测。卜卦占星就是如此简明。

Not every chart, as might be expected, it as simple as this one. But many are. A good proportion of horary charts can, with knowledge and practice, be judged at a glance. Horary was the main technique used by most astrologers during the Seventeenth century, and it is a matter of record that an astrological consultation using horary would have taken around fifteen minutes. This time would include the usual social niceties of greeting; the client explaining what he wanted to know and giving any relevant – or, more often, irrelevant – details of the situation; negotiation of an acceptable fee; the astrologer adjusting the chart he had set at the start of his day’s work to fit the time this question was asked; him judging the chart and telling the client his judgement; the client, if the answer given was not what he had hoped quite possibly reacting with disbelief,‘Huh! What do you know?’; the astrologer looking again at his chart and responding,‘I know you have a large red birthmark on your left thigh,’to convince him. All this in fifteen minutes. Even the most complex charts are judged not by any arcane or difficult tricks of method, but by doing a few simple operations over and over again. 诚如所料，并非每张星盘都如本例般简明，但多数确实如此。相当比例的卜卦星 盘凭借知识与经验便可一目了然。十七世纪时，卜卦占星是大多数占星师使用的 主要技法。据史料记载，一次完整的卜卦占星咨询通常只需约十五分钟。这短 短一刻钟涵盖了：常规的问候寒暄；客户说明诉求并提供相关（更多时候是不相 关）的细节背景；协商双方接受的酬金；占星师调整当日开盘星盘以对应提问时 辰；解盘并告知判断结果；若答案未达预期，客户可能质疑“哼！你能知道什么？”； 此时占星师会再次审视星盘，抛出“我知道你左大腿有块红色胎记”这类铁证令 其信服——所有这些环节都在十五分钟内完成。即便最复杂的星盘也无需倚仗玄 奥技法，仅需反复运用若干基础操作便可解析。

1. Keith Thomas, Religion and the Decline of magic, London, 1971. Rep. London, 1991, P. 364
1. 引自 Keith Thomas（基思·托马斯） 著 《宗教与魔法的衰落》，伦敦，1971 年版，1991 年重印本，第 364 页

It was not only its speed and economy of effort that made horary the mainstay of astrological practice: for most enquiries it was and still is the most appropriate tool. Whatever the situation might be, if the client wants to know something specific about it, use horary. Most answers can be found more quickly and more reliably from a horary chart than from the study of the birthchart; many answers cannot be found in the birthchart at all, no matter how detailed or lengthy the investigation, or how skilled the astrologer. The natal chart will not reveal whether it will rain on the day you’ve planned a barbecue, whether you should sell your dollars to buy silver, what your sweetheart really feels about you – or where the cat might be. Yet these and issues like them, woven together, make up the fabric of our life. 卜卦占星之所以能成为占星实践的核心手段，不仅因其迅捷高效，更因为对于大

多数咨询问题而言，它过去是、现在依然是最适用的工具。无论面对何种情境， 若咨询者希望获知具体问题的答案，皆可运用卜卦占星。相较于本命盘研究，通 过卜卦星盘能更快速、更可靠地找到多数问题的答案；而许多问题的答案根本无 法从本命盘中获取——无论分析多么细致深入，占星师技艺多么精湛。本命盘无 法揭示你计划烧烤当日是否会下雨，是否该抛售美元买入白银，心上人对你的真 实感受——抑或猫咪此刻身在何方。然而这些看似琐碎的议题，正交织构成我们 生命的经纬。

Most of those who approach an astrologer for a consultation have a particular question in mind. It is of course far simpler to look at a chart that concerns that question and it alone, than to attempt to pick the bones of that question from the birthchart, which shows a lifetime’s worth of questions tangled together. 大多数寻求占星咨询的访客心中都怀揣着特定疑问。直接解读针对该具体问题设 置的星盘，远比从承载着人生万千课题的本命盘中抽丝剥茧要简便得多——毕竟 本命盘呈现的是贯穿生命长河的无数命题盘根错节的交织。

Horary was traditionally regarded as being the student’s point of entrance to the study of astrology. One reason for this is that it is much simpler than other branches of astrology, such as natal or mundane. It thus enables the student to achieve with comparative ease a mastery of the techniques that form the bulk of those used, with greater elaboration, in these other branches. It can be seen as equivalent to mastering one’s scales when learning a musical instrument; as such it is a necessary prelude to more advanced study. Unlike mastery of the musical scales, however, horary is of immediate practical use. 传统上，卜卦占星被视为研习占星学的入门途径。这主要是因为相较于本命占星、 世运占星等其他分支，卜卦占星的体系更为简明。它能让学习者相对轻松地掌握 核心解读技法——这些技法经过深化拓展后，也构成了其他占星分支的主体方法 论。正如学习乐器必先精通音阶，掌握卜卦占星可视为进阶研究的必要前奏。然 而与枯燥的音阶练习不同，卜卦占星具有立竿见影的实用价值。

“Is horary solely predictive?” 卜卦占星是否仅用于预测？

Not at all. It is best known for its ability to provide accurate prediction. It can aslo be used to investigate the past ✷‘Did the builder steal my ring?’). Its most interesting use, however, is for analysis of a situation. Far more valuable than asking the predictive ‘Is my marriage heading for divorce?’ is asking the analytical ‘What is going wrong with my marriage and what can I do about it?’ This too can be done with horary. 绝非如此。卜卦占星虽以精准预测著称，但其应用远不止于此。它既能追溯过往 （例如“建筑工人是否偷了我的戒指？”），更引人入胜之处在于对现况的解析。 相较于预测型提问“我的婚姻会走向离婚吗？”，更具价值的其实是分析型提问：

“我的婚姻出了什么问题？我该如何应对？”——而这同样可以通过卜卦占星来 实现。

William Lilly and first principles 威廉·莉莉（William Lilly）和基本法则

The great master of horary is William Lilly, an English astrologer who lived from 1602 to 1681. His Christian Astrology, published in 1647, is, and will remain, the standard textbook. The book you have in your hand leans heavily on it. Where this differs, apart from being written in modern English for modern readers, is in its greater emphasis on first principles. Clarity on the first principles avoids the need for the long lists of minor testimonies, often empirically based, that are so large feature of Lilly’s work. 卜卦占星领域的宗师 William Lilly（1602-1681）是英国占星师。他于 1647 年出 版的《Christian Astrology（基督占星学）》始终是这一学科的权威著作 。本书 的论述体系深深植根于莉莉的理论框架，不同之处在于：本书采用现代英语为当 代读者撰写，并更加强调基本法则的阐释。厘清基本法则后，便无需赘述冗长的 次要征象体系——这些经验性推导的繁琐细则是 Lilly 著作的显著特点。

2. The best modern edition is the Astrology Classics edition, from The Astrology Center of Amercia, Abingdon, 2004. Christian Astrology will be referred to as Lilly from now on.
2. 最好的现代版本是《占星学经典》版本，美国占星中心 亚宾顿 著 （2004）。《基督 占星》一直指 LILLY 著的这本。

Minor testimonies do not a judgement make, and can usually be ignored. Consider: if we ask ‘Who won that football match?’ all that concerns us is the major testimony of who scored the most goals. Who had most possession of the ball; who had the most corners; whose players thrilled the crowd: these are minor testimonies, which do not directly affect the goals scored. This is one example of the Rule of Rules: Keep it Simple! 次要证据无法构成判断依据，通常可予以忽略。试想：若我们追问“那场足球赛 谁赢了？”，唯一关键的主要证据就是谁的进球数更多。至于谁的控球时间更长、 谁的角球机会更多、谁的球员更让观众沸腾——这些都是次要证据，并不会直接 改变进球总数。这正是“法则中的法则”的最佳例证：大道至简！

The reader who comes to horary afresh will forgive those passages where I discuss, clarify or refute points from Lilly. This is necessary for those readers who are familiar with his work. 初次接触卜卦占星的读者若见文中出现我对 Lilly 观点的商榷、澄清或驳斥，尚 请海涵。这部分内容对于熟悉其著作的读者实属必要。

Preliminaries 基础知识

First, inscribe these words of Jerome Cardan on your heart: 首先，请将 Jerome Cardan（吉罗拉莫·卡尔达诺）的箴言镌刻于心：

He that has too great a conceit of himself will be apt to fall into many errors in his judgement; yet on the other side, he that is too diffident, is not fit for this Science. 妄自尊大者，易生谬误；妄自菲薄者，难窥堂奥。

3. In Guido Bonatus, The Astrologer’s Guide, London, 1676; Cardan section, aphorism 2. Book herafter referred to as Bonatus.
3. 见 Guido Bonatus（圭多·博纳图斯）所著《占星师指南》，伦敦，1676 年版；Cardan（卡 尔达诺）章节，第二则格言。后文引用时将简称为 Bonatus

This study demands humility. You cannot remake astrology in your own image. You may find much here that differs from what you have previously learned, ideas that you may hold dear. Rather than imposing those ideas onto what is being taught, set them aside for a while, trying what is given here until you see that it works. 研习此道须怀谦卑之心。切莫以个人臆想重塑占星之学。书中诸多见解或与你既 往所学相左，亦可能触及你珍视的理念。请暂且搁置固有观念，勿将己见强加于 所学之道，而应亲身践行书中法门，待见证其效验真章。

The study demands a certain courage. Horary enables us to give clear, detailed answers. There are no helpful clouds of ambivalence for us to hide behind when we get it wrong. We read the chart; we give the judgement; we are proved right or wrong – sometimes quite quickly. The rules given here are your sound support. No astrologer has ever been infallible, but following these rules will allow you to achieve a steadily increasing reliability of judgement. 研习此道需要具备特定勇气。卜卦占星使我们能够给出清晰详尽的答案——当我 们判断失误时，没有模棱两可的迷雾可供躲藏。我们解读星盘、给出判断、验证 对错，有时这个过程迅速得令人措手不及。本书所述的规则是你坚实的后盾。纵 使再卓越的占星师也难免失误，但遵循这些规则将使你的判断准确度获得持续提 升。

The reader who has some knowledge of astrology may be tempted to skip the early chapters. Don’t! When teaching, I have found even those students with qualifications from the most noted astrological schools often have surprising holes in their knowledge of the basics. Being clear on these is essential. If you do not understand the basic building-blocks, whatever you build with them will be unsound. 对占星学有所涉猎的读者或想跳过前面几章——切勿如此！在教学过程中，我发 现即便是那些持有知名占星学院认证资质的学生，其基础知识体系也常存在令人

诧异的漏洞。厘清这些基础概念至关重要。若不能理解这些基础构建模块，无论 用它们搭建出怎样的体系都将是摇摇欲坠的。

This is a book to work with, not a book to real through. The margins are wide to allow room for notes. Pick the examples apart until you are sure you understand why I said what I’ve said. Keep asking yourself, ‘Why did he say this?’ and ‘Why didn’t he consider that?’ Then practice, practice and practice. Ask your own horary questions. Although, once mastered, horary is best used sparingly, while learning you can ask about every trivial matter that crosses your mind. Questions you would not usually spend time over: ‘When will the postman come?’ ‘Will my mother phone today?’ These are all grist to the mill. Look back at your judgements. If one is wrong, pull the chart apart until you have seen why. 本书旨在引导实践而非泛泛阅读。宽页边设计正是为批注留出空间。请逐一剖析 书中的示例，直至完全理解每个结论的推导过程。要持续追问“作者为何如此判 断”以及“为何未考虑其他因素”，继而通过反复实践来巩固认知。大胆提出自 己的卜卦疑问——虽掌握后需慎用此术，但学习阶段尽可针对日常琐事提问：诸 如“邮递员何时上门”、“母亲今日是否会来电”这类平日不会深究的琐事，正 是绝佳的练习素材。务必回顾自己的判断记录，若发现误判，务必解构星盘直至 找出症结所在。

Always force yourself to reach a judgement, and write this judgement down. Save the charts so you can examine them once the outcome is know. When answering one’s own questions, it is easy to fudge the issue, leaving judgements hanging in ambiguity. It is aslo easy to give up, thinking that the chart is beyond you. You will learn nothing that way. No matter how expert you become, horary will continually ask you to stretch beyond what you think you know. For an astrologer as for an athlete, it is the stretching beyond that brings excellence. Push yourself to go beyond your knowledge, and you will be amazed at what you achieve. Remember that even William Lilly described himself as a ‘student’ of astrology. 务必要求自己对每个星盘作出明确判断，并将结论落于笔端。保存所有星盘资料， 待事态明朗后重新检视推演过程。在解答自身疑问时，人往往容易陷入两种困境： 或含糊带过使判断悬而未决，或因觉星盘艰深而轻言放弃——这都将令你一无所 获。即便成为资深行家，卜卦占星仍会不断挑战你的认知边界。正如运动员通过 突破体能极限缔造辉煌，占星师也需通过突破认知桎梏达至精微。当你迫使自己 跨越知识舒适区，终将惊叹于所能达到的境界。请铭记：纵是 William Lilly 这样 的宗师，亦始终以占星学“学子”自居。

You do not need to have a question to judge a horary chart. Take any chart, either one of your own or one from a book, and make up new questions for it. Have some of these questions focus on people other than ‘I’ (e.g. ‘Will my brother’s marriage survive?’ ‘Is my boss going to take that new job?’ ‘When will my dog find a girlfriend?’). Just don’t take your judgements to these invented questions seriously! This is excellent practice: you are learing a language: you will not become fluent without repeatedly trying to speak.

研习卜卦星盘无需拘泥于真实疑问。任意选取星盘——无论是个人星盘或典籍案 例，皆可为其构思新问题。不妨设问聚焦他人而非自身（例如“我兄弟的婚姻能 维系吗？”、“上司会接受那份新工作吗？”、“我的狗狗何时能找到伴侣？”）。 但切记：对这些虚构问题的判断不必当真！这实为绝佳练习：正如学习语言必须 反复开口才能流利，占星技艺亦需通过持续实践方能精进。

Before you cast a chart, ask yourself what you expect to see in it. How will the situation be shown? You will often be wrong, but doing this will gradually align your thinking with the workings of the chart. 在绘制星盘之前，请先自问：你预期从中看到什么？这件事将如何呈现于星盘？ 虽然你的预判常会失误，但这样的思考训练将使你的思维与星盘运作规律逐渐契 合。

When judging a chart, I find it helps to think in the simplest of terms, as I have shown in the examples here. ‘Is he a good guy or is he a bad guy?’ ‘Good, indifferent, or yuk?’ It may sometimes sound like Learn to Read, Book 1, but doing this will stop you entangling yourself in abstract concepts. The chart will lead you to all the complexity you need; keeping each step as simple as this will enable you to understand the complexity when you get there. Keep it all down to earth. 在解读星盘时，我发现用最简单的方式思考最为有效——正如本书示例所展示的， “他是好人还是坏人？”“是优、是平、还是糟？”这类表述听起来或许像《启 蒙读本》般浅显，但能有效避免你陷入抽象概念的纠缠。星盘自会向你展现必要 的复杂性；而保持每个步骤的简洁明了，将使你在面对复杂状况时仍能游刃有余。 始终要让解读扎根于现实土壤。

Above all, do not beat yourself about the head for getting judgements wrong. The best of footballers can miss a penalty kick. This does not mean he has suddenly become a bad footballer. It does not mean that scoring penalties is impossible. It does not mean that football is nonsense. All it means is that he missed that kick. 最重要的是，切勿因判断失误而过度自责。最顶尖的足球运动员也会射失点球。 这并不意味着他突然变成了糟糕的球员，不意味着罚点球得分是不可能完成的任 务，更不意味着足球运动毫无意义。仅仅只是——他踢丢了那个球。

### ✸Above all, remember that the chart is not an abstraction. It is reflection of the

situation in this world, just as your mirror gives you a reflection of your face. What you read from the chart must make sense in the terms of this world. If it doesn’t, what you are reading is wrong. I am forever reminding students of the common-sense reality of the situation, as that joining the planet signifying the baby to planet signifying the husband will not give pregnancy, because the husband will not get pregnant. Head in the stars, please, but keep feet firmly on the ground. ✷

### ✸最重要的是，请记住星盘并非抽象概念。它如同映照现实的明镜，恰似你从

镜中看见自己的容颜。从星盘解读出的信息必须符合现实世界的逻辑——若与现

实相悖，则解读必然有误。我时常提醒学生注重生活常识：将象征婴儿的行星与 象征丈夫的行星相关联并不能推断怀孕，因为丈夫本身不可能怀孕。当我们仰望 星空时，务必要脚踏实地。✷

# Getting Started

# 起盘

The person asking the question is the querent. 提出问题的这个人即为问卜者。

The person or thing asked about is the quesited. 被问及的人或事物即为所占之事。

Cast the chart for moment the astrologer understands the question. In the past, the astrologer would usually have been sitting with the client when the question was asked. Today questions are often asked at a distance, both of time and space: by email, phone, or recorded on an ansaphone. It is the moment at which the astrologer reads or hears the question that is used for setting the chart, not the time at which the querent poses it. 星盘的绘制应基于占星师理解问题的那一刻。在过去，当问题被提出时，占星师 通常与客户面对面而坐。如今，提问常在时空上存在距离：通过电子邮件、电话 或应答机记录。用于确定星盘的时间点是占星师读到或听到问题的时刻，而非问 卜者提出问题的时刻。

If I come home to find a letter containing a question lying on my doormat, pick it up, make myself a coffee, then sit to read it, I would set the chart for the time at which I read it: not the time I picked it off the mat; not the time the querent has noted in her letter as the moment she wrote it. 如果我回到家，发现门垫上有一封载有问题的信件，我拾起信件，为自己冲了杯 咖啡，然后坐下阅读——此时，我会以自己阅读信件的那一刻来绘制星盘：既不 是我从门垫上拾起信件的时刻，也不是问卜者在信中标注的她写下问题的时刻。

### ✸Don’t feel that you must drop everything when a question arrives. If the shop is

closed, the shop is closed. If you are otherwise engaged when a letter or email comes, there is no need for you to read it at that moment. If you do choose to read it then, though, that is the moment for which the chart should be cast. ✷

### ✸不必觉得在问题到来时必须立刻放下手头一切事务。若已结束营业，便是已

结束营业。当信件或电子邮件送达时，你若另有要务在身，无需当即阅读。但若 你选择即刻阅读，那么此刻便是绘制星盘所依据的时刻。✷

If the question is asked by phone, the chart is cast for the moment the question is asked. This sounds straightforward, and usually is, but some questions have a long labour before they are born. The querent will hesitate, saying ‘I want to ask this……I’m not sure if I should……Or maybe I should ask that……’This can take longer than the whole of a typical Seventeenth-century consultation. The time taken for the chart is the time at which the querent finally gets to the point, not the time at which the conversation started. It is as if such querents are unconsciously feeling for the correct moment at which to ask: the moment that will provide a chart allowing the correct judgement of that question. This can often be verified by the appearance of datable past events in the chart cast, events that would not have been shown in a chart cast for the time the conversation started. 若问题通过电话提出，星盘的绘制时间应以问题被明确提出的那一刻为准。这听 起来简单直接，通常也确实如此，但有些问题在“诞生”前会经历漫长的“酝酿”。 问卜者可能会犹豫不决，说道：“我想问这个……我不确定是否应该……或者也 许我该问那个……”这种情况所耗费的时间，可能比整个十七世纪的一次典型咨 询还要长。此时，星盘的绘制时间应以问卜者最终切入主题的时刻为准，而非对 话开始的时间。这仿佛表明，此类问卜者正在无意识地探寻提出问题的正确时机 ——那个能生成一幅允许对该问题作出正确论断的星盘的时机。这一点常常可以 通过绘制的星盘中出现的、可确定时间的过往事件得到验证——这些事件若以对 话开始时间绘制星盘，是不会显现的。

If the question has been asked, but demands clarification before you understand the core issue, take the time when it is clarified as the time of the question. If you feel you have a reasonable understanding of the question, but when giving the judgement realise that this understanding was faulty, stick with the chart cast for the time you though you understood it. 若问题已被提出，但在你理解其核心议题前需要进一步澄清，则应以澄清完成的 时刻作为问题的提出时间。若你自认对问题已有合理理解，却在给出论断时发现 此前理解有误，则仍应坚持使用你自认为已理解问题时所绘制的星盘。

If the querent asks further questions on the same issue when you are giving judgement on the initial question, judge these from the same chart. For instance, the initial question might be, ‘When will I meet the man I will marry?’ and on being given the judgement the querent might add, ‘Will he get along with my daughter?’ You can read this from the initial chart. If the querent adds, ‘And when will I get a decent job?’ that is a new question requiring a new chart. 若问卜者在你对初始问题给出论断时，就同一事宜提出进一步的问题，应基于同 一张星盘进行判断。例如，初始问题可能是：“我何时会遇到我将嫁予之人？” 而在得到论断后，问卜者可能补充问道：“他会与我的女儿相处融洽吗？”你可 以从初始星盘中解读这一点。但若问卜者补充问道：“那我何时会得到一份体面 的工作？”这便是一个需要绘制新星盘的新问题。

### ✸There is no need to be precious about this idea of understanding the question. So

long as you have the broad gist of what is asked, that is sufficient. The lack of understanding would need to be gross to cause us to set a new chart for the moment when the penny drops. If she asks ‘Do I have a future with Jim?’ and we later realize that JIM is Japanese Imperial Motors, so she is asking about her career, not her lover-life, we would use the time of that realisation. But if she asks about jim and we then find, for instance, that she is married to Fred, we would use the time originally taken. After all, if we understood everything about the situation we wouldn’t need the chart. ✷

### ✸对于“理解问题”这一概念不必过分苛求。只要掌握所问内容的大致主旨，

便已足够。除非误解严重到需要我们豁然开朗时重新绘制星盘的程度，否则无需 调整。例如，若她问“我和 Jim 有未来吗？”，而后我们才意识到“JIM”是日 本帝国汽车公司的缩写，因此她实际询问的是事业前景而非感情生活——此时应 采用我们醒悟的时刻作为绘盘时间。但若她询问关于 Jim 的事，而后我们仅了解 到她已与 Fred 结婚之类的情况，则应沿用最初确定的时刻。毕竟，若我们对情 况了如指掌，也就不需要星盘了。✷

If you are judging your own question, the time to take is the time at which you decide that you will cast a chart to find its answer. This is the equivalent of taking the time at which the querent asks. Don’t try to trace the moment when the issue first wandered into your mind: we are using the time when the question was born, not the time at which it was conceived. The time you use may or may not be the time at which you sit down at your computer to cast the chart. If you wake in the night and decide to ask, note the time and use that. 若你正在判断自己的问题，则应以你决定绘制星盘寻求答案的时刻为准。这相 当于采用问卜者提出问题的时刻。不必追溯问题最初浮现于脑海的瞬间：我们采 用的是问题“诞生”的时刻，而非其“受孕”的时刻。你所采用的时间未必是你 坐在电脑前绘制星盘的那一刻。若你半夜醒来决定提问，请记下此时刻并以此为 准。

### ✸This time is, as it were, the moment at which You the client speak to You the

astrologer. ✷

### ✸这一时刻，可谓是作为问卜者的你与作为占星师的你展开对话的瞬间。✷

Yes, there is the possibility that the astrologer, having a close working knowledge of the positions of the planets, can carefully select a moment when they are aligned to give the answer desired. Yes, there is the possibility that the astrologer might be daft enough to credit the judgement drawn from such a chart. But we must allow our astrologer a modicum of self-awareness. The Heavens, meanwhile, are a mechanism of the greatest subtlety: attempt to choose such a moment at which to ‘spontaneously’

ask your question and you will invariably find that they are a good deal smarter than you. The difficult part in judging one’s own questions is not the choosing of the time, but the setting aside of one’s natural partiality. 确实，占星师若对行星位置了如指掌，或许能精心选择行星排列有利的时刻来获 得期望的答案。也确实，可能有占星师会愚钝到相信由此绘制的星盘所推演出的 论断。但我们必须承认每位占星师都应具备起码的自知之明。更何况，天体运行 机制精妙绝伦：若试图刻意选择某个时刻来“自发”提出问题，你终将发现它们 远比你们更精明。判断自身问题的难点并不在于择时起盘，而在于如何摒弃与生 俱来的偏袒之心。

The place for which the chart is set that of the astrologer. In the past astrologer and querent were usually in the same room; today they are often continents apart. As we take the time at which the question is understood, so we must take the place at which it is understood: the location of the astrologer. According to traditional philosophy the question does not really exist until it meets the ear of one who can answer it. Until then it is a no-thing. 星盘的设定地点应以占星师所在位置为准。在过去，占星师与问卜者通常同处一 室；如今双方常远隔重洋。正如我们采用理解问题的时间点，我们也必须采用理 解问题时的空间位置：即占星师所在之地。依据传统哲学理念，问题唯有传入能 解答者之耳，方真正存在。在此之先，它尚非实质存在。

Use a computer! There are those of ascetic inclination who see a virtue in casting charts by hand. There is no need for such self-flagellation. The situation today is quite different from the days when the astrologer would have querents queuing for his services, and so could cast one chart when he clocked on for work in the morning and adjust it to fit questions asked throughout the day. If you insist on casting charts by hand you are unlikely to cast sufficient charts for the practice needed to gain proficiency. 请使用计算机！有些崇尚苦修的同行认为手动绘制星盘是一种美德。实无必要进 行这般自我折磨。今时不同往日，昔日占星师或许会有问卜者排队等候服务，因 而可以在清晨上班时绘制一张星盘，再根据全天接收到的问题进行调整。若执意 坚持手动绘制星盘，则难以完成足量的练习来获得精进所需的实践经验。

For readers who do not have access to a computer, Appendix 1 shows how to calculate a chart by hand without the needless complications usually introduced. This method streamlines the process, making it as quick and painless as is possible. 对于无法使用计算机的读者，附录 1 展示了如何手动计算星盘，同时省去了通常 不必要的繁琐步骤。该方法对流程进行了精简，使过程尽可能快速轻松。

“Do I need special software for horary?” No! Most advanced astrological software has special ‘horary pages’, which overwhelm the student in a torrent of information, most of which is irrelevant to the question in hand and much of which is presented in ways that can mislead the inexperienced. I urge you not to use these pages, but only the simplest chart-form on the program, without the lists, tables and other

paraphernalia. Following the methods taught in this book, you will soon learn to decide exactly what information you need from the chart, and then to enter the chart looking for that and that alone. This is much quicker and much simpler than wading through a morass of data that you do not want. “进行卜卦占星是否需要特殊软件？”实无必要！多数高级占星软件都设有专门 的“卜卦页面”，这些页面以信息洪流淹没初学者——其中大部分内容与当前问 题无关，且很多信息的呈现方式容易误导经验不足者。我强烈建议不要使用这些 页面，仅使用程序中最基础的星盘图即可，无需加载各种列表、表格及其他辅助 工具。遵循本书所授方法，你将很快学会如何准确判断自己需要从星盘中获取哪 些信息，进而能够带着明确目标解读星盘——仅关注你需要的信息。这远比在无 关的数据泥潭中艰难跋涉要高效简捷得多。

### ✸I find my students reluctant to accept this advice – a reluctance which is never of

benefit to their work. Concision and economy of effort are at the very heart of horary. The more clutter you have, the more likely you are to fall over some of it. ✷

### ✸我发现我的学生们往往不愿接受这个建议——而这种不情愿对他们的学习从

无益处。简洁与省力正是卜卦占星的核心要义。冗余的信息越多，你受其干扰的 可能性就越大。✷

Expensive software is not required. Your aim is to get from A to B; you do not need to drive a Rolls-Royce to achieve this. There is freely downloadable software on the web that is completely adequate. 无需购买昂贵的软件。你的目标是从 A 点到达 B 点；实现这一目标无需驾驶劳 斯莱斯。网络上有可免费下载的软件，这些已完全够用。

4.There is free software in both PC and Mac versions at www.astrolog.org, while you can set a chart and print it out at www.astro.com.
4. 在 www.astrolog.org 网 站 可 获 取 适 用 于 PC 和 Mac 版 本 的 免 费 软 件 ； 您 也 可 以 在 www.astrolog.org 上设置并打印星盘。

Preparation for judgement 论断前的准备

It is my firm belief that no matter how skilled we may be as astrologer, correct judgement is not given unless by grace. Even if all the requisite elements of knowledge are in our head, we cannot make them join together as they should: this is a gift. So I strongly suggest that before entering upon judgement you pray for this grace. 我坚信，无论身为占星师的我们技艺如何精湛，正确的判断若非蒙恩便无从获得。 即便所有必备知识要素皆存于我们脑中，我们也无法使其恰如其分地融会贯通：

这实属一种馈赠。因此我强烈建议，在着手论断之前，你应祈求这份恩典。

Even if not praying, do something, if only washing your hands, or sitting quietly for a couple of minutes to clear your mind. It is far too easy to read the astrologer when you should be reading the chart; but the purpose of horary is to get a dispassionate view of the situation. You need to put your own views and assumptions aside and be open to what is before you. I find, for example, I am often asked question to which my immediate reaction is ‘Don’t be silly’, but where the chart shows that what the querent is suggesting, no matter how odd it might seem to me, is true. It is vital to remember that you do not know. It is the astrology that knows. 即便不祈祷，也请做些准备——哪怕是洗洗手，或是静坐几分钟清空思绪。人们 太容易在应该解读星盘时，反而在解读占星师自己的主观想法；但卜卦的宗旨在 于获得对局势的客观洞见。你需要将个人观点与先入之见搁置一旁，全然接纳呈 现在眼前的讯息。例如，我常遇到这类问题——乍听之下我的第一反应是“别犯 傻”，然而星盘却显示，无论问卜者的提议在我看来多么荒诞，事实确实如此。 务必牢记：你并非知晓一切。知晓一切的，是占星学本身。

You will find that some charts, like this one about the cat, are crystal clear. Many are not. Sometimes the lack of clarity is caused by the astrologer lacking knowledge or approaching the chart in the wrong way. Sometimes the chart appears muddy because the situation it describes is muddy. Many situations are ambivalent, with no clear answer. As a simple example, a common question is, phrased in one way or another, ‘Is this Mr. Right?’ A clear answer might be ‘Yes – he is your soul-mate!’ or ‘No – he is an axe-murderer!’ More often, the answer is, ‘Well, he’s OK; you could do a lot worse, and there’s nothing much better in prospect’. This too is an answer. 你会发现，有些星盘——比如关于猫咪的那个案例——清晰明了。但许多星盘并 非如此。有时模糊不清源于占星师知识欠缺或解读方式不当；有时则因星盘所描 述的局势本身混沌不明。许多情境本就充满矛盾，难有明确答案。举个简单的例 子：常见问题无论以何种形式提出，本质多是“这位是我的真命天子吗？”明确 的答案或许是“没错——他是你的灵魂伴侣！”或“绝非如此——他是个斧头杀 人魔！”但更多时候，答案会是：“呃，他还行；你可能会遇到更糟的，而且眼 前也没有更好的选择”。这，同样是一个答案。

Do not strive for certainty before you give judgement. Some charts are unequivocal; others demand that you tease out an answer. Wait for certainty in these and you will wait forever. But if you have thoroughly assimilated the basic rules, your judgement of such charts will be sound, no matter how cautiously you might edge forward towards it. I have found that it is with judgements like this, where I have felt that I am stepping onto a bridge of gossamer, that my work has been most applauded by clients, for the successful clarification of issues too tangled to resolve in any other way. 在作出论断前，切勿强求笃定。有些星盘清晰明确；有些则需要你抽丝剥茧方能 得出答案。若执意等待确凿无疑的结论，必将永无止境。但若你已彻底掌握基本 规则，即便步步为营地谨慎推进，对此类星盘的判断仍将稳健可靠。我发现，正 是在那些如履薄冰的论断中——当我感觉自己正踏上游丝之桥时——我的工作

反而最受客户赞誉，因为成功厘清了那些盘根错节、用其他任何方式都无从化解 的难题。

There is a common myth that we must find three testimonies in the chart before we can give judgement. This is nonsense, propagated by those who fear giving judgement. If half a testimony is all we have, that is all we have. We must work with what we are given. Few indeed are the charts with three clear testimonies. To continue with the footballing metaphor, we can win 6-0 or we can win by one disputed goal in the last minuter: we have still won. 有个普遍的误解，认为我们必须找到三个征象才能作出论断。这纯属无稽之谈， 是那些畏惧论断之人散布的观点。如果我们仅有一半征象，那便以这一半为依据 ——我们必须基于既有的线索开展工作。真正具备三个清晰征象的星盘实则凤毛 麟角。延续足球的比喻：我们既可以 6 比 0 大获全胜，也能在终场前凭一粒争议 进球险胜——但终究都是胜利。

The worksheet 工作单

I suggest you copy this worksheet and use it each time you judge a chart. It will help ensure that you have the information you need for judgement, while gradually training you to identify exactly what information you do need. 我建议你复印这份工作单，并在每次判断星盘时使用。它将帮助你确保掌握论断 所需的所有信息，同时逐步培养你精准识别真正需要信息的能力。

“Isn’t this the same as the software pages you’ve just told me not to use?”No. Those pages are a waste of time purporting to be a labour-saving device. This worksheet is an educational tool. To fill in this worksheet, you need to look at the chart, and look at it in some depth. Even though much of the information you put on it is the same as that given you by the horary pages, the act of extracting this information from the chart yourself will show you things that the study of a prepared list will not. As you gain familiarity with the horary process, you will reduce the amount of information you put on this form. After a while, you will abandon it altogether; but do not rush this process. “这难道跟你刚才让我别用的那些软件页面是一回事吗？”并非如此。那些页面 号称是省力工具，实则浪费时间。而这份工作单是一种教学工具。填写这份工作 单需要你仔细观察星盘，并进行一定深度的剖析。尽管你在单子上记录的许多信 息与卜卦页面提供的内容相同，但亲手从星盘中提取这些信息的过程，将让你看 到研读现成列表所无法展现的细节。随着你对卜卦流程日益熟悉，你会逐渐减少 填写在此表格中的信息量。一段时间后，你将完全不再需要它——但切勿急于求 成。

You may not yet understand some of the terms on this sheet: they are explained in the

following chapters. 您可能尚不理解本工作单中的部分术语：这些将在后续章节中阐述。

INVOCATION: to remind us of what we are doing. 祈请：用以提醒我们当下所为之事。

QUERENT/QUESTION: the querent’s name and the question asked. 问卦者/问题：记录问卜者姓名及其所提问题。

TIME, DATE, PLACE: the data on which the chart is set. 时间、日期、地点：用于设定星盘的数据。

QUERENT/QUESITED’S PLANETS: the significator or significators of the querent and of whatever is being asked about. 问卜者/所问之事的征象星：征象星，代表问卜者的征象星以及所问不论何事的 征象星。

MOON: the Moon’s most recent aspect and its next aspect. 月亮：月亮的最近一次相位及其下一次相位。

DIGNITIES: enter the glyph for the planet ruling the sign in which each planet falls; that which is exalted there; the triplicity ruler, and so on. Example: if the Sun were at 3 Aires in daytime chart, the Sun column would read: 尊贵： 填入每个行星所在星座的守护星符号、旺势行星符号、三分主星符号等。 例如：若太阳位于白羊座 3 度（日间盘），则太阳一栏应记为：

You may wish to highlight indications of the planet being in its own dignity or debility. 您或许需要重点标注出行星入庙或落陷的征象。

NOTE：anything of significance about the planet, e.g. its being combust, retrograde, in station. 注：记录行星的重要状态，例如：燃烧、逆行、停滞。

FIXED STARS: list any major stars that fall within a degree or so of the main significators or relevant house cusps. You can allow a couple of degrees for Regulus, Spica and Caput Algol. 恒星：列出所有与主要征象星或相关宫头成 1 度左右相位的主要恒星。对于轩辕

十四、角宿一、大陵五这三颗恒星，容许度可放宽至 2-3 度。

ANTISCIA: list the antiscia of any planets that fall on the main significators, or on relevant house-cusps (within about a degree). 映点：列出所有落在主要征象星或相关宫头（容许度约 1 度）上的行星映点。

RECEPTIONS: list all major mutual receptions between the planets. Reception does not have to be mutual to be significant, but strong mutual receptions can have a significance of their own. By ‘strong’, I mean reception by sign, exaltation or triplicity. Don’t forget negative mutual reception (by detriment or fall): this can be important too. 接纳关系：列出所有行星间的主要互溶关系。接纳关系未必需要是相互的才具有 意义，但强烈的互溶关系可能具有独特意义。此处“强烈”指通过入庙、旺势或 三分性实现的接纳关系。切勿忽略负面互溶（通过失势或落陷形成）：这类关系 同样可能至关重要。

# THE GOLDEN RULES

# 核心法则

KEEP IT SIMPLE 保持简单

No matter how complicated the chart, don’t panic. Keep asking yourself the same simple questions about aspect, dignity and reception and you will arrive at the answer. 无论星盘多么复杂，不必惊慌。只要持续追问关于相位、尊贵与接纳关系的相同 基础问题，你终将得出答案。

Resist the temptation to blame the chart for being uncooperative, and then to think that an answer will be revealed if only you add this or that new technique – minor aspects, perhaps, or an asteroid or two. If the answer doesn’t appear to be there, this is because you cannot yet see it. Concentrate on what is in the chart, assessing this in these same simple ways, and you soon will. 切忌因星盘看似不配合而归咎于它，更不要以为只需引入某种新技法——例如次 要相位或几颗小行星——答案便会自动显现。若答案尚未浮现，那是因为你尚未 洞察其踪迹。专注于星盘呈现的要素，以同样简洁的方式加以评估，你很快便能 拨云见日。

This refers to Golden Rule number 2, which is: 此处对应核心法则第二条：

THERE IS ALWAYS AN ANSWER IN THERE SOMEWHERE 答案必存于星盘之中

It is often found a few steps after the point at which you decide not to give up. 答案往往就在你决定坚持之后的不远处出现。

MIX DISCRETION WITH ART 融判断于技艺

This is Lilly’s oft-repeated phrase for ‘use your common sense’. 这正是 Lilly 常挂在嘴边的话，意为“运用你的常识”。

TALK TO THE QUERENT 与问卜者沟通

If you are not sure of the exact meaning of the question, ask for clarification. If you still aren’t sure, ask again. Some querents will ask questions of runic obscurity: make sure you understand before you cast the chart. 若不确定问题的确切含义，请主动寻求澄清。若仍存疑虑，不妨再次询问。。有

些问卜者会提出如符咒般晦涩的问题——务必在绘制星盘前确保自己真正理解 其意图。

If you find a planet is important in the chart, but you don’t know what it signifies, ask the querent. If you need to know who is involved in the situation, ask. 若发现星盘中某颗行星至关重要，却不知其象征意义，直接询问问卜者。若需了 解事件涉及的具体人物，也应主动提问。你无需猜测——直接询问问卜者即可。

It is easy, for example, to work out a detailed judgement about the lost object being with the querent’s husband, only to have the querent tell you that she is not married. 例如，你很可能耗费大量精力详细推断出失物正位于问卜者丈夫处，结果却被告 知她根本未婚。

YOU ARE ALLOWED TO BE WRONG 犯错是被允许的

Strive to make your judgements accurate, of course. But what we are doing here is remarkable: that we cannot always be successful is no cause to lament. That we can achieve what we do achieve is quite remarkable enough. 当然要力求论断精准。但我们此刻所从事之事本就非凡：无法始终成功无需哀叹， 能够取得现有的已足够了不起。

# The Houses

# 宫位

William Lilly rightly says that once the student has the ability to set a chart, the most important thing to understand is the meanings of the houses. Everything that exists can be assigned to one or other of the twelve houses of the chart. If we look at the wrong house to locate whatever our querent is asking about, we shall probably arrive at the wrong answer to the querent’s question. A clear understanding of the houses is therefore essential. William Lilly 曾正确指出，学生一旦掌握了排盘能力，最重要的便是理解宫位的 含义。万事万物皆可归属于星盘十二宫中的某一宫。若在解读问卜者所问之事 时找错了宫位，便很可能对其问题得出错误的答案。因此，清晰理解宫位含义至 关重要。

5. Lilly, introductory pages: To the Reader.

The chart is divided into twelve sections. Technically, these are called mundane houses (or earthly houses) in contrast to the celestial houses, which is another name for the signs of the zodiac. Although it is customary now to refer to the celestial houses as ‘signs’ it is worth remembering that they too are houses. The word ‘house’ can often be taken literally in the chart, as representing a physical abode, whether it is a celestial (sign) or mundane house. The old texts refer to both signs and houses as ‘houses’. Although this is correct, it can sometimes be confusing. 星盘被分成十二个部分。严格来说，这些部分称为“宫位”（即地上的居所）， 以区别于“天上的宫位”——后者是黄道十二星座的别称。尽管现今习惯将“天 上的居所”称为“星座”，但值得牢记的是：它们同样属于“宫所”的范畴。在 星盘中，“宫”字常可作字面理解，无论是指星座还是宫位，往往代表着实体居 所。古典文献中将星座与宫位统称为“宫所”。这种说法虽准确，但有时可能引 发混淆。

Imagine the chart is a cake. There are many ways of dividing it into twelve slices, giving us the twelve houses of the chart. Do we divide the cake by eye? Do we count the number of cherries in each section and divide it equally like that? Do we divide it according to the appetite of those who are to eat it, making sure each is equally satisfied? Similarly, there are many ways of dividing the chart into houses. These are called house systems. 不妨将星盘想象成一个蛋糕。我们可以用多种方式将其均分为十二份，这就构成

了星盘中的十二宫位。是凭肉眼切分？还是通过计算每份的樱桃数量来均分？或 是根据食客的胃口进行分配，确保每人获得同等的满足感？同理，划分星盘宫位 也存在多种方法——这些方法被称为“分宫制”。

The charts in this book are cast in the Regiomontanus house system. I urge you to use this for horary. It is the system used by Lilly, and it works, as can be shown not by the subjective criterion of ‘I prefer my birthchart cast by this system because it puts my Venus in this house not that house’, but because we can make accurate predictions from the position of the house-cusps it gives, which is the on variable between systems. 本书中的所有星盘均采用 Regiomontanus 分宫制绘制。我强烈建议您在卜卦占星 中使用这一分宫制。此分宫制为 Lilly 所沿用，且其有效性经得起检验——这并 非基于“我更喜欢用这个系统绘制本命盘，因为它会将我的金星安置在这个宫位 而非那个宫位”之类的主观判断，而是因为我们可以根据该分宫制确定的宫头位 置做出精准预测，而宫头位置正是不同分宫制中唯一的变量。

This does not imply that Regiomontanus is the best system for all purposes: I use Placidus for natal work. Regiomontanus is well suited to horary. If you were to divide the sky into equal chunks by eye, Regiomontanus is what you would get. It is observer-based, bringing the division of the heavens right down to Earth, which is wholly appropriate for horary, where the question asked by this person right here now is what determines the reality of the chart. 这并不意味着 Regiomontanus 分宫制在所有场景下都是最佳选择：我在分析本命 盘时会使用 Placidus 分宫制。Regiomontanus 分宫制尤其适用于卜卦占星——若 以肉眼将天空划分为均等区块，所得结果正与此分宫制吻合。分宫制尤其适用于 卜卦占星——若以肉眼将天空划分为均等区块，所得结果正与此分宫制吻合。

“But why are the house in the chart different sizes?”They aren’t. They are all equal. Consider your own home. This may be equal to someone else’s in many ways: because it covers the same number of square yards; because it has the same number of bedrooms; because it can fetch the same price on the market. It is the same with astrological houses: they are equal in many different ways. Regiomontanus houses are all 30 degrees across, but 30 degrees of Right Ascension, not of Celestial Longitude. As the degrees on the cusps (5 Taurus, 12 Gemini, and so forth) are measured in Celestial Longitude, the houses do not appear to be the same size – just as my house may not be the same size as yours in floor area, but it might be in terms of the number of rooms it has. “但为什么星盘中的宫位大小不一？”其实它们大小是相等的。不妨以您自己的 住宅为例：它在许多方面可能与别人的居所等价——比如占地面积相同、卧室数 量一致、市场售价相当。占星宫位也是如此：它们通过不同维度实现均等。 Regiomontanus 分宫制的所有宫位均横跨 30 度，但计量单位是赤经度数而非黄道 经度。由于宫头位置（金牛座 5 度、双子座 12 度等）是以黄道经度测算的，这 些宫位在视觉上显得大小不均——正如我的住宅可能与您的房屋占地面积不同， 但房间数量却可能恰好一致。

6. Right Ascension is measurement along the celestial equator. Celestial Longitude is measurement along the ecliptic. They both divide the sky into 360 degrees. Imagine there are two motorways leaving a city. One heads due east, so driving 30 miles along that takes you 30 miles east. The other heads a little north by east: drive 30 miles along that and you have travelled perhaps 25 miles east and a few miles north. But you have still travelled 30 miles. Right Ascension and Celestial Longitude are related to each other in the same way.
6. 赤经是沿天赤道的度量，而黄道经度是沿黄道的度量。二者均将天空划分为 360 度。试想有两条高速公路离开同一座城市：一条向正东方延伸，在此行驶 30 英里意味着向东前进了 30 英里；另一条则朝向东北偏北方向，沿其行驶 30 英里 后，您可能向东行进了约 25 英里，同时向北移动了若干英里。但两种情况下， 您的实际行驶距离都是 30 英里。赤经与黄道经度的相互关系正是如此。

There is a fashion among those astrologers who study ancient texts to practice horary with whole sign houses. Apart from being philosophically questionable, this sacrifices finesse. Use Regiomontanus: it works, and works well. 当前部分研习古籍的占星师间流行着采用整宫制进行卜卦占星的做法。这种做法 不仅在哲学层面值得商榷，更会牺牲推演的精准性。请坚持使用 Regiomontanus 分宫制：它经得起实践检验，且效果卓越。

This distinction between Right Ascension and Celestial Longitude means that charts cast in Regiomontanus will often have some signs sitting on more than on house cusp, while other signs are completely contained within a house, not being on any house cusp. Signs that are completely contained within a house, having no cusp falling within them, are called incepted or intercepted. Turn to the chart on page 92, where Aries and Pisces are incepted in the 12th house and Libra and Virgo in the 6th. There is nothing of any significance in a sign being incepted, or a planet being in a sign that is incepted. The sign doesn’t happen to have a house cusp in it – that’s all. 赤经与黄道经度的区分意味着：采用 Regiomontanus 分宫制绘制的星盘中，常会 出现某些星座横跨多个宫头，而另一些星座则完全包含在单一宫位内、未与任何 宫头重叠的情形。完全内含于某一宫位、未与任何宫头重合的星座，称为劫夺或 者截夺星座。请翻阅第 160 页的星盘示例：其中白羊座与双鱼座在 12 宫被截夺， 天秤座与处女座在 6 宫被截夺。星座被截夺或行星落入被截夺星座本身并无特殊 意义——这仅仅意味着该星座恰好未与任何宫头重合而已。

7. The same is true in natal astrology.
7. 在本命占星学中，这一原则同样适用。

### ✸May I repeat this in a very loud voice, please: There is nothing of any significance

in a sign being incepted, or a planet being in a sign that is incepted. It does not mean that a planet in such a sign is isolated, unable to act, or misunderstood because it’s more sensitive than other people realize. It just happens to be in a sign that does not fall onto a house cusp. That’s all.

### ✸请允许我在此高声强调：星座被截夺，或行星落入被截夺的星座，其本身并

无任何特殊意义。这绝不意味着该行星处于孤立状态、无法发挥作用，或是因其 比旁人认知中更为敏感而被误解——它仅仅恰好处在未与任何宫头重合的星座 中，仅此而已。

Nor does the ruler of an incepted sign share rulership of the house in which that sign is incepted. There is no such animal as the co-ruler of a house. ✷ 同样地，被截夺星座的守护星也不会共享该星座所在宫位的统治权。宫位根本不 存在所谓的“共同守护星”这一概念✷

When using Regiomontanus (or Placidus), a planet in the 5 degrees or so immediately before a house cusp is regarded as being in that next house. Example: in the chart on page 92 the Moon is at 26 Cancer and the 5th cusp at 28 Cancer. The Moon is within 5 degrees of that cusp, and so in the 5th, not the 4th, house. 使 Regiomontanus 分宫制（或者 Placidus 分宫制）时，若行星位于宫头前约 5 度 范围内，则该行星被视为已进入下一个宫位。例如：在第 160 页的星盘中，月亮 位于巨蟹座 26 度，而 5 宫头在巨蟹座 28 度。月亮在 5 度内接近宫头，因此被认 为在 5 宫内，而不是 4 宫。

This 5-degree limit is flexible: use your common sense. If the house before the cusp is a huge house with one or even two incepted signs in it, we would be more free with 5-degrees limit than if it were a narrow house, with perhaps only 20 degrees of longitude from one side to the other. 这个 5 度范围的界定是灵活的：请运用您的常识判断。若宫头前的宫位范围很大， 其中包含一个甚至两个截夺星座，那么我们应用 5 度范围时就可以比对待狭窄宫 位（其黄道经度跨度可能仅有 20 度）时更为宽松。

NB: to be counted as being in the next house, the planet must be in the same sign as the cusp, no matter how close it is to that cusp. If the cusp were at 5.59 Taurus, we would regard a planet at 0.01 Taurus as being in that house; if the cusp were at 0.20 Taurus, a planet at 29.50 Aries would not be regarded as being in that house. 注意：若要将行星计为位于下一个宫位，则该行星必须与宫头位于同一星座内， 无论其与宫头距离多近。若宫头位于金牛座 5 度 59 分，则位于金牛座 0 度 01 分的行星应被视为在该宫位内；但若宫头位于金牛座 0 度 20 分，则位于白羊座 29 度 50 分的行星仍不可被视为属于该宫位。

Think of this area in front of the cusp as the front garden of the house. You may not be inside the house, but if you are in the front garden you are on that property – and you are definitely not in the house next door. There is nothing fuzzy or ambiguous about this: the planet is either in the one house or in the other. 不妨将宫头前的这片区域视作该宫位的“前院”。你虽未进入建筑内部，但若身 处前院，便已属于该宫位的属地——且明确不属于相邻宫位。这种界定不存在任 何模糊或模棱两可：行星要么位于这个宫位，要么位于另一个宫位，非此即彼。

This 5-degree rule applies only to house, not to signs. A planet in the last few degrees of its sign is not regarded as being in the next sign. 这条 5 度规则仅适用于宫位划分，而不适用于星座界定。位于星座末几度的行星， 仍被视为处于当前星座而非下一个星座。

Throughout this book, when I describe a planet as being on a cusp, I mean that it is in the one or two degrees immediately before that cusp. When I say it is inside the cusp, I mean it is in the couple of degrees immediately following that cusp. 在本书中，当我描述某行星“位于宫头”时，意指该行星处于紧邻该宫头之前的 一至两度范围内；而当我说它“进入宫头”时，则指其位于紧接该宫头之后的数 度范围内。

### ✸There is never any significance in the cusp falling in a very early or very late

degree of a sign. If, for instance, the cusp is at 29.59 degrees of whichever sign, this does not mean that situation regarding that house is about to change. This is because cusps do not move. Ever. Seeing a cusp as moving would be like sitting in the theatre and seeing the balcony chase Romeo across the stage. Nor does a late degree of the cusp mean that the ruler of the next sign is really the significator of matters of that house.✷

### ✸宫头落于星座的极早期度数或极晚期度数，其本身从不具有任何特殊意义。

例如，若某宫头位于某个星座的 29 度 59 分，这并不意味着该宫位所对应的事务 即将发生变化。因为宫头是固定不动的——绝不会移动。将宫头视作会移动之物， 就如同坐在剧院里看着阳台在舞台上追逐罗密欧般荒谬。同样地，宫头位于晚期 度数也绝不意味着下一个星座的守护星能真正成为该宫位事务的征象星。✷

HOUSE MEANING 宫位的含义

As between them the house contain everything in our world, an exhaustive list of meaning is impossible; this list covers the main topics. Part 2 of this book considers questions typical to each house. 十二宫位囊括了世间万物的对应范畴，故其含义无法穷尽；此处仅列出主要议题。 本书第二部分将针对各宫位对应的典型问题展开探讨。

8. For a discussion of why things belong to the houses that they do, see my The Real Astrology Applied, Apprentice Books, London, 2002, p.147 onwards. Hereafter referred to as RA Applied.
8. 若需探讨事物归属特定宫位的原理，请参阅本人著作《The Real Astrology Applied》伦敦学徒出版社 2002 年版，第 147 页及后续内容。下文中简称 RA Applied。

If you are to assign things to their correct houses, it is vital to understand the difference between the thing itself and the function of that thing. The thing is what it is; its function may vary. Example: my piano is my possession and it is movable, so it is 2nd house. It has nothing to do with the 5th house of creativity and pleasure. To assign it to the 5th makes irrelevant assumptions: that I can play it; that it is playable; that I enjoy playing it. My piano is my movable possession, and so is 2nd house, even if my only use for it is to conceal a damp patch on the wall. 若要将事物准确归入对应宫位，关键在于理解事物本身与其功能之间的区别。事 物本质是固定的，但其功能可能变化。例如：我的钢琴是我的财物且可移动，因 此属于 2 宫范畴。它与代表创造力与愉悦的 5 宫毫无关联。若将其归入 5 宫，便 掺杂了无关的假设：诸如我会弹奏、钢琴可供演奏、我享受弹奏过程等。我的钢 琴是我的动产，故属于 2 宫——即便我唯一的用途是用它遮盖墙上的湿渍。

1st house 1 宫

Its main role is to show the querent. It shows the querent’s body, although in a medical question the whole chart can show the body, in which case the 1st shows the head. It shows ‘the ship that I sail in’: my immediate vehicle, on the analogy of the body being the vehicle of the soul. The querent’s name. 1 宫的主要角色是表征问卜者。它代表问卜者的身体（不过在医疗问题中，整个 星盘均可反映身体状况，此时 1 宫特指头部）。它象征着“我所乘坐的舟船”— —即最直接的载具，这源于“身体是灵魂的载具”之喻。同时也对应问卜者的姓 名。

The first is ‘me’; it can aslo be ‘us’. When one spouse asks about something that the couple plans to do, the chart can either show querent and spouse individually as 1th and 7th houses, or it can show them both as 1st:‘us’. It aslo shows larger groups of which the querent is a part (‘Will we get the contract?’) and large groups with which the querent identifies (‘Will we – meaning the football team the querent supports – win on Saturday?’). 1 宫代表“我”，亦可指代“我们”。当配偶一方询问双方计划进行的事务时， 星盘既可将问卜者与配偶分别呈现为 1 宫与 7 宫，也可将双方共同视为 1 宫（“我 们”）。它同样适用于问卜者所属的较大群体（例如“我们能拿下合同吗？”）， 以及问卜者认同的大型集体（例如“我们——指问卜者支持的足球队——周六能 获胜吗？”）。

The 1st shows the general situation in the querent’s location. So if I ask ‘Will we have a hot summer?’ I look to the 1st: the general situation here. 1 宫反映的是问卜者所在地的整体状况。因此，若我问“今年夏天会炎热吗？”， 我需要查看 1 宫——即此地的整体环境。

2nd house 2 宫

It shows the querent’s movable possessions. If it cannot be moved ✷e.g. your house or land) or if it is animate, it cannot truly be possessed. If it’s yours, inanimate and can be moved, it belongs here. So your car is shown by your 2nd house: it’s yours and it can be moved. It is not 3rd: remember the distinction between the thing itself and the function of that thing. 2 宫代表问卜者的动产。若物品无法移动（如房屋或土地），或具有生命，则不 能真正被“拥有”。凡是属于你、无生命且可移动的物体，皆归于此宫。因此你 的汽车由 2 宫表示：它归你所有且可被移动。它不属于 3 宫：请务必区分物体本 身与其功能之间的差异。

It is the querent’s money, in whatever form that takes: currency, bank account, stocks and bonds. It is the querent’s self-esteem, self-valuing, and aslo esteem for the partner: esteem, or value, seen as a transferable thing. 2 宫象征问卜者的财富（无论以货币、银行存款、股票债券等何种形式存在）。 它代表问卜者的自我价值感、自我认同，同时也包含对伴侣的看重——这种“重 视”被视作一种可转移的情感价值。

It is your closest advisors, like the consigliere in The Godfather. the one who whispers advice into your ear. In a duel it is your second; in court it is your lawyer and the witnesses who testify on your behalf. Your lawyer is 2nd only if acting for you in this case that is being asked about now; otherwise lawyers belong in the 9th, as learned people. 2 宫代表你身边最亲近的谋士，如同《教父》中的军师——那个在你耳边低语献 策之人。决斗中它是你的副手；法庭上它是你的律师及为你作证的证人。需注意： 仅当律师正在处理当前问卜事项时归入 2 宫；否则律师属于 9 宫范畴，因其属于 学者阶层。

It is the throat and whatever goes into the throat, hence food. It is what sustains the 1st house. 它 2 宫对应喉咙及经喉咙进入之物，故也代表食物。它是滋养 1 宫的生命之源。

### ✸The mouth and jaw should be regarded as 2nd house, not 1st, being seen as part of

the throat and what goes into it. The rest of the head is 1st house.✷

### ✸嘴与下颚应归属于 2 宫而非 1 宫，因其被视为喉咙及进食通道的组成部分。

头部的其余部分则属于 1 宫范畴。✷

3rd house 3 宫

Your siblings and cousins. Your daily round; the routine journeys that you make for the mundane business of your life. These tend to be shorter than the special journeys that we make, hence the common label of ‘short journeys’ for this house. But if I walk round the corner to visit a shrine, that is a pilgrimage, a 9th-house sort of journey, despite its being so short. Your office could be next door to the church you attend, but your journey to your office would be 3rd house, your journey to church 9th. 3 宫代表你的兄弟姐妹与堂表亲。涵盖你的日常行程：为处理生活琐事而进行的 例行出行。这类行程通常比特殊出行更短，故该宫位常被称为“短途出行”。但 若我前往街角参拜圣地，即便距离极近，也属于朝圣之旅，归 9 宫范畴。你的办 公室可能与你常去的教堂相邻，但通勤办公属于 3 宫，前往教堂则属 9 宫。

The knowledge that you need to negotiate your daily round: the ‘3 Rs’. The elementary school where you acquire this knowledge. The letter that you are sending. The letter you are expecting is usually shown by the 9th (3rd from the 7th); the letter you keep for sentimental reasons is your possession, and so is 2nd. Rumours and gossip. 3 宫代表应对日常所需的知识基础：“3R”基本技能（读、写、算）。授予这些 知识的初级学校。你发出的信件。你寄出的信件属此宫（而你期待的信件通常由 9 宫表示，即 7 宫之 3 宫）；因情感留存的书信属于个人财物，故归 2 宫。流言 蜚语与闲言碎语亦属此宫。

Being the opposite house to the 9th (the querent’s teacher), it shows the querent’s students. 作为 9 宫（问卜者的老师）的对宫，3 宫代表问卜者的学生。

【Which house shows a classmate? - Posted on May 30th, 2014 【哪个宫位显示同学？- 发布于 2014 年 5 月 30 日

A querent asked about ‘a former classmate’, which raises the interesting question of where we locate a classmate in the chart. That the querent described him as a classmate clearly rules out the 11th house. The astrological concept of friendship is something much more limited, much more precious, than that in common English usage. If you aren’t sure if the person is your friend, the person is not your friend. The classmate could be 7th house, as a workmate would be, the workmate being regarded as your equal in the working situation. But while we don’t choose our individual workmates there is yet an element of choice involved, in that we choose to work in this place or that place, which does not apply to a classmate. Classmates are more a part of our natural environment, like our brothers and sisters. For that reason, I would take the classmate as 3rd house, like an extended version of a sibling.】 一位问卦者询问“一位以前的同学”，这引出了一个有趣的问题：我们应该在星 盘的哪个宫位定位这位同学。问卦者将他描述为“同学”，这明确排除了第 11 宫。占星学中“友谊”的概念，比日常英语用法中的含义要有限得多、珍贵得多。 如果你不确定某人是否是你的朋友，那么他就不是你的朋友。这位同学可能归 7

宫，就像同事一样，同事在工作环境中被视为与你平等的人。但是，虽然我们不 能选择具体的同事，但其中仍然包含选择的因素，即我们选择在这个或那个地方 工作，而这对于同学来说并不适用。同学更像是我们自然环境的一部分，如同我 们的兄弟姐妹。因此，我会将同学归为 3 宫，像是兄弟姐妹的延伸版。】

It shows neighbours. Sometimes this is in the biblical sense of ‘all those I encounter in my daily round’; more often it is specifically those who live next to my home. 3 宫代表邻居。有时取圣经中“日常接触的所有人”之泛化含义；更多时候特指 居住在我住宅旁的人。

The arms, shoulders and hands. 3 宫对应手臂、肩膀与双手。

### ✸To clarify: the letter you are expecting is usually shown by the 3rd from the 7th

because it is mail from 7th-house people (sweethearts, spouses, those with whom we do business) that querents most often ask about. A letter from someone else would be shown by the 3rd from that person’s house: if from my boss or my mother, 3rd from the 10th; if from my child, 3rd from the 5th. As with letters, so with emails, phone-calls and whatever other forms of communication may be en vogue by the time you read this.

### ✸需要说明的是：通常期待的信件由 7 宫之 3 宫表示，因为问卜者最常询问的

往往是来自 7 宫相关人（恋人、配偶、商业伙伴）的邮件。若信件来自其他人， 则由该人对应宫位之 3 宫表示：例如来自老板或母亲的信件对应 10 宫之 3 宫； 来自子女的信件对应 5 宫之 3 宫。信件如此，电子邮件、电话通讯以及您阅读本 书时可能盛行的任何其他沟通形式亦遵循此规则。

Books and websites are not 3rd-house objects. If I wish to send a message to someone, I don’t write a book in order to do this. The book I have written is, as below, 5th house: ‘my baby’. Note that the book is distinct from whatever knowledge I may have put into it (9th house). If your website is promoting your business it is your shop-window: 10th house. So profit from it will be 2nd from the 10th, which is the 11th. The site on which you post amusing pictures of kittens is 5th house: entertainment. ✷ 书籍与网站不属于 3 宫范畴。若我想向某人传递信息，不会为此专门撰写书籍。 我所写的书籍如下文所述属于 5 宫：“我的孩子”。需注意：书籍本身与我写入 书中的知识（属 9 宫）截然不同。若你的网站用于推广业务，它便是你的“橱窗”： 属 10 宫。因此其盈利来自 10 宫之 2 宫，即 11 宫。而你发布趣味猫咪图片的网 站则属 5 宫：娱乐范畴。✷

4th house 4 宫

Your father; your parents in general; your ancestry. Your immovable possessions: houses and property. Your holiday home in Spain is still 4th house: it is your property that happens to be abroad; there is nothing 9th-house about it. Your orchard and all that grows in it – including that potted plant in your living-room. Your home country (‘abroad’ being 9th house). 4 宫代表你的父亲；泛指的父母；你的祖先。你的不动产：房屋与地产。你在西 班牙的度假屋仍属 4 宫——这是你恰巧位于国外的房产，与 9 宫无关。你的果园 及园中所有作物（包括你客厅里的盆栽植物）。你的祖国（“外国”则属 9 宫范畴）。

【Property rights - Posted on July 1st, 2014 【产权 - 发布于 2014 年 7 月 1 日

A student asks about a horary where the querent has a long-term lease on a property and is now in dispute with the state, which owns the property. Is the property shown by the querent’s 4th or the 4th from the 10th (property of the government)? 一位学生询问一个卜卦案例：问卦人长期租赁一处房产，现与拥有该房产所有权 的政府发生纠纷。该房产应由问卦人的第 4 宫代表，还是由第 10 宫的第 4 宫（政 府的财产）代表？

It’s not necessary for the person to have any kind of legal ownership of the property: it is still ‘his’ property, so it is shown by his 4th house. This is the whole point of the distinction between 2nd-house property, such as my computer, and 4th-house property, such as the house in which I live. 4th-house property is not really our possession, and no amount of legal documentation can change this. The idea is that if I can’t move it around I cannot in any meaningful way be said to own it; I just have the temporary use of it. It makes no difference whether the querent has bought the property, or is leasing it, renting it, or squatting in it: it is his 4th house. The stars have no interest in our legal documents.】 此人不必对该房产拥有任何形式的法律所有权：它仍然是“他的”房产，因此由 他的 4 宫代表。这正是区分 2 宫财产（如我的电脑）和 4 宫财产（如我居住的房 子）的全部要点。4 宫的财产并非我们真正拥有之物，无论多少法律文件都无法 改变这一点。其理念是：如果我无法移动它，就不能真正意义上说我拥有它；我 只是暂时使用它。无论问卦人是购买了该房产，还是租赁、租借或擅自占用，都 不影响：它都是他的 4 宫。星辰对我们的法律文件毫无兴趣。】

‘The end of the matter’: the way the situation will turn out. This can usually be ignored, except in can show the prognosis. If testimonies in other issues are finely balanced, it can be worth taking a look at the condition of the 4th and its ruler; but do this only as a last resort: strive to find your judgement from the main significators. 4 宫象征“事情的终局”：即事态发展的最终走向。通常可忽略此含义，除非用 于判断预后。若其他关键证象呈现胶着状态，可观察 4 宫及其守护星的状况作为 参考；但此举仅应作为最终手段：务必力求从主要征象星中得出结论。

Being at the bottom of the chart it shows mines and other things underground, such as buried treasure. 由于位于星盘底部，4 宫代表矿山及其他地下事物，例如埋藏的宝藏。

The chest and lungs. 4 宫对应胸部与肺部。

Note that although the 4th is at the bottom of the chart, it shows north. The convention here is different from that used on maps: the Ascendant is east, Descendant west, 10th house south. Intermediate directions are derived from these points. 需注意：尽管 4 宫位于星盘底部，但它代表北方。此处的方位设定与地图惯例不 同：上升点为东方，下降点为西方，10 宫为南方。中间方位则根据这些基点推 导得出。

The 4th cusp is aslo known as the IC (imum coeli: lowest part of the heavens). 4 宫头亦被称为 IC（天底，源自拉丁文 imum coeli，意为“天球最低点”）。

### ✸I was too generous, even with what I wrote above, with the idea of the 4th house

showing ‘the end of the matter’. Ignore this, except where ‘the end of the matter’ has a specific role in the situation. This is mainly in court cases, where it is the verdict, which is, of course, the end of that matter. The idea that we can use this in other circumstances comes only from the astrologer’s wish to have a Plan B available, to save telling the client something client will not wish to hear: ‘You think she might love you? Are you crazy! Ah, but if we look at the end of the matter…’ Regardless of the lack of truth in whatever this Plan B provides.

### ✸即便我先前关于 4 宫代表“事情终局”的论述，现在看来也过于宽泛了。请

忽略这一概念——除非“事情终局”在具体情境中具有特定作用（主要体现于诉 讼案件中的判决结果，这自然是该事件的终结）。将这一概念套用于其他情境， 不过是占星师为准备“备用方案”的自我安慰：当需要向客户传达其不愿接受的 真相时（“你以为她可能爱你？你疯了吗！啊，不过如果我们看看事情结局…”）， 便以此作为托辞——即便这个备用方案所提供的结论毫无真实依据。

Lilly gives cities to 4th house, in which, following Bonatti, he assumes the city is being besieged by the querent. As such, it would be seen as a piece of real-estate that the querent would like to possess. The city can be shown by different houses, as determined by the context. Often it will be 1st house, as the querent’s ‘here’. If I ask, ‘What will the weather be in Warsaw?’ the city is not 4th house, but simply the ‘here’ of where I live: 1st. If I live in the country and am thinking of moving to the city, the city will be 7th house, seen as the ‘there’ to which I may go. ✷

Lilly 将城市归入 4 宫范畴，其依据是 Bonatti（博纳蒂）的论述——假设问卜者 正在围困该城市。此时城市被视为问卜者意图占领的一块不动产。但城市的宫位

归属需根据具体语境确定：常作为问卜者所在的“此地”归于 1 宫（例如询问“华 沙天气如何”）；若问卜者居住于乡村并计划迁往城市，则该城市作为可能前往 的“彼处”应归于 7 宫。✷

5th house 5 宫

Pleasure, and the places where we take pleasure: ‘banquets, ale-houses and taverns’ as Lilly says; theatres, parties, sports. 5 宫象征愉悦，以及我们获得愉悦的场所：如 Lilly 所言——“宴会、酒馆与客 栈”；还包括剧院、派对、体育赛事。

Children and pregnancy. Not, note, pregnant women: a pregnant woman is a woman who happens to be pregnant, so she has the same house as she does when she is not pregnant (3rd for my sister, 7th for my wife, etc). As this is the house of pregnancy, it is the house of sex (emphatically not the 8th!). But no matter how tenuous might be the querent’s relationship with the sexual partner, that partner is a person, and so is 7th house, not 5th. So even if th querent is married, his mistress is still 7th house; what he does with her is 5th. It is that same distinction between the thing itself and the function of that thing. Although pregnancy is 5th, childbed itself is 12th (‘confinement’). The book that I have written or picture I have painted is considered as ‘my baby’: 5th house. 5 宫代表子女与妊娠。需注意：孕妇本身并不属于此宫——孕妇只是处于特殊生 理状态的女性，其宫位归属与未怀孕时相同（例如我的姐妹归 3 宫，我的妻子归 7 宫等）。由于此宫掌管妊娠，故也代表性行为（绝非 8 宫！）。但无论问卜者 与性伴侣的关系多么淡薄，对方作为独立个体仍属 7 宫而非 5 宫。因此即使问卜 者已婚，其情妇仍归 7 宫，而双方行为则属 5 宫——这再次体现了事物本身与其 功能的根本区别。虽然妊娠属 5 宫，但分娩过程本身归 12 宫（“限制”范畴）。 我所撰写的书籍或绘制的画作被视为“我的孩子”：属于 5 宫。

Being the second house from the 4th, the 5th has important meanings as the father’s money and the profit from the querent’s property. 作为 4 宫之 2 宫，5 宫具有重要含义：象征父亲的钱财，以及问卜者从财产中获 得的收益。

It shows messengers and ambassadors. 5 宫代表信使与外交使节。

In the body, it covers the heart, liver, stomach, sides and back. 在身体层面，5 宫对应心脏、肝脏、胃部、肋部与背部。

### ✸The messenger, in the sense here, is someone who speaks for himself. Like an

ambassador, he may carry a letter, but he will have been briefed on its contents and related matters. His job is not to hand over the letter in silence, but to elaborate, persuade, or even perform. The postman, delivering a letter of whose contents he knows nothing, is not a messenger, but a servant (6th house). For example, those who delivered St Paul’s letters to their destination churches were messengers in this sense. ✷

### ✸此处所指的“信使”，是具有自主发言权的代表。如同大使，他可能携带书

信，但他已对信函内容及相关事宜获得全面授权。其职责并非沉默地递交信件， 而是需要阐释、说服甚至执行任务。而对其递送内容一无所知的邮差则不属于信 使范畴，应视为仆役（属 6 宫）。例如：将 St Paul（圣保罗）书信送往各地教 会的传递者，便是这种意义上的信使✷

6th house 6 宫

This is the house of the unpleasantness the world throws at us, the slings and arrows of outrageous fortune, chief among which is illness. It signifies hospitals – a hospital being literally the house of illness. They are not shown by the 12th: they are places to treat sickness, not places to incarcerate the wicked. 6 宫象征世间降临于我们的厄运——诸如疾病这类“厄运的明枪暗箭”。它代表 医院（医院本质上是疾病之家），但需注意：医院不属于 12 宫范畴，因其是治 疗疾病的场所，而非囚禁罪恶之地。

The 6th has nothing whatever to do with the querent’s job, no matter how menial or how uncongenial that job might be. It is the querent’s employees and servants, such as the tradesman who repairs his car. So ‘Should I hire this builder?’ would be judged from the 6th house. 6 宫与问卜者自身的工作毫无关联——无论这份工作多么卑微或不讨喜。它代表 的是问卜者的雇员与仆役，例如为其维修汽车的工匠。因此“我是否该雇用这名 建筑工？”这类问题，应通过 6 宫进行判断。

It is the querent’s subordinates at work. It is those who work for him; not work he does himself. When Lilly says that the querent’s tenants are shown by the 6th, he assumes a master/servant relationship between them. This is no longer current: if I let a flat to someone, that tenant is shown by my 7th house, not my 6th. 6 宫代表问卜者在工作中的下属，即为他服务的人员，而非其本人从事的工作。 当 Lilly 提及问卜者的租户由 6 宫表示时，其前提是双方存在主仆关系。这一概 念已不适用于当今时代：若我将公寓出租给他人，该租户应由我的 7 宫而非 6 宫表示。

It shows small animals, the traditional criterion for a small animal being that it is smaller than a goat, or too small to ride. So this is the house for the lost cat or dog. It

is our uncles and aunts (3rd house from the 4th: our parent’s siblings), unless we wish to specify our mother’s siblings, in which case the uncles and aunts would be 12th house. 6 宫代表小型动物，传统上界定小型动物的标准是体型小于山羊或无法骑乘。因 此寻回走失的猫狗需看此宫。它也象征我们的叔伯/舅父与姑姨（即 4 宫之 3 宫： 我们父母的兄弟姐妹），但若需特指母亲一系的兄弟姐妹，则叔伯/舅父与姑姨 应归 12 宫。

It shows the lower belly, bowels and intestines. 6 宫对应下腹、肠道与脏腑。

7th house 7 宫

The 7th shows the querent’s partners, whether in an emotional or a business sense. Spouses and sweethearts, no matter how brief the relationship might be or how many such the querent might have. Even if the relationship does not yet exist, but is only desired (‘Will Kylie go out with me?’) or the individual is as yet unknown (‘When will I meet the woman I will marry?’), the person is shown by the 7th. The ‘ex’ too is 7th-house. 7 宫代表问卜者的伴侣，包括情感关系与商业合作层面的伙伴。无论关系存续时 间长短或问卜者拥有多少此类关系，配偶与恋人均归此宫。即使关系尚未建立（例 如“凯莉会和我交往吗？”）或对象身份未明（例如“我何时会遇到结婚对象？”）， 此人仍由 7 宫表示。前任伴侣同样属于 7 宫范畴。

The idea of partnership extends to cover doctors, including alternative practitioners, and astrologers, but only if the doctor is treating the illness at issue in a medical question (so he is the patient’s partner in returning to health) or if the astrologer is the one judging this horary right now (the querent’s partner in arriving at the truth). Otherwise they both belong to the 9th house, as learned people. 伙伴关系的概念可延伸至医生（包括非传统疗法医师）与占星师，但仅当医生正 在处理医疗问题中所涉疾病时（此时医患是共同恢复健康的伙伴），或占星师正 在解读当前这张卜卦盘时（问卜者是探寻真相的合作方）。其他情况下二者均属 9 宫范畴，因其属于学者阶层。

Important: if you are judging your own question, you do not aslo get the 7th house! Yours is the 1st, as querent. You cannot be your own partner. 重要提示：若您正在解读自己的问题，则 7 宫并不代表您本人！您作为问卜者由 1 宫象征。你无法同时担任自己的伙伴。

Even more important: although the 7th does in theory show the astrologer who is judging a question, I cannot recall it ever having been necessary to introduce myself into a client’s chart. While there are modern theoreticians of horary who encourage

such involvement, I cannot see this as anything other than invasive egotism. The chart belongs to the querent: keep yourself and your muddy boots out of it! 更为关键的是：尽管 7 宫在理论上确实代表解读问题的占星师，但我从未见过有 必要在客户的星盘中引入自身角色。尽管当代有些卜卦占星理论家鼓励这种介入， 但我认为这无非是自我膨胀的越界行为。星盘永远属于问卜者——请让你自己和 那双沾满泥泞的双脚远离它！

Also partners, albeit briefly, are those with whom we do deals, those from whom we buy or to whom we sell. In ‘Will I sell my house?’ the central issue is not the house, but the prospective buyer, the person with whom I will do the deal: 7th house. 7 宫同样涵盖那些与我们进行交易的对象（即使关系短暂），包括我们向其购买 商品或服务的卖方，以及我们向其销售商品或服务的买方。在“我能卖掉我的房 子吗？”这一问题中，核心并非房子本身，而是潜在的买家——那个我将与之达 成交易的人：7 宫。

The other class of people with whom we are intimately engaged is our open enemies: 7th house. My opponent in the chess match; the other party in a court case; anyone applying for the same job as me; the team that the team I support is playing: all 7th house. Thieves are regarded as open enemies. 7 宫还涵盖另一类与我们密切关联的对象：公开的敌人。象棋对弈中的对手、诉 讼案件中的对方当事人、与我竞争同一职位的申请人、我支持球队的对阵队伍— —皆属 7 宫范畴。小偷亦被视为公开的敌人。

The 7th shows those of greatest significance to us; it also shows those of least. It is the house of ‘any old person’: anyone who does not belong to one of the other houses. So ‘Will that big movie-star get convicted?’ or ‘Will that guy who’s gone missing come home?’ are 7th house. Combine this with the idea of doing deals, and the 7th shows Joe Public, the customer, the client. If you are a practicing astrologer, your clients are 7th house. 7 宫既代表对我们至为重要之人，也涵盖那些与我们毫不相关的个体。它是“任 何普通人”的宫位：即不属于其他任何宫位管辖的泛泛之辈。因此“那位大影星 会被定罪吗？”或“那个失踪的人会回家吗？”这类问题中的对象都属 7 宫。结 合交易关系的概念，7 宫也象征普罗大众、顾客、客户。若您是执业占星师，您 的客户即由 7 宫表示。

In the body, it is the reproductive system and the pelvis. 在身体层面，7 宫对应生殖系统与骨盆。

8th house 8 宫

This is the house of death, which in horary means exactly that: death. There is nothing

metaphorical here. Its usual role, however, is , because it is the 2nd house from the 7th, the other person’s money. Either the person with whom the querent is doing a deal (‘Will he ever pay me?’), the spouse (‘Has he really got as much money as he tells me ?’) or the enemy (‘Will I win the bookie’s money with this bet?’). 8 宫是象征死亡的宫位，在卜卦占星中特指实际意义上的死亡，并无隐喻含义。 但其更常见的功能是作为 7 宫之 2 宫，代表他人的钱财：既可指问卜者的交易对 象（“他到底会不会付钱给我？”），也可指配偶（“他是否真如所言那般富有？”） 或敌人（“我能否通过这次赌注赢得庄家的钱？”）。

As the 2nd shows the querent’s self-esteem, the 8th shows the partner’s esteem, seen here almost as a separate entity.
