If the querent in a relationship question is clearly interested in Lord 8 (the planet ruling the 8th house), this often shows a craving for the other person’s esteem rather than a craving for the other person’s money. 正如 2 宫象征问卜者的自我价值感，8 宫则代表伴侣的价值评判——在此几乎被 视作独立存在的实体。若在关系类问题中，问卜者明显对 8 宫主星（即 8 宫的守 护星）表现出关注，这往往意味着他/她渴求的是对方的价值认可，而非对方的 物质财富。

It is the house of wills and legacies, but only in the most general way (‘Will I ever be left a fortune?’). In any specific question on inheritance (‘Will I get so-and-so’s money?’), look to the dead person’s 2nd house. 8 宫确实代表遗嘱与遗产，但仅适用于最广义的提问（例如“我将来会获得遗产 吗？”）。若涉及具体继承事项（如“我能获得某某的遗产吗？”），则需查看 逝者的 2 宫。

Lilly says the 8th ‘signifies fear and anguish of mind’.By this he means that if the querent’s planet is found in the 8th, without any reason for being there (such as the question being about death or the spouse’s money), this shows that the querent is anguished over the issue. Fear as a thing in itself (‘Can I get over my claustrophobia?’) is a 12th-house matter. Lilly 指出 8 宫“象征恐惧与心灵煎熬”。此意涵指：若问卜者的行星出现在 8 宫，且无合理缘由（例如问题本身涉及死亡或配偶钱财），则表明问卜者正为此 事感到痛苦。而恐惧本身作为独立问题（如“我能克服幽闭恐惧症吗？”）则属 于 12 宫范畴。

9. Lilly,p.54.

In the body, it is the organs of excretion. 在身体层面，8 宫对应排泄器官。

The 8th has nothing to do with sex. Nothing. That is a 5th-house matter. 8 宫与性行为毫无关联。绝无关联。性行为属于 5 宫范畴。

### ✸Lilly says that wills and legacies belong to the 8th, but this is misleading. His

starting-point is that in a general question such as ‘Will I ever get rich, and how?’ a benefic in the 8th house could show benefit through death, which, of course, is most likely to be in the form of a legacy. Strictly, though, legacies are dead people’s money: 2nd from the 8th, not the 8th itself. In practice, a legacy always relates to someone specific, and so is that person’s 2nd house, whether that person is alive or dead. So the money I might inherit from my father would be 2nd from the 4th. Seen simply as a document ✷‘Where is the will?’) a will is a possession: 2nd house.✷

### ✸Lilly 虽将遗嘱与遗产归入 8 宫范畴，但这种归类具有误导性。他的出发点在

于：当遇到“我是否会致富，通过何种方式？”这类泛泛问题时，8 宫内的吉星 可能暗示通过死亡获益——这自然最可能以遗产形式呈现。然而严格来说，遗产 属于逝者的钱财：应属 8 宫之 2 宫，而非 8 宫本身。实践中，遗产总与特定对象 相关联，因此始终属于该对象的 2 宫（无论其生死）。例如我可能从父亲处继承 的财产，应查看 4 宫之 2 宫。若单纯将遗嘱视为文件（如“遗嘱在何处？”）， 则属于动产范畴：归 2 宫管辖。✷

9th house 9 宫

The 9th shows our special journeys. It is the house of God, religion and all things spiritual, including our pilgrimage, our journey to the Diving. As our special journeys tend to be longer than our routine journeys (3rd house) this aslo covers most long journeys. But it is the specialness, not the length, of the journey that is the distinguishing feature. If I commute from London to New York twice a week, this is a routine journey (3rd house). If I then take a weekend off in a spa 20 miles from my home, this is a special journey (9th house). All holidays (holydays) are 9th, as are foreign countries. 9 宫象征我们的特殊旅程。它是神性、宗教及一切精神事物的宫位，包括我们的 朝圣之旅——我们通往神性的旅程。由于特殊旅程通常比日常行程（3 宫）更长， 故此宫也涵盖大多数长途出行。但区分的关键在于旅程的特殊性而非距离长短。 若我每周两次从伦敦通勤至纽约，这属于日常行程（3 宫）；但若我在离家 20 英里的水疗中心度周末，这便属于特殊旅程（9 宫）。所有假期（及神圣节日） 均属 9 宫，外国亦归此宫管辖。

It is our higher knowledge: in essence, the knowledge that is beyond what we need for our daily routine and is taking us to God. It is the schools and universities where we gain such knowledge. It is our teacher, our priest. That monasteries belong in the 12th is a common error: they are not prisons, but houses of prayer – 9th.All learned people are here, as well as their learing. This includes astrologers. 9 宫代表我们的高等知识：本质上是超越日常所需、引领我们趋近神性的智慧。 我们获取此类知识的学府与大学归此宫管辖。它象征我们的导师与祭司。将修道

院归入 12 宫是常见谬误：它们并非监狱，而是祈祷之所——应属 9 宫。所有 学者及其学识皆归此宫，其中也包括占星师。

10. When Lilly speaks of ‘monkery’, by the way, he usually means celibacy, not the act of being a monk.
10. 需注意的是：当 Lilly 提及“修道戒律”时，通常特指独身主义，而非指修道 者本身的身份。

It is the house of dreams, predictions and prophecies, as well as those who predict and prophesy. Being the house of the wise man, it has an important role in marriage questions from certain cultures: it shows the marriage bureau, which fills the role of the local wise man who would once have arranged the match. 9 宫是梦境、预言与预兆的宫位，也代表那些进行预言与预兆的人。作为智者的 宫位，它在某些文化的婚姻问题中扮演重要角色：代表婚姻介绍所——其充当着 传统中安排匹配的当地智者的角色。

In the body, it is the hips and buttocks. 在身体层面，9 宫对应臀部与髋部。

10th house 10 宫

The 10th shows the king, the boss in any situation, the government, the prime minister or president, the judge in a court case (judge, jury and the whole court system can be taken as ‘the judge’). It is honour, success, glory (‘Will I win the Olympic gold?’). It shows the querent’s mother. 10 宫代表君主、任何情境中的上司、政府、首相或总统、诉讼案件中的法官（法 官、陪审团及整个司法体系均可视为“法官”范畴）。它象征荣誉、成功、声望 （“我能赢得奥运金牌吗？”）。此宫也显示问卜者的母亲。

It is the querent’s job or career, whatever that career might be – no matter how menial. 10 宫代表问卜者的工作或职业，无论其职业为何——无论多么卑微。

There is a connection between the 10th house and marriage. In the modern world this is relevant only to arranged or dynastic marriages, and then only to the marriage in its formal nature; the actual relationship between the two people is a 7th-house matter. 10 宫与婚姻存在关联。在现代社会中，这仅适用于包办婚姻或家族联姻，且仅 针对婚姻的形式层面；两人之间的实际关系则属 7 宫范畴。

It shows the thighs and knee. As with all house, the chunk of body extends through the sign, moving downwards from the cusp. The top of the thigh is shown by the cusp of the house, the knee by the end of the house, just before the 11th cusp. So with the 1st house, for example, the cusp shows the top of the head; the end of house, just

before the 2nd cusp, shows the chin. Suppose, then, we need a significator for the querent’s knees. We would look to the 10th house (thighs and knee). But if there is a sign boundary in that house, meaning that the end of the house, towards the 11th cusp, is under a different sign from the 10th cusp, it is the ruler of this second sign (the one ruling the end of the house) that we would take as significator of the knees. Example: 10th cusp is at 8 Aries; 11th cusp at 15 Taurus. Taurus therefore begins in the middle of the 10th house and covers the end of that house. We would take Venus, ruler of Taurus, to signify the knees, not Mars. 10 宫对应大腿与膝盖。与所有宫位相同，身体部位的覆盖范围贯穿整个星座， 从宫头开始向下延伸。大腿顶部由宫头表示，膝盖则由该宫位末端（紧邻 11 宫 头之前）表示。以 1 宫为例：宫头对应头顶，宫位末端（紧邻 2 宫头之前）则对 应下巴。假设我们需要确定问卜者膝盖的征象星：应查看 10 宫（大腿与膝盖）。 但若该宫位内存在星座边界，即宫位末端（靠近 11 宫头的部分）与 10 宫头处于 不同星座，则需取第二个星座（管辖宫位末端的星座）的守护星作为膝盖的征象 星。因此金牛座从 10 宫中部开始并覆盖其末端。此时应取金牛座的守护星金星 （而非火星）作为膝盖的征象星。

### ✸I now see that my mention of the chin is a bad example: see 2nd hous, above. The

point made should remain clear enough, though.✷

### ✸我现在意识到，先前以下巴为例并不恰当（参见前文 2 宫说明），但所述核

心观点应仍足够清晰。✷

11th house 11 宫

As the 8th takes key meanings from being the 2nd house from the 7th, so the 11th takes many of its most important roles from being 2nd from the 10th. As such it shows the boss’s money, or my job’s money: very important, as this is my wages. It shows the advisors or aides of the 10th house. If the 10th shows the king, the 11th might show the prime minister or the grand vizier; if the 10th shows the prime minister, the 11th would show his cabinet. It shows the king’s money, hence ‘the gift of the king’, and so is the relevant house when the querent wants favours from above (‘Will I get the government grant?’). As the king’s money, it is crucial in questions such as ‘How big is my tax bill going to be?’ 正如 8 宫的核心意义源自其作为 7 宫之 2 宫，11 宫许多最重要的职能也源于其 作为 10 宫之 2 宫的地位。因此它象征老板的钱财，或我工作带来的收入：这至 关重要，因为这就是我的工资。它代表 10 宫的顾问或助手。若 10 宫代表国王， 11 宫可能象征首相或宰相；若 10 宫代表首相，11 宫则指其内阁。它显示君主的 财富，故有“君王赏赐”之意，当问卜者想获得上位者的恩惠时（“我能获得政 府拨款吗？”）此宫便至关重要。作为君主财富的象征，它在“我的税单金额会 有多大？”这类问题中起决定性作用。

It shows ‘pennies from Heaven’: the bounty that drops into our lap without our struggle or desert – so the win on the lottery or the football pools. 11 宫象征“天降之财”：即无需努力或不应得却落入怀中的馈赠——例如彩票 中奖或足球博彩赢利。

The 11th is the house of ‘hopes and wishes’. This is rarely relevant except in a negative sense: what is preventing ‘When will I marry?’ having the answer desired? Lord 11, your hopes and wishes, is getting in the way: whenever you meet someone at all eligible, the deafening sound of wedding bells scares him off. It is said to cover such abstractions as ‘trust’ and ‘praise’, although I have never found these relevant in practice. 11 宫是“希望与愿望”的宫位。除负面反例外，此含义鲜少适用：例如当“我 何时结婚？”的答案未能如愿时，阻碍何在？11 宫主星（即你的希望与愿望） 正在制造障碍：每当你遇到略具潜力的人选，内心震耳欲聋的婚礼钟声便会将对 方吓退。理论上该宫位也涵盖“信任”“赞誉”等抽象概念，不过我在实践中从 未发现这些概念具有实际意义。

It is our friends. Be careful here: the modern use of ‘friend’, at least in England, is much freer than what is meant. Someone with whom I get along well at work is my colleague (7th house), not my friend; the person with whom I exchange amiable banalities in the pub is my acquaintance (7th again). Nor does the 11th show ‘social institutions’ as the moderns claim. Trades unions, for instance, are (‘Should I join the union?’) groups of colleagues: 7th house. They are ‘us’ (‘Can we get a pay-rise out of the boss?’): 1st house. They are groups of servants (‘Will the union in the factory I own elect a new leader?’): 6th. They are open enemies (‘Can I defeat the union that has closed down my factory?’): 7th. They are not groups of friends. 11 宫代表我们的朋友。此处需注意：现代意义上的“朋友”（至少在英格兰） 其含义远比占星学中的概念宽泛。工作中相处融洽的同事属 7 宫，而非朋友；酒 馆里互相寒暄的熟人亦归 7 宫。11 宫也不像现代占星宣称的那样代表“社会机 构”。例如工会（“我该加入工会吗？”）属于同事群体：7 宫；作为利益共同 体（“我们能争取到加薪吗？”）时属 1 宫；作为受管辖的群体（“我拥有的工 厂里工会会选出新领袖吗？”）时属 6 宫；作为公开敌对方（“我能击败让我工 厂停工的工会吗？”）时属 7 宫——但工会绝非朋友团体。

NB: consider this last paragraph carefully. Note how the same thing can be found in different houses depending on who is asking the question and what that question is. 注意：请仔细斟酌最后这段论述。需留意同一事物会根据提问者身份及具体问题 内容归属于不同宫位。

In the body, the 11th is the calves and ankles. 在身体层面，11 宫对应小腿与脚踝。

### ✸As with the 4th as ‘the end of matter’, so with the 11th as ‘hopes and wishes’: the

idea exists primarily to give the astrologer a Plan B. Rather than judge the chart properly and disappoint the client, we can have a happy client by sagely rubbing the chin and pronouncing, ‘Ah, but if we look at your hopes and wishes – wow!’ I would suggest that we stick to judging the chart properly.✷

### ✸正如将 4 宫视为“事情终局”的牵强解读，把 11 宫当作“希望与愿望”的做

法：这种概念的存在主要是为占星师提供备用方案。与其通过严谨判断星盘让客 户失望，我们只需故作高深地摩挲下巴宣称：“啊，但若观察您的希望与愿望— —哇！”便能换取客户的欢心。我的建议是：我们应当坚持对星盘进行准确研判。 ✷

12th house 12 宫

This is the house of secret enemies, in contrast to our open enemies in the 7th. Note that it is the nature of the way they harm us that makes our enemies 12th house, not whether we know who they are. Witchcraft, spreading malicious rumours, informing on people: these are 12th-house offences, even if the perpetrator is well known. It is the house of secret things, things hidden from the querent. 12 宫象征秘密敌人，与 7 宫的公开敌人形成对比。需注意：判定敌人属于 12 宫 的关键在于其伤害我们的方式性质，而非我们是否知晓对方身份。巫术、散布恶 意谣言、告密等行为均属 12 宫范畴的侵害——即使施害者身份众所周知。此宫 代表隐秘之事，即问卜者不为其所知的事物。

We do an effective job of being enemies to ourselves, so the 12th is ‘self-undoing’: the daft things we do to make our lives more difficult than need be. Our vices; sin. Our fears too undermine us, so our phobias are located here. 我们总是擅长与自己为敌，因此 12 宫代表“自毁行为”：即我们所做的那些让 生活变得不必要艰难的蠢事。我们的恶习与罪孽归于此宫；恐惧同样会侵蚀我们， 故恐惧症也归属此宫。

As an extension of the idea of the 12th as the house of our self-undoing, that in which we imprison ourselves, it aslo governs prisons. 作为 12 宫象征“自毁行为”及我们自我禁锢之概念的延伸，此宫同样管辖监狱。

The 12th shows animals larger than goats. In the body, it governs the feet. 12 宫代表体型大于山羊的动物。在身体层面，此宫对应双脚。

As we saw with the example of trades unions in the section on the 11th house, the house we look to for any person or thing will vary depending on the question. It is the

question that determines the reality of the chart. If the Prime Minister asks, ‘Will I be re-elected?’ he is 1st house, like any other querent. If I ask, ‘Will the Prime Minister be re-elected?’ he is my king, and so is 10th house. If an Amercian ask, ‘Will the Prime Minister be re-elected?’ the Prime Minister is the king of a foreign country: 10th from the 9th, which is the 6th house. If the Prime Minister’s wife asks, ‘Will my darling like the socks I bought him for Christmas?’ his role is as her husband:7th house. 正如我们在 11 宫章节中关于工会的示例所示，对任何人物或事物应取用的宫位 会随问题不同而变化。是问题本身决定了星盘的现实维度。若首相询问“我会连 任吗？”，他如同任何问卜者般属于 1 宫；若我询问“首相连任吗？”，他作为 我的君主归属 10 宫；若美国人询问“英国首相连任吗？”，首相作为外国君主 则对应 9 宫之 10 宫（即 6 宫）；若首相夫人询问“亲爱的会喜欢我买的圣诞袜 吗？”，他作为丈夫的角色应取 7 宫。

### ✸This last point is very important. People often play various roles in our lives, and

so can be shown by various houses in the chart. Which is the relevant role within the context of the question? For instance, if I ask ‘Will I beat my friend at chess?’ the 11th house has nothing to do within it. Within the context of the chess game he is my enemy: 7th house. That he is my friend is, for the purpose of the question, irrelevant. ✷

### ✸最后这一点至关重要。人们常在我们生命中扮演多重角色，因此在星盘中可

由不同宫位表征。关键在于：在问题所涉情境下，哪一角色具有相关性？例如， 若我问“我能战胜我的朋友吗？”，11 宫与此毫无关联。在棋局情境中，他是 我的对手：归 7 宫管辖。至于他是我的朋友这一事实——就当前问题而言，与此 毫不相干。✷

TURNING THE CHART 转宫

In this review of house meanings I have given several examples of houses that are derived from other houses, such as ‘the king of a foreign country (10th from the 9th)’ in the last paragraph. Deriving one house from another is called ‘turning the chart’. 在此番宫位含义综述中，我已列举了多个“由其他宫位推导得出”的案例，例如 前文提到的“外国君主（9 宫之 10 宫）”。从某一宫位推导另一宫位的技法， 即称为“转宫”。

Example: if I ask the question, ‘How is my daughter’s career shaping up?’ it is no good my looking at the 10th house of the chart, because that is my career, not hers. I need to look at her 10th house. First I must locate my daughter (5th house) and then take the 10th house from that. The 10th from the 5th is the 2nd house of the chart.

例如：若我提问“我女儿的事业发展如何？”，直接查看星盘的 10 宫是无效的， 因为那代表我的事业而非她的。我需要定位她的事业宫：首先确定代表女儿的宫 位（5 宫），再由此推导其 10 宫——即 5 宫之 10 宫，也就是基准盘的 2 宫。

What we are doing here is to treat the 5th as if it were the Ascendant and count 10 houses from there – hence the term ‘turning the chart’. 我们在此处的操作，是将 5 宫视作上升点，并由此顺数十个宫位——这正是“转 宫”一词的由来。

When turning, always count the house you start with as ‘I’. So the 5th house is my daughter’s 1st; the 6th is her 2nd house; the 7th is her 3rd house. Until you get used to this, you may find it helpful to put your finger on the house you are starting from, counting ‘I’, and then count round from there. The chart as we usually approach it, with the 1st house showing the querent, is called the radical chart. This is ‘radical’ in its literal sense of ‘root’. If I am the querent, I am shown by the radical 1st house and my daughter by the radical 5th. 进行转宫时，请始终将起始宫位视为“1 宫”。因此，5 宫是我女儿的 1 宫；6 宫是她的 2 宫；7 宫是她的 3 宫。在熟悉此方法前，您可将手指放在起始宫位， 默念“1 宫”，然后依次点数。我们通常使用的以 1 宫代表问卜者的星盘称为基 准盘——“基准”二字取其字面“根源”之意。若我是问卜者，基准盘的 1 宫代 表我，5 宫则代表我的女儿。

Follow these meanings round the chart, counting from the radical 5th house. Don’t just read this: look at the chart and let your fingers do the walking! 请循此脉络在星盘中推演：从基准盘 5 宫开始计数。切勿仅止于阅读——务必对 照星盘，用手指实际点数！

My daughter’s bracelet is her 2nd house. 2nd from the 5th is the radical 6th. 我女儿的镯子属于她的 2 宫，即基准盘 5 宫之 2 宫——6 宫。

My daughter’s neighbour is her 3rd. 3rd from the 5th is the radical 7th. 我女儿的邻居是她的 3 宫，即基准盘 5 宫之 3 宫——7 宫。

My daughter’s orchard is her 4th. 4th from the 5th is the radical 8th. 我女儿的果园是她的 4 宫，即基准盘 5 宫之 4 宫——8 宫。

My daughter’s son （hence my grandson) is her 5th. 5th from the 5th is the radical 9th. 我女儿的儿子（即我的外孙）是她的 5 宫，即基准盘 5 宫之 5 宫——9 宫。

My daughter’s dog is her 6th. 6th from the 5th is the radical 10th. 我女儿的狗是她的 6 宫，即基准盘 5 宫之 6 宫——10 宫。

My daughter’s husband is her 7th. 7th from the 5th is the radical 11th. 我女儿的丈夫是她的 7 宫，即基准盘 5 宫之 7 宫——11 宫。

My daughter’s husband’s money is the 2nd from her 7th. This is the 2nd from the 11th, which is the radical 12th. Here we have turned the chart twice. 我女儿丈夫的钱财是她 7 宫之 2 宫，即 11 宫之 2 宫——12 宫。此处我们进行了 两次转宫。

My daughter’s piano teacher is her 9th, which is the radical 1st. Her husband’s brother is aslo the radical 1st, because it is the 3rd house from her 7th. 我女儿的钢琴老师是她的 9 宫，即基准盘 1 宫。她丈夫的兄弟同样对应基准盘 1 宫，因为这是她 7 宫之 3 宫。

My daughter’s career is her 10th, which is the radical 2nd. So is her father-in-law: her husband’s father, which is the 4th from her 7th. 我女儿的事业是她的 10 宫，即基准盘 2 宫。她的公公（丈夫的父亲）同样归于 此宫，这是她 7 宫之 4 宫。

My daughter’s friend is her 11th, which is the radical 3rd. So is the money she might hope to inherit from her father-in-law: it is the 2nd from the 4th from her 7th. (Her 7th is husband; the 4th from there is her father-in-law; the 2nd from there is his money.) 我女儿的朋友是她的 11 宫，即基准盘 3 宫。她可能从公公处继承的财富也归于 此宫：这是她 7 宫之 4 宫之 2 宫（她的 7 宫代表丈夫；7 宫之 4 宫代表公公；7 宫之 4 宫之 2 宫则代表公公的钱财）。

My daughter’s horse is her 12th, which is the radical 4th. So is her husband’s manservant, which is the 6th from her 7th. 我女儿的马是她的 12 宫，即基准盘 4 宫。她丈夫的仆役（7 宫之 6 宫）同样归 属此宫。

You have seen examples here of turning the chart more than once. You can turn it as often as is necessary, but the more you do the more it loses focus: if there is a short-cut, take it. For instance, my daughter’s mother is never the 10th from the 5th; she is my wife, which is the radical 7th. This would be so even if I were now married to somebody else, or if we had never married. My daughter’s father is not the radical 8th (4th from the 5th); her father is me, and I am the querent: 1st house. 以上示例展示了多次转宫的情况。转宫操作可重复进行，但次数越多焦点越易模 糊：若有捷径可循，务必采用。例如：我女儿的母亲绝不可能是 5 宫之 10 宫； 她是我的妻子，应取基准盘 7 宫——即使我如今已另娶他人，或我们从未结婚， 此规则依然适用。我女儿的父亲也非基准盘 8 宫（5 宫之 4 宫）；她的父亲就是 我本人，作为问卜者应取 1 宫。

Do not read significance into other meanings of the house you reach when turning. The 8th house (death) from the 4th (my father) is the 11th (my friend). This does not

mean that my friend will kill my father; it means only that my father’s death is signified by the 11th house. 进行转宫时，切勿对推导出的宫位附加其他含义。从 4 宫（我的父亲）推导出的 8 宫（死亡）对应 11 宫（我的朋友）。这并非意味着我的朋友将杀害我的父亲， 仅表明我父亲的死亡由 11 宫作为征象。

Turning implies some kind of ‘belonging to’. If the object does not, in a real sense, belong to the person, avoid turning the chart. The bigger the thing, the more likely we are to look to the radical, not the turned, chart. If the question is ‘How will my brother get on in his new job?’ look at the 10th from the 3rd. But if it were ‘Will my brother win Olympic gold?’ look at the radical – not the turned – 10th. It is still a 10th house matter, but the victory does not belong to the brother in the same way that his job does. Or if it were ‘Is my brother’s teacher helping him?’ the teacher would be 9th from the 3rd; if it were ‘Will my brother do well at university?’ it would be the radical 9th. In some way, the teacher ‘belongs’ to the brother in a way that the university does not – even though we might talk about ‘my brother’s university’. 转宫法的运用需以“所属关系”为前提。若事物在现实层面不属于该人物，则应 避免转宫。事物越宏大，我们越应参考基准盘而非转宫盘。例如：“我哥哥的新 工作发展如何？”需查看 3 宫之 10 宫；但若问“我哥哥能赢得奥运金牌吗？” 则需考察基准盘 10 宫（非转宫盘）——虽同属 10 宫事务，但这份荣誉并不像他 的工作那样专属于他本人。同理，“哥哥的老师是否在帮助他？”老师对应 3 宫之 9 宫；而“哥哥在大学表现会好吗？”则取基准盘 9 宫。从某种意义而言， 老师“属于”哥哥的个人关联程度，远高于大学机构——即便我们常说“我哥哥 的大学”。

If, however, the question were ‘Will my grandson get into university?’ we would have to turn the chart. The grandson is himself 9th house (child’s child: 5th from 5th), so we cannot aslo use that for the university. We would have to take the 9th from the 9th. 但若问题是“我的孙子能考上大学吗？”，则必须使用转宫法。孙子本身已对应 9 宫（子女的子女：5 宫之 5 宫），故不能再以同一宫位代表大学。此时需取 9 宫之 9 宫（即基准盘 5 宫）作为大学的征象。

For death and imprisonment, look at both the turned and the radical 8th or 12th house. Usually one or other is clearly in play; sometimes both. 涉及死亡与监禁事项时，需同时观察转宫盘与基准盘中的 8 宫或 12 宫。通常其 中一方会明确发挥作用，有时则两者皆现。

Occasionally there is not a cut and dried answer to which house we should look at: in practice, I find that if there is a genuine ambivalence, the chart reflects this and gives the same answer from both possible houses. 偶尔我们会遇到难以明确判定应取何宫的情况：实践中我发现，若存在真正的模 棱两可，星盘会反映出这种不确定性，并从两个可能的宫位给出相同的答案。

### ✸It is sometimes necessary to turn the chart in order to distinguish different things

of the same kind. My brother’s university is radical 9th, because it doesn’t belong to him. So if my question is ‘Will my brother get into university?’ I am concerned only with the 3rd house (him) and the 9th (the university). But if my question were, ‘Is my brother’s university better than mine?’ I would have to use the 9th from the 3rd to locate his university, because the radical 9th is already in use showing my university.

### ✸有时需要通过转宫来区分同类事物。我哥哥的大学对应基准盘 9 宫，因为该

大学并非他的所属物。因此，若问题是“我哥哥能考上大学吗？”，我只需关注 3 宫（代表他）和 9 宫（代表大学）。但若问题是“我哥哥的大学比我的更好吗？”， 则需使用 3 宫之 9 宫来定位他的大学，因为基准盘 9 宫已被用于代表我的大学。

Similarly with children from a spouse’s previous relationship. These would usually be seen as radical 5th house, the querent’s children, whether querent is the biological parent or not. But if we need to distinguish (‘Who are all the cakes?’) we can take the radical 5th to show the querent’s own children and the 5th from the 7th to show the spouse’s. On occasion, the spouse’s child could be given the 5th from 7th even without the need to distinguish. This would be only if the relationship between querent and children were very tenuous – if, perhaps, the child had grown and left home long before querent met spouse, and contact between them is minimal.✷ 同理，对于配偶在前段关系中的子女：通常仍视作基准盘 5 宫（即问卜者的子女）， 无论问卜者是否为生物学父母。但若需明确区分（例如“蛋糕都归谁？”这类情 境），可取基准盘 5 宫代表问卜者亲生子女，7 宫之 5 宫代表配偶的子女。在某 些特殊情况下，即使无需区分，配偶的子女也可直接由 7 宫之 5 宫表示——这仅 适用于问卜者与子女关系极其疏远的情形，例如该子女在问卜者与配偶相识前早 已成年离家，且双方几乎毫无往来。✷

### ✸I have been asked why I didn’t turn the chart in the lost cat question at the start of

this book, using the 6th from the 3rd to signify Puss, as the neighbors’ cat. This is because I didn’t regard him as the neighbours’ cat. He was in the process of transferring his allegiance and had for the most part moved in with us. My question was definitely ‘Where is our cat?’✷

### ✸曾有读者问及：为何本书开篇“寻猫案例”未使用转宫法，通过 3 宫之 6 宫

来象征那只作为邻居家猫的猫咪？这是因为当时我并未将其视作邻居家的猫。它 正处于转移其忠诚度的过程中，且已基本上与我们同住。我的问题明确是“我们 的猫在哪儿？”✷

We’ve worked all the way round the chart, turning from the 5th house. Now look at some other examples, taken at random. Work through this list, writing down your answers. Don’t just think them: write them down. Then turn to Appendix 2 for the answers. Some of these require you to turn the chart, some don’t. Assume that you are

the querent, so e.g. your father will be 4th house, your cat 6th. You will never be asked questions about many of these, but every example in creases your facility in turning the chart, increasing your fluency in the language of astrology. 我们已围绕星盘完成了一轮从 5 宫出发的转宫练习。现在随机考察其他示例，请 逐一写下答案而非仅作思考，随后查阅附录 2 核对。部分案例需运用转宫法，部 分则无需。默认您作为问卜者（例如您的父亲对应 4 宫，您的猫对应 6 宫）。尽 管许多情境可能永远不会成为您的占卜问题，但每个示例都能提升您运用转宫法 的熟练度，增强您驾驭占星学语言的流畅性。

Even if you are a hardened horary astrologer, do this exercise and read the answers: there is a lot of important information there. 即使您是经验丰富的卜卦占星师，也请务必完成此练习并阅读解析部分：其中蕴 含大量关键信息。

Your son’s pet rabbit 您儿子的宠物兔

Your father’s house 您父亲的住宅

Your pregnant sister 您怀孕的姐妹

Your new car 您的新车

Your journey to work 您的通勤行程

Your boss 您的上司

The guy who shares your office 与您共用办公室的同事

The dream your friend is telling you about 朋友向您描述的梦境

Your brothers 您的兄弟们

Your younger brother, in contrast to your elder brother 您的弟弟（与哥哥区分）

Your ex-spouse 您的前配偶

The local priest 本地神父

The priest’s brother 神父的兄弟

The priest’s sister-in-law 神父的嫂嫂/弟媳

The priest’s sister-in-law’s neighbor 神父嫂嫂/弟媳的邻居

The king of Spain 西班牙国王

Your father’s liver 您父亲的肝脏

That packet of rice you bought this morning 今早购买的那包米

That wrap of cocaine you bought this morning 今早购买的那包可卡因

The book you borrowed from the library 从图书馆借的书

The book you have written 您撰写的书籍

The person who told the cops about your secret life as a criminal mastermind 告发您秘密犯罪生涯的举报人

Your butler 您的男管家

Your job as a butler 您担任男管家的工作

Mines 矿场

The man who’s come to repair your plumbing 前来修理水管的工人

The man who’s just whispered a hot tip for the next race into your ear 在您耳边透露赛马内幕消息者

Your university 您就读的大学

Your daughter’s university 您女儿就读的大学

Your teacher’s university 您老师所在的大学

Astrology 占星学

Particle physics 粒子物理学

Your mistress’s brother’s Great Dane 您情妇的兄弟的大丹犬

The cruise you’re thinking of taking 您计划乘坐的游轮

The ship on which you’ll be taking ti 您将搭乘的船只

Your dog’s ball 您爱犬的玩具球

Your mother’s friend’s child 您母亲朋友的子女

# The Planets

# 行星

Planets acquire meaning in two ways. One is by the houses that they rule; the other is through their natural associations. The first of these is by far the more important in horary. 行星通过两种方式获得意义：一是通过它们所守护的宫位；二是通过其先天属性。 在卜卦占星中，前者远比后者重要得多。

The planet that rules the sign in which a house cusp falls rules that house, or is Lord of that house. So if the cusp of the second house were at 15 Cancer, the Moon, ruler of Cancer, would be Lord of the second, or Lord 2. If the cusp of the fourth house were at 29 Virgo, Mercury, ruler of Virgo, would be Lord 4. This planet is the significator of that house. Hence it represents the things of that house in the chart – whichever things are relevant to the question asked. The Moon as Lord 2 might be significator of the querent’s money or his lawyer; Mercury as Lord 4 might significator of the querent’s father or his home. Which meaning it takes will be determined by the question. 当一个宫头所在的星座由某颗行星守护时，该行星即为此宫位的守护星，或称该 宫的宫主星。例如，若 2 宫头位于 15 度巨蟹座，则巨蟹座的守护星月亮即为 2 宫主。若 4 宫头位于 29 度处女座，则处女座的守护星水星即为 4 宫主。此行星 即为该宫的征象星。因此，它代表盘中与该宫位相关的事物——亦即与所问问题 相关的内容。月亮作为 2 宫主，可能是问卜者钱财或其律师的征象星；水星作为 4 宫主，可能是问卜者父亲或其家庭的征象星。具体代表何种含义，将由问题本 身决定。

It doesn’t matter which planet it is: if it rules the house it is significator of the things of that house. This is so even if the planet does not appear to describe that thing. Example: if a boy asks, ‘Dose my girlfriend really love me?’ his girlfriend is signified by the ruler of the 7th house, even if that planet is Mars; the boy himself will be signified by the ruler of the 1st, even if that is Venus. Nor would this tell us that he is effeminate and she wears the trousers. The planets are the actors in the drama that is the chart; when the casting-director is handing out parts he evidently doesn’t take much time choosing who gets which. 不论该行星是何种性质：只要它守护某个宫位，便是该宫所代表事物的征象星。 即使该行星本身的特质看似与所象征的事物不符，此规则依然成立。例如：若一 位男孩问道：“我的女朋友真的爱我吗？”他的女朋友由 7 宫主象征，哪怕那颗

行星是火星；男孩自己则由 1 宫主象征，哪怕那是金星。这并不代表他女性化或 她强势。行星是星盘这场戏剧中的演员；当“选角导演”分配角色时，显然并不 会花太多时间去斟酌谁该扮演哪个。

### ✸The Planet is the actor. What interests us in the role. We become concerned with

the actor only when it is necessary to describe something. If the querent asks, ‘When will I meet my husband and what will he look like?’ we need a description, and we can take this from the planet concerned. If she asks, ‘Will my boyfriend marry me?’ she knows what he looks like, so it would be daft describing him from the chart. If, for instance, his significator is Saturn, we do not try to persuade her that he is really twice her age but keeping this secret from her. As in the theatre, so in the chart: most of the time the choice of actor has no effect upon the role. Sarah Bernhardt played Hamlet: this said nothing about the nature of Hamlet’s feelings for Ophelia.✷

### ✸行星是演员。我们所关注的是其扮演的角色。只有在需要描述某些特征时，

我们才会去关心演员本身。如果问卜者问：“我何时会遇到我的丈夫？他长什么 样？”我们需要一个描述，这可以从相关的行星获取。如果她问：“我的男朋友 会娶我吗？”她已知道他的长相，因此试图从星盘去描述他就显得多余了。例如， 即使她的征象星是土星，我们也不会试图说服她：其实他年龄是她的两倍，只是 对她隐瞒了这一点。正如在戏剧中一样，在星盘中亦是如此：大多数时候，演员 的选择对角色的本质并无影响。Sarah Bernhardt（莎拉·伯恩哈特）曾扮演 Hamlet （哈姆雷特）：这并不能说明 Hamlet 对 Ophelia（奥菲莉亚）的感情本质有何不 同。✷

A house has one ruler and one ruler only. This is the planet that rules the sign on its cusp. This is so even if that cusp is at 29.59 degrees of its sign. There is no such thing as a co-ruler. this is a modern abomination. 一个宫位有且仅有一个守护星，即其宫头所在星座的守护行星。即使该宫头位于 其星座的 29.59 度，此规则依然成立。不存在所谓的“共同守护星”——这是现 代的糟粕。

The planet ruling another sign in that house may, however, be significant; but this will only be if the concept of next is relevant to the question. ‘Will my next job be any better than the one I’ve got now?’ The ruler of the sign on the 10th cusp will show the present job; the ruler of the next sign, in the usual order of the signs, will show the putative next job. (This next could equally well be shown by Lord 10 about to leave the sign it is in. The sign it is about to enter would then show the next job.) 然而，该宫位内另一个星座的守护星也可能具有重要性；但这仅当“下一个”的 概念与问题相关时才适用。例如：“我的下一份工作会比现在这份更好吗？”10 宫头所在星座的守护星代表当前的工作；按照星座通常的顺序，下一个星座的守 护星则代表可能的下一份工作。（这种“下一个”同样可以由 10 宫主即将离开 其当前所在星座来显示。那么，它即将进入的星座便会代表下一份工作。）

### ✸If the sign on the cusp is Capricorn, the ruler of the next sign will be Saturn, the

same planet that rules Capricorn. This is not a problem: ‘Will my next job be better than this one?’ ‘No, they will be much the same.’

### ✸如果宫头星座是摩羯座，那么下一个星座的守护星将是土星——这与摩羯座

的守护星是同一颗行星。这并不构成问题：“我的下一份工作会比这份更好吗？” “不会，它们大致相同。”

Do be strict in applying this idea of next, when looking for significators of two things falling under the same house. If my doctor has told me something and I am now going for a second opinion, the doctor who will give this is my next doctor. If I am being treated by two doctors, one of whom says one thing and the other something else, there is no basis for regarding one of them as the next. So don’t do it! There will be other ways to distinguish between them. See pages 198, 224 and 271. 在寻找同一宫位内两件事物的征象星时，务必严格应用“下一个”这一概念。如 果我的医生给出了诊断，而我现在正寻求第二诊疗意见，那么将提供此意见的医 生就是我的“下一位”医生。如果我正在接受两位医生的治疗，且他们各执一词， 那么就没有理由将其中任何一位视为“下一位”。所以不要这么做！会有其他方 法来区分他们。参见第 198、224 和 271 页。

There is never a significance in one planet ruling two houses that are relevant to the question. This does not mean those houses are connected.✷ 若有一颗行星同时守护两个与问题相关的宫位，这本身并无特殊意义。这并不意 味着那些宫位之间存在联系。✷

Sign-rulers 星座的守护星

The planets ruling each sign are these: 各星座的守护星如下：

You will notice that there is no place here for Uranus, Neptune or Pluto. If your previous astrological study has taught you that these planets ruler signs, put that idea aside while you are studying horary. You will soon find that using the traditional sign-rulers works. 你会注意到，这里没有天王星、海王星或冥王星的位置。如果你之前的占星学习 使你相信这些行星守护某些星座，那么在研习卜卦占星时，请先将这个观念搁置。 你将很快发现，使用传统的星座守护星体系确实有效。

11. For a full discussion of the recently discovered planets, see my The Real Astrology, Apprentice Books, London,2001,chapter 6. Hereafter referred to as Real Astrology.
11. 关于新近发现行星的完整讨论，请参阅我的《The Real Astrology》，（伦敦学徒出版社， 2001 年）第 6 章。下文中简称《Real Astrology》.

Alternatives to house rulers 替补宫主星

The ruler of the next sign round will never be co-ruler of that house; it can become sole ruler if the Lord of that house is already busy doing something else. Suppose I ask ‘Will I get this job?’ and find Virgo on the Ascendant and Gemini on the 10th cusp. Mercury, as ruler of both these signs, would signify me (the querent: Lord 1) and the job (Lord 10). We can take the ruler of the next sign to the sign on the 10th cusp to signify the job (following the usual order of the signs). This will usually be necessary only if we need to find an aspect between querent and quesited in order to answer the question, in which case we must, of course, have different significators for them. 沿着星座顺序的下一个星座的守护星，永远不会成为该宫的共同守护星；只有当 该宫主星已经忙于其他事务时，它才可能成为唯一的宫主星。假设我问“我能得 到这份工作吗？”，并发现上升点为处女座、10 宫头为双子座。水星作为这两 个星座的守护星，将同时象征我（问卜者：1 宫主）和工作（10 宫主）。此时，

我们可以取 10 宫头星座之后（按照星座通常的顺序）的下一个星座的守护星来 象征这份工作。这通常只在我们需要观察问卜者与所占之事之间的相位以回答问 题时才必要，因为在这种情况下，两者当然必须有不同的征象星。

Sometimes it is not necessary to distinguish between the querent and the thing asked about. It is common, for instance, when the self-employed ask about their jobs, to find Lords 1 and 10 the same. This makes sense: within the context of the question, person and job are effectively the same. But if the question is ‘Will I get the job?’ we must have different significators for person and job. 有时，并不需要区分问卜者与其所问之事。例如，当个体经营者询问其工作时， 常会出现 1 宫主与 10 宫主为同一颗行星的情况。这合乎情理：在该问题的语境 下，人与工作本质上是同一的。但如果问题是“我能得到这份工作吗？”，那么 我们必须为人和工作设定不同的征象星。

### ✸Note that this does not contradict my addition, above. We do not deduce that the

person is self-employed from the same planet ruling 1st and 10th houses. We know that anyway. Our querent would be just as self-employed if different planets ruled those houses.✷

### ✸请注意，这与我在上文中的补充说明并不矛盾。我们并不能从同一颗行星同

时守护 1 宫和 10 宫这一现象，推断出问卜者是个体经营者。我们本就知道这一 点。即便守护这些宫位的是不同的行星，我们的问卜者同样可能是个体经营者。 ✷

Sometimes the querent is of less importance to the issue than the quesited, so the quesited can be given the disputed planet. In many questions about third parties the querent has no part in the drama, so does not need to be assigned a significator. ‘My friend is ill; will she get better?’: we do not need to involve the querent in our judgement at all. ‘Where is the cat?’: the cat is where it is, regardless of the querent; so if Lords 1 and 6 (small animals: 6th house) were the same, we could use that planets as significator of the cat. Such a question usually has an implied ‘Will I see him again and when?’: we can still answer this by using the Moon to signify the querent. 有时，问卜者对于所问之事的重要性低于所占之事，因此可将有争议的行星赋予 所占之事。在许多涉及第三方的问题中，问卜者并未参与事件本身，因此无需为 其分配征象星。例如：“我的朋友病了；她会好转吗？”：我们完全无需将问卜 者纳入判断之中。“猫在哪里？”：猫的位置是客观存在的，与问卜者无关；因 此，如果 1 宫主和 6 宫主（小动物：6 宫）是同一颗行星，我们可以用该行星作 为猫的征象星。这类问题通常隐含了“我还能再见到它吗？什么时候？”：我们 仍可通过使用月亮作为问卜者的征象星来回答这个问题。

Instead of taking the ruler of the next sign, we can use another planet if – and only if – it is within a couple of degrees of the cusp of the house in question and in the same

sign as that cusp. This is the only time when a planet can be taken as significator because it is in a house: when the house ruler is already in use and the planet is right on the cusp. Otherwise: planets in a house affect that house for better or for worse; they do not rule it. 若不采用“下一个星座的守护星”这一方法，我们也可以使用另一颗行星——但 前提是，且仅当它位于该宫头几度之内，且与该宫头位于同一星座。这是唯一一 种情况，即行星可以仅因其落在某宫位内而被选为征象星：即当该宫的宫主星已 被占用，且该行星正好紧邻宫头。除此之外：落在某宫内的行星只会对该宫位产 生或好或坏的影响；它们并不守护该宫。

### ✸Be clear on this: a planet does not take on the nature of the house in which it is

placed. If I am asking ‘Where is the cat?’ and Lord 1 is in the 6th house, this does not mean that I am a cat. Nor does the planet take on the nature of the house in any other circumstance. Not even if you want it to. The only exception to this is my point above: if the house-ruler is already busy and we must have a separate significator for what is shown by that house, a planet within a degree or two of the cusp of that house can be pressed into service.✷

### ✸务必明确这一点：行星不会因为它所落宫位而获得该宫的性质。如果我问“猫

在哪里？”，而 1 宫主落在 6 宫，这并不意味着我就是一只猫。在任何其他情况 下，行星也不会获得所在宫位的性质。即使你希望如此也不行。唯一的例外是我 在上文提到的：如果宫主星已被占用，且我们必须为该宫所代表的事物寻找一个 独立的征象星，那么位于该宫头一两度之内的一颗行星可以被临时充任此职。✷

We can also use the almuten of the house cusp, but I suggest you keep this for emergencies: only when none of the options above makes sense. I can recall having done this in only one chart. Finding the almuten is discussed on page 59. 我们也可以使用宫头的宫神星，但我建议你仅将此作为应急方案：只有当上述所 有选项都不适用时才使用。我记得自己只在唯一一张星盘中这样做过。寻找宫神 星的方法在第 51 页讨论。

### ✸I would now strongly advise against using almuten under any circumstances, in

any branch of astrology. The idea is yet one more variety of the Plan B with which the astrologer needed to keep his cupboard fully stocked in order to be able to keep client smiling no matter how grim the judgement should really be. There is no sense in the concept. There is a fuller discussion on p. 59.✷ 我现在强烈建议，在任何占星学分支中，都不要在任何情况下使用宫神星。这个 概念不过是众多“B 计划”中的又一种——占星师需要让他的“工具箱”满满当 当，以便无论实际判断多么严峻，都能让客户满意。这一概念毫无意义。更详细 的讨论见第 109 页。✷

The Moon 月亮

The Moon is always cosignificator of the querent, unless it is main significator of the quesited. This means that the querent usually has two significators: Lord 1 and the Moon. But if, for example, the question is ‘Will I get the job?’ and the Moon rules the 10th house, it signifies the job, not the querent. If the Moon signifies the quesited, the quesited has prior claim on its services and the querent must do without it as cosignificator. 月亮通常作为问卜者的共同征象星，除非它是所占之事的主要征象星。这意味着 问卜者通常有两个征象星：1 宫主和月亮。但例如，如果问题是“我能得到这份 工作吗？”，而月亮守护 10 宫，那么它就象征着工作，而非问卜者。如果月亮 象征着所占之事，则所占之事对它的“征象服务”享有优先权，而问卜者必须放 弃它作为共同征象星。

In third-party questions (‘Will my sister marry this man?’) the Moon does not get transferred to the person asked about: it is cosignificator of the querent, not of anyone else. In such questions it is not usually necessary to involve the querent’s planets, but the placement of the Moon will often show where the querent’s interest lies. 在涉及第三方的问题中（例如“我姐姐会嫁给这个男人吗？”），月亮并不会转 移给被询问的第三方：它始终是问卜者的共同征象星，而非其他人的。在这类问 题中，通常无需考虑问卜者的行星，但月亮的位置往往能显示出问卜者的关注点 所在。

### ✸The ‘always’ in the first line, above, is an exaggeration. In questions on some

subjects, most notably questions on illness, court cases and contests, don’t use the Moon as cosignificator of the querent. This is discussed further in the relevant chapters below.✷

### ✸上文第一行中的“通常”一词是一种夸张说法。在某些主题的问题中，尤其

是关于疾病、诉讼案件和竞赛的问题，不要使用月亮作为问卜者的共同征象星。 这一点将在后续相关章节中进一步讨论。✷

Although both Moon and Lord 1 signify the querent, the Moon is more weighted towards the querent’s emotions, especially in relationship matters. Although both Moon and Lord 1 signify the querent, and an aspect from either of them to the significator of the quesited will usually give a positive answer, aspects from the Moon are never quite as convincing as those from Lord 1. In such cases it is reassuring if we can find some supporting testimony. 虽然月亮和 1 宫主都象征问卜者，但月亮更侧重于问卜者的情感层面，尤其是在 涉及关系的问题中。尽管两者都代表问卜者，且其中任一与所占之事的征象星形 成相位通常都会给出肯定答案，但月亮形成的相位往往不如 1 宫主的相位那样具

有说服力。在这种情况下，若能找到其他支持性证据，则会令判断更加可靠。

What does this planet signify? 行星象征着什么？

We begin our judgement with the houses that are relevant to the question, taking the planets that rule them as significators of the things of those houses. These planets are our main players, the actors of the leading roles in the drama. Often, however, another planet will involve itself in the action, whether by aspect, strong reception or placement in one of the relevant houses. How do we find out what such a planet represents? 我们以问题相关的宫位作为判断的起点，取其宫主星作为该宫所代表事物的征象 星。这些行星是我们的主要角色，是这场戏剧中的领衔演员。然而，往往会有另 一颗行星通过相位、强烈的接纳关系或落入相关宫位的方式介入事件。我们该如 何判断这样一颗行星代表什么呢？

With great caution. It is here that we face the biggest risk of committing the cardinal sin of the horary astrologer: writing our own stories, our own assumptions, into the chart. Suppose we are judging a relationship question. The rulers of the 1st and 7th houses are our main players. We notice another planet involved in the action, and see that it rulers the 9th house. ‘Aha!’ we think, ‘The 9th is the 3rd from the 7th: the wife’s brother.’ And so we quickly construct a compelling fantasy starring the wife’s brother. Only to be to be told that the wife doesn’t have a brother, but that the couple’s grandson (5th from the 5th = 9th) is central to the issue at hand. Any house can mean a huge number of things, and we are most unlikely to plump on the right one by chance. 必须极其谨慎。正是在这里，我们面临着犯下卜卦占星师首要大罪的最大风险： 将我们自己的故事、自己的假设写入星盘。假设我们正在判断一个关系问题。1 宫和 7 宫的宫主星我们的主要角色。我们注意到有另一颗行星牵涉其中，并且发 现它是 9 宫主。“啊哈！”我们想，“9 宫是 7 宫的 3 宫（即配偶的兄弟宫）”。 于是我们迅速构建了一个以配偶兄弟为主角的、引人入胜的幻想。结果却被告知 配偶根本没有兄弟，而是这对夫妇的孙子（5 宫的 5 宫=9 宫）才是当前问题的核 心。任何宫位都可能代表海量事物，我们几乎不可能碰巧选对那唯一正确的含义。

When deciding what an unidentified planet might mean, keep your imagination on a short lead and, if possible, bounce your ideas off the querent. Remember it is a consultation: we are allowed to ask the querent whatever questions we need in order to elucidate the chart. Even a completely open question can be useful: ‘There seems to be someone else involved in this matter – do you have any idea who that might be?’ 在判断一颗身份不明的行星可能代表什么时，务必严格控制你的想象力，如果可 能的话，可以向问卜者求证你的想法。记住这是一次咨询：我们可以询问问卜者 任何必要的问题，以阐明星盘。即使一个完全开放的问题也可能有用：“这件事

似乎牵涉到另一个人——你知道那可能是谁吗？”

Sometimes the house that planet rules will give us its meaning. Often the planet can be taken as ‘some other person’, its meanings by house rulership being irrelevant. As a general rule, always go for the most concrete of the options available. For example, Lord 10 can signify glory or honour, and sometimes does; it is more likely to signify something less abstract: the boss, the job, the mother. 有时，该行星所守护的宫位会告诉我们它的含义。但通常，这颗行星可被视为“其 他相关之人”，其通过宫位守护关系所代表的含义可能并不相关。作为一般规则， 应始终从可选项中选择最具体的那一个。例如，10 宫主可以象征荣耀或声誉， 有时确实如此；但它更可能象征不那么抽象的事物：老板、工作、母亲。

### ✸As so often, the comparison of the chart with the stage in a theatre is a valid one.

As in the theatre actors rarely play abstractions, such as honour or wishes, so in the chart. 诚如常见的情形，将星盘比作戏剧舞台是恰当的类比。就像戏剧舞台上的演员很 少扮演诸如荣耀或愿望这类抽象角色一样，在星盘中也同样如此。

An important difference between the stage and the chart is that all the planets appear in every chart. This does not mean that all the planets are involved in every judgement. Always start with the bare minimum of planets and draw in others only as necessary. ✷ 星盘与舞台的一个重要区别在于：所有行星都会出现在每一张星盘中。但这并不 意味着所有行星都参与每一次判断。始终应从尽可能精简的行星开始，仅在实际 需要时再引入其他行星。✷

### ✸A general rule: NEVER GIVE A PLANET MORE THAN ONE JOB UNLESS

YOU REALLY HAVE TO. Planets can play different roles at differnet points in the judgement. If necessary, this is fine. But if you are tempted to give a planet a second role, more often than not you will find that introducing this second role is superfluous. If you can manage without it, do so.✷

### ✸一条通用法则：除非万不得已，切勿赋予一颗行星一个以上的职责。在判断

过程的不同节点，行星可以扮演不同的角色。若有必要，这样做并无不可。但如 果你试图赋予一颗行星第二个角色，多半会发现引入这第二个角色是多余的。如 果无需它也能完成判断，那就不要用它。✷

Once you have decided upon a plausible identification, studying the receptions involving that planet – hence what the other players think of it and what it thinks of them – will usually either confirm this identification or prove it wrong. Then you can either proceed with judgement or think again about what this planet signifies. 一旦你对行星的角色有了一个看似合理的认定，研究涉及该行星的接纳关系——

即其他参与者对它的看法以及它对它们的看法——通常就能要么证实这一认定， 要么证明它是错误的。然后，你可以据此继续判断，或者重新思考这颗行星究竟 代表什么。

### ✸The acid test when identifying a stray planet is ‘Does it fit the picture?’ That is,

does it fit the whole picture, without contradicting any other evidence, either from what we know of the situation or from what we are shown by the chart. It’s like a detective movie. The butler may have a nasty character and blood on his shirt, but if one piece of evidence contradicts our case against him, we know it wasn’t him who dunnit. In which case we must forget about him and find another suspect. The temptation is to turn a blind eye to conflicting evidence when it doesn’t fit with our assumptions. But horary is not about confirming our assumptions: it is about finding the truth.✷

### ✸在识别一颗游离行星时，最终检验标准是“它是否与整体图景吻合？”也就

是说，它是否契合完整的局面，而不与我们已知的任何其他证据——无论是来自 我们对情况的了解，还是星盘所显示的——相矛盾。这就像一部侦探电影。管家 可能品行恶劣且衬衫上有血迹，但只要有一条证据与我们指控他的案情相悖，我 们就知道犯案者并非是他。若是如此，我们就必须排除他，去寻找另一个嫌疑人。 当证据与我们的假设不符时，我们很容易对相互矛盾的证据视而不见。但卜卦占 星的目的不是为了证实我们的假设：而是为了寻求真相。✷

NATURAL RULERSHIPS 先天守护关系

Rulerships determined by the house a planet rules in that chart, called accidental rulerships, are what primarily concern us, but the planets also have their natural associations. Everything is made of all seven planetary influences combined in differing proportions. One or two of these influences will be particularly obvious in any thing that we might consider. Which one of them takes our attention will depend upon the context of the enquiry. The classic example is the rose: it is ruled by Venus, as shown by its beauty; it is ruled by Mars, as shown by its thorns. Or the slug: ruled by Satrun, as being black and nasty and living under stones; by the Moon, as being soft and moist and coming out at night. 通过行星在特定星盘中所守护的宫位确定的守护关系，称为偶然守护关系，这是 我们首要关注的；但行星也拥有其先天属性。万物皆由全部七种行星影响力以不 同比例混合构成。在任何我们可能考量的事物中，其中一两种影响力会尤为突出。 具体是哪一种引起我们的注意，将取决于询问的语境。经典的例子是玫瑰：它由 金星守护，这体现在其美丽上；它也由火星守护，这体现在其尖刺上。又如蛞蝓 （鼻涕虫）：它由土星守护，因其色黑、令人生厌且栖身石下；它也由月亮守护， 因其柔软、湿润且夜间出没。

These natural rulerships will occasionally be significant in the chart. If we are looking for some lost documents, for example, we might look at Mercury, the natural ruler of documents. In boy/girl questions we will look to the Sun, as natural ruler of men, and Venus, natural ruler of women. The Moon is natural ruler of any lost object, especially an animate one. These natural rulers will sometimes offer information supplementary to what the house ruler tell us; sometimes the chart will emphasise them in so strong a way that we can judge by them alone. 这些先天守护关系偶尔会在星盘中具有重要意义。例如，如果我们正在寻找一些 丢失的文件，我们可能会查看水星——文件的先天守护星。在涉及男孩/女孩的 问题中，我们会关注太阳（男性的先天守护星）和金星（女性的先天守护星）。 月亮是任何失物（尤其是有生命之物）的先天守护星。这些先天守护星有时会提 供宫主星所告知信息之外的补充；有时，星盘会以如此强烈的方式突显它们，以 至于我们可以仅凭它们进行判断。

Although the importance of natural rulerships is minor compared to that of the accidental rulerships, it is worth becoming fluent in them. This is best done by putting planets to objects as you come across them in your daily round, as you might learn a language by translating everthing you see into that language. Working from the guidelines below, you will soon find it simple: ‘Corn Flakes: Sun, as corn is a staple food; Saturn, because they are crispy; Mercury, because they are small and come in great number. Milk: Moon, as a liquid, and because it’s white. Sugar: Venus, as it’s sweet; Mars, for the energy it gives.’ 尽管先天守护关系的重要性相较于偶然守护关系为次，但仍值得熟练掌握。最佳 方式是在日常生活中，将遇到的事物对应到行星，就像学习一门语言时，将所见 一切翻译成那种语言一样。参照以下指引练习，你将很快发现这很简单：“玉米 片：太阳，因为玉米是主食；土星，因为其酥脆；水星，因为其细小且数量众多。 牛奶：月亮，因为是液体，且是白色的。糖：金星，因为它是甜的；火星，因为 它提供能量。”

If you need to find the ruler of an object, go for the essential nature of that object. Consider: what is the natural ruler of a camera? It is a mechanical contrivance: Mercury. It is used to take pretty pictures: Venus. It is used for reportage: Mercury. It works by writing (Mercury) with light (Sun) by means of mirrors (Moon). All this is true. But what is its essential nature? What does a camera do? Its essence is in what it is, not in what it can be used for (taking pretty pictures, reportage), nor in how it does it (machinery, writing with light). A camera’s essential function is to capture the ephemeral. So its essence is in capturing, preserving, and its natural ruler is Saturn. Follow this logic with any other item and you will not go wrong. 若要确定一个物体的守护星，应着眼于该物体的本质。思考：相机的先天守护星 是什么？它是一种机械装置：水星。它用于拍摄美丽的照片：金星。它用于新闻 报道：水星。它通过镜子（月亮）利用光线（太阳）进行“书写”（水星）。这 些都对。但它的本质是什么？相机是做什么的？其本质在于它是什么，而不在于 它能用来做什么（拍美照、新闻报道），也不在于它如何实现（机械装置、用光

书写）。相机的基本功能是捕捉短暂瞬间。因此，其本质在于捕捉、保存，所以 它的先天守护星是土星。对任何其他物品都遵循此逻辑，你便不会出错。

An exhaustive listing of natural rulerships is impossible: it would mean listing everything that exists. The following should give sufficient clues to enable you to find the appropriate ruler for anything. 一份先天守护关系的详尽列表是不可能完成的：那意味着要列出所有存在的事物。 以下内容应能提供足够的线索，使你能够为任何事物找到恰当的守护星。

Saturn 土星

Cold and dry; diurnal; masculine. 冷且燥；日星；阳性

12. Diurnal planets prefer being above the Earth by day, below it by night. Nocturnal planets prefer the reverse. See p. 68. hayz.
12. 日星在白天倾向于位于地平线之上，在夜晚则倾向于位于地平线之下。夜星 则相反。参见第 143 页，得时。

Saturn rules things that are old, black, hard, heavy, dead, decayed, restrictive, dry, cold, solitary, sad. 土星守护古老、黑色、坚硬、沉重、死亡、腐朽、限制、干燥、寒冷、孤独、悲 伤的事物。

Example: root vegetables, because they grow underground. Nightshade, because of its colour and because it is deadly (also Venus for its cosmetic qualities). Liquorice, for its colour and as a root. Mildew. All waste products and refuse. Lead, for its weight; hence aslo plumbers, who work with lead. Sewermen. Undertakers. Miners. Farm labourers. Gardeners (Saturn was god of agriculture). Discipline. Prisons, ruins, toilets. 例如：根茎类蔬菜（因其生长于地下）；龙葵（因其颜色且具有毒性——其美容 特性也受金星守护）；甘草（因其颜色且为根茎）；霉菌；所有废弃物与垃圾； 铅（因其重量，故也守护水管工，因其与铅打交道）、下水道工人、殡葬人员、 矿工、农场工人、园丁（土星曾是农业之神）；纪律；监狱、废墟、厕所。

Opium, as a narcotic and because it is addictive, creating new barriers. The yew is very saturnine: it has dark foliage; it is poisonous; it grows to a great age; it lives in graveyards. Saturn rules locks; Mercury rules keys. Saturn in natural ruler of fathers in night charts. 鸦片（因其为麻醉剂且具成瘾性，会制造新的障碍）。紫杉极具土星特质：叶色 深暗、有毒、寿命极长、生长于墓地。土星先天守护锁具；水星守护钥匙。在夜 生盘中，土星是父亲的先天守护星。

13. A night chart is one cast during the night; a day chart one cast during the day. In a day chart the Sun will be in house 7-12; at night it is below the Earth, in houses 1-6. Allow a few degrees in favour of day at both the Ascendant and Descendant, as it is light for a little while before the Sun rises and after it sets.
13. 夜生盘是指在夜间起算的星盘；日生盘则是在白天起算的。在日生盘中，太 阳将位于 7-12 宫；在夜生盘中，太阳位于地平线以下，即在 1-6 宫。在日出前 和日落后，天光仍会持续片刻，因此在上升点和下降点处，昼夜的划分需允许有 几度的余裕。

Moles, dogs, cats, scavengers, things that live under stones. Sapphire, lapis lazuli. In the body, it rules the right ear, bones, teeth, skin, joints, spleen. 土星还守护鼹鼠、狗、猫、食腐动物、生活在石头下的生物；蓝宝石、青金石； 在身体部位中，它守护右耳、骨骼、牙齿、皮肤、关节、脾脏。

Jupiter 木星

Hot and moist; diurnal; masculine. 热且湿；日星；阳性。

Jupiter rules things that are big, expansive, expensive, luxurious, religious, purple, laxative (in contrast to Saturn, which is binding), generous. 木星守护庞大、扩张、昂贵、奢华、宗教性、紫色、通便的（与土星的收敛特性 相反）、慷慨的事物。

Examples: fruit trees, for the abundance of good things they produce. Rich men, aristocrats, judges, priests. Rhubarb. Feasts. Foie gras. Teachers (who have knowledge and pour it out). Gurus. Ivy is ruled by Jupiter because it spreads, by Satrun for its dark colour and association with dark places and decay. Rain. Mercy. 例如：果树（因其产出丰盛美物）；富人、贵族、法官、神职人员；大黄；盛宴； 肥肝；教师（因其拥有知识并倾囊相授）；精神导师。常春藤由木星守护，因其 蔓延生长；也受土星守护，因其深暗的颜色以及与阴暗处、腐朽的关联；此外， 木星还守护雨水、仁慈。

Big animals; animas that are gentle and of benefit to mankind. Amethyst, sapphire (has both Jupiter and Saturn nature), emerald, crystal, tin. 木星守护大型动物；温顺且对人类有益的动物。紫水晶、蓝宝石（兼具木星与土 星特性）、祖母绿、水晶、锡。

In the body it rules the left ear, lungs, liver, blood, semen. 在身体部位中，它守护左耳、肺、肝、血液、精液。

Mars 火星

Hot and dry; nocturnal; masculine. 热且燥；夜星；阳性。

Mars rules things that are sharp, burning, cutting, red, abrasive, hot, aggressive. 火星守护尖锐、灼热、锋利、红色、粗糙、炽热、侵略性的事物。

Example: soldiers, butchers, tailors, surgeons, barbers, pirates. Anyone who works with fire, hence alchemists, cooks, firemen. Executioners. Peppers, garlic ( also by the Moon, for its colour), radishes (also Moon). Nettles, thistles (both also Saturn, as they grow on waste ground). Divorce. Fevers. Lust. 例如：火星守护的事物举例：士兵、屠夫、裁缝、外科医生、理发师、海盗；任 何与火相关工作的人，如炼金术士、厨师、消防员；刽子手；胡椒、大蒜（也受 月亮守护，因其颜色）、萝卜（也受月亮守护）；荨麻、蓟（两者也受土星守护， 因它们生长在荒地）；离婚、发烧、情欲。

Animals that are fierce or fiery; creatures that bite or sting. Iron, bloodstone, jasper, coral. 火星守护凶猛或暴躁的动物；会咬人或叮咬的生物。铁、血石、碧玉、珊瑚。

In the body, Mars rules the gall bladder and the genitals (especially male). 在身体部位中，火星守护胆囊与生殖器官（尤其男性）。

The Sun 太阳

Hot and dry; diurnal; masculine. 热且燥；日星；阳性。

The Sun rules things that are unique, royal, golden, life-giving, honest. 太阳守护独特、尊贵、金色、赋予生命、诚实的事物。

Example: as giver of life, the Sun rules all food, and staples in particular. Citrus fruit, for its appearance, as also sunflowers, marigolds etc. The king of every classification: gold, as king of metals; the eagle, as king of birds; lions, as king of beasts; diamond as king of jewels. Palaces and other grand buildings. The Sun is natural ruler of fathers in day charts. 例如：作为生命的赋予者，太阳守护所有食物，尤其是主食。柑橘类水果（因其 外观），以及向日葵、金盏花等。各类别中的“王者”：黄金（金属之王）；鹰 （鸟类之王）；狮子（兽类之王）；钻石（宝石之王）。宫殿及其他宏伟建筑。

在日生盘中，太阳是父亲的先天守护星。

In the body it rules the vital spirit or life-force, the heart, the brain (seen as the controlling principle) and the eyes – the eyes in general and, specifically, the right eye in males, the left eye in females. 在身体中，太阳守护生命力或生命能量、心脏、大脑（被视为控制中枢）以及眼 睛——泛指双眼，具体而言，在男性中守护右眼，在女性中守护左眼。

Venus 金星

Cold and moist; nocturnal; feminine. 冷且湿；夜星；阴性。

Venus rules things that are soft, pretty, fragrant, attractive, pleasant. 金星守护柔软、美丽、芬芳、迷人、令人愉悦的事物。

Examples: flowers （in general: each variety has its own ruler.) Soft fruit. Chocolate. Kisses. Marriage. Treaties. Fun. Art, music. Make-up and perfume. 例如：花卉（泛指：每个品种各有其守护星）；软质水果；巧克力；亲吻；婚姻； 协议；娱乐；艺术、音乐；化妆品与香水。

Jewellers, musicians, the person whose main function at work is to look nice, fashionistas, prostitutes, drapers, decorators. Beds, wardrobes. Wives, young women. 珠宝商；音乐家；工作中主要职责是展现美观的人；时尚人士；妓女；布料商； 室内装饰师。床；衣柜。妻子；年轻女性。

Soft and cuddly animals – the typical inhabitants of a children’s zoo. Copper, brass, cornelian, azure sapphire, lapis lazuli, beryl, chrysolite. 柔软且令人想拥抱的动物——典型的儿童动物园居民。铜、黄铜、玛瑙、天蓝色 蓝宝石、青金石、绿柱石、橄榄石。

Venus is natural ruler of mothers in daytime charts. 在日生盘中，金星是母亲的先天守护星。

In the body she rules the kidneys, the sense of smell and the genitals (especially female). 在身体中，金星守护肾脏、嗅觉与生殖器官（尤其女性）。

Mercury 水星

Cold and dry; diurnal if preceding the Sun (oriental), nocturnal if following it (occidental); mixed male/female nature, becoming male if with male planets, female if with female. 冷且燥；若位于太阳之前（东出），则为日星；若位于太阳之后（西入），则为 夜星；它兼具阴阳双重特质，与阳性行星结合时显阳性，与阴性行星结合时 显阴性。

14. See p.79 for an explanation of oriental and occidental.
14. 关于东出与西入的解释，参见第 141 页。

### ✸For all its famed androgyny, Mercury is always more likely to be male: take it as

male unless there is good reason to do otherwise.✷ 尽管水星以兼有阴阳两性特质著称，但它通常更倾向于阳性：除非有充分理由， 否则应将其视为阳性。✷

Mercury rules things that are parti-coloured, ambiguous, dexterous, tricky, mixed. 水星守护多变、模棱两可、灵巧、狡猾、混合的事物。

Examples: sweet & sour sauce, cocktails, pizza. Things that are small and come in great number: berries, currants, aniseeds. Things that grow in husks, on the analogy of the brain within the skull – especially walnuts, which look like brains. Beans, which produce wind (ruled by Mercury, whether bodily or atmospheric). Earthquakes (wind in the Earth). Anything that speaks, or otherwise resembles man: monkeys, parrots, puppets, bees, hyenas (because they laugh). Things that are volatile, such as lavender oil. Siccatives. Things that mimic mental process, hence keys, that undo the lock of a problem. Thieves, servants. Tricksters, con-men, pickpockets. Variety. Virtuosi. Auctioneers, agents and dealers. Merchants. The knowledge needed for any trade. Wits, humorists. The human being. Articulation, talk, lies. Computers. Astrology and astrologers. Clerks, accountants, scribes, messengers, ‘media people’. Doctors, medicines. Lawyers (who speak for you). Anyone’s ‘right-hand man’. Documents, papers, books, magazines. 例如：甜酸酱、鸡尾酒、披萨。细小且数量众多之物：浆果、醋栗、茴香籽。有 外壳包裹生长之物（类比头骨内的大脑）——尤其是形似脑部的核桃。豆类（因 其产生气体——无论是体内之气还是大气之风，皆由水星守护）。地震（地中之 风）。任何能发声或类似人类之物：猴子、鹦鹉、木偶、蜜蜂、鬣狗（因其似笑）。 挥发物，如薰衣草油；干燥剂。模拟思维过程之物，如钥匙（用以解开问题的锁）。 小偷、仆人；骗子、诈欺者、扒手；多样化；行家；拍卖师、中介与经销商；商 人；任何行业所需的知识；机智者、幽默家；人类；言语、交谈、谎言；计算机； 占星学与占星师；文员、会计、抄写员、信使、“媒体人”；医生、药物；律师 （为你发声者）；任何人的“得力助手”；文件、纸张、书籍、杂志。

In the body it rules the tongue, brain (as seat of reason), arms, hands and fingers. 在身体中，水星守护舌头、大脑（作为理性之所在）、手臂、手和手指。

The Moon 月亮

Cold and moist; nocturnal; feminine. 冷且湿；夜星；阴性。

The Moon rules things that are liquid, soft, of little flavor or substance, formless, white, new. 月亮守护液态、柔软、寡淡或无实质、无形、白色、新生的事物。

Example: cabbages, for their shape. Cucumbers, melons for their water content. Babies; midwives; the mother, in a night chart. Mushrooms, for their colour, shape, and because they appear overnight. Candles, because they light the darkness. Lost objects. Intoxicants. Changeability, fickleness. Novelty. The common people. Queens, but only as the wife of the king (Sun), nor if ruling in her own right, when she would be the Sun. Tramps, pilgrims, beggars, sailors, midwives, barmen, nurses, cleaners. 例如：卷心菜（因其形状）；黄瓜、瓜类（因其含水量高）；婴儿、助产士；在 夜生盘中，象征母亲；蘑菇（因其颜色、形状，且一夜之间出现）；蜡烛（因其 照亮黑暗）；失物；致醉物；善变、反复无常；新奇事物；平民；王后，但仅作 为国王（太阳）的妻子，除非她本身是统治者，此时她则是太阳；流浪者、朝圣 者、乞丐、水手、助产士、酒保、护士、清洁工。

Creatures that live in water: fish, otters, frogs, ducks, oysters. Or that come out at night: slugs, owls, bushbabies. Pearls, moonstone, alabaster. 生活在水中的生物：鱼、水獭、青蛙、鸭子、牡蛎；或夜间出没的生物：蛞蝓、 猫头鹰、婴猴。珍珠、月光石、汉白玉。

In the body she rules the breasts, womb, belly and intestines. 在身体中，月亮守护乳房、子宫、腹部与肠。

Age 年龄

There is a rising scale of age from the Moon, which rules babies, through Mercury, Venus, Sun, Mars and Jupiter to Saturn, which rules the old. This is ‘the Seven Ages of Man’. 从月亮（守护婴儿）开始，经水星、金星、太阳、火星、木星，直至土星（守护 老人），存在一个年龄递增的阶梯。这便是“人生七阶”。

The outer planets 外行星

Uranus, Neptune and Pluto do have their uses in horary, but these uses are limited. They have not a fraction of the importance with which they are invested by most contemporary astrologers. They each have a very few things with which they seem to have a natural connection: Uranus with divorce and other disruption, such as house-moving; Neptune with illusion and deceit; Pluto seems generally and unspecifically malefic. 天王星、海王星与冥王星在卜卦占星中确有其用途，但这些用途有限。它们的重 要性远不及大多数当代占星师所赋予的那般。它们各自仅与少数事物存在看似自 然的关联：天王星与离婚及其他破坏性事件（如搬家）相关；海王星与幻觉和欺 骗相关；冥王星则普遍且非特定性地具有凶性。

Treat them much like fixed stars: ignore them unless they are right on a relevant house cusp or in immediate aspect with one of the main significators. 对待它们应如恒星一般：除非它们正好位于相关宫头，或与某个主要征象星形成 紧密相位，否则均可忽略。

Example 2: a client asked a series of questions relating to the sale of her business. Each of these charts had Neptune on the cusp of either the 7th house (the buyer) or the 8th (the 2nd from the 7th: the buyer’s money). She was being cheated. 例子 2：一位客户询问了关于出售其业务的一系列问题。在这些星盘中，每一张 都有海王星位于 7 宫（买家）或 8 宫（7 之 2 宫：买家的钱财）的宫头。她正在 遭受欺诈。

The outer planets do not rule signs and they do not have any particular associations with any of the signs. The reasoning that they might is utterly groundless. The reader familiar with modern astrology may be reluctant to abandon these ideas, but if you insist on incorporating them in your charts you will consistently get wrong answers. This is not a matter of opinion. 外行星不守护任何星座，它们与任何星座均无特定关联。认为它们可能有关联的 推理是毫无根据的。熟悉现代占星学的读者或许不愿放弃这些观念，但如果你坚 持将它们纳入你的星盘解读，你将持续得到错误的答案。这并非个人见解的问题。

If the placement of an outer planet demands our attention, it can, like a powerful fixed star, provide a shorthand answer. We will never need to go looking for them (‘What is Uranus doing in this chart?’) and we will never find them telling us anyting that is not equally well shown by the seven planets of the traditional cosmos. 若某一外行星的位置引起了我们的注意，它可以像一颗强力的恒星那样，提供一 个速记式答案。我们永远无需刻意寻找它们（例如“天王星在这张星盘中正在做 什么？”），也永远不会发现它们能告诉我们任何无法由传统七颗行星同样清晰 揭示的信息。

Example: a client asked about her impending divorce. Uranus was on the Midheaven, symbolically halfway between the Ascendant (the querent) and the 7th cusp (her husband). Mars, the traditional ruler of divorce, exactly squared the Ascendant/Descendant axis. Both planets showed the same thing. 例如：一位客户询问她即将到来的离婚。天王星位于中天，象征性地处于上升点 （问卜者）与 7 宫头（她的丈夫）之间。而火星——离婚的传统守护星，则精确 刑克着上升点/下降点的轴线。两颗行星共同指向同一结论。

Chiron, asteroids, Dark Moon Lilith, Sedna: none of these has any place in horary. No matter how attached to these little fellas you might be, incorporating them in your charts will do nothing but confuse you. 凯龙星、小行星、暗月莉莉丝、塞德娜：这些在卜卦占星中皆无位置。无论你对 这些小东西多么青睐，将它们纳入你的星盘只会让你困惑不已。

Friends and enemies 朋友和敌人

If you’ve read the old texts you will have found lists of which planets are friendly with which, and which are enemies. These lists are irrelevant in horary, because the ‘who likes whom’ in the immediate context – which is all that concerns us – is shown by the receptions. Example: it is all very well that Mars is in principle a friend to Venus, but that he hates this Venus here right now is all that concerns us when judging this particular chart. 若你读过古典占星文献，会发现其中列有行星间孰友孰敌的清单。这些清单在卜 卦占星中并不适用，因为当前情境下的“谁喜欢谁”——这才是我们唯一关心的 ——完全由接纳关系来揭示。例如：尽管火星在原则上与金星友好，但在此刻判 断这张特定星盘时，我们只关心他此刻讨厌这个金星这一事实。

### ✸ Actors and roles again. What interests us is whether Romeo likes Juliet. The

opinions of the actors are not our concern.✷

### ✷再次回到演员与角色的比喻。我们关心的是 Romeo（罗密欧）是否喜欢 Juliet

（朱丽叶）。演员本人的看法则与我们无关。✷

Superior and inferior 地外和地内

The superior planets are Mars, Jupiter and Saturn, the inferior are Mercury, Venus and

the Moon. They are so called because the superior planets have, from the perspective of the Earth, their orbits above that of the Sun (superior in Latin = higher) and the inferior have theirs below (inferior in Latin = lower). This distinction has no practical relevance in horary. 地外行星包括火星、木星与土星，地内行星则为水星、金星与月亮。如此命名是 因为，从地球的视角看，地外行星的轨道位于太阳之上（拉丁语 superior 意为“较 高”），而地内行星的轨道位于太阳之下（拉丁语 inferior 意为“较低”）。这 种区分在卜卦占星中并无实际意义。

# The Signs

# 星座

The signs of the zodiac are treated quite differently in traditional and modern astrology. Now is the time to reach into your head, locate all you have learned about the signs from the moderns and set that aside. 在传统占星学和现代占星学中，黄道星座的处理方式截然不同。现在，是时候梳 理你脑海中的知识，找出所有你从现代占星学中学到的关于星座的内容，并将它 们暂时搁置一旁。

The signs describe the planets that are in them. In our astrological sentences, the planets are the nouns, the signs are the adjectives and the aspects are the verbs. The sign does not do anything: it has no power to act. It simply describes. 星座描述位于其中的行星。在我们的占星学语句中，行星是名词，星座是形容词， 而相位是动词。星座本身不执行任何行动：它不具备行动的能力。它仅仅是描述。

The sign a planet is in describes it in three different ways: 行星所在的星座以三种不同方式描述该行星：

1.it tells us how much essential strength the planet has 1.它告诉我们该行星拥有多少先天力量

2.it tells us about that planet’s attitude to other planets 2.它告诉我们该行星对其他行星的态度

3.it has certain qualities of its own. 3.它自身具备某些特定品质。

Point 1 will be considered in chapter 6 and point 2 in chapter 8. Here we shall consider point 3: the divisions of the signs into various groups with shared characteristics. 第 1 点将在第 6 章讨论，第 2 点将在第 8 章讨论。在此，我们将探讨第 3 点：根 据共同特征将星座划分成不同的组别。

In most questions most of these characteristics will be irrelevant, just as if I am asking my friend to lend me some money, the fact that he walks with a limp is of no concern.

But in some questions these points can be crucial. If the question is ‘Will I have a baby this year?’ and every significator is in a barren sign, it is most unlikely that we could judge ‘Yes’, whatever aspects there might be. It is easy to overlook such basic information in the rush to hunt down an aspect. 在大多数问题中，这些特征大多无关紧要，就像当我向朋友借钱时，他走路是否 跛行并不重要。但在某些问题中，这些点可能至关重要。如果问题是“我今年会 有孩子吗？”，而每个征象星都落在贫瘠的星座，那么无论存在何种相位，我们 都几乎不可能判断为“是”。在急于寻找相位时，很容易忽略这类基本信息。

Note: while the signs do have a set of shared characteristics, they do not have the rounded personalities that they are given in modern astrology. For instance, a planet in Leo is not going to behave in a regal fashion. Leo is a feral sign, and so is inclined to behave like a wild beast – if the context supports this. It is unlikely to manage to be both feral and regal at the same time. 注意：虽然星座确实拥有一系列共同的特性，但它们并不具备现代占星学所赋予 的那种完整的“人格”。例如，一颗在狮子座的行星并不会表现得像个君王。狮 子座是一个野性的星座，因此——如果背景支持的话——它倾向于表现得像一头 野兽。它不太可能同时兼具野性与威严。

Male and female 阳性与阴性

      are male ；       female. This division is useful mainly for determining the sex of babies or thieves. It can be helpful when we need to distinguish between various options, as in ‘Which of these candidates should I employ?’ In such questions we must find a way to distinguish the various candidates, so a division by sex may help. 白羊、双子、狮子、天平、射手、水瓶是阳性的；金牛、巨蟹、处女、天蝎、摩 羯、双鱼是阴性的。这种划分主要用于确定婴儿或小偷的性别。当我们需要区分 不同选项时，它也会有所帮助，例如“我应该雇用哪位候选人？”在这类问题中， 我们必须找到区分不同候选人的方法，因此按性别划分可能具有参考价值。

Elements 元素

  are earth;   air;    fire;   water. Useful mainly in locating lost objects. Can be helpful in vocational questions: ‘Should I become an accountant (air, because air relates to the faculty of reason) or a farmer (earth)?’ Lord 10 strong in an air sign: testimony in favour of accountancy. 金牛、处女、摩羯是土象；双子、天平、水平是风象；白羊、狮子、射手是火象；

巨蟹、天蝎、双鱼是水象。主要用于定位失物。在职业问题中也能提供帮助：“我 应该成为一名会计师（风象，因为风象与理性思维相关）还是一名农民（土象）？” 如果 10 宫主在风象星座有力：则征象支持选择会计职业。

Earth signs are cold and dry; water, cold and moist; fire, hot and dry; air, hot and moist. These few words contain almost everything that is needed for forecasting the weather through horary. 土象星座冷且燥；水象，冷且湿；火象，热且燥；风象，热且湿。这寥寥数词几 乎囊括了通过卜卦占星来预测天气所需的一切信息。

Modes 型态

are cardinal; fixed; mutable. The cardinal signs show action that is quick but doesn’t last; fixed signs are slow and stable; mutable come and go. This division is useful in many contexts. 白羊、巨蟹、天平、摩羯是基本星座；金牛、狮子、处女、水瓶是固定星座；双 子、处女、射手、双鱼是变动星座。基本星座的行动迅速但不持久；固定星座的 行动缓慢且稳定；变动星座的行动则来去反复。这种划分在许多情境下都很有用。

The significator of an illness is fixed: it is chronic; cardinal: it is acute; mutable: it will come and go. 疾病的征象星若在固定星座：表示是慢性病；在基本星座：表示是急性病；在变 动星座：则表示病情会反复。

‘I want to win this dispute, but I don’t think it’s worth going to court; can I win?’ Opponent’s significator in a fixed sign: ‘No, he’ll fight it out’. In a cardinal sign: ‘Show him you mean business and he’ll give in’. “我想赢得这场争论，但觉得不值得上法庭；我能赢吗？”如果对手的征象星在 固定星座：“不能，他会抗争到底。”如果在基本星座：“向他表明你是认真的， 他就会让步。”。

Mutable signs are less inclined to be reliable or honest. 变动星座不太倾向于可靠或诚实。

The cardinal signs are aslo known as moveable signs. Be careful here: moveable and mutable are words easily confused. 基本星座也可称为可动星座。此处需注意：“可动”与“变动”是容易混淆的词 语。

Double-bodied signs 双体星座

The mutable signs are aslo known as Double-bodied. This emphasises the duality that is so important a part of their nature. 变动星座也被称为双体星座。这强调了双重性是其本质中极为重要的一部分。

In questions where someone is considering leaving a steady job to freelance or work part-time, the transition is often shown by the significator entering a double-bodied sign. Duality: freelancing means having more than one boss and sometimes pursuing more than one trade; in part-time work and job-sharing the time or the job is split. 在有人考虑辞去稳定工作转为自由职业或兼职工作的卜卦中，这种转变常常通过 征象星进入双体星座来显示。双重性体现在：自由职业意味着拥有不止一个雇主， 有时还从事不止一项业务；而在兼职工作和岗位共享中，时间或工作内容被分割 了。

In some questions (‘Should we do such and such?’) it is unclear whether the 1st house should be given to the couple or group, or if the querent should have the 1st and the partner or colleagues should be treated separately and given the 7th. Finding Lord 1 in a double-bodied sign is strong testimony for taking it as significator for the couple or group. 在某些问题中（例如“我们应该做某某事吗？”），究竟应将 1 宫分配给这对伴 侣或团体整体，还是应将问卜者本人分配给 1 宫，而将伴侣或同事单独处理并分 配给 7 宫，这一点并不明确。如果发现 1 宫主位于双体星座，便是将其视为伴侣 或团体整体之征象星的有力佐证。

In questions of number (how many babies or thieves), double-bodied signs show more than one. 在数量类问题中（例如有多少婴儿或窃贼），双体星座表示数量不止一个。

Note: the double-bodied signs are     . These and these only. Regardless of whether you can see the duality in the image of this sign, or if you can find duality in the image of any other sign. 注意：双体星座是指双子座、处女座、射手座和双鱼座。仅此这些。无论你是否 能在此星座的形象中看到双重性，或者你是否能在其他任何星座的形象中找到双 重性。

Fertile and barren 肥沃和贫瘠

The water signs are fertile. Gemini, Leo and Virgo are barren. The other six signs can be regarded as neutral.This relates of course to procreation, but also to other things.

If my investments are in a fertile sign they are more likely to grow than if they are in a barren. 水象星座是肥沃的。双子座、狮子座和处女座是贫瘠的。其余六个星座可视为中 性。这当然与孕育有关，但也适用于其他事物。如果我的投资落在肥沃星座， 相比落在贫瘠星座，它们更有可能增长。

15. This is only in horary. In natal work we divide the other six into mildly fertile and mildly barren. 这仅适用于卜卦占星。在本命占星中，我们会将另外六个星座进一步划分为轻度肥沃和 轻度贫瘠。

Of the barren signs, Gemini and Virgo are also double-bodied, so in questions like ‘Will I have children?’ they are testimonies for ‘No’; but if the judgement from the whole chart is ‘Yes’, their double-bodiedness will be testimony for more than one child. 在贫瘠星座中，双子座和处女座同时也是双体星座。因此，在诸如“我会有孩子 吗？”这类问题中，它们是判断为“否”的征象；但如果根据全盘得出的判断是 “是”，那么它们的双体特性则会成为不止一个孩子的征象。

Voiced and mute 发声和无声

The water signs are mute; Gemini, Virgo and Libra are loud-voiced; Aries, Taurus, Leo and Sagittarius are half-voiced; Capricorn and Aquarius weak-voiced. 水象星座是无声的；双子、处女和天平是高发声的（话痨）；白羊，金牛，狮子 和射手是半发声的（普通）；摩羯和水瓶是弱发声的（话少）。

This division is useful in vocational questions (‘Am I the singer or the songwriter?’). Another example: a woman asked about her marital problems. Among other testimonies in the analysis, her heart was seen to love her husband while her head disliked him. Her head was in a loud-voiced sign, while her heart was mute – so all he heard from her was the dislike. 这种划分在职业问题中很有用（例如“我适合当歌手还是作曲家？”）。另一个 例子：一位女性询问她的婚姻问题。在分析中的其他征象之外，我们看到她的内 心爱着她的丈夫，而她的头脑却不喜欢他。她的头脑落在高发声的星座，而她的 心却落在无声的星座——因此，他能听到的只有她的不满。

Humane and bestial 仁慈和野蛮

The air signs and Virgo are humane. Aries, Taurus, Leo, Sagittarius and Capricorn are bestial, of which Leo and the second half of Sagittarius are feral. 风象星座和处女座是仁慈的。白羊、金牛、狮子、射手和摩羯是野蛮的，其中狮 子和射手的下半部分是野性的。

Suppose I ask how my neighbour will react if I complain about the noise he makes: his significator in a humane sign is one testimony that he will behave in a reasonable fashion, in a manner befitting a human being; in a bestial sign suggests he will behave like a beast; in a feral sign, like a wild beast. 假设我问，如果我抱怨邻居制造的噪音，他会作何反应：他的征象星在仁慈的星 座，表明他会以理性的方式、以符合人类身份的方式行事；在野蛮的星座暗示他 会表现得像只野兽；在野性星座，则会表现得像一头猛兽。

Maimed 残缺

Aries, Taurus, Leo and Pisces are described as maimed. This may be useful for physical descriptions. 白羊、金牛、狮子和双鱼被描述为残缺星座。这可能对形体描述有帮助。

There are many other such divisions, but these are the only ones I have ever found of practical use. Important: all these testimonies are ‘all things being equal’. Any single testimony can be outweighed. Use your common sense. For example, fixed signs show stability, but a planet at the end of a fixed sign will show a stable situation coming to an end. ‘Will Bugsy squeal?’ with his significator at the end of Scorpio, a fixed, mute sign: ‘Not now, but he soon will’. 还有其他许多类似的划分方式，但以上这些是我发现唯一有实际用途的。重要提 示：所有这些征象都是基于“在其他条件相同的情况下”。任何单一的征象都可 能被其他因素所超越。运用你的常识。例如，固定星座显示稳定，但一颗行星位 于固定星座的末端，则可能显示一种稳定的局面即将结束。以“Bugsy（巴格西） 会告密吗？”这个问题为例，如果他的征象星位于天蝎座——一个固定、无声星 座——的末端：“现在还不会，但他很快会的。”

While these testimonies can all be overruled, in some charts the information given by these basic divisions will be all we need for judgement. ‘Is my job secure?’ with Lord 10 in the middle of a fixed sign. All we need do is glance quickly around the chart to check for contrary testimonies; if we find none we can give our answer: ‘Yes, it is’. Judgement can be this simple. 尽管这些征象都可能被其他因素所超越，但在某些星盘中，这些基本划分所提供 的信息可能就是我们判断所需的全部依据。“我的工作稳定吗？”如果 10 宫主 位于一个固定星座的中间位置。我们只需要快速扫视全盘，检查是否存在相反的

征象；如果没有找到，我们就可以给出答案：“是的，很稳定。”判断有时可以 如此简单。

The body 身体

The body is divided among the signs, starting with Aries at the top and working down to Pisces at the toes. 人体部位对应星座，从顶部的白羊座开始，向下依次对应，直至脚趾的双鱼座。

：the head 头部 ：the neck 颈部 ：hands, arms and shoulders 手、手臂和肩膀 ：the breast 胸部 ：the heart and ribs 心脏和肋骨 ：intestines and related organs 肠及相关器官 ：urinary system, lower back 泌尿系统，下背部 ：genitals and anus 生殖器和肛门 ：thighs and buttocks 大腿和臀部 ：the kness 膝盖 ：calves and ankles 小腿和脚踝 ：the feet 脚

### ✸There is never any significance in the nature of the sign on an angle or the cusp of

a house. The only function of the sign on the cusp is to show us which planet rules that house. There is no exception to this. All the points above relate to the sign the significator is in, not to the sign on any cusp. For example, the person’s significator in a water sign could be testimony of fertility if fertility is relevant or of muteness if speech is relevant; that the person’s cusp is in a water sign is not testimony of anything.✷

### ✸位于四轴点或宫头处的星座的属性本身没有任何意义。宫头星座的唯一作用

就是向我们显示哪颗行星是那个宫位的守护星。这一点毫无例外。上述所有要点 都只与征象星所在的星座有关，而与任何宫头星座无关。例如，如果生育能力相 关，问卜者的征象星在水象星座可以成为生育能力的佐证；如果言语相关，则可 以成为沉默寡言的佐证；但问卜者的宫头落在水象星座则不构成任何佐证。✷

# Essential Dignity

# 先天尊贵

Horary is commonly presented as being aspect driven. Find your significators, find an aspect between them, and there you have a Yes to the question. This works fine – so long as you don’t mind being consistently wrong in your judgements. 卜卦占星常被简单地表述为以相位驱动。找到你的征象星，找到它们之间的一个 相位，于是你对问题就有了肯定的答案。这样做也行——只要你不介意自己的判 断一错再错。

The aspect is an important part of judgement, but it is only a part. What the aspect provides is the occasion for an event to take place. No occasion: no event. That is clear enough; but we can have an occasion without an event, or without the event turning out as we wish. We have the occasion: I ask her to marry me; but she can’t stand me, so she says ‘No’. Occasion alone does not give us a full answer. 相位是判断的重要组成部分，但仅仅是其中一部分。相位所提供的是事件发生的 契机。没有契机：就没有事件。这足够清楚；但我们可能拥有契机却没有事件发 生，或者事件的结果不如我们所愿。我们拥有契机：我向她求婚；但她无法忍受 我，于是她说“不”。仅有契机并不能给我们完整的答案。

For this reason, dignity and reception are of supreme importance. They are the twin keys to judgement. 因此，尊贵与接纳关系至关重要。它们是判断的双重关键。

Dignity shows power to act 尊贵显示行动的能力

Reception shows inclination to act 接纳关系显示行动的意愿

Aspect shows occasion to act. 相位显示行动的契机。

There is a clear theoretical distinction between essential and accidental dignity. In theory it is accidental dignity that shows the power to act, while essential dignity shows how pure is the motive behind this action. We do not live in a theoretical world, however, so in practice this distinction is often blurred, even to the extent of

disappearing altogether. If the context allows an opportunity for this distinction to manifest, it will – for instance in questions about court cases, where the essential dignity shows who is in the right and the accidental considerations show who is going to win. 先天尊贵与偶然尊贵在理论上存在清晰的区别。理论上，偶然尊贵显示的是行动 的能力，而先天尊贵则显示此行动背后动机的纯粹程度。然而，我们并非生活在 一个纯粹理论的世界中，因此在实践中，这种区别常常是模糊的，甚至可能完全 消失。如果具体情境允许这种区别显现出来，它便会显现——例如在有关法庭案 件的问题中，先天尊贵显示谁在法理上正确，而偶然尊贵的考量则显示谁会获胜。

Accidental dignity is considered in chapter 7, reception in chapter 8. This chapter is one essential dignity. 偶然尊贵在第 7 章探讨，接纳关系在第 8 章探讨。本章则聚焦于先天尊贵。

The word ‘essential’ is used in its strict sense: this is dignity that pertains to the essence of the thing. Essence in from the Latin esse: to be. It is the is-ness of the thing; its being that and no other; the John-ness in me, that makes me me and no one else; the Malinka-ness in my dog that makes her what she is and no thing else; the you-ness in you that is the intangible but so important quality rendering you different from all others who share your race, sex, size, hair-colour, attitudes, etc. The idea of essence is not accepted in the modern world, because we cannot grab a chunk of essence and weigh it or measure it; it is nonetheless, in the common sense of the word, essential. “先天”一词在此取其严格意义：这是属于事物本质的尊贵。本质一词源于拉丁 语“esse”，意为“存在”。它是事物之“所是”；是其成为其自身而非他者的 存在；是我身上的“John（约翰）性”，使我成为我而非他人；是我的狗身上的 “Malinka（玛琳卡）性”，使其成为其自身而非他物；是你身上的“你性”， 这种无形却至关重要的特质，使你不同于所有与你共享种族、性别、体型、发色、 态度等的其他人。本质的概念在现代世界不被接受，因为我们无法抓取一块本质 去称重或测量；然而，就其通常意义而言，它仍是根本性的。

16. For a fuller discussion of essence and its relevance to astrology, see Real Astrology, chapter 7.
16. 关于本质及其与占星学关联的更完整论述，请参阅《Real Astrology》，第七章。

Being created by God, who is infinitely good, all things are created good. This includes planets. Evil is not a thing in itself: it has no essence, no being. It is the absence of good, in the same way that darkness is not a thing in itself, but is the absence of light. So although Saturn and Mars are known as malefics, the Greater and the Lesser Malefic respectively, they are not in their essence malign. We just don’t much like them, even when they are on their best behaviour. Mars, for instance, rules surgery: however necessary surgery might be, it is not pleasant. When Jupiter or Venus – the Greater and the Lesser Benefic – is in detriment or fall there is likely to be a pleasing veneer over something unpleasant or harmful. A question was asked about a woman who had suffered a severe allergic reaction to a soft drink. The drink was signified by Venus in Virgo, the sign of its fall: the drink tasted good (Venus) but was

harmful (in fall). 既然万物皆为至善的上帝所造，则一切事物生而良善。这包括行星。邪恶本身并 非实体：它没有本质，没有存在。它是良善的缺失，正如黑暗本身并非实体，而 是光明的缺失。因此，尽管土星和火星被称为凶星，分别为大凶星和小凶星，它 们的本质并非邪恶。我们只是不太喜欢它们，即便在它们表现最佳时也是如此。 例如，火星守护外科手术：无论手术多么必要，它总不令人愉快。而当木星或金 星——即大吉星与小吉星——处于弱势或落陷时，不愉快或有害的事物上便可能 覆盖着一层悦目的表象。曾有一个关于一位女性对某种软饮料产生严重过敏反应 的问题。该饮料由处于处女座（其落陷位置）的金星征象：饮料口感上佳（金星）， 但却有害（处于落陷）。

The more essential dignity a planet has, the better it conforms to its innate good nature, and so is able to show itself at its best. The more debilitated it is, the more it is deformed from this innate goodness, and so manifests its nastier sider. This is true of any planet: 行星拥有的先天尊贵越多，就越能契合其天生的良善本性，从而能展现其最佳状 态。它越是衰弱，就越是偏离这种天生的良善，从而表现出其更恶劣的一面。这 对任何行星都适用：

Any planet in its detriment or fall can be malign. 任何处于其失势或落陷位置的行星都可能为凶。

Any planet in its sign or exaltation can behave well. 任何处于其入庙或旺势位置的行星都可能为吉。

This is one of the most important rules in astrology. Although it is usual to call Jupiter and Venus benefics and Saturn and Mars malefics, I urge you to treat any planet that is essentially debilitated as malefic, any planet that is essentially strong as benefic. 这是占星学中最重要的规则之一。尽管通常将木星与金星称作吉星，土星与火星 称作凶星，但我强烈建议你将任何先天衰弱的行星视为凶星，任何先天强旺的行 星视为吉星。

### ✸ Our forebears, such as Lilly, were stuck on the idea that Mars and Saturn are

always malefic, Venus and Jupiter always benefic. Despite the paragraph above, I was still slipping into this usage when I wrote this book. For instance, on the first page I write, ‘Signified by a strongly dignified benefic, the cat is doing just fine’. But Puss would have been just as fine if he had been signified by a strongly dignified Saturn. Again, the planets are only the actors; what interests us is the role. The actor who plays Macbeth could be lovely guy, but this has no relevance to what unfolds on stage. ✷

### ✸我们的先辈，例如 Lilly，固守于火星和土星永远是凶星、金星和木星永远是

吉星的观念。尽管有上一段的说明，我在撰写本书时仍不自觉地沿用了这种说法。

例如，在第一页我写道：“由一颗强旺的吉星所征象，这只猫过得很好。”但如 果猫咪由一颗强旺的土星征象，它同样会过得很好。重申一遍，行星只是演员； 我们关注的是角色。扮演 Macbeth（麦克白）的演员可能是个很好的人，但这与 舞台上展开的情节无关。✷

This strength or weakness is usually contained within the context of the question. A querent asked ‘Will I get this job?’ and was signified by Saturn retrograde in Aries. Our first thought might well be, ‘Would anyone employ Saturn retrograde in its fall?’ and this first thought is an important testimony. But it does not mean that our querent is an evil person; it means that she is in a mess, may well be applying for the job out of desperation, and is probably little qualified to do it. Always read testimonies in context. Similarly another querent asked when she would find her next boyfriend. Her significators were Venus in Taurus and the Moon in Cancer. This does not mean that she was a candidate for sainthood, only that she was very good-looking and knew it. Context, again. 这种强旺或衰弱通常蕴含在问题本身的语境之中。一位问卜者问“我能得到这份 工作吗？”，其征象星是位于白羊座且逆行的土星。我们最初的想法很可能是： “有人会聘用一颗处于落陷且逆行的土星吗？”而这最初的想法就是一个重要的 征象。但这并不意味着我们的问卜者是个邪恶之人；它意味着她处境混乱，很可 能出于绝望才申请这份工作，并且可能几乎无法胜任。永远要在具体语境中解读 征象。类似地，另一位问卜者问她何时能找到下一任男友。她的征象星是位于金 牛座的金星和位于巨蟹座的月亮。这并不意味着她是圣徒的候选人，只表明她非 常漂亮并且自知这一点。再次强调，语境至关重要。

A direct descriptive relevance within the context can override the positive or negative indications of an dignity or debility, whether essential or accidental. A lost umbrella was signified by Saturn in Cancer. This is a perfect description of the object: it is a barrier (Saturn). What sort of barrier? A wet sort of barrier (Cancer). Even though Saturn is in its detriment, this placement can be taken as descriptive and does not mean it was a decrepit umbrella. 在具体语境中，一种直接的描述性关联可以覆盖尊贵或衰弱（无论是先天的还 是偶然的）通常所暗示的正面或负面征象。一把丢失的伞由巨蟹座的土星征象。 这是对该物品的完美描述：它是一个屏障（土星）。什么样的屏障？一种潮湿的 屏障（巨蟹座）。尽管土星处于其失势位置，但这一位置可被视为描述性的，并 不意味着那是一把破旧的伞。

Another example: Jupiter in Pisces is a strongly dignified benefic. But if I ask what the weather will be at the beach, Jupiter, god of rain, in watery Pisces would be a malefic within the context of my question. 另一个例子：木星在双鱼座是一个强旺的吉星。但如果我问海滩上的天气如何， 作为雨神的木星落在水象的双鱼座，在我的问题语境中就会成为凶星。

The essential dignities and debilities of the planets are given in the following table. Planets gain dignity or debility by being in certain signs or in certain parts of signs.

Let us work through this table from left to right. Don’t worry – you don’t need to memorise it! You will find it is worth knowing the major dignities and debilities by heart; the terms and faces will begin to stick over time. 行星的先天尊贵和衰弱如下表所示。行星通过位于特定星座或星座的特定部分获 得尊贵或衰弱。让我们从左到右了解这个表格。别担心——你不需要记忆它！你 会发现记住主要的尊贵与衰弱，是值得的；得界与得面会随着时间的推移逐渐熟 悉。

Sign rulership 星座守护星（入庙）

Being in its own sign is the strongest essential dignity. Example: Mars in Aries, Jupiter in Pisces. This is likened to a man being in his own home, in the sense of ‘an Englishman’s home is his castle’. He is the master there, able to order every-thing as he wishes, and so is content. Such a planet is well able to manifest its essential goodness. Old texts often have a D or an N next to the planetary glyph in this column, standing for Day or Night. The distinction between a planet’s day sign and its night sign is, however, of purely theoretical significance: it has no use in practice and

should be ignored. 处于其入庙星座是最强的先天尊贵。例如：火星在白羊座，木星在双鱼座。这好 比一个人待在自己家里，正如“英国人的家就是他的城堡”。他是那里的主人， 能够随心所欲地安排一切，因此心满意足。这样的行星能充分展现其先天的良善。 古代文献常在此栏的行星符号旁标注 D 或 N，代表昼星或夜星。然而，行星的 昼间星座与夜间星座之分仅有理论意义：实践中并无用处，应予以忽略。

Exaltation 擢升（旺势）

Each planet is exalted in one sign; some signs have no planet exalted. Examples: Venus is exalted in Pisces, Saturn in Libra.
