A planet in its exaltation is likened to an honoured guest in someone’s home. In some ways the honoured guest is better off than the master of the house: the guest is given the best of everything – he doesn’t get last night’s dinner warmed up again for this lunch. But there are limits to this strength: the guest cannot wander into the bedroom and start sorting through the cupboards. With the honoured guest, there is a sense of exaggeration: we treat him better than he could ever deserve. This sense of exaggeration is important to an understanding of exaltation. 每个行星在一个星座中拥有旺势；有些星座没有行星旺势。例如：金星在双鱼座 旺势，土星在天秤座旺势。处于旺势的行星被比作某人家中尊贵的客人。在某些 方面，这位尊贵的客人比房子的主人过得更好：客人得到最好的款待——他不会 吃到昨晚的剩菜重新加热当作午餐。但这种力量有限制：客人不能随意走进卧室， 开始翻找橱柜。对于尊贵的客人，存在一种夸张感：我们对待他的方式好到他自 己都配不上。这种夸张感对于理解旺势至关重要。

Consider a cat preparing to fight. He puffs himself up. This doesn’t make hime any stronger, but it makes him look stronger. He is exalting himself. It is as if the person shown by the planet in exaltation is pretending to be a better version fo himself than he is usually able to be. A planet in its own sign is stronger than a planet in its exaltation – except in one specific circumstance. In a question about a contest of any kind, a planet in its exaltation trumps one in its own sign. As the cat knows, it’s not only how tough you are, but how tough you look. 想象一只准备打架的猫。它会让自己炸毛。这并不能让它真正变得更强壮，但却 让它看起来更强壮。它是在抬高自己。这就好比，由一颗处于旺势的行星所代表 的人，正在假装成为一个比平时能力所及的、更好的自己。一颗处于其入庙位置 的行星比一颗处于旺势的行星更强——除了一种特定情况。在任何类型的竞争问 题中，处于旺势的行星会胜过处于入庙位置的行星。正如猫所知道的，重要的不 仅是你有多强悍，而是你看起来有多强悍。

Be careful not to exaggerate this sense of exaggeration. Exaltation is very good; it just isn’t quite as good as it makes out. Students sometimes overstate this falling short,

making exaltation almost into a debility. It is not: it is most strengthening. Example: the querent’s favourite team had been playing above itself, reaching an unexpectedly high position in the league. The team’s significator was a planet in its exaltation: very good – but appearing better than it really is. 请注意，不要过度夸大这种夸张感。旺势是非常好的；它只是没有它所表现出来 的那么好。学生有时会夸大这种“不及”，几乎将旺势当作一种衰弱。它不是： 它是非常强旺的。示例：问卜者最喜欢的球队一直表现超出自身水平，在联赛中 达到了意外的高位。该球队的征象星是一颗处于旺势的行星：非常好——但看起 来比实际更好。

A planet is exalted all the way through its exaltation sign (so the Sun is exalted anywhere in Aries), but there is one degree where it is super-exalted. This is called its exaltation degree, and is shown by the number next to the planetary glyphs in the exaltation column of the table. NB: this number is an ordinal, not a cardinal, so the Sun is super-exalted in the 19th degree of Aries (18.00-18.59) not at 19.00-19.59; the Moon is super-exalted in the 3rd degree of Taurus (2.00-2.59) not 3.00-3.59. ‘Will I make the team?’ with your planet in its exaltation degree: you’ll make the team and be named captain. 行星在其整个旺势星座中都处于旺势状态（因此太阳在白羊座的任何位置都旺 势），但有一个度数让它处于最强旺势。这被称为其强旺度数，在表格的旺势一 栏中，它由行星符号旁边的数字标示。注意：此数字是序数，而非基数，因此太 阳在白羊座 19 度（即 18.00-18.59 度）最强旺势，而非在 19.00-19.59 度；月亮 在金牛座 3 度（即 2.00-2.59 度）最强旺势，而非 3.00-3.59 度。如果你的行星位 于其强旺度数时提出“我能入选队伍吗？”：你不仅能入选，还会被任命为队长。

There is no practical significance in the exaltation of the Nodes. 月交点的旺势没有实际意义。

Triplicity 三分

The signs divide into four groups of three (hence ‘triplicity’): earth, air, fire and water. Each element has its own rulers. You see that the triplicity column is divided into two: there is a different ruler by day and by night. 星座分为四组，每组三个（因此称为“三分”）：土、风、火、水。每个元素有 其各自的守护星。可以看到三分这一栏分为两部分：日间与夜间的守护星不同。

“How do I know which one to use? ”Look at the chart you are judging. The line joining the Ascendant to the Descendant represents the horizon. If the Sun is above the horizon (in houses 7-12) it is daytime; if the Sun is below the horizon (in houses 1-6), it is night. Allow a few degrees in favour of day at either end, so if the Sun is only a couple of degrees below the Ascendant or the Descendant you will count it as

day. This is because the Sun’s light is visible before the Sun rises and after it sets. ‘A few’ degree is all the precision necessary here: the precise number varies with latitude and time of year. “我该如何知道该用哪一个？”查看你正在判断的星盘。连接上升点与下降点的 轴线代表地平线。如果太阳位于地平线之上（在 7 宫至 12 宫），则为日生盘； 如果太阳位于地平线之下（在 1 宫至 6 宫），则为夜生盘。在两端可允许几度的 偏差以倾向于日间，因此，如果太阳仅位于上升点或下降点之下几度，仍应视为 日间。这是因为太阳的光芒在其升起前与落下后仍可见。此处只需“几度”的精 度即可：具体的度数随纬度和季节变化。

The fire signs (Aries, Leo, Sagittarius) are ruled by the Sun by day and Jupiter by night. Earth signs (Taurus, Virgo, Capricorn) by Venus by day, the Moon by night. Air signs (Gemini, Libra and Aquarius) by Saturn by day and Mercury by night. The water signs (Cancer, Scorpio, Pisces) have Mars as their ruler by day and by night. 火象星座（白羊座、狮子座、射手座）日间由太阳守护，夜间由木星守护。土象 星座（金牛座、处女座、摩羯座）日间由金星守护，夜间由月亮守护。风象星座 （双子座、天秤座和水瓶座）日间由土星守护，夜间由水星守护。水象星座（巨 蟹座、天蝎座、双鱼座）日间与夜间均由火星守护。

“But what has Mars got to do with water?”The water in the water signs is not sweet water, but is the ocean: wild, tempestuous, untameable. It is our desire nature – hence the connection with Mars. “但火星与水有什么关系呢？”水象星座中的水并非甘泉之水，而是海洋：狂野、 汹涌、不可驯服。它代表我们的欲望本性——因此与火星相关联。

A planet in its own triplicity (such as Jupiter in a fire sign in a night chart or Venus in an earth sign in a daytime chart) is comfortable. It is literally ‘in its element’. Things could be better, but they’re pretty good right now. It is in its comfort zone. It is moderately strong, so we have a moderately good version of that planet. 一颗行星位于其自身的三分主星位置（例如在夜生盘的火象星座中的木星，或在 日生盘的土象星座中的金星）会感到舒适。这可谓“处于其本元之中”。情况本 可以更好，但目前已经相当不错。它处于舒适区。它具有中等强度，因此我们得 到的是该行星中等良好的表现。

There is another system of triplicity rulers which gives each element three rulers. Both systems date back to antiquity: the idea that the two-ruler system is a modern usurper is erroneous. The 3-ruler system has certain specific uses when judging the natal chart; it is the 2-ruler system, as discussed here, that is to be used for horary. 此外，另有一种三分主星系统，为每个元素分配三个守护星。这两种系统均可追 溯至古代：认为两守护星系统是现代篡改者的观点是错误的。三守护星系统在判 断本命盘时有某些特定用途；而如这里所讨论的，用于卜卦占星的应是两守护星 系统。

Term 界

The next section of the chart divides each sign into five unequal chunks, called terms. The Sun and Moon do not rule any terms; each of the other planets rules a term in each sign. ‘Term’ means boundary, as in the words terminus or terminate. The terms are sometimes called ‘bounds’. 星盘的下一部分将每个星座划分为五个不等份，称为得界。太阳与月亮不主宰任 何得界；其他每颗行星在每个星座中主宰一个得界。“Term”意为边界，如同词 语“终点”或“终止”所示。得界有时也被称为“界”。

The numbers show where the term or bound of each planet’s little chunk of power is. As with the exaltation degrees, these numbers are ordinals, nor cardinals. Look at the Aries row in the table. The first term is ruled by Jupiter, whose bound is the 6th degree: Jupiter rules this part of Aries up to the end of the 6th degree, which is 5.59 degrees of Aries. Venus takes over from 6.00 degrees until the end of the 14th degree, which is 13.59. Then Mercury’s section runs from 14.00 to 20.59; Mars’ from 21.00 to 25.59; Saturn’s from 26.00 to 29.59. A planet must be in its own little chunk of the sign to be dignified by term. Example: at 7.30degrees of Taurus, Venus is in its own sign, its own triplicity (if it is a daytime chart) and in its own term. At 8.30 Taurus it is in its own sign, its own triplicity (in a daytime chart) and is not in its term. 数字显示每颗行星所掌管的得界（或称界）的权力范围。与强旺度数一样，这些 数字是序数，而非基数。查看表格中白羊座所在的行。第一个得界由木星主宰， 其边界是第 6 度：木星主宰白羊座的这一部分直到第 6 度末，即白羊座 5.59 度。 金星从 6.00 度开始接管，直到第 14 度末，即 13.59 度。然后水星的得界从 14.00 度到 20.59 度；火星的从 21.00 度到 25.59 度；土星的从 26.00 度到 29.59 度。一 颗行星必须位于其所主宰的星座的特定得界范围内，才能获得得界带来的尊贵。 例如：在金牛座 7.30 度，金星处于其入庙位置、其自身的三分主星位置（如果 是一张日生盘）以及其自身的得界。在金牛座 8.30 度，它虽处于入庙位置及其 自身的三分主星位置（在一张日生盘中），但不在其得界之内。

The term rulers can be likened to the non-commissioned officers in an army. They have a small amount of power, but nothing so glorious as the officers (major dignities). Still, it is much better being a corporal than being a private (no dignity at all). The terms find their greatest importance when we are progressing the natal chart. In horary they are not so much a positive factor as the absence of a negative. As being a corporal is not so wonderful, but is better than being a private, so a planet in its term is not so strong, but is better than if it has no dignity are all. It is a very minor positive. 界主星可以比作军队中的士官。他们拥有少量权力，但远不及军官（重要尊贵） 那样显赫。然而，当下士总比当列兵（毫无尊贵）要好得多。得界在我们进行本 命盘推运时最为重要。在卜卦占星中，它与其说是一个积极因素，不如说是一种 消极因素的缺失。正如当下士并不那么了不起，但总比当列兵要好；因此，一颗

行星处于其得界虽不算很强，但比它没有任何尊贵要好。这是一个非常轻微的积 极因素。

I have never seen a convincing explanation of why the terms are as they are. There are several rival arrangements. This one works. 我从未见过关于“得界”为何如此划分的令人信服的解释。存在数个不同版本， 但当前这套体系行之有效。

Face 面

Term is a very minor positiver; face is even more minor. The faces divide each sign into three equal chunks of 10 degrees each. The numbers, which are again ordinal, show the boundary of each face. Following along the Aries row, the first face of Aries is ruled by Mars. Mars’s face finishes at 9.59 Aries, when the Sun takes over from 10.00 till 19.59, when Venus takes over from 20.00 to 29.59. 得界是一种非常轻微的积极因素；得面则更为次要。得面将每个星座平分为三个 10 度的区间。数字（再次强调，是序数）显示每个得面的边界。沿着白羊座所 在行看，白羊座的第一个得面由火星主宰。火星的得面结束于白羊座 9.59 度， 随后太阳从 10.00 度接管到 19.59 度，之后金星从 20.00 度接管到 29.59 度。

A planet in its own face is likened to a man in the porch of his house before being thrown out into the street. His position is not good, but it is better than being out in the wind and the rain: better dignity by face than no dignity at all. 一颗行星处于其自身的得面，好比一个人在被扔到大街上之前，还站在自家门廊 上。他的处境并不好，但总比直接暴露在风雨中要强：拥有得面的尊贵聊胜于无。

Detriment 落陷

A planet in the sign opposite the rules is in its detriment (e.g. Mars in Libra, Venus in Scorpio). It is severly debilitated. This speaks badly of whatever is signified by that planet, in a way determined by the context. For example, if a man with a serious illness is signified by a planet in its detriment this shows that he is badly ill, not that he is a wicked person. 一颗行星处于与其守护星相对的星座时，便处于落陷状态（例如火星在天秤座， 金星在天蝎座）。它严重衰弱。此时行星受克严重，其象征的事物将呈现凶兆， 具体应验方式需结合星盘语境判断。例如，若一位重病之人由一颗处于落陷的行 星征象，这表明他病情危重，而非意指他是个邪恶之人。

Fall 弱势

A planet in the sign opposite its own exaltation is in its fall. At the degree exactly opposite its exaltation degree it has the degree of its fall, where it is super-debilitated. Just as exaltation carries the sense of exaggeration, so does fall. With fall it is exaggerated badness. Whether this is better or worse than detriment depends on the context: it can be reassuring to know that the situation is not as dire as you fear. With the planet in its detriment, things look bad and they really are as bad as they seem. With the planet in fall, things seem worse than they are – but they are still bad. There are many contexts in which the idea of “fall” can be taken literally. 当一颗行星位于其自身旺势星座的对宫星座时，即处于弱势状态。在恰好与其强 旺度数相对的度数上，它会达到其弱势度数，此时处于超级衰弱状态。正如旺势 带有一种夸张感，弱势也是如此。处于弱势意味着一种被夸大的恶劣性。这比失 势更好还是更糟，取决于具体语境：有时知道情况并不像你害怕的那么可怕，反 而令人安心。当行星处于落陷时，情况看起来很糟，而事实也确实如看上去那样 糟糕。当行星处于弱势时，情况似乎比实际更糟——但它仍然很糟。在许多语境 中，“弱势”这个概念可以按其字面意义“落下”理解。

### ✸Ibn Ezra calls the sign of a planet’s fall ‘the house of its dishonour’. This can

sometimes be a relevant reading.✷

### ✸Ibn Ezra（伊本·埃兹拉）将行星处于其弱势的星座称为“其失势之宫”。这

种解读有时颇为贴切。✷

NB：it is common to speak of planets in their detriment or fall as ‘weak’. In terms of how much essential dignity they have, yes, they are weak. But this does not translate into wekness of action. In detriment or fall they are nasty or unhappy; whether the are strong or weak – able or not able to act – is shown by accidental dignities more than essential dignities. 注意：通常人们会说处于落陷或弱势的行星是“弱”的。就它们拥有的先天尊贵 多寡而言，是的，它们确实弱。但这并不一定意味着行动能力的虚弱。在落陷或 弱势时，它们表现为恶劣或不幸；至于它们是强是弱——即是否有能力行动—— 更多地是由偶然尊贵而非先天尊贵来显示的。

Peregrine 游离

A planet that is not in any of its own dignities, nor in its detriment or fall, is peregrine.

It is likened to a homeless wanderer, drifting. Bonatti says that this signifies ‘one that shall know how to act both good and evil, but be more inclinable to the latter’.It lacks the moral direction implicit in essential dignity (behaving well) and even that implicit in essential debility (behaving badly); it is rudderless. But, by the nature of things, he who is drifting is more likely to fall into doing evil than into doing good. 当一颗行星不处于其任何先天尊贵，也不在失势或弱势状态时，即为游离状态。 它被比作无家可归的流浪者，漂泊无依。Bonatti（博纳提）指出，这象征“一个 知晓如何行善亦能作恶，却更易倾向后者之人”。它缺乏先天尊贵所隐含的道德 导向（行为良善），甚至缺乏先天无力所隐含的导向（行为恶劣）；它是无舵的。 然而，依事物的本性，漂泊者更易陷入作恶，而非行善。

17. Bonatus, aphorism 55.
17. Bonatus，格言 55.

Being in mutual reception does not stop a planet being peregrine: essential dignity cannot be transferred from one planet to another. 处于互溶状态并不影响一颗行星是游离的：先天尊贵无法从一颗行星转移至另一 颗行星。

As ever, the context may give a benign meaning to being peregrine. If someone is on a long journey he would be aptly described by a planet peregrine. So would someone casting about looking for a job or a home. 与往常一样，具体语境可能赋予游离状态以良性的含义。如果某人正在长途旅行， 用一颗游离的行星来描述他是恰如其分的。同样，对于正在四处寻找工作或住所 的人也是如此。

18. My understanding of peregrine has clarified since I wrote The Real Astrology (see p.81). The best description of what it is to be peregrine is in canto III of Dante’s Inferno.
18. 我对于“游离”状态的理解，在撰写的《The Real Astrology》（见 81 页）。（参见第 81 页）之后已更为清晰。关于“游离”状态的最佳描述，见于 Dante（但丁）的《Inferno（地 狱篇）》第三章。

Almuten 宫神星

Every degree has its almuten. This is the planet with most essential dignity in that degree. By extension, this planet is said to be the almuten of anyting that is in that degree, such as another planet, a house-cusp or an Arabian Part. 每个度数都有其宫神星。这是在该度数中拥有最多先天尊贵的行星。延伸开来， 该行星被称为位于该度数任何事物（例如另一颗行星、一个宫头或一个阿拉伯点） 的宫神星。

To calculate the almuten, add the various planetary dignities in that degree, scoring 5 for sign, 4 for exaltation, 3 for triplicity, 2 for term, 1 for face. Example: what is the almuten of 5 Libra in daytime chart? Venus scores 5 as it is the sign-ruler. Saturn scores 4 for its exaltation, 3 for being triplicity ruler and 2 for being term ruler: total 9. The Moon scores 1 for being face ruler. Saturn scores the most, so is almuten. 计算宫神星时，需将该度数中的各项行星尊贵度评分相加：入庙得 5 分，旺势得 4 分，三分得 3 分，得界得 2 分，得面得 1 分。例如：在一张日生盘中，天秤座 5 度的宫神星是什么？金星作为星座守护星得 5 分。土星因其旺势得 4 分、作为 三分主星得 3 分、作为得界主星得 2 分：总计 9 分。月亮作为得面主星得 1 分。 土星得分最高，因此为宫神星。

In many degrees there are two or even three planets which have equal claim to being almuten. Choose the one that is strongest in that particular chart. For instance, prefer the one on the MC to the one in the 12th house. Or if one is in close aspect to the Ascendant, use that. 当某一度数中有两颗甚至三颗行星具有同等资格成为宫神星时，应选择在该特定 星盘中力量最强的那一颗。例如，优先考虑位于中天附近的，而非位于 12 宫的。 或者，若其中一颗与上升点形成紧密相位，则选用该颗。

There is only one use for almuten in horary, and that a rare one. Taking the almuten of a cusp is one of our options when we cannot use the house-ruler as significator of that house. 在卜卦占星中，宫神星仅有一种用途，且极少使用：当无法以宫主星作为该宫的 征象星时，取用该宫头的宫神星是备选方案之一。

### ✸I would now strongly urge that there is not even this use for almuten in either

horary or in any other branch of astrology. The idea of almuten lacks all sense. First, we cannot add dignities on this scale of 54321, because dignities are not a matter of a greater or lesser amount of the same thing (e.g. that exaltation is the same as term, but doubled); they are different in quality. Things that are different in quality cannot be added: 2 apples + 2 apples = 4 apples, but 2 apples + 2 tables = 2 apples + 2 tables. Second, the dignities differ greatly in their strength. Sign rulership and exaltation are both hugely stronger than triplicity rulership, which is itself hugely stronger than term or face. Consider: suppose we have a general (sign ruler) arguing with a sergeant and a corporal (triplicity and term rulers). Who will win? The general, of course. But according to the theory of almuten they are equal in strength.

### ✸如今，我强烈主张，不仅在卜卦占星学，而且在占星学的任何其他分支中，

宫神星甚至连这一用途都不存在。宫神星这一概念完全不合逻辑。首先，我们无 法按照 5-4-3-2-1 的评分来累加尊贵，因为尊贵并非同种事物在数量上的多寡（例 如，旺势并非等同于得界的两倍）；它们在性质上是不同的。性质不同的事物不 能简单相加：2 个苹果 + 2 个苹果 = 4 个苹果，但 2 个苹果 + 2 张桌子 = 2 个苹 果 + 2 张桌子。其次，各种尊贵的强度差异巨大。星座守护和旺势两者，远比三

分主星强得多，而三分主星本身又远比得界或得面强大。试想：假设一位将军（星 座守护星）与一位士官和一位下士（三分主星和得界主星）发生争执。谁会赢？ 当然是将军。但按照宫神星的理论，他们的力量却是相等的。

So why does this nonsensical theory exist? It is one more way of giving the astrologer a Plan B. ‘Oh dear, she doesn’t love you. Ah, but wait a minute – if we look at your almuten…!’✷ 那么，为何这种不合逻辑的理论会存在？这不过是给占星师提供 B 计划的又一 种方式。“哎呀，她不爱你。啊，但请稍等——如果我们看看你的宫神星……！” ✷

Dispositor 定位星

The dispositor of a planet or Arabian Part is the ruler of the sign in which that planet or Part is. So anything in Aries is disposited by Mars, anything in Taurus by Venus. Mars disposes of anything in Aries, Venus of anyting in Taurus. In the texts you will sometimes come across disposition by other dignities: Saturn disposits anyting in Libra by exaltation. In such cases the dignity is always mentioned. 行星或阿拉伯点的守护星，是指该行星或阿拉伯点所在星座的守护星。因此，任 何在白羊座的事物都由火星守护，任何在金牛座的事物由金星守护。火星守护白 羊座内的任何事物，金星守护金牛座内的任何事物。在典籍中，你有时会遇到基 于其他尊贵的守护关系：土星因其旺势而守护天秤座内的任何事物。在此类情况 下，总会明确指出其依据的尊贵类型。

### ✸This word is now obsolete in English, beyond its astrological usage, but means

simply ‘the one in charge of’ or ‘the boss’. I was amused to find that the manager of the car-park at Warsaw airport is the dyspositor parkingu.✷

### ✸该词在英语中现已过时，仅保留其占星学用法，其含义简单来说就是“负责

人”或“上司”。我饶有兴味地发现，华沙机场停车场的经理被称为 dyspositor parkingu（停车场管理人）。✷

How much dignity? 尊贵的程度

Dignities are cumulative. The Sun is exalted in Aries. In a daytime chart the Sun in Aries is also in its own triplicity; so it has more dignity by day in Aries then it does by night, when it does not also have the triplicity rulership.

尊贵可以叠加。太阳在白羊座处于旺势。在一张日生盘中，位于白羊座的太阳同 时也处于其自身三分主星的位置；因此，太阳在白羊座日间比夜间拥有更多的尊 贵，因为在夜间它不兼有三分主星的地位。

Although the scoring of 5-4-3-2-1 is adequate for determining almutens, it does not accurately reflect the relative strengths of the dignities. Sign-rulership and exaltation (and also detriment and fall) are very much stronger than triplicity, which is itself very much stronger than term and face. There is not a way of accurately measuring how much dignity a planet has. This lack is not important: we are doing astrology, not arithmetic. In published horaries you will sometimes read statements such as ‘Jupiter has a strength of 10’ This is meaningless. 10 what? In practice, counting dignity as ‘lots’, ‘some’ or ‘a little’ is accurate enough. 尽管 5-4-3-2-1 的评分体系足以确定宫神星，但它并不能准确反映各种尊贵的相 对强度。星座守护与旺势（以及失势与弱势）远比三分主星强大，而三分主星本 身又远比得界和得面强大。目前尚无精确测量一颗行星拥有多少尊贵的方法。但 这种缺失并不重要：我们从事的是占星学，而非算术。在已发表的卜卦案例中， 你有时会读到诸如“木星拥有 10 点强度”的陈述，这毫无意义。10 点是什么？ 在实践中，将尊贵程度描述为“很多”、“一些”或“一点”已是足够准确。

Contradictions 矛盾性

You may have noticed that there are apparent contradictions in the Table of Dignities. Mars, for instance, is in its fall in Cancer, yet it is also triplicity-ruler. Venus is in its fall in Virgo, yet in a day chart it too is triplicity ruler. There are many others. This is not contradictory, because the dignities differ in their quality, not only in their strength, so strength is not given with one hand and taken away with the other. Such apparent contradictions reflect ambiguities that are part of daily life: things are not always all good or all bad. 你或许已经注意到，在《尊贵表》中存在一些表面上的矛盾。例如，火星在巨蟹 座处于其弱势，却又是三分主星。金星在处女座处于其弱势，但在日生盘中也是 三分主星。此类情况还有很多。这并不矛盾，因为各种尊贵的性质不同，不仅仅 在于强度，所以并非一手给予强度，另一手又将其夺走。这些表面上的矛盾反映 了日常生活中固有的模糊性：事物并非总是全好或全坏。

Example: a querent asked about her son’s drug habit. The boy was signified by Mars, which was in Cancer – appropriately enough, as the Moon is natual ruler of all intoxicants. Mars is in its triplicity: it is comfortable there. This is only reasonable: if the boy is taking the drugs, it is probable that he likes them. Mars is also in it fall: he is being harmed by them. Fall is far stronger a negative than triplicity rulership is a positive, so the harm outweighs the pleasure. But it is fall, with its sense of exaggerated badness, not detriment: he is being harmed, but not as much as the

querent fears. 例如：一位问卜者询问她儿子的吸毒习惯。男孩由火星征象，火星位于巨蟹座— —这相当贴切，因为月亮是所有致瘾物的先天守护星。火星处于其三分主星的位 置：它在那里感到舒适。这很合理：如果男孩在吸毒，他很可能喜欢这样。火星 同时也处于其弱势：他正因此受到伤害。弱势作为负面因素的强度，远超过三分 主星作为正面因素的强度，因此危害大于快感。但这是弱势，带有其“夸张的恶 劣性”之感，而非失势：他正在受到伤害，但程度并不如问卜者所恐惧的那样严 重。

When lecturing, I find a couple of examples helpful in explaining how dignity works. Imagine that you own a Las Vegas casino. You are sitting in your office, enjoying the feeling of well-being that comes from sitting in your own successful enterprise as you savour a bourbon and a fine cigar. You are in your own sign, so you are able to manifest your best qualities. So when the croupier timidly knocks on your door and apologetically explains that he has dropped $50,000 on the last spin of the wheel, you smile understandingly and toss him the key to the safe. But next morning you awake to find a horse’s head in your bed. You are no longer the secure ruler of all you survey: you are not only no longer in your own sign, but have entered your detriment. In your desperation to save your skin, you will not manifest your best qualities. So when the croupier apologetically explains that he has dropped another $50,00, you snap your fingers and send hime to sleep with the fishes. 在讲课时，我发现用几个例子有助于解释尊贵的运作方式。想象你拥有一家拉斯 维加斯赌场。你坐在自己的办公室里，品味着波本威士忌和优质雪茄，享受身处 于自己成功事业中的那份悠然自得。你正处在“入庙”状态，因此能够展现出自 己最佳的品质。所以，当赌台管理员怯生生地敲响你的门，满怀歉意地解释他在 最后一轮轮盘赌中输掉了五万美元时，你报以理解的微笑，并把保险柜钥匙扔给 了他。但第二天早晨醒来，你发现床上放着一个马头。你已不再是所掌控领域内 安稳无虞的统治者：你不仅不再处于“入庙”状态，更是进入了“落陷”的境地。 在拼命保命的绝望中，你将无法展现出自己最佳的品质。所以，当赌台管理员再 次歉疚地解释他又输掉了五万美元时，你打了个响指，便将他送入了海底长眠。

Or consider the typical Sunsign idea of a Libran living-room: all scrupulously neat and tidy, with delicate knick-knacks and every cushion placed just so. Along comes Mars, in the person of Charles Bronson. Placed in that living-room, he will be in an alien environment: he is in his detriment. The tension from being so out of place is likely to make him behave badly, exhibiting the worst sides of his Mars nature. 或者，想想典型的太阳星座观念中天秤座的客厅：一切一丝不苟地整洁，精致的 摆件，每个靠垫都摆放得恰到好处。这时，火星来了，以 Charles Bronson（查 尔斯·布朗森）的形象出现。置身于那样的客厅里，他会处于一个格格不入的环 境：他正处在“落陷”状态。这种因与环境极度不符而产生的紧张感，很可能使 他行为恶劣，展现出他火星本性中最糟糕的一面。

This does not mean that Mars is a bad thing. If you were a Mexican villager surrounded by bandits you would be delighted to see Mars, in the person of Charles

Bronson and his magnificent friends, cresting the hill towards you, six-guns blazing. There, Mars is in its right environment and so can behave at its best. You and your fellow villagers would be far less pleased to see Margot Fonteyn and the corps de ballet cresting the hill and coming towards you – even though Venus is nominally a benefic. 这并不意味着火星就是坏的。如果你是一个被土匪包围的墨西哥村民，你会很高 兴看到火星——以 Charles Bronson 及其非凡的伙伴们的形象——出现在山脊 上，六轮手枪火光四射地朝你而来。在那里，火星处于它恰当的环境中，因此能 展现出其最佳状态。而你和你的村民们如果看到 Margot Fonteyn（玛戈特·芳 婷）和芭蕾舞团出现在山脊上朝你们走来，恐怕就不会那么高兴了——即使金星 名义上是一颗吉星。

# Accidental Dignity

# 偶然尊贵

The manager of a football team must choose which of two players to pick for Saturday’s match. Both have lots of essential dignity: they are good players. It is not enough for the manager to consider only how much skill they have: he must consider other factors. One of them knows that a good performance will get him into the England team, so he’s fired up. The other’s mother died last week, so he’s feeling low. One is beginning to show his age and is increasingly slow in motion. The other got kicked last week and hasn’t fully recovered. These factors are accidental dignities and debilities. It is essential that they are considered in judgement. 一位足球队经理必须为周六的比赛在两名球员中选择一人。两人都有很高的先天 尊贵：他们都是优秀球员。但对经理来说，仅考虑他们有多少技术是不够的：他 还必须考虑其他因素。其中一人知道，一场出色的表现能让他入选英格兰队，所 以他斗志昂扬。另一人的母亲上周去世了，因此他情绪低落。一人开始显露年龄， 动作越来越慢。另一人上周被踢伤，尚未完全恢复。这些因素就属于偶然尊贵与 衰弱。在判断中必须考虑它们。

Consider: I am the kindest man in the world – I have lots of essential dignity. But I am locked up in solitary confinement – accidental debility. No matter how kind I am, this accidental debility prevents me from manifesting this kindness, just as accidental factors help or hinder our footballers in playing to their best. In principle, essential dignity tells us whether that planet signifies something good or something bad; accidental dignity tells us whether this thing, good or bad, has power to act. There is a planet right on the Midheaven (strong accidental dignity): it has lots of power to act; it is in the driving-seat. In its own sign: it knows how to drive. In its detriment: it doesn’t know how to driver. But being on the Midheaven, it is still in the driving-seat. 试想：我是世上最善良的人——我拥有极高的先天尊贵。但我被关在单人牢房里 ——这是偶然衰弱。无论我多么善良，这种偶然衰弱都使我无法展现这份善良， 正如偶然因素会帮助或阻碍我们的足球运动员发挥出最佳水平一样。原则上，先 天尊贵告诉我们一颗行星所象征的事物本质上是好是坏；偶然尊贵则告诉我们这 件事——无论好坏——是否有力量去行动。有一颗行星正位于中天（很强的偶然 尊贵）：它拥有很大的行动力量；它正坐在驾驶座上。如果它入庙：它知道如何 驾驶。如果它落陷：它不知道如何驾驶。但由于它位于中天，它依然坐在驾驶座 上。

In practice this distinction between essential and accidental qualities is often blurred,

but starting from this principle and adapting it as necessary will keep you on the right track. 在实际应用中，先天品质与偶然品质之间的区别常常是模糊的，但从这一基本法 则出发，并根据需要对其进行调整，将使你保持在正确的轨道上。

Broadly speaking, the more accidental dignity a planet has, the more able it is to act; the more accidental debilities it has the weaker it is and the less power it has to act. But specific dignities or debilities may or may not be relevant to the issue at hand. My friend has a broken leg, a serious accidental debility. If my question is ‘Will he lend me some money?’ this debility is irrelevant. If my question is ‘Will he play tennis with me?’ it is most relevant. 总的来说，一颗行星拥有的偶然尊贵越多，其行动能力就越强；它拥有的偶然衰 弱越多，其力量就越弱，行动能力也越差。但具体的尊贵或衰弱是否与当前问题 相关，则视情况而定。我的朋友腿骨折了，这是一个严重的偶然衰弱。如果我的 问题是“他会借钱给我吗？”，这个衰弱就无关紧要。如果我的问题是“他会和 我打网球吗？”，那它就至关重要了。

### ✸Do avoid importing the idea of strength to act, or the lack of it, to contexts where

it does no belong. Which is most contexts. If I am asking ‘Will I win the gold medal?’ having power to act is important; if I’m asking ‘What will the weather be tomorrow?’ the concept is irrelevant. Even with ‘With I get the job?’ the reality of the situation is usually that power to act is irrelevant: other than turning up at the interview on time and with my hair combed, there isn’t much I can do. Or with ‘When will the letter arrive?’ No matter how much accidental dignity its significator may have, the letter has no power to act. The chart reflects reality. If something doesn’t make sense in reality, it doesn’t make sense in the chart.✷

### ✸务必避免将“行动力”或其缺失的概念，套用到它并不适用的情境中——这

在大多数情况下都不适用。如果我问“我会赢得金牌吗？”，拥有行动力很重要； 但如果我问“明天天气如何？”，这个概念就无关紧要。即便是“我能得到这份 工作吗？”，实际情况通常也是行动力无关紧要：除了准时出席面试并梳理好头 发，我能做的并不多。或者对于“信什么时候会到？”这样的问题，无论其征象 星拥有多少偶然尊贵，那封信本身都没有行动力。星盘反映现实。如果在现实中 讲不通的事，在星盘中也同样讲不通。✷

Accidental considerations may or may not be cumulative. Common sense will tell you whether they are cumulative in the question under consideration. If our footballer who is slowing down with age is the same one whose mother has died, these debilities may add to each other. But if my trousers are held up with a belt, they are not held up any the more if I add a pair of braces. 偶然因素可能具有累积性，也可能没有。常识会告诉你，在所要考量的问题中它 们是否具有累积性。如果我们那位因年龄增长而动作变慢的足球运动员，正好也 是母亲去世的那位，那么这些衰弱可能会相互叠加。但如果我的裤子是用皮带系

住的，那么即使我再加一副背带，它也不会被系得更牢。

The list of accidental considerations would be inexhaustible, as each question provides its own list of what is favourable and what is not. If the question is ‘Will I become an opera singer?’ finding my significator in mute sign is an accidental debility. If it is ‘Will I make a good mime?’ it would be an accidental dignity. Here is a checklist of useful considerations. I have also discussed some others that can be safely ignored, for completion and because you will come across these terms in other books. The checklist is usually printed with numbers giving each consideration a score. I have omitted these because of the obsession astrologers have with arithmetic. Give an astrologer two numbers and he will immediately add them up. This is most unhelpful. All these numbers do is give a broad guide to the relative strength of these dignities and debilities, and this I shall give below; putting them in the table causes more confusion than it’s worth. 偶然考量的清单是无穷无尽的，因为每个问题都自带一份清单，列明什么有利、 什么不利。如果问题是“我会成为歌剧演唱家吗？”，发现我的征象星位于沉默 星座就是一种偶然衰弱。如果问题是“我会成为一个优秀的默剧演员吗？”，那 它反而是一种偶然尊贵。以下是一份有用的考量要点清单。为了内容的完整性， 并且因为您会在其他书籍中遇到这些术语，我也讨论了一些可以放心忽略的其他 因素。这份清单通常印有数字，为每项考量打分。我省略了这些数字，因为占星 师们对算术太过痴迷。给一个占星师两个数字，他会立刻把它们加起来。这样做 毫无帮助。这些数字唯一的作用是为这些尊贵与衰弱的相对强度提供一个大致指 南，我将在下文给出；把它们放在表格里引起的困惑远比其价值要多。

CHECKLIST OF ACCIDENTAL DIGHITY AND DEBILITY 偶然尊贵和衰弱表

Which house is the planet in? 行星落入哪个宫位？

Is it in its joy? 它在喜悦位置吗？

Is it retrograde? 它正在逆行吗？

Is it fast, slow or in station? 它在加速，减速或者停滞吗？

Is it combust, under the sunbeams, opposing the Sun or cazimi? 它在燃烧，在日光下，对冲太阳或者在日核中吗？

Is it besieged or besieged by the rays? 它受围攻攻或者光线受围攻了吗？

Is it closely aspected? 它有紧密的相位吗？

Is it on one of the Nodes? 它与（南北）交点合相了吗？

Is it on Regulus, Spica or Algol? 它合相于轩辕十四，角宿一，大陵五了吗？

Does the Moon have light? Is it increasing or decreasing in light? 月亮被照亮了吗？它增加或减少光线了吗？

Is the Moon void of course? 月亮空亡了吗？

Is the Moon in the via combusta? 月亮在燃烧之路吗？

You’ll soon find you notice these things almost without thinking. But for now, work through this list methodically.

您很快会发现，您几乎不假思索就能注意到这些因素。但眼下，还请系统地依照 这份清单来推进。

House placement 宫位配置

This is important and must be considered. The general principle is ‘angular houses strong; succedent houses middling; cadent houses weak’. But the 3rd and 9th houses, although cadent, are regarded – for this purpose only – as being honorary succedents, while the 8th house, although succedent, is as weak as the 6th or 12th. 这一点很重要，必须纳入考量。基本法则是：“角宫强；续宫中等；果宫弱”。 但 3 宫和 9 宫，虽属果宫，为此目的被视为名誉上的续宫；而 8 宫虽属续宫，其 力量却与 6 宫或 12 宫一样弱。

Listing the houses in order of power is too precious: the angles are all much the same; the succedents (with their honorary members) are much the same; the candents are much the same. Put simply: 按宫位力量强弱顺序逐一列出未免太过繁琐：所有角宫力量大体相当；所有续宫 （包括其名誉成员）力量大体相当；所有果宫力量也大体相当。简而言之：

* Angular houses strong *角宫强

* 6th, 8th and 12th weak
* 6 宫，8 宫和 12 宫弱

* Others neutral
* 其他宫位中性

The exception to the rule is when the question gives the planet good reason to be in that house. For instance, if I ask ‘Will I recover the money I’ve lent?’ and find Lord 1 in 8th house (2nd from the 7th: the other person’s money), it is not weak there; it is the appropriate place for it because I am thinking of 8th house matters. 此规则有一个例外：当问题本身使行星有充分理由位于该宫位时。例如，如果我 问“我能收回借出的钱吗？”并发现 1 宫主在 8 宫（即 7 宫的 2 宫：他人的钱财）， 那么它在此处并非弱势；相反，这是它应处的位置，因为我正在思考 8 宫相关的 事务。

A planet in an angular house gains more strength the closer it is to the cusp. If a planet is in a house but not in the same sign as the house cusp (e.g. cusp is at 25 Aries, planet is at 4 Taurus) it is as if there is a layer of insulation between the planet and the house. It is not strengthened as much as it would be if it were in that house and also in the

same sign as the cusp. But don’t overstate this: a planet in an angular house but in a different sign is still stronger than one in a succedent house. 位于角宫的行星，越接近宫头，力量越强。如果行星位于某宫但不在该宫宫头的 星座内（例如宫头在牡羊座 25 度，行星在金牛座 4 度），则行星与该宫之间仿 佛存在一层隔阂。其得到的力量增强，不如它既在该宫、又与宫头同星座时那么 大。但不要夸大这一点：一颗在角宫但位于不同星座的行星，仍然比在续宫的行 星更强。

Remember that a planet within around 5 degrees of the next house cusp, and in the same sign as that cusp, is counted as being in that house. 请记住，如果一颗行星距离下一个宫头约 5 度以内，并且与该宫头位于同一星座， 则应被视为已进入该宫。

### ✸Note that most of the time there is no significance in which house a planet is in.

As in the theatre: sometimes it’s important that the actor is in this particular – under the balcony, perhaps, or over a trap-door. But most of the time it doesn’t matter where the actor is, he just has to be standing somewhere. So it is with planets in the chart.✷

### ✸请注意，在大多数情况下，行星位于哪个宫位并无特殊意义。正如在剧院中：

有时演员所处的位置很重要——或许是在阳台下，或是在活板门上。但大多数时 候，演员站在哪里并不重要，他只需要站在某个地方即可。星盘中的行星也是如 此。✷

Joy 喜悦

This is much less significant, but still worth noting. Each planet joys in one of the house: Mercury in the 1st; Moon 3rd; Venus 5th; Mars 6th; Sun 9th; Jupiter 11th; Saturn 12th. It is as if it finds that house a congenial place to hang out. Because it likes being there, feels better about itself there, it has a little more power to act. It is also more likely to act according to its own nature – Mercury will do Mercury–type stuff; Mars will do Mars-type stuff. This idea is very close to that behind the essential dignities. 这一条的重要性要低得多，但仍值得注意。每颗行星在一个宫位中喜乐：水星在 1 宫；月亮在 3 宫；金星在 5 宫；火星在 6 宫；太阳在 9 宫；木星在 11 宫；土 星在 12 宫。这就像是它发现那个宫位是一个宜于停留的舒适之所。因为它喜欢 待在那里，在那里自我感觉更好，所以它的行动力也略强一些。它也更容易按其 自身本性行事——水星会做水星类的事情；火星会做火星类的事情。这一概念与 先天尊贵背后的理念非常接近。

### ✸In most question, joy can safely be ignored. It is useful mostly in horaries where

we need to decide which of two planets is the stronger, such as with questions about contests (‘Will we win the match?’). Even there, other testimonies will usually be sufficiently stronger that joy is not important.✷

### ✸在大多数问题中，喜乐可以放心忽略。它主要在卜卦占星中有用，即当我们

需要判断两颗行星中哪一颗更强时（例如涉及竞争的问题，如“我们会赢得比赛 吗？”）。即便在那里，其他征象通常也足够强大，以至于喜乐并不重要。✷

Retrograde 逆行

Except for the Sun and Moon, all the planets appear from time to time to be going backwards in the sky: they are retrograde. If a significator is retrograde, this must be considered. It may or may not be an affliction; if it is, it is a serious one. 除太阳和月亮外，所有行星都会不时在天空中倒退运行：即发生逆行。如果一颗 征象星正在逆行，这一点必须纳入考量。它可能受到折磨，也可能不是；如果它 受到了折磨，那将是一种严重的折磨。

In many questions retrogradation is exactly what we hope to see: ‘Will I get my old job back?’ ‘Can I get back with Britney?’ ‘Will the cat come home?’ In any circumstance involving returning or going back over something, a significator being retrograde is entirely appropriate, so the retrogradation is not a debility. Even if return is not sought, but still makes sense in context: ‘When will I meet a man?’ and the aspect is to a planet that is retrograde: ‘You’ll get back with an ex’. 在许多问题中，逆行正是我们希望看到的征象：“我能要回原来的工作吗？”“我 能和 Britney（布兰妮）复合吗？”“猫会回家吗？”在任何涉及回归或重蹈覆 辙的情形中，征象星处于逆行状态是完全合适的，因此逆行并非一种衰弱。即使 问题本身不寻求回归，但在语境中仍能讲得通：“我何时会遇到一位男性？”且 相位关联到一颗逆行的行星：“你会与一位前任复合”。

This is an example of what I would call the law of sufficient explanation. If the context of an enquiry explains a debility, it is no debility. 这是我称之为充分解释法则的一个例子：如果查询的背景能够解释某个衰弱，那 它就不再是衰弱。

If there is no such favourable spin given by the context, retrogradation is a problem. The planet is going the wrong way: it is against nature. This is a powerful debility, and, being against nature, things are unlikely to turn out well. Consider: the planet has lots of essential dignity, so he’s one of the good guys. He’s on the Midheaven, so is strongly dignified by house: he has a gun and lots of ammunition. But he’s retrograde:

with the best will in the world, he’s shooting in the wrong direction. 如果没有此类由语境赋予的有利倾向，那么逆行就是个问题。行星在朝错误的方 向运行：它违背了自然之道。这是一种强有力的衰弱，并且由于违背自然，事情 不太可能有好结果。试想：该行星拥有大量的先天尊贵，所以它是“好人”之一。 它位于中天，因此因宫位而获得强烈的尊贵：它有一把枪和充足的弹药。但它正 在逆行：即便怀着世界上最美好的意愿，它也是在朝着错误的方向开枪。

If the planet has only recently turned retrograde, it can be important to consider what it has previously done and is now returning to do again, or what it was about to do but turned away from. Take a look at where it’s been and at where it didn’t go. But: in retrogradation a planet will either conjunct or oppose the Sun, do not look at its actions beyond that. 如果该行星是刚刚转为逆行，那么考量它先前做过什么、现在又返回重做，或者 它原本打算做什么却转而回避，可能会很重要。可以审视它曾经到过的位置以及 它未曾前往的位置。但请注意：在逆行期间，一颗行星必定会与太阳形成合相或 对冲相位，除此之外，不必考察其超出此范围的行动。

Being direct in motion is usually listed as a dignity. It isn’t. This is the usual state of affairs, from which retrogradation is an aberration. 处于顺行状态通常被列为一种尊贵。但其实并非如此。这只是通常的状态，而逆 行才是异常状态。

### ✸I stress most strongly the point I make above, because I know how reluctant

students can be to abandon the idea that retrogradation is always a Bad Thing. Retrogradation can be good, bad or neither, depending upon the context and what the planet is moving either towards or away from. The arrivals gate at an airport is full of scenes of joyful retrogradation, and if my car is rolling towards the edge of the cliff, turning retrograde is an excellent idea. But if I am retrograding towards the prison from which I have escaped, I will not be happy.✷ 我上面强调这一点，是基于一个非常强烈的认知：我知道学生们通常多么不情愿 放弃“逆行永远是坏事”的观念。逆行可以是好事、坏事，或者无关紧要，这完 全取决于背景，以及行星正在移向或远离什么。机场的到达大厅里充满了喜悦的 逆行场景；如果我的车正滑向悬崖边缘，那么转为逆行是个绝佳的主意。但如果 我正逆行逃回我刚越狱的监狱，那我可就高兴不起来了。✷

Station 停滞

A planet passing from direct motion to retrogradation or from retrogradation to direct motion passes through station: first station when turning retrograde; second station when turning direct. These are so called because the planet’s apparent motion slows to

zero, leaving it stationary in the sky. This is extremely important. 一颗行星从顺行转为逆行，或从逆行转为顺行，会经历停滞：转为逆行时称为第 一次停滞；转为顺行时称为第二次停滞。之所以如此命名，是因为行星的视运动 会减速至零，使其在天空中看似静止不动。这一点极为重要。

Station is a time of great weakness and vulnerability for a planet. Only the strongest of extenuating circumstances will render it capable of action at such times. First station is likened to a man feeling so ill he decides to take to his sickbed: he feels bad, and is going to get worse. Second station is likened to man getting up from his sickbed for the first time: he feels weak, probably worse than he did than when he was lying down, but he is getting better. I think this fails to state quite how grim second station is. 停滞对行星而言是一个极为虚弱和脆弱的时期。只有在非常强的特殊条件下，它 才可能在这种时刻有所作为。第一次停滞被比作一个人感到严重不适，决定卧床 休息：他感觉糟糕，并且会变得更糟。第二次停滞则被比作一个人初次从病床上 起身：他感觉虚弱，可能比躺着时感觉更糟，但他正在好转。我认为这个比喻未 能充分说明第二次停滞是多么严峻的情况。

When considering station, it is vital to look at surrounding conditions. Maybe the planet is turning rettograde to avoid opposing Saturn: this could show the person signified by that planet making a smart move to avoid something nasty. Maybe it happens neat the end of a sign: is that planet avoiding losing essential dignity, or is it failing to gain it? Often the retrograde motion will take a planet back into a sign it has recently left: this may well be relevant to our enquiry. What does the change of reception at the change of sign tell us? 在考量停滞时，观察周围环境至关重要。或许这颗行星转为逆行是为了避免与土 星对冲：这可能表明由该行星所象征的人正在采取明智行动以避免某些糟糕的事 情。或许它发生在一个星座的末尾附近：这颗行星是在避免失去先天尊贵，还是 未能获得它？通常，逆行运动会使行星退回到它刚刚离开的星座：这很可能与我 们的查询相关。星座变更时接纳关系的变化告诉了我们什么？

### ✸As with retrogradation, context is of the utmost importance in deciding whether

station is good, bad or neither. With the river near which I live in flood, I cast a horary to see if the embankment would be washed away. The significator of the embankment was in station. Excellent! If it isn’t going anywhere: it will not be washed away. Within the context, station was extremely strengthening, because not moving is exactly what the embankment should be doing – exactly where its strength lies.✷

### ✸与逆行一样，在判断停滞是吉、是凶还是中性时，背景至关重要。我曾居住

的河流附近遭遇洪水，我起了卜卦盘来看堤坝是否会被冲毁。堤坝的征象星正处 于停滞。太好了！如果它哪里也不去：它就不会被冲走。在此具体背景下，停滞 是极其有力的加强，因为静止不动正是堤坝应该做的，这正是其力量所在。✷

Speed 速度

The Sun always moves at almost the same speed (i.e covers almost the same amount of the zodiac each day). The Moon’s speed fluctuates around its average.The other planets slow to zero at station and move faster than their average at other times. This can be of great importance. 太阳的运行速度几乎总是恒定的（即每天在黄道上移动的距离几乎相同）。月亮 的速度则围绕其平均值上下波动。其他行星在停滞时速度会降至零，而在其他时 间则可能比其平均速度快。这一点可能至关重要。

The faster the planet is moving, the more power it has to act. This is a question of impetus, just as in physics class: a car travelling at 60 miles per hour does a lot more damage than one travelling at 20. 行星运行速度越快，其拥有的行动力就越强。这是一个冲力的问题，正如物理课 所示：一辆时速 60 英里的汽车造成的破坏远大于时速 20 英里的汽车。

‘How do I know if the planet is moving fast or slow?’I trust that you have taken my advice and turned off the ‘helpful’ page on your software that gives you this and far too much other information. Either click your chart forward by a day to see how far your planet has moved in that time, then compare this with its moved between noon yesterday and noon today. Raphael’s Ephemeris has a handy table giving the daily motion of all planets out to Mars. “我如何知道行星运行得快还是慢？”我相信你已经采纳了我的建议，关闭了软 件上那个“提供此信息及过多其他信息”的“帮助”页面。只需将你的星盘向前 点击一天，看看这段时间内你的行星移动了多远，然后将其与昨天中午到今天中 午之间的移动距离进行比较。《Raphael（拉斐尔）星历表》中有一个方便的 表格，列出了所有行星（直至火星）的每日行度。

19. Foulsham, Slough, annual publication. 19.斯劳，弗尔沙姆出版社，每年出版。

The average daily motions of the planets are: 行星的平均每日行度如下：

Moon 13°11′ Mercury 0°59′ Venus 0°59′ Sun 0°59′ Mars 0°31′ Jupiter 0°05′ Saturn 0°02′

This is expressed in degrees and minutes (of arc, not of time). 60 minutes = 1 degree. So the average motion of the Sun, Mercury and Venus is fractionally less than 1 degree per day. But this is their daily forward motion, counting their retrograde periods as negative. A planet can be moving fast but in a retrograde direction. The slower a planet moves, relative to its own norm, the less able it is to act. A planet moving fast and retrograde is well able to act, but in the wrong way: our cowboy is gung-ho about his shooting, which is in the wrong direction. 这以度和分（弧分，而非时间分）表示。60 分 = 1 度。因此，太阳、水星和金 星的平均行度略小于每天 1 度。但这是它们的每日顺行行度，将其逆行时段计为 负值。一颗行星可能运行得很快，但方向是逆行的。一颗行星相对于其自身常态 运行得越慢，其行动力就越弱。一颗运行速度快但处于逆行的行星有很强的行动 力，但方向是错误的：就像我们的牛仔热衷于射击，却瞄错了方向。

We don’t need to be fussy here: a planet must be significantly faster or slower than its norm for this to be worth noting. A few minutes per day makes a big difference for slow moving Jupiter, but is nothing for the Moon. The Sun is guide; but compiling this table was the first time I have ever found it necessary to think about the limits of ‘fast’ and ‘slow’, so don’t treat this as an exact definition. 我们不必在此过分纠结：只有当行星的运行速度显著快于或慢于其常态时，才值 得注意。对于运行缓慢的木星来说，每天几弧分的差异影响巨大，但对月亮而言 则没什么影响。太阳可以作为参照标准；但编制这个表格是我第一次发现有必要 思考“快”与“慢”的界限，所以不要将此视为精确的定义。

Fast when above:Slow when below: 超过如下速度即为快速低于如下速度即为慢速 13°30′12°30′ The Moon per day（每天）per day（每天） Mercury 1°30′ 1°00′ Venus 1°10′ 0°50′ Mars 0°40′ 0°30′ Jupiter 0°10′ 0°05′ Saturn 0°05′ 0°02′

This does, of course, have specific reference to questions about speed: ‘Can I win the race?’ ‘Will they process this transaction quickly?’ In some cases a planet slow in motion may be exactly what suits you: ‘Will I gain by dragging this case out?’ 当然，这一点特别适用于关于速度的问题：“我能赢得赛跑吗？”“他们会快速 处理这笔交易吗？”在某些情况下，行星运行缓慢可能恰恰符合你的需求：“我 通过拖延这个案子能获利吗？”

The exception to the ‘fast is strong’ rule is Saturn. Moving fast is against Saturn’s ponderous nature and so for Saturn should be counted as a weakness. But this does not mean its usual slow motion is necessarily a benefit. It often shows things bogged

down in one way or another. For example, when Saturn was moving slowly in the fixed earth sign of Taurus I was besieged with medical horaries about either psychic or physical constipation. “快速即强”规则的例外是土星。运行速度快违背了土星本身沉重缓慢的天性， 因此对土星而言，快速应被视为一种衰弱。但这并不意味着它通常的缓慢运行就 一定是益处。例如，当土星在固定土象星座金牛座中运行缓慢时，我接到了大量 关于精神或身体上迟滞现象的医学卜卦。

### ✸While the above is quite correct, giving the subject this amount of attention

exaggerates the importance of speed. In almost all charts, whether planets are moving fast or slow is of no significance. In a question such as ‘Should I buy this racehorse?’ it is of course extremely important, but such contexts are rare.✷

### ✸尽管上述内容相当正确，但给予这个主题如此多的关注，会夸大速度的重要

性。在几乎所有的星盘中，行星运行得快或慢都没有意义。只有在诸如“我应该 买这匹赛马吗？”这类问题中，它才当然极其重要，但这类情境很罕见。✷

Combustion 燃烧

This is of huge importance. It can decide a judgement on its own. ‘Will my team beat their team?’ and Lord 7 (their team) is combust: your team wins. End of judgement. There is no greater affliction to a planet than this. 这一点至关重要。它可以单独决定一个论断。“我的队伍能打败他们的队伍吗？” 如果 7 宫主（代表他们的队伍）被燃烧：你的队伍获胜。论断结束。再没有比这 更严重的行星受克了。

Technically, a planet within eight and a half degrees of the Sun is combust. But combustion varies in its seriousness: a planet eight degrees from the Sun and separating is much less afflicted than one that is two degrees from the Sun and applying. NB: to be combust a planet must be in the same sign as the Sun. 从技术上讲，行星与太阳距离在八度半以内时，即被燃烧。但燃烧的严重程度有 所不同：一颗距离太阳八度且正在出相位的行星，其所受影响远小于一颗距离太 阳 2 度且正在入相位的行星。注意：要被燃烧，行星必须与太阳位于同一星座。

Apart from being utterly destructive, combustion can also show that whoever or whatever is signified by that planet cannot either see or be seen. This can give a positive sense to combustion: ‘Can I do such-and-such without applying for a permit?’ and the querent’s significator is combust: ‘Yes. No one can see you: you can do what you like.’ 除了具有彻底的破坏性之外，燃烧也可能表示由该行星所象征的人或事物无法看

见或不被看见。这可以为燃烧赋予一种积极的意义：“我能否不申请许可就做某 某事？”，而问卜者的征象星被燃烧：“可以。没人能看见你：你可以随心所欲。”

If its significator is combust, a lost object will often come to light when, in real time, its significator leaves combustion. 如果其征象星被燃烧，失物往往会在现实时间中，当该征象星离开燃烧状态时重 见天日。

If this planet cannot see, the person it signifies cannot see reason. The querent whose significator is combust will not take any notice of the judgement. The lamentable truth of this is repeated in chart after chart. 如果这颗行星无法看见，它所象征的人也就看不到理智。征象星被燃烧的问卜者， 将不会留意任何论断。这一可叹的事实在一个又一个星盘中反复得到验证。

### ✸The house the Sun rules may allow us to identify what it is that is obscuring the

querent’s judgement. Lilly unwittingly gives an example of this in his judgement on his own question about buying some houses.His significator is combust. The Sun rules the 11th house, which is the 5th from the 7th. What is obscuring his judgement? The seller’s beautiful daughter, leading him on so he pays far more than the houses are worth.✷ 如果太阳所掌管的宫位可能让我们识别出是什么蒙蔽了问卜者的判断力。Lilly 在对自己关于购买几处房屋的提问所作论断中，无意中给出了一个例子。他的 征象星被燃烧。太阳掌管 11 宫，即 7 宫之 5 宫。是什么蒙蔽了他的判断力？是 卖家的漂亮女儿，她引诱他，导致他支付了远高于房屋价值的价格。✷

21. Lilly, chapter ⅩⅩⅩⅧ

It is sometimes claimed that as Mars, like the Sun, is hot and dry, combustion does not affect it. It does. The idea with combustion is that it is not safe to come too close to the king (unless you are in his bosom); it is no less unsafe if you are a soldier (Mars) than Ann Boleyn (Venus). 有时有人认为，由于火星和太阳一样具有燥热性质，燃烧对它没有影响。但事实 是有影响。燃烧的理念在于：过于接近国王（除非你是他的心腹）是不安全的； 无论你是士兵（火星）还是 Ann Boleyn（安妮·博林）（金星），这种不安全 程度并无不同。

If conjunction with the Sun would give a Yes to the question, combustion can be ignored: the poor Sun would never get conjuncted otherwise. 若与太阳形成合相本身就会对问题给出肯定的答案，那么燃烧可以忽略不计：否 则可怜的太阳将永远无法与其他行星合相。

The debate on how combustion affects a planet in that planet’s own sign (e.g. Venus combust in Taurus) is an ancient one. Treat it exactly as a mutual reception: the planet

has power over the Sun by dispositing it; the Sun has power over the planet by combustion. So the combustion does not harm the planet; the idea of not being able to see or be seen still remains, however. 关于燃烧如何影响一颗入庙的行星（例如，金星在金牛座被燃烧）的争论自古有 之。可以将其完全视作一种互溶关系：该行星通过定位太阳而拥有对太阳的权力； 太阳则通过燃烧而拥有对该行星的权力。因此，燃烧并不会伤害该行星；然而， “无法看见或不被看见”的概念仍然存在。

### ✸The same is true of combustion in the sign of that planet’s exaltation (e.g. Venus

combust in Pisces).✷

### ✸同样适用于行星在其旺势星座被燃烧的情况（例如，金星在双鱼座被燃烧）。

✷

Athough combustion is so destructive, there can be a big difference between combustion with the planet applying to the Sun and combustion when the planet is separating. ‘Will I survive this illness?’ combust and applying: maybe not. And separating: the worst is past. 尽管燃烧极具破坏性，但行星入相位太阳时的燃烧，与行星出相位太阳时的燃烧， 两者之间可能存在巨大差异。“我能从这场疾病中幸存吗？”如果是燃烧且入相 位：或许不能。如果是出相位：最坏的时期已经过去。

Being free of combustion is usually listed as a dignity. It isn’t. This is the usual state of affairs, from which combustion is an aberration. 未被燃烧的状态通常被列为一种尊贵。其实并非如此。这只是通常的状态，而燃 烧才是异常状态。

### ✸Shakespeare gives a near example of the idea that combustion makes something

invisible. The king has fallen for a married woman, who wants nothing to do with him, so he leans on her father to use his influence with her. Among other arguments, the father tells her not to fear losing her reputation, because if she’s close to the king the rays of majesty are so bright that no one will be able to see her.✷Edward Ⅲ, 2.1. 399-401)✷

### ✸Shakespeare（莎士比亚）提供了一个近乎完美的例子，来说明燃烧使某物不

可见的理念。国王爱上了一位已婚妇人，而妇人对他毫无兴趣，于是国王向她父 亲施压，要他利用自己对女儿的影响力。在诸多说辞中，父亲告诉女儿不必担心 名誉受损，因为如果她接近国王，帝王威仪的光芒如此耀眼，以至于无人能看见 她。(《爱德华三世》, 2.1. 399-401) ✷

Cazimi 日核

In the centre of combustion there is a tiny oasis called cazimi, or in the heart of the 1/2 Sun. To be cazimi a planet must be within 17′ of the Sun’s position – though actually measuring half minutes is being far too precious. While combustion is the worst thing that can happen to a planet, cazimi is the best: a planet cazimi is likened to a man who is raised up to sit beside the king. If you are the king’s favourite, in his bosom, you have great power. To be cazimi a planet must be in the same sign as the Sun. 在燃烧的中心，有一小片绿洲，称为近日点，或称位于太阳心脏。要处于日核， 行星必须位于距离太阳位置 17.5 分以内——不过，实际上去测量半分的精度， 未免太过较真了。燃烧是行星可能遭遇的最糟糕的情况，而日核则是最好的：处 于日核的行星被比作被提拔起来、坐在国王身边的人。如果你是国王的宠臣，在 他的心腹之地，你就拥有巨大的权力。要处于日核，行星必须与太阳位于同一星 座。

Do not think, ‘This planet is combust, but it’s heading towards cazimi, so all will be well’. Combustion is utterly destructive: there is no moving through it to cazimi. The exception to this principle is if we are electing with the horary chart and the planet we wish to make strong is combust (see chapter 27). 切勿这样想：“这颗行星被燃烧了，但它正朝日核移动，所以一切都会好起来的。” 燃烧具有彻底的破坏性：不可能通过燃烧状态而进入日核。这一原则的例外情况 是，如果我们在利用卜卦盘进行择日，并且我们希望增强的行星正好处于燃烧状 态（参见第 27 章）。

Under the sunbeams 日光之下

Beyond combustion lies a less harmful area where a planet is under the sunbeams, under the rays, or sub radiis. This extends from the end of combustion until the planet 1/2 is 17degrees from the Sun. Like combustion, the strength of the effect varies: 9 degrees from the Sun and approaching combustion is serious; 16 degrees from the Sun and separating is trivial. 在燃烧区域之外，存在一个危害较小的区域，即行星处于日光之下，或称受日光 照耀或太阳光束下。此区域从燃烧结束处延伸，直至行星距离太阳 17.5 度。与 燃烧类似，其影响强度也有所变化：距离太阳 9 度且正在接近燃烧时，影响严重； 距离太阳 16 度且正在出相位时，则影响甚微。

A planet does not need to be in the same sign as the Sun to be under the sunbeams. 一颗行星无需与太阳位于同一星座，即可处于日光之下。

“Why these dimensions?” The Sun’s position marked on a chart is that of its centre; but the Sun has a visible disc. The apparent size of this varies, of course, but 35’ in diameter is the norm. This is a useful guide to distance when skywatching: the usual diameter of both Sun and Moon is roughly half a degree. “为什么是这些度数？”星盘上所标记的太阳位置是其中心点；但太阳有一个可 见的圆面。这个视直径当然会变化，但 35 角分是标准值。这对于天文观测时的 距离判断是一个有用的参考：太阳和月亮的通常直径大致都是半度。

1/21/2 As its disc has a diameter of 35’, its radius is 17.So a planet within 17of the Sun’s position is within the Sun’s disc (at least, it is by longitude. It may be above or below it by latitude; this doesn’t matter). By extrapolation, jumping up a unit from minutes ‘ 1/2 of arc to degrees, anything within 17of the Sun is under the beams. Combustion is simply this distance halved. 由于太阳的圆面直径为 35 分，其半径为 17.5 分。因此，与太阳位置相距 17.5 分以内的行星，即处于太阳的圆面之内（至少就黄经而言是如此。其在黄纬上可 能高于或低于太阳，但这无关紧要）。依此推断，将单位从弧分放大到度，与太 阳相距 17.5 度以内的任何星体都处于日光之下。而燃烧则恰好是这个距离的一 半。

### ✸Although a planet can be under the sunbeams in a different sign from the Sun, if it

is more than about 8 degrees from the Sun, in a different sign, the effect of the sunbeams is so trivial that it can be ignored.

### ✸尽管一颗行星可能在与太阳不同星座的情况下仍处于日光之下，但如果它与

太阳相距超过约 8 度且在不同星座，那么日光之下的影响就微乎其微，可以忽略 不计。

Combustion can prevent seeing or being seen; being under the sunbeams does not.✷ 燃烧会阻碍看见或不被看见；而处于日光之下则不会。✷

Opposition to the Sun 对冲太阳

The area of 8 degree or so either side of exact opposition to the Sun is also a place of extreme affliction, not quite so serious as combustion, but not so far short of it. There is no equivalent of cazimi here. 在太阳精确对冲两侧约 8 度的区域内，同样是极端受克的位置，其严重程度虽不 及燃烧，但相去不远。此处没有类似于日核的正面对应区域。

Besiegement 围攻

If a significator is placed between two malefic planets it is besieged. Whichever way it turns, there is something nasty there: the rock and the hard place. If a planet is placed between two benefic planets, it is still ‘besieged’; but in this case the besiegers are vying with each other to present rich gifts: a cushion and a very soft place. As ever, we must pay attention to the condition of the planets: being stuck between Mars and Saturn in Capricorn, where they both have lots of dignity, it not so bad; being stuck between Jupiter and Venus in Virgo, where they are both debilitated, is destructive. 如果一颗征象星被夹在两颗凶星之间，它就被被围攻了。无论它转向哪边，都会 遇到麻烦：可谓前狼后虎。如果一颗行星被夹在两颗吉星之间，它仍然处于“被 围攻”状态；但在此情况下，围攻者竞相献上厚礼：可谓左右逢源。和以往一样， 我们必须关注这些行星的状态：被夹在摩羯座的火星和土星之间（两者在该星座 都拥有很多尊贵）并不那么糟糕；被夹在处女座的木星和金星之间（两者在该星 座都处于衰弱状态）则具有破坏性。

The closer the besieging planets are to each other, the stronger is the effect of besiegement. If they are not within the same sign, the effects are trivial, unless you have the rare circumstance when all the planets – or all the relevant planets – are in a neat line with the besieging malefics or benefics at either end. 围攻行星彼此靠得越近，围攻效应就越强。如果它们不在同一星座内，其影响就 微不足道，除非你遇到罕见的情况：所有行星——或所有相关行星——整齐排列， 凶星或吉星各居两端。

A planet besieged by malefics yet receiving an aspect from a benefic has solace amid his problems: OK, I’m besieged, but the warehouses are full of caviar and the TV’s still working. Besieged by benefics and receiving an aspect from a malefic, there is something that blights the promise: I can have the ice cream, I can have the cake, but I’ve got a toothache. 一颗行星被凶星围攻，但接收到一颗吉星的相位，则意味着在其困境中仍有慰藉： 好吧，我是被围攻了，但仓库里堆满了鱼子酱，电视也还能看。若被吉星围攻却 接收到一颗凶星的相位，则预示着某种东西会破坏这美好的承诺：我能吃冰淇淋， 也能吃蛋糕，但我牙疼。

Besiegement by the rays 光线受到围攻

Instead of being bodily between the two besieging planets, the significator casts its aspect between them. For instance: Venus is at 5 Pisces, Jupiter at 8 Pisces. A planet at 6 Pisces is in strong positive besiegement. A planet at 6 Scorpio is not besieged bodily, but it casts its trine aspect between Venus and Jupiter: it is besieged by the rays. This

is like besiegement, but much weaker. 征象星并非在实体上位于两颗围攻行星之间，而是其相位投射在两者之间。例如： 金星在双鱼座 5 度，木星在双鱼座 8 度。一颗在双鱼座 6 度的行星处于强烈的、 积极的实体围攻之中。而一颗在天蝎座 6 度的行星并未受到实体围攻，但其拱相 位投射在金星与木星之间：它是被光线围攻。这类似于围攻，但力量要弱得多。

Aspects 相位

A planet closely aspected by or closely conjunct with another planet is affected by that planet, for better or for worse. The old texts list such contacts with Jupiter or Venus as being strengthening, with Mars or Saturn as being weakening. But this is not always so: as we have seen, Jupiter and Venus in their essential debilities are not helpful, Mars and Saturn in essential dignity are not harmful. Even this statement needs qualifying, because we must also consider what their role is in the chart: death, for instance, may be signified by a strong Jupiter, but Jupiter being a strongly dignified benefic won’t make the person any the less dead. Whether the aspecting planet is strong or weak, we must also consider its receptions with the significator: for example, Jupiter in Cancer is strong, a very nice Jupiter; but it is in the detriment of Saturn, so if it casts its aspect to Saturn it will not be much help to it. Reception is treated in more detail in chapter 8. 一颗行星与另一颗行星形成紧密相位或紧密合相时，便会受到该行星的影响，无 论这种影响是好是坏。古代文献将与木星或金星形成此类接触列为加强因素，与 火星或土星则列为削弱因素。但这并非总是如此：正如我们所见，处于先天衰弱 的木星和金星并无助益，而处于先天尊贵的火星和土星也未必有害。即使这一说 法也需要限定条件，因为我们还必须考量它们在星盘中的角色：例如，死亡可能 由一颗强大的木星象征，但木星作为一颗强而有力的吉星，并不会让此人减少半 分死亡的可能。无论形成相位的星体是强是弱，我们还必须考量它与征象星之间 的接纳关系：例如，木星在巨蟹座是强大的，是一颗非常好的木星；但它位于土 星落陷的位置，因此如果它向土星投射相位，对土星的帮助并不会太大。接纳关 系将在第 8 章更详细地探讨。

A clear example of the principle would be a horary for a contest: ‘Will my team beat his team?’ In such a chart we have only two significators, Lord 1 for my team, Lord 7 for his. If Lord 1 were aspected by Saturn in Aries, a nasty kind of Saturn, my team would be afflicted. If Lord 7 were aspected by Jupiter in Cancer, his team would be strengthened. In this context it would not be necessary to work out what Satrun and Jupiter meant; in some questions it could be, although it is not always possible to do so with confidence. 该原则的一个清晰例证可见于关于比赛的卜卦盘：“我的队伍能打败他的队伍 吗？”在此类星盘中，我们只有两个征象星：1 宫主代表我的队伍，7 宫主代表 他的队伍。如果 1 宫主受到白羊座土星的相位影响（一种很糟糕的土星），我的

队伍就会受克。如果 7 宫主受到巨蟹座木星的相位影响，他的队伍则会得到加强。 在此情境下，无需探究土星和木星的具体含义；但在某些问题中，这可能是有必 要的，尽管并不总是能够有把握地做到这一点。

There is a general rule in all astrology: the closer the stronger. The closer the aspect is, the greater the effect it will have. But we must aslo consider the strength of the aspecting place: an opposition from Saturn in the 10th house, where it has lots of accidental dignity, will have a greater effect than an opposition from Saturn in the 6th house, where it has little. For its general effect on a planet you can ignore any aspect that is more than 3 degrees away: beyond this any effect is trivial. More often, though, we are reading aspects as showing future or occasionally past events, in which case they can be relevant at any degree of separation. 所有占星学都有一个通用法则：距离越近，影响越强。相位越紧密，其产生的影 响就越大。但我们也必须考量形成相位的星体本身的强弱：一颗位于 10 宫（拥 有大量偶然尊贵）的土星所形成的对冲相位，其影响将大于一颗位于 6 宫（偶然 尊贵甚少）的土星所形成的对冲相位。就其对行星的一般影响而言，你可以忽略 任何超过 3 度距离的相位：超过此范围，任何影响都微不足道。然而，更常见的 情况是，我们将相位解读为显示未来或偶尔过去的事件，此时即便相位距离各异， 其相关性仍可能存在。

### ✸I was being generous with the ‘3 degrees’ here. Regarding a planet being affected

for better or worse by an aspect, without us needing to have that aspect perfecting in order to show an event, the aspect needs to be within a degree or so to have any significant effect. Within 2 or 3 degrees only if the planets are conjunct.✷ 我之前说“3 度”是放宽了标准。关于一颗行星因相位而受到或好或坏的影响（且 我们不需要该相位形成精确相位来显示事件），该相位需要在大约 1 度以内才会 产生任何显著影响。只有在行星处于合相时，才适用 2 到 3 度的范围。✷

The Nodes （南北）交点

The Moon’s Nodes are the two points, directly oppsite each other, where the Moon’s apparent path around the Earth crosses the Sun’s. 月交点月交点是天空中彼此正对的两个点，即月亮绕地球运行的视轨道与太阳运 行轨道（黄道）相交之处。

The Nodes do not cast aspects, nor can they have aspects cast to them. They affect planets only by conjunction. A planet conjunct the North Node is helped, strengthened or increased. A planet conjunct the South Node is harmed, weakened or decreased. Which of these meanings is relevant will be clear enough in context. In some contexts we might think, ‘That significator is just separating from the South Node: something

unpleasant has happened to that person recently’; in others, we’d read the proximity to the South Node as showing that whatever that planet signifies is being diminished. 月交点不产生相位，也不接受相位。它们仅通过合相影响行星。与北交点形成合 相的行星会得到帮助、加强或增加。与南交点形成合相的行星则会受到伤害、削 弱或减少。其中哪种含义相关，在上下文中会足够清晰。在某些情况下，我们可 能会想：“那颗征象星刚刚离开南交点：那个人最近发生了不愉快的事情”；在 另一些情况下，我们会将近距离的南交点解读为显示该行星所象征的事物正在减 少。

Example: suppose I ask, ‘Will I win on the horses today?’ and find an applying aspect between the ruler of the 8th house (2nd from the 7th: my enemy’s money) and my own significator: yes, I will win. If Lord 8 is conjunct the North Node I will win a lot. If it is conjunct the South Node I will still win, but not much. Lord 8, which is the money that I am winning, is increased by its contact with the one, diminished by its contact with the other. 例如：假设我问“我今天赛马能赢吗？”，并发现 8 宫主（即 7 宫的 2 宫：我对 手的钱财）与我的征象星之间有一个入相位：是的，我会赢。如果 8 宫主与北交 点形成合相，我会赢很多。如果它与南交点形成合相，我仍然会赢，但赢得不多。 8 宫主——即我将赢得的钱财——因与前者（北交点）的接触而增加，因与后者 （南交点）的接触而减少。

If one of the Nodes falls in a house relevant to the question, it can affect that house. The North Node falling in a house is good for the affairs of that house, or shows the querent benefitting from that house. The South Node falling in a house harms the affairs of that house, or shows the querent losing through the affairs of that house. The effect is much more marked if the Node is close to the cusp. 若某一月交点落在与问题相关的宫位中，它会影响该宫。北交点落入某一宫位， 对该宫位的事务有利，或显示问卜者从该宫获益。南交点落入某一宫位，则损害 该宫位的事务，或显示问卜者因该宫事务而受损。若月交点接近宫头，其影响会 更加显著。

Example: ‘Will I get the job?’ with the North Node in the 10th (the house of work): this does not improve the querent’s chances of getting the job, but does show that it will be good for her if she gets it. ‘Should I employ this builder?’ with the South Node in the 6th (the house of servants): No! 例如：“我能得到这份工作吗？”北交点落在 10 宫（代表工作的宫位）：这并 不会增加问卜者获得这份工作的机会，但确实表明如果她得到这份工作，将对她 有益。“我应该雇用这个建筑商吗？”南交点落在 6 宫（代表雇工的宫位）：不！

Remember, though, that the Nodes comes as a pair: the one is always opposite the other. This means that we can rarely use the house placements of both, else we fall into the trap of thinking that if Mum is good, Dad must automatically be bad; my small animals benefit me, my large animals harm me. The context will show us which end of the nodal axis – if either – we should heed.

请记住，月交点总是成对出现：一个永远在另一个的对宫。这意味着我们很少能 同时使用两个交点的宫位位置，否则就会陷入一种思维陷阱，认为如果母亲好， 父亲就必然坏；或者我的小动物对我有益，我的大动物就对我有害。上下文会告 诉我们，应该关注月交点轴线的哪一端——如果需要关注的话。

Becareful to avoid dragging them into judgement unnecessarily. The chart does not have a dressing-room where they can go to relax when they are not involved in the drama: the Nodes wil appear in every chart, but in most charts they have nothing to tell us. If one of them falls into a house that concerns us, we can take note of it; if the Nodes fall in houses that do not concern us, there is no need for us to rack our brains wondering what those might mean. Just ignore them. 务必注意，避免不必要地将它们牵强地引入论断。星盘并没有一个化妆间，让它 们在未参与这场“戏剧”时可以进去放松：月交点会出现在每一张星盘中，但在 大多数星盘中，它们并无信息要告诉我们。如果其中一个落在我们关注的宫位， 我们可以留意它；如果月交点落在与我们无关的宫位，我们则无需绞尽脑汁去琢 磨它们可能意味着什么。忽略它们就好。

Although the Nodes do not cast or receive aspects you will often find a significator square to the Nodes (i.e. exactly halfway between them). This seems to show that person torn between two courses of action, often with neither of them being appealing. But this describes his predicament; there is nothing actively malefic about this placement. The planet is not affected by being square the Nodes. The idea in some modern books of the degree of the Nodes in any sign as ‘a degree of fatality’ is groundless. 尽管月交点本身不产生或接受相位，但你常常会发现一颗征象星与月交点形成刑 相位（即正好位于两个交点之间的中点）。这似乎显示此人正在两个行动方案之 间左右为难，且往往两者都缺乏吸引力。但这描述的只是他的困境；这个位置本 身并无主动的凶性。行星并不因与月交点形成刑相位而受到影响。某些现代书籍 中将任何星座中的交点度数视为“致命度数”的观点是没有根据的。

We have the choice of using the Mean Node or the True Node: the rough position or the exact position. Given the choice, we might as well use the exact position. Most software allows you to set your preference for this. 我们可以选择使用平均交点或真实交点：即粗略位置或精确位置。若有选择，我 们不妨使用精确位置。大多数软件允许你对此项进行偏好设置。

### ✸The debate about the effect of the Nodes has been running since ancient times. Is

it ‘North good, South bad’? Or is it ‘North increases, South decreases’, meaning that if a nasty planet is on the North Node it too is increased, becoming more strongly nasty? Lilly favours the simple North good, South bad, although the balance of opinion is against him. The meeting-point of these apparently different concepts is in human physiology: as is easily observable, nice things have the effect of expanding and dilating, nasty ones of diminishing and contracting. If puzzled, keep your eyes

firmly on the context of the question. You will almost always find that within that context either good/bad or expand/contract will make much more sense than the other.

### ✸关于月交点效应的争论自古有之。是“北交点吉，南交点凶”吗？还是说“北

交点增强，南交点减弱”，这意味着如果一颗凶星位于北交点上，它也会被增强， 变得更凶？Lilly 倾向于简单的“北交点吉，南交点凶”，尽管主流意见与之相 左。这两种看似不同的概念在人类生理学上找到了交汇点：正如很容易观察到的， 美好的事物具有扩张和舒张的效果，而糟糕的事物则具有减损和收缩的效果。如 果感到困惑，请务必紧盯问题的具体情境。你几乎总是会发现，在该情境下，吉 /凶或增强/减弱中的一组解释会比另一组显得合理得多。

Suppose we have Saturn in Aries – nasty Saturn, or unhappy Saturn – in the 2nd house and conjunct the South Node. How do we read this? If what interests us is the condition of Saturn, we would say that nasty Saturn is afflicted by the South Node. In most contexts the house-placement would be irrelevant. If what interest us is the condition of 2 house, we would say that the house is afflicted by both nasty Saturn and the South Node. We would not read this as the house being afflicted by nasty Saturn, but in only a limited way (i.e. Saturn’s power to afflict the house being diminished by its conjunction with the South Node). 假设我们有白羊座的土星——这是一种凶恶的或不幸的土星——位于 2 宫并与 南交点合相。我们该如何解读？如果我们关注的是土星的状态，我们会说凶恶的 土星受到南交点的受克。在大多数情况下，其宫位位置是无关紧要的。如果我们 关注的是 2 宫的状态，我们会说该宫受到凶恶的土星和南交点的双重受克。我们 不会将其解读为：该宫受到凶恶的土星的受克，但受克程度有限（即土星受克该 宫的力量因其与南交点的合相而减弱）。

You will sometimes see the Table of Dignities (page 54) printed with the North and South Node each having its exaltation. This is some busy-body’s attempt to fill up a couple of empty spaces in the chart: ignore it. The nature of the Nodes is not subject to change, so there is no possible significance in their being exalted. Nor in whether they are direct or retrograde (which is their usual direction of motion). 你有时会看到尊贵表（第 101 页）印有北交点和南交点各自的旺势位置。这只是 某些好事之徒试图填补表格中几处空白的尝试：忽略它即可。月交点的本质不可 改变，因此谈论它们是否处于旺势毫无意义。谈论它们是顺行还是逆行（这是它 们通常的运行方向）同样没有意义。

The South Node can on occasion be welcome. If the question is ‘Will I really lose weight on this diet?’ Lord 1 conjunct the contracting South Node would be a strong positive testimony.✷ 南交点在某些情况下也可能是受欢迎的。如果问题是“这种节食法真的能让我减 肥吗？”，1 宫主与具有收缩特性的南交点形成合相，将是一个强有力的正面征 象。✷

The Moon 月亮

Generally, the more light the Moon has – the closer it is to full – the stronger it is and so the more able it is to act. It is also stronger if it is increasing in light (moving from new to full Moon) than if it is decreasing in light (moving from full to new). But at full it is weak (see the point on opposition to the Sun, above), so its optimum position is around separating trine to the Sun: there it has lots of light and is still increasing. This point is important if the Moon is the planet whose aspect is showing the event in question. 一般而言，月亮拥有的光亮越多——即越接近满月——它就越强，因而行动力也 越强。与光减（从满月移向新月）时相比，它在光增（从新月移向满月）时也更 强大。但在满月时它其实较弱（参见前述关于与太阳对冲的要点），因此其最佳 位置大约是在与太阳形成出相位的拱相位时：此时它拥有大量光亮且仍在增加。 如果月亮是显示相关事件的征象星，这一点非常重要。

“How can I tell if the Moon is increasing in light?” Look at the Sun in the chart you are judging. Which is the shorter: the clockwise distance from Sun to Moon, or the anticlockwise distance? If the clockwise distance is the shorter, the Moon is getting closer to the Sun, moving from full to new, and so is decreasing in light. If the anticlockwise distance is shorter, it is moving towards full (opposition to the Sun) and so is increasing in light. “我如何判断月亮是在光增还是光减？”观察你正在论断的星盘中的太阳位置。 哪一个距离更短：从太阳到月亮的顺时针距离，还是逆时针距离？如果顺时针距 离更短，月亮正在靠近太阳，即从满月移向新月，因此处于光减。如果逆时针距 离更短，它正在移向满月（即与太阳形成对冲相位），因此处于光增。

### ✸With the exception that immediate application to opposition with the Sun (i.e. a

full Moon) is generally a minor negative, the amount of light the Moon has and whether it is gaining or losing light are hardly ever of relevance. Unless the context makes the amount of light or visibility of whatever the Moon signifies important, these terms can be ignored.✷ 除了一个例外情况——即立即与太阳形成入相位的对冲相位（也就是满月时）通 常有轻微的负面性——之外，月亮拥有的光亮多少，以及它是在光增还是光减， 几乎从来都无关紧要。除非问题背景使得月亮所象征事物的光亮多少或可见性变 得重要，否则这些概念可以忽略。✷

Void of course 空亡

It is rumoured that Quentin Tarantino was inspired by make Reservoir Dogs by the sight of astrologers discussing the meaning of void of course. It is quite simple and need not involve bloodshed. 传闻 Quentin Tarantino（昆汀·塔伦蒂诺）是受占星师们讨论空亡含义的场景启 发，才拍摄了《落水狗》。其实它很简单，并不需要引发流血事件。

The Moon is void of course if it does not perfect another aspect before leaving its present sign. If it perfects an aspect immediately after leaving this sign – at 0 degrees of the next sign, perhaps – it is void of course now; it will not be void of course once it has changed sign. In principle any planet can be void of course, but the term has practical significance only with the Moon. An aspect to the Part of Fortune or any other Arabian Part does not prevent the Moon being void. 当月亮在离开当前星座前，未与任何行星形成精确相位时，它便处于空亡状态。 如果它刚一离开当前星座（例如在下个星座的 0 度）就形成了一个相位，那么它 此刻是空亡的；一旦它换了星座，就不再是空亡。原则上，任何行星都可能空亡， 但该术语仅在涉及月亮时才具有实际意义。与福点或任何其他阿拉伯点形成的相 位，并不能阻止月亮处于空亡状态。

If the Moon in a horary chart is void, this is a general indication that not much is going to happen. For instance, if the question is ‘Should I emigrate?’ a void Moon suggests that the querent is unlikely to do so, whether it is a good idea or not. A void Moon can provide the full answer to a question, either favourably or unfavourably. ‘Will I lose my job?’ ‘Will I win the lottery?’ In both case a void Moon would give the answer ‘No: nothing will happen’. 如果卜卦盘中的月亮处于空亡状态，这通常预示着不会发生太多事情。例如，如 果问题是“我应该移民吗？”，空亡的月亮表明问卜者不太可能这样做，无论移 民是否是个好主意。空亡的月亮本身就可以为问题提供完整的答案，无论是肯定 还是否定。“我会失业吗？”“我会中彩票吗？”在这两种情况下，空亡的月亮 给出的答案都是“不：什么都不会发生”。

A void Moon is not always the final answer, however. Like any other individual testimony, it can be overruled. If the main significators are strong and applying to aspect, the event can still happen. 然而，空亡的月亮并不总是最终答案。像任何其他单独的征象一样，它也可能被 推翻。如果主要的征象星很强，并且正在入相位，事件仍然可能发生。

The Moon is also void of course if it has a long way to travel before making its next aspect, even though that aspect perfects within that same sign. Example: Moon at 4 Taurus, separating from a sextile with Venus at 3 Cancer. Its next aspect is not perfected till reaches 22 Taurus. The Moon can be considered void. This often shows a period of stagnation before the querent finds the will to act. There is no set distance here: simply ‘a long way’. It has nothing to do with being in or out of orb. I would suggest taking 15 degrees or so as a minimum. 月亮在与其下一个相位形成前，若需运行很长一段距离（即使该相位仍在同一星

座内完成），也可被视为空亡。例如：月亮在金牛座 4 度，刚与巨蟹座 3 度的金 星形成出相位的六合相位。它的下一个相位要到金牛座 22 度才会形成。此时月 亮可被视为空亡。这通常显示在问卜者找到行动意愿之前，会有一段停滞期。这 里没有固定的距离标准：只需判断是否为“很长一段距离”。这与相位是否在容 许度内无关。我个人建议将大约 15 度左右作为最小参考距离。

Sometimes there is a clear reason for a void Moon showing nothing happening. A querent had applied for a job on the understanding that he present incumbent was leaving. That person was signified by a void Moon in a fixed sign: she was going nowhere. She didn’t leave, so nothing came of the application. In many situation the reason nothing happens is the querent’s inaction. As the Moon is usually cosignificator of the querent, its being void can show this lack of will to act. ‘Will she marry me?’ ‘Not if you don’t ask her.’ 有时，空亡月亮显示无事发生是有明确原因的。一位问卜者申请了一份工作，前 提是现任者即将离职。而那位现任者由一颗位于固定星座的空亡月亮象征：她哪 儿也不会去。她没有离开，因此这份申请也就没有结果。在许多情况下，无事发 生的原因是问卜者的不作为。由于月亮通常是问卜者的共同征象星，其空亡状态 可能正显示了这种行动意愿的缺乏。“她会嫁给我吗？”“如果你不去问她，就 不会。”

Occasionally the Moon will travel all the way through a sign without making an aspect. At such times it is feral, like a wild beast. This is an emphatic version of void of course. Little can be expected from the situation. 有时，月亮会贯穿整个星座而不形成任何相位。此时它处于流浪状态，如同失控 的野兽。这是空亡的一种强烈表现形式。对此情境不必抱太大期望。

### ✸ In common astrological parlance, ‘the Moon’s void of course’ seems to be

regarded as a full explanation of why just about anything didn’t work out as hoped. It is not! What is above is more reserved than most writing on the subject, but that too overstates the importance of the term. Unless the Moon has a specific role in the drama, and lack of action by whomever or whatever it signifies will prevent anything happening – as with my example of the job application – its being void of course will be, at the very most, a minor testimony.

### ✸在常见的占星学用语中，“月亮空亡”似乎被当作解释几乎所有事情未能如

愿以偿的万用理由。但事实并非如此！上述内容已比大多数关于此主题的论述更 为审慎，即便如此，它仍然夸大了这个术语的重要性。除非月亮在这出“戏剧” 中扮演特定角色，并且其象征的人或事物因缺乏行动力而导致事件停滞——就像 我关于工作申请的例子——否则，它的空亡状态充其量只是一个次要的征象。

Lilly’s statement that when the Moon is void ‘things go hardly on’ is commonly misunderstood. ‘Hardly’ has changed its meaning since Lilly’s day. The idea that nothing will happen comes from giving it its modern meaning of ‘scarcely’. For Lilly

it meant literally ‘hardly’, the adverb from hard: in a hard way. Things will proceed with difficulty. Of course, if things proceed with difficulty, people often give up, so it can amount to the same thing, but that’s not what Lilly meant. Lilly 关于月亮空亡时“诸事难行”的论断常被误解。“难”这个词的含义自莉 莉的时代以来已经发生了变化。认为“无事会发生”的观点，源于赋予了这个词 现代的“几乎不”的含义。而对 Lilly 而言，它字面上的意思是“艰难地”，是 “hard”的副词形式：表示以一种艰难的方式。事情将会艰难地进行。当然，如 果事情进展艰难，人们往往会放弃，所以这可能最终导致相同的结果，但这并非 Lilly 的本意。

When the Moon is very late in its sign – at, say, 28 or 29 degrees – the concept of void of course becomes irrelevant. The idea with void of course is that the Moon isn’t going to do anything; but when the Moon is at so late a degree it is going to do something: it is going to change sign.✷ 当月亮位于其星座极晚的度数时——例如，在 28 或 29 度——空亡的概念就变得 无关紧要了。空亡的核心概念是月亮将无所作为；但当月亮处于如此晚的度数时， 它即将有所作为：它将换星座。✷

The via combusta 燃烧之路

Meaning ‘the burned-up road’ this is the area of the zodiac between 15 Libra and 15 Scorpio. It affects only the Moon, which does not like being there at all. Being here does not make the Moon any weaker, but does distress it. This is primarily of significance in questions where the querent’s emotions are important: the Moon’s passage through the via combusta show a period of unpleasant emotional turbulence. Note the Moon’s position relative to the via combusta: is it about to enter it, stuck in the middle of it, or about to leave it? So ‘Will I be happy if I dump him?’ with the Moon at 13 Libra, on the point of entering this area of unpleasant emotional turmoil: ‘No’ (although this iteself would not be the complete judgement). 此术语意为“燃烧之路”，指黄道上天秤座 15 度至天蝎座 15 度之间的区域。它 只影响月亮，而月亮极不喜位于此处。处于此区域并不会削弱月亮的力量，但会 使其苦恼不安。这主要在问卜者的情绪至关重要的问题中具有意义：月亮行经燃 烧之路显示一段不愉快的情绪动荡期。需注意月亮相对于燃烧之路的位置：是即 将进入其中、困于其正中，还是即将离开？因此，对于“如果我甩了他，我会快 乐吗？”这样的问题，若月亮位于天秤座 13 度，即将进入这片不愉快的情绪动 荡区域，答案将是“不会”（尽管这本身并非完整论断）。

“Why this portion of the zodiac?” The idea of the via combusta is connected with the ancient purification rituals around menstruation. That it is between 15 Libra and 15 Scorpio rather than anywhere else in the zodiac is because of the relationship of the Moon (the female principle) here to the exaltation of the Sun (he male principle)

in Aries. Ideas that it is determined by ancient placements of fixed stars or the influence of Mars and Saturn over Libra and Scorpio are transparently incorrect. “为何是黄道的这一部分？”燃烧之路的概念与古代关于月经的净化仪式有关。 它位于天秤座 15 度至天蝎座 15 度之间，而非黄道上的其他位置，是因为此处的 月亮（阴性法则）与太阳（阳性法则）在白羊座的旺势之间存在关联。那些认为 它是由古代恒星位置或火星与土星对天秤座和天蝎座的影响所决定的观点，显然 是错误的。

Fixed stars 恒星

The fixed stars are discussed in chapter 11. For the general assessment of a planet’s strength or weakness there are only three stars of major significance. These are Regulus (29 Leo), Spica (23 Libra) and Caput Algol (26 Taurus). Fixed stars neither give nor receive aspects: we are concerned only with conjunction. If a significator or relevant house cusp, especially the Ascendant, is within a couple of degrees of conjunction with one of these stars, it will be strongly affected in the following ways: 恒星的影响将在第 11 章详述。在评估行星强弱时，仅有三颗恒星具有显著意义： 它们是轩辕十四（狮子座 29 度）、角宿一（天秤座 23 度）和大陵五（金牛座 26 度）。恒星既不产生相位也不接受相位：我们只关注合相。如果一颗征象星 或相关宫头（特别是上升点）与其中一颗恒星形成合相且在 2 度之内，它将受到 强烈影响，方式如下：

* Regulus gives great power for material achievement. It does not necessarily bring happiness; it does bring success. *轩辕十四会赋予达成物质成就的强大力量。它未必带来快乐；但确实带来成功。

* Spica is generally fortunate. It doesn’t have the will to power that is seen in Regulus, but is a much happier star. It is strongly protective, so is an indication that even if things don’t work out as desired, the consequences will not be so bad. 角宿一通常是吉利的。它不具备轩辕十四所展现的那种权力意志，但是一颗能带 来更多幸福的星。它具有很强的保护性，因此预示着即使事情未能如愿，后果也 不会太糟。

* Caput Algol bring difficulties. The usual indication is of losing one’s head, whether literally or metaphorically, with unfortunate results. Example: a querent asked, ‘I’ve fallen in love with the man on TV; is there a future in our relationship?’ Her main significator was conjunct Caput Algol. *大陵五带来困难。其通常的征象是“失去头脑”（无论是字面意义还是比喻意 义），最终导致不幸结果。例如：一位问卜者问道：“我爱上了电视上的那个男 人；我们的关系有未来吗？”她的主要征象星与大陵五形成合相。

### ✸The fixed stars do move, albeit far more slowly than any planet. Regulus is now at

0 Virgo.✷

### ✸恒星确实会移动，尽管比任何行星都要慢得多。轩辕十四现在位于处女座 0

度。✷

MINOR POINTS 次要要点

I am including the following only because you may come across these term in other texts. Some have (very) occasional uses in fine-tuning judgements, but, remembering our golden rule of ‘Keep it Simple!’ they can all be ignored. We always have testimonies of so much greater significance than these that we can disregard these without fear of error. 我之所以纳入以下内容，仅仅是因为你可能在其他文献中遇到这些术语。其中一 些在微调论断时（非常）偶尔有用，但请牢记我们的黄金法则“保持简单！”， 它们全都可以忽略。我们总是拥有比这些重要得多的征象，因此我们可以放心地 忽略这些，无需担心出错。

Oriental and occidental 东出和西入

Meaning ‘eastern’ and ‘western’, these terms refer to a planet’s position relative to the Sun. If the planet rises before the Sun it is visible in the eastern sky before dawn, so is oriental. If it rises after the Sun if will still be visible in the western sky after the Sun has set, and so is occidental. 意为“朝东的”与“朝西的”，这两个术语指的是行星相对于太阳的位置。如果 行星在太阳之前升起，它将在黎明前出现在东方天空，因此是东出的。如果它在 太阳之后升起，则会在太阳落下后仍出现在西方天空，因此是西入的。

“How do I know whether a planet is oriental or occidental?” Look at the Sun in the chart you are judging. Which is the shorter: the clockwise distance from the Sun to the planet you are considering , or the anticlockwise distance? If the clockwise distance is the shorter, the planet is oriental. If the anticlockwise distance is shorter, it is occidental. Look at the chart on page 78. Venus, as well as Uranus, Neptune and Pluto, is oriental; all the other planets are occidental. The Moon is increasing in light and will soon be full. “我如何判断一颗行星是东出还是西入？”观察你正在论断的星盘中的太阳位置。 哪一个距离更短：从太阳到你所考量的行星的顺时针距离，还是逆时针距离？如 果顺时针距离更短，该行星是东出的。如果逆时针距离更短，则是西入的。参见

第 160 页的图表。金星，以及天王星、海王星和冥王星，是东出的；所有其他行 星都是西入的。月亮正在光增，即将满月。

An oriental planet will be more obvious in its actions. If the question were ‘Am I best suited for work on stage or behind the scenes?’ this could be a minor consideration; but even there you would find more important testimonies and so could ignore this. That Mars, Jupiter and Saturn are favoured by being oriental, Mercury and Venus by being occidental, is with reference only to natal charts, where the distinction between oriental and occidental is important. 一颗东出的行星，其行动会更加明显。如果问题是“我更适合台前还是幕后的工 作？”，这可能是一个次要考量；但即便在那里，你也会发现更重要的征象，因 此可以忽略这一点。至于火星、木星和土星因东出而更有利，水星和金星因西入 而更有利，这仅适用于本命盘，因为在本命盘中，东出与西入的区分才是重要的。

The Moon occidental is increasing in light, oriental is decreasing in light. This is important and is discussed above. 月亮西入则处于光增，东出则处于光减。这一点很重要，上文已作讨论。

Hayz 得时

Just as animals are nocturnal or diurnal, so are planets. The Sun, as is obvious, is diurnal: it belongs up in the sky during the day. The Moon is nocturnal: it belongs up in the sky during the night. Jupiter and Saturn are also diurnal; Mars and Venus are nocturnal. If Mercury is oriental it is diurnal, if occidental it is nocturnal. 正如动物有夜行性与昼行性之分，行星亦然。太阳显然是昼行性的：它属于白昼 闪耀于天际。月亮是夜行性的：它属于黑夜闪耀于天际。木星和土星也属于日星； 火星和金星属于夜星。若水星为东出的，则属日星；若为西入的，则属夜星。

If a diurnal planet is above the Earth (in houses 7-12) in a daytime chart, or below it (in houses 1-6) in a night chart, it is in its halb. So is a nocturnal planet that is above the Earth by night or below it by day. Halb is so minor a consideration that it can always be ignored: it pales into insignificance beside other testimonies. 若一颗日星在日生盘中位于地平线之上（即在 7-12 宫），或在夜生盘中位于地 平线之下（即在 1-6 宫），则其处于 halb 状态。同样，若一颗夜星在夜间位于地 平线之上，或在白天位于地平线之下，也处于 Halb 状态。Halb 是如此次要的一 个考量因素，以至于总是可以忽略：与其他征象相比，它显得微不足道。

The Sun, Mars, Jupiter and Saturn are masculine; the Moon and Venus are feminie. Mercury takes the nature of whichever planet is (in order of preference) close to conjunction with it, close to aspect with it, or its dispositor. A planet is in its hayz if it is in its halb and also in a sign of its own gender.The masculine sign are Aries, Gemini, Leo, Libra, Sagittarius and Aquarius; the feminine signs are Taurus, Cancer, Virgo, Scorpio, Capricorn and Pisces. 太阳、火星、木星和土星属阳性；月亮和金星属阴性。水星的性别则取自与其合 相、相位最接近的行星，或取其定位星的性别（按此优先顺序）。若一颗行星既 处于 halb 状态，又位于与其自身性别相同的星座，则其处于得时状态。阳性星 座为：白羊座、双子座、狮子座、天秤座、射手座、水瓶座；阴性星座为：金牛 座、巨蟹座、处女座、天蝎座、摩羯座、双鱼座。

20. Lilly and authors working from him without other reference state mistakenly that a nocturnal planet should be above the Earth by day and below it by night. Lilly (Christian Astrology p.113) is following the French astrologer Dariot, who gives the correct version, but in such a muddy fashion that it is easy to see how Lilly picked up the wrong end of the stick (see Claude Darior, A Brief and Most Easie Introduction to the Judgement of the Stars, trans. Fabian Wither, London c. 1583, reprinted Ascella, Nottingham, n.d., p.19, although Lilly used a translation published in 1598). The correct version is clearly explained in Abu’l-Rayhan Muhammad Ibn Ahmad Al-Biruni, The book of instruction in the Elements of the Art of Astrology, trans. R. Ramsey Wright, Luzac, London, 1934; reprinted Ascella, Notttingham, n.d.; para.496.
20. Lilly 以及仅以其为参考而未查证其他来源的作者们，错误地陈述了夜星应在白昼位于地

平线之上、在夜晚位于地平线之下。Lilly（《基督教占星学》第 113 页）是遵循了法国占星 师 Dariot（达里奥特）的观点，后者给出了正确的版本，但表述如此含糊不清，很容易理解 Lilly 为何会误解其意（参见 Claude Darior【克劳德·达里奥特】，《星体判断简明入门》， Fabian Wither【法比安·威瑟】译，伦敦约 1583 年出版，Ascella 重印，诺丁汉，无日期， 第 19 页，尽管 Lilly 使用的是 1598 年出版的译本）。正确的版本在 Abu’l-Rayhan Muhammad Ibn Ahmad Al-Biruni【阿布·拉扬·穆罕默德·伊本·艾哈迈德·阿尔·比鲁尼】的《占星 术基础要素指导书》（R. Ramsey Wright【R. 拉姆齐·赖特】译，卢扎克出版社，伦敦，1934 年；Ascella 重印，诺丁汉，无日期；第 496 段）中有清晰阐释。
