Example: Saturn in Aries is in its hayz if above the Earth by day or below it by night; Venus in Scorpio is in its hayz if above the Earth by night or below it by day. The tricky one is Mars, which is masculine and, unlike the other masculine planets, nocturnal: it needs to be in a mssculine sign and below the Earth by day, above it by night. 例如：土星在白羊座，若在白昼位于地平线之上，或夜晚位于地平线之下，则处 于得时状态；金星在天蝎座，若在夜晚位于地平线之上，或白昼位于地平线之下， 则处于得时状态。较为复杂的是火星，它属阳性，但与其他阳性行星不同，属于 夜星：它需要位于阳性星座，且在白昼位于地平线之下，在夜晚位于地平线之上。

Hayz is worth noting in a natal chart, but can be ignored in horary. If you are feeling exceptionally fussy while judging a chart that requires you to quantify something (‘How much did the last boss embezzle?’) you could take hazy as adding slightly to that quantity. 得时在本命盘中值得注意，但在卜卦中可以忽略。如果你在论断一个需要量化某 事的星盘时（例如：“上任老板贪污了多少钱？”）感到异常挑剔，那么可以将 得时视为略微增加该数量的因素。

Latitude 纬度

The ecliptic is the Sun’s apparent path around the Earth. While the other planets all follow this path, they weave up and down the sky relative to it. Imagine there is a road across the sky, along which the planets travel: the Sun keeps strictly to the white line down the centre of that road, while the other planets wander from side to side. This side to side wandering is movement in celestial latitude. 黄道是太阳绕地球运行的视路径。虽然其他行星都遵循这条路径，但它们相对于 此路径在天空中上下摆动。想象天空中有一条道路，行星沿着它行进：太阳严格 地沿着道路中央的白线行驶，而其他行星则在道路两侧徘徊。这种左右徘徊就是 黄纬上的运动。

In the northern hemisphere, which has been regarded as the standard since astrology’s birth, north latitude takes a planet higher in the sky, south latitude takes it lower. The higher it is, the less of the Earth’s atmosphere its rays need to penetrate to reach us, so

the brighter it appears. For this reason, north latitude increases, south decreases. The difference is minor, but if you are estimating quantity you could add it to the mix. If you want to describe someone, a planet having significant north latitude would make that person taller and broader, significant south latitude, shorter and leaner. 在北半球——自占星学诞生以来，一直被视为标准视角——北黄纬使行星在天空 中的位置更高，南黄纬则使其更低。位置越高，其光芒需要穿透地球大气层到达 我们的部分就越少，因此它看起来就越明亮。因此，北黄纬增强，南黄纬减弱。 这种差异是轻微的，但如果你在估算数量，可以将其纳入考量。如果你想描述一 个人，一颗行星具有显著的北黄纬会使此人显得更高大宽阔；显著的南黄纬则使 其显得更矮小瘦削。

You cannot tell a planet’s latitude from looking at the chart. Most astrological software has a latitude option somewhere; some ephemerides, such as Raphael’s list daily latitude. If you can’t find it, don’t worry: you are not missing anything important. 仅凭观察星盘，你无法得知行星的黄纬。大多数占星软件在某个选项里可以查看 黄纬；一些星历表，比如《拉斐尔星历表》，会列出每日的黄纬数据。如果找不 到，也不用担心：你并没有遗漏任何重要的信息。

Lame, azimene, etc. 跛足、暗星度，等等

Lilly gives a table of degrees that are among other things deep, azimene, smokey or void.These degrees are based upon the positions of fixed stars, which, although relatively fixed, do yet slowly move. Even by Lilly’s day, this table was hopelessly out of date, having been passed down from text to text without anyone thinking to update it or knowing when it was originally composed. It is possible that these points could be of value – if anyone could work out where they are. Until then, leave well alone. Lilly 给出了一份度数表，其中包含深星度、暗星度、烟雾状星度或空洞星度等 度数的表格。这些度数基于恒星的位置，而恒星虽然相对固定，却也在缓慢移 动。即使在 Lilly 的时代，这份表格也早已过时，它只是在不同文本间辗转抄录， 无人想到去更新它，也无人知晓其最初编纂于何时。这些点或许有价值——如果 有人能弄清楚它们现在究竟对应何处的话。在那之前，最好置之不理。

21. Lilly, p.116

22. See Avraham Ibn-Ezra, The Book of Reasons, 12th century, trans. Meira B. Epstein, Berkeley Springs, 1994; pp. 69-70 Ms Epstein suggests that ibn-Ezra refers to tables composed around 568 B.C., though I suspect they were older still. 22.参见 Avraham Ibn-Ezra（阿夫拉罕·伊本-以斯拉），《理由之书》，12 世纪，Meira B. Epstein （迈拉·B·爱泼斯坦）译，伯克利斯普林斯，1994 年；第 69-70 页。Epstein 女士认为，ibn-Ezra 引用的表格大约创作于公元前 568 年，不过我怀疑它们的历史可能更为久远。

Increasing in number 增加数量

Lilly mentions this frequently, although his use suggests that it is a tag phrase of whose meaning he is unaware. It does not mean, as is sometimes explained, that the planet is passing through degrees of increasing number, such as from 26 Aries to 27 Aries: this is the same as being direct in motion. It refers to the planet’s position on its epicycle in the ptolemaic model of planetary motions. The more astrologers relied on ephemerides to plot planetary positions, the more the knowledge of how to calculate this was forgotten. Long before Lilly’s day nobody bothered with this; nor should you. Lilly 经常提及此说法，尽管他的使用情况表明，这只是一个他并不知晓其含义 的标签式短语。它并非如有时所解释的那样，指行星正经过递增的度数，例如从 白羊座 26 度到 27 度：这与处于顺行状态是同一回事。它实际上指的是在托勒密 行星运动模型中，行星在其本轮上的位置。随着占星师们越来越依赖星历表来标 绘行星位置，如何计算这一点的知识就逐渐被遗忘了。早在 Lilly 的时代之前， 就已无人费心于此；你也不应该为此费心。

Other points 其他的点

There are yet more even more minor considerations, but unless you are an especially avid reader of ancient texts you will never come across them. If astrologers did not pass such points down, it was because they knew they were not important; so if you come acroos a term that is not listed here, you don’t need it for horary. 还有更多甚至更次要的考量因素，但除非你是特别热衷于阅读古代文献的读者， 否则你永远不会遇到它们。如果历代占星师没有传承这些要点，那是因为他们知 道这些并不重要；所以，如果你遇到一个这里没有列出的术语，你在卜卦占星中 并不需要它。

# Receptions

# 接纳关系

In a detective film it is not sufficient for the sleuth to prove that the suspect had the opportunity to commit the crime; he must also establish a motive. It is the same in the horary chart. If we are to fully understand the situation described in the chart, and to draw the correct conclusions from it, we must understand the motives of the various people involved. 在侦探电影中，侦探不仅要证明嫌疑人有作案的机会，还必须确立其动机。卜卦 占星亦是如此。若要充分理解星盘所描述的情境，并从中得出正确结论，我们必 须理解相关各方的动机。

Event-based horaries revolve upon action, and people do not act without motive. Situation-based horaries often find their entire answer in an analysis of attitude and motivation (‘What does he really feel about me?’). So it is vital that we know how to find motive, attitude and values in the chart. This knowledge is found by the study of reception. 以事件为核心的卜卦盘围绕行动展开，而人的行动必有动机。以情境为核心的卜 卦盘，其答案往往完全蕴含在对态度与动机的分析之中（“他对我究竟是何感 受？”）。因此，我们必须懂得如何从星盘中探寻动机、态度与价值观，这至关 重要。而这项知识，正是通过研究接纳关系来获取的。

The information we need is drawn from the Table of Dignities. When assessing the amount of dignity a planet has, we are concerned only with finding if it is in any of its own dignities or debilities. When assessing receptions, we must consider all the dignities and debilities it is in. 我们所需的信息来自先天尊贵表。在评估一颗行星的尊贵程度时，我们只关心它 是否处于自身的任何尊贵或衰弱状态。而在评估接纳关系时，则必须考虑其所处 的所有尊贵与衰弱状况。

The texts use confusing language for receptions, with talk of planets ‘receiving’ each other, or ‘rendering virtue’ from one to another. Far simpler to state simply ‘Venus is in the sign of Jupiter’, or ‘Mars exalts Saturn’. 传统文献在描述接纳关系时，使用的语言往往令人困惑，例如谈论行星之间“相 互接纳”或“传递力量”。其实远不如简单明了地说“金星位于木星的入庙星座”， 或“火星位于土星旺势的位置”。

Let’s work through the table again, column by column, supposing our significator is the Moon, at 3 Aries in a daytime chart. It is in the sign of Mars (first column). It is in the exaltation of the Sun, or it exalts the Sun (second column). It is in the triplicity of the Sun (because it is a daytime chart). It is in the term of Jupiter and the face of Mars. It is in the detriment of Venus and the fall of Satrun. 让我们再次逐列分析尊贵表，假设我们的征象星是月亮，位于白羊座 3 度，且为 日生盘。月亮位于火星的入庙星座（第一列）。它位于太阳的旺势位置，或者说， 它旺势太阳（第二列）。它位于太阳的三分主星位置（因为是日生盘）。它位于 木星的得界和火星的得面。它位于金星的落陷和土星的弱势位置。

“What does this tell us?”In most contexts, reception can be seen as liking or loving. The significator – in this example, the Moon – likes or loves to various extents the planets in whose dignities it falls. At its simplest, we see that in this example the Moon loves Mars and the Sun. It has a further moderate liking for the Sun, because it is in the Sun’s triplicity. It has a minor liking for Jupiter and a further, even more minor, liking for Mars. It can’t stand Venus and Satrun. “这向我们揭示了什么？”在大多数情境中，接纳关系可视为喜欢或爱慕。此例 中的征象星——月亮——在不同程度上喜欢或爱慕那些它落入其尊贵位置的行 星。最简单的理解是，在此例中，月亮爱慕火星与太阳。它对太阳还有一层中等 程度的喜欢，因为它位于太阳的三分位置。它对木星有轻微的喜欢，而对火星则 有更微弱的喜欢。它完全无法忍受金星与土星。

The concept of liking or loving may seem limited in the contexts to which it is relevant, but it is not. Suppose I am asking when my wages will arrive. If I find that the wages love me (their significator is in strong dignity of mine) I am encouraged: if they love me they will want to be with me. Traditional science saw many phenomena which modern science explains differently in terms of love, a word that had far wider application than is common today. A piece of iron, for instance, loves the magnet. “喜欢或爱慕”这一概念在其相关语境中看似局限，实则不然。假设我正在询问 工资何时能到账。如果我发现工资“爱慕”我（其征象星位于我星体的强烈尊贵 位置），便会受到鼓舞：既然它爱慕我，便会渴望与我相聚。传统科学将许多现 代科学以不同方式解释的现象都视作“爱”——这个词在当时的应用远比今日广 泛。例如，一块铁“爱”磁铁。

Just as dignities vary in their nature, so do receptions: 正如尊贵各有其属性，接纳关系也是如此：

Sign rulership 入庙

The planet loves the planet that rules the sign it is in. It sees it for what it is and loves it. Simple and straightforward. The Moon (or any other planet) at 3 Aries loves whatever is signified by Mars. 行星爱慕其所在星座的入庙行星。它看清其本质并爱慕它。简单而直接。位于白 羊座 3 度的月亮（或任何其他行星）爱慕火星所象征的一切。

Exaltation 旺势

A planet literally exalts the planet in whose exaltation it falls: it puts it on a pedestal. Exaltation carries the same sense of exaggeratedly good as it does when we are considering dignity. So whomever the Moon signifies in our example sees whatever the Sun signifies as being super-good. You will be familiar with this feeling: it is exactly what you have felt whenever you have first fallen for of clay. It is the idea of ‘the honoured guest in someone else’s house’: the guest is treated as if he were the wonderful person that he ought to be; we do not treat our honoured guests according to their true deserts. 一颗行星字面上擢升了它所在位置处于旺势的行星：即将其奉若神明。 旺势带 有与我们考量尊贵时相同的、被过度美化的意味。因此，在我们所举的例子中， 月亮所象征的人会将太阳所象征的一切视为超凡卓绝。这种感受你应该很熟悉： 它完全就是你初次迷恋某人时所体会到的感觉——那种将对方理想化，直到后来 才骤然发现偶像缺陷时的幻灭。这就像“他人家中的贵宾”这一概念：客人被当 作他理应成为的完美之人来款待；我们并非依据其真实品性来对待贵宾。

Don’t overstate this exaggeration: it does not mean that the person who is being exalted is in any way bad; it means only that they are being seen through rose-tinted spectacles. Reception by exaltation is common in horaries cast at the start of relationships. Exaltation, as you have no doubt experienced, tends not to last: the delicious bubble bursts. 切勿夸大这种美化作用：这并不意味着处于旺势的人有任何不好；这只是表明他 们被戴上了玫瑰色眼镜看待。通过旺势产生的接纳关系，在关系初始阶段所起的 卜卦盘中很常见。而旺势——正如你无疑曾体验过的那样——往往难以持久：那 迷人的泡沫终会破灭。

A querent asked about a job for which she had applied. Her significator was in the job’s exaltation (Jupiter, Lord 1, was in Pisces, the exaltation of Venus, which was Lord 10 in that chart). The querent exalted the job. Note – importantly - that this tell us nothing about the qualities of the job: we need to look at Lord 10 itself for that. But it does tell us that no matter how good a job it might be, it is unlikely to live up to the querent’s inflated expectations. 一位问卜者询问她申请的一份工作。她的征象星（该盘中作为 1 宫主的木星）位 于双鱼座——即该盘中 10 宫主金星的旺势位置。问卜者使这份工作处于旺势。

请注意——这一点很重要——这并未告诉我们这份工作本身的品质：为此我们需 要审视 10 宫主本身。但它确实告诉我们，无论这份工作可能有多好，它都未必 能满足问卜者过高的期望。

This sense of exaggeration can be a valuable part of judgement, not only when suggesting caution to infatuated lovers. Suppose our querent exalts the person he is thinking of taking to court: he thinks the other guy is more powerful than he really is. We can then look at the other guy’s significator to find out exactly how strong a case he has. 这种夸大的感觉可以是判断中一个有价值的部分，不仅限于提醒热恋爱侣保持谨 慎。假设我们的问卜者使他正考虑提起诉讼的对象处于旺势：他会认为对方比实 际更强大。此时，我们可以查看对方的征象星，以确切了解其实际的底气。

### ✸As the examples above illustrate, reception by exaltation can be hard to live up to.

In questions about the wisdom of taking on a business partner, it seems almost compulsory for the querent to have these exaggerated expectations, seeing the prospective partner as a combination of the 7th Cavalry and the Wizard of Oz. Similarly, when a fledgling astrologer asked about her career, the significator of her clients exalted her own significator. In itself, this could mean that they think she is wonderful. Very nice! As part of the overall picture, though, it showed that they expected her to be wonderful – expectation that it is unlikely anybody could match.✷

### ✸如以上案例所示，旺势所产生的接纳关系可能让人难以企及。在涉及是否应

接纳商业伙伴的问题中，问卜者几乎总是不可避免地抱有这种被夸大的期待，将 潜在的合作伙伴视为第七骑兵团和绿野仙踪的魔法师的结合体。同样，当一位初 出茅庐的占星师询问她的职业生涯时，其客户的征象星位于她的征象星旺势的位 置。这本身可能意味着他们认为她很出色。这当然很好！然而，作为整体星象的 一部分，这也显示出他们期待她是出色的——这种期待恐怕是任何人都难以满足 的。✷

Triplicity 三分

If sign-rulership is like love and exaltation like infatuation, triplicity is like friendship: warm and comfortable, but with no grand passion. In most relationship questions, our querents would be hoping for more than this, but in many contexts it will do fine. ‘Will I like this job?’ and Lord 1 (querent) is in the triplicity ruled by Lord 10 (the job): ‘Yes. It won’t be the best job in the world, but you’ll like it well enough’. 如果入庙像爱情，旺势像迷恋，那么三分就像友谊：温暖舒适，但没有强烈的激 情。在多数情感关系问题中，我们的问卜者会期望比这更多，但在许多情境下， 这也足够好了。“我会喜欢这份工作吗？”如果 1 宫主（问卜者）位于 10 宫主

（工作）守护的三分位置：“会的。这虽非世上最好的工作，但你会相当喜欢它。”

Because of the exaggeration implicit in exaltation, it is often good to find it backed up by some other reception. In our example, the Moon exalts the Sun and is also in the Sun’s triplicity, so there is something solid in the Moon’s feelings for the Sun, beneath the brittle infatuation. 由于旺势本身带有夸大的意味，因此若能发现它同时有其他接纳关系作为支撑， 通常是好的。在我们所举的例子中，月亮使太阳处于旺势，同时也位于太阳的三 分位置，因此在月亮对太阳的情感中，在那脆弱的迷恋之下，存在某种坚实的东 西。

### ✸I have regretted making this comparison with friendship. It’s not meant to be taken

literally. All I meant was that reception by triplicity has a certain amount of strength, but nowhere near as much as reception by sign-rulership or exaltation, just as friendship has a certain amount of strength, but is nowhere near as powerful as love or infatuation. It may or may not manifest literally as friendship.✷

### ✸我曾后悔将其与友谊作比。这个比喻不应从字面上理解。我的本意仅仅是：

通过三分产生的接纳关系具有一定的强度，但远不如通过星座守护或旺势产生的 接纳关系那么强烈，正如友谊具有一定的力量，但远不及爱情或迷恋那样强大。 它可能在现实中表现为友谊，也可能并非如此。✷

Term and Face 界和面

When considering dignity, we saw how these dignities are not so much a positive as they are the absence of a negative: they are better than nothing. So it is with reception. The Moon here is in the term of Jupiter: whomever the Moon signifies has a minor interest in whomever Jupiter signifies. This is better than indifference, but not by much. ‘Will she go out with me?’ and her significator is in the term or face of the querent’s: ‘Yes, she will – if her boyfriend is out of town, her fridge is empty and there’s nothing on TV’. Face shows are even more trivial degree of interest than term. 在考量尊贵时，我们曾看到这些尊贵与其说是一种积极状态，不如说是一种消极 性的缺失：有总比没有好。接纳关系也是如此。这里的月亮位于木星的得界：月 亮所象征的人对木星所象征的人有轻微的兴趣。这比漠不关心要好，但也好不了 太多。“她会和我约会吗？”如果她的征象星位于问卜者的得界或得面：“会的， 她会——前提是她的男朋友出城了、她的冰箱空了，而且电视上什么好节目都没 有。”得面所显示的兴趣程度甚至比得界更加微不足道。

Cumulatively, though, they can be significant. ‘Does he love me?’ with his significator in the triplicity and term ruled by her planet: it’s maybe not the grand

amour she longs for, but if she wants a relationship this might ye be an option worth considering. 然而，累积起来，它们可能具有显著意义。“他爱我吗？”——如果他的征象星 同时位于她的行星所守护的三分和得界位置：这或许并非她渴望的那种伟大的爱 情，但如果她想要一段关系，这或许仍是一个值得考虑的选项。

Detriment 落陷

Being in a planet’s detriment is opposite of being in its sign, so this shows hatred. The Moon here is in the detriment of Venus: whomever the Moon signifies has a clear enough view of what Venus is, and hates it. 处于某颗行星的落陷位置，与其处于它的入庙位置相反，因此这显示出厌恶。这 里的月亮位于金星的落陷位置：月亮所象征的人对金星所象征的事物有足够清晰 的认识，并且厌恶它。

Fall 弱势

This is the opposite to exaltation, so it carries a similar sense of exaggeration, showing loathing rather than hatred. Just as it is common to find the lovers exalting each other in charts cast at the beginning of a relationship, so it is common to find them in each other’s fall in charts cast when the relationship is going wrong: fall well describes the exaggerated loathing that spouses conceive for each other at such times. 这与旺势相反，因此带有类似的夸大意味，显示出憎恶而非单纯的厌恶。正如在 关系初始阶段起出的星盘中，常见恋人双方的征象星相互处于对方的旺势；同样， 在关系出现问题时所起的星盘中，也常见它们相互处于对方的弱势：弱势恰如其 分地描述了彼时配偶双方对彼此产生的、被夸大的厌恶。

### ✸ Because fall is the opposite of exaltation, it often makes sense to read fall as

disappointment. If Romeo is in the sign of Juliet’s fall, he is disappointed in her.✷

### ✸由于弱势与旺势相反，因此将弱势解读为失望往往是合理的。如果 Romeo（罗

密欧）位于 Juliet（朱丽叶）的弱势位置，那么他对她感到失望。✷

Nothing 什么也没有

There is no technical term for a planet not being in any dignity or debility of another planet. This shows complete indifference to whatever is signified by that planet. But this is not necessarily the end of the story: motives are not always direct. Maybe she doesn’t love him, but wants his money (her significator in sign or exaltation of Lord 2). 对于一颗行星不处于另一颗行星的任何尊贵或衰弱位置，并没有专门的术语。这 表明对该行星所象征的事物完全漠不关心。但这未必是事情的全貌：动机并不总 是直接的。也许她并不爱他，但却想要他的钱（她的征象星位于 2 宫主的入庙或 旺势位置）。

Ambivalence 矛盾

There are many places in the table where a planet is in both dignity and debility of another planet. For example, any planet in Cancer is in both the triplicity and fall of Mars; a planet at 4 Leo is in the detrimnet of Saturn, but also its term and face. As we saw when considering dignity, this is not contradictory: it reflects ambiguities which are part of our daily experience in relating to people, and which must be understood if we are to give an accurate picture of a situation. For instance: she loathes her husband, but does appreciate that he’s a good father to their children; he hates his wife, but likes the home comforts she provides. 尊贵表中存在许多位置，使得一颗行星同时处于另一颗行星的尊贵和衰弱状态。 例如，任何位于巨蟹座的行星都同时处于火星的三分和弱势位置；一颗位于狮子 座 4 度的行星既在土星的落陷位置，也在它的得界和得面位置。正如我们在考量 尊贵时所看到的，这并不矛盾：它反映了我们日常人际交往中那些模棱两可的部 分，而我们要想准确描述一个情境，就必须理解这些部分。例如：她厌恶她的丈 夫，但也认可他是孩子们的好父亲；他憎恨他的妻子，却喜欢她所提供的家庭舒 适。

The metaphor of liking or loving usually works well, but there are some contexts where concepts of rulership, domination or influence make better sense. For example, in charts about three-way relationships it is common to find the sinificators of the lover and the cheated spouse in each other’s sign: this doesn’t mean that they love each other, but shows the politics of the situation, who has power over whom. In some circumstances being in someone’s house (celestial house, i.e. sign) shows exactly that: being inside their home. 用喜欢或爱慕作为隐喻通常很有效，但在某些情境下，守护、支配或影响力的 概念能更好地传达含义。例如，在关于三方关系的星盘中，常见情人和被欺骗配 偶的征象星相互位于对方的入庙星座：这并不意味着他们爱慕彼此，而是揭示了 该情境中的权力动态——谁对谁具有支配力。在某些情况下，位于某人的“家” （即其星座）中，恰恰显示了这一点：身处于对方的领地之内。

### ✸Sometimes it makes better sense to read reception by detriment or fall as harming

rather than hating. ‘Is my job in the chemical plant harming me?’ Lord 10 in the detriment of Lord 1: yes, it is.✷

### ✸有时，将落陷或弱势产生的接纳关系解读为伤害，而非憎恨，更为合理。“我

在化工厂的工作正在伤害我吗？”10 宫主位于 1 宫主的落陷位置：是的，它确 实在伤害你。✷

An example of receptions 接纳的例子

Follow this, refering to the table above. Suppose the querent is signified by Mars. She is being courted by Johnny Depp and Leonardo di Caprio, signified by the Sun and Saturn respectively. 请根据上文尊贵表，遵循以下分析。假设问卜者的征象星是火星。她正受到 Johnny Depp（约翰尼·德普），由太阳代表，和 Leonardo di Caprio（莱昂纳多·迪卡 普里奥），由土星代表，的追求。

Let her significator, Mars, be at 15 Leo, in a daytime chart. Which of the two does she prefer? 让她的征象星火星位于狮子座 15 度，且为日生盘。她更喜欢两人中的哪一个？

At 15 Leo it is also in the detriment of Saturn. What is Saturn? Di Caprio. She hates di Caprio. 在狮子座 15 度，它也位于土星的落陷位置。土星代表什么？Di Caprio。她厌恶 di Caprio。

NB: this tells us only about her feelings. It tells us nothing at all about whether they are reciprocated. 注意：这只告诉我们她的感受。丝毫没有告诉我们这些感受是否得到回应。

So what do they feel about her? Let the Sun be at 4 Scorpio and Saturn at 1 Aquarius. 那么，他们对她感觉如何？让太阳位于天蝎座 4 度，土星位于水瓶座 1 度。

What does Depp (the Sun) feel about her (Mars)? At 4 Scorpio he is in her sign, triplicity, term and face: he is besotted with her. Depp （太阳）对她（火星）感觉如何？在天蝎座 4 度，他位于她的入庙、三分、 得界和得面位置：他完全为她着迷。

What does di Caprio (Saturn) feel about her? At 1 Aquarius Saturn is not in any

dignity of Mars: he is indifferent to her. di Caprio（土星）对她感觉如何？在水瓶座 1 度，土星不处于火星的任何尊贵位 置：他对她漠不关心。

Hmm. So why is he courting her then? What is of value to him? Saturn is in the sign, triplicity and term of Saturn. What is Saturn? Di Caprio. So what does di Caprio love? Himself. So he could see her as a trophy, rather than having any real affection for her. A situation which is not unusual, especially in charts about affairs. 嗯。那他为什么要追求她？对他来说什么有价值？土星位于土星自身的入庙、三 分和得界位置。土星代表什么？Di Caprio。那么 di Caprio 爱什么？他自己。所 以他可能把她看作一个战利品，而不是对她有任何真正的感情。这种情况并不少 见，尤其是在涉及婚外情的星盘中。

But look! In Aquarius Saturn is in the detriment of the Sun. What is the Sun? Depp. Di Caprio hates Johnny Depp. Maybe that is his motive for courting our querent: he wants to spite Depp by stealing the girl he’s so crazy about. 但是看！在水瓶座，土星位于太阳的落陷位置。太阳代表什么？Depp。Di Caprio 憎恨 Johnny Depp。也许这就是他追求我们问卜者的动机：他想通过抢走 Depp 为之疯狂的女孩来羞辱 Depp。

Note that, as here, negative reception can provide motivation and is as important as positive reception. As here, the major receptions will usually give us all the information that we need: we rarely need to get involved with the minor receptions. 请注意，如此处所示，负面接纳关系也能提供动机，并且与正面接纳关系同样重 要。同样如本例所示，主要接纳关系通常就能提供我们所需的所有信息：我们很 少需要牵涉到次要接纳关系。

### ✸Not all receptions are necessarily relevant. Suppose Jupiter is one of our main

significators. Another main significator being in a sign ruled by Jupiter will, in horaries on most questions, be an important point of judgement. If in the sign of Jupiter, that planet will also be in the detriment of Mercury. This does not necessarily mean that Mercury is involved in the drama. Once the main roles have been identified, be cautious about introducing new characters. Do so only if necessary to make sense of what is going on.✷

### ✸并非所有接纳关系都必然相关。假设木星是我们的主要征象星之一。在大多

数问题的卜卦盘中，另一个主要征象星位于木星守护的星座，将是一个重要的判 断依据。如果位于木星守护的星座，该行星同时也将位于水星的落陷位置。这并 不必然意味着水星也卷入了这场戏码。一旦确定了主要角色，在引入新角色时要 谨慎。除非确有必要厘清事态逻辑方可引入。✷

Mutual reception 互溶

So far we have been looking at receptions. The various dignities and debilities in which Mars falls tell us about the attitudes of the person Mars signifies. If Mars is in the dignity or debility of Venus and Venus is also in the dignity or debility of Mars, it is a mutual reception. In essence, this is all that mutual reception is: it is reception that is in some way reciprocated. 至此，我们一直在探讨接纳关系。火星落入的各种尊贵与衰弱位置，告诉我们火 星所象征之人的态度。如果火星处于金星的尊贵或衰弱位置，且金星也处于火星 的尊贵或衰弱位置，这便是互溶。本质上，互溶就是如此：它是一种在某种程度 上相互回应的接纳关系。

This reciprocity does not need to be by the same dignity or debility (Mars in the sign of Venus, Venus in the sign of Mars); it can be by any combination of digities or debilities. Mars in the sign of Venus: he lovers her. Venus in the exaltation of Mars: she’s crazy about him too. Venus in only the face of Mars: his love is unrequited – she is all but indifferent to him. We can also have ambivalent reciprocity: Mars in the sign of Venus, Venus in both triplicity and fall of Mars. He loves her; there are some qualities she likes in him, but overall she loathes him. As these examples show, considering the particular receptions the planets have for each other will tell us exactly what feeling are between these two people. 这种互惠性不一定需要基于相同的尊贵或衰弱方式（火星在金星入庙星座，金星 在火星入庙星座）；它可以是任何尊贵或衰弱的组合。火星在金星入庙星座：他 爱慕她。金星在火星的旺势位置：她也为他痴狂。金星仅位于火星的得面位置： 他的爱没有回应——她几乎对他漠不关心。我们同样可以有矛盾的互惠性：火星 在金星入庙星座，金星同时位于火星的三分和弱势位置。他爱她；她喜欢他身上 的某些特质，但总体上厌恶他。如这些例子所示，通过考量行星之间具体的接纳 关系，我们能确切得知这两人之间存在何种感受。

Negative receptions (by detriment or fall) are commonly ignored. Don’t! They are extremely important. The chart below gives examples of how they work. 负面接纳关系（通过落陷或弱势）常被忽略。切勿如此！它们极为重要。下文的 星盘示例展示了它们如何运作。

Mutual reception by dignity shows us that two planets like each other. If they like each other, they will want to help each other. So mutual reception strengthens planets. Negative mutual reception weakens them. 通过尊贵产生的互溶表明两颗行星彼此喜欢。如果它们彼此喜欢，就会想要互相 帮助。因此，互溶会增强行星的力量。负面互溶则会削弱它们。

We cannot, however, give any set value to how much a planet is strengthened, because this varies. It varies according to the strength of the reception and according to the strength of both planets.

然而，我们无法为行星被增强的程度设定一个固定值，因为这存在差异。其差异 取决于接纳关系的强度以及两颗行星各自的强度。

The more powerful the dignities in which the planets receive each other, the more they strengthen each other. Planets in each other’s sign like each other lots, so will rush to offer help; planets in each other’s face might grudgingly lend a hand if they really have to. If Mars is in the sign of Venus and Venus is in the face of Mars, Mars wants to help Venus lots; Venus has much less enthusiasm for helping Mars. But if Venus is in only the face of Mars, she may be reluctant to let Mars help her: the smaller the dignity of the reception, the less that planet can accept help, as well as the less it can give it. There is nothing abstract about this: it is simple human experience. If I am stuck in an embarrassing situation, I might gladly let my best friend help me, but would be reluctant to let a mere acquaintance see my need. 行星之间互溶所依据的尊贵力量越强，它们相互增强的程度就越大。位于彼此入 庙星座的行星非常喜欢对方，因此会急于提供帮助；位于彼此得面位置的行星， 如果实在不得已，可能会勉强搭把手。如果火星位于金星的入庙星座，而金星仅 位于火星的得面位置，那么火星非常想帮助金星；金星帮助火星的热情则低得多。 但如果金星仅位于火星的得面位置，她可能不愿意让火星帮助她：接纳关系的尊 贵程度越小，该行星接受帮助的能力就越弱，其提供帮助的能力也越弱。这一点 毫不抽象：它就是简单的人类经验。如果我陷入窘境，我会乐意让挚友帮助我， 但会不愿意让仅仅认识的人看到我的需求。

To be significantly strengthened by mutual reception, both planets need to be strong. They need to be strong by essential dignity: good guys help each other more than bad guys. They need to be strong accidentally, else they lack the ability to help or – and this is important – be helped. 要通过互溶得到显著增强，两颗行星自身都需要强壮。它们需要具备强有力的先 天尊贵：好人之间比坏人之间更能互相帮助。它们也需要具备有力的偶然尊贵， 否则就缺乏帮助的能力，或者——这一点很重要——被帮助的能力。

Consider. Positive mutual reception is like friendship. I can have a strong friendship with someone (major mutual reception), but if he is a nasty piece of work (in his own detriment) he will not help me in my hour of need. Or he may be a lovely person (in strong essential dignity), but lacks the ability to show his friendship by action (accidental debility), as if I were asking him to lend me some money and he wished to do so but could not, because he didn’t have any to lend. Or I may be so weak that I cannot be helped: I ask my friend to lend me money to pay my rent; he does so, but I head for the nearest bar and drink it all. His money has not helped me, because of my own weakness. 试想：积极互溶如同友谊。我可以与某人建立牢固的友谊（主要互溶），但如果 他是个品行不端的人（处于自身的落陷），他在我急需帮助时不会伸出援手。或 者，他可能是个很好的人（具有强有力的先天尊贵），但缺乏通过行动展现友谊 的能力（偶然衰弱），就好比我请他借我一些钱，他愿意借但没有能力借，因为 他自己也没有钱可借。或者，我可能太过衰弱而无法被帮助：我请朋友借钱给我

付房租；他借了，但我却去了最近的酒吧把钱全喝光了。由于我自身的软弱，他 的钱并没有帮到我。

So even though Mars in Taurus and Venus in Aries have mutual reception by sign, this is not very helpful: both planets are too weak to either help or be helped. The, apparently weaker, mutual reception by triplicity between Mars in Capricorn and Venus in Pisces is much more helpful (all things being equal in terms of accidental strength) because here both planets are exalted, so they are able both to help and be helped. 因此，即使火星在金牛座、金星在白羊座形成互溶（通过星座守护），这也没有 太大帮助：两颗行星都过于衰弱，既无法帮助对方，也无法被帮助。而火星在摩 羯座、金星在双鱼座之间，那种看似较弱的通过三分产生的互溶，实际上更有帮 助（在偶然力量相当的情况下），因为在此两颗行星都处于旺势，因此它们既有 能力帮助，也有能力被帮助。

If you have read other modern books on horary, you may have come across the idea that planets in mutual reception can swap places, so if Mars is in Taurus and Venus in Aries, we can regard it as if Mars were in Aries and Venus is Taurus. This is based on a blatant misreading of Ptolemy, makes no sense (I may be friends with someone, but I don’t go to live in his house and he in mine) and must be ignored. 如果你有读过其他关于卜卦的现代书籍，你可能会无意中看到互溶的行星能互换 如果你读过其他现代的卜卦占星书籍，可能会遇到一种观点，认为处于互溶的行 星可以互换位置，因此如果火星在金牛座、金星在白羊座，我们可以视同火星在 白羊座、金星在金牛座。这种观点基于对 Ptolemy 的明显误读，毫无道理（我可 能和某人是朋友，但我不会去住在他家，他也不会来住在我家），必须予以摒弃。

There is another idea that peregrine planets cannot be in mutual reception. Of course they can. A peregrine planet is like a homeless wanderer, mutual reception like friendship. A homeless wanderer can still have friends. He may not be able to help them much, but such friendship is better than nothing. 还有另一种观点认为游离行星不能处于互溶状态。它们当然可以。游离行星如同 无家可归的流浪者，互溶如同友谊。一个无家可归的流浪者仍然可以有朋友。他 可能无法给朋友太多帮助，但这样的友谊总比没有好。

Receptions in action 接纳关系的实际运作

Time to look at another chart. I am jumping ahead here, as there many points in this judgement that are explained in later chapters. For now, pay attention mainly to the handling of the receptions, then look back at this chart for the other points when you have worked further through the book. I suggest that you read through this judgement several times, following as best you can with what you have learned so far and

stretching to comprehend the other points. Work with this, referring continually to the table of dignities: you will learn far more by actively working with these judgements than by passively reading them. 现在来看另一张星盘。在此我提前引用此例，因为该判断中有许多要点将在后续 章节阐述。目前，请主要关注对接纳关系的处理方式，待你学习到本书更深入的 部分后，再回顾此星盘的其他要点。我建议你多次阅读这个判断，尽你目前所学 尽力跟进，并尝试理解其他要点。请结合此例进行练习，并持续查阅先天尊贵表： 通过积极练习这些判断，你将比被动阅读收获更多。

Did he he really love me? February 17th 2000, 9.12 am GMT, London. 他是真的爱我吗？2000 年 2 月 17 日，09:12 GMT，伦敦。

The querent wrote that she had married young, only because she was pregnant. Then she had met another man, who ‘told me such wonderful things about myself’. Then she discovered that he was sleeping with another woman. He didn’t want to do this, but she was blackmailing him into it. ‘Did he really love me? Is there a future in our relationship?’ 问卜者来信称，她早年因怀孕而结婚。后来她遇到了另一个男人，他“对我说了

许多关于我自己的美好话语”。之后她发现他与另一名女子有染。他辩称自己是 被对方胁迫发生关系。“他真的爱过我吗？我们的关系还有未来吗？”

The chart is set for the time and place at which I read her letter. She, as querent, is given the Ascendant and Lord 1, which is Venus. As querent, she has the Moon as her cosignificator. Because this is a relationship question – and only in relationship questions – we would also give her Venus as significator, as natural ruler of women; but she already has it. 此星盘根据我阅读她来信的时间与地点起盘。作为问卜者，她由上升点和 1 宫主 （金星）代表。作为问卜者，月亮是她的共同征象星。由于这是一个情感关系问 题——且仅在此类问题中——我们也会赋予她金星作为征象星（作为女性的先天 守护星）；但她已经以金星作为征象星了。

As it is a relationship question, we look to the 7th house. There are two 7th-house people involved in this situation: the husband and the lover. They can’t both be signified by Lord 7, so we must choose. Take the one about whom the question is asked, which in this case in the lover: he is given Lord 7 (Mars) and – only in a relationship question – the Sun, because he is a man. 由于是情感关系问题，我们查看 7 宫。此情境中涉及两个 7 宫相关人物：丈夫和 情人。他们不能都由 7 宫主代表，因此我们必须选择。选取问题所指向的那一位， 此例中为情人：他由 7 宫主（火星）代表，并且——仅在情感关系问题中——也 由太阳代表，因为他是男性。

His main significator, Mars, is in the 12th house. So is the Sun, his second significator, because a planet within around 5 degrees of a cusp is counted as being in the next house if it is in the same sign as that cusp. With both his significators in the 12th, the house of things hidden from the querent, we can dismiss any ideas of his black mail story being true. 他的主要征象星火星位于 12 宫。太阳（他的第二个征象星）也在 12 宫，因为如 果一个行星在宫头附近约 5 度内，且与该宫头位于同一星座，则计入下一个宫位。 由于他的两个征象星都在 12 宫（问卜者无法窥见的领域），可知其所谓“被胁 迫”的说法纯属虚构。

What does he think of our querent? To determine this, we must look to see if either of his significators is in any dignity or debility of either of hers. Neither Mars nor the Sun is in any reception with the Moon. The Sun is not in any reception with Venus. Mars is in the detriment of Venus: he hates her. 他对我们的问卜者看法如何？要确定这一点，我们必须观察他的任一征象星是否 处于她的任一征象星的任何尊贵或衰弱位置。火星和太阳与月亮均无任何显著的 接纳关系。太阳与金星无任何接纳关系。火星位于金星的落陷位置：他憎恨她。

### ✸This should read: ‘Neither Mars nor the Sun is in any significant reception with

the Moon’. The ‘significant’ fell off during typesetting. The Sun, signifying her lover

as Man, is in the face of the Moon. But this is trivial: it would need a very sensitive thermometer to distinguish between complete indifference and the level of interest shown by face.✷

### ✸此处应解读为：“火星和太阳与月亮均无任何显著的接纳关系。”“显著的”

一词在排版时遗漏。太阳（作为其情人作为男性的征象星）位于月亮的得面位置。 但这微不足道：需要极其灵敏的温度计才能区分完全漠不关心与得面所显示的兴 趣程度。✷

But she is not asking about his attitude to her now; she is asking what his attitude was in the past. So we must look into the past, which we do by backtracking the planets, sending them back in the direction from which they have come. 但现在她询问的并非他目前对她的态度；她想知道的是他过去的态度。因此我们 必须回顾过去，方法是回溯行星的轨迹，将它们送回它们来时的方向。

Mars, at 4 Aries, has only recently changed sign. It has only recently changed sign. It has only recently entered the detriment of Venus: he has only recently started hating her. Before that it was in Pisces. What was his attitude to her then? In Pisces, Mars exalts Venus. He worshipped her! 火星位于白羊座 4 度，是最近才刚换座的。它最近才进入金星的落陷位置：他是 最近才开始憎恨她的。在此之前，它在双鱼座。那时他对她的态度如何？在双鱼 座，火星使金星处于旺势。他曾视她如珍宝！

All the time that Mars was in Pisces, he was exalting her, so yes, he did really love her: he was perfectly sincere in his protestations. But exaltation tends not to last, and once the bubble burst he did not merely become indifferent to her, but began to hate her, no doubt for failing to live up to his glorious illusion. This change of attitude is shown by the change of reception as Mars moves from Pisces into Aries. 在火星位于双鱼座的整个期间，他都使她处于旺势，所以没错，他确实真正爱过 她：他的誓言完全真诚。但旺势往往难以持久，一旦泡沫破裂，他不仅变得对她 漠不关心，更开始憎恨她，无疑是因为她未能达到他光辉的幻想。这种态度的转 变，通过火星从双鱼座进入白羊座时接纳关系的变化显示出来。

When I say ‘all the time that Mars was in Pisces’, I am not referring to Mars’ real-time transit of that sign. Here, Mars’ passage through that sign can be read as ‘for a long time’. 当我说“在火星位于双鱼座的整个期间”，我指的不是火星实时运行经过该星座。 在这里，火星经过该星座的过程可以解读为“在很长一段时间内”。

With practice, you will find you begin to know what a chart will look like before you cast it, from the information you are given in the question. As soon as we read the words ‘he used to say such wonderful things about me’, we can be sure that we shall find exaltation in the chart. 通过练习，你会发现，在起盘之前，仅凭问题中提供的信息，你就能开始预知星

盘的面貌。一读到“他曾对我说了那么多关于我的美好话语”这句话，我们就可 以确信会在星盘中找到旺势。

‘Is there a future in our relationship?’ Much as we might feel that his blackmail story makes this question redundant, it is important that we answer the question asked and answer it from the chart, not from our own assumptions and prejudices. From what we have seen so far, things do not look promising: he hates her. Mars in not going to turn retrograde and go back to exalting Venus: once the bubble to exaltation has burst it may be replaced by something more enduring, but it cannot be put back together. But his other significator, the Sun, is about to enter Pisces, where it will start exalting Venus. Maybe there is hope. “我们的关系还有未来吗？”尽管我们可能觉得他那套被勒索的说法让这个问题 显得多余，但重要的是，我们要回答所问的问题，并且依据星盘而非我们自己的 假设和偏见来回答。根据我们目前所见，情况并不乐观：他憎恨她。火星不会转 为逆行并回到使金星处于旺势的状态：一旦旺势的泡沫破裂，它或许会被更持久 的东西取代，但无法恢复原状。然而，他的另一个征象星——太阳，即将进入双 鱼座，在那里它将开始使金星处于旺势。也许还有希望。

What does she feel about him? Venus is in Capricorn, the exaltation of Mars. She is still besotted with him. Venus and the Moon both signify our querent, but they show her in different ways: head and heart. Lord 1 shows the querent as thinking being and sometimes as body; the Moon is more the querent’s emotions. The opposition between them here shows graphically head and heart at odds with each other, and is common in such charts. People tend not to ask relationship questions when they are happy. 她对他什么感觉呢？金星落入摩羯座，火星旺势的位置。她仍然痴迷于他。金星 和月亮都代表我们的问卜者，但是它们代表她的不同位置：头和心脏。1 宫主代 表问卜者的思想且有时代表身体；月亮更多的代表问卜者的情绪。它们之间处于 对冲位置代表了头与心彼此明显的矛盾，这在这类星盘中很常见。人们在高兴的 时候不会去问关系类的问题。

The Moon, her heart, is in both the triplicity and the fall of Mars (the lover). Her emotios still feel warmly towards him; but this warmth is overshadowed by loathing: she must be feeling very hurt. 代表她情感的月亮，同时位于火星（情人）的三分和弱势位置。她的情感深处仍 保留着温暖；但这暖意已被憎恶笼罩：她一定感到非常受伤。

### ✸Reading reception by fall as disappointment would make sense here: her heart is

disappointed in him.✷

### ✸在此处，将弱势的接纳关系解读为失望是合理的：她的情感对他感到失望。

✷

Venus is in the last degree of Capricorn. It is about to change sign, on which its receptions will change. This change of reception shows that she will undergo a change in her attitudes – as her lover did, as shown by Mars moving from Pisces to Aries. How will her attitudes change? She will stop exalting Mars. As soon as Venus enters Aquarius it is no longer in any dignity or debility of Mars: she will become indifferent to him. 金星位于摩羯座末度，即将换座，其接纳关系也将随之改变。这种接纳关系的变 化显示，她的态度将经历转变——正如她的情人所经历的那样（由火星从双鱼座 移入白羊座所示）。她的态度将如何改变？她将不再使火星处于旺势。一旦金星 进入水瓶座，它将不再处于火星的任何尊贵或衰弱位置：她将变得对他漠不关心。

The Moon too is about to change sign. It leaves this troubled ambivalence of triplicity and fall of Mars for Leo, where it too has no interest in Mars. She is very soon to fall completely out of love with him. Is there a future in this relationship? No; largely because she will soon no longer want it. 月亮也即将换座。它将离开当前这种与火星既处三分又处弱势的困扰矛盾状态， 进入狮子座，在那里它对火星同样毫无兴趣。她很快就会完全不再爱他。这段关 系有未来吗？没有；主要因她将不再心存留恋。

That has given the brief answer to the querent’s questions. We may wish to put flesh on these bare bones by looking a little deeper. What else is going on here? 以上给出了对问卜者问题的简要回答。我们或许希望通过更深入的观察来为这些 骨架增添血肉。这里还发生了什么？

We might notice that Saturn is playing a big part in this chart. Venus and the Sun are in signs ruled by Saturn; Mars is in Saturn’s fall; the Moon is in Saturn’s detriment. When Venus changes sign and stops exalting Mars, Saturn is going to become even more important to the querent: in the first degrees of Aquarius Venus will be in the sign, triplicity and term of Saturn. So what does Saturn signify, that will suddenly become so much more significant to her as soon as she stops exalting her lover? 我们可能会注意到土星在此星盘中扮演着重要角色。金星和太阳位于土星守护的 星座；火星位于土星的弱势位置；月亮位于土星的落陷位置。当金星换座并停止 使火星处于旺势时，土星对问卜者将变得更加重要：在水瓶座初度，金星将处于 土星的入庙、三分和得界位置。那么土星象征什么，以至于一旦她停止使她的情 人处于旺势，土星就会突然对她变得如此重要？

In charts cast about affairs, presenting us with two 7th-house type people, if the lover is given Lord 7 as his significator, Saturn can be taken to signify the cheated spouse. If the querent is exalting the lover, the spouse is usually perceived as ‘the great malefic’ frustrating their possible happpiness. Does this fit with the chart? 在涉及婚外情的星盘中，若出现两个 7 宫类型的人物，且情人以 7 宫主为其征象 星，则土星可视为象征被欺骗的配偶。如果问卜者正使其情人处于旺势，配偶通 常会被视为“巨大的煞星”，阻碍他们可能的幸福。这与星盘相符吗？

There is a weak (peregrine) planet in the first house. This is an affliction to the querent. What is afflicting the querent? Saturn: the husband. 有一个虚弱的（游离）行星在 1 宫。这对问卜者是一种折磨。是什么在折磨问卜 者？土星：即丈夫。

### ✸‘Can often be taken to signify…’would be better. This identification cannot be

assumed, but must fit with the chart. If another planet fits better than Saturn, use that instead.✷

### ✸或许译为“通常可视为象征……”更好。这种指认不能臆断，必须与星盘相

符。如果有其他行星比土星更符合，则应使用那个行星。✷

Venus is in the sign of Saturn. This could mean that the querent loves her husband. But if your heart is busy exalting someone, there isn’t enough room there to love someone else. So here it makes better sense to read this as the husband having great influence over the querent, or ruling her, or even to take it quite literally: she is in his house. 金星位于土星的入庙星座。这可能意味着问卜者爱她的丈夫。但若你的心正忙于 使某人处于旺势，就没有足够空间再去爱别人。因此在这里，将其解读为丈夫对 问卜者具有巨大影响力、或支配着她，甚至可直译为：她身处丈夫的屋子里。

Saturn is in the sign of Venus. The husband loves her. It is in the exaltation of the Moon. So what does the husband really really want? The thing that he exalts: the querent’s heart. 土星位于金星的入庙星座。丈夫爱她。它也位于月亮的旺势位置。那么丈夫真正、 真正想要的是什么？他所使之处于旺势的事物：问卜者的心。

What does the querent’s heart think of him? The Moon is in the detriment of Saturn: her heart hates him. And also in Saturn’s term?: her heart sees some minor redeeming features in him. 问卜者的心如何看待他？月亮位于土星的落陷位置：她的心憎恨他。但同时也在 土星的得界位置：她的心在他身上看到一些次要的、可弥补的优点。

Note that the querent’s head/heart split, shown by the Venus/Moon opposition, makes perfect sense in her attitude to both the lover and the husband. 请注意，问卜者理智与情感的分裂（由金星/月亮的对冲相位所示），在她对情 人和丈夫的态度上都完全说得通。

Once Venus has changed sign, losing interst in the lover, it will become much more dominated by Saturn. The powerful mutual reception between these two planets will become yet stronger. This must mean a strengthening of her relationship to the husband. Note that we do not need to see an aspect between her and him to show this, because the relationship is already in existence: we don’t need to prove an event. Note

also that although she is going to become more centred on the husband（moving from sign and term of Saturn to sign, triplicity and term of Saturn) she is not suddenly going to start exalting him (both her planets move into signs where nothing is exalted). As is only to be expected. 一旦金星换座，对情人失去兴趣，它将更多地受土星支配。这两颗行星之间强有 力的互溶将变得更强。这必然意味着她与丈夫的关系会得到加强。注意，我们无 需看到她与他之间存在相位来显示这一点，因为关系已经存在：我们无需证明一 个事件。还需注意，尽管她将更加关注丈夫（从位于土星的入庙和得界位置，移 动到其入庙、三分和得界位置），她并不会突然开始迷恋他（她的两颗行星都进 入了没有行星处于旺势的星座）。这也在意料之中。

The Moon, meanwhile, is entering Leo, which is also the detriment of Saturn. Her heart will still hate him. 与此同时，月亮正进入狮子座，这也是土星的落陷位置。她的心仍将憎恨他。

### ✸It will also be in both term and face of Saturn. It is in Saturn’s term now, but not

its face. So her heart will feel a tiny increase in the minor positives she sees in him.✷

### ✸它也同时位于土星的得界和得面位置。它现在已在土星的得界，但不在其得

面。因此，她的心对他所看到的那些微小的积极面，会感到一丝微不足道的增加。 ✷

Why is her attitude to these two men going to change? Our attitudes do not change of themselves: we do not awake one morning to find that we love this person or hate that. There is a trigger that sets off these changes. The change of attitude is shown by the change of reception (as here in the change of sign). The trigger is shown by the aspect happening immediately before this change of reception. 为何她对这两个男人的态度即将改变？我们的态度不会自行改变：我们不会某天 醒来发现自己爱这个人或恨那个人。总有一个触发因素引发了这些变化。态度的 改变通过接纳关系的变化来显示（如此处换座所示）。而触发因素则通过这种接 纳关系改变之前即刻发生的相位来显示。

What aspect happens immediately before Venus and the Moon change signs? The Moon/Venus opposition. This must be the trigger – the reason for the change of attitude. What does this aspect mean? 在金星和月亮换座之前，即刻发生的相位是什么？月亮与金星的对冲相位。这必 然是触发因素——态度改变的原因。这个相位意味着什么？

Yes, we can read it as showing her head/heart split reaching a climax; but this doesn’t help us much: we are still left wondering why. 是的，我们可以将其解读为她理智与情感的分裂达到了顶点；但这对我们帮助不 大：我们仍然在疑惑为什么。

When a significator is placed right on a house cusp, it is often there for a reason. It almost is as if the chart puts it there as a way of attracting our attention, of saying ‘Hey, look over her!’ The Moon is right on the 5th house – the house of children. The Moon is ruler of that house, so could be playing a secondary role as Lord 5. The Moon is natural ruler of babies and is in the fertile sign of Cancer. So the Moon applying to Venus must show her getting pregnant. By opposition: she is not happy about this. But it is this that concentrates her mind (Venus) on her marriage. Even though her heart (Moon) will still hate her husband. It is probably in the pregnancy that the position of Jupiter, natural ruler of fertility, so prominent on the Ascendant, finds its significance. 当一个征象星正好位于宫头时，往往有其原因。这几乎就像是星盘特意将其放在 那里，以吸引我们的注意，仿佛在说“嘿，看这里！”月亮正好在 5 宫头——5 宫是子女的宫位。月亮是该宫的宫主星，因此可能同时扮演着 5 宫主的次要角色。 月亮是婴儿的先天守护星，并且位于肥沃的巨蟹座。因此，月亮入相位金星必然 显示她将怀孕。通过对冲相位：她对此并不开心。但正是这件事让她的理智（金 星）聚焦于她的婚姻。尽管她的情感（月亮）仍将憎恨她的丈夫。很可能，正是 在怀孕这件事上，木星（生育能力的先天守护星）如此显著地位于上升点的位置， 找到了它的意义。

“But who’s the father?”The aspect showing her getting pregnant (Moon to oppose Venus) has not yet happened, so the event is still in the future. Had the aspect been separating (perhaps Moon at 29 Cancer separating from opposition to Venus at 28 Capricorn) we would have judged that it had already happened, hence that she was already pregnant. So she is not yet pregnant; the boyfriend hates her; she is still in the husband’s house; the chart does not show any other suspects: the husband must be the father. “但父亲是谁呢？”显示她怀孕的相位（月亮即将对冲金星）尚未发生，因此事 件仍在未来。如果相位是出相位（比如月亮在巨蟹座 29 度，出相位与摩羯座 28 度的金星形成对冲），我们就会判断此事已经发生，即她已经怀孕。所以，她尚 未怀孕；男朋友憎恨她；她仍在丈夫的领地内；星盘没有显示任何其他嫌疑人： 父亲必然是丈夫。

We saw in passing the boyfriend’s attitude to the husband: the Sun is ruled by Saturn; Mars is in Saturn’s fall. As with our querent’s head and heart, the two significators of the lover show him in different ways. Lord 7 (Mars, here) is him as person, as thinking/feeling being. The Sun, given to him because he is a man, shows him as animal male. When I am lecturing, for the entertainment value, I refer to the division of main significator, Moon (if we are considering the querent) and Sun as head, heart and trousers. This may lack subtlety, but it makes the distinction clear enough. Had our querent not had Venus as her main significator by its being Lord 1, we would have given it to her as significator of woman, in which case it would show animal woman. As it is Lord 1, it plays a dual role here. 我们顺便看到了男朋友对丈夫的态度：太阳受土星守护；火星位于土星的弱势位 置。如同我们问卜者的理智与情感，情人的两个征象星以不同方式显示他。7 宫

主（此处为火星）代表他作为人，作为思考/感受的存在。赋予他太阳是因为他 是男性，这代表他作为雄性动物的本能。在我讲课时，为了趣味性，我会将主要 征象星、月亮（如果我们考虑问卜者的话）和太阳之间的区分称为头脑、心和裤 子。这可能不够细腻，但足够清晰地表明了区别。如果我们的问卜者不是因为金 星是 1 宫主而将其作为主要征象星，我们本应赋予她金星作为女性的征象星，那 样的话，它将显示女性的本能。既然它是 1 宫主，它在此就扮演了双重角色。

So the Sun, the boyfriend’s man-stuff, is ruled by the husband (Saturn). No doubt: the existence of the husband probably means he cannot exercise his man-stuff as much as he might wish. His thinking/feeling person loathes the husband (Mars in fall of Saturn). Which is not surprising, because it exalts his own man-stuff (exalts Sun) which is ruled by the husband. So the boyfriend is feeling thoroughly frustrated by the existence of our querent’s husband, and is therefore resentful. 因此，太阳（男朋友的男性本能）受丈夫（土星）支配。毫无疑问：丈夫的存在 很可能意味着他无法如自己所愿地充分行使他的男性本能。而他的思考/感受主 体（火星在土星的弱势位置）则憎恶丈夫。这并不奇怪，因为它使其自身的男性 本能（使太阳处于旺势）受制于丈夫的支配。因此，男朋友因我们问卜者丈夫的 存在而感到彻底挫败，并因此产生怨恨。

You may have noticed that the imminent changes of sign bring some positive reception between our querent and her lover: the Sun will enter Pisces, where it exalts Venus, while Moon enters Leo, where it is ruled by the Sun. His man-stuff (Sun) will start exalting Venus, which can probably be read here in its role as our querent as animal woman, while her emotions (Moon), still hating the husband, become ruled by her boyfriend’s man-stuff (Sun). As we have seen that the relationship between the querent and her boyfriend will not continue, we can read this as a good deal of frustrated nostalgia that they will carry with them, looking back fondly on a passion that found too little realisation. 你可能已经注意到，即将发生的换座会给我们的问卜者和她的情人之间带来一些 积极的接纳关系：太阳将进入双鱼座，在那里它使金星处于旺势，而月亮进入狮 子座，在那里它受太阳守护。他的男性本能（太阳）将开始使金星处于旺势（在 此处，金星可解读为我们问卜者作为女性的本能），而她的情感（月亮）虽然仍 然憎恨丈夫，却开始受她男朋友的男性本能（太阳）支配。既然我们已经看到问 卜者和她男朋友的关系不会继续，我们可以将此解读为：他们将怀揣大量受挫的 怀旧情绪，深情地回望一段未能充分实现的激情。

# Aspects

# 相位

Some horary questions are about a state of affairs: ‘Am I pregnant?’ ‘What will the weather be on my holiday?’ ‘Does he really love me?’ These can be judged by assessing the condition of the relevant significators. Most questions, however, ask if or when something will happen. For these, we must not only consider the condition of the significators, but see whether or not they will connect with each other by aspect. If they do, there is at least the opportunity for the event to happen; if they do not, there is not. 有些卜卦问题关乎事态状况：“我怀孕了吗？”“我假期期间的天气会如何？” “他真的爱我吗？”这类问题可通过评估相关征象星的状态来判断。然而，大多 数问题询问的是某事是否会发生或何时发生。对此，我们不仅需考虑征象星的状 态，还必须观察它们是否会通过相位彼此连接。若能连接，则事件至少有可能发 生；若不能，则不会发生。

If I ask ‘Will she marry me?’ – though this is surely a question better asked to the person concerned than to an astrologer – finding strong receptions between my significators and hers is encouraging: we love each other. But if there is no aspect bringing our planets together, no matter how we love each other there will be no marriage. 如果我提问“她会嫁给我吗？”——尽管这个问题最好去问当事人而非占星师— —若能发现我的征象星与她的征象星之间存在强烈的接纳关系，则是令人鼓舞的： 这意味着我们彼此相爱。但如果没有任何相位将我们的行星连接起来，那么无论 我们多么相爱，婚姻也不会发生。

Most questions are concerned with the future, so we are looking for applying aspects: aspects that have not yet been made, but will be made in the future. Some questions are about the past (‘Did the builder steal my bracelet?’), in which case we are interested in separating aspects: aspects that have happened. 大多数问题关乎未来，因此我们寻找的是入相位：即尚未形成、但未来将会形成 的相位。有些问题则关乎过去（“是建筑工人偷了我的手镯吗？”），在这种情 况下，我们关注的是出相位：即已经发生过的相位。

We are concerned only with the major aspects: conjunction, trine, square, sextile and opposition. These are also known as ptolemaic aspects, because Ptolemy writes about them in his Tetrabiblos, the most influential book on astrology ever written. The

conjunction is not technically an aspect, but for all practical purposes can be treated as if it were, so for simplicity it will be treated as such here. 我们只关注主要相位：合相、拱相位、刑相位、六合相位与对冲相位。这些也被 称为托勒密相位，因为 Ptolemy 在其著作《四书》——史上最具影响力的占星学 著作——中论述过它们。严格来说，合相并非相位，但在所有实际应用中都将其 视作相位处理，为简便起见，此处也如此处理。

“Why is a conjunction not an aspect?”The word aspect is taken from the Latin word for a glance. A glance, in this sense, is seen as a ray of light passing from the eyes of one person into the eyes of another. In conjunction the two planets are as one, and you cannot glance into your own eyes. Hence conjunction is not an aspect. “为何合相不是相位？”“相位”一词源于拉丁语，意为“一瞥”。在此语境下， “一瞥”被视为一道光线从一人眼中投向另一人眼中。而在合相中，两颗行星合 为一体，你无法瞥见自己的眼睛。因此，合相不是相位。

There is no place for the so-called minor aspects either in horary or anywhere else in astrology. “But Lilly mentions them.” Never to any purpose. When he was writing, they were the new hot thing in town. Now that their novelty has worn off they can be ignored. 在卜卦占星学或占星学的任何其他领域，所谓的次要相位都没有存在意义。“但 Lilly 提到过它们。”那也从未用于任何实际判断目的。在他写作的年代，它们 是当时新兴的热门概念。如今其新奇性已褪去，大可忽略不计。

Aspects can be made only if the signs the planets occupy are themselves in that aspect. Taurus is in trine to Capricorn. So a planet at 29 Taurus is trine planet at 29 Capricorn. It is not trine a planet at 0 Aquarius. It probably either will be in aspect to it, or recently has been in aspect to it, and either of these may be relevant to our judgement; but it is not in aspect to it now. 只有当行星所在星座彼此处于特定相位关系时，行星之间才能形成该相位。例如， 金牛座与摩羯座成拱相位。因此，一颗在金牛座 29 度的行星与一颗在摩羯座 29 度的行星成拱相位。但它与一颗在宝瓶座 0 度的行星则不成拱相位。它可能即将 与之形成相位，或最近刚与之形成过相位，这两种情况都可能与我们的判断相关； 但此刻它们并不处于相位之中。

To find whether one planet will aspect another, it is essential to know which planet is moving faster. As we saw when considering accidental dignities, the average daily motion of the planets is: 要判断一颗行星是否会与另一颗行星形成相位，关键在于了解哪颗行星运行得更 快。正如我们在探讨偶然尊贵时所看到的，行星的平均日运动速度依次为：

Moon 13°11′ Mercury 0°59′ Venus 0°59′ Sun 0°59′

Mars 0°31′ Jupiter 0°05′ Saturn 0°02′

When I say ‘it is essential to know which planet is moving faster’, I mean ‘which planet is moving faster right now’. This is not always the same as ‘which generally moves faster’. You will need to check your ephemeris. For example, as I write this, Mars has recently applied to aspect with Venus – possible only because Venus had just changed direction and was moving so slowly that Mars could catch it. Looking at the chart cold, without consulting the ephemeris, we would assume that Venus was separating from Mars, so any judgement based on those two planets would be wrong. There is usually at least one planet, doing something untoward, so checking your ephemeris is essential. If you don’t, your judements will be consistently wrong. 当我说“关键在于了解哪颗行星运行得更快”时，我指的是“哪颗行星此刻运行 得更快”。这并不总是等同于“哪颗行星通常运行得更快”。你需要查阅你的星 历表。例如，在我撰写此文时，火星最近正入相位于金星——这之所以可能，仅 仅是因为金星刚刚改变方向且移动极为缓慢，以至于火星得以追上它。若仅冷眼 观盘而不查星历表，我们可能会认为金星正在与火星出相位，那么任何基于这两 颗行星的判断都将错误。通常至少会有一颗行星正在做出反常举动，因此查阅星 历表至关重要。若不这样做，你的判断将始终错误。

It is vital that you know what the planets are going to do, not just what they look as if they are going to do! 你必须了解行星将要做什么，而不仅仅是它们看起来将要做什么，这一点至关 重要！

Planets do not suddenly change direction while running full tilt along their usual path. Planets gradually slow down until they are apparently stationary, then set off in the opposite direction, gradually picking up speed again. 行星不会在全速运行中突然转向。行星会逐渐减速直至停滞，然后朝相反方向出 发，再次逐渐加速。

If you are working from software and do not have an ephemeris, you can check how fast a planet is moving by clicking your chart forward to the same time next day: the difference in planetary positions will give you each planet’s daily motion at that time. 如果你使用软件工作而没有星历表，可以通过将星盘向前点击至次日同一时间， 来检查行星的移动速度：行星位置的变化将给出每颗行星在该时刻的日运动速度。

The list above is of the planets’ average forward motion. More useful for our purposes is a knowledge of each planet’s usual speed, whichever direction it is travelling in. We don’t need precision here: a rough guide, easily, easily memorable, is sufficient for our purposes. Memorise this list: 以上列表是行星的平均顺行速度。对我们的目的而言，更有用的是了解每颗行星 的通常速度（无论其行进方向为何）。我们此处无需精确：一个粗略的、便于轻

松记忆的指南足以满足我们的需求。请熟记此列表：

Moon 月亮 13 degrees 13 度 Mercury 水星 A degree and a half 1 度半 Venus 金星 A degree and a bit 1 度多一点 Sun 太阳 1 degree 1 度 Mars 火星 Half a degree 半度 Jupiter 木星 Barely moving 几乎不动 Saturn 土星 Barely moving 几乎不动

If you compare this with the list of average forward motions above, you will see that although Mercury and Venus are usually moving faster than the Sun, their average forward motion is the same. It is as if the Sun were a man taking two dogs for a walk. The man ambles along steadily, while the dogs race hither and thither, but they all reach home at the same time. 如果你将此列表与前面的平均顺行速度列表对比，会发现尽管水星和金星通常比 太阳移动得更快，但它们的平均顺行速度却与太阳相同。这就像太阳是一个遛两 只狗的人：此人稳步漫步，而两只狗四处奔跑，但它们最终都同时到家。

Consider: if the Moon is at 10 Aries, applying to conjunct Venus at 20 Aries, Venus will not have moved far before the Moon catches it. The Moon takes less than a day to travel that 10 degrees, during which time Venus will have moved on only about a degree. So the aspect would perfect at 21 Aries. If it were Mercury at 10 Aries, the situation would be quite different. Every time Mercury moves a degree and a half towards Venus, Venus moves a degree and a bit away from Mercury. It will take Mercury ages to perfect this conjunction; it will not catch Venus before Venus leaves Aries. 试想：如果月亮在白羊座 10 度，入相位于白羊座 20 度的金星，在月亮追上它之 前，金星移动不了多远。月亮走完这 10 度所需时间不足一天，在此期间金星仅 移动了约 1 度。因此，该相位将在白羊座 21 度形成。如果是水星在白羊座 10 度，情况则大不相同。每当水星向金星移动 1.5 度，金星便远离水星约 1 度。水 星将耗费很长时间才能完成这次合相；它在金星离开白羊座前将无法追上金星。

### ✸Very important: if you have that device on your software that advances the chart

through time, don’t use it! This produces nothing but confusion. Always work only from the chart as it is cast. What you are in effect doing by using this device is creating a multitude of new charts. We have one chart: the one for the time at which the question was asked.

### ✸非常重要：如果你的软件带有随时间推移推进星盘的功能，切勿使用！这只

会带来混淆。始终仅基于提问时点所绘制的星盘进行工作。使用此功能实际上是 在创建大量新盘。我们只有一个星盘：即提问时刻对应的基准盘。

Now go into the Preferences in your software and select a chart display without aspect lines. These too produce only confusion.✷ 现在请进入你软件的设置选项，选择不显示相位线的星盘视图。这些相位线同样 只会造成混淆。✷

Aspects 相位

Most readers will know how to spot an aspect, both in the chart and in the ephemeris, so I have put this information in an appendix for those who are coming to astrology afresh. If you aren’t sure, stop now and work through Appendix 3. 多数读者会知道如何在星盘和星历表中识别相位，因此我将这部分信息放在了附 录中，供初学占星学者参考。如果你不确定，请现在暂停并学习附录 3。

In horary we are concerned mainly with exact aspects. Exact means exact. If the aspect fails to perfect by even one minute of arc, it is not exact and the event that it would be shown by Venus reaching a conjunction with Mars at 22.17 Leo, but Venus turns retrograde at 22.16 Leo, thus failing to perfect the aspects, the marriage will not happen. 在卜卦占星中，我们主要关注精确相位。精确即意味着分毫不差。如果相位哪怕 仅差 1 弧分未能形成，它就不是精确的，而事件也就不会发生。举例来说，如果 金星与火星在狮子座 22.17 度形成合相才能预示婚姻，但金星在狮子座 22.16 度 转为逆行，从而未能形成该相位，则婚姻不会发生。

To show the event asked about, we need an exact aspect between the main significators. A planet that is not a main significator aspecting one that is may show other influences on the situation, without showing an event. Such aspects need to be close but need not be exact. They can usually be ignored, as with boy marrying girl: that one of them is worried about a tax demand will usually not be crucial to the judgement. But, for example, if the question is ‘Will my team win the match?’ and my team’s significator is closely squared by Saturn, this has an effect: my team is weakened. Keep to a maximum of about 3 degrees apart for this; anything beyond that is trivial. 要显示所询问的事件，我们需要主要征象星之间形成精确相位。非主要征象星与 主要征象星之间的相位可能显示情境中的其他影响，但不代表事件本身。此类相 位需要接近但不必精确。它们通常可以被忽略，正如男孩娶女孩时，其中一人对 税务问题的担忧通常不会成为判断的关键。但例如，若问题是“我的队伍会赢得 比赛吗？”，而我方队伍的征象星与土星成紧密的刑相位，这便会产生影响：我 方队伍被削弱了。对此类情况，相位容许度最大保持在大约 3 度以内；超出此范 围的任何影响都可忽略不计。

The old texts use the words platick and partile when discussing aspects. I’ll explain

them so you know what they mean, but there is no need to use them yourself. An excess of technical terms brings nothing but confusion. A partile aspect is one where the planets are in the same degree of their respective signs. Venus at 21.05 Taurus is in partile trine to Mars at 21.22 Capricorn: they are both at 21 degrees. If Venus were at 20.59 Taurus, it would not be in partile trine to Mars, because it is not at 21 degrees, even though they are within 1 degree of each other. A degree is, literally, a step (Old French), and you are either on one step or you are on another; there is no fuzzy area between them. 古典文献在讨论相位时使用 platick（不同度相位）和 partile（同度相位）这两 个词。我将解释它们以便你理解其含义，但你自己无需使用。过多的技术术语只 会带来混淆。同度相位是指行星位于各自星座的同一度数。例如，金星在金牛座 21.05 度与火星在摩羯座 21.22 度成同度拱相位：它们都位于 21 度。如果金星在 金牛座 20.59 度，则它与火星不成同度拱相位，因为它不在 21 度，尽管它们彼 此相距在 1 度以内。一度，字面意义上就是“一级台阶”（古法语），你要么在 一级台阶上，要么在另一级上；它们之间没有模糊地带。

The term ‘partile’ is superfluous, however. The planets are in the same degree: so what? To give us an event they must perfect an aspect, not merely share a degree; to show influence, they need only be within 2 or 3 degrees of each other. 然而，“同度”这个术语是多余的。行星在同一度数上：那又怎样？要给我们一 个事件，它们必须完成一个相位，而不仅仅是共享一个度数；要显示影响，它们 只需彼此相距在 2 或 3 度以内。

A platick aspect is an aspect that is not partile. As we are abolishing the term ‘partile’ we can dispose of ‘platick’ as well. 不同度相位是指非同度的相位。既然我们废除了“同度”这个词，那么“不同度” 也可以一并舍弃。

The nature of the aspects 相位的本质

Forget all ideas you may have picked up about certain aspects being ‘good’ and others ‘bad’. It is the nature of the planets involved and their attitude towards each other that show this, not the nature of the aspects themselves. 摒弃你可能接触到的关于某些相位“好”而另一些“坏”的所有观念。显示这一 点的是所涉及行星的本质及其彼此间的态度，而非相位本身的性质。

Conjunction 合相

Planets 0 degrees apart. When two planets are conjunct they are as one. The word is

from the Latin, where it is a usual word for two bodies coming together as one. But is this a desirable thing or not? In the tenderest of lovemaking or the most savage of rapes the two bodies are together: it is not the union in itself – the conjunction – that is desirable. Only the study of the dignities of the planets involved and, especially, the receptions between them will tell whether the conjunction is a desirable outcome. The chart may show me conjunct the woman of my dreams or conjunct the dole queue: these are both conjunction. 行星相距 0 度。当两颗行星合相时，它们合为一体。这个词源自拉丁语，在拉丁 语中是两个物体合而为一的常用词。但这是否可取呢？在最温柔的做爱或最野蛮 的强奸中，两个身体都在一起：并非结合本身——即合相——是可取的。只有研 究相关行星的尊贵状态，尤其是它们之间的接纳关系，才能判断合相是否是一个 理想的结果。星盘可能显示我与梦中情人合相，也可能显示我与领取救济金的队 伍合相：这两者都是合相。

Trine 拱相

Planets 120 degrees apart. Trine can happen only between planets in the same triplicity: fire signs trine fire signs, water signs water, etc. This means there is always common ground between planets in trine. So trines show things happening easily. ‘Easy’ and ‘good’ are not synonymous! If the brakes on my car fail, it will easily roll down the hill and into the river. Whether this easy contact is desirable or not will be shown by the nature of the planets (nice or nasty) and their receptions (their attitude to each other). 行星相距 120 度。拱相位只能发生在同一三分性质的行星之间：火象星座与火象 星座成拱相位，水象与水象成拱相位，依此类推。这意味着成拱相位的行星之间 总有共同基础。因此，拱相位显示事情容易发生。“容易”和“好”并非同义词！ 如果我汽车的刹车失灵，它会轻易滚下山坡坠入河中。这种轻松的接触是否可取， 将由行星的性质（善或恶）及其接纳关系（它们彼此的态度）来显示。

Square 刑相

Planets 90 degrees apart. Squares bring things together with difficulty or with delay. These may still be nice things. ‘Will she marry me?’ with our planets coming together by square may well show a ‘Yes’, but maybe I’ll need to ask her twice, or maybe there will be delays in arranging the ceremony. In many situations, delay or difficulty is only to be anticipated – ‘Will I get my tax rebate?’ ‘Will this house sale go through?’ – so a square aspect can be an excellent outcome. The key, as ever, is in the dignities and the receptions. 行星相距 90 度。刑相位使事情结合得困难或有所延迟。这些可能仍然是好事。 “她会嫁给我吗？”如果我们的行星通过刑相位结合，很可能显示“是”，但也

许我需要问她两次，或者安排仪式会有延迟。在许多情况下，延迟或困难是可以 预料的——“我能拿到退税吗？”“这栋房子的出售能完成吗？”——因此，一 个刑相位可能是个极好的结果。关键一如既往，在于尊贵和接纳关系。

Sextile 六合

Planets 60 degrees apart. The sextile is the runt of the litter when it comes to aspects. It is by far the weakest of them, but it will usually do the job. Although the sextile is an easy aspect, like a lightweight tirne, I’d put more faith in a square with good receptions. But don’t overstate this weakness; just be a little more cautious with checking whether the planets are strong enough to act and whether they wish to act. 行星相距 60 度。在相位中，六合相位好比一窝幼崽中最弱小那个。它是目前最 弱的相位，但它通常能起作用。尽管六合相位是一个轻松的相位，像一个轻量级 的拱相位，但我更相信一个有良好接纳关系的刑相位。但不要夸大这种弱势；只 需在检查行星是否足够强大以采取行动以及它们是否愿意行动时，稍微更加谨慎 一些。

Opposition 对冲

Planets 180 degrees apart. The opposition brings together only to split them apart again. Or it bring them together with the expenditure of so much effort that the result it not worth it. Or it brings them together with regret. William Lilly says that if ‘Will she marry me?’ has the significators coming together by opposition, they will marry, but will be ‘wrangling and jangling all their lives’. In the modern world, wrangling and jangling are grounds for divorce. ‘Will I get the job?’ with an opposition between Lords 1 and 10: yes, but you’ll wish you hadn’t, or you won’t stay there long. 行星相距 180 度。对冲相位将它们结合在一起，只是为了再次将它们分开。或耗 费巨大力气实现结合却得不偿失；或伴随悔恨的结合。William Lilly 说，如果“她 会嫁给我吗？”的问题中，征象星通过对冲相位结合，他们会结婚，但将“终生 争吵不休”。在现代世界，争吵不休是离婚的理由。“我能得到那份工作吗？” 如果 1 宫主与 10 宫主成对冲相位：是的，但你会后悔入职，或者你不会在那里 待很久。

If you look at the receptions, it is easy to see why this is so. If two planets are in opposition, their values are totally opposed to each other. If one loves whatever Juptier signifies, the other hates it; if one exalts whatever Saturn shows, the other loathes it. 如果你观察接纳关系，很容易明白为什么会这样。如果两颗行星成对冲相位，它 们的价值观完全相反。如果一方喜爱木星所象征的一切，另一方则憎恶它；如果 一方尊崇土星所显示的一切，另一方则厌恶它。

It is the condition of the planets and their attitudes to each other – the dignities and receptions – that show whether an aspect is fortunate. Not the nature of the aspect itself. 显示一个相位是否幸运的，是行星的状况及其彼此的态度——即尊贵和接纳关 系。而不是相位本身的属性。

Let’s look at some examples. Whenever I am lecturing in America, my hosts regard a trip to the Indian casino as suitable retribution for England’s excesses during colonial days. So suppose I cast a horary to ask if I will win: 让我们看一些例子。每当我到美国讲学，东道主总认为带我去印第安赌场是对英 国殖民历史的恰当补偿。那么假设我卜卦问自己是否会赢：

※ There is an applying trine between Lord 1 (me) and Lord 8 (the other people’s money): I win, and win easily. ※ 1 宫主（我）与 8 宫主（他人的钱财）之间有入拱相位：我赢，且赢得轻松。

※ There is a square between Lord 1 and Lord 8. I still win, but it takes a lot of effort. Maybe I have to play for hours; maybe there are lots of ups and down before I show a profit. ※ 1 宫主与 8 宫主之间有刑相位。我仍然赢，但需要付出很多努力。也许我得 玩上几个小时；也许在我显示盈利之前有许多起伏。

※ There is an opposition between Lord 1 and Lord 8. I still win (Lord 1 in contact with Lord 8). But maybe I win a pittance – not enough to cover the cost of getting to the casino. Or maybe I win but lose my winnings on the way to my car. ※ 1 宫主与 8 宫主之间有对冲相位。我仍然赢（1 宫主与 8 宫主有接触）。但 也许我只赢了一点小钱——还不够支付去赌场的路费。或者我赢了，但在去 停车场的路上把赢的钱弄丢了。

※ There is an aspect to Lord 8, and Lord 8 is in its own exaltation and conjunct the North Node. Yippee! The aspect shows that I win; the strength of Lord 8 (the other people’s money, which the aspect has shown will come to me) shows that I will win big. ※ 与 8 宫主有一个相位，且 8 宫主位于其旺势位置并与北交点合相。太棒了！ 相位显示我赢；8 宫主的强劲（他人的钱财，相位已显示将来到我身边）显 示我将赢一大笔钱。

※ There is the same aspect, but Lord 8 is in its detriment and squared by Saturn. I still win (aspect) but very little (weakness of Lord 8). ※ 有同样的相位，但 8 宫主位于其落陷位置且被土星刑相位。我仍然赢（有相 位），但赢得很少（8 宫主衰弱）。

Considerations such as these can be a major part of judgement. ‘Should I go for the

risky bet/investment at high return, or the safe option at low return?’ The answer is here. 诸如此类的考量可能是判断的重要组成部分。“我应该选择高回报的风险赌注/ 投资，还是低回报的安全选项？”答案就在这里。

Squares become trines 刑相变为拱相

No they don’t! Lilly and others would claim that between certain signs a square can be treated as if it were a trine. This is nonsense: if signs were flexible like this, the Moon would not oppose the Sun at Full Moon, the Nodes would not oppose each other, and so forth. 不，它们不可以！Lilly 及其他一些人曾声称在某些星座之间，刑相位可以当作 拱相位来处理。这是无稽之谈：如果星座可以如此灵活，满月时月亮就不会与太 阳对冲，月交点也不会彼此对冲，诸如此类。

The problem he faced was how some squares bring happier outcomes than some trines. What he lacked was the full understanding of dignity and reception that makes clear why this is so. Getting to see my best friend with difficulty is far nicer than easily meeting someone I don’t like. The key is dignity and reception. The importance of these cannot be overstated. 他所面临的问题在于，为什么有些刑相位比有些拱相位带来更愉快的结果。他所 欠缺的是对尊贵和接纳关系的充分理解，而这正是解释其原因的关键。费尽周折 见到我最好的朋友，远比轻松遇到一个我不喜欢的人要好得多。关键在于尊贵和 接纳关系。它们的重要性无论如何强调都不为过。

ASPECTS CANNOT BE FORMED IF PLANETS ARE IN THE WRONG SIGN. 如果行星位于错误的星座，则无法形成相位。

If you have come from the world of modern astrology you will be accustomed to regarding a planet at 29 Aries as conjunct a planet at 1 Taurus, or being trine a planet at 2 Virgo. This is not so. Never. Ever. No matter how much you would like it to be so. 如果你来自现代占星学的领域，你可能习惯于认为在白羊座 29 度的行星与在金 牛座 1 度的行星是合相，或者与在处女座 2 度的行星成拱相位。但事实并非如此。 绝不。永远不会。无论你多么希望它是如此。

Consider conjunction. As we have seen, conjunction is two bodies becoming one. The signs, to give them their correct name, are celestial houses. If you think your body can become one with someone else’s body while you are in different houses, you evidently haven’t tried it. 想想合相。正如我们所知，合相是两个个体合而为一。星座，用正确的名称来说，

是天上的屋子。如果你认为你的身体能与身处不同房屋的他人的身体合而为一， 那你显然没有尝试过。

Consider the trine. The trine brings together planets that are in signs of the same element. This is why it is harmonious. Suppose I am an accountant, using an office in a big block. There is another accountant in an office across the corridor, and we have a happy relationship: when either of us has a knotty problem with his books, he wanders over to get some help. We may not be the best of friends, but we have something important in common: the same triplicity – we are both accountants. 想想拱相位。拱相位将位于相同元素的星座中的行星结合在一起。这就是它和谐 的原因。假设我是一名会计师，在一栋大楼里办公。走廊对面办公室里有另一位 会计师，我们关系融洽：当我们任何一人的账目遇到棘手问题时，会走过去寻求 帮助。我们可能不是最好的朋友，但我们有重要的共同点：相同的三分性质—— 我们都是会计师。

The office next to that other accountant is rented by a dentist. If I take my knotty accountancy problem across to him, he is no use at all. It doesn’t matter how close to the wall of his office he might stand, he is still a dentist. Being within a couple of degrees of that wall does not transform him into an accountant. 那位会计师隔壁的办公室租给了一位牙医。如果我带着棘手的会计问题去找他， 他毫无用处。无论他站得离他办公室的墙有多近，他仍然是一位牙医。离那面墙 几度之内并不会把他变成会计师。

So it is with aspects. 相位也是如此。

It is possible that an aspect may perfect immediately inside the next sign. Example: Moon at 28 Aries applies to Mars at 2 Taurus. There is no connection between them now. None at all. This is not an aspect. But it will be an aspect. 相位有可能在刚进入下一个星座时就形成。例如：月亮在白羊座 28 度入相位于 火星在金牛座 2 度。它们之间此刻没有连接。完全没有。这不是一个相位。但它 将成为一个相位。

Such an aspect can show something happening after a change. But we must make sense of this change, as shown by the change of sign and consequent change of reception, if we are to allow this aspect to show the desired event. Example: ‘Will she go out with me?’ with aspect between you and her perfecting only after your planet has changed sign. Depending on what the receptions show, this might tell us ‘Yes she will – but only after you’ve got a job’. The change of sign shows a change in circumstance, and/or a change in attitude. 这样的相位可以显示某事在改变之后发生。但我们必须理解这一改变的意义，正 如换座以及随之而来的接纳关系变化所显示的那样，如果我们允许这个相位来显 示期望的事件的话。例如：“她会和我约会吗？”你与她的征象星之间的相位只 有在你的行星换座之后才形成。根据接纳关系所显示的内容，这可能告诉我们：

“是的，她会——但要在你找到工作之后。”换座显示了环境的改变和/或态度 的转变。

Limit this to a few degrees inside the next sign. If the aspect does not perfect within, at most, 3 or 4 degrees of the next sign, the thing will not happen. 将此限制在下一个星座内的几度。如果相位没有在最多进入下一个星座 3 或 4 度内形成，事情就不会发生。

Often, the aspect not perfecting until the next sign gives us a ‘No’. It is an example of frustration (see below). ‘What time today will the repairman arrive?’ The aspect perfects, but only after a change of sign. ‘He’s coming, but not today.’ 通常，相位直到下一个星座才形成，这给了我们一个“不”的答案。这是阻挠（见 下文）的一个例子。“修理工今天几点会来？”相位会形成，但只在换座之后。 “他会来，但不是今天。”

It doesn’t matter which planet applies to which. If the question is ‘Will my mother come to visit?’ this could be shown by either her significator applying to aspect mine or my significator applying to asepect hers. Who goes to whom is shown by the question itself and, if necessary, by the receptions. 哪颗行星入相位于哪颗行星并不重要。如果问题是“我母亲会来看我吗？”，这 可以由她的征象星入相位我的征象星来显示，也可以由我的征象星入相位她的征 象星来显示。谁去找谁由问题本身显示，必要时由接纳关系显示。

Dexter, sinister 右交角，左交角

In the texts you will read of planets casting ‘a dexter trine’, or ‘a sinister square’. Dexter and sinister are right and left respectively in Latin. They relate to the right and left of somebody satanding in the centre of the chart and looking outwards. 在古典文献中，你会读到行星投射“一个右交角拱相”或“一个左交角刑相”。 Dexter 和 sinister 在拉丁语中分别表示“右”和“左”。它们与一个站在星盘中 心、向外看的人的左右侧相关。

A dexter aspect is cast towards the right of this person. This means it is cast against the order of the signs. Example: a planet at 4 Gemini casts a dexter sextile to a planet at 4 Aries. 右交角相位是向此人的右侧投射的。这意味着它是逆着星座顺序投射的。例如： 一颗在双子座 4 度的行星向一颗在白羊座 4 度的行星投射一个右交角相位。

A sinister aspect is cast towrads this person’s left, which means it is cast along the order of signs. A planet at 4 Gemini casts a sinister sextile to a planet at 4 Leo. There is nothing sinister, in the modern sense, about this. 左交角相位是向此人的左侧投射的，这意味着它是沿着星座顺序投射的。一颗在

双子座 4 度的行星向一颗在狮子座 4 度的行星投射一个左交角相位。在现代意义 上，这并无任何不祥之意。

All aspects are two-way streets. If A casts a dexter trine to B, B will cast a sinister trine to A. 所有相位都是双向的。如果 A 向 B 投射一个右交角拱相位，那么 B 将向 A 投射 一个左交角拱相位。

These terms have no practical significance. I mention them only because you may find them in other books. Ideas that one is stronger than other can be ignored, because we are not in the situtation of having numerous aspects which we need to compare, and because aspects are two-way streets. 这些术语没有实际意义。我提及它们只是因为你可能在其他书籍中遇到。关于一 个比另一个更强之类的观念可以忽略，因为我们并不处于需要比较众多相位的情 境中，而且相位本就是双向的。

Indirect perfection 间接完美

As well as having one significator aspect a second significator to show an event, the event can be shown by a third planet connecting the two significators. This is called translation or collection of light. 除了以一个征象星与第二个征象星形成相位来显示事件外，事件也可以通过第三 颗行星连接这两个征象星来显示。这被称为光线传递或光线收集。

Translation of light 光线传递

Suppose we want to connect Mercury and Jupiter. Mercury is at 10 Cancer and Jupiter at 12 Leo. They are in adjacent signs, so there can be no aspect between them. If the Moon is at 11 Aries, it has just separated from sextile Mercury and is applying immediately to square Jupiter. It carries or translate (which means, literally, ‘carries across’) the light of Mercury to Jupiter, and so brings about the event. The involvement of a third party in the situation. 假设我们想要连接水星与木星。水星在巨蟹座 10 度，木星在狮子座 12 度。它们 位于相邻星座，因此彼此之间无法形成相位。如果月亮在白羊座 11 度，它刚刚 与水星结束六合相位（出相位），并立即入相位于木星的刑相位。它将水星的光 线携带或传递（字面意为“携带跨越”）至木星，从而促成事件发生。这常预示 着第三方介入情境。

Translation of light can happen in various ways, all of them variations on the basic

theme of a fast planet connecting two slower planets. As in the example here, we can have the situation where a fast planet has separated from aspecting a slower planet and is on its way to aspect another slower planet. 光线传递可以通过多种方式发生，都是快速行星连接两颗较慢行星这一基本模式 的变体。如此处的例子所示，可能存在一种情况：一颗快速行星已与一颗较慢行 星结束相位（出相位），并正在前往与另一颗较慢行星形成相位的途中。

The faster planet may not yet have made the first of these aspects, so it applies to aspect one of the significators and then goes on to aspect the other. This is common in situations where the initiating action has not yet been taken: ‘If I apply for this job, will I get it?’ 这颗快速行星可能尚未与第一颗征象星形成相位，因此它先入相位于其中一颗征 象星，然后继续入相位于另一颗。这在起始行动尚未采取的情境中很常见：“如 果我申请这份工作，我能得到它吗？”

We can have the situation where planet A goes to aspect planet B, then planet B goes on to aspect planet C. This gives a chain reaction, linking planet A to planet C. 也可能存在行星 A 入相位于行星 B，然后行星 B 继续入相位于行星 C 的情况。 这会产生连锁反应，从而将行星 A 与行星 C 连接起来。

Examples of translation: 光线传递示例：

* Mars at 10 Aries, Venus at 15 Aries. Venus is separating from Mars: this doesn’t look hopeful. But the Moon at 8 Aries will conjunct Mars and then go on to conjunct Venus, remaking the aspect and bringing the event.
* 火星在白羊座 10 度，金星在白羊座 15 度。金星正与火星出相位：这看起来并 不乐观。但月亮在白羊座 8 度将先与火星合相，然后继续与金星合相，重建相位 并促成事件。

* Jupiter at 8 Leo, Saturn at 12 Pisces. The Sun at 7 Scorpio applies to square Jupiter and then applies to trine Saturn, translating the light of Jupiter to Saturn.
* 木星在狮子座 8 度，土星在双鱼座 12 度。太阳在天蝎座 7 度入相位于木星的 刑相位，随后入相位于土星的拱相位，将木星的光线传递至土星。

Collection of light 光线聚集

The two significators both apply to aspect a third, slower planet. It is as if this third planet stands with its arms outspread, collecting the light of the two significators and drawing them together. I want to go out with the belle of the school, but don’t dare ask her. Then we both aspect the wicked headmaster, who puts us both in detention, drawing us together. The wicked headmaster has collected our light.

两颗征象星都入相位于第三颗较慢的行星。就好像这第三颗行星张开双臂，聚集 两颗征象星的光线并将它们拉到一起。我想和学校的校花约会，但不敢问她。然 后我们俩都入相位于邪恶的校长，他把我们都关禁闭，从而把我们拉到一起。邪 恶的校长聚集了我们的光线。

Example of collection: 光线聚集示例：

* Mars at 5 Taurus, Venus at 6 Aries. No aspect between them. But they both apply to Jupiter at 8 Cancer, who therefore collects their light, bringing Mars and Venus together.
* 火星在金牛座 5 度，金星在白羊座 6 度。它们之间没有相位。但两者都入相位 于巨蟹座 8 度的木星，因此木星聚集了它们的光线，将火星和金星连接起来。

* Mercury at 24 Pisces, the Moon at 22 Libra. They both apply to Saturn at 26 Gemini, who collects their light.
* 水星在双鱼座 24 度，月亮在天秤座 22 度。它们都入相位于双子座 26 度的土 星，土星聚集了它们的光线。

It is theoretically possible that we could have a collection where one of the significators has already made its aspect with the collecting planet (I have already been put in detention; all that remains is for the belle of the school to incur the headmaster’s wrath). I cannot recall having seen this in a chart, but do be aware of the possibility. 从理论上讲，可能存在一种聚集情况：其中一颗征象星已经与聚集行星形成了相 位（我已经被关禁闭；现在只等校花也惹怒校长）。我不记得在星盘中见过这种 情况，但请意识到这种可能性。

Translation and collection can happen by any aspects or by conjunction. They can be prohibited or frustrated like any other aspect (see below). Like any other aspect, the aspects here do have to perfect: exact means exact. 光线传递和光线聚集可以通过任何相位或合相发生。它们也可能像任何其他相位 一样被阻止或阻挠（见下文）。与任何其他相位一样，这里涉及的相位也必须完 美形成：精确意味着分毫不差。

In translation, the planet doing the translating must be moving faster than the other two planets. In collection, the planet doing the collecting must be moving slower. There is nothing significant about this: it is simply that the situation cannot arise if this is not so. 在光线传递中，进行传递的行星必须比另外两颗行星移动得更快。在光线聚集中， 进行聚集的行星必须移动得更慢。这本身并无深意：只是因为若非如此，这种情 况就无法发生。

Contrary to what is said in some texts, there is no set amount of reception needed to

make translation and collection work. What we do need is whatever reception makes sense in the context. Example: if my friend goes to ask Bill Gates to lend me some money (translating light from me to him), Bill Gates liking my friend could be more useful than Bill Gates liking me. If my friend goes to ask Susie to come on a date with me (translating light between me and her), Susie’s feelings for me are far more important than her feelings for my friend. So with the receptions. It is usually more important that the two significators have reception than that either of them has reception with the connecting planet. 与某些文献所述相反，要使光线传递和光线聚集生效，并不需要固定数量的接纳 关系。我们真正需要的，是在当前情境中合乎情理的接纳关系。例如：如果我的 朋友去请求 Bill Gates（比尔·盖茨）借我一些钱（将我的光线传递给他），Bill Gates 喜欢我的朋友可能比喜欢我更有用。如果我的朋友去请求 Susie（苏茜）与 我约会（在我和她之间传递光线），Susie 对我的感觉远比她对我的朋友的感觉 更重要。接纳关系也是如此。通常更重要的是两颗征象星之间有接纳关系，而不 是它们任何一方与连接行星有接纳关系。

### ✸You will often read that for translation or collection of light it is necessary that the

planets being connected are in signs from which they are unable to form a direct aspect with each other. This is not so, and contradicts examples given in the very texts from which this idea is said to be taken. It is common to find translation or collection either remaking an aspect that has already been made (see the chart on page 220 for an example) or speeding up an aspect that would eventually happen by itself.✷ 你常会读到，进行光线传递或光线聚集，需要被连接的行星位于彼此无法直接形 成相位的星座中。事实并非如此，并且这与提出该观点的原始文献中所给的例子 相矛盾。我们经常发现，光线传递或光线聚集要么是重建一个已经发生过的相位 （参见第 352 页星盘示例），要么是加速一个最终本会自行发生的相位。✷

Preventing aspects 阻止形成相位

Aspects that look as if they are going to perfect do not always do so. In astrology too, there’s many a slip ’twixt cup and lip. 看似会形成的相位未必总能实际形成。在占星学中，也存在许多在即将成功时却 功亏一篑的情况。

Prohibition 阻碍

A planet getting in the way of an aspect is said to prohibit it. This happens in three ways:

一颗行星妨碍了相位的形成，被称为对该相位的阻碍。这通过三种方式发生：

* A is applying to B when it bumps into C. Example: Moon at 8 Taurus is applying to trine Saturn at 12 Capricorn, when it collides with Jupiter at 10 Virgo. I have a date with Julie, but I collide with Lord 6: I get ill and can’t go.
* A 入相位于 B 时撞上了 C。例如：月亮在金牛座 8 度入相位于摩羯座 12 度的 土星的拱相位，却先与处女座 10 度的木星发生碰撞。我与 Julie（朱莉）有约， 但我撞上了 6 宫主：我生病了，去不了。

* A is applying to B, but C aspects B first. Example: Venus at 12 Libra applies to square Mars at 15 Cancer, but before this aspect perfects Mercury at 14 Virgo perfects a sextile with Mars. I have a date with Julie, but before I get to her door to collect her, some other guy turns up and whisks her away.
* A 入相位于 B，但 C 先与 B 形成相位。例如：金星在天秤座 12 度入相位于巨 蟹座 15 度火星的刑相位，但在该相位形成前，处女座 14 度的水星先与火星完成 了六合相位。我与 Julie 有约，但在我到她家门口接她之前，另一个家伙出现并 把她带走了。

* A is applying to B, but before this aspect perfects, C aspects A. Example: Venus at 12 Libra applies to square Mars at 15 Cancer, but before this aspect perfects the Moon at 10 Libra conjuncts Venus. I have a date with Julie, but before I leave to meet her Jane says she wants me back, so I don’t go.
* A 入相位于 B，但在该相位形成前，C 与 A 形成相位。例如：金星在天秤座 12 度入相位于巨蟹座 15 度火星的刑相位，但在该相位形成前，天秤座 10 度的 月亮与金星。我与 Julie 有约，但在我动身去见她之前，Jane（简）说她想与我 复合，所以我没有去。

### ✸Prohibitions also work retrospectively. Suppose the question is ‘Did Romeo kiss

Juliet?’ Venus (Romeo) is at 10 Aries. Mars (Juliet) is at 5 Aries. That Venus is separating from conjunction with Mars shows, ‘Yes, he did’. But suppose Saturn is at 8 Aries. If we rewind Venus till it makes its conjunction with Mars, it bumps into Saturn first. This prohibits that past conjunction with Mars. So far as we are concerned, that conjunction never happened. So no, he didn’t kiss her.

### ✸阻碍也具有追溯效力。假设问题是“Romeo（罗密欧）吻了（朱丽叶）吗？”

金星（Romeo）在白羊座 10 度，火星（Juliet）在白羊座 5 度。金星正与火星出 合相位显示“是的，他吻了”。但假设土星在白羊座 8 度。如果我们回溯金星直 至它与火星形成合相，它会先撞上土星。这就阻碍了过去与火星的那个合相。就 我们所关心的而言，那个合相从未发生。所以，不，他没有吻她。

Important: it is the significator’s own aspects that concern us. If we want A to aspect B, the fact that in real time C aspect D first is irrelevant. It has nothing to do with the aspect we are interested in, so it does not prohibit. C would prohibit only if it aspected

A or B before their own aspect perfected. We are rarely – very rarely – concerned with real time.✷ 重要：我们只关心征象星自身的相位。如果我们希望 A 与 B 形成相位，那么在 现实时间中 C 先与 D 形成相位这一事实是无关的。它与我们感兴趣的相位无关， 因此不构成阻碍。只有 C 在 A 与 B 自身的相位形成之前，与 A 或 B 形成相位， 才会构成阻碍。我们很少——极少——关心现实时间。✷

Frustration 挫败

This is really a particular example of prohibition. A is applying to B, but before the aspect is made, B makes an aspect with C. Example: Venus at 8 Aquarius applies to sextile Mars at 12 Aries, but before the aspect perfects, Mars conjuncts Jupiter at 14 Aries. I plan to propose to Julie, but before I do so she elopes with Alphonse. 这实际上是阻碍的一个具体例子。A 入相位于 B，但在相位形成前，B 与 C 形成 了相位。例如：金星在宝瓶座 8 度入相位于白羊座 12 度火星的六合相位，但在 相位形成前，火星与白羊座 14 度的木星合相。我计划向 Julie 求婚，但在我行动 之前，她与 Alphonse（阿方索）私奔了。

B entering the next sign before A can perfect the aspect can usually be taken as a frustration. B 在 A 能完成相位前进入下一个星座，通常也可视为一种挫败。

Refrenation 违约

This is an old legal term for breaking a contract. A is applying to B, but before the aspect perfects A turns retrograde, so the aspect fails to perfect. Example: Mercury at 17 Sagittarius applies to square Jupiter at 19 Virgo, but at 18 Sagittarius Mercury turns retrogarde, failing to make the aspect.
