Julie has accepted my proposal, but on the morning of the wedding she comes to her senses and runs away. No matter how close the planets get, if they do not perfect, the event will not happen. A planet turning retrograde usually shows that person changing their mind. 这是一个古老的表示违反合同的法律术语。A 入相位于 B，但在相位形成前 A 转为逆行，导致相位未能形成。例如：水星在射手座 17 度入相位于处女座 19 度木星的刑相位，但在射手座 18 度水星转为逆行，未能形成该相位。Julie 接受 了我的求婚，但在婚礼当天早上她醒悟过来并逃跑了。无论行星多么接近，如果 相位未能形成，事件就不会发生。行星转为逆行通常显示该人所代表的一方改变 了主意。

NB: all these points work by conjunction and all aspects. When you read Lilly’s description of them and find him speaking of ‘corporeal aspects’, he means aspects

that are body to body in contrast to those that are only orb to orb, i.e. he means that the aspects must be exact. ‘Corporeal aspect’ does not mean conjunction. 注意：以上所有要点都适用于合相及所有相位。当你读到莉莉对此的描述，发现 他提到“实体相位”时，他指的是身体对身体的相位，以区别于仅靠容许度计算 的相位，即，他指的是相位必须是精确的。“实体相位”并非特指合相。

Don’t get stressed about these technical terms. All we are saying here is, ‘Either we can join our significators in a plausible fashion, or we can’t’. The context is the key. The chart is giving us a picture of the situation: if the connection in the chart makes sense in the life, it will work. The touchstone always is ‘What makes sense in context?’ 不必为这些技术术语感到压力。我们在此所阐述的核心是：“我们要么能以合 理的方式连接我们的征象星，要么不能。”情境是关键。星盘为我们描绘了事态 的图景：如果星盘中的连接在现实生活中讲得通，它就会生效。试金石始终是“在 情境中什么讲得通？”

Preventions do not always prevent. Consider the example above, where my collision with Lord 6 shows my falling ill and so not going on the date. Perhaps I collide with Lord 6, but dose myself with remedies and go on the date anyway. Whether the prevention stops the event or not depends on three factors: 阻碍并非总是能阻止事件发生。考虑上面的例子，我撞上 6 宫主显示我生病因此 未能赴约。也许我撞上了 6 宫主，但我自己服药治疗，无论如何还是去赴约了。 阻碍是否会阻止事件发生，取决于三个因素：

* the strength of the various planets
* 各行星的强弱

* the receptions
* 接纳关系

* the context. Or, in other word, common sense.
* 情境。或者，换句话说，常识。

How strong are the planets? If I am strong and the illness is weak, I may well be able to shrug is off. Is the prevented planet strong enough to overcome the prevention? 行星有多强？如果我强大而疾病弱小，我很可能能够摆脱它。被阻碍的行星是否 有足够的力量克服阻碍？

What are the reception? The receptions show attitude, and so they show how much the prevented planet wants to overcome the obstruction. Am I crazy with love for my date, or am I going out with her only because I’ve nothing better to do ? The more the planet wants to perfect the aspect, the more it will strive to overcome the prevention. 接纳关系如何？接纳关系显示态度，因此也显示了被阻碍的行星有多想克服障碍。 我是为约会对象爱得疯狂，还是仅仅因为没有更好的事可做才和她约会？行星越

想完成相位，它就越会努力克服阻碍。

What is the situation? It is always helpful if we can identify what the preventing planet shows, although this is not always possible. Do this by looking at the houses it rules and then bouncing possibilities off the querent to find one that seems likely. The more we understand the situation, the more we can tell if the prevention will hold or not. Example: boy goes to meet girl. Is their date ten minutes in a coffee-shop or a romantic evening on which he has already invested large amounts of time and money? The illness shown by Lord 6 might prevent the former even if it were only mild, but would need to be far stronger to prevent the latter. 情境如何？如果我们能识别出阻碍行星所代表的事物，通常很有帮助，尽管这并 非总能做到。可以通过观察它所守护的宫位，然后向问卜者提出各种可能性来找 到看似合理的一个。我们对情境理解得越深入，就越能判断阻碍是否会成立。例 如：男孩去见女孩。他们的约会是在咖啡店的十分钟小聚，还是他已经投入了大 量时间和金钱的浪漫夜晚？6 宫主显示的疾病如果是小病可能阻止前者，但需重 病才能阻断后者。

Especially in long-term questions, aspects that would otherwise prevent can be regarded as events happening along the way, but which are not obstacles. So in a general enquiry of ‘When will I die?’ this encounter with Lord 6 could show a bout of illness, but it will not prevent me dying at some point. 尤其是在长期问题中，原本会造成阻碍的相位可被视为途中发生的事件，但并非 无法逾越的障碍。因此，在“我何时会死？”这种一般性询问中，与 6 宫主的这 次相遇可能显示一段患病时期，但它不会阻止我在某个时间点死亡。

The more we are able to understand the situation, which we can do by a careful analysis of the chart, the more we can suggest ways of circumventing preventions. Here horary goes beyond the merely predictive. ‘Yes, she’s longing for you to propose; but you’ll need to act fast because she’s getting tired of waiting and there’s this other guy who’s keen on her’. ‘Yes, you will get the job. Don’t let being ill stop you going to the interview.’ 我们越能理解情境——这可以通过仔细分析星盘来实现——就越能提出规避阻 碍的方法。在此，卜卦超越了单纯的预测功能。“是的，她渴望你求婚；但你需 要快点行动，因为她已经等得不耐烦了，而且有另一个家伙对她很感兴趣。”“是 的，你会得到这份工作。别让生病阻止你去面试。”

### ✸Let’s have another example. I plan to drive to the city, but the road is blocked. My

journey is prohibited. I may be delighted at this: ‘Yippe, I don’t have to visit weird Uncle Igor after all!’ In which case I have no interest in removing or circumventing the prohibition. It may be that I can take another route or catch the train, so I can avoid the prohibition. In the chart this could be shown by a second aspect connecting me to the thing asked about, but without bumping into the prohibiting planet. Or it may be that my brother owns a bulldozer and can remove the tree that is blocking the

road. This might be shown by a translation of light connecting me to my goal, again avoiding the prohibiting planet. When trying to identify what the prohibition is and what, if anything, can be done about it, remember that basic principle: the chart is not an abstraction; it is a reflection of the reality of the situation. ✷

### ✸让我们再看一个例子。我计划开车进城，但道路被封锁了。我的行程被阻碍

了。我可能为此高兴：“太好了，我终于不用去拜访古怪的 Igor（伊戈尔）叔叔 了！”那样的话，我就没有兴趣去消除或规避这个阻碍。也许我可以走另一条路 线或乘火车，从而避开阻碍。在星盘中，这可能显示为第二个相位将我与所问之 事连接起来，但没有撞上阻碍行星。或者，也许我兄弟有一台推土机，可以移开 堵路的树。这可能通过光线传递将我连接到目标来显示，同样绕开了阻碍行星。 当试图识别阻碍是什么以及可以为此做什么（如果有的话）时，请记住那个基本 原则：星盘不是抽象的；它是情境现实的反映。✷

Bonatti says that a conjunction cannot be prohibited by an aspect.It demonstrably can, but a conjunction is certainly more likely to be able to overcome the prohibition. As discussed above, consider the planets’ strengths and receptions, together with the reality of the situation, to decide whether the prohibition will prohibit. Bonatti（伯纳提）认为合相不能被相位所阻碍。事实显然可以，但合相确实更 有可能克服阻碍。如前所述，需综合考虑行星的强弱、接纳关系以及情境现实， 来判断阻碍是否会生效。

23. Bonatus, aphorism 31. 23.Bonatus, 箴言 31

The Moon’s aspects rarely prohibit, unless it is ruling a house which would make sense of the prohibition. If Capricorn rises in the chart for ‘Will I get the job?’ Cancer will be on the 7th cusp, so the Moon will signify my rivals for the job. If the Moon prohibits an aspect between Lord 1 and Lord 10, then, this prohibition would make sense: my rival gets the job. 月亮的相位很少构成阻碍，除非它守护某个能使阻碍在情境中讲得通的宫位。例 如在“我能得到这份工作吗？”的星盘中，若摩羯座上升，则巨蟹座在 7 宫头， 因此月亮将象征我的工作竞争者。如果月亮阻碍了 1 宫主与 10 宫主之间的相位， 那么这种阻碍就讲得通：是我的竞争者得到了这份工作。

### ✸ “Can a conjunction or opposition by antiscion prohibit?” It depends on the

context. The better able we are to judge what that antiscial conjunction or opposition signifies, the better able we will be to decide if it will prohibit. ✷

### ✸ “映点的合相或对冲相位能构成阻碍吗？”这取决于情境。我们越能判断该

映点合相或对冲相位所象征的意义，就越能决定它是否会阻碍。✷

Note that a benefic can prohibit as much as a malefic. ‘Will I get the job?’ My planet

is going towards the job’s planet, but a strong Jupiter gets in the way. By analysing the chart I see that this means I win the lottery. This is very nice, but it still prevents me getting the job. 请注意，吉星和凶星一样都能构成阻碍。例如“我能得到这份工作吗？”我的行 星正朝向代表工作的行星，但一颗强大的木星挡在了中间。通过分析星盘，我发 现这意味着我中了彩票。这固然是好事，但它仍然阻止了我得到那份工作。

You may have noticed that prohibition and translation of light can look much the same. Which is which will be shown by the context and the receptions. Consider: I am in the schoolyard, longing for the glamorous Nancy. I ask my friend to go and tell her that I am pining for her. He walks across the yard to her. But does he give her my message, thus translating light from me to her, or does he chat her up himself, thus prohibiting my aspect to her? His physical action of walking across the yard is exactly the same in either case. Look at his planet and its receptions. Is he an honourable lad who likes me more than he likes Nancy, or is he morally dubious and crazy about her? 你可能已经注意到，阻碍和光线传递看起来可能非常相似。究竟是哪一种，将由 情境和接纳关系来显示。试想：我在校园里，渴望见到迷人的 Nancy（南希）。 我请我的朋友去告诉她我多么思念她。他穿过院子走向她。但他是转达了我的消 息（从而将我的光线传递给她），还是自己去和她搭讪（从而阻碍了我与她的相 位）？他穿过院子的物理动作在两种情况下是完全一样的。观察他的行星及其接 纳关系。他是一个更喜欢我而不是 Nancy 的诚实小伙，还是一个道德可疑且为她 疯狂的家伙？

In most horaries we are concerned only with the next aspect a planet makes, or sometimes its next two aspects if there is a translation of light. Do not push planets through aspect after aspect (‘The Moon goes to square Mars, then to conjunct Saturn, then trine Venus, then…’). It is most unlikely that these later aspects will be relevant to the issue. 在大多数卜卦中，我们只关心行星形成的下一个相位，或者如果存在光线传递， 有时也关心其下两个相位。不要将一个行星连续推进通过一个又一个相位（“月 亮入相位于火星的刑相位，然后入相位于土星的合相，再然后入相位于金星的拱 相位，然后……”）。这些后续相位与所问事件相关的可能性极低。

What this amounts to is: Keep to the point! 这归根结底是：紧扣要点！

### ✸Student find this a hard one to grasp, so I repeat: do not push planets through

aspect after aspect! Unless there is a translation of light, the first aspect the planet makes will prohibit any subsequent aspect. Prohibition means just what it says on the tin: so far as we are concerned, that subsequent aspect does not happen.

### ✸学生发现这一点很难掌握，所以我重申：不要将一个行星连续推进通过一个

又一个相位！ 除非存在光线传递，否则行星形成的第一个相位将阻碍任何后续

相位。阻碍就是其字面意思：就我们所关心的而言，那个后续相位不会发生。

Nor can we move planets backwards and forwards through signs. Except in very rare cases, where we know the event asked about must happen (such as discussed on p.215) we can move a planet into its next sign only if it is currently in the last 3 or 4 degrees of its present sign. And then into only the first 3 or 4 degrees of the next sign. Similarly, we can push a planet back into its previous sign only if now in the first 3 or 4 degrees of its present sign, and then into only the last 3 or 4 degrees of the previous sign. ✷ 我们也不能来回移动行星跨越星座。除极少数情况外（例如第 347 页讨论的已知 所问事件必然发生的情况），我们只能在一颗行星当前处于其所在星座最后 3 或 4 度时，将其推进到下一个星座。且只能推进到下一个星座的最初 3 或 4 度。 类似地，只有在一颗行星目前处于其所在星座的最初 3 或 4 度时，我们才能将其 推回前一个星座，且只能推回前一个星座的最后 3 或 4 度。✷

Orbs 容许度

This is another technical term which must be explained because you will come across it in the texts, but which has no practical use. Orb is probably the most moverrated concept in traditional astrology. 这是另一个必须解释的技术术语，因为你会在文献中遇到它，但它没有实际用处。 容许度或许是传统占星学中最被高估的概念。

Each planet is said to have an orb around it. This is like an aura or a forcefield, except that it extends not only around the body of the planet, but around the points to which the planet casts its aspects. So if a planet has an orb of 10 degrees, this means 10 degrees around the planet, 10 degrees around its square, its trine, its sextile and its opposition. 据说每颗行星周围都有一个容许度范围。这就像光环或力场，只不过它不仅环绕 行星本体，也环绕行星投射其相位的那些点。因此，如果一颗行星有 10 度的容 许度，这意味着围绕行星本体 10 度，以及围绕它的刑相位点、拱相位点、六合 相位点和对冲相位点各 10 度。

The word ‘orb’ refers to the diameter of this force-field, which has the planet in its centre. The radius of the force-field is called the moitie (French for half). The distance to which the orb extends in any one direction is the moitie. It is, of course, the moitie that concerns us, not the orb, just as with a boxer we are concerned with his ‘reach’, which is how far he can punch with either hand, not how far he can stretch from fingertip to fingertip. “Orb”一词指这个以行星为中心的力场的直径。这个力场的半径被称为“moitie” （法语，意为“一半”）。容许度在任何单一方向延伸的距离就是“moitie”。

当然，我们所关心的是“moitie”而非“orb”，就像对拳击手我们关心的是他的 “臂展”（即他每只拳头能击打到的距离），而不是他指尖到指尖的伸展距离。

The theory is that when the edge of one planet’s moitie touches the edge of another planet’s moitie, they are in aspect by orb. Example: if planet A has an orb of 10 degrees, its moitie will be half this: 5 degrees. If planet B has an orb of 8 degrees, its moitie will be 4 degrees. When the planets are exactly 9 degrees apart (the sum of their two moities: 5+4) they are touching by orb – as if we had two boxer just touching each other’s glove at full stretch. 理论认为，当一颗行星的“moitie”边缘触及另一颗行星的“moitie”边缘时，它 们就通过容许度形成相位。例如：如果行星 A 的容许度为 10 度，其“moitie” 就是一半：5 度。如果行星 B 的容许度为 8 度，其“moitie”就是 4 度。当两颗 行星恰好相距 9 度时（两者“moitie”之和：5+4），它们通过容许度触及—— 就像两个拳击手在完全伸展时手套刚好碰到。

“What does this mean?”Absolutely nothing. Which is why you don’t need to bother with it. “这意味着什么？” 毫无意义。这就是为什么你无需为此费神。

“Why does it mean nothing?”In the first place, orbs do not come to a sharp end. The planets’ auras are not really like boxers’ arms which can reach exactly so far and no further. The aura gradually peters away into insignificance. This is why Lilly gives two different lists of the sizes of the planets’ orbs, saying he uses whichever he happens to remember, and why I am not giving such a list here: it is a list of what does not exist. “为什么它毫无意义？” 首先，容许度并非戛然而止。行星的光环并不真的像 拳击手的手臂那样只能到达确切的距离而无法更远。光环是逐渐减弱至微不足道 的。这就是为什么莉莉给出了两份不同的行星容许度大小列表，并说他用他碰巧 记得的那份，也是为什么我在此不提供这样一份列表：它列出的东西并不存在。

24. Lilly, p. 107.

Any two planet in the same sign have an effect on each other, no matter how far apart they might be. Any two planets in signs that signs that aspect each other have such an effect. They behold each other. Beholding plays only a tiny role in horary, but is of great significance in natal work – it is probably the most underrated concept in traditional astrology. It is like peripheral vision: two planets may be a long way apart by degree, but if they are in signs that behold each other（literally, that can see each other）it is as if they are in each other’s field of peripheral vision. While this may not seem much, any car driver will know how aware we really are of what is at the edges of our visual field. 任何两颗在同一星座的行星，无论相距多远，都会彼此影响。任何两颗位于彼此 成相位的星座中的行星，也有这样的影响。它们彼此“注视”。“注视”在卜卦

中作用甚微，但在本命工作中意义重大——它或许是传统占星学中最被低估的概 念。这就像外围视觉：两颗行星在度数上可能相距甚远，但如果它们位于彼此“注 视”（字面意思，即能看到对方）的星座中，就好像它们在彼此的视野外围。虽 然这看起来作用不大，但任何司机都知道我们对视野边缘的事物实际有多敏感。

In horary, we are concerned mainly with planets exactly aspecting each other. Exact means exact, so orb and moitie have no place here. We are sometimes concerned with planets close to each other, casting an influence on each other. But the maximum separation for this to be worth noting, whether by conjunction or aspect, is around 3 degrees: much less than the theory of orb and moitie would have it. On either count, orbs are useless. 在卜卦中，我们主要关心行星是否精确地彼此形成相位。精确意味着分毫不差， 因此容许度和“moitie”在此没有地位。我们有时关心彼此接近、相互施加影响 的行星。但值得注意的这种影响的最大间距，无论是合相还是相位，都在 3 度左 右：远小于容许度和“moitie”理论所规定的距离。无论如何，容许度是无用的。

There are those who regard the point at which the moities meet as a kind of starting gate: if the planets are not within that distance when the chart is set they cannot go on to form an aspect. Of course they can. This idea has no support anywhere in the texts and is contrary to reason: it is the equivalent of saying that nothing can come from my peripheral vision into my full field of view. 有些人将“moitie”相遇的点视为一种起跑门：如果行星在星盘设定的时刻不处 于该距离内，它们就无法继续形成相位。它们当然可以。这种观点在文献中没有 任何支持，且违背常理：这等同于说，没有任何东西能从我的外围视觉进入我的 完整视野。

NB: when modern astrologers speak of orbs, they usually attach them to aspects rather than to planets (‘A sextile has an orb of X degrees’) and they mean the radius of the force-field, not its diameter. Modern ‘orb’ = traditional ‘moitie’. 注意：当现代占星师谈及容许度时，他们通常将其附着于相位而非行星（“一个 六合相位的容许度是 X 度”），并且他们指的是力场的半径，而非直径。现代 “orb” = 传统“moitie”。

Now you know what orbs are, you can forget all about them. 现在你知道了容许度是什么，你可以完全忘记它们了。

Retrograde aspects 逆行相位

The texts are often negative about aspects made when one or, especially, both planets are retrograde. But usually the context shows a good reason for this retrogradation. It is common when the person signified by the retrograde planet is coming back, either

literally or metaphorically. If the question were, ‘Will I get back with my old boyfriend?’ the significators coming together to an aspect with one of them retrograde would make sense in the context. 古典文献通常对在一颗或（尤其是）两颗行星皆逆行时形成的相位持负面看法。 但通常情境会为这种逆行提供一个合理的解释。当逆行行星所象征的人实际或象 征性地“返回”时，这种情况很常见。如果问题是“我会和我的前男友复合吗？”， 征象星在其中一个逆行的情况下形成相位，在情境中就说得通。

Aspects between two retrograde planets are rare. If there were a context to support the idea that both parties were coming back (bosses and workers going back to the negotiating table, for instance), this too would not carry any negative indications. Without such a context, however, it must be regarded as against the natural order of things, so giving the sense that matters will not fall out well. 两颗逆行行星之间的相位较为罕见。如果有情境支持双方都在“返回”的想法（例 如，老板和工人重回谈判桌），那么这也不会带有任何负面指示。然而，若无此 类情境，则必须视其为违背事物的自然秩序，从而给人以事态发展不会顺利之感。

Separating aspects 出相位

As we have seen, these show things that have happened in the past. But what if the significators that we are hoping will show an applying aspect (something happening in the future) are in fact separating from aspect to each other? 如我们所见，出相位显示的是过去已发生的事。但如果我们希望显示入相位（未 来某事将发生）的征象星，实际上却正彼此出相位，又该如何判断？

Judgement will depend on the context. In many questions this can be taken as ‘You’ve come as close to that thing as you are going to, and you’re not getting any closer’. If the thing in question is the woman of the querent’s dreams, this is not a favourable answer; if the thing in question is death, the querent will be delighted. 判断将取决于情境。在许多问题中，这可以理解为“你已经尽可能接近那件事了， 但不会更近了”。如果所问之事是问卜者梦寐以求的女子，这不是一个有利的答 案；如果所问之事是死亡，问卜者则会欣喜。

Sometimes the context supports the idea that the separating aspect has put events in motion, so if nothing untoward is happening to the significators in the future, we can judge that things are rolling and will proceed to their intended outcome. If the question is ‘Will I marry Fred?’ when the marriage has already been agreed, a separating aspect could well show the agreement being made. If there is nothing obstructive happening in the chart, the wedding will take place as planned. If the question were ‘Will I marry Fred, whom I met for the first time two hours ago?’ a separating aspect would be a definite No.

有时，情境支持这样的观点：出相位已经使事件启动，因此，如果征象星在未来 没有发生异常情况，我们可以判断事情正在推进并将达到预期结果。如果问题是 “我会和 Fred（弗雷德）结婚吗？”，而婚姻已经商定，那么一个出相位很可能 显示协议已经达成。如果星盘中没有任何阻碍性事件发生，婚礼将按计划举行。 如果问题是“我会和两小时前初次见面的 Fred 结婚吗？”，那么一个出相位将 明确表示“不会”。

Placement 位置

In some questions, we do not need an aspect. You will find many examples of this in the chapters on chart interpretation. This is common in questions that ask about a state of affairs rather than a specific event: ‘Am I pregnant?’ Lord 5 (the baby) in the 1st house gives a clear picture of the baby inside the querent: ‘Yes, you are’. ‘Where is the book?’ The lost book is where it is, regardless of what might be happening to it. Its significator’s house placement will show its location. 在某些问题中，我们不需要相位。你会在星盘解读章节中找到许多这样的例子。 这在询问事态状况而非具体事件的问题中很常见：“我怀孕了吗？”5 宫主（代 表孩子）在 1 宫清晰地描绘了孩子在问卜者体内的画面：“是的，你怀孕了。” “书在哪里？”丢失的书就在它所在的地方，不管它可能发生了什么。其征象星 的宫位位置将显示其地点。

There are other contexts where placement alone will give the answer to an event-based judgement. ‘Will I win this tennis match?’ with Lord 7 just inside the 1st house: my opponent is in my power – Yes, I will win. 在其他情境中，仅凭落宫就能给出基于事件的判断答案。“我会赢得这场网球比 赛吗？”7 宫主刚好在 1 宫内：我的对手在我的掌控之中——是的，我会赢。

But in most contexts placement shows desire or fear rather than an event. ‘Will she marry me?’ My significator on the 7th cusp is not a strong testimony for ‘Yes’. It shows that I want her to marry me, and so the marriage is more likely than if I don’t want her to, but it shows no more than that. ‘Will I get the job?’ with Lord 1 on the 10th cusp. I clearly want the job, and so am more likely to get it than if I didn’t want it; but no more than that. It does not show a Yes. 但在大多数情境中，位置显示的是欲望或恐惧，而非事件本身。“她会嫁给我吗？” 我的征象星在 7 宫头，并不是一个有力的“是”的证据。它显示我想要她嫁给我， 因此相比我不想要她，结婚的可能性更大，但它仅此而已。“我能得到这份工作 吗？”1 宫主在 10 宫头。我显然想要这份工作，因此相比我不想要，更有可能 得到它；但也仅此而已。它并不显示“是”。

If something else in the chart shows the Yes, the movement of the significator onto the cusp can show the timing. 如果星盘中的其他因素显示了“是”，那么征象星移动到宫头可以显示应期。

Similarly, ‘Will I get the job?’ with Lord 10 on the 1st cusp does not show a Yes. What a planet on the Ascendant usually shows is the idea of that thing weighing on the querent. The idea of the job, or of getting any job, is weighing on the querent’s shoulders. 类似地，“我能得到这份工作吗？”10 宫主在 1 宫头并不显示“是”。行星在 上升点通常显示的是那件事压在问卜者心头的想法。这份工作，或者得到任何工 作的想法，正压在问卜者的肩上。

One of my students set a chart for ‘Will my ex come to the family party?’ The ex’s significator was sitting on the Ascendant, but made no aspect to either the querent or the party (Lord 5). No aspect: he didn’t come. But the placement showed that the idea of his coming was weighing on the querent’s mind. 我的一个学生为“我的前夫会来参加家庭聚会吗？”设了盘。前夫的征象星正位 于上升点，但与问卜者或聚会（5 宫主）都没有形成相位。没有相位：他没有来。 但落宫显示他可能会来的想法正压在问卜者的心头。

Finding the querent’s significator in the relevant house (rahter than on the cusp of that house) still shows only desire or concern. For instance, ‘Will I survive this illness?’ with Lord 1 in the 8th house shows that the querent is worried about dying, whether he will do so or not. Finding the significator of the thing desired in, rather than on the cusp of, the querent’s house: things look good – you have it in your pocket. This is not a certain Yes, but it is strong positive testimony. It shows that the job wants the querent, which is much more encouraging than the querent wanting the job. 发现问卜者的征象星在相关宫位内（而非在该宫头），仍然只显示欲望或关切。 例如，“我能从这场疾病中康复吗？”1 宫主在 8 宫显示问卜者担心会死，无论 他实际上是否会死。发现所渴望之事的征象星在问卜者的宫位内（而非在宫头）： 情况看起来不错——你已将它收入囊中。这不是一个确定的“是”，但它是强有 力的积极证据。它显示工作想要问卜者，这比问卜者想要工作更令人鼓舞。

If, however, the event is known or assumed, application to a cusp can show the event happening and give the timing. ‘When will Granny arrive?’ with Granny’s significator applying to the 1st cusp confirms that she is on her way and, by the number of degrees her significator needs to travel reach the 1st cusp, shows the timing of her arrival. 然而，如果事件已知或已设定，入相位于宫头可以显示事件正在发生并给出时间。 “奶奶什么时候到？”奶奶的征象星入相位于 1 宫头，证实她正在路上，并且根 据她的征象星需要移动多少度才能到达 1 宫头，可以显示她到达的时间。

Planets move, house cusps and Arabian Parts stand still. So planets can apply to cusps or Parts; cusps and Parts cannot apply to planets. 行星是移动的，宫头和阿拉伯点是静止的。因此，行星可以入相位于宫头或阿 拉伯点；宫头和阿拉伯点不能入相位于行星。

# Antiscia

# 映点

When I first read about antiscia, the idea struck me as so bizarre that I was sure someone had sucked it out of his thumb. I quickly learned better. These little creatures are an essential part of judgement. If you do not use them, you will consistently get judgement wrong. So pay attention! 当我初次读到关于映点的内容时，觉得这个想法古怪极了，简直像是有人凭空捏 造出来的。但我很快便意识到自己的浅见。这些看似不起眼的点位，实则是星盘 判断中不可或缺的一部分。若你忽略它们，便总会得出错误的结论。所以请务必 留心！

The theory 原理

‘Antiscion’ is from the Greek word for ‘shadow’. Every degree in the zodiac has its antiscion degree, and so anyting in that degree has its antiscion in that place. We are usually concerned with planets, so the antiscion is the ‘shadow’ placement of that planet. “映点”一词源于希腊语，意为“影子”。黄道上的每一度数都有其对应的映点 度数，因此位于该度数的任何星体，其映点也落在相应的位置上。我们通常关注 的是行星，所以映点就好比是该行星的“影子”落位。

Forget any Jungian meanings of ‘shadow’: there is no such sense here. ‘Reflection’ might be a better word for it. It is as if the planet has an alternative placement in its antiscion degree. It acts there exactly as it does in the degree where it stands bodily, except that contacts by antiscion usually carry a sense of hiddenness. ‘Will I marry Kylie?’ and our significators apply to conjunction: ‘Yes, you will’. They apply to conjunction by antiscion: ‘No, but you will have an affair with her’. 暂且抛开任何荣格心理学中关于“影子”的涵义：此处并无那种含义。用“映射” 来理解可能更为贴切。这就像是行星在其映点度数上拥有一个替代位置。它在映 点处的作用与它实际所在度数的表现完全相同，只是通过映点形成的相位通常带 有一层隐匿的意味。比如问：“我会和 Kylie（凯莉）结婚吗？”若征象星直接 形成合相，答案是：“是的，你会。”但若征象星是通过映点形成合相，则意味 着：“不，但你将会与她有一段私情。”

【Antiscia and things hidden - Posted on July 21st, 2014 【映点与隐藏事物 - 发布于 2014 年 7 月 21 日

My students often get hung up on the idea that whatever is shown by antiscia must be something hidden or secret. This is not so. It can be hidden or secret – but this is only if the context allows such a meaning. If the context does not allow it, whatever is shown by antiscia can be quite as overt as anything else. If an antiscion is what shows that the cat will come home, this does not mean that Puss will turn up in disguise.】 我的学生们常常纠结于这样一种观念：凡是映点所显示的事物，必定是隐藏的或 秘密的。事实并非如此。它可以是隐藏的或秘密的——但这仅在星盘背景允许这 种含义的前提下才成立。如果背景不允许，那么映点所显示的事物可能和其他任 何事物一样公开。如果映点显示猫会回家，这并不意味着猫咪会乔装打扮出现。】

THE CALCULATION

计算方法

If you already know how to do this, you can skip this box. 如果你已经知道如何计算，可以跳过此框。

Imagine a line drawn between the solstice points (0 Capricorn and 0 Cancer). Imagine that this line is a mirror. The antiscion of any degree, and of anyting in that degree, is its position seen in that mirror. So if something is 2 degrees on one side of this line (at 2 Cancer, say: 2 degrees forward from 0 Cancer) its antiscion will be at 2degrees on the other side of that line (28 Gemini: 2 degrees back from 0 Cancer). 想象在至点（摩羯座 0 度和巨蟹座 0 度）之间画一条线。将这条线视作一面 镜子。任何度数，以及位于该度数上的任何星体，其映点就是它在这面镜子 中映出的位置。因此，如果某点位于这条线的一侧 2 度处（例如巨蟹座 2 度： 即从巨蟹座 0 度向前 2 度），那么它的映点就会位于这条线另一侧的 2 度处 （即双子座 28 度：从巨蟹座 0 度向后 2 度）。

This reflection around the solstice points shows that the idea is grounded in reality – it was not sucked out of somebody’s thumb. There is a direct connection between degrees that are the same distance either side of the solstices. Open your ephemeris at the summer solstice for any year (Sun at 0 Cancer). Pick a number between 1 and 180. Count that number of days forward through the year and note the degree of the Sun on that day. Now count the same number of degrees backwards through the year. The degree of the Sun on that day will be the antiscion of the degree you have just noted. This means that on those two days the time between sunrise and sunset will be exactly the same. 这种以至点为对称轴的映射原理表明，该概念并非凭空捏造，而是基于现实 ——位于至点两侧相同距离的度数之间存在着直接的联系。翻开任意年份夏 至（太阳在巨蟹座 0 度）那天的星历表，选取一个 1 到 180 之间的数字。从 该日期起向前数出对应的天数，并记下当天太阳所在的度数。然后，从该日 期起向后数出相同的天数。那天太阳所在的度数，就是你刚才所记度数的映 点。这意味着，在这两天里，日出到日落的时长是完全相同的。

Each sign reflects onto one other sign: 每个星座会映射到另一个特定的星座：

So anything in Aries has its antiscion in Virgo; anything in Taurus has its antiscion in Leo. Learn this table. 因此，任何位于白羊座的星体，其映点都在处女座；任何位于金牛座的星体， 其映点都在狮子座。请熟记此对应表。

Once you know which sign the antiscion of something is in, you need to find its degree in that sign. Original degree + antiscion = 30. The degree the planet is in bodily, added to the degree of its antiscion, will equal 30. So, to find the antiscion, we must take the original degree away from 30. Look back at the example above: if a planet is 2 degrees forward of 0 Cancer, which is 28 Gemini. 28+2=30. 一旦知道某星体映点所在的星座，接下来需要确定它在该星座内的具体度数。 原度数 + 映点度数 = 30。行星实际所在度数与其映点度数之和等于 30。所 以，要计算映点度数，我们必须用 30 减去原度数。回顾上面的例子：如果一 颗行星位于巨蟹座 0 度向前 2 度，其映点就在双子座 28 度。28+2=30。

Don’t worry! However innumerate you may feel you are, this is not complicated. Each sign consists of 30 degrees. Each degree consists of 60 minutes. 60 minutes = 1degree. 别担心！无论你觉得自己对数字多么不敏感，这个计算并不复杂。每个星座 包含 30 度，每度包含 60 分（60 分 = 1 度）。

Instead of thinking of each sign as 30 degrees, call it 29 degrees and 60 minutes. It’s the same thing (because 60 minutes is the same as 1 degree). But it makes the arithmetic simpler. 我们不妨将每个星座视为 29 度 60 分，而不是 30 度。这其实是相同的（因 为 60 分等于 1 度），但会让计算更简便。

Follow this example: 请看以下示例：

Let’s say Mras is at 22.35 Taurus. What is its antiscion? 假设火星位于金牛座 22 度 35 分。它的映点在哪里？

If Mars is in Taurus, its antiscion must be in Leo (from the table above). 既然火星在金牛座，根据上文对照表，其映点必定在狮子座。

What degree of Leo? 那么是狮子座的多少度呢？

Mars is at 22.35 Taurus. 火星位于金牛座 22 度 35 分。

Take this away from 30 degrees. 用 30 度减去这个值。

But to make it easier, call it 29.60 degrees. 但为了方便计算，我们将其视为 29 度 60 分。

29.60 22.35 - ———— 07.25

So the antiscion of Mars at 22.35 Taurus is 7.25 Leo. 因此，火星在金牛座 22 度 35 分的映点位于狮子座 7 度 25 分。

We can check this, because starting degree + antiscion must add up to 30. 我们可以验证一下，因为起始度数 + 映点度数之和必须等于 30。

07.25 22.35 + ———— 29.60 即等于 30

Let’s do another one. 我们再试一个例子。

What is the antiscion of 14.35 Aries? 白羊座 14 度 35 分的映点是多少？

From the table above, anything in Aries has its antiscion in Virgo. 根据上表，任何位于白羊座的星体，其映点都在处女座。

Take 14.35 from 29.60. 用 29.60 减去 14.35。

29.60 14.35 - ———— 15.25

So the antiscion of 14.35 Aries is 15.25 Virgo. 因此，白羊座 14 度 35 分的映点是处女座 15 度 25 分。

The common error here is to end up with starting degree + antiscion = 31 degrees. So, until you get used to this calculation, always check by adding the antiscion you've calculated onto the initial degree to make sure they equal 30. If you follow my suggestion of calling 30 degrees 29.60, you will not make this mistake. 这里常见的错误是算出起始度数加映点度数等于 31 度。所以，在你习惯这个 计算之前，务必将你算出的映点度数加上起始度数进行验证，确保它们之和 等于 30。如果你按照我的建议，将 30 度视为 29.60 来计算，就不会犯这个错 误。

If this seems like hard work, believe me: it isn't. In a very short time you will get used to glancing around the chart to see if the antisia of any of the significators are doing anything interesting. With a little effort at first you will find that checking antiscia happens almost automatically. You do not have to do the whole calculation. It is enough to think ‘Lord 1 is at 19 Gemini. Is there anything around 11 Cancer or Capricorn?’ If not - forget it. If there is, then you can calculate the antiscial placement exactly. 如果这看起来有些费力，请相信我：其实并非如此。用不了多久，你就会习 惯在星盘中扫视，看看是否有任何征象星的映点正在产生有趣的影响。起初 只需稍加练习，你就会发现检查映点几乎会成为自动的步骤。你不必每次都 进行完整计算。只需快速思考：“1 宫主在双子座 19 度。那么在巨蟹座 11 度或摩羯座 11 度附近是否有其他星体？”如果没有，就无需在意。如果有， 那时你再精确计算映点位置即可。

Contrantiscia 反映点

If a planet is at 25.42 Gemini, its antiscion will be at 4.18 Cancer. The point opposite its antiscion, 4.18 Capricorn, is its contrantsicion. Contrantiscion is directly opposite antiscion. 如果一颗行星位于双子座 25 度 42 分，其映点将在巨蟹座 4 度 18 分。与该映点 直接相对的点，即摩羯座 4 度 18 分，就是它的反映点。反映点与映点形成对冲 相位。

You need to know this word, because you will come across it in other books, but I strongly suggest you do not use it yourself. Call it an opposition by antiscion. That is what it is, and this makes its meaning clear. We can do without superfluous technical terms. 你需要知道这个词，因为在其他书籍中可能会遇到它，但我强烈建议你自己不要 使用它。直接称之为“通过映点形成的对冲相位”。这就是它的本质，这样表述 也使其含义清晰明了。我们可以省去多余的技术术语。

Example: suppose my significator in a chart is at 3.17 Leo. Its antiscion is at 26.43 Taurus. If there is a planet at 26 Scorpio, it opposes my significator by antiscion. Or, if you wish, is on my contrantiscion. 示例：假设我星盘中的征象星位于狮子座 3 度 17 分。它的映点在金牛座 26 度 43 分。如果天蝎座 26 度处有一颗行星，那么它就通过映点与我的征象星形成对 冲相位。或者，如果你愿意，也可以说它落在我的反映点上。

In natal charts, other aspects to antiscia have minor significance. In horary they can be ignored. Keep to conjunction and opposition. 在本命盘中，映点形成的其他相位意义较小。在卜卦盘中则可以忽略。只关注合 相和对冲相位即可。

If this is your first introduction to antiscia, take a break now and work out where the antiscia fall in your natal chart. You will probably find you have some new and important aspects that you knew nothing about. 如果这是你初次接触映点，现在不妨休息一下，计算一下你本命盘中映点的位置。 你很可能会发现一些以前完全不知道的、新的重要相位。

How do we use antiscia? 我们如何运用映点？

If the conjunction or opposition is going to show an event, it must be exact, just as with a bodily aspect. Don’t try moving the antisicion: you’ll tie your brain in knots, especially if you are dealing with the antiscion of a retrograde planet. Plot the antiscion on the chart and let the applying planet come to it. 如果合相或对冲相位预示着某个事件，它必须像实际相位一样精确。不要试图移 动映点的位置：这只会让你的大脑打结，尤其是在处理逆行行星的映点时。直接 在星盘上标出映点，让运行中的行星逐渐与之形成相位。

### ✸When both planets are direct, if A applies to the antiscion of B, B will also apply

to the antiscion of A. When one planet is retrograde, the relative movement of the planets can cause confusion. They can appear to be both applying and separating, depending on whether we cast the antiscion of A or B. Keep it simple: calculate the antiscion of the retrograde planet and use the movement of the direct planet to decide whether the aspect is applying or separating.✷ 当两颗行星都顺行时，如果行星 A 运行至行星 B 的映点，那么行星 B 也同时会 运行至行星 A 的映点。当其中一颗行星逆行时，行星的相对运动可能导致混淆。 根据我们计算的是 A 还是 B 的映点，它们可能同时呈现出入相位和出相位的状 态。保持简单：计算出逆行行星的映点，然后根据顺行行星的运动来判断该相位 是正在形成入相位还是正在分离出相位。✷

If the antiscion of planet A is conjunct planet B, the antiscion of planet B will be conjunct planet A. This is automatic, so don’t get excited about it: ‘Look, the antiscion of Mars is on Venus, and wow, the antiscion of Venus is on Mars!’ 如果行星 A 的映点与行星 B 形成合相，那么行星 B 的映点也必然与行星 A 形成 合相。这是自动对应的关系，所以不必为此兴奋不已：“看，火星的映点落在金 星上，而且，哇，金星的映点也落在火星上！”

Often, we are not looking for the aspect to show an event. If two planets are conjunct or opposed by antiscion, they will influence each other. For example, if Lord 10 is the new job I am asking about, and Saturn in Aries opposes it by antiscion, I can see that something nasty is afflicting this job in (by antiscion) a hidden sort of way. For this influence to be significant, the planets need to be close, a couple of degrees apart at most. If this nasty Saturn were on the 10th cusp by antiscion, the judgement would be the same: my job is afflicted in a hidden way. 很多时候，我们寻找映点相位并非为了预示具体事件。如果两颗行星通过映点形 成合相或对冲相位，它们就会相互影响。例如，如果 10 宫主代表我所询问的新 工作，而位于白羊座的土星通过映点与之形成对冲相位，我就能看出某种糟糕的 事物正以一种（通过映点所暗示的）隐匿方式损害这份工作。要使这种影响显著， 两颗行星需要足够接近，最多相距两三度。如果这颗讨厌的土星通过映点落在 10 宫头上，判断也是一样的：我的工作正受到某种隐匿方式的损害。

As this example shows, a planet’s antiscion works as if the planet itself were in that place, with the exceptions that 正如这个例子所示，行星的映点作用就如同行星本身位于那个位置一样，但有以 下例外：

* we are concerned only with conjunction and opposition
* 我们只关心合相和对冲相位

* antiscia usually carry a sense of the hidden
* 映点通常带有隐匿的含义

* antiscia are less likely to prohibit other aspects.
* 映点不太会阻碍其他相位。

I have judged many horaries by antiscia alone. The things that will not be shown by antiscia are death and pregnancy. 我曾仅凭映点就判断过许多卜卦盘。但死亡和怀孕这两类事情通常不会通过映点 显示。

Use the planet’s essential dignities as shown by its bodily position, not the position of its antiscion. If Jupiter is at 23.07 Cancer its antiscion will be at 6.53 Gemini. When considering its antiscion, treat Jupiter as exalted (as it is at its bodily position in Cancer) not as in detriment (as it is where its antiscion falls in Gemini). Antiscia can gain or lose accidental strength, however. In a contest horary one team’s significator fell exactly on an angle: this is greatly strengthening, and that team won. I don’t think antiscia are affected by falling on fixed stars, but I could be convinced otherwise. 采用行星实体位置的先天尊贵，而不是其映点位置。如果木星位于巨蟹座 23 度 07 分，其映点将在双子座 6 度 53 分。在考虑其映点时，应将木星视为处于旺势 （因为它实际位于巨蟹座），而非落陷（如同其映点落在双子座所提示的那样）。 然而，映点可以增强或削弱偶然力量。在一次比赛卜卦中，一方队伍的征象星的

映点恰好落在四轴点上：这是极大的增强，而那支队伍最终获胜。我不认为映点 落在恒星上会对其产生影响，但我也可以被相反的证据说服。

### ✸ No, I cannot be convinced otherwise. Antiscia are not affected by falling onto

fixed stars.✷

### ✸不，我无法被相反的证据说服。映点落在恒星上不会对其产生影响。✷

If an antiscion falls right on a house cusp, this shows that this person – if the planet is someone’s significator – has an interest in the affairs of that house, or that the house is affected, for better or for worse, by whatever that planet signifies. This is only if it falls right on the cusp: if the antiscion is floating around in the middle of the house its effect on that house can be ignored. Example: if I ask ‘Will she marry me?’ and my significator’s antiscion falls on the cusp of the 8th (2nd from 7th: the other person’s money) this suggests that I have a major interest in her money. If my significator’s antiscion were a few degrees inside that house, it would carry no such meaning. 如果一个映点恰好落在宫头上，这表明——如果该行星是某人的征象星——此人 对于该宫位所掌管的事务有兴趣，或者该宫位受到该行星所象征事物的影响（无 论好坏）。这仅当映点正好落在宫头上时才成立：如果映点只是漂浮在宫位的中 间区域，那么它对该宫位的影响可以忽略不计。例如：如果我问“她会嫁给我吗？”， 而我的征象星的映点落在 8 宫头（即 7 宫的 2 宫：对方的钱财）上，这就暗示我 极其看重她的钱财。如果我的征象星的映点只是在该宫位内几度的地方，则不会 带有这样的含义。

Worked example 实例分析

The event in this chart is shown solely by an antiscion.The querent had an email and telephone relationship with a man. She had not heard from him for a few weeks, and he was not answering or returing her calls. She asked, ‘Why isn’t he calling me? Will I hear from him, and when?’ Some of the techniques discussed here are explained later in the book; follow what you can for now, then come back to this chart when you’ve worked through the practical section. 此星盘中的事件完全通过映点显现。问卜者曾与一位男士保持电子邮件和电 话联系。几周没有他的消息，他也不接或不回她的电话。她问道：“他为什么不 打电话给我？我会收到他的消息吗？什么时候？” 文中讨论的一些技巧将在本 书后续章节解释；现在请尽量理解，并在学习完实践部分后，再回来看这个星盘。

25. There is another such in R A Applied , pp. 26-28. 25.《R A Applied》书中另有一例，第 26-28 页.

The querent is shown by Lord 1, which is Venus, and the Moon. As this is a relationship question, we would also give her Venus because she is a woman; but she already has it. 问卜者由 1 宫主（金星）和月亮表示。由于这是一个感情关系问题，我们也会将 金星分配给她，因为她是女性；不过她本身已经拥有金星了。

How is she? Yuk! Venus is in its detriment, in the 12th house. She is not happy and she has little power: as we know, because she is having to wait for him to call. 她的状况如何？糟透了！金星处于落陷状态，且在 12 宫。她并不快乐，也几乎 无能为力：正如我们所知，因为她只能等着他打电话来。

The position of the Moon often shows what the querent is thinking about, especially if this placement is emphasised in some way – as it is here, by being so close to a house cusp. This acts like a highlighter pen, drawing our attention to it. What is she thing about? Probably having some fun (5th house). It is unlikely that she is thinking about

that other major 5th- house concern, children, because the Moon is in a barren sign. 月亮的位置常显示问卜者正在想什么，尤其是当这个位置以某种方式被强调时— —就像这里，因为它非常接近一个宫头。这就像一支荧光笔，将我们的注意力吸 引过去。她在想什么？很可能是寻些乐子（5 宫）。不太可能是在想 5 宫所主的 另一件大事——孩子，因为月亮位于一个贫瘠星座。

Her boyfriend is shown by Lord 7, which is Mars, and – only in a relationship question – by the Sun, because he is a man. 她的男友由 7 宫主（火星）表示，并且——仅在感情关系问题中——也由太阳表 示，因为他是男性。

Does she like him? For this we need to find out her attitudes, which is done by examining her planet’s receptions. Look at the table on page 72. Venus is in the sign and face of Mars (him) and the exaltation and triplicity of the Sun (him). The Moon is in the sign and triplicity of the Sun. Yes, she likes him lots! 她喜欢他吗？为此我们需要找出她的态度，这通过检查她行星的接纳关系来完成。 查看第 101 页的表格。金星位于火星（他）所守护的星座和得面的位置，以及太 阳（他）的旺势和三分位置。月亮位于太阳所守护的星座和三分位置。是的，她 非常喜欢他！

NB: Venus is in the sign ruled by Lord 7 and is in its own detriment. If Venus were close to the 7th cusp, at, say, 24 Scorpio, it would still be in the sign ruled by Lord 7 and in its own detriment. But that would be a far healthier situation. In that case, she has gone right over to his side of the chart, and Lord 1 will always be in its own detriment on the 7th cusp. Had she been at 24 Scorpio, we could have judged ‘She loves him (in his sign), because of which she is very vulnerable (detriment) – as we are if we love someone’. In this chart, however, Lord 1 is in the other sign ruled by Lord 7. She has not gone across to his side of the chart. The implication here is that she is unhappy, so she loves him: a quite different dynamic. 注意：金星位于 7 宫主所守护的星座，并且自身落陷。如果金星靠近 7 宫头，比 如在天蝎座 24 度，它仍然会处于 7 宫主守护的星座并且自身落陷。但那将会是 一个健康得多的状况。那时她已完全进入星盘对方领域，而 1 宫主落在 7 宫头必 然落陷。如果她当时在天蝎座 24 度，我们可以判断“她爱他（在他的星座里）， 正因如此她非常脆弱（落陷）——当我们爱一个人时就是如此。” 然而，在此 星盘中，1 宫主位于 7 宫主守护的另一个星座。她并未跨越至对方领域。这暗示 她因爱而苦，形成截然不同的心理动态。

Are her feelings reciprocated? Look at the receptions of his planets to find out what his attitudes are. The Sun is in the sign and triplicity of Venus and the exaltation and face of the Moon. The Sun is very keen on her. At 28 Sagittarius, however, Mars has no interest in her at all: it is not in any dignity or debility of either Venus or the Moon. So while the Sun is so keen on her, Mars is completely indifferent. Maybe this is the clue to why he isn’t calling her. 她的感情得到回应了吗？查看他行星的接纳关系以了解他的态度。太阳位于金星

所守护的星座和三分位置，以及月亮的旺势和得面位置。太阳对她非常感兴趣。 然而，火星在射手座 28 度，对她毫无兴趣：它不在金星或月亮的任何尊贵或衰 弱位置。所以，虽然太阳对她很热情，但火星完全无动于衷。也许这就是他不给 她打电话的线索。

Lord 7 and the Sun both signify him; but they signify him in different ways. Lord 7 is him as thinking, feeling person; the Sun is him as animal man. So his animal nature is strongly attracted to find a mate. As person, however, he has no interest in her at all. Interested or not, with his significators in the 8th and 12th houses, he is not in a good position to act. 7 宫主和太阳都象征他；但代表不同层面。7 宫主是思维情感的人格层面；太阳 是生理本能的动物层面。所以他的动物本性强烈渴望配偶，但人格层面毫无兴趣。 无论感不感兴趣，他的征象星在 8 宫和 12 宫，行动力严重受限。

Especially unable to act is Mars. Its condition here does not look so bad: it has some essential dignity (term) and is about to enter Capricorn, where it is exalted. But appearances are often deceptive. You must be aware of what the planets are doing – not only of what they look as if they are doing. You must check your ephemeris. Mars is in first station: scarcely moving as it turns retrograde. It fails to reach the promised land of its exaltation. Station is a time of great vulnerability. 尤其无法行动的是火星。它在这里的状况看起来没那么糟：它有一些先天尊贵（得 界），并且即将进入摩羯座，在那里它将处于旺势。但表象常常具有欺骗性。你 必须意识到行星正在做什么——不仅仅是它们看起来像在做什么。你必须查对你 的星历表。火星正处于停滞状态：在转为逆行时几乎不动。它未能到达它所许诺 的旺势之地。停滞是一个极其脆弱的时期。

So Mars (the boyfriend as thinking/feeling being) is in a very vulnerable position. Why? The planet’s being so close to the house cusp points us to the answer. On the cusp of the 2nd house from his own 1st house (which is the querent’s 7th house), he is concerned with his money. How is his money? Look at the ruler of that house, Jupiter. It is in its detriment. His money is in a mess. 所以火星（作为思考/感觉存在的男友）处于一个非常脆弱的位置。为什么？该 行星如此接近宫头为我们指明了答案。在他自身 1 宫（即问卜者的 7 宫）的 2 宫头上，他关心的是他的钱财。他的钱财如何？查看该宫的宫主星木星。它处于 落陷状态。他的财务状况一团糟。

So we see that her boyfriend is bogged down (Mars not moving) amid his financial worries. Which is why he hasn’t called her, even though we can reassure the querent that he is indeed still strongly interested in her. 因此我们看到，她的男友深陷（火星不动）在他的财务忧虑之中。这就是为什么 他没有打电话给她，尽管我们可以向问卜者保证，他确实仍然对她非常感兴趣。

Will he get in touch? To judge ‘Yes’ to this we need an aspect. The Moon (her) does apply to Mars (him); but this aspect is prohibited by Mercury: the Moon squares

Mercury first. Even were this not so, we would much prefer to join one of her planets with Sun (the bit of him that is keen on her) rather than with Mars (the bit of him that isn’t). 他会联系吗？要对此做出“是”的判断，我们需要一个相位。月亮（她）确实在 入相位于火星（他）；但这个相位被水星阻碍了：月亮首先刑水星。即使不是这 样，我们也更愿意将她的一颗行星与太阳（他渴望她的那部分）结合，而不是与 火星（他无动于衷的那部分）结合。

The Sun is at 10.54 Taurus. Where is its antiscion? 太阳在金牛座 10 度 54 分。它的映点在哪里？

From the table, Taurus has its antiscion in Leo. Hmm – that’s where the Moon is: this might be interesting. But where in Leo? 根据对照表，金牛座的映点在狮子座。嗯——月亮就在那里：这可能很有趣。但 在狮子座的哪一度呢？

29.60 10.54 – ———— 19.06

The Sun’s antiscion is at 19.06 Leo. Keep the antiscion still, letting the planet apply to it: the Moon applies immediately to conjunct the Sun. Great news, because (judging essential dignity from the bodily position, not the antiscion) they have powerful mutual reception. He wil be back in touch. 太阳的映点在狮子座 19 度 06 分。保持映点不动，让行星入相位于它：月亮立即 入相位与太阳形成合相。好消息，因为（根据其实际位置判断先天尊贵，而非其 映点位置）它们之间有强大的互溶关系。他会恢复联系。

When? With the Moon at 17.37 Leo, it must travel a degree and a half to reach the Sun’s antiscion at 19.06 Leo. So he will call in 11/2 somethings. 11/2 whats? ‘Years’ is obviously not a relevant answer to this question: for our smitten querent ‘years’ might as well ‘never’. As he hasn’t called for weeks, ‘hours’ is probably too small a time unti. Which leaves us with days, weeks or months. 什么时候？月亮在狮子座 17 度 37 分，它需要运行 1.5 度才能到达太阳的映点狮 子座 19 度 06 分。所以他将在 1.5 个某单位内打电话。1.5 个什么单位？“年” 显然不是这个问题的相关答案：对我们这位饱受相思之苦的问卜者来说，“年” 无异于“永不”。因为他已经几周没打电话了，“小时”可能又太短了。这就只 剩下天、周或月。

Following the sign + house formula, 11/2 degrees in a fixed sign in a succedent house would give us weeks. But we could take just the fixity of the sign, which would give our longest unit: months. The judgement given was that he would call, possibly in a week and a half, more likely in a month and a half. He phoned her in a month and

a half. 遵循“星座+宫位”公式，在固定星座和续宫中的 1.5 度会给我们“周”这个 单位。但我们也可以仅依据星座的固定性，这会给出我们最长的单位：“月”。 给出的判断是：他会在一个半星期内打电话，更可能是在一个半月内。他一个半 月后给她打了电话。

26. See chapter 13 on timing.
26. 关于应期的判断，参见第 13 章。

Note that his calling her is shown only by the antiscion. Ignore that and the judgement is wrong. These little creatures are important! 请注意，他给她打电话这件事仅由映点显示。忽略这一点，判断就会出错。这些 小家伙很重要！

# The Fixed Stars

# 恒星

### ✸The fixed stars are extremely important in natal astrology. They are rarely of any

significance in horary. Even the brief treatment in this chapter gives them more attention than they merit and, I have found, leads students to overuse them. As always, keep it simple: if you’re doubtful about bringing a star into judgement, it is probably better to leave it out.

### ✸在本命占星学中，恒星极为重要，但在卜卦占星中它们很少具有任何意义。

即使本章简短的论述给予它们的关注也已超出其应得的范围，并且据我发现，这 会导致学生过度使用它们。一如既往，保持简单原则：如果你对将某颗恒星纳入 判断存有疑虑，那么或许最好不予考虑。

I would limit their use to occasions when the context gives a clear, specific relevance to the nature of that star. For instance, the Roman consul Regulus was killed on returning to Africa. So if the question were ‘Should I go to Africa?’ Lord 1 on the star Regulus would not necessarily foretell death, but would be a very strong ‘No!’ ✷ 我会将恒星的使用限制在以下情况：即背景明确、具体地与那颗恒星的性质相关。 例如，罗马执政官 Regulus（雷古鲁斯）在返回非洲时被杀。因此，如果问题是 “我应该去非洲吗？”，1 宫主位于恒星轩辕十四上未必预示死亡，但会是一个 极其强烈的“不去！”信号。✷

The fixed stars are what we commonly call ‘stars’, in contrast to the ‘wandering stars’, or planets. As a trip outdoors on a clear night will show – at least, if you are not in a city – there are any number of these. A hundred or so among them have significant astrological use, but of that hundred or so only a handful need to be noted in horary. The fixed stars become more significant the higher up the astrological scale we go: they are useful in natal astrology; they are invaluable in mundane astrology; horary queries are generally beneath their concern. 恒星即我们通常所说的‘星体’，与“游星”（即行星）相对。在一个晴朗的夜 晚到户外看看就会明白——至少如果你不在城市里的话——它们的数量数不胜 数。其中约一百颗具有重要的占星学用途，但在这一百颗左右中，只有少数需要 在卜卦中予以关注。恒星的重要性随着占星学层级的提升而增加：它们在本命占 星学中很有用；在世运占星学中则不可或缺；而卜卦问题通常不在其关注范围之

内。

The stars that that can have a major bearing on horary judgement are: 对卜卦判断可能具有主要影响的恒星有：

Algol which is at 26 大陵五 位置在 金牛座 26 度

Alcyone 29 昴宿六 金牛座 29 度

Aldebaran 9 毕宿五 双子座 9 度

Regulus 29 轩辕十四 狮子座 29 度

Vindemiatrix 10 太微左垣四 天平座 10 度

Spica 23 角宿一 天平座 23 度

Antares 9 心宿二 射手座 9 度

These placements are as precise as we need, and are accurate for the time of writing, which is 2005. Despite being ‘fixed’, the stars do move, albeit very much more slowly than the planets: roughly one degree every 72 years. After 2010 you can regard Regulus as being at 0 Virgo. If a significator or relevant house-cusp is within a couple of degrees of one of these stars (limit this to 1 degree for Vindemiatrix), this may be important – if the star carries a meaning relevant to the context of the question. 这些位置已足够精确，且适用于撰写时的 2005 年。尽管被称为“固定”，恒星 实则也在缓慢移动，只是比行星缓慢得多：大约每 72 年移动一度。2010 年之后， 你可以将轩辕十四视为位于处女座 0 度。如果某颗征象星或相关宫头位于这些恒 星几度之内（对太微左垣四则限制在 1 度以内），这可能很重要——前提是该恒 星的含义与问题的背景相关。

We are concerned only with conjunction to fixed stars: no aspects. Planets are either on stars or they are not: do not (in horary) think of planets moving onto stars. Example: if the question were, ‘Can I hold my marriage together?’ Lord 7 on Vindemiatrix would be an indication that the querent’s spouse wants a divorce. That Lord 7 will be on Vindemiatrix when it has moved forwards 5 degrees does not mean that the spouse will be wanting a divorce in the near future. Such movement should be

ignored. The exception to this general rule is when we are using horary to elect a time to act.In that case a planet moving onto Regulus, for instance, might well show the optimum moment. 我们只关注与恒星的合相：不考虑其他相位。行星要么在恒星上，要么不在：（在 卜卦中）不要考虑行星运行到恒星上的情况。例如：如果问题是“我能维持住我 的婚姻吗？”，7 宫主位于太微左垣四将暗示问卜者的配偶想要离婚。7 宫主在 向前运行 5 度后会位于太微左垣四，但这并不意味着配偶在不久的将来会想要离 婚。此类运行应予以忽略。此通用规则的一个例外是当我们使用卜卦来择时行动 时（可以这么考虑）。在那种情况下，例如，一颗行星运行到轩辕十四上，很 可能指示了最佳时机。

27. See chapter 27.
27. 参见第 27 章。

Ignore antiscia falling onto fixed stars. 忽略落在恒星上的映点。

Algol 大陵五

Caput Algol. Medusa’s Head. This is the most unfortunate of the stars. In horary, the general idea with it is of losing one’s head. This can be literal, but do keep any impulse to grand opera that you might have out of your horary judgements. Yes, such gory events do happen; but they tend not to, especially if the question is ‘Will I get the job?’ or ‘Can I buy this flat?’ The losing of heads can usually be taken metaphorically. 大陵五。即 Medusa（美杜莎）之首。这是最不吉利的恒星。在卜卦中，它的一 般含义是“失去头脑”。这可以是字面意思，但务必将你可能有的任何歌剧式的 夸张冲动排除在卜卦判断之外。是的，此类血腥事件确实会发生；但它们往往不 会，尤其是当问题是“我能得到这份工作吗？”或“我能买下这套公寓？”时。 “失去头脑”通常可以按比喻意义理解。

Example: the querent was concerned that a nanny she was thinking of hiring might not be able to cope. The nanny’s significator was on Caput Algol, exactly confirming the querent’s fears: the nanny could lose her head. 示例：问卜者担心她正考虑雇佣的一位保姆可能无法胜任。该保姆的征象星位于 大陵五，正好证实了问卜者的担忧：这位保姆可能会“失去头脑”（即慌乱失措）。

Algol being in Taurus, the Moon or Venus will have lots of essential dignity if placed on it. In this example, the nanny’s significator was the Moon. Lost of dignity, so she was a decent person, but still unable to cope. 由于大陵五位于金牛座，月亮或金星若位于其上将拥有大量的先天尊贵。在此例 中，保姆的征象星是月亮。她虽有（先天）尊贵，是个正派的人，但仍无力应对。

Alcyone 昴宿六

This is the main star in the cluster that is the Pleiades, or the Weeping Sisters. Weeping is the main idea here: there will be regret; things will not turn out well. 这是昴宿星团中的主星，或称“哭泣的姐妹们”。哭泣是这里的核心概念：将会 有遗憾；事情不会有好结果。

Like all star clusters, the Pleiades afflict the eyesight, so this may be an indication that whoever’s significator is on Alcyone cannot see clearly, or is deluded. 像所有的星团一样，昴宿星团不利于视力，因此这可能表明，任何征象星位于昴 宿六的人都无法看清状况，或是受到了蒙蔽。

Aldebaran 毕宿五

The South Eye of the Bull. This is the brightest star in the constellation of Taurus (even though by zodiacal measurement it is in that part of the zodiac that is called Gemini).It is associated with the spring equinox, the start of the year, so the idea here is of inception, of a positive start. 牛眼星。这是金牛座中最亮的恒星（尽管按黄道度测量，它位于被称为双子座的 那部分黄道中）。它与春分点、一年的起始相关，因此这里的含义是开端， 是积极的开局。

28. For a discussion of the distinction between the signs of the zodiac and the constellations that bear the same names, see Real Astrology, chapter 5. For now, the important point is that the signs and the constellations are different and must not be confused.
28. 关于黄道星座与同名星座之间区别的讨论，参见《Real Astrology》第 5 章。目前重要 的是，黄道星座与天文星座是不同的，切勿混淆。

Example: if the question were ‘Should I look for a new job?’ finding Aldebaran on the Ascendant would be an indication that it is time to start a new cycle, so ‘Yes, a new job could be appropriate’. 示例：如果问题是“我应该寻找新工作吗？”，发现毕宿五位于上升点，这将表 明是时候开始一个新的周期了，所以答案是“是的，一份新工作可能是合适的”。

Regulus

轩辕十四

Cor Leonis. The Heart of the Lion. This is the brightest star in Leo. Any star that is the ‘heart’ of its constellation is the epitome of the idea which that constellation expresses, so Regulus is the most Leo bit of Leo: super-Leo. It is highly auspicious for material achievement, and in horary its significance can usually be limited to that. It is not necessarily happy, but it does bring success. 狮心星。这是狮子座中最亮的恒星。任何作为其星座“心脏”的恒星，都是该星 座所表达理念的缩影，因此轩辕十四是狮子座中最具狮子座特质的部分：超级狮 子座。它对于物质成就而言是非常吉祥的，在卜卦中，其意义通常可以仅限于此。 它不一定带来快乐，但确实能带来成功。

If the question were, ‘Will I get the promotion?’ finding the querent’s significator on Regulus would be a strong positive testimony. If the question were, ‘Does she love me?’ or ‘Will Puss come home?’ that a significator is on Regulus is unlikely to add anything to our judgement. 如果问题是“我会得到晋升吗？”，发现问卜者的征象星位于轩辕十四，将是一 个强有力的积极征象。如果问题是“她爱我吗？”或“猫咪会回家吗？”，征象 星位于轩辕十四不太可能为我们的判断增添任何信息。

Vindemiatrix 太微左垣四

The Gatherer of Grapes. The Widow-Maker. This has a strong association with divorce and separation. So if the question were, ‘Is there a future in our relationship?’ finding Vindemiatrix on the Ascendant would be an immediate testimony of ‘No’. 摘葡萄者。寡妇制造者。它与离婚和分离有很强的关联。因此，如果问题是“我 们的关系有未来吗？”，发现太微左垣四位于上升点，将直接构成一个“没有” 的征象。

It is also associated with the story of the Sorcerer’s Apprentice – you have probably seen this in Fantasia. Overstretching. Assuming powers you are unable to control. Stupid’s sake: doing something daft even though you’re aware that it’s daft. ‘Should I open a spiritual school?’ with the querent’s significator on Vindemiatrix: ‘Only if you wish to damage yourself and others’. 它也与“魔法师的学徒”故事有关——你可能在《幻想曲》中看过。过度扩张。 承担你无法控制的力量。愚蠢的行为：明知某事很蠢却仍去做。“我应该开一所 灵性学校吗？”，如果问卜者的征象星位于太微左垣四：“除非你希望伤害自己 和他人”。

Spica 角宿一

The Virgin’s Spike. This is the brightest star in the constellation of Virgo. It is associated with Our Lady, so is strongly protective. Spica rising is not necessarily an indication that all will go as is hoped, but even if things don’t work out, you will be OK at the end; you will be looked after. 室女之穗。这是室女座中最亮的恒星。它与圣母有关，因此具有强大的保护性。 角宿一位于上升点并不一定表示一切都会如希望般发展，但即使事情不顺利，你 最终也会安然无恙；你会得到庇佑。

Spica can be most fortunate, bringing bounty, but it doesn’t carry quite the sense of material achievement of Regulus. It is, however, much the happier of the two stars. 角宿一可能非常幸运，带来丰饶，但它不像轩辕十四那样带有强烈的物质成就意 味。然而，在这两颗恒星中，它是更为愉悦的那一颗。

Antares 心宿二

Cor Scorpionis. The Heart of the Scorpion. As Regulus is the Leo-most bit of Leo, this is the Scorpio-most bit of Scorpio (even though it is currently placed in Sagittarius). This is the star that is Blake’s. 蝎心星。正如轩辕十四是狮子座中最具狮子座特质的恒星，这是天蝎座中最具天 蝎座特质的恒星（尽管它目前位于射手座）。这就是 Blake（布莱克）诗中的那 颗星。

Tyger, tyger burning bright 老虎，老虎光焰闪耀

In the forests of the night. 在黑夜的丛林中.

It is very powerful, but – as we might expect from Super Scorpio – not the most benign of stars. 它非常强大，但——正如我们对“超级天蝎座”所预期的那样——并非最仁慈的 恒星。

Being directly opposite Aldebaran, star of the spring equinox, Antares is associated with the autumn equinox. So as Aldebaran is about inception and new cycles starting, Antares is about closing down and cycles ending. This is by no means always negative. Suppose the question were, ‘Should I take early retirement?’ Antares on the Midheaven (or the Ascendant) would be an indication that a cycle is closing and it is

time to move on. 由于与代表春分点的毕宿五直接相对，心宿二与秋分点相关联。因此，正如毕宿 五关乎开端和新周期的开始，心宿二关乎结束和周期的终结。这绝不一定都是负 面的。假设问题是“我应该提前退休吗？”，心宿二位于中天（或上升点）将表 明一个周期正在结束，是时候继续前进了。

Other stars 其他的恒星

Other stars can be important in specific contexts. Suppose a woman were to ask, ‘Should I join the army?’ and Lord 10 were on Bellatrix (‘the female warrior’): this would be important testimony. But to deal with all these possibilities here, the fixed star chapter would be longer than the rest of the book, which would greatly exaggerate the overall importance of the stars in horary judgement. I plan to devote a future book to the fixed stars; in the meantime, I would suggest that there is a greater danger in overstating their significance than there is in ignoring them. Fear not, ignorance of their meanings will not keep you from sound judgement: there will always be other testimonies. 其他恒星在特定情境下可能很重要。假设一位女性问：“我应该参军吗？”而 10 宫主位于参宿五（“女战士星”）：这将是一个重要的征象。但若在此处探 讨所有这些可能性，恒星章节的篇幅将超过本书其余部分，从而极大地夸大恒星 在卜卦判断中的整体重要性。我计划未来专门撰写一本关于恒星的书；与此同时， 我认为过度强调其重要性的危险远大于忽略它们。请放心，不了解恒星的含义并 不会妨碍你做出可靠的判断：总会有其他征象存在。

If you wish to investigate the stars further, I commend Vivan Robson’s The Fixed Stars and Constellations in Astrology.This is based on traditional sources, though much diluted. If studying his book, ignore all his references to Alvidas and Wilson. For horary purposes, ignore also his specific notes for each of the planets falling on stars. In natal work, being specific like this makes sense: we can say ‘Your Satrun is on Regulus, therefore….’ But in horary it is not ‘your Saturn’, which is one facet of you, but ‘your significator’, which is all of you: it is not ‘your Saturn is on Regulus’ as much as ‘you are on Regulus’. So keep to the general meanings of the stars. 如如果你希望进一步研究恒星，我推荐 Vivan Robson（维万·罗布森）的《The Fixed Stars and Constellations in Astrology》。此书基于传统资料，尽管已大 为稀释。若研读他的书，请忽略其中所有关于 Alvidas（阿尔维达斯）和 Wilson （威尔逊）的引述。出于卜卦目的，也请忽略他对每颗行星落在恒星上的具体注 释。在本命占星中，这样具体化是有意义的：我们可以说“你的土星在轩辕十四 上，因此……”。但在卜卦中，它不是“你的土星”（这只是你的一部分），而 是“你的征象星”（代表完整的你）：与其说是“你的土星在轩辕十四上”，不 如说是“你在轩辕十四上”。因此，请坚持恒星的一般含义。

29. London (?) 1923. Available in a new edition under the Astrology Classics imprint of The Astrology Center of America. 29.伦敦（？）1923 年出版。美国占星中心的“占星经典”系列有新版本。

Robson’s list of stars gives their positions in 1920. To bring these up to date you will need to add ‘a degree and a bit’ to the positions he gives. The stars have their own individual motions as well as the general progression of 1 degree in 72 years (50″ in one year). These individual motions are tiny, but are sufficient to make exact calculation from 1 degree in 72 years inaccurate.But there is no benefit in computing these positions to the minute. By 2015, we can raise the ‘degree and a bit’ to ‘a degree and a half’. When studying Lilly’s charts, subtract 4 degrees from Robson’s positions, 5 from the positions I’ve given above. Robson 的恒星列表给出了它们在 1920 年的位置。要更新到现代位置，你需要在 他给出的位置上增加“大约 1 度多”。恒星除了每 72 年 1 度（每年 50 角秒）的 总体进动外，还有各自的自行。这些自行很小，但足以使得按 72 年 1 度进行的 精确计算变得不准确。但将这些位置计算到角分毫无益处。到 2015 年，我们 可以将“大约 1 度多”提升到“大约 1.5 度”。在研究 Lilly 的星盘时，从 Robson 给出的位置减去 4 度，从我上面给出的位置减去 5 度。

30. You have probably seen TV programmes showing how the shapes of the constellations change over thousands of years: that is these individual motions at work.
30. 你可能在电视节目中见过星座形状如何在数千年间变化的展示：那就是这些自行在起作 用。

If you involve other stars in your judgements, perhaps because you are already familiar with them, be wary of taking them too literally. Sometimes the context will demand a literal interpretation, as with the female warrior above. Usually it does not, so regard them instead as giving a descriptive tone. A star on the Ascendant of a horary chart can be seen as the illustration on the cover of a novel: it does not reveal the details of what will transpire, but it does give a general indication of the novel’s theme. If you want the details, read the book – or, in our case, judge the chart. The story will be told by the chart whether you look at the cover or not. 如果你将其他恒星纳入你的判断（或许因为你已经熟悉它们），请注意不要过于 按字面意思理解。有时背景会要求字面解释，如上文的女战士星。但通常不会， 因此应将其视为提供一种描述性的基调。卜卦盘上升点上的一颗恒星，可以看作 小说封面上的插图：它不会揭示即将发生事件的细节，但确实对小说的主题给出 一般性提示。如果你想要细节，就去读这本书——或者在我们的情况下，去判断 星盘。无论你是否看封面，故事都会由星盘讲述。

Example: I had been advised by the vet that I should have my dog spayed. I cast a chart to see if this was wise. Fixed stars all have the nature of one or more planets. All the relevant significators in this chart had stars of Venus/Saturn nature on them: limitation (Saturn) of her female reproductive system (Venus). But this told me

nothing that I didn’t already know by the nature of the question. 示例：兽医建议我为我的狗做绝育手术。我起了一张盘来看这是否明智。所有恒 星都具有一颗或多颗行星的性质。此盘中所有相关的征象星上都带有金星/土星 性质的恒星：对她雌性生殖系统（金星）的限制（土星）。但这并没有告诉我任 何超出问题本身性质之外的东西。

The soul of horary is quick, efficient judgement. You do not need the majority of the fixed stars for this. You may be tempted to race off and explore their use. Better far to work with simple tools and produce a sound result. In horary, less is truly more. Burning this maxim upon your heart is a more important lesson than learning the manifold details of the legion of fixed stars. 卜卦的灵魂在于快速、高效的判断。你不需要大多数恒星来实现这一点。你可能 很想立刻去探索它们的用途。但远不如使用简单的工具并得出可靠的结果。在卜 卦中，少即是多。将这句格言铭记于心，比学习众多恒星纷繁复杂的细节是更重 要的一课。

The main stars afflicting the eyes, physically or metaphorically, are: 在生理或隐喻上影响视力的主要恒星有：

The Andromeda nebula which is at 27 仙女座星云 白羊座 27 度

Capulus 24 天船二 金牛座 24 度

The Pleiades 29 昴宿星团 金牛座 29 度

The Hyades 5 毕宿星团 双子座 5 度

Ensis 23 参宿增三 双子座 23 度

Praesepe 7 鬼宿星团 狮子座 7 度

Copula 25 漩涡星云 处女座 25 度

Foramen 22 海山二 天平座 22 度

Aculeus 25

蝴蝶星团 射手座 25 度

Acumen 28 托勒密星团 射手座 28 度

Spiculum 0 三叶星云 摩羯座 0 度

Facies 8 人马座球状星团 摩羯座 8 度

Manubrium 14 建二 摩羯座 14 度

Other than where noted above, however, I suggest ignoring these unless the question specifically directs you to them (‘Am I in full possession of the facts here?’ ‘Is this eye operation a good idea?’) 然而，除非问题本身明确指向它们（例如“我是否完全掌握了此处的事实？”或 “这个眼部手术是个好主意吗？”），对于上述提到的影响视力的恒星，我建议 予以忽略。

# Arabian Parts

# 阿拉伯点

I used to use Arabian Parts a lot in horary. I now use them less and less, as I find that in most charts they tell nothing of major significance – and in horary we are not concerned with minor significance. Yet there are circumstances when it is worth taking a look at one of them. In most questions, an Arabian Part will not give the main answer. So resist the impulse to calculate ever more recondite Parts in the hope that one will suddenly transform your judgement. It won’t. 我曾经在卜卦占星中频繁使用阿拉伯点。如今我越来越少使用它们，因为我发现， 在大多数星盘中，它们并不能揭示主要征象——而在卜卦占星中，我们并不关心 次要的征象。然而，在某些情况下，值得查看其中的某一个点。在大多数问题中， 阿拉伯点不会给出主要答案。因此，请克制去计算更多冷门点的冲动，不要指望 其中一个会突然改变你的判断。它不会的。

An Arabian Part is a point in the chart that gives information about a specific subject. There are hundreds of such Parts, cast for anything from apricots to the death of kings to facilitating fraudulent marriage. The Part is calculated by taking the distance between two points (usually two planets) and extending that distance from a third point (usually the Ascendant). The most valuable and most often used of Parts is the Part of Fortune, or Fortuna. This is cast by measuring the distance from the Sun to the Moon and then extending that distance from the Ascendant. If the Sun is at 10 Taurus and the Moon at 25 Taurus, there are 15 degrees between the Sun and Moon, so Fortuna will be 15 degrees from the Ascendant, travelling anticlockwise. 阿拉伯点是星盘中的一个点，能提供关于特定主题的信息。这类点有成百上千个， 覆盖的主题从杏子到国王之死，再到促成欺诈婚姻等。计算该点的方法是：取两 点（通常是两颗行星）之间的距离，然后将此距离从第三点（通常是上升点）开 始延伸。其中最有价值且最常用的是福点。它的计算方法是测量从太阳到月亮的 距离，然后将此距离从上升点开始延伸。如果太阳在金牛座 10 度且月亮在金牛 座 25 度，太阳和月亮之间有 15 度的距离，因此福点将会在上升点逆时针方向 15 度的位置。

Most software will present you with a list of Arabian Parts for any chart. But if you are still using the page of the software that gives you this and other information, you haven’t been paying attention: stop it! Calculating Parts is not difficult, but the exercise involved may be sufficient to deter you from using them unnecessarily. 大多数软件会为任何星盘提供一个阿拉伯点列表。但如果你还在使用软件中提供

此类信息的页面，说明你没有专心听讲：快停下！计算阿拉伯点并不困难，但其 中涉及的计算过程足以阻止你不必要地使用它们。

More important, the way the Parts are presented in computer programs is wrong. What the software gives is a list of whichever Parts happen to be in close aspec to a planet in that chart. If the Part of Lentils is ‘Will she marry me?’ and lentils have nothing to do with it. That some random Part happens to be in aspect to a planet is irrelevant. It does not mean that the Part is therefore significant in that chart. 更重要的是，计算机程序中呈现阿拉伯点的方式是错误的。软件提供的是在该星 盘中恰好与某颗行星形成紧密相位的阿拉伯点列表。如果“扁豆点”对应的问题 是“她会嫁给我吗？”，而扁豆与此毫无关系。某个随机的点恰好与行星形成相 位是无关紧要的，这并不意味着该点在该星盘中具有重要性。

The correct use of Parts is to decide which Part we are interested in, calculate it, and then see what it and – most importantly – its dispositor are doing. They may or may not be in aspect to a planet. 正确使用阿拉伯点的方法是：先确定我们感兴趣的点，计算它，然后观察它以及 ——最重要的是——它的守护星的运作情况。它们是否会与行星产生相位。

THE CALCULATION

计算方式

If you already know how to do this, you can skip this box. 如果你已经知道如何计算，可以跳过此框。

All our degree measurements (6 Aries, 17 Cancer, etc) are measurements of celestial longitude. They tell us how far round the ecliptic a point is. A planet at 12 Taurus is in the second 30-degree chunk of the zodiac (which chunk we call Taurus) and is 12 degrees into that 30-degree chunk. 我们所有的度数测量（白羊座 6 度、巨蟹座 17 度等）都是对黄道经度（亦称 黄经）的测量。它们告诉我们一个点在黄道上绕行了多远。一颗行星在金牛 座 12 度，意味着它位于黄道十二宫的第二段 30 度区间（我们称该区间为金 牛座），并且已进入该区间的 12 度处。

When we are measuring the distance from one planet to another, counting how many degrees there are between them, we are measuring their distance apart in celestial longitude. But thinking, ‘The distance between them is 3 signs and 17 degrees’ is clumsy and invites error. It is much easier to work in absolute longitude. This is the distance something is from 0 Aries, but is expressed as a number of degrees, not as so many signs and so many degrees. Our example planet at 12 Taurus is at 42 degrees of absolute longitude. To reach it, starting from 0 Aries, we must travel through the 30 degrees that make up Aries, then

another 12 degrees of Taurus: 42 degrees in all. 当我们测量从一颗行星到另一颗行星的距离，计算它们之间有多少度时，我 们是在测量它们在黄道经度上的距离间隔。但是，用“它们之间的距离是 3 个星座又 17 度”这样的方式来思考是笨拙且容易出错的。使用绝对经度来计 算要容易得多。绝对经度是指某点距离白羊座 0 度的黄道经度，但它以度数 表示，而不是以“多少个星座又多少度”来表示。我们例子中位于金牛座 12 度的行星，其绝对经度是 42 度。为了从白羊座 0 度到达该点，我们必须先穿 过构成白羊座的 30 度，然后再经过金牛座的 12 度：总共 42 度。

The absolute longitude of 0 degrees of each sign is: 每个星座 0 度位置的绝对经度是：

Learn this table. 学习这个表格。

So a planet at 14 Leo has an absolute longitude of 120 degrees (0 Leo) + 14 degrees = 134 degrees. A planet at 8 Pisces has 330 degrees (0 Pisces) + 8 =338 degrees. 因此一颗行星在狮子座 14 度的绝对经度是 120 度（狮子座 0 度）+14 度=134 度。一颗行星在双鱼座 8 度的绝对经度是 330 度（双鱼座 0 度）+8 度=338 度。

The business of finding the distance between planet 1 and planet 2, then adding this distance to the Ascendant (or some other point) can be expressed more simply as Asc + planet 2 – planet 1. 计算阿拉伯点一般是先计算行星 1 和 2 之间的距离，然后加上上升点的距离 （或者其他别的点），可以更简单的标示为上升+行星 2-行星 1。

Suppose we wish to calculate the position of Fortuna in a chart where the Sun is at 17.34 Leo, the Moon is at 4.52 Libra and the Ascendant is 22.36 Virgo. 假设我们要计算星盘中福点的位置，根据太阳在狮子座 17.34 度，月亮在天 平座 4.52 度，上升点在处女座 22.36 度。

The formula for Fortuna is Asc + Moon – Sun. 福点的计算公式是上升点+月亮-太阳。

Asc is 22.36 Virgo. 上升点在处女座 22.36 度。 0 Virgo is 150 degrees, + 22.36 = 172.36 处女座 0 度（的绝对经度）是 150 度，+22.36=172.36

Moon is at 4.52 Libra. 月亮在天平座 4.52 度。 0 Libra is 180 degrees, + 4.52 = 184.52 天平座 0 度是 180 度，+4.52=184.52

Sun is at 17.34 Leo. 太阳在狮子座 17.34 度。 0 Leo is 120 degrees, + 17.34 = 137.34 狮子座 0 度是 120 度，+17.34=137.34

Note the number in the minutes column: 88 minutes. There are only 60 minutes in one degree, but ignore that arithmetical nicety here. If you avoid changing the minutes up into degrees (leaving them here as 88) you ensure that you can take away the third part of the formula without problem. Treat each side of the point as a separate sum, even if you have over 100 in the minute column. This will keep you clear of the usual errors with this calculation. 请注意弧分栏的数字：88 分钟。1 度只有 60 分，但在此处请忽略这个算术细 节。如果你避免将分进位成度（就让它保持 88 分钟），就能确保在减去公式 的第三部分时不出问题。将小数点前后的数字视为独立的两部分进行计算， 即使弧分栏的数字超过 100。这将使你避免在此类计算中常见的错误。

So Fortuna is at 219.54°of absolute longitude. 因此福点的绝对经度是 219.54 度。

Look at the table of absolute longitudes to find the biggest number that is less than 219.54. 从绝对经度列表中找出小于 219.54 度的最大值。

It is 210, which is 0 Scorpio. 是 210 度，在天蝎座 0 度。

So Fortuna is in Scorpio. 因此福点在天蝎座。

Take this 210 away from its absolute longitude of 219.54: 计算 210 度与 219.54 度之间的绝对经度的差值：

So Fortuna is at 9.54 Scorpio. 因此福点在天蝎座 9.54 度。

Note: you can add or subtract 360.00 at any time during this calculation if it will make the sum easier. If you find that the number you have to subtract is bigger than the number you got by adding the other two together, add 360 to the number you got from the addition. If the number you end up with when you’ve finished the sum is bigger than 360, subtract 360 from it. If your final total gives you a number of minutes greater than 60, subtract 60 from it and add 1 to the number of degrees. 注意：在此计算的任何阶段，如果能使运算更简便，你都可以随时加上或减 去 360.00。如果你发现要减去的数字大于你从另外两个数字相加得到的结果， 那么就在相加得到的结果上加上 360。如果计算最终得到的数字大于 360，就 从中减去 360。如果你的最终结果中分钟数大于 60，则从中减去 60，并将度 数部分的数字加 1。

Let’s do another one. Suppose we want to find the Part of Resignation and Dismissal, the formula for which is Saturn + Jupiter – Sun. Suppose Saturn is at 17.54 Aries, Jupiter at 4.58 Taurus, the Sun at 20.17 Sagittarius. 让我们来计算另外一个。假设我们想要找到辞职和解雇点，公式是土星+木星 -太阳。假设土星在白羊座 17.54 度，木星在金牛座 4.58 度，太阳在射手座 20.17 度。

note the minutes column 注意分值列

we can’t do this, so add 360.00 我们不能这么做，因此要加上 360.00

now we can subtract the Sun 现在我们能减去太阳了

So the Part is at 151.95°of absolute longitude. 因此该点在绝对经度 151.95 度。

This is degrees and minutes, though, not degrees and decimals. So now we must adjust the minutes column: 95 minutes = 1 degree and 35 minutes. 这里是度和分，而不是度和十进制小数位。所以现在我们必须调整分钟栏： 95 分钟 = 1 度 35 分钟。

So 151.95=152.35 因此 151.95=152.35

What is the biggest number less than this in the table? 列表中比这小一点的最大的数值是什么？

150. So the Part is in Virgo. 150。因此该点在处女座。

So the Part is at 2.35 Virgo. 因此该点在处女座 2.35 度。

As a little practice will soon show you, this calculation is far simpler than it might seem. I have had many students professing their innumeracy, but all have learned to do this without too much anguish. 一点练习很快就会向你证明，这个计算远比看起来简单。我遇到过许多自称 不擅长计算的学生，但他们都学会了这个方法，并且没有感到太痛苦。

Using the Parts 阿拉伯点的运用

It is a general principle that Parts don’t do, they are done to. They don’t cast aspects (a Part is nothing but a point in space: it has no light and so cannot cast an aspect); they have aspects cast to them. Suppose Jupiter is exactly square the Part of Marriage: whatever Jupiter signifies is putting a strain on the marriage; this does not show that the marriage has any effect on Jupiter.

一个普遍原则是：阿拉伯点本身不主动作用，而是被作用。它们不投射相位（阿 拉伯点仅是空间中的一个点：它没有光，因此不能投射相位）；它们接受其他星 体投射的相位。假设木星精确刑相位婚姻点：无论木星象征什么，它都在给婚姻 施加压力；这并不表示婚姻对木星有任何影响。

That said, certain Parts in certain circumstances can act as if they were casting aspects. If my significator applies to oppose the Part of Resignation and Dismissal, this is testimony that I may lose my job. What the Part is doing here is marking the time of an event, much as a milestone marks a place on a road, rather than showing the event itself. If the milestone tells me it is 100 miles to town, I may decide to stop for some dinner; this does not mean that the milestone has made me stop for dinner. But this is a quibble: in the chart the link between Part and action can be regarded as direct. 话虽如此，某些阿拉伯点在特定情况下可以表现得仿佛在投射相位。如果我的征 象星正在入对冲相位辞职与解雇点，这便是我可能失业的一个征象。此时阿拉伯 点的作用更像是标志事件发生的时间，如同路标标记路上的某个地点，而非显示 事件本身。如果路标告诉我距离城镇还有 100 英里，我可能决定停下来吃晚餐； 但这并不意味着是路标让我停下来吃饭。不过这是个细节问题：在星盘中，阿拉 伯点与行动之间的联系可以被视为直接的。

If you are taking an aspect to the Part to show an event, stick to conjunction and opposition. Other aspects are unlikely to give the event unless there is strong, congruent testimony elsewhere. 如果你将投射到阿拉伯点的相位视为事件的预示，请只关注合相与对冲相位。其 他相位不太可能预示事件，除非在其他地方存在强烈且一致的征象。

Consider the strength of Parts as with a planet: they are affected by combustion, aspects from planets, and so forth. Be cautious with gauging strength from house placement: if the Part of Work to be Done is in the 12th, does it mean it is weak, or does it suggest working with large animals? 评估阿拉伯点的强弱可参照行星：它们受燃烧、行星相位等影响。但根据宫位位 置判断强弱时要谨慎：如果工作完成点落在 12 宫，这是意味着它虚弱，还是暗 示要与大型动物一起工作？

Keep to the point. Do not introduce Parts unless they are directly relevant to the context. If the question is ‘When will I marry?’ the Part of Death conjunct Lord 7 does not mean you will marry an axe-murderer. It does not mean anything at all: it is not relevant and should not be used. If the question is ‘I am terminally ill; will I marry before I die?’ the Part of Death might well be relevant. 紧扣要点。除非阿拉伯点与问题直接相关，否则不要引入。如果问题是“我何时 会结婚？”，那么死亡点与 7 宫主合相并不意味着你会嫁给一个杀人犯。它根本 不代表任何意义：它与问题无关，不应被使用。如果问题是“我已病入膏肓；我 会在死前结婚吗？”，那么死亡点很可能就相关了。

Turned charts 转宫

If you are turning the chart, turn the Parts too. If I am asking, ‘Is being a ballerina really my daughter’s heart’s desire?’ it is no good my looking at the radical Part of Vocation. It is not my vocation that is in question; it is hers. So we must turn the Part, casting this Part from her 10th cusp, not mine. 如果你在进行转宫，也要将阿拉伯点一并转换。如果我问：“成为一名芭蕾舞演 员真的是我女儿内心的渴望吗？”，那么看我本命盘的职业点是没用的。问题不 在于我的职业，而是她的。因此我们必须转换这个点，从她的 10 宫头开始计算， 而不是我的。

The Part of Fortune 福点

Although this is the most important Part in natal astrology, and will be displayed on the chart by most software as a matter of course, its role in horary is limited. It rarely tells us anything that is not shown elsewhere. 尽管这是本命占星学中最重要的阿拉伯点，并且大多数软件会默认在星盘中显示 它，但它在卜卦占星中的作用有限。它很少能告诉我们其他位置没有显示的信息。

The formula for Fortuna is Asc + Moon – Sun. It is common practice to reverse this formula in night charts (Asc + Sun - Moon). I strongly advise against this: use the standard formula by day and by night. Most software allows you to choose whether to reverse by night or not. 福点的计算公式是：Asc + Moon – Sun。常见的做法是在夜生盘中反转此公式 （Asc + Sun - Moon）。我强烈建议不要这样做：无论日盘还是夜盘，都请使用 标准公式。大多数软件允许你选择是否在夜间反转公式。

Fortuna can show the querent’s treasure – whatever that might be in the context of the question. So if Fortuna is right on a house cusp, this can show that the affairs of that house are important to the querent. ‘When will I marry?’ with Fortuna on the 5th cusp might suggest that the querent’s ‘treasure’ is having children. The Part needs to be within a degree or two of the cusp to carry this meaning. 福点可以显示问卜者的“珍宝”——在问题的语境中，这“珍宝”可能是任何事 物。因此，如果福点正好位于某个宫头，这可能表明该宫位所掌管的事务对问卜 者很重要。例如“我何时会结婚？”，若福点在 5 宫头，可能暗示问卜者的“珍 宝”是拥有孩子。福点需要距离宫头一度或两度以内才具有此含义。

As Fortuna is the querent’s treasure, it can signify the missing thing in a lost object question. But it usually doesn’t: Fortuna is a long way down our list of possible

indicators. 由于福点是问卜者的珍宝，在失物问题中，它可以象征丢失的物品。但通常并非 如此：在我们可能使用的指示星列表中，福点的优先级相当靠后。

It can have a role in questions about money. The more general the question, the more likely it is to have this role. ‘How do my finances look over the coming months?’ with strong Jupiter trine Fortuna: very rosy! In a more specific question, such as ‘Will I make money by buying this flat to let out?’ even so rosy a testimony would have only a secondary significance. For the main line of the judgement, look to the house given by the question (in this case the 5th: 2nd from the 4th, hence profit from property). 它可能在关于金钱的问题中扮演角色。问题越笼统，它越可能扮演此角色。例如 “未来几个月我的财务状况如何？”，若有强旺的木星拱相位福点：前景非常光 明！在更具体的问题中，例如“我买下这套公寓出租会赚钱吗？”，即便是如此 积极的征象也只具有次要意义。判断的主要依据，应看向问题给出的宫位（此例 中为 5 宫：即 4 宫的 2 宫，代表来自房产的利润）。

As a general principle, if you notice that something is happening to Fortuna, such as an exact aspect, this can be worth considering, although it is unlikely to be of major significance. You don’t need to go looking for it specially (‘I wonder what Fortuna is up to.’). 作为一个普遍原则，如果你注意到福点正在发生某些情况，例如一个精确相位， 这可能值得考虑，尽管它不太可能具有主要重要性。你无需特意去寻找它（比如 “我想知道福点在干什么。”）。

### ✸I followed the old texts far too closely here, especially in the comments about

money. There is never, ever, in either horary or natal astrology, a direct connection between Fortuna and material fortune. Our illustrious forebears often claim that there is, especially in their judgements upon 2nd house matters, but this is a gross misunderstanding of the nature of Fortune, prompted by the need to provide the astrolgoer with yet one more thing to throw into the mix in order to somehow come up with a pleasing judgement. Had they known about asteroids, they would have been throwing them in by the bucketful.

### ✸我在此处过于拘泥于古典文献，尤其是在关于金钱的评论中。无论是在卜卦

占星还是本命占星学中，福点与物质财富之间都从来不存在直接联系。我们杰出 的前辈们经常声称存在这种联系，特别是在他们对 2 宫事务的判断中，但这严重 误解了福点的本质，其动机是为了给占星师提供更多可混入判断的因素，以便最 终得出一个令人满意的结论。如果他们知道有小行星的存在，恐怕会成桶地往里 扔。

I cannot remember ever judging a horary where Fortuna showed anything of importance. Lilly gives example charts that show it doing so, but the careful analysis of these judgements shows that he was wrong. See, for instance, the charts in

Christian Astrology chapters LXIII and LIV. I will discuss these in detail in Horary Practice.✷ 我不记得曾经判断过任何一个福点显示了重要信息的卜卦盘。Lilly 给出的示例 星盘显示它有此作用，但对这些判断的仔细分析表明他是错误的。例如，参见 《Christian Astrology》第六十三章和第五十四章中的星盘。我将在《Horary Practice》中详细讨论这些案例。✷

The Part of Marriage: Asc + Desc – Venus 婚姻点：Asc + Desc – Venus

This Part plays an important role in many relationship questions. I use it more than all the other Parts put together. 此点在众多关系问题中扮演重要角色。我使用它的频率超过其他所有阿拉伯点的 总和。

This Part tells us about the quality of the relationship between two people, and of their attitude towards it. It also tells, metaphorically, of the relationship’s attitude to each of them: if reception shows that this Part hates one partner, we see that the relationship harms that person. 此点告诉我们两人之间关系的质量，以及他们对这段关系的态度。同时，它也隐 喻性地揭示了这段关系对其中每一方的态度：如果接纳关系显示此点厌恶其中一 方，我们便看到这段关系对那个人造成了伤害。

### ✸I could have been clearer here. Receptions are read from the dispositor of the Part,

not from the Part itself. See the added note below.✷

### ✸我本可以在此处表述得更清晰。接纳关系需从该点的守护星来解读，而非从

该点本身。请参见下文补充说明。✷

It does not relate solely to the relationship between those persons signified by the 1st and 7th houses. If Lord 7 is the married querent’s lover, the Part of Marriage describes her relationship with the lover, not her marriage. 它不仅限于象征 1 宫和 7 宫所指代的那两个人之间的关系。如果 7 宫主是已婚问 卜者的情人，那么婚姻点描述的是她与情人的关系，而非她的婚姻。

Consider this example: 考虑以下例子：

Lord 1 is Mars at 19 Virgo, showing the querent 1 宫主是位于处女座 19 度的火星，代表问卜者

Lord 7 is Venus at 12 Gemini, showing the querent’s wife

7 宫主是位于双子座 12 度的金星，代表问卜者的妻子

The Part of Marriage is at 5 Virgo. 婚姻点位于处女座 5 度。

It is a night chart. 这是一个夜生盘。

Do the spouses like each other? 这对夫妻喜欢对方吗？

Check the receptions to find out (chapter 8). 检查接纳关系以找出答案（参见第 8 章）。

Mars is in the face to Venus. Venus is in the face to Mars. 火星位于金星的得面位置。金星位于火星的得面位置。

So there is a mutual reception between them, but only by face. This is very weak – scarcely a flicker of affection. 因此它们之间存在互溶，但仅通过得面。这种联系非常微弱——几乎谈不上有感 情。

Mars is also in the fall of Venus: the querent loathes his wife. 火星也位于金星的弱势位置：问卜者厌恶他的妻子。

But Mars and Venus share a powerful interest in Mercury: Mars is in Mercury’s sign and exaltation; Venus is in its sign and triplicity. Whatever Mercury signifies is of major importance to both of them. 但是，火星和金星都对水星有强烈的兴趣：火星位于水星入庙和旺势的位置；金 星位于水星入庙和三分的位置。无论水星象征什么，对双方都至关重要。

What is Mercury? 水星是什么？

The Part of Marriage is at 5 Virgo, so Mercury is the dispositor of the Part of Marriage. Mercury signifies the marriage. 婚姻点位于处女座 5 度，因此水星是婚姻点的定位星。水星象征着这段婚姻。

So we see that although the partners don’t like each other, they both value their marriage. This is common, especially in charts of the ‘Will our marriage survive?’ type. It is also common in such cases to find that the dispositor of the Part of Marriage is itself disposited by Lord 5: what is important to the marriage? The childern. 于是我们看到，尽管伴侣并不喜欢彼此，但他们都珍视他们的婚姻。这很常见， 尤其是在“我们的婚姻能维持下去吗？”这类星盘中。在此类案例中，也常发现

婚姻点的守护星本身又由 5 宫主守护：对婚姻重要的是什么？是孩子。

In relationship questions, if you find that both parties share a strong interest in an as yet unidentified plant, you will usually find that this planet disposits the Part of Marriage. It is as if there were three distinct entities involved: the husband, the wife and the marriage itself. 在关系问题中，如果你发现双方都对一颗尚未确定的行星有强烈兴趣，通常你会 发现这颗行星正是婚姻点的守护星。这仿佛涉及三个独立的实体：丈夫、妻子和 婚姻本身。

The dispositor of an Arabian Part signifies that thing. The dispositor of the Part of Marriage signifies the marriage; the dispositor of the Part of Surgery signifies the surgery; the dispositor of the Part of Wheat signifies the querent’s wheat. 阿拉伯点的定位星代表该事物。婚姻点的定位星象征婚姻；手术点的定位星象征 手术；小麦点的定位星象征问卜者的小麦。

This is important: it is this that enables us to discover the attitudes of the people involved towards that thing, while the condition of the dispositor will tell us at least as much as the condition of the Part itself about the condition of that thing. 这一点很重要：正是这一点使我们能够发现相关人士对该事物的态度，同时，该 定位星的状态所能告诉我们的关于该事物状况的信息，至少不亚于该阿拉伯点本 身的状态。

Some examples of what this can show us: 以下是一些它能向我们展示的例子：

* ‘Have I got a future with Bob?’ with querent’s significators showing no interest in Lord 7 (Bob) but in major dignities of the dispositor of the Part of Marriage. ‘You don’t seem to like Bob that much. The chart suggests that you want a relationship, and he’s just the guy who happened along.’ *“我和 Bob（鲍勃）有未来吗？”——问卜者的征象星对 7 宫主（Bob）没有兴 趣，但对婚姻点的定位星表现出强烈的尊贵关系。“你似乎并不那么喜欢 Bob。 星盘暗示你想要一段关系，而他只是恰好出现的那个男人。”

* ‘When will I find a husband?’ with Lord 1 having recently entered the sign ruled by the dispositor of the Part of Marriage. The querent has only recently decided that she wants to marry. This is common in questions where the marriage will be arranged.
* “我什么时候能找到丈夫？”——1 宫主最近刚进入由婚姻点的定位星所守护 的星座。问卜者只是最近才决定她想结婚。这在婚姻将由他人安排的问题中很常 见。

* ‘Is she leaving me?’ with Lord 7 at 29 degrees of the sign ruled by dispositor of the Part of Marriage. She is at the very least about to lose interest in the marriage, and is quite possibly physically leaving. Which it is will be shown by other testimonies. But

perhaps her planet is in station, turning retrograde before it leaves the sign: ‘She’s seriously thinking of going, but she’ll change her mind’.
* “她要离开我吗？”——7 宫主位于婚姻点的定位星所守护的星座的 29 度。 她至少即将对这段婚姻失去兴趣，并且很可能正在身体力行地离开。具体是哪种 情况将由其他征象显示。但也许她的行星正处在停滞状态，在离开该星座前转为 逆行：“她认真考虑过要走，但她会改变主意。”

* ‘Will our marriage be long and happy?’ with the dispositor of the Part of Marriage placed at the beginning of a fixed sign and having lots of essential dignity. ‘It will be long （fixed sign) and happy （essentially strong).’ *“我们的婚姻会长久而幸福吗？”——婚姻点的定位星位于一个固定星座的开 头，并拥有许多先天尊贵。“婚姻将会长久（固定星座）而幸福（先天强旺）。”

* ‘Will my mother approve?’ with Lord 10 （Mum) in the fall of the dispositor of the Part of Marriage. ‘No!’
