* “我母亲会同意吗？”——10 宫主（母亲）位于婚姻点的定位星的弱势位置。 “不会！”

* ‘Will we have children?’ with Part of Marriage and its disposiotr in fertile signs: strong testimony for ‘Yes’.
* “我们会有孩子吗？”——婚姻点及其定位星位于肥沃的星座：强有力的“是” 的征象。

What the Part of Marriage does not do is give the answer to ‘When will we marry?’ The timing will not be given by an aspect from one of the partners to the Part of Marriage or its dispositor. We need an aspect between the two people. This Part shows the relationship, not the event of the marriage. 婚姻点无法做到的是回答“我们什么时候结婚？”这个问题的答案不会由伴侣一 方的行星与婚姻点或其定位星形成相位来给出。我们需要的是两个人之间的相位。 此点显示的是关系，而非结婚这一事件。

### ✸As said, the dispositor of a Part signifies that thing, so the dispositor of the Part of

Marriage signifies the relationship between these two people. There is no significance whatever in any of the other dignities and debilities in which the Part stands. We would never think ‘The Part exalts Mars’ or ‘The Part is in the detriment of Saturn’. All receptions involving the Part are read from its dispositor, not from the position of the Part itself. If, for instance, the dispositor of the Part of Marriage were in the fall of Lord 1, we would judge that the relationship disappoints the querent. If the Part itself were in the fall of Lord 1 this would tell us nothing. This is because receptions are a two-way street, but it is not possible for a planet to be in the dignity or debility of a Part. Look at the Table of Dignities on page 54. There are planets in it, but no Parts: a planet cannot be in the exaltation of a Part or the detriment of a Part, but only in that of another planet.✷

### ✸如前所述，一个阿拉伯点的定位星象征该事物，因此婚姻点的定位星象征着

这两人之间的关系。该阿拉伯点本身所处的任何其他尊贵或衰弱位置都没有意义。 我们绝不会去思考“该点位于火星的旺势位置”或“该点位于土星的落陷位置”。 所有涉及该点的接纳关系都从其定位星来解读，而非从该点本身的位置。例如， 如果婚姻点的定位星位于 1 宫主的弱势位置，我们会判断这段关系让问卜者失望。 如果婚姻点本身位于 1 宫主的弱势位置，这则无法说明任何问题。这是因为接纳 关系是双向的，而行星不可能处于一个阿拉伯点的尊贵或衰弱位置。请查看第 101 页的尊贵表。表中有行星，但没有阿拉伯点：一颗行星不可能位于一个阿拉 伯点的旺势或落陷位置，而只能是位于另一颗行星的此类位置。✷

The Part of Marriage of Women: Asc + Saturn – Venus 女性婚姻点：Asc + Saturn – Venus

The Part of Marriage of Men: Asc + Venus – Saturn 男性婚姻点：Asc + Venus – Saturn

The Part of the Marriage Partner: Asc + Desc – Lord7 婚姻伴侣点：Asc + Desc – Lord7

I mention these Parts only so you don’t get confused when you come across them elsewhere. They are relevant only to arranged marriages, and despite my having done many horaries on that subject, I have never found them helpful there either. Keep them for natal work. The first two of these Parts reverse their formulae by night, so Marriage of Women by day is Marriage of Men by night and vice versa. 我提及这些点，只是为了让你在其他地方遇到时不至于困惑。它们仅与包办婚姻 相关，尽管我曾就这一主题做过许多卜卦，但从未发现它们在那里有何助益。请 将它们保留用于本命分析。前两个点的公式在夜盘中需反转，因此白天的女性婚 姻点在夜间即为男性婚姻点，反之亦然。

The Part of Divorce: Asc + Desc – Mars 离婚点：Asc + Desc – Mars

There is an idea that the formula for this Part is that for the Part of Marriage reversed. This is wrong: divorce is not the oposite of marriage. 有一种观点认为，此点的公式是婚姻点公式的反转。这是错误的：离婚并非婚姻 的对立面。

Unsurprisingly, one or both spouses are often found in major dignities of the dispositor of this Part in questions where divorce is a live option. One partner may well exalt it, regarding the divorce as the solution to all problem; the other may be in

its fall, hating and fearing the idea. 不足为奇的是，在离婚是一个现实选择的问题中，经常发现夫妻一方或双方都与 此点的定位星存在主要的尊贵关系。一方可能非常旺势此星，视离婚为解决所有 问题的方法；另一方则可能处于此星的弱势位置，憎恶并恐惧离婚的想法。

Unlike the Part of Marriage, this Part does relate to a specific event, so an aspect to it can give that event and its timing. Significator applies to conjunct the Part of Divorce: ‘You’ll get divorced’ (other testimonies agreeing, of course). Significator applies to oppose the Part of Divorce: ‘You’ll get divorced, but wish you hadn’t’. 与婚姻点不同，此点确实与一个具体事件相关，因此与其形成的相位可以给出该 事件及其时间。征象星入合相位离婚点：“你会离婚”（当然，需要其他征象同 意）。征象星入对冲相位离婚点：“你会离婚，但事后会后悔”。

‘Will our divorce affect the children?’ with Lord 5 and the dispositor of the Part of Divorce in each other’s detriment: ‘You bet! They hate it and it hates them’. “我们的离婚会影响孩子吗？”——5 宫主与离婚点的定位星处于彼此的落陷位 置：“当然会！他们痛恨此事，此事也对他们有害。”。

Do not cast this Part unless the question states that divorce is a serious option! No matter how the Part might be placed, if divorce is not an option it will not be relevant, as if an actor playing Hamlet wanders on stage during a production of Othello. It doesn’t matter how convincingly he might ad lib: he’s in the wrong play and should be ignored. This is true of all Parts. 除非问题明确指出离婚是一个严肃的选项，否则不要计算此点！无论此点位置如 何，如果离婚并非一个选项，它就无关紧要，如同扮演 Hamlet（哈姆雷特）的 演员在《奥赛罗》演出中误入舞台。无论他即兴表演得多有说服力：他进错了戏， 应当被忽略。这对所有阿拉伯点都是如此。

### ✸I no longer use this Part. No one is interested in divorce. People might say ‘I want

a divorce’, but this isn’t what they mean. What they mean is ‘I no longer wish to be married.’ ✷

### ✸我已不再使用此点。没有人对离婚本身感兴趣。人们可能会说“我想离婚”，

但这并非他们的本意。他们的本意是“我不再希望维持这段婚姻。”✷

The Part of Resignation and Dismissal 辞职和解雇点

This is a rarity among Parts, being calculated from the positions of three planets: Saturn + Jupiter – Sun. Look at this in questions of the ‘Will I keep my job?’ variety. 此点在阿拉伯点中较为罕见，其计算基于三颗行星的位置：土星 + 木星 – 太

阳。在诸如“我能保住工作吗？”这类问题中查看此点。

Like the Part of Divorce, this relates to an event, so an aspect to this Part can give us that event. If the question were ‘Should I resign?’ the querent’s planet applying to oppose the Part of Resignation and Dismissal would suggest, ‘It looks as if you may, but you’ll regret it’. 与离婚点类似，此点与一个事件相关，因此与其形成的相位可以给出该事件。如 果问题是“我应该辞职吗？”，问卜者的行星入对冲相位辞职与解雇点将暗示： “看起来你可能会辞职，但你会后悔。”。

Suppose the dispositor of the Part of Dismissal is sitting on the Ascendant: the idea of being sacked is weighing on the querent. In itself, though, this testimony shows only that the idea is weighing on him; it does not show him being sacked. 假设解雇点的定位星正落在上升点上：被解雇的想法正困扰着问卜者。然而，这 个征象本身仅表明这个想法在困扰他；并不显示他会被解雇。

The Part of Vocation: MC + Moon – Sun 职业点：MC + Moon – Sun The Part of Fame: Asc + Jupiter – Sun 名望点：Asc + Jupiter – Sun

Although these are most useful in natal work, it can be worth looking at them in horaries on vocational questions. The Part of Vocation is the same as Fortuna, except that it is extended from the Midheaven instead of the Ascendant. As it is based on Fortuna, I advise against reversing the formula in night charts. The Part of Fame does reverse by night. 尽管这两点在本命分析中最有用，但在涉及职业问题的卜卦中，查看它们也值得 一试。职业点与福点的计算方式相同，区别在于它是从中天而非上升点开始延伸。 由于它基于福点，我建议在夜生盘中不要反转公式。而名望点的公式在夜盘中需 要反转。

Although it would be a rare horary where it carries this meaning, Fortuna is the soul, which is why it carries the idea of being the querent’s treasure, ‘the pearl of great price’. The vocation is what the soul is called to do, hence the Part of Vocation being the same arc as Fortuna, extended from the MC, which (10th house) shows our action. This Part can give insight into our querent’s deepest longings in the direction of action. 尽管在卜卦中罕见此意，但福点即是灵魂，这就是为什么它被赋予“问卜者的珍 宝”、“无价之宝”这层含义。职业是灵魂的召唤，因此职业点与福点的弧长相 同，但从中天（即 10 宫，代表我们的行动）开始延伸。此点可以让我们洞悉问 卜者在行动方向上最深切的渴望。

‘I’m gonna die if Dad makes me become an accountant!’ with Mercury opposing the Part of Vocation: we can see why. Accountancy is opposed to the nature of the querent’s soul. Part of Vocation in a fertile sign on the 5th cusp: ‘Maybe you should stay at home and have children’. Common is a strong emphasis on the 2nd house: ‘You need to stop living on air and earn some serious money, for the good of your soul’. “如果我爸逼我当会计，我会死的！”——水星对冲职业点：我们可以理解原因。 会计职业与问卜者灵魂的本性相悖。职业点位于肥沃的星座，且在 5 宫头：“也 许你应该待在家里生孩子”。通常也会有对 2 宫的强烈强调：“为了你灵魂的好 处，你需要停止不切实际的生活，去赚点实实在在的钱。”。

The Part of Fame is also called the Part of Work to be Done. This is perhaps the better name for it, because it does not necessarily make us famous, but it does carry the sense of ‘a man’s gotta do what a man’s gotta do’. This is at a more material level than vocation. If that is the soul’s calling, this is ‘You’re in this time, this place, and have these abilities; this is what need to be done’. 名望点也称为待完成工作点。这或许是它更贴切的名称，因为它不一定会让我们 出名，但它确实带有“尽其本分”的意味。这比职业点处于更物质的层面。如果 职业点是灵魂的召唤，那么这一点则是“你身处这个时代、这个地方，拥有这些 能力；这些就是需要完成的事”。

The Part of Death 死亡点

There are several formulae for this. The ones I use are Asc + 8th cusp – Moon and 8th cusp + Saturn – Moon. This is not to suggest that other formulae are wrong, but two is quite sufficient. 此点有多个计算公式。我使用的是：Asc + 8th cusp – Moon 和 8th cusp + Saturn – Moon。这并不是说其他公式错误，但两个已经足够了。

Be careful how you use this. Death is an important event in the life: we do not have to scrape up minor testimonies in order to show it. Do not take an aspect to the Part of Death as sole testimony that someone will die. 使用时要谨慎。死亡是生命中的重要事件：我们无需搜集次要的征象来证明它。 不要将与死亡点形成的相位作为某人将会死亡的唯一征象。

In questions directly about death I no longer use these Parts. If the person will die it will be shown by other testimonies (aspect to Lord 8, for example). I have yet to see a chart where death was shown only, or even primarily, by a Part. If you do not exercise a little restraint here your horary charts will have more dead bodies than a Hong Kong cop movie. 在直接关于死亡的问题中，我已不再使用这些点。如果某人将会死亡，会有其他

征象显示（例如与 8 宫主的相位）。我还没见过死亡仅由阿拉伯点，甚至主要由 阿拉伯点显示的星盘。如果你在此处不稍加克制，你的卜卦盘恐怕会比香港警匪 片出现更多尸体。

Keep these Parts for questions where Death is a shadowy figure lurking in the background: will he walk out on stage? A political exile asks, ‘Is it safe for me to go back to my country?’ with the Parts of Death or their significators very much in play: ‘Too risky’. This is not a clear testimony of ‘No, you’ll be killed’; it is enough to warrant caution. 这些点适用于死亡如阴影潜伏在背景中的问题：它是否会登上舞台？例如政治流 亡者问“我回国是否安全？”，若死亡分点或其征象星显著活跃：“风险过高”。 这并非明确的“不，你会被杀”的征象，但足以成为需要谨慎的理由。

Similarly with ‘Should I have this operation?’ Finding the Part of Death on the Midheaven (dominating the chart) or in the same degree as the Part of Surgery: ‘No, too much risk’. The Part on its own will not show that Death carries you off; it can show that you’re coming closer to him than is wise. “我应该做这个手术吗？”这类问题也类似。发现死亡点位于中天（主宰星盘） 或与手术点同度：“不，风险太高”。此点本身不会显示死亡将带走你；它可以 显示你正不明智地接近死亡。

The Part of Surgery: Asc + Saturn – Mars 手术点：Asc + Saturn – Mars

This reverses by night, giving Asc + Mars – Saturn. In most horaries on surgery we can take Mars, its natural ruler, to signify the surgery. If Mars is the significator of either the querent or the ailment, we need another option, which this Part can provide. Even if we are able to use Mars, it is worth casting this Part to see what it has to tell us. 此点在夜盘中公式反转，变为 Asc + Mars – Saturn。在大多数关于手术的卜卦中， 我们可以用其先天守护星火星来象征手术。如果火星是问卜者或疾病的征象星， 我们就需要另一个选项，而此点可以提供。即使我们能使用火星，也值得计算此 点来看看它能告诉我们什么。

Be careful! Even at its best, surgery is not nice: don’t expect to see happy planets in friendly aspect. Finding the significator of the illness ruled by the dispositor of this Part is most encouraging: the surgery has power over the illness. The illness dispositing the Part of Surgery or its ruler is most unfortunate. 小心！即使在最佳情况下，手术也不轻松：不要期望看到快乐的行星形成和谐的 相位。发现疾病的征象星受此点定位星的守护，是最令人鼓舞的：手术对疾病有 控制力。而疾病定位此手术点或其定位星，则非常不利。

People ask about laser surgery on their eyes. Finding the Part of Surgery or its dispositor on a star that afflicts the eyes (see page 131) would be a negative indicator. Look also at the relationship between the Part, together with its dispositor, and the Sun and Moon, the natural rulers of the eyes. 人们会询问关于眼睛激光手术的问题。发现手术点或其定位星位于一颗伤害眼睛 的恒星上（见第 220 页），将是一个负面指示。同时也要观察此点及其定位星与 眼睛的先天守护星太阳和月亮的关系。

Reversing the formula for this Part gives the Part of Sickness. This is one option for the significator of an illness, but we have better. I suggest leaving this for natal work. 将此点公式反转即得到疾病点。这是疾病征象星的一个选项，但我们有更好的选 择。我建议将此点留待本命分析中使用。

Parts of Commodities 商品点

Wheat, olives, cotton, grapes: these and more all have their Parts. In days long past a staple of the astrologer’s trade was queries on when to market one’s crop, or whether to plant this or that. These Parts are invaluable for deciding such questions – though in the modern world such questions are few and far between. Strong Jupiter trines the Part of Maize; weak Saturn opposes the Part of Wheat: go for maize next year. Lord 8 (2nd from 7th: the other people’s money) conjuncts the Part of Cucumbers in two degrees: take your cucumbers to market in two days and you’ll make a killing. 小麦、橄榄、棉花、葡萄：这些和更多商品都有其对应的阿拉伯点。在遥远的过 去，占星师业务的一个重要部分是关于何时出售收成，或种植何种作物的咨询。 这些点对于决定此类问题是无价的——尽管在现代世界，此类问题已非常罕见。 强旺的木星拱相位玉米点；衰弱的土星对冲小麦点：明年种玉米吧。8 宫主（7 宫的 2 宫：他人的钱财）在 2 度内与黄瓜点在两度内形成合相：两天后把你的黄 瓜拿到市场去卖，你会大赚一笔。

As this is a textbook and not an encyclopaedia, I will not list these Parts here. If you are asked such a question – and among the thousands of horaries I have done I can recall but one – refer to al-Biruni, who gives a comprehensive list of Parts.If you need the Part for a commodity he does not list, study the way his other formulae are constructed, then substitute the natural ruler of the commodity in question. 由于这是一本教科书而非百科全书，我不会在此列出这些点。如果你被问到此类 问 题 — — 在 我 做 过 的 成 千 上 万 个 卜 卦 中 ， 我 只 能 回 忆 起 一 次 — — 请 参 考 al-Biruni 的著作，他提供了全面的阿拉伯点列表。如果你需要的商品点他未列 出，请研究他其他公式的构建方式，然后用该商品的先天守护星进行替换。

31. Al-Biruni, op. cit. paras 476-479.

Other Parts 其他阿拉伯点

If you feel the urge to incorporate other Parts in your charts, see al-Biruni for their formulae. Working with his table, the arithmetic is Place 3 + Place 2 – Place 1. But if you feel the urge to incorporate other Parts in your charts you probably have not understood the basics of horary. Let’s build the house before we start sticking fancy bits on the outside. You don’t need them! Extra techniques will never substitute for a lack of work on the basics. So do some more work on the basics. 如果你感到有必要在你的星盘中纳入其他阿拉伯点，请查阅 al-Biruni 以获取其 计算公式。根据他的表格计算，其算术原理是：位置 3 + 位置 2 – 位置 1。但 如果你感到有必要在你的星盘中纳入其他阿拉伯点，那你很可能还未理解卜卦占 星的基本法则。让我们先建好房屋的主体结构，再去考虑外部装饰。你并不需要 它们！额外的技巧永远无法弥补基本法则功底的缺失。所以，多在基本法则上下 功夫吧。

### ✸In the first line of this chapter I wrote that I use the Parts less and less. With the

exception of the Part of Marriage, which can be useful, I now use them scarcely at all. Like the fixed stars, they are very important in natal astrology but have little use in horary. If you find you are using them in more than the occasional chart, you are using them too much. Keep it simple!✷

### ✸在本章开头我曾写道，我越来越少使用阿拉伯点。除了可能有些用处的婚姻

点之外，我现在几乎完全不使用它们了。如同恒星一样，它们在本命占星学中非 常重要，但在卜卦占星中用途甚微。如果你发现自己在超过偶尔的星盘中用到它 们，那你就用得太多了。保持简单！✷

# Timing

# 应期

Brace yourself: this is the tricky bit. Querents do not want to know only if things will happen; they have the habit of wanting to know when things will happen. So we must be able to time our predictions. 做好心理准备：这部分比较棘手。问卜者不仅想知道事情是否会发生；他们往往 还习惯想知道事情何时会发生。因此，我们必须能够预测应期。

This is possible with great accuracy: I have timed predictions to the minute, although it would be foolish to do this for clients – it is amusing, but serves no practical purpose. Sometimes the judgement of timing is clear, so clear that it can be as simple as anything else we have considered. More often, however, it does involve balancing considerations and possibilities. 这可以做到非常精确：我曾将预测的应期精确到分钟，尽管对客户这样做是愚蠢 的——这很有趣，但没有实际意义。有时，对应期的判断是清晰的，如此清晰， 以至于它可以像我们考虑过的任何其他事情一样简单。然而，更多时候，它确实 涉及到对各种考量和可能性进行权衡。

The Method 方法

Assume that you have set a horary and judged that there will be an event: ‘Yes, such and such will happen’. This event will usually have been shown by an aspect. It is usually this aspect that gives us the timing of that event. 假设你已经设立了一个卜卦盘，并判断出某事件会发生：“是的，如此这般的事 情将会发生”。这个事件通常是通过一个相位来显示的。通常也正是这个相位为 我们提供了该事件的应期。

Occasionally we have to look elsewhere for the timing, either because the event-giving aspect provides no timing that could be true, or because the event is shown by something other than an aspect. Look back at the lost cat chart in chapter 1. The event – the cat’s return – was shown not by an aspect, but by Jupiter being retrograd. Jupiter was making no significant aspect, so something else had to show the

timing of the cat’s return. In this case, it was the Moon’s application to an aspect with the Ascendant. 偶尔，我们不得不从别处寻找应期，这要么是因为显示事件的相位未能提供一个 可能成立的应期，要么是因为事件是通过相位之外的其它征象显示的。回顾第 1 章中丢失猫咪的星盘。事件——猫咪的回归——并非通过一个相位显示，而是通 过木星的逆行。木星当时没有形成任何重要的相位，因此必须有其他征象来显示 猫咪回归的应期。在那个案例中，是月亮与上升点的入相位。

The appropriate aspect, once identified, can show us the timing of the event in various ways. 一旦确定了相关的相位，它可以通过多种方式向我们显示事件的应期。

All timing is with reference to the moment for which the horary is cast. This is ‘time zero’. 所有的应期都是相对于卜卦盘设立的那个时刻而言的。这个时刻就是“时间零 点”。

Using past events 利用往事

If it is available to us, this is by far the most reliable and most accurate method for timing. It depends upon the chart showing us a past event. Suppose the question is ‘When will I marry again?’ and we know that our querent divorced three years ago. The chart shows her significator separating from Mars, the natual ruler of divorce. If it is 5 degrees separated from Mars, we know that on the scale of this chart, 5 degrees = 3 years. So if her significator now applies to aspect the ruler of the seventh house, signifying the future husband, in 10 degrees, judgement is simple: ‘You will remarry in 2×3=6 years’. It is as if the chart carries its own scale of calibration, as we might find the scale marked on a map. 如果条件允许，这是目前为止最可靠、最精确的确定应期的方法。它依赖于星盘 向我们显示一个过去的事件。假设问题是“我何时会再婚？”，并且我们知道问 卜者三年前离婚了。星盘显示她的征象星与代表离婚的先天守护星火星刚形成出 相位。如果它与火星刚刚分离了 5 度，我们就知道在这张星盘的时间刻度上，5 度 = 3 年。那么，如果她的征象星现在正与象征未来丈夫的 7 宫主形成入相位， 相差 10 度，判断就很简单了：“你将在 2 × 3 = 6 年后再婚”。这就像星盘自 带一个校准刻度，好比我们在地图上找到标注的比例尺一样。

32. The chart discussed in The Real Astrology pp. 4-7 gives an example of this.
32. 《The Real Astrology》第 4-7 页讨论的星盘为此提供了一个例子。

Sign and house 星座与宫位

Unfortunately, few charts show past events. Or as in principle I suppose that they all should, few are they that show them with sufficient clarity for this to be of use. So we need to find other methods. This is when it starts to get complicated. 遗憾的是，很少有星盘会显示过去的事件。或者，从原则上讲，我认为它们都应 该显示，但很少有星盘能足够清晰地显示它们以供利用。因此，我们需要找到其 他方法。这时事情就开始变得复杂了。

Timing, for reasons that I do not understand, is the one area of horary where students display the utmost resistance to absorbing knowledge. Pay attention! This works. 出于我不理解的原因，应期判断是卜卦占星学中学生最抗拒吸收知识的领域。请 注意！以下方法是有效的！

We have our aspect. If we have an aspect there will be a number of degrees between where the applying planet is now and where it will be when the aspect perfects. Unless this is one of those charts where we can take the timing from a pase event, this number is the number of time units (hours, days, years, etc) between the time of question and the time of the event. 我们有我们的相位。如果我们有一个相位，那么在入相行星当前所在位置与该相 位成相时它所处的位置之间，会存在若干度数。除非这是那种我们可以从过去事 件中获取应期信息的星盘，否则这个度数就代表了从提问时刻到事件发生时刻之 间的时间单位（小时、天、年等）数量。

Take the number of degrees that the applying planet must travel before perfecting the aspect. Suppose the aspect is Sun at 10 Taurus applying to Mars at 14 Leo. How far must the Sun travel to make the aspect? 取入相行星在成相前必须运行的度数。假设相位是位于金牛座 10 度的太阳正向 位于狮子座 14 度的火星入相。太阳必须运行多远才能形成这个相位？

The answer is not 4 degrees. 答案不是 4 度。

Mars is not standing still, waiting for the Sun to catch up. Mars is moving too. What concerns us is not the distance the applying planet must travel to reach the position of the other planet as it is in the chart. 火星并非静止不动，等着太阳赶上。火星也在移动。我们关心的并不是入相行星 需要运行多远才能到达星盘中另一颗行星所在的位置。

What concerns us is the distance the applying planet must travel to perfect the aspect. For this, you will need to consult your ephemeris. 我们关心的是入相行星需要运行多远才能使该相位成相。为此，你需要查阅你的 星历表。

My students can be recognised by having the words CONSULT YOUR EPHEMERIS branded onto their foreheads. Branding is painful, so please pay attention here. It is where the aspect perfects that matters. 我的学生额头上都烙着“查阅你的星历表”这几个字，这是他们的标志。烙印很 痛苦，所以请务必注意这里。重要的是形成完美相位的位置。

The Sun at 10 Taurus applying to Mars at 14 Leo would typically perfect when the Sun is at about 17 Taurus, not 14 Taurus. The Sun has had to travel 7 degrees to perfect the aspect, not 4. 位于金牛座 10 度的太阳向位于狮子座 14 度的火星入相，通常会在太阳运行到大 约金牛座 17 度时成相，而不是金牛座 14 度。太阳必须运行 7 度才能使该相位成 相，而不是 4 度。

It is this 7 degrees that is important. 这 7 度才是关键。

So: ask yourself 所以，要问自己

* where does this aspect perfect? (from your ephemeris)
* 这个相位在何处形成完美相位？（从你的星历表中查找）

* how far does the applying planet have to travel to reach this point?
* 入相行星需要运行多远才能到达这一点？

We have now identified the number of degrees. This tells us how many time untis will elapse before the event. Now we must find which time unit is relevant. Is it hours, days, weeks, months or years? If you have read Lilly, you will have found that he brings nothing but confusion here. First, he gives two contradictory scales of timing; second, he pins both to fixed units. The suggestion that, for instance, angular houses = years is most unhelpful. If the question is ‘When will my boyfriend phone?’ years is not a relevant concept. Put Lilly away and listen up. 我们现在已经确定了度数。这告诉我们距离事件发生将要经过多少个时间单位。 现在我们必须找出哪个时间单位是相关的。是小时、天、周、月还是年？如果你 读过 Lilly 的著作，你会发现他在这里除了带来困惑，别无他物。首先，他给出 了两个相互矛盾的应期尺度；其次，他将两者都固定于特定的单位。例如，认为 角宫 = 年的建议就非常无益。如果问题是“我男朋友什么时候会打电话？”， 年就不是一个相关的概念。把 Lilly 的书放到一边，听我说。

Any question carries its own timeframe, which will usually have a short, a medium and a long possibility. For the love-struck teenager demanding ‘When will my boyfriend phone?’ minutes as short, hours as medium and days as long might be the options. For the older querent asking ‘When will I meet Mr Right?’ years must be the

longest option, giving months as medium and weeks as short. The three units will follow consecutively one from the other: we do not have minutes, months and years. 任何问题都自带其时间框架，这通常包含短期、中期和长期三种可能性。对于恋 爱中的青少年追问“我男朋友什么时候会打电话？”，短期可能是分钟，中期可 能是小时，长期可能是天。对于年长的问卜者询问“我什么时候会遇到真命天 子？”，长期必须是年，中期是月，短期是周。这三个单位是连续递进的：我们 不会同时用分钟、月和年。

“But this assumed timeframe limits the possibilities of what the chart can tell us.” No. We can have perfection in less than one degree, so our decision that years, months or weeks is the reasonable range of choice for ‘When will I meet Mr Right?’ does not clip Cupid’s wings. A perfection at less than one degree on our fastest option could still give us ‘This afternoon!’ “但是，这个假定的时间框架是否限制了星盘能告诉我们的可能性。”不。形成 完美相位可以发生在不到一度之内，所以我们决定对于“我什么时候会遇到真命 天子？”这个问题，年、月或周是合理的选择范围，这并不会束缚丘比特的翅膀。 在我们最快的选项上，如果成相小于一度，仍然可能告诉我们“今天下午！”

Yes, the choice of the right selection of time units (fast/middle/slow) is sometimes open to debate; but less often than you might think. Usually, it is obvious enough. In cases of doubt, remember that the maximum theoretical separation of an aspect is a little under 30 degrees (planet at 0 degrees of a sign perfects an aspect at 29 degrees of that sign). This gives a maximum of a little under 30 of any time-unit. For example, ‘hours’ might seem unlikely as a fastest unit if you are thinking only of a couple of hours; but think of a maximum of 29 hours – more than one day – and you see that it holds wider possibilities. 是的，选择正确的一组时间单位（快/中/慢）有时确实存在争议；但比你想的要 少。通常，这是足够明显的。在存疑的情况下，请记住，一个相位理论上最大的 分离度数略小于 30 度（行星在星座 0 度与同星座 29 度成相）。这给出了任何时 间单位的最大值略小于 30。例如，如果你只考虑几个小时，“小时”作为最快 单位似乎不太可能；但想想最大值 29 小时——超过一天——你就会看到它包含 了更广泛的可能性。

Once you have chosen the range of short, medium and long units, decide which of these is the appropriate one by considering the sign and the house in which the applying planet stands. Ignore the sign and house in which the planet applied to stands. We are concerned only with the applying planet. Only with the applying planet. Students resist this, and persist in factoring in the house and sign of the planet that is applied to. If you feel I am labouring this point, remember that I speak from long experience of teaching. Only, only, only! 一旦你选定了短期、中期和长期的单位范围，就通过考虑入相行星所在的星座和 宫位来决定其中哪一个是合适的。忽略被入相行星所在的星座和宫位。我们只关 心入相行星。只关心入相行星。学生们会抗拒这一点，并坚持把被入相行星的宫 位和星座也考虑进去。如果你觉得我在这一点上强调过度，请记住，我这是基于

长期的教学经验。切记，切记！！

Finding the applying planet in a fixed sign will give the longest time-unit, cardinal the shortest and mutable the middle from what we have decided is the reasonable timeframe for the question. 如果入相行星在固定星座将给予最长的时间单位，基本星座最短单位和变动星座 中等单位，这三者需结合问题本身合理的时间框架。

That is simple enough. It becomes more complicated when we introduce the houses, as there is an inbuilt contradiction. Of their nature, angular houses equate with fixed signs and so indicate the slowest time unit. Cadent – as might be expected from a houses that is literally ‘falling’ – gives the fastest; succedent the middle. Combining house and sign will give us, for instance, long + long, which must indicate our longest unit. Or short + short, which is our shortest. Any other combination will give our middle unit. 这相当简单。但当我们引入宫位时，情况就变得复杂了，因为存在一个内在的矛 盾。就其本质而言，角宫等同于固定星座，因此指示最慢的时间单位。果宫—— 正如其字面“下降”之意所预示的那样——给出最快的；续宫给出中间的。结合 宫位和星座，会给我们例如“长 + 长”的组合，这必然指示我们最长的单位。 或者“短 + 短”，指示我们最短的单位。任何其他组合都会给出我们中间的时 间单位。

Yes, the system is heavily weighted in favour of the middle unit. This probably says something about the nature of things; but if the chart wishes to show us the fastest or the slowest it is quite capable of so doing. 是的，这个系统严重偏向于中间的时间单位。这或许说明了事物的本质；但如果 星盘希望向我们显示最快或最慢的，它完全有能力做到。

Now for the contradiction: angular houses of their nature are slow. But a planet in an angular house has a good deal of accidental dignity. Accidental dignity increases the planet’s power to act. So if that planet wants to act, it is well able to do so, and is therefore likely to act quickly. So angular houses are fast. 现在来看这个矛盾点：角宫就其本质而言是缓慢的。但位于角宫的行星拥有相当 的偶然尊贵。偶然尊贵增加了行星行动的能力。因此，如果该行星想要行动，它 完全有能力做到，所以很可能行动迅速。那么，角宫又是快速的。

The key is the word ‘wants’: the issue of volition. If things are unfolding as a natural process, whatever is in an angular house will unfold slowly. If whatever or whomever the angular planet signifies is, within the context of the question, in a position to act, and if (and only if) the receptions indicate that it wants to act, it will act quickly. This inherent (apparent) contradiction is the reason for Lilly giving two apparently contradictory tables. 关键在于"想要"这个词：意愿的问题。如果事物是作为一个自然过程展开的，那 么位于角宫的任何事物都会缓慢展开。如果角宫行星所象征的事物或人，在问题

情境中，处于可以采取行动的位置，并且如果（且仅当）接纳关系表明它想要行 动，那么它就会迅速行动。这种内在的（表面上的）矛盾，就是 Lilly 给出两个 看似矛盾的表格的原因。

Example: I ask ‘When will the cheque arrive?’ and find the significator of the cheque in an angular house. There is nothing the cheque can do to expedite its own arrival. The question of volition is irrelevant. The angular house would suggest a slow time unit. 举例：我问“支票何时会到？”，并发现支票的征象星在角宫。支票本身无法做 任何事情来加速自己的到达。意愿的问题不相关。角宫将暗示一个缓慢的时间单 位。

On the other hand, when Indian women ask the question ‘When will I meet the man I will marry?’ it is common to find their significators in angular houses. Once they have taken the decision that it is time to marry, there is a good deal that they can do to expedite the process, in contrast to Bridget Jone, who can only wait until Cupid squeezes himself into her life. If these angular significators provide us with an applying aspect, and if (as the fact that she is paying to ask the question would lead us to expect) their receptions show that she wants the match, we can take this angularity as showing a fast unit, because she has power and wishes to use it. 另一方面，当印度女性问“我何时会遇到我将要嫁的人？”时，常常会发现她们 的征象星位于角宫。一旦她们决定是时候结婚了，她们可以做很多事情来加速这 个过程，这与 Bridget Jone（布里吉特·琼斯）不同，她只能等待丘比特挤进她 的生活。如果这些位于角宫的征象星为我们提供了一个入相位，并且如果（正如 她付钱问卜的事实会让我们预期的那样）它们的接纳关系表明她想要这段姻缘， 我们就可以将这种角宫特性视为显示一个快速的单位，因为她有力量并希望运用 它。

The reverse is also true. For things unfolding of themselves, like an apple falling from a tree, cadent houses show things happening quickly. But if volition is at issue the person signified by the cadent planet has little power to act, so candency will slow matters down. 反之亦然。对于自行展开的事物，比如苹果从树上落下，果宫显示事情发生得很 快。但如果涉及意愿，由果宫行星所象征的人行动能力很弱，因此果宫特性会使 事情进展缓慢。

Memorise this table: 请记住这个表格：

Shortest(最短) Medium(中等) Longest(最长) Sign(星座)： Cardinal(基本星座) Mutable(变动星座) Fixed(固定星座) House（宫位）： Candent(果宫) Succedent(继宫) Angular(角宫)

But: Volition can make angular fast and cadent slow

但是： 意愿可以使角宫变快，果宫变慢

Example: ‘When will I get a better job?’ Years must be our longest unit, so months will be medium and weeks fast. The querent’s planet in a succedent house and a cardinal sign applies to perfect the aspect in 6 degrees. Our answer will be ‘6 somethings’. Succedent is medium; cardinal is fast. This is not fast + fast, which would give our fastest unit (weeks); nor is it slow + slow, which would give our slowest (years); so it must be medium. You will get a better job in 6 months. 举例：“我什么时候能找到更好的工作？” 年必须是我们最长的单位，所以月 是中等，周是快速。问卜者的行星位于续宫和一个基本星座，入相将在 6 度后成 相。我们的答案将是“6 个某单位”。续宫是中等；基本星座是快速。这不是快
+ 快（这会给最快的单位：周）；也不是慢 + 慢（这会给最慢的单位：年）； 所以必须是中等。你将在 6 个月内找到更好的工作。

‘My flat is on the market. When will I sell it?’ Days, weeks or months would be reasonable. The buyer’s significator (Lord 7) applies to perfect the aspect in 5 degrees. It is in a fixed sign and an angular house. Slow + slow. This would give a timing of 5 months, our longest unit. BUT: remember about volition! It is angular, so the buyer has lots of power to act. Does he want to act? Check the receptions: ‘Oh good – the receptions show that he is eager to buy’. He is willing and able, so we can treat his angularity as fast. Fast (angular with volition) + slow (fixed) gives us a medium unit: 5 weeks. “我的公寓挂牌出售。我什么时候能卖掉？”天、周或月是合理的。买家征象星 （7 宫主）入相将在 5 度后成相。它位于一个固定星座和一个角宫。慢 + 慢。 这将给出一个 5 个月的应期，我们最长的单位。但是：记住关于意愿！它在角宫， 所以买家有很强的行动能力。他想行动吗？检查接纳关系：“噢，很好——接纳 关系显示他急于购买。”他既愿意也能够，因此我们可以将他的角宫特性视为快 速。快（有意愿的角宫） + 慢（固定星座）给我们一个中等单位：5 周。

Even with the variable nature of angular houses, this is really not so complicated. In the majority of charts, this is all you will need to give accurate timing. But not in all charts: there are variations. 即使角宫具有可变性，这其实并不那么复杂。在大多数星盘中，这就是给出准确 应期所需的全部。但并非所有星盘都如此：还存在一些变化。

Much as I emphasised that what concerns us is the distance the planet must travel to perfect the aspect, and much as this is usually true, there are some charts where we do treat the planet applied to as if it were standing still. I gave the example above: ‘The Sun at 10 Taurus applying to Mars at 14 Leo would typically perfect when the Sun is at about 17 Taurus, not 14 Taurus. The Sun has had to travel 7 degrees to perfect the aspect, not 4 . It is this 7 degrees that is important’. Sometimes, however, we would take the 4 degrees from the Sun to where Mars is now, ignoring the fact that Mars too is moving. This is done when: 尽管我非常强调我们关心的是行星形成完美相位必须运行的距离，并且这通常是

正确的，但有些星盘中，我们确实将被入相行星视为静止不动来处理。我在上面 给出了例子：“位于金牛座 10 度的太阳向位于狮子座 14 度的火星入相，通常会 在太阳运行到大约金牛座 17 度时成相，而不是金牛座 14 度。太阳必须运行 7 度才能使该相位成相，而不是 4 度。这 7 度才是关键。”然而，有时我们会取从 太阳到火星当前位置的 4 度，忽略火星也在移动的事实。这样做的情况是：

* regarding the second planet as moving would give a timing that is not possible within the reality of the question *认为第二颗行星正在移动会给出一个在该问题现实中不可能发生的应期

* we have two testimonies of timing in the chart, and treating the planet applied to in this aspect as if it were standing still brings these testimonies into agreement (i.e. both showing the same timing). *星盘中有两个应期的征象，而将此相位中的被入相行星视为静止不动能使这两 个征象达成一致（即显示相同的应期）。

In some charts, we consider only the sign of the applying planet, not its house. “Which charts?” The charts where we consider only the sign of the applying planet, not its house. I would like to be able to quote a rule, but have never found one. They just look like ‘sign – only charts’. Given enough practice, you will develop an eye for them. It may be that a preponderance of them have the planet in a fixed sign, and so give the longest time unit. That, at least, is my impression; but treat this suggestion with caution. See the chart on page 122 for an example. 在某些星盘中，我们只考虑入相行星的星座，而不考虑其宫位。“哪些星盘？” 就是那些我们只考虑入相行星的星座而不考虑其宫位的星盘。我希望我能引述一 条规则，但从未找到过。它们看起来就像是“只看星座的星盘”。经过足够的练 习，你将培养出识别它们的眼力。可能这类星盘中行星较多位于固定星座，因此 给出最长的时间单位。至少，这是我的印象；但请谨慎对待这个建议。参见第 207 页的星盘示例。

So far we have taken number of degrees = number of time units. This is usually accurate enough. For added precision, we can adjust this number. If the applying planet is moving significantly faster or slower than its usual speed, it will take a greater or lesser time to cover the same number of degrees. We can, if we wish, adjust the number of units up or down accordingly. Don’t be too precious here: the planet needs to be significantly faster or slower than usual for this to be worth considering. A couple of minutes of arc per day is a great deal for Jupiter; it is inconsequential for the Moon. 到目前为止，我们采用度数 = 时间单位数。这通常足够准确。为了更加精确， 我们可以调整这个数字。如果入相行星的运行速度明显快于或慢于其通常速度， 那么它覆盖相同度数所需的时间就会更多或更少。如果我们愿意，可以相应地向 上或向下调整单位数量。此处不必过于斤斤计较：只有当行星速度明显快于或慢 于通常时，才值得考虑这一点。对木星而言，每天差几分钟弧已经是很大的差异； 对月亮来说则微不足道。

I have timed predictions with an unnecessary degree of accuracy by carefully calculating the exact proportion by which the planet is faster or slower than average; but there is little point to this. ‘A bit’ is quite accurate enough an adjustment. Striving to tell our client that she will meet Mr Right at 3 minutes past 10 on Monday 28th serves only our ego. ‘Around the end of the month’ is all the accuracy required. Use your common sense: if the event will happen later this week, it is reasonable that we should predict the day; if it will happen in twenty years’ time, selecting the year is quite accurate enough. Do resist the impulse to show off. If you predict, ‘You will marry on August 17th in 3 year’s time,’ and she marries on August 18th, you will be the astrologer who got it wrong. 我曾通过仔细计算行星比平均速度快或慢的确切比例，将预测的应期精确到不必 要的程度；但这几乎没有意义。“稍微”调整一下就已经足够准确了。努力告诉 客户她将在“28 号星期一 10 点过 3 分”遇到真命天子，只是为了满足我们的自 我。“大约月底”就是所需的全部精度。运用你的常识：如果事件将在本周晚些 时候发生，我们预测到哪一天是合理的；如果将在二十年后发生，能确定到哪一 年就已经足够精确了。一定要克制炫耀的冲动。如果你预测"你将在 3 年后的 8 月 17 日结婚"，而她在 8 月 18 日结婚，你就会是那个预测错了的占星师。

NB: if the applying planet is moving faster or slower than usual, this will affect only the number of time units; it will not affect our choice of what time units they are. If we have worked out the timing to be 6 weeks, adjusting this by planetary speed might make it 5 weeks or 7weeks; it will not make it 6 days or 6 months. 注意：如果入相行星比平时运行得快或慢，这只影响时间单位的数量；不影响我 们对这些单位是什么（小时、天、周等）的选择。如果我们计算出应期是 6 周， 根据行星速度调整可能使其变为 5 周或 7 周；但不会变成 6 天或 6 个月。

Double-bodied signs make things slower. This too will affect only the number of time units, not their nature. ‘A bit’ slower is as accurate as we can or need be. In practice, it is not usually necessary to consider these factors, work though they do. 双体星座会使事情变慢。这也只影响时间单位的数量，而不影响其性质。变慢“一 点点”是我们能做到或需要的精确度。在实践中，通常没有必要考虑这些因素， 尽管它们确实起作用。

If the aspect is to a retrograde planet, so that both planets are applying to perfection, the event can happen faster than the number of degrees would suggest. How much faster? Again, ‘a bit’. In such cases it is probably best to use the number of degrees to give an outer limit of time, qualified by ‘probably sooner’. 如果相位是与一颗逆行行星形成的，以致两颗行星都在向形成完美相位移动，那 么事件可能比度数所暗示的发生得更快。快多少？同样，“一点点”。在这种情 况下，最好用度数来给出一个应期的外部上限，并加上“可能更快”的限定。

If the chart shows two aspects indicating that the event will happen, these aspects will usually, as we might expect, show the same time. ‘Close enough’ is good enough. If

one shows 12 units and the other shows 3, a correlation of 12 weeks = 3 months is sufficiently close to add confidence to our prediction. 如果星盘显示有两个指示事件将发生的相位，通常如我们所料，它们会显示相同 的时间。“足够接近”就已经够好了。如果一个显示 12 个单位，另一个显示 3 个，那么 12 周 = 3 个月的对应关系就足够接近，可以增加我们预测的信心。

Disregard real time. It is a common error among students, no matter how hard they are beaten, to cling to the idea that if the ephemeris shows that the aspect will happen next Tuesday, the event shown by that aspect will happen next Tuesday. It won’t! What the ephemeris shows us is time from our perception, which is an illusion; what the planets show us is as close an approximation as we may easily get to what time truly is. Work from the symbolic methods of timing, as discussed above. 请忽略真实时间。 这是一个学生中常见的错误，无论他们被教训得多狠，都执 着于一种想法：如果星历表显示相位将在下周二发生，那么该相位所显示的事件 就会在下周二发生。不会的！星历表向我们展示的是我们感知中的时间，那是一 种幻象；而行星向我们展示的，则是我们能够轻松获得的、最接近真实时间本质 的近似值。请运用前面讨论过的象征性应期方法来工作。

When ephemeris time does become relevant is when our questions are on general indications over long periods of time, or when we wish to look beyond the immediate limits imposed by the question to see what may happen over a longer period. This is often to reassure the querent that all is not lost. 星历表时间变得相关的情况是：当我们的问题涉及长期的总体征象时，或者当我 们希望超越问题所设定的即时限制，去观察更长时间内可能发生的事情时。这通 常是为了让问卜者放心，一切并未失去。

Example: suppose the question is ‘Can you give some general indications for my business over the next few months?’ and we find that the querent’s business is signified by Jupiter, which will enter its own sign in three months’ time. We might judge that things will start looking up around then. My experience is that the querent will usually respond, ‘Oh yes – that’s immediately after the big trade show,’ or some such, and that such indications will prove accurate. 举例：假设问题是"您能对我未来几个月的生意给出一些总体指示吗？"，我们发 现问卜者的生意以木星为征象星，而木星将在三个月后进入自己的星座。我们可 能会判断，届时情况将开始好转。我的经验是，问卜者通常会回应：“噢，是的 ——那正好是在大型贸易展之后，”或类似的话，并且这些指示往往会被证明是 准确的。

Or, suppose the question were ‘Is this really the man of my dreams?’ and the chart gives an obvious judgement of ‘Are you mad?’ We might look further, noting that in a couple of months the querent’s significator moves out of its detriment and into some interesting mutual receptions, and so add ‘Buy by the autumn you’ll be feeling much better in yourself, and so be able to enter a relationship that nurtures you, rather than grabbing someone unsuitable out of desperation, as you are doing now’. Or words to

that effect. 或者，假设问题是“这真的是我的梦中情人吗？”，而星盘给出了一个明显的“你 疯了吗？”的判断。我们或许可以看得更远，注意到几个月后问卜者的征象星将 走出其落陷位置并进入一些有趣的互溶关系，从而补充道：“但到秋天时，你自 我感觉会好很多，因此能够开始一段滋养你的关系，而不是像现在这样出于绝望 而抓住一个不合适的人。”或类似意思的话。

When considering the longer term, a planet’s passage through an entire sign shows one of the natural time-units, usually a month or a year. So if, for instance, the querent’s business were signified by Venus, placed at 28 Leo, in a question about long-term prospects, we might judge (other testimonies concurring), ‘You may feel you have the world at your feet now (Venus on Regulus), but you are entering a sticky period(into Virgo). The next year (passage through Virgo) looks set to be a story of considerable potentials (Venus in triplicity) never quite unfolding (Venus in fall). Overall, the downside during this period is going to be significantly more than the up; but after that (Venus into Libra) all falls happily into place. So grit your teeth and hang on in till then’Don’t look beyond the next sign or two; if we do that we find everything happening to everybody. 在考虑长期前景时，一颗行星穿过整个星座的旅程，显示了自然时间单位之一， 通常是一个月或一年。因此，举例来说，如果问卜者的生意以金星为征象星，落 在狮子座 28 度，在一个关于长期前景的问题中，我们可能会判断（在其他征象 一致的情况下）：“你可能觉得现在世界就在你脚下（金星位于轩辕十四），但 你正进入一个胶着期（进入处女座）。接下来的一年（穿过处女座）看起来将是 充满巨大潜力（金星在其三分位置）却从未完全展开（金星在弱势）的故事。总 体而言，这段时期的低谷将显著多于高峰；但之后（金星进入天秤座）一切都会 顺理成章地好起来。所以咬紧牙关，坚持到那时。”不要看超过接下来一两个 星座；如果我们那样做，就会发现所有事情都会发生在所有人身上。

33. The medical chart on p.128 of RA Applied shows an example of this.
33. 《RA Applied》第 128 页的医疗占星案例为此提供了一个例子。

This looking ahead must be done sparingly. Those new to horary are often tempted to race planets around the chart as if it were a Snakes and Ladders board; this impulse is better curbed. In all but a few charts, we are concerned only with a planet’s next aspect and nothing beyond that. 这种前瞻性观察必须慎用。卜卦占星的新手常常忍不住像玩“蛇梯棋”一样在星 盘上快速推进行星；这种冲动最好加以克制。除了极少数星盘外，我们只关心行 星的下一个相位，除此之外概不考虑。

Lilly gives several examples where a ‘real time’ transit is significant. So if Mercury applies to Jupiter he judges not ‘It’s four degrees till perfection: it will happen in for weeks’, but ‘My ephemeris shows this aspect happening next Tuesday at 3.56: it will happen then’.Don’t try this at home! Please. Lilly 举了几个例子，其中“真实时间”的行运是重要的。所以，如果水星向木

星入相，他的判断不是“还需 4 度成相：将在 4 周内发生”，而是“我的星历表 显示此相位在下周二 3 点 56 分发生：那时就会发生”。请勿在家尝试！拜托。

34. See Lilly pp. 385-8 for an example.

If you really must dabble in this kind of thing, it is best kept to side issues. Example: we have decided that our querent will marry his girlfriend in six months’ time, judging from the six degrees needed to perfect the aspect between them. We note that both planet are in major dignities of the ruler of her fourth house, showing that her father has a major say in this matter. We note also that at 11.52 on Firday 28th, our querent’s planet transits the twelfth cusp, there being a mutual rectption between the ruler of the twelfth and the significator of the girl’s father. The twelfth being the house of animals larger than goats, we advise that at 11.52 on the 28th he attend the market, where he will be able to purchase the very camel that will persuade the father to allow his daughter to wed. 如果你真的必须涉足这类（真实时间）方法，最好将其限于次要事项。举例：我 们已判断问卜者将在六个月内与女友结婚，这是根据他们之间形成完美相位所需 的六度得出的。我们注意到两颗行星都位于她 4 宫主的主要尊贵位置，这表明她 父亲对此事有重要发言权。我们还注意到，在 28 日周五 11 点 52 分，问卜者的 行星将行运至 12 宫头，而 12 宫主与女孩父亲的征象星存在互溶关系。12 宫是 代表大于山羊的动物之宫，我们建议他在 28 日 11 点 52 分去市场，在那里他将 能买到那匹能说服父亲允许女儿出嫁的骆驼。

On the subject of transits, let us deal with the idea that if something in the horary chart conjuncts something in the querent’s nativity, the chart is ‘radical’ or somehow more real. I ask a question about love, and find in the horary that Venus is right on my natal Ascendant. Does this make the chart ‘radical’? Of course not. It shows that Venus is transiting my Ascendant, and I, not surprisingly, am thinking about love. No more than that. Let us not forget that this with which we deal is a congruent system: it all fits together, in the most intricate and endlessly remarkable of ways. That Venus is on my Ascendant may show that I am thinking about love – a fact that might be obvious from my going to an astrologer and asking ‘Does she love me?’ – but it tells us nothing about whether this love is reciprocated. These considerations serve only to confuse the issue. All charts are ‘radical’, and we are well advised to keep the querent’s nativity well apart from his horaries, lest they breed monsters. 关于行运这个话题，让我们处理一种观点，即如果卜卦盘中的某个点与问卜者本 命盘的某个点形成合相，那么这个星盘就是“基准”的或某种程度上更真实。我 问了一个关于爱情的问题，并在卜卦盘中发现金星正好在我本命盘的上升点上。 这是否使星盘成为“基准”？当然不是。这表明金星正在行运经过我的上升点， 而我，毫不奇怪，正在思考爱情。仅此而已。我们不要忘记，我们打交道的这个 体系是协调一致的：它以最错综复杂且无比奇妙的方式契合在一起。金星在我的 上升点上可能表明我正在思考爱情——这一事实从我找占星师并询问“她爱我 吗？”来看可能显而易见——但它并没有告诉我们这份爱是否得到了回应。这些 考量只会混淆问题。所有星盘都是“基准”的，我们最好将问卜者的本命盘与其

卜卦盘严格分开，以免它们滋生谬误。

A particular instance in which the ‘real time’ movement of the planets can be significant occurs in lost object questions. In the chart for such it will often be found that the significator of the object is combust: the object cannot be seen. Assuming that all else in the chart is indicative of a recovery, we can reach down our ephemeris, note the exact moment at which the planet leaves combustion, and judge, ‘You’ll find it then’. This may present the odd picture of thousands of people around the world throwing up their hands in glee as they recover cherished possessions at exactly 8.22 GMT, but it seems to work with the reasonable degree of reliability that is all we ask. 行星“真实时间”运动可能具有重要性的一个具体例子出现在失物问题中。在此 类星盘中，常常发现物体的征象星处于燃烧状态：物体无法被看见。假设星盘中 所有其他征象都指示可以找回，我们可以查阅星历表，记下行星离开燃烧状态的 精确时刻，并判断“你那时会找到它”。这可能会呈现出一种奇特的景象：全世 界成千上万的人在格林威治标准时间 8 点 22 分整欣喜地举手欢呼，因为他们找 回了珍爱的物品，但这似乎能以我们所要求的合理可靠程度有效。

When a date is specifically mentioned in the question, it is often of significance, so it is worth checking the planetary placements on that date against the horary chart. As a general rule, if we restrict the querent to few words, whatever those few words are will usually be important; if those few words relate to timing, let us look at them. 当问题中明确提到一个日期时，它通常具有重要意义，因此值得将该日期的行星 位置与卜卦盘进行比对。一般而言，如果我们限制问卜者用尽可能少的词语描述， 那么这少量的词语通常会是重要的；如果这些少量词语与应期有关，让我们仔细 审视它们。

A querent was desperate for her son to be accepted into a school, which prospect was looking increasingly unlikely. Her ambitions to place him in a private school had excluded him from the acceptable state school options, while he had been turned down from the private school she wanted, for reasons which she believed were unsound. The boy had an entrance exam at another school, and an appeal at the school desired, both on named dates. How would he fare? 一位问卜者非常希望她的儿子能被一所学校录取，而这个前景看起来越来越渺茫。 她将他送入私立学校的雄心使他错失了合适的公立学校选择，同时他已被她心仪 的私立学校拒绝，理由她认为站不住脚。这个男孩在另一所学校有一场入学考试， 并在期望的学校有一次申诉，两者都有指定的日期。他会表现如何？

His significator, Lord 5, was Jupiter. The schools were shown by the ninth house and its ruler, the Moon. The exam was on the 18th of May. By transit, the Moon, Lord 9, was on the 5th cusp of the horary chart on that day. This is a positive testimony, but there was no mutual reception with Lord 5. At this school the boy passed satisfactorily, but with no scholarship. The appeal at the second school was due on August 10th. On that day, the boy’s significator, Jupiter, transited the 9th cusp, where, it being in Cancer, it was exalted – so the boy is there and is highly thought of. Will he get the

scholarship? Yes. And so it proved. 他的征象星，5 宫主，是木星。学校由 9 宫及其守护星月亮显示。考试在 5 月 18 日。根据行运，那天月亮（9 宫主）正位于卜卦盘的 5 宫头。这是一个积极的征 象，但与 5 宫主没有互溶关系。在这所学校，男孩顺利通过，但没有获得奖学金。 第二次学校的申诉定在 8 月 10 日。在那一天，男孩的征象星木星将行运至 9 宫 头，在那里，由于它在巨蟹座，它处于旺势——所以男孩身在那里且备受好评。 他会获得奖学金吗？会的。事实也证明了这一点。

Similarly, if the question contains a given bound of time, this too will be reflected in the chart. It can be taken that the end of the relevant planet’s present sign is the end of the given timeframe. If I ask, ‘Will I win the lottery this year?’ and find my significator conjuncting the ruler of the 11th house (pennies from Heaven) immediately after it leaves its present sign, I would judge, ‘No; but I will early next’. 同样，如果问题包含一个给定的时间范围，这也会在星盘中反映出来。可以认为 相关行星当前所在星座的结束就是给定时间范围的结束。如果我问“我今年会中 彩票吗？”，并发现我的征象星在离开其当前星座后立即与 11 宫主（来自天堂 的便士）合相，我会判断：“不会；但明年年初会”。

Finally, there are those welcome questions that admit of only one possible time unit. ‘When will such and such happen today?’ is the most common of these. ‘Minutes’ is usually not an option, because we know the event cannot happen within 29 minutes. ‘Days’ is impossible, because we are concerned only with today. ‘Hours’ is our only option. Yippee! 最后，还有一些令人欣慰的问题只允许一种可能的时间单位。“这件事今天什么 时候会发生？”是这类问题中最常见的。“分钟”通常不是选项，因为我们知道 事件不可能在 29 分钟内发生。“天”是不可能的，因为我们只关心今天。“小 时”是我们唯一的选择。太好了！

The golden rule in matters of timing, as in all else in astrology, is that we do not have to be perfect. We are allowed to judge, ‘It might be in three days; but weighting all the evidence I think it more likely to be in six’. 关于应期判断的黄金法则，正如占星学中其他所有方面一样，是我们不必完美。 我们可以判断：“可能在三天内；但权衡所有证据后，我认为更可能在六天内”。

### ✸A couple of points made above were not emphasised strongly enough. First, if

volition is important in calculating timing, remember that inanimate objects do not have volition. No matter which house its significator is in or what its receptions might suggest, there is nothing a letter can do to speed up its own arrival. Second, we cannot assume volition from the question having been asked. It might seem obvious that if the querent asks ‘When will I marry?’ she wants to marry, but this is not so. It is not unusual for the response, after looking at the chart, to be, ‘You don’t really want to marry, do you?’ ‘No, not really.’ We must establish volition from the evidence in the chart, not from our own assumptions.✷

### ✸上面提到的几点没有得到足够强烈的强调。第一，如果意愿在计算应期时很

重要，请记住无生命的物体没有意愿。无论其征象星在哪个宫位或其接纳关系可 能暗示什么，一封信件本身无法做任何事来加快自己的到达。第二，我们不能因 为问题被提出就假定存在意愿。如果问卜者问“我什么时候会结婚？”，她似乎 显然想结婚，但事实并非总是如此。在查看星盘后得到的回应“你并不是真的想 结婚，是吗？”——“不，不是真的。”这种情况并不罕见。我们必须根据星盘 中的证据来确定意愿，而不是我们自己的假设。✷

### ✸ On the rare occasions when the planet whose movement shows the timing is

moving in more than one sign or house, always use the time-unit shown by the sign and house that the planet is in now. Don’t try modulating this, thinking, for instance, ‘That’s 6 units at the longest timing, then 4 at the middle timing’. 在极少数情况下，显示应期的行星运动跨越了不止一个星座或宫位，请始终使用 该行星当前所在星座和宫位所显示的时间单位。不要试图调整，比如想当然的“那 是最长应期的 6 个单位，然后是中等应期的 4 个单位”。

Stick to real units of time, such as hours, days and weeks. You would never say ‘I’ll do it in 3 fortnights’. Nor does the chart. 坚持使用真实的时间单位，如小时、天和周。你永远不会说“我将在 3 个双周内 完成”。星盘也不会。

Timing is not always shown in so many days, months or years. It is often shown as ‘after such and such happens’. This is completely acceptable. ‘When will I find a new man?’ ‘When you stop obsessing about the last one.’ ‘When will I get a better job?’ ‘When you get some qualifications.’ ✷ 应期并非总是以多少天、多少月或多少年来显示。它常常显示为“在某某事情发 生之后”。这是完全可以接受的。“我什么时候会找到新男人？”“当你不再沉 迷于上一个的时候。”“我什么时候会找到更好的工作？”“当你获得一些资格 的时候。”✷

# What is the Question and

# Who is Asking It?

# 问题是什么以及谁在提问？

Perhaps the most important part of horary judgement is done before we even cast the chart. This is the determining of what question is really being asked. 或许在卜卦判断中，最重要的部分甚至在我们绘制星盘之前就已经完成了。即确 定问题真正所指为何。

Questions often come swathed in clouds of irrelevant detail. There is a skill in cutting through these swathes to reach the bones of the issue. You have probably had the experience while watching a film of suddenly realizing, ‘Hey - this is Romeo and Juliet, dressed up!’ or ‘This is Snow White set in modern New York!’ You have noticed that beneath its disguise the bones of the plot are those of Romeo and Juliet or Snow White. So it is with horary: there are certain standard questions which recur again and again in different guises. 问题常常包裹在大量无关细节的迷雾之中。要掌握一种技巧，即穿透这些层层迷 雾，触及问题的核心。你可能曾有过这样的观影体验：突然意识到，“嘿——这 不过是穿了新衣的《Romeo 与 Juliet》！”或者“这是设定在现代纽约的《白雪 公主》！”你已经注意到，在它的伪装之下，故事的核心骨架依然是《Romeo 与 Juliet》或《白雪公主》。卜卦也是如此：存在某些标准问题，它们以不同的 伪装反复出现。

* Does she love me?
* 她爱我吗？

* Will I get the job?
* 我能得到那份工作吗？

* Will I win?
* 我会赢吗？

* Am I bewitched?
* 我被施咒了吗？

* Will the king be deposed?
* 国王会被废黜吗？

* Will I get the gift from the king?
* 我能得到国王的礼物吗？

* Can we do the deal?
* 我们能做成这笔交易吗？

Keep your ears open and you will quickly recognize them when you hear them. Allow yourself to be sidetracked by irrelevant details and you will end up answering a question that has not been asked. 保持耳聪目明，当你听到时，就能迅速认出它们。如果让自己被无关的细节带偏， 你最终回答的将是一个未被提出的问题。

Similarly, the fact of who is asking the question is not always as clear as it might seem. There are direct questions posed by the person concerned. There are direct questions asked by someone about somebody else. So far so simple. 同样，“谁在提问” 这个事实也并非总是看起来那样清晰明了。有些是当事人 自己提出的直接问题。有些是某人就他人之事提出的直接问题。这还比较简单。

Then there are questions asked by someone acting as mouthpiece for someone else. Suppose Erika wishes to ask me a question, but we do not have a common language. She has a friend who speaks English, so she asks the friend to ask the question on her behalf. The friend is not asking her own question about Erika; she is relaying Erika’s question to me. I must ignore the friend, treating this exactly as if Erika herself were asking me, so Erika will be given the 1sht house as querent. 此外，还有代他人提问的情况。假设 Erika（埃里卡）想问我一个问题，但我们 没有共同语言。她有一位会说英语的朋友，于是她请这位朋友代她提问。这位朋 友并非在问她自己关于 Erika 的问题；她是在向我转达 Erika 的问题。我必须忽 略这位朋友，完全将其视为埃里卡本人在向我提问，因此 Erika 将被赋予 1 宫作 为问卜者。

Be clear on the distinction: 请明确区分：

* the friend asks her own question, ‘Is my friend Erika going to marry Rudolph?’
* 朋友问自己的问题：“我的朋友 Erika 会嫁给 Rudolph（鲁道夫）吗？”

* the friend relays Erika’s own question, ‘Will I marry Rudolph?’
* 朋友转述 Erika 自己的问题：“我会嫁给 Rudolph 吗？”

In the first example, Erika would be given the 11th house; in the second, she would be given the 1st.

在第一个例子中，Erika 对应 11 宫；在第二个例子中，她对应 1 宫。

Then there are questions that arise in conversation, it being unclear who is really asking. I am chatting with my friend about his work prospects. The question comes up, ‘When will I get a better job?’ But who is really asking it? Is it my friend, is it me, or is my friend articulating the question that I am forcing into his mouth? Be wary of such situations, especially when you are eagerly pressing everyone you know for horaries so you can practice your skills. This is one advantage of professional practice: the fee changing hands makes it quite clear who is the querent. 还有一种情况是问题在交谈中产生，难以确定真正是谁在提问。我正在和朋友闲 聊他的工作前景。问题产生了：“我什么时候能找到更好的工作？”但究竟是谁 在提问？是我的朋友，是我自己，还是我的朋友在替我说出我强加给他的问题？ 要警惕此类情况，尤其是当你热切地催促你认识的每个人给你卜卦案例，以便练 习你的技能时。这也是专业实践的一个优势：费用的交换使得谁是问卜者变得非 常明确。

### ✸When dealing with question from friends and family there is a risk of having too

much information. The more you think you know about the situation, the harder it can be to see past these preconceptions in order to judge the chart objectively. This risk is even greater with one’s own questions: when judging the chart on an issue you have been talking over in your head for weeks, seeing anything other than the script you have so thoroughly rehearsed demands levels of objectivity that few of us possess.✷

### ✸在处理来自朋友和家人的问题时，存在信息过多的风险。你自认为对情况了

解得越多，就越难以超越这些先入之见，从而客观地判断星盘。这种风险在判断 自己的问题时甚至更大：当你对盘判断一个已在脑海中反复思量数周的问题时， 想要看到的不是你精心排练过的剧本，而是其他可能性，这需要一种我们大多数 人都难以具备的客观性。✷

There are those who would rigorously limit the scope of horary enquiry. ‘You can’t ask that: it’s too trivial’. ‘You can’t ask that: it’s too important.’ Between what is trivial and what is important, precious little survives. 有些人会严格限制卜卦询问的范围。“你不能问那个：它太琐碎了。”“你不能 问那个：它太重要了。”然而，在琐碎与重要之间，能被允许的所剩无几。

With a very few small restrictions, you can ask anything. Trivial? So who am I to tell you that your concerns are trivial, and apply a cosmic veto to them? Maybe in the great scheme of things ‘Who will be president?’ is of more moment than ‘Where is the cat?’ but in fact it is my bystander’s curiosity in the former of these that is trivial; the whereabouts of Puss most certainly is not. Compared to the rise and fall of empires, our grandest concerns are as nothing – and yet salvation is gained or lost in an instant, so the matter of any instant cannot be trival. 除了极少数的小限制外，你可以询问任何事情。琐碎？那么，我凭什么断定你关

心的事是琐碎的，并代表宇宙加以否决？也许在宏大的格局中，“谁会成为总统？” 确实比“猫在哪里？”更重要，但事实上，我对前者的旁观者式好奇才是琐碎的； 而猫咪的下落则绝非如此。与帝国的兴衰相比，我们最重大的关切也微不足道— —然而，救赎往往在一瞬间得失，因此任何瞬间之事都不能被视作琐碎。

It is claimed that we cannot ask ‘importan’ questions, such as ‘Who will win the election?’ because so many people are asking this same question and the same question cannot be asked more than once. Let us consider this statement, ‘The same question cannot be asked more than once’. 有人认为我们不能询问“重要”的问题，例如“谁会赢得选举？”，因为太多人 在问同一个问题，而同一个问题不能被问一次以上。让我们来思考一下“同一个 问题不能被问一次以上”这个说法。

It is true; but it is not true in the way in which it is meant. Fundamental to astrology is the fact that every instant is different. THIS instant is different from THIS instant. Each is different, and whatever happens in it will be distinct to that instant. Take this away and we have no astrology. So it is not undesirable to ask the same question twice – it is impossible. Even if the question has the same words, it is not the same question. 这是事实；但其真实含义并非如字面所示。占星学的基本法则是：每个瞬间都是 不同的。这个瞬间不同于那个瞬间。每一个瞬间都不同，其中发生的任何事都将 是该瞬间所独有的。如果否定这一点，我们就没有占星学了。所以，并非“不应 该”两次问同一个问题——而是“不可能”。即使问题的字面相同，它也不是同 一个问题。

Nor is there any reason why someone should not ask the same question of more than one astrologer. Doctors can give second opinions; so can astrologers. Truth is a sturdy beast; it does not run away if more than one person looks at it. Each separate question on the same subject is like a cross-section of the same situation, as a zoologist might take cross-sections of a worm to put under the microscope. Different cross-sections, but still the same worm, so still the same answer. If fifty or five hundred people ask ‘Who will win the next election?’ the cosmos, which is an infinitely subtle mechanism, will find fifty or five hundred ways of showing the same answer. No matter how many people examine individual stills from Gone with the Wind, Rhett Butler always leaves at the end of the story. 同样，也没有理由禁止某人向多于一位占星师询问同一个问题。医生可以提供第 二意见；占星师也可以。真相是坚固的野兽；不会因为多一个人审视它就逃走。 关于同一主题的每个独立问题，就像对同一情况的一个横截面，正如动物学家可 能对一条蠕虫进行多个横切面以置于显微镜下观察。不同的横截面，但仍是同一 条蠕虫，因此答案也仍然相同。如果有五十或五百个人问“谁将赢得下次选举？”， 宇宙这个无限精妙的机制，会找到五十或五百种方式来展现同一个答案。无论多 少人审视《乱世佳人》，Rhett Butler（瑞德·巴特勒）总会在故事结尾离开。.

A querent will ask what is apparently the same question at different stages of a

situation. Common is ‘Should I throw him out?’ followed by ‘Should I really throw him out?’ and ‘Will I be OK if I throw him out?’ These consequent charts can be seen to relate to each other in exactly the same ways as birthcharts of family members relate to each other. The same patterns occur, and usually, in question after question, the querent edge towards a position from which she feels able to make a decision one way or the other. 一个问卜者可能会在情况的不同阶段提出表面上相同的问题。常见的是“我该把 他赶出去吗？”，接着是“我真的该把他赶出去吗？”，然后是“如果把他赶出 去，我会好吗？”。这些连续星盘间的关联，恰似家庭成员本命盘之间的相互呼 应。相同的模式会反复出现，而且通常，在一个接一个的问题中，问询者会逐渐 接近能做出决断的立场。

Other querents will ask similar questions about different situations. ‘Will I get a job from this audition?’ The first few of these will have clear results. After a while, however, the charts become more and more vapid, almost as if the cosmos is losing interest in the situation and saying, ‘If you haven’t taken the hint by now, I’m not going to keep performing for you’. Typically, these charts will start showing minor events that are going to occur on that day (‘Oh look, your father’s coming to visit you’) but say little of significance about the job situation. It is possible that this reflects either querent or astrologer losing interest in the repeated questions, or the nature of the true question changing as the querent despairs of having a successful audition. In the latter case, the querent is not so much asking for information as hoping that the consultation will work magic. It will not. 另一些问卜者会对不同情境提出类似的问题。“我能从这次试镜得到工作吗？” 起初的几个问题会有明确的结果。然而，过一段时间后，星盘会变得越来越空洞， 几乎就像宇宙对这个情况失去了兴趣，并说：“如果你到现在还没领会到暗示， 我就不再为你表演了。”通常，这些星盘会开始显示那天将发生的次要事件（“哦， 看，你父亲要来看你”），但对工作状况却言之甚少。这可能反映了问卜者或占 星师对重复性问题失去了兴趣，或者，随着问卜者对试镜成功感到绝望，真正问 题的性质发生了变化。在后一种情况下，问卜者与其说是在寻求信息，不如说是 希望这次咨询能施展魔法。这不会发生。

Questions like this verge on the mechanical, and the mechanical is one real limit to what can be asked. There must be some spark of genuine interest in the question, even if the question is a ‘trivial’ one and hardly of life-changing significance. There is no such spark of genuine interest in, for instance, ‘Will I come up on this week’s lottery?’ ‘Will 2 come up on this week’s lottery?’ etc. 这类问题近乎机械重复，而“机械性”是真正能提问的范围限制之一。问题中必 须存在一丝真正的兴趣火花，即使是一个“琐碎”的、几乎无关人生改变的问题。 而对于例如“我这周彩票会中奖吗？”、“2 这个数字会在这周彩票中出现吗？” 等等，则不存在这种真正的兴趣火花。

Then there are such products of the fourth-form as ‘Is horary true?’ and ‘Is the Bible the word of God?’ A moment’s reflection should make clear why these cannot be

asked. 此外，还存在一些类似“学生式提问” 的产物，例如：“卜卦占星是真的吗？” 以及“《圣经》是上帝的话语吗？”片刻的思考就应该能明白为何这些问题无法 被回答。

Supplementary questions are fine. ‘When will I marry? Will we have children? Will he get along with my family? Will he have a good job?’ These can all be judged from the same chart. But it is best to discourage questions on different issues: ‘When will I marry? When will I get a better job? Where is the cat?’ Sometimes querents will have two or three issues weighing on them, so if necessary these questions can be answered from the same chart. But the asking of many unrelated questions suggests that none of them is the real issue. It is better to ask the querent to reflect on what is most important and then ask that. 补充性问题是没问题的。“我何时会结婚？我们会有孩子吗？他能与我的家人相 处融洽吗？他会有一份好工作吗？”这些都可以从同一张星盘中进行判断。但最 好避免在同一张盘中询问不同主题的问题：“我何时会结婚？我何时能找到更好 的工作？猫在哪里？”有时问卜者可能有两三件心事压着，所以如有必要，可以 从同一张盘中回答这些问题。但提出许多不相关的问题，往往暗示着其中没有一 个触及真正的核心。更好的做法是请问卜者反思什么是最重要的事情，然后就此 提问。

### ✸Be wary of questions that ask not for information but for some kind of celestial

permission to do whatever the querent wants to do. These are particularly common in troubled relationships, as the querent longs to hear ‘Yes, the stars confirm it: he really is horrible and you should kick him out’. A question, for instance, such as ‘Should I divorce him?’ has everyting to do with personal morality and nothing to do with anything that can be found in an astrological chart. I do not see that the giving of celestial permission is part of the astrologer’s job, and would suggest that it is more useful to encourage the querent to rephrase a permission question as one that allows an objective answer, such as ‘Why is it going wrong?’ ‘Can it get better?’ or ‘Can I do something to mend this?’✷

### ✸要警惕那些并非寻求信息，而是寻求某种宇宙许可来做问卜者想做的任何事

的问题。这在陷入困境的关系中尤为常见，因为问卜者渴望听到：“是的，星辰 证实了：他真的很糟糕，你应该把他踢出去。”例如，“我应该和他离婚吗？” 这样的问题，完全关乎个人道德，而与星盘中可能发现的任何信息无关。我不认 为给予宇宙许可是占星师工作的一部分，并且建议，更有益的做法是鼓励问卜者 将这种许可式问题重新表述为能够获得客观答案的问题，例如：“问题出在哪里？” “情况能好转吗？”或者“我能做些什么来修复这段关系？”✷

The default option

默认选项

Always be aware when judging charts of what the ‘default’ is – what happens if nothing happens. If I ask ‘Will she marry me?’ five minutes after I saw her for the first time, there would need to be strong testimony to give a Yes. If there is no such testimony the answer will be No. If I awake on the morning of our wedding and ask the same question, there would need to be strong testimony of something going wrong to make the answer No. In the absence of such testimony, things will go as planned: the default option is that the marriage will go ahead. In the first instance, if nothing happens there will be no marriage; in the second, if nothing happens to disrupt them, events will roll along as planned and the marriage will take place. Similarly with questions on other subjects. 在判断星盘时，要时刻意识到什么是“默认选项”——即如果没有任何变化发生， 事情会怎样发展。如果我第一次见到她五分钟后问：“她会嫁给我吗？”，那么 必须有强有力的征象才能给出肯定的答案。如果没有这样的征象，答案就是否定 的。如果我在我们婚礼的早晨醒来问同样的问题，那么必须有强有力的征象表明 出了岔子，才能使答案为否定。如果没有这样的征象，事情将按计划进行：默认 选项是婚礼将如期举行。在第一种情况下，如果无事发生，就不会有婚姻；在第 二种情况下，如果无事发生来扰乱计划，事件将按计划推进，婚姻将会举行。其 他主题的问题也与此类似。

The Considerations before Judgement 判断前需考虑的因素

This is another of those topics that we must cover only because you will read about it elsewhere. 这是另一个我们必须涉及的议题，仅仅因为你会在别处读到它。

In ages past, when the astrologer was working for the king, upsetting his employer with an unpleasing judgement could be fatal. But twisting the judgement to give a pleasing answer was little better an option, as events would soon show that the judgement was wrong. The astrologer needed a diplomatic way of fending off unwelcome questions, so a list of ‘considerations before judgement’ was developed. This list is sufficiently comprehensive to ensure that it gives an excuse for not judging any chart that might endanger the astrologer. 在过去，当占星师为国王服务时，用一个不讨喜的判断激怒其雇主可能是致命的。 但为了给出一个讨喜的答案而扭曲判断，也不是什么好选择，因为事件很快会证 明判断是错误的。占星师需要一种外交手段来回避不受欢迎的问题，于是便发展 出了一套“判断前需考虑因素”的清单。这份清单包罗万象，足以成为拒判任何 危及其性命的星盘的借口。

When a king whom not even his mother could love asked, ‘Does the princess of the

next country love me?’ the astrologer could draw up the chart, confident he would find Saturn in the 7th house, or Lord 7 debilitated, or fewer than 3 degrees (some lists state 5) or more than 27 degrees of a sign on the Ascendant, or, or, or. This would enable him to explain, ‘I’m sorry, your Highness. I’d love to judge this chart, but I can’t. See – here, it says so in my textbook’. 当一个连他母亲都无法喜爱的国王问道：“邻国的公主爱我吗？”占星师可以排 盘，并自信地发现 7 宫内有土星，或 7 宫主处于衰弱，或上升点位于某个星座的 不足 3 度（有些清单写的是 5 度）或超过 27 度，等等。这将使他能够解释：“抱 歉，殿下。我很想判断这个星盘，但我不能。看——这里，我的教科书上是这么 写的。”。

The only one of these considerations that is more than an empty excuse capable of impressing ignorant monarchs is that about the number of degrees of a sign on the Ascendant. If an early or late degree of a sign is there, the Ascendant is close to changing from sign to sign. As the Ascendant represents the querent, it is crucial that the astrologer has the right sign on it, otherwise he will use the wrong planet to signify the querent and arrive at an incorrect judgement. Nowadays this is not a problem: timekeeping is so accurate that we can always overcast skies making it impossible to do more than guess at the correct time. 这些考量中唯一起过敷衍作用的，是关于上升点度数的规定。如果上升点位于一 个星座的早期或晚期度数，意味着它接近从一个星座转换到另一个星座。由于上 升点代表问卜者，占星师确保其星座正确至关重要，否则将用错误的行星来象征 问卜者，从而得出错误的判断。如今这已不是问题：计时如此精确，我们总能准 确重现天象，即使我们只能猜测正确时间，也能模拟对应星盘。

The one consideration that is more than an excuse is no longer current. The considerations that are excuses are no longer needed – unless you find yourself working for a short-tempered king, in which case I suggest you pull any excuse out of the air and say it is handed down in the secret oral tradition in which you were trained. So you can forget these considerations. 那一个不止是借口的考虑因素现已不再适用。那些纯属借口的考虑因素也不再需 要——除非你发现自己正在为一个脾气暴躁的国王工作，那样的话我建议你随便 找个借口，就说这是训练你的秘密口传传统中流传下来的。因此，你可以忘记这 些考虑因素了。

There are astrologers who make much of them, deliberating long over whether a chart is ‘radical’, by which they mean ‘capable of being judged’. These astrologers have their own translation of that famous Hermetic dictum, running ‘As above, as every now and again so below’. Every chart can be judged. Astrology does not stop working. 有些占星师对此大做文章，长时间纠结于一个星盘是否“基准”，他们意指“能 够被判断”。这些占星师对那句著名的 Hermetic（赫尔墨斯）格言有自己的翻译， 变成了“在上如在下，只是偶尔如此”。事实上，每张星盘都可以被判断。占星 学从未失效。

I am not going to list the considerations here: my experience with students is that in too many cases once the considerations have been inserted into the head it is impossible to completely flush them out again. Better not to insert them into the head. You will not miss them. 我不打算在这里列出这些考虑因素：根据我与学生的经验，太多情况下，一旦这 些考虑因素被塞进脑子里，就不可能再完全清除掉。最好不要把它们塞进脑子里。 你们绝不会因此缺失什么。

# First House Questions

# 1 宫的问题

Questions relating only to the first house are rare. The hero recovering consciousness and asking ‘Where am I?’ would be an example, but I have yet to be consulted in such circumstances. 仅与 1 宫相关的问题较为罕见。好比故事主角恢复意识后问“我在哪儿？”，但 我至今尚未在这样的情境下接受过咨询。

An actress asked if she would be more successful if she gave up her stage name and reverted to her own name. One’s name is a 1st-house matter, so Lord 1 signified the name. It was retrograde: going backwards, which fitted with her idea of reverting to her own name. But was this a wise dicision? 一位女演员曾问，如果放弃艺名、改回本名，她是否会更加成功？姓名属于 1 宫事务，因此 1 宫主象征她的名字。当时 1 宫主星正逆行：意味着“倒退”，这 符合她想改回本名的念头。但这是明智的决定吗？

Suppose her planet were Venus, at 2 Gemini, retrograding back into its own sign. Going back will make it much stronger: ‘Yes, change back to your own name’. Suppose her planet were Venus, having just turned retrograde, at 28 Aries: it would have been about to enter its own sign, Taurus, becoming much stronger; but it has turned away and is not going to do so: ‘No, the change is harmful; persevering in your present direction will bring you success’. 假设她的宫主星是金星，位于双子座 2 度，正逆行回到它自己守护的金牛座。这 种“退回”将使金星大为增强：“是的，改回本名对你有利”。再假设她的宫主 星是金星，刚刚转为逆行，位于白羊座 28 度：本来它即将进入自己守护的金牛 座并变得更强，但它却转而逆行，不再进入：“不，改名有害；坚持当前方向才 能为你带来成功”。

Testimony could also be given by accidental factors. Perhaps her planet was retrograding away from the South Node and applying to a dignified Jupiter: changing the name is the better option. Retrograding out of the angular 1st house into the cadent 12th: the chang is harmful and will remove her from view. 此外，偶然因素也能提供征象。也许她的宫主星正逆行离开南交点，并正接近一 颗得吉的木星：那么改名是更好的选择。若从角宫 1 宫逆行落入弱宫 12 宫：则 改名有害，会使她淡出公众视野。

THE SHIP THAT I SAIL IN 我乘坐的船

Contemplating my car, and asking ‘Will it get me to Glasgow?’ I am seeing my car as what Lilly calls ‘the ship that I sail in’, hence 1st house. Similarly with ‘Will my flight arrive safely?’ The analogy is with the body (1st house) seen as the vehicle of the soul. If I ask ‘Will someone buy my car?’ I am seeing the car as a movable possession, not as a vehicle, so it is shown by my 2nd house. In the first question its role is as a vehicle; in the second its role is as a possession, which happens to be a vehicle. 当我注视着自己的汽车并问“它能把我带到格拉斯哥吗？”，此时我将汽车视为 Lilly 所说的“我乘坐的船”，因而对应 1 宫。同理，“我的飞机会安全抵达吗？” 也是如此——这类似于将身体（1 宫）视为灵魂的载具。但如果我问“会有人买 我的车吗？”，此时我将汽车视为可移动的财产而非载具，因此它由我的 2 宫表 示。在第一个问题中，它的角色是载具；在第二个问题中，它的角色是财产，只 不过这件财产碰巧是辆汽车。

I do not need to be in the ship at the time of asking the question; nor, indeed, to be in it at all. If I ask ‘Will my treasure-ship reach port safely?’ the ship is 1st house, even if I have never set foot on it. It is as if my soul has sent my body off on an errand. 提问时我并不需要正在这艘“船”上；事实上，甚至完全无需身处其中。如果我 问“我的珍宝船能否安全抵港？”，即使我从未踏上过那艘船，它仍然对应 1 宫。这好比我的灵魂派遣我的身体去执行一项任务。

Such judgements are simple: take Lord 1 and see if anything nasty is going to happen to it. For serious accidents, the prime suspects would be aspects from debilitated Mars or Saturn, or from Lord 8; combustion; conjunction with the South Node. Milder afflictions, such as an aspect from debilitated Venus or Jupiter, would be troublesome but not disastrous. The lack of any such affliction would promise a safe journey. 此类判断很简单：取 1 宫主，观察是否有任何凶险之事将发生在它身上。对于严 重事故，首要怀疑对象包括：来自衰弱的火星或土星的相位、来自 8 宫主的相位、 燃烧、与南交点合相。较轻的侵害，例如来自衰弱的金星或木星的相位，则会带 来麻烦但并非灾难。若没有任何此类侵害，则预示旅途平安。

【‘Here’ is not necessarily where I am right now. - Posted on April 3rd, 2014 【“这里”不一定是我此刻所在的地方 - 发布于 2014 年 4 月 3 日

It depends entirely upon the question. I don’t have to be in my house for it to be my house: whether I am at home, in the mall, or visiting Japan, my house remains my house.If I'm in a hotel in Tokyo and ask what the weather will be, I'm asking about 'here': so the 1st house will show Tokyo, not the place where I live. Or if I ask 'Where

is my passport?' the significator in the 1st would not indicate that I had left it at home. But if I'm in Tokyo and ask 'Should I continue to live in Poland or move back to England?' Poland would be 1st house. If I hear that my flight has been delayed and ask 'When will I get home?' I would be looking at the 1st house to show my home. Or if my wife phones to tell me the cat has gone missing and I ask the question 'When will she come back?' Lord 6 applying to Asc would show Puss coming home, not coming to my hotel.】 这完全取决于问题本身。我不必待在我的房子里：无论我是在家、在商场，还是 在日本访问，我的房子始终是我的房子。如果我在东京的一家酒店里问天气如何， 我问的是“这里”：那么 1 宫将显示东京，而不是我居住的地方。或者，如果我 问“我的护照在哪里？”，位于 1 宫的征象星并不表示我把它落在了家里。但如 果我在东京，问“我应该继续住在波兰，还是搬回英格兰？”，波兰将是 1 宫。 如果我听说我的航班延误了，问“我什么时候能到家？”，我将看 1 宫来代表我 的家。或者，如果我妻子打电话告诉我猫不见了，我问“它什么时候能回来？”， 6 宫主合相上升点将显示猫咪回家，而不是来我的酒店。】

PHYSICAL APPEARANCE 外貌特征

Describing the querent’s appearance from the chart might seem one of the more pointless of astrological operations, especially if querent and astrologer are in the same room. Lilly found it useful: 从星盘描述问卜者的外貌，似乎是占星术中较无意义的操作之一，尤其在问卜者 与占星师同处一室时。但 Lilly 认为这在以下情况有用：

* when the Ascendant was in an early or late degree of its sign
* 当上升点位于其星座的早期或晚期度数时

* when he needed to convince the clinet of his abilities.
* 当他需要让客户信服其能力时。

In the first of these cases, finding that Lord 1 accurately described the querent, who would have been sitting in front of him at the time, was confirmation that he had set the chart with the correct rising sign, and so could proceed to judgement. With modern methods of timekeeping, we no longer need such confirmation. As for the second case, while it must be satisfying to see client’s reactions on hearing the whereabouts of their hidden marks and scars, I would advise against performing such gymnastics to convince clients of your abilities. Imagine a surgeon being asked, ‘I’m not sure that heart operation you’ve done will be effective; can you whip out my gall bladder to show me you know what you’re doing?’ 在第一种情况下，若发现 1 宫主能准确描述当时正坐在面前的问卜者，便可确认 他设置的星盘上升星座正确，从而可继续进行分析判断。凭借现代的计时方法，

我们已不再需要这种确认。至于第二种情况，虽然看到客户听到其隐藏标记和疤 痕位置时的反应必定令人满足，但我仍建议不要通过这种技巧来使客户信服你的 能力。试想：若有人问外科医生“我不确定你做的心脏手术是否有效；你能顺便 切除我的胆囊来证明你知道自己在做什么吗？”

So there is no need to describe the querent. We are, however, sometimes asked for a description of another person, usually the future marriage partner, sometimes a thief. In that case, take the description from the main significator of that person. Qualify the basic characteristics of that planet by the ruler and other major dignities of the sign it is in. This is no place for precision: I hate the thought that we might tell the querent that her husband will be 6′3″and she refuses the perfect spouse because he is 6′ 4″. 因此，无需描述问卜者。然而，我们有时会被要求描述另一个人，通常是未来的 婚姻伴侣，有时是小偷。此时，应从代表该人的主要征象星获取描述。依据该行 星所在星座的守护星及其他主要尊贵来修饰该行星的基本特征。此处并非追求精 确之地：我厌恶这样一种想法——我们可能告诉问卜者她的丈夫身高 6 英尺 3 英寸，结果她因对方是 6 英尺 4 英寸而拒绝了完美伴侣。

There is a problem with the racial determination of appearance. We can follow the astrological rules and describe the man as having curly red hair and freckles, but if he is Japanese we are unlikely to be right. Hair, skin and eye colour are primarily racially determined, and I know of no way of finding which race a person might belong to from the chart. Suppose Miss English Rose asks us to describe her future husband; our description of ‘black hair and sallow complexion’ could well fit the Japanese guy she ends up marrying. But the usual context of such an enquiry is with an Indian or Pakistani woman who will be marrying someone of her own race. In such situations the chart seems to take ‘black hair’ for granted, feeling under no obligation to involve Saturn in the description. 外貌的种族判定存在难题。我们可以遵循占星规则描述此人拥有红色卷发和雀斑， 但如果他是日本人，我们很可能出错。头发、皮肤和眼睛颜色主要由种族决定， 而我不知道如何从星盘判断一个人可能属于哪个种族。假设一位英国白玫瑰小姐 要求描述她未来的丈夫；我们“黑发、肤色暗黄”的描述很可能符合她最终嫁给 的日本男性。但此类询问的常见背景是印度或巴基斯坦女性将嫁给同族者。在此 类情况下，星盘似乎视“黑发”为理所当然，不觉得有必要让土星参与描述。

The following guidelines are all that is needed: 以下标准即已足够：

Saturn: tall and slim. Can give darker hair and complexion. 土星：高而瘦削。可赋予深色头发与肤色。

Jupiter: big, both in height and build; fleshy, especially if in water signs. 木星：高大，身高和体格皆然；肥胖，尤其是在水象星座时。

Mars: short, muscular, solidly built. 火星：矮小，肌肉发达，体格结实。

Sun: tall and well-built, but not as big as Jupiter. Big hair. 太阳：高大匀称，但不及木星魁梧。发量浓密。

Venus: short, soft-bodied (in contrast to the muscularity of Mars). 金星：矮小，身体柔软（与火星的肌肉感形成对比）。

Mercury: mid-height or a little above; slim; straight hair. 水星：中等或略高；瘦削；直发。

Moon: fleshy; not tall. Generally bigger if waxing than if waning. 月亮：肥胖；不高。通常盈月比亏月更显丰满。

Suppose the person’s significator is Mars at 4 Libra. Mars is short, and is ruled by Venus, which is also short. It is in strong Saturn dignities (at 4 Libra it is in the exaltation and the term of Saturn), which will add some height. This can only qualify our basic Mars testimony, however; so while it can make him taller, it will not make him tall. He will be about mid-height or slightly above. Mid-height for his race. The Saturn influence will also make him slimmer. Mars is in its detriment, so he will not have the muscle that Mars usually shows; both Mars and Saturn are lean, so he will be non-muscular, but in a lean, non-flabby sort of way. Had Mars been in Taurus, again in its detriment, the other major dignity (besides Venus) would be the Moon. In Taurus Mars would again lack its usual muscle, but would be bigger built and more fleshy than Mars in Saturn-influenced Libra. Mars in a Venus sign, as also Venuns in a Mars sign, is sure to be attractive. 假设此人的征象星是位于天秤座 4 度的火星。火星主矮小，且受金星（亦主矮小） 守护。它处于土星的强旺状态（在天秤座 4 度位于土星的旺势和得界），这将增 加一些身高。但这只能修饰我们关于火星的基本征象；因此，虽可令他更高些， 却不会让他变得高大。他将是中等或略高身高——以其种族而言的中等。土星的 影响也会让他更瘦削。火星处于落陷，因此他不会拥有火星通常显示的肌肉；火 星与土星皆主精瘦，所以他不会肌肉发达，而是精瘦、不松弛的类型。若火星在 金牛座（同样落陷），另一主要尊贵（除金星外）是月亮。在金牛座的火星同样 缺乏通常的肌肉，但会比受土星影响的天秤座火星更魁梧、多肉。火星在金星星 座，或金星在火星星座，必定具有吸引力。

This description is quite sufficient. ‘You’ll know him by the dragon tattooed on his left forearm,’ sounds good in a novel, but the aim of astrology is not to make the astrologer feel clever. 此描述已完全足够。“你会凭他左前臂的龙纹身认出他”——这小说中听起来不 错，但占星学的目标并非让占星师自觉聪明。

Close aspects to the main significator can show the details of appearance: a Mars

square, for example, showing a visible scar; a gentler aspect from Mars showing patches of pigmentation on the face. But I suggest that such details are better left for confirming what the querent may tell you about the person. If the querent says, ‘The one I suspect of being the thief has a big scar on his cheek,’ we can refer to the chart, note the Mars square and reply, ‘Yes, that would fit: bring him in for questioning’. 与主要征象星的紧密相位可显示外貌细节：例如，火星刑相位可见疤痕；火星的 柔和相位则显示面部色素斑块。但我认为此类细节最好留作确认问卜者可能告诉 你关于此人的信息。如果问卜者说：“我怀疑是小偷的那个人脸颊上有道大疤”， 我们可以查阅星盘，注意到火星刑相位并回答：“是的，这吻合：带他来问话吧。”。

Conjunction with the fixed stars listed on page 114 will show affliction to the eyes, although in an age of contact lenses and laser surgery this is less useful for description than once it was. 与第 220 页所列恒星的合相会显示眼部疾患，但在隐形眼镜和激光手术的时代， 这类描述的用处已不如从前。

Although the planets show a fixed rising scale of age, from babies (Moon) to the most aged (Saturn), for purposes of description these should be regarded as comparatives. That the husband is signified by the Moon shows that she will marry someone younger than her, not that she will marry a baby; Saturn would show that she marries someone significantly older, but not necessarily ancient. The Sun, Venus and Mars can all, in this context, be taken as showing much the same age. 尽管行星显示了一个固定的年龄递增尺度，从婴儿（月亮）到最年长（土星）， 但就描述目的而言，这些应视为比较级。丈夫由月亮征象表明她会嫁给比她年轻 的人，而非嫁给婴儿；土星则显示她嫁给明显年长者，但不一定是耄耋老人。在 此语境下，太阳、金星和火星皆可视为显示大致相同的年龄。

If you feel you cannot live without checking the querent’s marks and scars, this should be done off the first, heartfelt question. We cannot expect the stars to show the same arrangement of bodily blemishes every time a regular client asks a horary. Look first at the sign rising. Which part of the body does this signify? (see page 49) These will be a scar or mark there. The degree of that sign that is on the Ascendant will show where in that part of the body the mark lies: at 0 degrees it will at the top of that part, at 29 degrees it will be near the bottom. 如果你觉得不查验问卜者的标记疤痕就活不下去，这应基于第一个发自内心的问 题进行。我们不能指望每当一位常客提出卜卦时，星辰都显示相同的身体瑕疵排 列。首先看上升星座。它象征身体的哪个部位？（见第 96 页）该处会有疤痕或 标记。上升点所在星座的度数将显示标记在该身体部位的位置：0 度在部位顶部， 29 度在底部附近。

Treat the cusp of the 6th house and the position of the Moon in the same way, by sign and degree, showing two more marks. A debilitated planet in the 1st house will show a mark on the face, the whereabouts on the face being shown by its degree. Close aspects to the Ascendant from Mars or Saturn will show marks according to the

planet’s sign and degree – but do keep these aspects close. The more debilitated the planet is, the larger the mark. If the significator is above the Earth, the mark is at the front or on the visible area of that body-part; if below the Earth it will be hidden. If the dispositor of the planet showing the mark is in a masculine sign, it will be on the right; if in a feminine, on the left. 以同样方式（通过星座和度数）处理 6 宫头及月亮位置，可显示另外两处标记。 1 宫内一颗衰弱的行星显示面部有标记，其度数显示在面部的具体位置。火星或 土星与上升点的紧密相位会根据该行星的星座和度数显示标记——但务必确保 这些相位足够紧密。行星越衰弱，标记越大。若显示标记的征象星在地平线上， 标记在该身体部位的前部或可见区域；若在地平线下，则隐藏。若显示标记的行 星的定位星在阳性星座，标记在右侧；在阴性星座则在左侧。

Lilly says that these rules not only convinced his clients, but had a major part in persuading him of the veracity of astrology.On the odd occasion I’ve used them they have worked well enough. Lilly 称这些规则不仅令他的客户信服，更在说服他本人相信占星学真实性方面 起了主要作用。在我偶尔使用它们时，其效果也相当不错。

35. Lilly p.148

### ✸I was deferring too much to Lilly when writing about the querent’s marks and

scars. The idea that we can see such marks in the chart, whether horary or natal, is a fairy-tale: it’s not meant to be taken seriously. Consider: in Lilly’s day smallpox was endemic in London. A high proportion of his clients had scars on the face. They did not all flock to his office when Mars was in the 1st house, nor has there been any realignment of planets to match the far smaller proportion of horary clients who have facial scars today.

### ✷我在撰写关于问卜者标记疤痕的部分时过于遵从莉莉的观点。认为我们能在

星盘（无论是卜卦还是本命盘）中看到此类标记的想法纯属童话：它本不应被严 肃对待。试想：在 Lilly 的时代，天花是伦敦的地方病。他的客户中很高比例面 部有疤。他们并非都在火星在 1 宫时涌向他的办公室，行星也未曾重新排列以匹 配如今比例低得多的卜卦客户面部有疤的情况。

In many of the example judgements in Christian Astrology Lilly gives physical descriptions of the people concerned. Superficially impressive, on closer examination these can be seen to ower far more to reading-in than they ever do to astrology. For instance, in the chart in chapter LX Lilly attributes the man’s dark (‘sad’) hair to an aspect to his significator from Saturn. He ignores the closer aspect from Mars that would have shown him to be a red-head. Do not expect the chart to show physical appearance unless the question specifically requests this.✷ 在《Christian Astrology》的许多示例判断中，Lilly 给出了相关人物的体貌描述。 这些描述表面令人印象深刻，但细究之下可见其更多归功于主观解读而非占星学

本身。例如，在第 60 章的星盘中，Lilly 将此人深色（“暗淡”）头发归因于土 星对其征象星的相位。他忽略了火星更紧密的相位——那本会显示此人红发。除 非问题明确要求，否则不要期望星盘显示外貌。✷

# Second House Questions

# 2 宫的问题

LOST,STOLEN AND STRAYED 遗失、被盗与走失

Finding a lost object by casting a horoscope is spectacular. Not finding it is an excellent way of losing credibility quickly. My success rate with these questions is far below what I have with horaries in general. The problem lies in translating the symbolism of the chart into life.
