In most questions, we have a limited range of possibilities – ‘Yes, he’ll marry you’ or ‘No, he won’t’, at an extreme of simplicity – but a lost object can be anywhere. As we are usually dealing with places which we haven’t seen, we have little information to work with when deciding what the planets represent. Mars in one room might represent the fireplace, in another it might be the gun-cabinet. I find I am often looking at the chart, seeing exactly where the object is in astrological terms and knowing that it would be so obvious – if only I knew where it was. Which, of course, I don’t. 通过绘制占星盘寻找失物，其效果堪称惊艳。但若找不到，则是迅速丧失信誉的 绝佳方式。我对这类问题的成功率远低于一般卜卦。问题在于将星盘的象征符号 转化为现实情境。在大多数问题中，我们的可能性范围有限——极端简单的情况 如“是的，他会娶你”或“不，他不会”——但失物可能在任何地方。由于我们 通常处理的是未曾见过的场所，在判断行星代表什么时，我们掌握的信息极少。 火星在一个房间里可能代表壁炉，在另一个房间则可能是枪柜。我常常发现自己 盯着星盘，从占星角度完全清楚物品所在，并知道那会如此显而易见——前提是 我知道那个地方在哪里。当然，我并不知道。

And when locating a lost object, we must be exactly right; in many other questions we have an amount of leeway. Explaining to your client, ‘You almost found it,’ is unlikely to impress. 而在定位失物时，我们必须完全准确；在许多其他问题中，我们有一定回旋余地。 向客户解释“你差点就找到了”不太可能令人印象深刻。

I would love to be able to give you Frawley’s Foolproof Method, with a guarantee of 100% success; but I can’t. Frawley’s Non-Foolproof Method, as I explain it here, works well enough. It will find some objects with astonishing accuracy; it will fail to find others in the most frustrating manner. As with all astrology, however, we should

celebrate what we can do, not lament what we cannot. 我多希望能给你一套 Frawley 的万全之法，并保证 100%成功；但我不能。Frawley 的非万全之法，正如我在此解释的，效果尚可。它会以惊人的准确度找到某些物 品；也会以最令人沮丧的方式找不到其他物品。然而，正如所有占星学一样，我 们应庆幸力所能及之事，而非哀叹力所不及之处。

Main significators 主要征象星

The object will be shown by either the 2nd or the 4th house if it is inanimate, either the 6th or the 12th if it is animate. 若是无生命物体，由其 2 宫或 4 宫表示；若是有生命物体，则由 6 宫或 12 宫表 示。

With an inanimate object we have the choice of the 2nd, the house of our movable possessions, and the 4th, the house of buried treasure. Treasure need not have been buried deliberately: it can be that document you put down which someone has buried under a pile of magazines. Some modern texts make much of a distinction between lost objects (2nd house) and mislaid objects (4th). The authors who can make such a clear distinction between losing something and mislaying it have subtler minds than mine. Nor, in practice, do we need to invoke the distinction between lost objects and buried treasure. Whatever the circumstances of the loss, look to the rulers of the 2nd and the 4th, and use whichever of them best describes the object. 对于无生命物体，我们可选择 2 宫（我们可移动财产的宫位）与 4 宫（埋藏宝藏 的宫位）。宝藏未必是刻意埋藏：也可能是你放下后被人埋在一堆杂志下的那份 文件。某些现代文献对遗失物（2 宫）与错置物（4 宫）作了大量区分。能在“遗 失”与“错置”间作出如此清晰区分的作者，心思比我更为缜密。实践中，我们 也无需援引遗失物与埋藏宝藏的区别。无论遗失的具体情形如何，观察 2 宫与 4 宫的守护星，并选用能最好描述该物体的那颗。

Example: ‘Where are my keys?’ with the chart showing Cancer on the 2nd cusp, Virgo on the 4th. Mercury, ruler of Virgo, is the natural ruler of keys: Mercury will be the significator. 示例：“我的钥匙在哪里？”星盘显示 2 宫头为巨蟹座，4 宫头为处女座。处女 座守护星水星是钥匙的先天守护星：水星将成为征象星。

If the querent asks about somebody else’s lost object, so you must turn the chart, always take the person’s 2nd house, whether it appears to describe the object or not. ‘Where is my daughter’s watch?’: the ruler of the 6th house (2nd from the 5th) will signify the watch. 若问卜者询问他人遗失的物品，则必须转宫，始终取该人的 2 宫（无论其是否看 似描述该物体）。“我女儿的手表在哪里？”：6 宫（5 之 2 宫）守护星将征象 手表。

If the object is signified by the same planet as the querent, give the disputed planet to the object. In these questions the most important point is the whereabouts of the thing; its relationship to the querent is secondary. 若物体与问卜者由同一行星征象，将该争议行星分配给物体。在此类问题中，最 重要的是物体的下落；其与问卜者的关系是次要的。

If you are looking for a lost animal, take the 6th if it is smaller than a goat, the 12th if large. We are concerned here with generic distinctions: my Great Dane may be bigger than my Shetland pony, but dogs are small animals (6th) and horses are large ones (12th). 若寻找走失动物，体型小于山羊者取 6 宫，体型较大者取 12 宫。此处我们关注 的是类别区分：我的大丹犬可能比设得兰小马更大，但狗属于小型动物（6 宫）， 而马属于大型动物（12 宫）。

If you are looking for a missing person, use whichever house shows that person’s relationship to the querent, e.g. 5th for a missing child, 6th for a missing employee. The 7th is said to be the house of fugitives; it is more reliable to use the specific house for that individual. Keep the 7th for missing spouses or for ‘any old person’. 若寻找失踪人员，使用代表该人与问卜者关系的宫位，例如失踪儿童用 5 宫，失 踪雇员用 6 宫。7 宫据称是逃亡者之宫；但使用代表该特定个体的具体宫位更为 可靠。7 宫保留给失踪配偶或“任何普通人”。

Other significators 其他征象星

The Moon is the natural ruler of all lost objects, especially animate ones. But keep with the main significator, as above, as far as you can: looking at two planets for location will only confuse you. In most lost object charts we don’t need to consider the Moon. As a secondary significator, it is useful for timing recovery when the main significator is not making any aspects. For an example of this, look back at the cat chart in chapter 1. 月亮是所有失物（尤其是有生命物体）的先天守护星。但请尽可能遵循上述主要 征象星的原则：同时参考两颗行星来定位只会令你困惑。在大多数失物盘中，我 们无需考虑月亮。作为次要征象星，当主要征象星未形成任何相位时，月亮有助 于判断寻回时机。相关示例可回顾第 1 章中关于猫的星盘。

Yes, this does mean that the Moon can signify both the object and the querent, sometimes both in the same chart. This is not as confusing as it sounds, because it will represent each of them at different stages of the judgement. 是的，这意味着月亮可同时征象物体与问卜者，有时在同一星盘中两者皆是。这 并不像听起来那么令人困惑，因为它将在判断的不同阶段分别代表两者。

Sometimes the natural ruler of the object can be used, whether it rules the relevant house or not. Do this if the chart thrusts this planet on your attention, or if, considering both the planet and the sign it is in, it perfectly describes the object. A client asked ‘Where are my pistols?’ and the chart showed Mars (gun) in Virgo (Mercury sign, so small gun; double-bodied sign, so more than one small gun) right on the Ascendant. 有时，物体的先天守护星亦可使用，无论它是否守护相关宫位。若星盘强烈吸引 你关注该行星，或该行星及其所在星座完美描述了该物体，则可如此操作。曾有 客户问“我的手枪在哪里？”，星盘显示火星（象征枪支）在处女座（水星星座， 故为小手枪；双体星座，故不止一把小手枪）且正好位于上升点。

Fortuna, which shows the querent’s treasure, in whatever sense fits the context of the question, can occasionally be useful. I suggest you ignore it until you get really stuck. Even then, you will more often reach a judgement by persevering with the main significator. 福点象征问卜者的财富（其含义需符合问题语境），偶尔也有用处。我建议你先 忽略它，除非你真的束手无策。即便如此，坚持分析主要征象星往往更能得出结 论。

### ✸Fortuna can be ignored. Two points I would emphasise: if there is a planet in the

chart that exactly describes the object, use that, even if it doesn’t rule the 2nd or 4th house. Use only the main significator of the object to locate it: the Moon can confirm recovery and show the timing of recovery, but will not show where the thing is, unless it is itself the main significator.✷

### ✸福点通常可以忽略。我想强调两点：若星盘中有行星能精确描述该物体，即

使它不守护 2 宫或 4 宫，亦可使用；仅使用物体的主要征象星进行定位——月亮 可确认寻回及判断时机，但不会显示物品位置，除非月亮本身就是主要征象星。 ✷

Will it be found? 能否找回？

If it will not be found there is not usually much point describing where it is, no matter how fervently the client may demand that you do. 通常，若物品无法找回，描述其所在位置便没有多大意义，无论客户如何热切要 求你这样做。

The strongest testimony of recovery is an applying aspect between the object and the querent, or between the object and Lord 2 (if the object is signified by something else), showing it returning to the querent’s possession. We see here the two roles of the Moon: recovery of my lost cow could be shown by Moon (querent) applying to Lord

12 (cow); it could also be shown by Moon (natural ruler of lost objects) applying to Lord 1 (querent). Be open to either possibility. 预示寻回的最有力征象，是物体与问卜者之间、或物体与 2 宫主之间（若物体由 其他征象星代表）正在形成的入相位，显示它将回归问卜者手中。在此我们看到 月亮的双重角色：我丢失的母牛可能通过月亮（问卜者）与 12 宫主（牛）形成 入相位显示寻回；也可能通过月亮（失物的先天守护星）与 1 宫主（问卜者）形 成入相位显示寻回。需对两种可能性持开放态度。

The Moon applying to its own dispositor is a good testimony of recovery. 月亮与其定位星形成入相位，是寻回的有利征象。

Having at least one of the Lights (the Sun and Moon) above the horizon (the Ascendant/Descendant axis) is helpful. This is quite literal: if there is no light we cannot see to find anything. 至少有一颗发光体（太阳与月亮）位于地平线（上升点/下降点的轴线）之上， 亦有所帮助。这相当直白：若没有光，我们便无法看见、无法寻找任何东西。

### ✸Note: ‘It is helpful.’ This is not definite testimony of recovery. It is the absence of

a negative rather than a compelling positive.✷

### ✸注意：“有所帮助。”这并非寻回的确定征象。它只是负面因素的缺失，而

非强有力的正面征象。✷

If Lord 1 is combust the querent can’t see. If the object is combust is can’t be seen. But combustion doesn’t last forever: especially if the planet has already made its conjunction with the Sun and so is moving out of combustion, this is a positive sign for recovery. 若 1 宫主处于燃烧状态，问卜者无法看见。若物体征象星处于燃烧状态，则物体 无法被看见。但燃烧不会永远持续：特别是当行星已与太阳完成合相并正移出燃 烧状态时，这是寻回的积极迹象。

The object’s significator being close to an angle increases the likelihood of recovery, even without an aspect. So does a clear location: in such cases we would often not even bother looking for an aspect. ‘Where is the teddy-bear?’ ‘In the 5th house: in the child’s room’. With such information we can get up and got to look for it, without wasting our time hunting aspects. 物体征象星靠近四轴点会增加寻回可能性，即使未形成相位。位置明确时亦然： 在此类情况下，我们甚至常常无需费力寻找相位。“泰迪熊在哪里？”“在 5 宫：在孩子的房间里。”有了这样的信息，我们可以起身直接去寻找，无需浪费 时间搜寻相位。

The 1st or 2nd house favoured by the presence of a strongly dignified Jupiter or Venus, or the North Node, is mildly encouraging testimony.

1 宫或 2 宫内出现强旺的木星或金星、或北交点，是微弱的积极征象。

### ✸If this has any significance at all it is so minor that it can safely be ignored.✷

### ✸即便有意义，其影响也微乎其微，完全可以忽略。✷

Lilly says that if the object’s significator is in its detriment or fall, the object will be damaged or only partly recovered. This is true on occasions, but I have not found it generally so. Lilly 指出，若物体征象星处于落陷或弱势，该物将受损或仅部分找回。有时确 实如此，但我发现这并非普遍情况。

### ✸In most cases, testimony of either recovery or timing is superfluous. If we can see

where the object is, we can usually go to pick it up. If we know where it is, there is no point wasting time looking for testimony that we will find it if we look there. As it is superfluous, charts often seem not to bother providing such testimony: even with hindsight it cannot be seen, or is, at least, beyond any knowledge of mine. The exception is when Puss is missing. The important thing there is the knowledge that she will come home; where she is right now is usually irrelevant.

### ✸若我们能看出物体在哪里，通常可以直接去取回。若已知位置，便无需浪费

时间寻找"去那里就能找到"的征象。正因其多余，星盘往往似乎懒得提供此类征 象：即使事后回顾，也看不到，或至少超出我的认知范围。例外情况是猫咪走失。 那时重要的是知道它会回家；它此刻身在何处通常无关紧要。

Timing: if the aspect showing the recovery of a lost object perfects in less than 1 degree, this can usually be read as ‘more to less immediately’, regardless of sign and house. ✷ 应期：若显示失物寻回的相位在 1 度内形成入相位，通常可解读为"近乎立即"， 无论其位于何种星座或宫位。✷

Has it been stolen? 是否被盗？

Probably not. Lilly gives a long list of testimonies showing that the thing has been stolen;apply these rigorously and you will find cause to hang anyone. Most things are lost because we cannot remember where we put them; but as soon as we find they have gone, thoughts of theft, or any other way of pinning the blame on someone else, crowd to our mind. The wise astrologer will not encourage this. I strongly suggest that you do not invoke a thief unless the querent raises the possibility of theft. This follows the usual rule: Don’t write extra characters into the story unless you really must.

Imagine yourself a TV scriptwriter, and remember that every new character you introduce is another actor who will have to be paid! 很可能并非如此。Lilly 列出了一长串显示物品被盗的征象；若严格套用，你会 发现几乎人人皆有盗窃嫌疑。大多数物品遗失是因为我们记不清放置的位置；但 一旦发现东西不见，关于被盗或将责任归咎于他人的念头便涌上心头。明智的占 星师不会助长这种想法。我强烈建议，除非问卜者主动提出被盗的可能性，否则 不要引入"小偷"这一角色。这遵循通常的原则：除非确有必要，否则不要在故事 中添加额外角色。设想自己是一名电视剧编剧，记住你引入的每个新角色都意味 着需要支付片酬的演员！

36. Lilly pp. 331-6

There are three testimonies which would provide evidence of theft: 有三种征象可提供被盗证据：

* a separating aspect between the suspect and the object, showing that the suspect has come into contact with the object. Similarly with the general significator of a thief (see below).
* 嫌疑人与物品之间存在出相位，显示嫌疑人曾接触该物品。同样适用于盗贼的 通用征象星（见下文）。

* a close conjunction of suspect and object, showing that the object is with the suspect. This can be by antiscion.
* 嫌疑人与物品紧密合相（包括通过映点），显示物品与嫌疑人在一起。

* the object being in the suspect’s house, especially if just inside the cusp.
* 物品位于嫌疑人的宫位内，尤其是紧贴宫头内侧时。

If there is any doubt at all that the object may not have been stolen, I would be most reluctant to cry ‘Thief’ without one of these testimonies. 只要对物品是否被盗存有丝毫疑问，若无上述任一征象，我极不愿意断言“有贼”。

Examples: ‘Did the builder steal my bracelet?’ with Lord 6 (the builder) separating from aspect to whichever of Lord 2 or Lord 4 signifies the bracelet. Yes, he did. No such aspect: no, he didn’t. Note: this must be a separating aspect. An applying aspect, which shows something that hasn’t happened yet, cannot signify a theft that has already taken place. Lilly gives a chart about some stolen money.Lord 2 (the querent’s money) is conjunct the significator of the thief by antiscion (antiscion implying something secret or hidden). Had the builder and the bracelet been conjunct, bodily or by antiscion, this would show that builder still had the bracelet. 示例：“是建筑工人偷了我的手镯吗？”若 6 宫主（建筑工人）与代表手镯的 2 宫主或 4 宫主形成出相位，则答案为是，他偷了。若无此类相位，则答案为否， 他没偷。注意：这必须是出相位。入相位显示尚未发生之事，无法表征已发生的 盗窃。Lilly 曾给出一个关于钱财被盗的星盘：2 宫主（问卜者的钱财）通过映点

（暗示隐秘或隐藏）与盗贼的征象星合相。若建筑工人与手镯形成实体或映点合 相，则表明工人仍持有手镯。

37. Lilly p.394

If the querent knows that the object has been stolen, things are different. We do not then need to prove the fact of theft. Questions where theft is certain are discussed below. 若问卜者已知物品被盗，情况则不同。此时我们无需证明盗窃事实。下文将讨论 盗窃已确定的情况。

Where is it? 它在哪儿？

Once you have identified the significator of the object, look to the chart to find out where it is. Remember: this planet is the missing object; where the planet is, there the object will be. 一旦确定了物体的征象星，即可观察星盘以查明其位置。记住：这颗行星即代表 失踪物品；行星所在之处，即是物品所在之处。

By far the most reliable way of determining this is by house meanings. In my experience, this is the only method worth using. As with the lost cat in chapter 1 (‘Where is the cat?’ ‘In the cat’s house.’) so with most other questions. ‘Did I leave my keys at my friend’s house?’ with significator of the keys in the 11th house (friend): ‘Yes, they are with your friend’. A querent had lost the stone from a ring. The significator was conjunct the Ascendant, showing that the stone was very (very!) close to the querent. It had fallen into the lining of his jacket. 目前最可靠的判断方法是依据宫位含义。以我的经验，这是唯一值得使用的方法。 如同第 1 章中丢失的猫（“猫在哪里？”“在猫的房子里。”），大多数其他问 题也是如此。“我把钥匙忘在朋友家了吗？”若钥匙的征象星在 11 宫（朋友）： “是的，钥匙在你朋友那里。”一位问卜者丢失了戒指上的宝石。征象星与上升 点合相，显示宝石离问卜者非常（非常！）近。它掉进了他夹克的内衬里。

It is tempting to take what the querent says as truth. Don’t! If the querent knew what was going on the object would not be lost. The querent’s statements must be treated with extreme caution. Always remember: The truth is in the chart, not in what you are told. My experience is that the most common locations for lost objects are: 人们容易将问卜者所言当作事实。切勿如此！如果问卜者知道发生了什么，物品 就不会丢失。必须极其谨慎地对待问卜者的陈述。永远记住：真相在星盘中，而 非在你所闻中。我的经验是，失物最常见的位置是：

* exactly where the querent tells you it definitely isn’t
* 恰恰在问卜者坚称绝不可能的地方

* with the children
* 与孩子们在一起

* with the spouse.
* 与配偶在一起

If the charts supports one of these, ignore all protestations to the contrary. 若星盘支持其中一种情况，请无视所有相反的抗议。

If the significator is in the 7th, our first choice must be that it is with the spouse. The 7th is the house of the thief, so this could mean that a thief has it; but remember the comments on theft, above. There are a lot more spouses than there are thieves. Do remember, though, that the 7th is not only the house of the spouse. It is also the 3rd from the 5th, making it the house of the child’s sibling: the younger brother or sister. Always go for the most obvious option first, whichi in this case is the spouse; if that doesn’t produce the object, you can move on to the younger child. You do not have to get it right first time: this is a consultation, not a magic act. 若征象星在 7 宫，我们首先必须考虑它在配偶那里。7 宫也是盗贼之宫，因此可 能意味着盗贼持有它；但请记住上文关于盗窃的评论。配偶可比盗贼多得多。不 过，请记住 7 宫不仅是配偶之宫。它也是 5 之 3 宫，即孩子的兄弟姐妹（弟弟或 妹妹）之宫。始终首先选择最明显的选项，本例中即配偶；若此路不通，再考虑 年幼的孩子。你不必一次就猜对：这是咨询，而非魔术表演。

Ask the querent for a list of suspects. If the object is lost at home, who lives there? If outside the home, where has the querent been? Does the querent work? Whom has he visited? You are entitled to ask these questions. 可向问卜者索要一份可疑人员名单。若物品在家中丢失，谁住在那里？若在户外 丢失，问卜者去过哪里？问卜者工作吗？他拜访过谁？你有权询问这些问题。

For the basic ‘Where is it?’ the Moon being void of course is irrelevant: the object must be somewhere, even if that somewhere is ‘destroyed’. 对于基本的“它在哪里？”问题，月亮空亡无关紧要：物品必定在某个地方，即 使那个地方是“已毁坏”。

In the home 在家中（的位置）

1st house: the front door or entry hall (entrance to the chart); the querent’s own place in the home. 1 宫：前门或门厅（星盘的入口）；问卜者在家中的专属位置。

2nd house: the kitchen (2nd rules the throat and hence what goes into it). The

storeroom or larder. The cloakroom (in the strict sense of the word: see 8th house) or wardrobe. The room next to the entrance. Any house can be read as being next to the room shown by the house adjacent. 2 宫：厨房（2 宫掌管喉咙，因而关联进食之处）。储藏室或食品柜。衣帽间（严 格意义上，见 8 宫）或衣柜。紧邻入口的房间。任何宫位都可解读为紧邻其相邻 宫位所代表的房间。

3rd house: in an office, this would be the post-room. The communications hub. Corridors, halls and landings. 3 宫：在办公室，此处为邮件收发室。通讯枢纽。走廊、大厅和楼梯平台。

4th house: the informal room of the house (in contrast to the 10th: the formal room). The granny flat. The cellar (bottom of the chart). 4 宫：家中的非正式房间（与 10 宫正式房间相对）。老人房。地下室（星盘底 部）。

5th house: the child’s room or nursery. The games room. 5 宫：孩子的房间或育儿室。游戏室。

6th house: the servants’ quarters, hence the utility room. The dog kennel. 6 宫：仆人居所，引申为杂物间。狗窝。

7th house: the spouse’s lair. 7 宫：配偶的领地。

8th house: the toilet (2nd being where food comes in, 8th being where it goes out). The bathroom (where dirt is removed). 8 宫：厕所（2 宫为食物进入之处，8 宫为排出之处）。浴室（去除污垢之处）。

9th house: the study. The chapel, shrine, meditation room. A landing or upstairs corridor (higher version of the 3rd house). 9 宫：书房。小礼拜堂、神龛、冥想室。楼梯平台或楼上走廊（3 宫概念的更高 版本）。

10th house: the home office. The formal room of the house (when Lilly calls this ‘the hall’ he means the great hall where you entertain visiting royalty, not a corridor). The attic (top of the chart). 10 宫：家庭办公室。家中的正式房间（Lilly 称此为“大厅”时，指的是接待王 室宾客的宴会厅，而非走廊）。阁楼（星盘顶部）。

11th house: the guest room (where your friends stay). 11 宫：客房（朋友留宿之处）。

12th house: the garage (where the horses are kept) or stables. The junk room.

12 宫：车库（停放马匹之处）或马厩。杂物间。

Above the Ascendant/Descendant axis can mean upstairs; below it downstairs. 位于上升点/下降点的轴线之上可表示楼上；之下表示楼下。

Within the room 在房间内（的位置）

Once you have decided on a room, look at other factors of the planet’s placement for further information. 一旦确定了房间，可观察行星位置的其他因素以获取更多信息。

Significator in an: 征象星位于：

* Earth sign: on, near or under the floor.
* 土象星座：地板上、地板附近或地板下。

* Air sign: high up, maybe on a shelf or hook. Somewhere light. By the window or TV.
* 风象星座：高处，可能在架子或挂钩上。明亮处。窗边或电视机旁。

* Fire sign: somewhere hot. Near the walls.
* 火象星座：炎热处。靠近墙壁。

* Water sign: somewhere wet. Somewhere comfortable.
* 水象星座：潮湿处。舒适处。

* Mutable signs can show that it is inside something – in a box or cupboard.
* 变动星座可显示它在某物内部——盒子或橱柜里。

### ✸The connection of fire signs and walls is false and should be ignored. The idea is

that walls are built from bricks and bricks are made by firing, but what the wall is built from and how that material is made have no relevance.✷

### ✸火象星座与墙壁的关联是错误的，应予忽略。其逻辑是墙壁由砖砌成，而砖

需烧制，但墙壁的建材及其制作方式并无关联。✷

A planet on the cusp of the house or at a change of sign within that house will show the object is near the door. Near to the following cusp can show it at the opposite end to the door. 行星位于宫头或该宫内星座交界处，可显示物品靠近门。靠近下一个宫头则可能

显示它在远离门的一端。

Look at close aspects to this planet. Conjunct the Moon: it’s next to the fishtank. Opposed Saturn: it’s opposite the clock. 观察与该行星的紧密相位。与月亮合相：在鱼缸旁边。与土星对冲：在钟的对面。

This is, as noted above, the biggest problem with locating lost objects. Everything in the universe is described by only seven planets. We might imagine that the Moon signifies a fish tank; it could be a candelabra, a white sofa, or any one of a million other possibilities. That said, connections with Mercury often show that it is with books or knick-knacks; connections with Venus, near clothes (especially women’s), bedding or soft furnishings. I haven’t noticed similar major indications with the other planets. 如上所述，这是定位失物的最大难题。宇宙万物仅由七颗行星描述。我们可能想 象月亮象征鱼缸；它也可能是枝形吊灯、白色沙发，或无数其他可能性之一。尽 管如此，与水星的关联常显示它在书籍或小摆设旁；与金星的关联，则常在衣物 （尤其是女性衣物）、寝具或软装饰附近。我尚未注意到其他行星有类似的主要 指示意义。

Outside the home 在户外

Being in an angular house can show that the object is close at hand or near where it ought to be. In a cadent house in may be a long way off. In a succedent house, somewhere between the two. How far ‘a long way off’ is will be determined by the context: ‘Where is my globe-trotting son whom I haven’t heard from?’ is likely to be further away than ‘Where is the cat?’ 处于角宫可能表示物品近在手边或处于应在之地。处于果宫则可能意味着它在很 远的地方。处于续宫则表示介于两者之间。“很远的地方”具体多远需依据上下 文判断：“我那环游世界、杳无音信的儿子在哪里？”很可能比“猫在哪里？” 要远得多。

Give priority to the natural meaning of the house, however. If the object is in the 9th and we know the querent goes to college, it may well be at her college, even if that is very close to home. 然而，应优先考虑宫位的自然含义。若物品在 9 宫，且我们知道问卜者正在上大 学，那么它很可能就在她的大学里，即使大学离家非常近。

In some cases we do not know if the missing object is inside or outside the home. Being in the 9th might show that it is a long way off, possibly in a 9th-house sort of place (church, school). Or it could show that it is at home in a 9th-house sort of place: in the study or near a shrine. Being in the 10th: is it at work, or is it in the feasting-hall at home? I do not know any way of distinguishing which it will be. Try the most

likely; if that doesn’t work, try the alternative. Remember: you do not have to get it right first time. 在某些情况下，我们不知道失踪物品是在室内还是户外。在 9 宫可能表示它在很 远的地方，可能在某类 9 宫性质的地方（教堂、学校）。或者也可能表示它在家 中的某个 9 宫性质场所：在书房或神龛附近。在 10 宫：是在工作场所，还是在 家中的宴会厅？我不知道有任何方法可以区分究竟是哪种情况。先尝试最可能的 那种；如果不对，再尝试另一种。记住：你不必一次就猜对。

There are several methods of determining direction in the chart. The only method with any reliability is based on the North South East West that forms the fundamental structure of the chart: the Sun rises in the east (Ascendant), travels through the south (MC) to set in the west (Descendant), returning to the east by way of the IC, which is north. Midway between north and east is, of course, north-east. Involving the signs only confuse matters: it may offer the promise of refining the direction, but in practice gives only contradiction. North by west is a refinement; north by south is a nonsense. NB: remember that in the chart, unlike a map, south is at the top. 有几种方法可以确定星盘中的方向。唯一稍有可靠性的方法是基于构成星盘基本 结构的东南西北：太阳从东方（上升点）升起，经过南方（中天）在西方（下降 点）落下，再经由天底（北方）返回东方。介于北与东之间，自然是东北方向。 引入星座只会混淆问题：它或许提供了细化方向的可能性，但在实践中只会带来 矛盾。“北偏西”是细化；“北偏南”则是胡扯。注意：记住在星盘中，与地图 不同，南方在上方。

Direction-finding is meant only for use outdoors, locating lost people or animals: don’t use it within the home – unless the querent’s house has its east and wet wings. 方向判断仅适用于户外，用于定位失踪的人或动物：不要在室内使用——除非问 卜者的房子有明确的东翼和西翼。

If you are asking about somebody’s whereabouts, remember that in the turned chart that person’s home will almost always be shown by their 1st, not their 4th – as with the cat in chapter 1. ‘Where’s my brother?’ with Lord 3 (my brother) in the 3rd (he house of brothers): he’s at home. 如果你询问某人的下落，请记住在转宫盘中，那个人的家几乎总是由他的 1 宫表 示，而非他的 4 宫——如同第 1 章中的猫一样。“我哥哥在哪里？”若 3 宫主（我 哥哥）在 3 宫（兄弟之宫）：他在家里。

Fido’s significator in the 12th is an indication that he may be in the pound (12th being the house of prisons). Fido（菲多，狗名）的征象星在 12 宫，可能表示它在动物收容所（12 宫为监狱 之宫）。

Theft 盗窃

Some questions on theft have a specific suspect: ‘Did the builder steal my bracelet?’ with the implication that if he didn’t, the querent probably lost it. In others, the thief is ‘person or persons unknow’. 一些关于盗窃的问题有具体的嫌疑人：“是建筑工人偷了我的手镯吗？”暗示着 如果他没偷，问卜者很可能只是弄丢了。另一些问题中，小偷是“身份不明者”。

If there is a specific suspect, use the ruler of that person’s house in the usual way, e.g. Lord 3 for the neighbour, Lord 6 for the builder. If there is no specific suspect, the choices for significator of the thief, in order of preference, are: 如果有具体嫌疑人，按常规方式使用代表该人宫位的守护星，例如 3 宫主代表邻 居，6 宫主代表建筑工人。如果没有具体嫌疑人，小偷征象星的选择按优先顺序 如下：

* a planet that is peregrine, in its detriment or its fall, and is in an angle or the 2nd house
* 一颗游离、处于落陷或弱势、且位于角宫或 2 宫的行星

* Lord 7
* 7 宫主

* Mercury, the natural ruler of thieves.
* 水星，小偷的先天守护星。

If we know that the object is stolen, we do not need to have a separating aspect between thief and object to prove this. 若已知物品被盗，则无需证明小偷与物品之间存在出相位。

Once we have the thief’s significator, we can draw a description in the usual way (see page 164). If we are taking Mercury as significator because it is natural ruler of thieves, we cannot, of course, use Mercury for the description – not all thieves look mercurial. In this case, use its dispositor. 一旦确定了小偷的征象星，便可按常规方式描绘其外貌（见第 269 页）。若因水 星是小偷的先天守护星而将其作为征象星，当然不能用水星来描绘外貌——并非 所有小偷都长得像水星。此时，应使用其定位星。

The significator in a double-bodied sign is a good indication that there is more than one thief. 征象星位于双体星座，强烈暗示存在多名窃犯。

Unfortunately, unless the thief is known to the querent there is not much point in describing him. 遗憾的是，除非小偷为问卜者所认识，否则描述他并没有太大意义。

### ✸“Why don’t we just use Lord 7 as the significator of the thief?” Because doing

that excludes what is in the most cases the only useful identification we can give. Unless there is a very short list of suspects, physical description of the thief is useless. But what we can valuably do is confirm or rule out that it was stolen by the builder, or the neighbour, or the girlfriend’s brother, based on the house rulership of the planet signifying the thief. Use Lord 7 as a matter of course and we are left with no identification except ‘the thief … is the thief’.

### ✸“为什么我们不直接用 7 宫主作为小偷的征象星？”因为这样做排除了在大

多数情况下我们唯一能提供的有效识别信息。除非嫌疑人名单很短，否则对小偷 的体貌描述是无用的。但我们能做的有价值的事是，根据代表小偷的行星的宫位 守护关系，来确认或排除小偷是建筑工人、邻居或女友的兄弟。若惯常使用 7 宫主，我们就只剩下“小偷…就是小偷”这种无法识别的描述。

The idea of prioritising a peregrine planet is that this is not some deep-dyed villain who would spend weeks planning the big heist (planet in detriment or fall), but the one without moral compass who will gladly pick your purse if you leave it on a table. But this reading of essential dignity falls short in this context. The planet in exaltation could in this context show one who thinks himself so wonderful that the property rights of mere mortals need not concern him. 优先考虑游离行星的理念在于，小偷并非那种花费数周策划大案的穷凶极恶之徒 （行星落陷或弱势），而是没有道德准则、只要你把钱包留在桌上就会乐于顺手 牵羊的人。但先天尊贵的这种解读在此语境下并不充分。在此语境中，处于旺势 的行星可能显示一个自视甚高、认为凡人的财产权无需在意的人。

But that he suspect is not a paragon of virtue does not prove that he was the thief. Remembering that the chart is a reflection of reality, we must dismiss this. While, on the principle of the role not the actor, we certainly cannot blame everything on Mercury! Who stole it? The one whose fingerprints are on it. Which, in terms of the chart, is the planet that is in separating aspect with the significator of the object, or is in exact aspect with it now. That, and only that, is the one we must bring in for questioning. 但嫌疑人并非道德楷模，并不能证明他就是小偷。牢记星盘是现实的反映，我们 必须摒弃这种推断。根据“角色而非演员”的原则，我们当然不能把所有事都归 咎于水星！谁偷的？就是那个留下指纹的人。用星盘术语来说，就是与物品征象 星形成出相位，或正与之形成精确相位的行星。这个，且只有这个，才是我们必 须带来审问的对象。

Lilly unwittingly this in his example chart for theft in Christian Astrology (chapter LXIII). He takes Mercury as significator of the thief because it is the only peregrine planet in an angular house, and his identification was found to be true. But this was a lucky hit. What Lilly seems not to have noticed is that Lord 2, the querent’s stolen money, is exactly conjunct Mercury by antiscion: Mr Mercury has the loot. It is this

that identifies the thief.✷ Lilly 在《Christian Astrology》（第 63 章）的盗窃示例盘中无意间展示了这一点。 他用水星作为小偷的征象星，因为它是角宫中唯一的游离行星，并且他的指认被 证实为真。但这是一次幸运的猜中。Lilly 似乎没有注意到，2 宫主（问卜者被盗 的钱财）通过映点与水星精确合相：水星先生持有赃物。正是这一点指认了小偷。 ✷

### ✸If we know for sure that the object has been stolen, it will be signified by Lord 2;

we no longer have the option of Lord 4. We could prefer a planet that gives a very obvious description of the object, but that would be rare: if in doubt, use Lord 2. Unless the thing stolen is animate, in which case use Lore 6 or 12, as usual.

### ✸若确知物品已被盗，它将由 2 宫主征象；我们不再有选择 4 宫主的余地。我

们也可以优先选用能极其明显描述该物品的行星，但这种情况很少见：如有疑问， 使用 2 宫主。除非被盗物有生命，此时如常使用 6 宫主或 12 宫主。

“But if I’ve lent money to someone, that money is no longer seen as my possession, but as the other person’s. As such it is signified by that person’s 2nd house, not by mine. The stolen object is definitely not my possession right now. Why, then, do we still use my 2nd house to signify it?” Because not doing so would, is most cases, remove all usefulness from the judgement. We don’t know who stole it: this is why the question is asked. So whose 2nd house to use? The only option would be to use the 2nd from the 7th: the possessions of the thief. Which means Lord 7 signifies the thief. ‘So who is the thief?’ ‘Ah, it’s the thief?’ This is not helpful. Retaining the querent’s 2nd as the object allows us to rule suspects in or out, according to whose significator has been in contact with Lord 2: ‘No, it wasn’t the builder; but has your ex been to visit recently?’ Different scripts for different situations.✷ “但如果我借钱给某人，那笔钱不再被视为我的财产，而是对方的。因此它应由 该人的 2 宫表示，而非我的。被盗物品此刻显然已非我所有。那么，为何我们仍 用我的 2 宫来征象它？”因为不这样做，在大多数情况下将使判断完全失效。我 们不知道谁偷了它：这正是提问的原因。那么该用谁的 2 宫？唯一的选择是使用 7 之 2 宫：小偷的财产。这意味着 7 宫主代表小偷。“那么小偷是谁？”“啊， 就是小偷？”这并无帮助。保留问卜者的 2 宫作为物品征象，使我们能够根据谁 的征象星曾与 2 宫主接触来排除或纳入嫌疑人：“不，不是建筑工人；但你前任 近期是否来访？”不同情境，不同剧本。✷

### ✸Do be cautious when judging questions on theft. While there can be great value in

such judgements, what has once been said can never be unsaid, so think very carefully before making accusations. Lilly’s words have the wisdom of long experience: Unless for a very friend, I hate thievish question, the which usually bring scandal to the artist, few men believing the person of the thief can be described by any lawful art, as also many times the party is mistaken, one man being accused for another, and so much

mischief comes thereon. For if the artist describe a person anything near to the shape of the party they mistrust, they build confidently on the judgement, let us do what we can to contradict them. I have known the judicious to have benefitted themselves very mch by our judgement, and to have recovered beyond expectation, etc. And so on the contrary. (Englands Propheticall Merline, p 133.)✷

### ✸判断盗窃问题时务必谨慎。虽然此类判断可能极具价值，但话一旦说出便无

法收回，因此在提出指控前需深思熟虑。Lilly 的话语凝聚了长期经验的智慧： “除非为至交好友，我厌恶盗窃类问题，此类问题常给占星师带来丑闻，鲜有人 相信小偷其人能通过任何合法技艺描述出来，且当事人常被误认，一人被错怪为 另一人，由此滋生诸多祸端。因若占星师描绘的人物形貌与对方所疑之人略有相 似，他们便对判断深信不疑，任凭我们如何反驳也无济于事。我知明智者曾藉我 等判断获益良多，并意外追回失物等。反之亦然。”（Englands Propheticall Merline, p 133.）✷

Where is my shawl? 我的披肩在哪里？

The querent, an elderly woman, had been wearing an antique, black shawl, which she had hung up somewhere, but she couldn’t remember where. Lord 2 or Lord 4? Saturn, Lord 4, well describes something black and antique. 问卜者是一位老妇人，她曾披着一条古董黑色披肩，并将其挂在了某处，但记不 起具体位置了。用 2 宫主还是 4 宫主？土星作为 4 宫主，恰好能描述某物是黑色 且为古董。

Where is my shawl? September 29th 1996, 9.22 am BST, London. 我的披肩在哪里？ 1996年 9月 29日上午 9:22（英国夏令时），伦敦。

Where is Saturn? In the 5th. So the shawl is in a place of recreation. If the querent’s children were possible suspects, the obvious suggestion here would be ‘blame the kids’, but they were not. 土星在哪里？在 5 宫。所以披肩在一个玩乐消遣的场所。如果问卜者的孩子是可 能的嫌疑人，这里明显的暗示会是“怪孩子们”，但事实并非如此。

Describe the place of recreation. Saturn is in a fire sign, so a fiery place of recreation. A restaurant would fit. 描述一下这个玩乐消遣的场所。土星在火象星座，所以是一个“火热”的玩乐场 所。一家餐厅很符合。

OK – let’s say it is in a restaurant. There may be other options, but this seems reasonable, so we can pick it up, run with it and see where it gets us. We now need to describe/locate the restaurant. So we go one step deeper into the chart. Saturn is the shawl. Its being in Aries has told us it is in a restaurant, so the ruler of Aries is that restaurant. 好的——假设它在餐厅里。可能还有其他选项，但这看起来很合理，所以我们可 以抓住这条线索，继续深入，看看能发现什么。现在我们需要描述/定位这家餐 厅。因此，我们需要更深一步分析星盘。土星是披肩。它在白羊座告诉我们披肩

在餐厅里，所以白羊座的守护星就代表那家餐厅。

Mars is exactly on the MC. On a angle: close to home. Within one degree of an angle: very close to home. We might have taken the 10th as a workplace, and judged that the restaurant was very close to the workplace, but the querent was retired. 火星精确位于中天。在角宫：离家很近。与四轴点相差不到 1 度：非常近。我们 本可能将 10 宫视为工作场所，并判断餐厅离工作场所非常近，但问卜者已退休。

Aries has told us it is in a restaurant. The planet ruling Aries shows us where this restaurant is. It does this by its placement – as if the restaurant itself were the lost object. The sign this planet is in will describe the restaurant. If Mars were in Capricorn, an Indian restaurant; in Cancer, a Chinese; in Leo, French or Italian. 白羊座告诉我们它在餐厅里。守护白羊座的行星则告诉我们这家餐厅在哪里。这 是通过它自身的位置来显示的——仿佛餐厅本身就是丢失的物品。该行星所在的 星座将描述这家餐厅。如果火星在摩羯座，可能是印度餐厅；在巨蟹座，中式餐 厅；在狮子座，法式或意式餐厅。

The shawl is in a French or Italian restaurant very close to the querent’s home. ‘Oh yes – there’s a French restaurant just next door. I was there the other night.’ And that is where the shawl was found. 披肩就在离问卜者家很近的一家法式或意式餐厅里。“哦，对了——隔壁就有一 家法式餐厅。我前几天晚上还在那里。”披肩正是在那里找到的。

Note here a clear example of a general principle in all traditional astrology: Planets are, signs describe. Planets are nouns, signs are adjectives. 这里请注意一个贯穿所有传统占星学的通用原则的清晰示例：行星是实体，星座 是描述。行星是名词，星座是形容词。

Important point: here, we have taken successive steps deeper into the chart. Suppose the situation were different. Suppose Mars were itself significator of the lost object and the querent worked in an office. Mars is in the 10th: she’s left it at work. Where at work? Mars is right on the cusp: near the door. Mars is in a fire sign: is there a heater near the door? Or maybe right by the wall. 重要一点：在这里，我们逐步深入地分析了星盘。假设情境不同。假设火星本身 就是失物的征象星，而问卜者在办公室工作。火星在 10 宫：她把东西忘在了工 作地点。工作地点的哪里？火星正好在宫头：靠近门边。火星在火象星座：门边 有取暖器吗？或者可能就在墙边。

“What’s the difference?” If the significator tells us the object is in a specific place, we don’t need to locate the place. So we can take other indictions as showing its location within that place. But Saturn in the shawl chart showed us only that the shawl was in some place of recreation. This gives us a range of possible locations, so we must choose one out of this range – we are still looking for the specific place. Look at the cat chart again. The cat is in the cat’s house. There is only one cat’s house relevant to

the question: we need look no further. Had Mars been the object in this chart, showing it to be in the office: there is only one office, so we don’t need to look further. Out of the broad span of ‘places of recreation’ we must choose one, so we do need to define the range as is shown above. “这有什么区别？”如果征象星告诉我们物品在一个具体的地点，我们就不需要 再定位这个地点本身。因此，我们可以将其他指示视为显示物品在该地点内的具 体位置。但在披肩案例的星盘中，土星仅仅告诉我们披肩在某个玩乐消遣的场所。 这给了我们一系列可能的地点，所以我们必须从中选择一个——我们仍在寻找具 体的地点。再看一下猫咪案例的星盘。猫在猫的房子里。与问题相关的猫的房子 只有一个：我们无需再进一步寻找。如果在这个星盘中火星是失物的征象星，显 示它在办公室：办公室只有一个，所以我们无需再进一步寻找。而从“玩乐消遣 场所”这个宽泛的范围中，我们必须选出一个，因此我们确实需要像上面那样去 界定这个范围。

We’ve taken the sign Saturn is in to describe the kind of place of recreation: it’s in a fire sign, so it’s a fiery kind of place, such as a place where things get cooked. Suppose Saturn had been in an air sign. We can’t be overly literal about this: a hot-air balloon is an airy place of recreation; more likely would be a cinema or theatre, a café, where people meet to talk, maybe a chess club. Air is the mental faculty, so could describe anything that engages that. Similarly, a watery place of recreation could be a swimming-pool, but is more likely to be a pub. Take this as a general rule: be flexible. 我们利用土星所在的星座来描述玩乐场所的类型：它在火象星座，所以是那种" 火热"的场所，例如烹饪食物的地方。假设土星在风象星座。我们不能过于字面 理解：热气球是一个"通风"的玩乐场所；更可能的是电影院或剧院、咖啡馆、人 们见面聊天的地方，也许是棋类俱乐部。风象关联心智能力，因此可以描述任何 涉及心智活动的事物。同样，水象的玩乐场所可能是游泳池，但更可能是酒吧。 请将此作为通则：保持灵活。

MONEY 钱财

Although the 2nd is the house of money, when people ask about money it is not usually the 2nd that is of chief concern. They are asking not about their own money, but about someone else’s money that they would like to have. Where we find this other money in the chart depends upon the context of the question. Who’s money is it? 尽管 2 宫是钱财之宫，但当人们询问钱财时，通常主要关切的并非 2 宫。他们询 问的往往不是自己的钱财，而是他们希望获得的他人钱财。我们在星盘中何处找 到这笔他人钱财，取决于问题的具体语境。这是谁的钱？

It is usually either 8th house or 11th house. 8th, being 2nd from the 7th, is the money of spouses, business partners, clients, enemies and ‘any old person’. The 11th, being

2nd from the 10th, is the money of the job, of the boss, or of the king. It is also ‘pennies from Heaven’. SO: 通常它要么是 8 宫，要么是 11 宫。8 宫作为 7 之 2 宫，是配偶、商业伙伴、客 户、敌人及“任何普通人”的钱财。11 宫作为 10 之 2 宫，是工作、老板或国王 的钱财。它也指“天上掉下的馅饼”。因此：

* ‘When will I get my wages?’ 11th house
* “我什么时候能拿到工资？” —— 11 宫

* ‘Will this job pay well?’ 11th house
* “这份工作报酬好吗？” —— 11 宫

* ‘Will I get a tax rebate?’ 11th house
* “我能拿到退税吗？” —— 11 宫

* ‘When will this client pay me?’ 8th house
* “这位客户什么时候会付钱给我？” —— 8 宫

* ‘Will I win on the horses tonight?’ 8th house
* “今晚赛马我能赢钱吗？” —— 8 宫

* ‘Has my sweetheart got any money?’ 8th house
* “我的心上人有钱吗？” —— 8 宫

* ‘Will I win the lottery?’11th house
* “我能中彩票吗？” —— 11 宫

And: 以及：

* ‘Can I earn a living from astrology?’ 10th house (see chapter 22)
* “我能靠占星学谋生吗？” —— 10 宫（见第 22 章）

* ‘Will I inherit Dad’s cash?’ 5th house
* “我能继承父亲的财产吗？” —— 5 宫

* ‘Will I profit by buying this house?’ 5th house (see chapter 18)
* “买这所房子我能获利吗？” —— 5 宫（见第 18 章）

Let us pick out way through this maze, one step at a time. 让我们一步一步理清这个迷宫。

Stocks and shares

股票与证券

This is the most straightforward, so we’ll dispose of this one first. There is a myth that stocks, bonds and shares are 8th house matters, as ‘other people’s money’. They are not: your stocks are your own money (2nd house) in a different form. When you buy stock your money no more becomes someone else’s than it does when you change your cash into a foreign currency. It remains your money, which may increase or diminish in value. 这是最直接的情况，所以我们先处理它。有一个误解认为股票、债券和股份是 8 宫事务，因其属于“他人钱财”。事实并非如此：你的股票是你自己钱财（2 宫） 的另一种形式。当你购买股票时，你的钱并不会比你将现金换成外币时更变成他 人的钱。它仍然是你的钱，只是价值可能增减。

So questions about investments should be judged from the state of the 2nd house and the condition and actions of Lord 2. Change of sign is often crucial here. ‘Should I switch my savings from A to B?’ Lord 2 is leaving a fertile sign and entering a barren: ‘No, your savings won’t grow’. Lord 2 leaving a sign where it is peregrine and entering one where it is dignified: ‘Yes, your savings will benefit’. 因此，关于投资的问题应根据 2 宫的状态以及 2 宫主的状况和行动来判断。换星 座在这里常常是关键。“我是否应该将储蓄从 A 转到 B？”2 宫主正离开一个肥 沃的星座并进入一个贫瘠的星座：“不，你的储蓄不会增长。”2 宫主离开一个 它处于游离状态的星座，进入一个它得吉的星座：“是的，你的储蓄将受益。”

As a general rule, where Lord 2 is going shows the future if the change is made. So Lord 2 applying to the South Node is testimony not to change; applying to the North Node is testimony for change. But be prepared to be flexible if the chart suggests otherwise. For example, suppose that Lord 2 is near the end of a sign when it hits the South Node, and that in the next sign it will be dignified. We can take its meeting with the South Node in the present sign as what will happen if the situation stays as it is, and its movement into the next sign as the prospective change. In this example the querent would benefit by changing: stay put and his money will suffer (Lord 2 conjunct South Node). The chart has given us an overriding indicator of change in the change of sign. 一般来说，2 宫主正前往之处显示了如果做出改变后的未来。因此，2 宫主正入 相位南交点，是反对改变的征象；入相位北交点，则是支持改变的征象。但如果 星盘有相反暗示，需准备好灵活处理。例如，假设 2 宫主在即将遇到南交点时已 接近一个星座的末端，而在下一个星座它将得吉。我们可以将其在当前星座与南 交点的会合视为维持现状将发生的事，而它进入下一个星座则视为预期的改变。 在此例中，问卜者将通过改变而受益：保持不动，他的钱财将受损（2 宫主合相 南交点）。星盘已通过换星座给了我们一个压倒性的改变指示。

If the querent is asking about a specific commodity, it is worth looking at the natural ruler of that commodity. ‘I’m thinking of selling gold and buying dotcom shares’, with the Sun (gold) about to conjunct Saturn and Mercury (computers) about to enter

Virgo: ‘Buy the dotcoms!’ Be careful, though: this applies only to specific horaries; it does not mean that every time the Sun conjuncts Saturn the price of gold falls! 如果问卜者询问的是特定商品，则值得查看该商品的先天守护星。“我考虑卖出 黄金，买入网络公司的股票”，若太阳（黄金）即将合相土星，而水星（电脑） 即将进入处女座：“买入网络公司股票！”但要小心：这仅适用于具体的卜卦问 题；并不意味着每次太阳合相土星时金价都会下跌！

If your querent is thinking of cornering the market in cucumbers or some other product, you can also look at the Arabian Part for that commodity, considering both the Part and its dispositor. 如果你的问卜者考虑垄断黄瓜或某些其他产品的市场，你也可以查看该商品的阿 拉伯点，同时考虑该点及其定位星。

Getting paid or repaid 获取报酬或偿还债务

We need to be clear about where the money is coming from. This is usually obvious enough: if you work for a company, your wages are shown by the 2nd from the 10th, which is the 11th. But sometimes it is necessary to think about the nature of the working relationship. Is it an employee/boss relationship, or is it a client relationship? For example, if you decide to work as an astrologer, the person who comes to you for a consultation is your client: 7th house. For ‘Will he pay me?’ you would look at the 8th to show his money. This is also the case if your client is a company. If the company takes you onto its payroll, as its in-house astrologer, however, your wages are 11th house. So also for any freelance work you might do for AstroCharts Inc. Your general question, ‘Can I make a living from astrology?’ concerns the 10th house, because it is the 2nd from the 9th and as such shows profit from your knowledge (chapter 22). Do not use that approach in any enquiry about a particular payment. 我们必须清楚钱财从何而来。这通常足够明显：如果你为一家公司工作，你的工 资由 10 之 2 宫即 11 宫表示。但有时需要考虑工作关系的性质。是雇员/老板关 系，还是客户关系？例如，如果你决定以占星师为业，前来咨询的人是你的客户： 7 宫。对于“他会付钱给我吗？”你需要查看 8 宫以代表他的钱财。即使你的客 户是一家公司，也是如此。然而，如果公司把你纳入其工资单，作为其内部占星 师，那么你的工资就是 11 宫事务。同样适用于你可能为 Astro Charts 公司做的任 何自由职业工作。你的一般性问题“我能靠占星学谋生吗？”则关乎 10 宫，因 为它是 9 之 2 宫，因此代表从你的知识中获利（第 22 章）。不要在关于特定付 款的任何询问中使用这种方法。

If the question concerns the amount of the payment, look at the ruler of the house that shows the money, considering its essential and accidental dignities. The stronger the planet, the greater the amount. Look also at afflictions or benefits to the house in question: for example, strong Juptier on its cusp is good news; weak Saturn is not. 如果问题涉及付款金额，查看代表钱财宫位的守护星，同时考虑其先天尊贵与偶

然尊贵。行星越强，金额越大。同时观察相关宫位所受的侵害或吉助：例如，强 旺的木星位于其宫头是好消息；衰弱的土星则不是。

NB: in any question concerning only the amount of money, we do not need an aspect. But if there is one, we must consider its nature. The idea of profit assumes that it is coming to us: it wouldn’t be profit otherwise. So also with wages. Suppose Lord 11 is strong, and applies to Lord 1 by square: ‘The wages are good, but there may be delays in your getting them, or you may have to press for them’. 注意：在任何仅关乎金额的问题中，我们不需要相位。但如果存在相位，我们 必须考虑其属性。获利的概念假定钱财正流向我们：否则就不叫获利。工资同理。 假设 11 宫主强旺，并以刑相位入相位 1 宫主：“工资不错，但你拿到它们可能 会有延迟，或者你可能需要催促才能拿到。”

More often, such questions are less about the amount involved and more about the ‘when’ or ‘if’ of its arrival. Here we do need an aspect: no aspect, no arrival. Look for an aspect between the significator of the money and either the querent (Lord 1 or Moon) or Lord 2. The 2nd can be taken as the querent’s pocket or bank-account, so an aspect from the money to Lord 2 shows it arriving in the querent’s pocket. 更常见的是，这类问题较少涉及具体金额，而更多关乎钱财“何时”或“是否” 会到账。这里我们确实需要相位：无相位，则无到账。寻找钱财的征象星与问卜 者（1 宫主或月亮）或 2 宫主之间的相位。2 宫可视为问卜者的口袋或银行账户， 因此钱财与 2 宫主之间的相位显示钱财进入问卜者的口袋。

If you have lent money to someone, it is now that person’s money. If you ask, ‘Will he pay me back?’ it is that person’s 2nd house that is of interest (so 2nd from the 3rd if I lent it to my brother; 2nd from the 11th if I lent it to my friend). Look for an aspect between the ruler of that house and either Lord 1, the Moon or Lord 2. If there is no aspect showing repayment, a favourable aspect between the person’s own significator and the querent’s can show an agreement being reached. Watch out for severe afflictions to the significator of the person’s money: you won’t be paid, because he has no money. No matter how strong it might be, the significator inside its own house is aslo bad news: he may have plenty of money, but it is staying in his pocket. 如果你借钱给某人，那笔钱现在属于那个人。如果你问"他会还钱给我吗？"，那 么令人感兴趣的是那个人的 2 宫（例如，如果我借给我兄弟，就是 3 之 2 宫；如 果我借给我朋友，就是 11 之 2 宫）。寻找该宫守护星与 1 宫主、月亮或 2 宫主 之间的相位。如果没有显示还款的相位，那个人自身的征象星与问卜者征象星之 间的吉相位可以显示达成协议。警惕代表那人钱财的征象星受到严重侵害：你将 得不到付款，因为他没有钱。无论它可能多强旺，征象星位于其自身宫位内也是 坏消息：他可能有很多钱，但钱会留在他的口袋里。

Gambling 赌博

I once sent an article to an American astrology magazine, including judgement on a horary ‘Will I win on the horses today?’ I received a heated letter in reply, berating me for my foolishness in even considering such a question, because it is impossible to know whether someone has won or not. As astrologers are beings far above vulgar concepts of profit and loss, I should explain that if you end up with more money than you started with, you have won; if you end up with less, you have lost. 我曾给一家美国占星杂志寄过一篇文章，其中包括对卜卦“我今天赛马能赢吗？” 的判断。我收到了一封言辞激烈的回信，斥责我考虑这样的问题十分愚蠢，因为 不可能知道某人是否赢了。由于占星师是远高于庸俗盈亏概念的存在，我应该解 释一下：如果你最终的钱比开始时多，你就赢了；如果你最终的钱变少了，你就 输了。

Gambling is often regarded as a 5th-house activity. But if someone is asking a question about gambling, the point at issue is the profit to be made; I have never been asked ‘Will I have a good time at the racecourse?’ Having a good time is a 5th-house matter; turning a profit is not. 赌博常被视为 5 宫活动。但如果某人询问关于赌博的问题，争议点在于能否获利； 我从未被问过“我在赛马场会玩得开心吗？”玩得开心是 5 宫事务；获利则不是。

The bet is a contest between you and the bookmaker, so he is your enemy (7th house) and his money is his 2nd, which is the radical 8th. It is his money that you want, so success will be shown by an aspect between Lord 8 and either Lord 1, the Moon (assuming the Moon does not signify either the bookie or his money), or Lord 2. Again, it doesn’t matter which planet applies to which. 赌注是你和庄家之间的竞赛，因此他是你的敌人（7 宫），他的钱财是他的 2 宫， 即基准盘 8 宫。你想要的是他的钱，因此成功将体现为 8 宫主与 1 宫主、月亮（假 设月亮不代表庄家或其钱财）或 2 宫主之间的相位。同样，哪颗行星入相位哪颗 并不重要。

Provided there is such an aspect, the strength of Lord 8 will show how much the querent will win, relative to his stake. This can help decide on the bet. Suppose the querent has decided to back a certain team. The bookie might offer a range of bets on that team’s victory, each at different odds. If Lord 8 is strong, showing a good win, the querent can take the more adventurous bet at longer odds. If Lord 8 is weak, he should stick to the safer, short-odds option. 只要存在这样的相位，8 宫主的强度将显示问卜者相对于其赌注能赢多少。这有 助于决定如何下注。假设问卜者已决定支持某支队伍。庄家可能就该队伍的胜利 提供一系列不同赔率的投注选项。如果 8 宫主强旺，显示能大赢，问卜者可以选 择赔率更高、更冒险的投注。如果 8 宫主衰弱，他应该坚持更安全、赔率较低的 选项。

With such question – and with those about investments – the querent should be persuaded to do his homework first. The chart will be more reliable if he has

expended some effort in selecting the proposed bets. 对于此类问题——以及关于投资的问题——应说服问卜者先做好功课。如果他付 出了一些努力来选择拟投注的对象，星盘判断会更可靠。

Lotteries are not a contest. At least, they are a contest only if the querent has developed a scheme to outwit the lottery company: then it becomes ‘us against them’ and should be judged from the 8th house, as above. Lotteries are seen as the querent holding out his hands to see if good fortune will fall into them: pennies from Heaven. As such, they are judged from the 11th house: does Lord 11 aspect the querent or his pocket? If the querent is asking only about a jackpot win, Lord 11 would have to be exceptionally strong to allow a ‘Yes’. 彩票不是竞赛。至少，只有当问卜者制定出智胜彩票公司的计划时，它才是竞赛： 那样就变成了“我们对阵他们”，应如上所述从 8 宫判断。彩票被视为问卜者伸 出手看好运是否会落入手中：天上掉下的馅饼。因此，从 11 宫判断：11 宫主是 否与问卜者或其口袋形成相位？如果问卜者只询问是否赢得头奖，11 宫主必须 异常强旺才能给出“是”的判断。

If the querent is asking about winning prize-money with his own horse, look to the horse’s 2nd (profit from the horse). The horse is 12th house, so its 2nd is the radical 1st. Ignore the querent for a moment, giving Lord 1 to the profit from the horse. Ideally, it would be a strong benefic, benefitting either the 1st or 2nd house (1st now seen as the querent) by placement. Otherwise, an aspect between Lord 1 and either the Moon or Lord 2 will show a profit. 如果问卜者询问用自己的马赢得奖金，查看马的 2 宫（从马获利）。马是 12 宫， 所以它的 2 宫是基准盘 1 宫。暂时忽略问卜者，将 1 宫主赋予从马获利。理想情 况下，它应是一颗强吉星，通过其位置吉助 1 宫或 2 宫（1 宫现在视为问卜者）。 否则，1 宫主与月亮或 2 宫主之间的相位将显示获利。

I once asked a horary about a bet on a football match. The chart showed Lord 2 applying to Lord 1 by opposition. This made no sense. How could my money come to me? Either my money would disappear or the bookie’s money would come to me. Consumed with curiosity, I placed the bet. The match was abandoned at half-time and all bets refunded. My money did come to me – by opposition, as I had the nuisance of having to make the journey to collect it. 我曾就一场足球赛的投注提问卜卦。星盘显示 2 宫主以对冲相位入相位 1 宫主。 这说不通。我的钱怎么可能来到我这里？要么我的钱会消失，要么庄家的钱会来 到我这里。在好奇心的驱使下，我下了注。比赛在半场时取消，所有投注退款。 我的钱确实回到了我这里——通过对冲相位，正如我必须费事跑一趟去取回钱所 显示的那样。

### ✸ Horaries on this subject are discussed in much greater detail in my Sports

Astrology.✷

### ✸关于此主题的卜卦在我的《Sports Astrology》中有更详细的讨论。✷

The partner’s money 伴侣的钱财

A favourite question in Lilly’s day was ‘Has my prospective spouse got any money, and can I get my hands on it?’ The spouse’s money is shown by the 8th house. To find how much money there is, look at the condition of Lord 8 and any afflictions or benefits to the 8th house. To see if the querent will get the cash, look for an aspect to Lord 1, the Moon or Lord 2. Judge aspects according to their nature: e.g. by trine it comes easily, by opposition it comes with such effort that it isn’t worth the fight. Lilly 时代一个备受青睐的问题是：“我未来的伴侣有钱吗，我能拿到这笔钱吗？” 伴侣的钱财由 8 宫表示。要了解有多少钱，观察 8 宫主的状况以及 8 宫所受的任 何侵害或吉助。要查看问卜者能否拿到现金，则寻找 8 宫主与 1 宫主、月亮或 2 宫主之间的相位。根据相位的性质判断：例如，通过拱相位轻松获得，通过对冲 相位则需费力争取以至于得不偿失。

Example: suppose Lord 1 is in the exaltation of Lord 8. Querent thinks there is lots of money, and badly wants it. Suppose Lord 8 is in its detriment. There is little money. Querent makes a trine to Lord 8. There may not be much money, but the querent is welcome to what there is. 示例：假设 1 宫主位于 8 宫主的旺势位置。问卜者认为有很多钱，并且非常想得 到。假设 8 宫主处于落陷状态。钱很少。问卜者与 8 宫主形成拱相位。钱可能不 多，但问卜者可以随意取用现有的部分。

This can be an important consideration when weighing up prospective business partners. 在评估未来商业伙伴时，这可能是一个重要的考量因素。

The government’s money 政府的钱财

If the querent is asking about a tax rebate, pension, social security or any other payment from the government, the money is shown by Lord 11 (2nd from the 10th: the government’s money). Look for an aspect to the querent or Lord 2 to show receipt; the strength of Lord 11 and the 11th house to show how much. 如果问卜者询问退税、养老金、社会保障或任何其他来自政府的付款，这笔钱财 由 11 宫主（10 之 2 宫：政府的钱财）表示。寻找与问卜者或 2 宫主的相位以显 示收款；根据 11 宫主和 11 宫的强度判断金额大小。

The 11th also shows ‘the gift of the king’: whatever favour we require from the

person in power. For a social security payment to which the person is entitled, the receptions of Lord 10 (the government) can be ignored: the process does not depend on who likes whom. But for e.g. ‘Will I get the Arts Council grant?’ the attitude of the awarding body (Lord 10) is important. Ideally, we would hope to find its significator exalting our querent. Kings are busy people, and so may not have time to exalt everyone who qualifies for their gift, but negative reception (by detriment or fall) would be unpromising. The more unique the gift (the Victoria Cross or just a campaign medal?) the stronger the reception that we would expect to see. 11 宫也代表“国王的赏赐”：即我们当权者那里所求的任何恩惠。对于个人有 权获得的社会保障付款，10 宫主（政府）的接纳关系可以忽略：该流程不取决 于谁喜欢谁。但对于例如“我能获得艺术委员会资助吗？”这类问题，授予机构 （10 宫主）的态度就很重要。理想情况下，我们希望发现其征象星位于我们的 问卜者旺势位置。国王们日理万机，可能无暇垂青每一位有资格获得其赏赐的人， 但负面的接纳关系（通过落陷或弱势）则前景不妙。赏赐越独特（是维多利亚十 字勋章还是普通的战役纪念章？），我们预期看到的接纳关系就应越强。

Example on making money 关于赚钱的示例

Using techniques other than horary, I had made an astrological assessment of a sports match. I was tempted to bet on my choice of victor, so asked the question, ‘Will I win by backing X?’ 我使用了卜卦以外的占星技术，对一场体育赛事进行了评估。我忍不住想为自己 选择的胜者下注，于是提问：“押注 X 能赢吗？”

Should I buy silver? October 31st 1997, 12.36 pm GMT, London. 我应该买白银吗？ 1997年 10月 31日，中午 12:36（格林尼治标准时间），伦敦。

The bookie’s money, which I hope to win, is Lord 8: Mercury. Is there an applying aspect between Mercury and Lord 1 (Saturn)? No. 我希望赢得的庄家的钱财是 8 宫主：水星。水星和 1 宫主（土星）之间有入相位 吗？没有。

Is there an applying aspect between Mercury and Lord 2 (Jupiter)? No, although the Moon does aspect first Jupiter, then Mercury, so translating light from Jupiter to Mercury. 水星和 2 宫主（木星）之间有入相位吗？没有，尽管月亮确实先与木星、后与水 星形成相位，因此将光线从木星传递给水星。

Note also that Mercury and Jupiter are very close by antiscion (antiscion of Mercury at 10.55 Aquarius; of Jupiter at 17.01 Scorpio). But each planet is separating from the antiscion of the other. 还需注意，水星和木星通过映点非常接近（水星的映点在宝瓶座 10.55 度；木星 的映点在天蝎座 17.01 度）。但每颗行星正与另一颗的映点形成出相位。

So: there are two positive testimonies. First, the Moon goes to Mercury, and, because aspects often don’t prohibit conjunctions, that will bring me and the money together. Second, the Moon picks up Jupiter (my money) and carries it to Mercury (the money I want). 那么：有两个积极的征象。第一，月亮走向水星，并且因为相位通常不阻止合相， 这会将我和钱财联系在一起。第二，月亮接上木星（我的钱）并将其带给水星（我 想要的钱）。

This looks promising. BUT: both these testimonies depend on the Moon, and the Moon is combust. It has no power to act. Insofar as it is possible to be weaker than totally destroyed, the Moon combust is weaker than any other planet combust, because the Moon’s power to act is always dependent upon its having light, and when conjunct the Sun it has none. 这看起来很有希望。但是：这两个征象都依赖于月亮，而月亮正处于燃烧状态。 它没有行动力。就“比彻底毁灭更弱”的程度而言，燃烧的月亮比其他任何燃烧 的行星都弱，因为月亮的行动力始终依赖于其拥有光线，而当它合相太阳时，它 没有任何光线。

Will I win? No. The extreme weakness of the Moon cannot make the positive testimonies work. 我会赢吗？不会。月亮的极端虚弱无法使积极的征象生效。

Such a judgement was, and will be for you, given a little practice, the matter of a few moments: a quick glance around the chart. I still had this chart on my computer screen

when a client phoned. He was a regular client, asking simple questions directly, so no significant time elapsed between my setting my own chart and my hearing his question. The chart was the same. 这样的判断，过去是，将来也会是，对于经过一点练习的你来说，只是片刻之事： 快速扫视星盘即可。当一位客户来电时，这张星盘仍显示在我的电脑屏幕上。他 是一位常客，直接询问简单问题，因此在我设置自己的星盘和听到他的问题之间， 没有耗费太多时间。星盘是同一张。

His question was, ‘Should I buy silver?’ We can judge such question by looking at Lord 2, construing the question as ‘Should I convert my money into silver?’ But the word ‘silver’ directs our attention to the Moon. 他的问题是：“我应该买白银吗？”我们可以通过观察 2 宫主来判断此类问题， 将问题理解为“我应该把我的钱换成白银吗？”但“白银”这个词将我们的注意 力引向月亮。

How is the Moon? Yuk! It is in the sign of its fall; it is combust, so close to the Sun that it has no light. It could hardly be weaker. 月亮状况如何？糟透了！它在其弱势星座；它处于燃烧状态，如此接近太阳以至 于没有光线。它几乎不能再弱了。

The Moon is silver; so is this a good time to buy silver? Yes! It is so weak that it cannot get weaker: this is, at the very least, a no-lose bet. 月亮代表白银；那么现在是购买白银的好时机吗？是的！它如此虚弱，以至于不 可能变得更弱：这至少是一笔不会亏损的买卖。

That the Moon is beginning to separate from the Sun is important. Though it has almost no light, it is starting its upward swing, beginning to pick up light. 月亮正开始与太阳出相位这一点很重要。虽然它几乎没有光线，但它正开始向上 运行，开始获取光线。

This testimony is sufficient for judgement. It is confirmed by Lord 2, which is heading towards Pisces, its own sign. 这个征象足以做出判断。2 宫主正移入其双鱼座，亦印证此判断。

‘Yes, buy silver.’ The price of silver increased dramatically in the months that followed. “是的，买入白银。”在随后的几个月里，白银价格大幅上涨。

This chart is of particular interest as it shows two questions which are overtly the same – ‘Will I make a profit?’ – judged from the same chart, yet giving opposing answer. For all its simplicity, the method is unendingly subtle. 这张星盘特别有趣，因为它展示了两个表面相同——“我会获利吗？”——却根 据同一张星盘判断给出了相反答案的问题。尽管方法简单，但其精妙之处无穷无 尽。

# Third House Questions

# 3 宫的问题

TRUE OR FALSE? 真实或欺骗？

Is this information, gossip, rumour true? 此信息、闲言、谣传是真的吗？

We are looking here for testimonies that it is true. If we have few or none of these, it will, by default, be false. A void of course Moon indicates that nothing will come of it, true or false. 我们在此寻找其为真的征象。如果此类征象极少或没有，则通常为假。空亡月亮 表明无论真假，都不会有结果。

To be true: 为真的条件：

* the angles of the chart should be in fixed signs
* 星盘的角宫应位于固定星座

* Lord 1, Lord 3, the Moon and the Moon’s dispositor should be in fixed signs and angular houses, or at least fixed signs and succedent houses.
* 1 宫主、3 宫主、月亮以及月亮的定位星应位于固定星座及角宫，或至少位于 固定星座及续宫。

Look at the condition of the third house: an affliction there (such as debilitated Saturn on the cusp) could show falsehood; but be cautious: it could also show that the querent will be harmed by this information. The context will usually make clear which is the more likely. 观察 3 宫的状况：若 3 宫受克（例如弱势的土星位于 3 宫头），可能表明为假； 但需谨慎：也可能表示问卜者将因此信息而受伤害。结合上下文通常能明确哪种 情况更可能。

With so many testimonies we will rarely get a unanimous verdict. A majority decision will do.

我们很少会得到完全一致的征象。多数证据即可做出判断。

Angularity and fixity both carry a sense of solidity, so what we are doing here is banging the information against the chart to see if it is real or illusion. 角宫和固定星座都带有实质、稳固的含义，因此我们在此所做的，是将信息对照 星盘进行检验，以判断它是真实的还是虚幻的。

### ✸I would now reject the idea that the signs the angles are in is of any significance.

In no other type of question do we take notice of whether the angles or relevant cusps are cardinal, fixed or mutable; there is no reason why we should make an exception here. 我个人现在倾向于否定“角宫所在星座具有重要性”这一观点。在其他任何类型 的问题中，我们都不会关注角宫或相关宫头位于基本、固定还是变动星座；没有 理由在此处例外。

Do note that to show truth the relevant planets need to be fixed and angular, not fixed or angular. I see no reason to involve the Moon’s dispositor in this; the idea of involving the Moon itself is, at the very least, highly dubious. One could argue for including Lord 1 as a check to see if the querent has any grasp of reality, but by far the most important testimony is that of Lord 3. ✷ 请注意，要证明为真，相关行星需要既位于固定星座又位于角宫，而非二者居其 一。我认为没有理由在此处牵涉月亮的定位星；牵涉月亮本身的观点至少是高度 可疑的。或许可以主张将 1 宫主纳入，以检查问卜者是否把握了现实，但迄今为 止最重要的征象是 3 宫主的状况。✷

Is this prediction or dream true? 此预测或梦境是真的吗？

Take the same testimonies as above, but look at the 9th house and Lord 9 instead of the 3rd and Lord 3. 采用上述相同的征象标准，但观察 9 宫和 9 宫主，而非 3 宫和 3 宫主。

Caution 注意

These questions are rare; keep them rare! You can say ‘Is it true that I will marry Jane?’ ‘Is it true that I will get the job?’ Fall into this trap and you will soon be judging every question as a 3rd house matter. You can fall into the same trap with the 11th, the house of hopes and wishes: ‘Will I get my wish of marrying Jane/getting the job?’ Always take the shortest route: what appears to be an ‘Is it true?’ question can usually be relocated. If the querent asks, ‘I’ve heard a rumour that my boyfriend is

two-timing me. Is it true?’ cut to the chase: this is a 7th house question about her boyfriend, not a 3rd house question about truth or falsehood. Even if you have had a dream about marrying your sweetheart, rather than asking ‘Is my dream true?’ ask ‘Will I marry her?’ 此类问题很罕见；请保持其罕见性！你可以问“我会和 Jane（简）结婚，这是真 的吗？”“我会得到这份工作，这是真的吗？”若陷入此思维陷阱，你很快就会 把每个问题都当作 3 宫事务来判断。对于代表希望和愿望的 11 宫，也可能陷入 同样的陷阱：“我希望能和 Jane 结婚/得到这份工作，这个愿望能实现吗？”始 终采用最直接的路径：看似“是否为真？”的问题通常可以重构。如果问卜者问： “我听到传言说我的男朋友对我不忠。这是真的吗？”请直指核心：这是一个关 于她男朋友的 7 宫问题，而非关于真伪的 3 宫问题。即使你做了一个与心上人结 婚的梦，与其问“我的梦是真的吗？”，不如问“我会和她结婚吗？”

Throughout my career I have not judged more than a handful of questions as ‘Is it true?’ The ones that come to mind are a querent who was hoping to claim the reward for finding a missing boy, asking if rumours of his whereabouts were accurate, and my own question about an unlikely prediction made by a media astrologer on a New Year’s Eve TV show. 在我的整个职业生涯中，我判断为“是否为真？”的问题屈指可数。能记起的例 子包括：一位问卜者希望领取寻找失踪男孩的赏金，询问关于男孩下落的谣言是 否准确；以及我自己关于一位媒体占星师在除夕电视节目中做出的一个看似不可 能的预测的提问。

Can I trust him? 我可以信任他吗？

Look at that person’s significator, chosen by house as usual. The more essential dignity it has, the more honourable he is. Fixity here is not necessarily a good thing: if his planet is in detriment and fixed he will be stubborn in his dishonesty. 按照常规通过宫位选择那个人的征象星。其先天尊贵越多，其人就越可信。此处 固定星座未必是好事：若其行星处于落陷且在固定星座，他将在其不诚实上顽固 不化。

Mercury is always tricky, even if dignified. Mercury is by nature amoral, so even if it is strong or another planet has plenty of essential dignity by being in a Mercury sign, it is likely to show someone who is honest only as long as it suits him. If in Gemini he may have a playful disregard for truth, a joy in sleight of hand; if in Virgo he will bring out the small print to prove that his dishonesty is honest after all, and more fool you for believing him. 水星即使拥有先天尊贵也总是难以捉摸。水星本质上是非道德的，因此即使它很 强旺，或其他行星因位于水星星座而拥有大量先天尊贵，它也往往显示出一个人 只在对其有利时才是诚实的。若在双子座，他可能玩世不恭地漠视真相，以诡计 为乐；若在处女座，他会搬出细则条款来证明他的不诚实终究是诚实的，而相信

他的你则是更大的傻瓜。

### ✸This question is usually too vague to be useful: I can trust a thief – to behave like

a thief. It is better rephrased in more concrete terms: ‘Will he have his fingers in the till if I leave him in charge of my shop?’ ‘Will he really support my application as he promised?’

### ✸这个问题通常过于模糊而无用：我可以信任一个小偷——会做出小偷的行为。

最好用更具体的措辞重新表述：“如果我让他负责我的店铺，他会监守自盗吗？” “他真的会如承诺那样支持我的申请吗？”

In principle the more essential dignity the significator has, the more honourable that person is. But be careful. If the planet is in its own sign or, especially, its own exaltation, the main priority of that person will be that person. That can be coupled with a contemptuous attitude towards other. ✷ 原则上，征象星的先天尊贵越多，那个人就越可信。但要小心。如果行星在其自 身星座或特别是其自身的旺势位置，那个人的首要优先事项将是其自身。这可能 伴随着对他人的蔑视态度。✷

LETTERS, PHONE-CALLS, VISITORS 信件、电话、访客

The radical 3rd is rarely of relevance here. If the question were, ‘Did she get my letter?’ we could look for a separating aspect (showing something that has already happened) between her and Lord 3, the letter. Lord 3 in either her 1st or her 2nd house would be testimony of its arrival: the letter is with her or in her possession. 此类问题中，星盘的基准盘 3 宫很少相关。如果问题是“她收到我的信了吗？”， 我们可以查看她（的征象星）与代表信件的 3 宫主之间是否存在一个出相位（表 示已发生之事）。3 宫主位于她的 1 宫或 2 宫，都是信件已抵达的征象：信在她 那里或由她持有。

Usually, the question is about someone else’s letter: ‘When will I hear from him?’ ‘When will the book I ordered arrive?’ Take the ruler of the sender’s 3rd house to show that person’s letter. This usually brings us to the 9th, as such questions are usually asked about either sweethearts or those with whom the querent has a business deal (such as ordering the book). All such people are shown by the 7th house, the 3rd from which is the radical 9th. Once you have located the correct significator, look for an applying aspect with Lord 1, the Moon or Lord 2. An aspect with Lord 2 shows the letter coming into the querent’s possession. Then time the arrival by degrees in the usual way. No aspect: no arrival. 通常，问题是关于他人的信件：“我何时会收到他的消息？”“我订购的书何时

会到？”取发送方 3 宫的守护星来代表那个人的信件。这通常会将我们引至 9 宫，因为此类问题通常是关于恋人或有商业往来的人（例如订购书籍）。所有这 些人都由 7 宫代表，其 3 宫（即发送方的 3 宫）就是基准盘的 9 宫。一旦确定了 正确的征象星，就寻找它与 1 宫主、月亮或 2 宫主之间的入相位。与 2 宫主成相 位，表示信件将归问卜者所有。然后按通常方式以度数来推算到达时间。若无相 位，则无到达。

If you have ordered a book, the point at issue is the arrival of the book: the seller’s parcel, 3rd from the 7th. With your sweetheart or the phone-call from Mum, the point at issue is the contact with that person. As such, an aspect from that person (Lord 7 or Lord 10) to the querent will give a ‘Yes’: there is no need to particularise the phone-call as the turned 3rd house. Once we’ve ordered the book, we don’t want any further contact with the seller, so an applying aspect with Lord 7 in that case will not do. 如果你订购了一本书，问题的焦点是书的到达：即卖家的包裹，7 宫之 3 宫。对 于恋人或母亲的来电，问题的焦点是与那个人的联系。因此，那个人（7 宫主或 10 宫主）与问卜者成相位即表示“肯定”：无需将电话特别指定为转宫后的 3 宫。一旦我们订购了书，就不想与卖家再有进一步联系，所以那种情况下与 7 宫主的入相位并不表示书的到达。

Remember that once you have the letter it is no longer the sender’s 3rd, but your 2nd: your possession. 请记住，一旦你收到信件，它就不再是发送方的 3 宫事务，而是你的 2 宫事务： 即你的所有物。

If the question is ‘When will this person arrive?’ take the ruler of that person’s house (11th if it is the querent’s friend; 6th if it is the plumber) and look for an aspect to – in order of preference – the Ascendant, Lord 1, the Moon, the 4th cusp (being the querent’s home). No aspect, no arrival. If there is an aspect, time it in the usual way. Such questions typically have a limited time-scale, assuming, for instance, that the arrival will be sometime that afternoon. This makes timing much easier. Anything less than a degree can usually be taken as ‘immediately’, although we can time to the minute. In such questions minutes of arc can often be taken as minutes of time, so if the significator is 35′from the Ascendant, arrival will be in 35 minutes. 如果问题是“这个人何时会到？”，取代表那个人的宫位的守护星（如果是问卜 者的朋友则为 11 宫；如果是水管工则为 6 宫），并寻找它与——按优先顺序— —上升点、1 宫主、月亮、4 宫头（代表问卜者的家）之间的相位。无相位，则 无抵达。若有相位，按通常方式推算时间。此类问题通常时间范围有限，例如假 定抵达时间会在当天下午的某个时候。这使得时间推算容易得多。通常小于 1 度的距离可视为“立即”，尽管我们可以精确到分钟推算。在此类问题中，弧分 通常可视为时间上的分钟数，因此，如果征象星距离上升点 35’，则将在 35 分钟 后抵达。

It doesn’t matter which planet applies to which. If Lord 1 applies to the visitor instead

of the visitor applying to Lord 1, it doesn’t mean that the querent needs to set out to collect her. Who goes to whom is given by the question. 哪颗行星入相位于哪颗行星并不重要。如果是 1 宫主入相位于访客的征象星，而 非访客的征象星入相位于 1 宫主，这并不意味着问卜者需要出发去接她。谁去找 谁，由问题本身表明。

Aspects to the Ascendant show arrival only if that person’s arrival is assumed by the question (as in my examples here) or confirmed by other testimony in the chart. If the question is ‘Will I ever see my long-lost friend again?’ the friend’s significator applying to the Ascendant shows that he is weighing on my mind; it doesn’t show that he will be knocking on my door at any moment. 只有当某人的抵达为问题所假设（如我此处的例子）或为星盘中其他征象所确认 时，与上升点成相位才表示抵达。如果问题是“我还能再见到我失散多年的朋友 吗？”，朋友的征象星趋近上升点，表示他正萦绕在我的心头；并不表示他随时 会来敲我的门。

### ✸Be clear about what is of importance. If you are asking about money due to arrive

by post, your question is ‘When will the money arrive?’ not ‘When will the letter arrive?’ It is the sender’s 2nd house, not the sender’s 3rd, that is of interest. Despite what I wrote above, the same is true of merchandise, such as books, arriving by post. It is the seller’s possession that is on its way to you, so it is the seller’s Lord 2, not Lord 3, that is of interest. Even if you have paid for the merchandise, it is not your possession until it arrives, so it is not shown by your own 2nd house. The 2nd is the house of movable possessions: if you don’t have it yet, you can’t move it around.

### ✸要明确什么是重点。如果你问的是通过邮寄方式应到的钱款，你的问题是“钱

何时会到？”，而非“信何时会到？”。你感兴趣的是发送方的 2 宫，而非发送 方的 3 宫。尽管我上面写了关于信件的内容，但对于通过邮寄送达的商品（例如 书籍）也是如此。正在路上向你而来的是卖家的所有物，因此你感兴趣的是卖家 的 2 宫主，而非 3 宫主。即使你已经为商品付了款，在它到达之前，它并非你的 所有物，因此不由你自己的 2 宫代表。2 宫是动产之宫：如果你尚未拥有它，你 就无法移动它。

A question such as ‘What will he think of the letter I sent him?’ is usually not about the reaction to the letter (‘What pretty paper it’s written on!’) but about the reaction to the person who wrote it. So the letter itself is irrelevant in judgement. ✷ 像“他会如何看待我寄给他的信？”这类问题，通常不是关于对信件的反应（“信 纸多漂亮啊！”），而是关于对写信人的反应。因此，信件本身在判断中是无关 紧要的。✷ ``

# Fourth House Questions

# 4 宫的问题

PROPERTY DEALS 房产交易

Will I buy/sell the house? 我能否买/卖这栋房子？

These questions are both judged in the same way. The querent, whether buyer or seller, is, as ever, given the 1st house; the other party is given the 7th. What we want to see is an applying aspect between Lord 1 and Lord 7. This question is really, ‘Will we do the deal?’ hence our concern being with Lords 1 and 7 rather than with the property itself, which is Lord 4. 这两类问题的判断方式相同。问卜者，无论是买方还是卖方，一如既往地由 1 宫代表；另一方由 7 宫代表。我们需要观察的是 1 宫主与 7 宫主之间是否形成入 相位。这个问题本质是“我们能否达成交易？”，因此我们关注的是 1 宫主和 7 宫主，而非房产本身（房产由 4 宫主代表）。

If the other party has a specific house in the chart, use that instead of the 7th. If the question is ‘Will my brother buy my house?’ or ‘Can I buy my friend’s house?’ use the 3rd or the 11th. 如果交易对方在星盘中有特定的宫位代表，则使用该宫位而非 7 宫。例如，问题 是“我的兄弟会买我的房子吗？”或“我能买我朋友的房子吗？”，则应使用 3 宫或 11 宫。

It doesn’t matter what the aspect between buyer and seller is: few charts on these questions have anything more optimistic than a square. Oppositions seem to be the norm, but without their usual connotations of regret. This probably reflects the inordinate effort usually needed to force these deals to a conclusion. Note the receptions. A mutual reception between Lords 1 and 7 is most encouraging: they both want to do the deal. The absence of reception is not usually a problem; negative reception (by detriment or fall) is. A seller whose significator is in the fall of the buyer’s will be reluctant to sell to him, although need may force his hand. 买卖双方征象星之间的相位类型无关紧要：这类星盘中很少出现比刑相位更乐观 的相位。对冲相位似乎才是常态，但并不带有其通常代表的后悔涵义。这可能反

映了促成此类交易通常需要付出超常的努力。需注意接纳关系。1 宫主与 7 宫主 之间的互溶是最令人鼓舞的：双方都希望达成交易。没有接纳关系通常不是问题； 但负面的接纳关系（通过落陷或弱势）则是问题。卖方的征象星位于买方征象星 弱势的位置，表明卖方不愿卖给他，尽管需求可能迫使他就范。

The positions of the significators and their strength show who has the upper hand in the negotiations. In this context there is a vital distinction between being on or inside a house cusp. The planet on the cusp has power over that house, like the enemy battering at your castle gate; the planet inside the cusp is in the power of that house, like the enemy trapped within. So: Lord 7 on the Asc shows the other party is keen to do the deal (in sign of Lord 1) and may be forcing the pace (the planet on Asc can often be seen as something weighing down on the querent). Lord 7 just inside the 1st house shows the querent has the other party in the palm of his hand. More often, we find Lord 1 just inside the 7th house: the querent is desperate and the other party knows it. 征象星的位置及其力量显示了谁在谈判中占上风。在此背景下，星体位于宫头位 置还是宫头之内有至关重要的区别。位于宫头上的星体对该宫有控制力，如同敌 人正在敲打你的城堡大门；位于宫头之内的星体则受该宫控制，如同被困在城 堡内的敌人。因此：7 宫主位于上升点，表明对方渴望交易（处于 1 宫主的星座）， 并可能推动进程（位于上升点的星体常可被视为施加在问卜者身上的压力）。7 宫主刚进入 1 宫，表明问卜者已将对方掌控在手中。更常见的情况是，我们发现 1 宫主刚进入 7 宫：问卜者非常急切，而对方心知肚明。

### ✸Note, though, that the matter of strength is rarely relevant in such questions. The

buyer is rarely able to force the seller to sell, the seller rarely able to force the buyer to buy. So while the one party’s significator on the other party’s cusp shows that person’s enthusiasm, it can be an unfortunate testimony. If the question is ‘Can I persuade the seller to reduce the price?’ your planet on the seller’s cusp is a strong negative. If you are so keen, what incentive does the seller have to reduce the price? ✷

### ✸但需注意，在此类问题中，星体力量强弱的问题很少相关。买方很少能强迫

卖方出售，卖方也很少能强迫买方购买。因此，虽然一方的征象星位于另一方的 宫头显示了此人的热情，但这可能是不利的征象。如果问题是“我能说服卖方降 价吗？”，那么你的星体位于卖方的宫头就是一个强烈的否定征象。如果你如此 迫切，卖方还有什么降价的动机呢？✷

While it might seem logical that Lord 4 applying to aspect with the buyer’s significator will show the property being sold, this is a much less convincing testimony than Lords 1 and 7 coming together. Lord 10 shows the price of the property. Having this going to the seller is so minor a testimony it can usually be ignored: don’t be tempted to hang a judgement on that alone. Without the deal, as shown by Lords 1 and 7, neither property nor money will change hands. 虽然 4 宫主与买方的征象星形成入相位似乎能逻辑性地显示房产将被出售，但这

远不如 1 宫主和 7 宫主会合有说服力。10 宫主代表房产的价格。此星体与卖方 形成相位是一个如此次要的征象，通常可以忽略：不要试图仅凭此点作出判断。 如果没有交易（由 1 宫主和 7 宫主显示），房产和金钱都不会易手。

### ✸I understated the importance of an aspect between Lord 4 and the buyer. Always

look for the Lord 1 / Lord 7 aspect first. If there isn’t one but there is an aspect between Lord 4 and buyer, this will usually do the job. ✷ 我之前低估了 4 宫主与买方之间相位的重要性。总是首先寻找 1 宫主/7 宫主之间 的相位。如果没有，但 4 宫主与买方之间有相位，这通常也能促成交易。✷

A common scenario: Lords 1 and 7 are applying to aspect, showing that the seller (our querent, Lord 1) will sell his property. But before the aspect perfects, there is a prohibition. What is this planet that gets in the way? Lord 8: the buyer’s money (2nd from 7th: the other person’s money). It is in its detriment. What is it that stops the deal being done? The buyer can’t raise the money. 一个常见场景：1 宫主和 7 宫主正在形成入相位，显示卖方（我们的问卜者，1 宫主）将出售其房产。但在相位完成前，出现了阻碍。这个介入的星体是什么？ 是 8 宫主：买方的资金（7 宫的 2 宫：对方的钱财）。它处于落陷状态。是什么 阻止了交易完成？买方无法筹到资金。

Any unidentified planet aspecting the seller before the buyer’s significator perfects an aspect can be taken as some other person coming in to buy the property. 在买方的征象星完成相位之前，任何与卖方形成相位的未识别星体，都可以被视 为是另一个介入购买房产的人。

You do not need to go looking for the estate agent. If there is an aspect between Lords 1 and 7, the involvement of an agent is irrelevant; we do not need that character on stage. If, however, there is a planet translating or collecting light or bring this aspect about, this can be taken as showing the agent. 你不需要特意寻找房产中介。如果 1 宫主和 7 宫主之间有相位，中介的参与就无 关紧要；我们不需要这个角色登场。然而，如果有星体通过传递光线或聚集光线 来促成此相位，则可以将其视为中介的显示。

### ✸An applying aspect between the seller and Lord 4 has no meaning and can be

ignored, except if it prohibits an aspect with the buyer. Aspects bring things into contact. But the seller is already in contact with the property: he wouldn’t be able to sell it otherwise.

### ✸卖方与 4 宫主之间的入相位没有意义，可以忽略，除非它阻碍了与买方的相

位。相位带来联系。但卖方本就已经与房产有联系：否则他无法出售它。

Bear in mind the stage negotiations have reached. At an early stage, we need strong

testimony to show the deal being done. At a very late stage, when all has been agreed but the worried buyer asks ‘Is this going to go through?’ all we need to judge Yes is the absence of a compelling negative (see pp. 160-161). Suppose in such a chart the 7th cusp were at 10 Aries. Lord 1 at 9 Aries would show nothing except the querent’s concern for the deal. But Lord 1 at 29 Pisces, about to move into Lord 7’s house, would be strong testimony: ‘Yes, you will move in there’. 需牢记谈判所处的阶段。在早期阶段，我们需要强有力的征象来显示交易会达成。 在非常晚的阶段，当一切已商定，但忧心忡忡的买方问“这事能成吗？”，我们 判断为“是”只需要没有强有力的否定征象（参见 264 - 265 页）。假设在此类 星盘中，7 宫头在白羊座 10 度。1 宫主在白羊座 9 度，除了显示问卜者对交易的 关切外，别无他意。但如果 1 宫主在双鱼座 29 度，即将进入 7 宫主的宫位，这 就是强有力的征象：“是的，你将进入那里（完成交易）”。

Note that the property is shown by Lord 4 whether the querent is buying or selling. If selling, it is Lord 4 because it is his property; if buying, it is Lord 4 because it is his potential property. Everyting in the chart derives from the querent’s perspective. The potential property, just as Lord 7 shows the potential girlfriend (‘Will she go out with me?’) or Lord 10 the potential job (‘Will I get this job?’). 请注意，无论问卜者是买方还是卖方，房产都由 4 宫主代表。如果是卖方，4 宫 主代表其财产；如果是买方，4 宫主代表其潜在财产。星盘中的一切都源自问卜 者的视角。潜在的房产，正如 7 宫主代表潜在的女友（“她会和我约会吗？”） 或 10 宫主代表潜在的工作（“我能得到这份工作吗？”）。

‘But doesn’t this contradict the point about the package sent by the seller in the additions to the previous chapter?’ No, because the question ‘When will the package arrive?’ is not about what is potentially mine, but about what is really still his. The question about the girlfriend, the job or the house is asking if a potential will be made real; the question about the package is asking when a real thing will come. ✷ “但是，这与上一章增补部分关于卖方寄出的包裹的观点不是矛盾吗？” 不矛 盾，因为“包裹何时到达？”这个问题并非关于潜在属于我的东西，而是关于实 质上仍属于他的东西。关于女友、工作或房子的问题是询问一个可能性是否会成 为现实；关于包裹的问题是询问一个实体的东西何时会到来。✷

【‘When will I sell my house?’- Posted on April 22nd, 2014 【“我什么时候能卖掉房子？”- 发布于 2014 年 4 月 22 日

I’m reluctant to accept such questions if the house is not yet on the market. ‘When will I sell it?’ ‘After you start trying to sell it,’ is a little pointless. In such cases it makes more sense to ask the question about whatever it is that determines when the house will be offered for sale: ‘When can I retire?’ ‘When will the kids leave home?’ ‘When will the market pick up?’ etc.】 如果房子尚未挂牌出售，我不太愿意接受此类问题。“我什么时候能卖掉它？” 答案是“在你开始尝试卖它之后”，这有点毫无意义。在这种情况下，更有意义 的是询问那些决定房子何时可以出售的因素背后的时机问题：“我什么时候能退

休？”“孩子们什么时候能离家？”“市场什么时候能回暖？”等等。】

The condition of the house 房屋的状况

Lord 4 is the house, so its condition will show the state of the property. Lord 4 in its own sign: very good – the property is sound. In its exaltation, remembering the sense of exaggerated good that this dignity carries, the house is in good condition, but perhaps not quite as good as it seem: watch out for a cosmetic coat of paint hiding minor problems. Lesser dignities show lesser degrees of good condition. If Lord 4 is peregrine, the house is not so good, and – peregrine planets inclining more to evil – may be deteriorating. Unless it is a mobile home, when the significator being peregrine can be taken as describing the nature of the property without any such malign implications. 4 宫主代表房屋，因此其状态将显示房产的状况。4 宫主位于其入庙星座：非常 好——房产状况良好。位于其旺势星座时，需记住此尊贵带有夸大的好处之意， 房屋状况良好，但可能不如看起来那么好：需提防一层装饰性涂料掩盖了小问题。 较弱的尊贵显示较差的状况。如果 4 宫主处于游离状态，房屋状况就不太好，并 且——游离星体更倾向于描述负面状况——可能正在恶化。除非它是移动房屋， 此时游离状态仅描述房产属性而无不良暗示。

If Lord 4 is in its detriment or fall, there are problems. The nature of the sign will indicate what these problems are: 如果 4 宫主处于落陷或弱势状态，则存在问题。星座的属性将指示这些问题的类 型：

* air signs: check the roof and the windows
* 风象星座：检查屋顶和窗户

* water signs: check the plumbing and the damp-course
* 水象星座：管道系统和和防水层

* fire signs: check the heating, walls and plastering
* 火象星座：检查供暖系统、墙壁和墙漆

* earth signs: check the foundations.
* 土象星座：检查地基。

### ✸As noted with regard to lost objects, p. 175 above, the association of fire signs

with walls and, by extension, plastering is false. That walls are – perhaps – made of brick and bricks are made with fire does not mean fire signs signify walls.✷ 如前文关于失物部分所述（见第 285 页），将火象星座与墙壁乃至墙漆关联是错

误的。墙壁可能由砖砌成，而砖是用火制成的，这并不意味着火象星座象征墙壁。 ✷

Look out for other afflictions to the significator. Opposed by Saturn, for instance: the house might be lovely, but that factory opposite will make life there a misery. Debilitated planets in the 4th will show other problems, identified by the nature of the sign. 需留意征象星所受的其他刑克。例如，被土星对冲：房屋可能很漂亮，但对面的 工厂会让居住体验变得痛苦。4 宫内虚弱的星体将显示其他问题，可根据星座属 性来识别。

Lord 10 is the price. Its condition will tell whether the price is high or low. If the querent is the buyer, it can be significant that the price is in a fixed sign: it is no use making a lower offer. At the end of a fixed sign: an offer is worth a try. Be aware here too of the nature of exaltation: it suggests the price is inflated. In a seller’s market this may be inescapable, but there may be other reasons for this exaggeration – rumours that the railroad is coming to town, or that a film star has bought a house locally. 10 宫主代表价格。其状态将说明价格高低。如果问卜者是买方，价格位于固定 星座可能具有意义：提出更低报价没有用处。位于固定星座末尾：报价值得一试。 此处也需注意旺势的本质：它暗示价格被抬高。在卖方市场中这可能无法避免， 但也可能存在其他夸大价格的原因——例如传闻铁路将修到镇上，或有电影明星 在当地买了房。

What we hope for is a balance between the condition of the property and the condition of the price. Ideally, any imbalance would be in the querent’s favour. There may be a strong imbalance against him, yet even so there are reasons for him to buy: the house may be falling down, but granny used to live there, or he is desperate to be near his favourite team’s stadium. The chart will provide a clear analysis so the querent can decide whether the imbalance is acceptable or not. 我们希望的是房产状况与价格状况之间的平衡。理想情况下，任何不平衡都应有 利于问卜者。可能存在严重不利于他的不平衡，即便如此他可能仍有购买理由： 房屋可能摇摇欲坠，但奶奶曾住在那里，或者他极度渴望离他最爱球队的体育场 近一些。星盘将提供清晰的分析，以便问卜者决定这种不平衡是否可接受。

Example: 示例：

* Lord 4 in its own sign; Lord 10 in its own sign: the house is expensive, but you will get what you pay for
* 4 宫主在其入庙星座；10 宫主在其入庙星座：房屋昂贵，但物有所值

* Lord 4 in its term; Lord 10 in its exaltation: the house is OK, but the price is inflated
* 4 宫主在其得界位置；10 宫主在其旺势位置：房屋尚可，但价格虚高

* Lord 4 in its detriment; Lord 10 in its detriment: the place is a dump, but the low price means it could still be worth buying.
* 4 宫主在其落陷位置；10 宫主在其落陷位置：房子是个破烂，但低廉的价格意 味着仍值得购买。

Note receptions between Lords 1 and 4. Lord 1 in the exaltation of Lord 4: the querent has, as it were, a crush on the house. No matter how good the house might be, it is unlikely to live up to expectations. If the querent is buying the house where his favourite poet lived, the exaltation would be understandable: he values the house more highly than it really deserves. Lord 4 in the detriment of Lord 1: the house hates the querent, and so will not make him happy. 注意 1 宫主与 4 宫主之间的接纳关系。1 宫主位于 4 宫主的旺势位置：可以说， 问卜者对房屋极为痴迷。无论房屋多好，都难以满足其期望。如果问卜者购买的 是他最喜爱的诗人曾居住的房屋，这种旺势关系可以理解：他对房屋的评价高于 其实际价值。4 宫主位于 1 宫主的落陷位置：房屋“厌恶”问卜者，因此不会让 他幸福。

Most purchasers would like to see scope for future improvement in the price: consider the condition of Lord 10 now, its condition as it moves forward through the zodiac and the nature of its present sign – fixed signs showing lack of change. 大多数购买者希望看到未来价格有改善空间：需考虑 10 宫主当前的状态、它沿 黄道前行时的状态，以及其当前所在星座的属性——固定星座显示缺乏变化。
