If the house is being bought primarily for profit, whether to improve and sell on or to let out, the profit is shown by Lord 5 (2nd from the 4th: the house’s money). 如果购房投资，无论是翻新转售还是出租，利润由 5 宫主代表（4 宫的 2 宫：房 产的钱财）。

If the querent is asking about a property he is thinking of buying, have a look at the neighbours. We are concerned with the neighbours of the house that is being bought, not the querent’s neighbours now, so the neighbours will be shown by the 6th, which is the 3rd from the 4th: the house’s neighbours. A querent asked if she should relocate permanently to her holiday home. Lord 4 was the Sun in Libra, so the house was in a bad way (in its fall). It was ruled by, or dominated by, Venus, which was itself in detriment. Venus ruled the 6th. The house was in its fall (in Libra) because it was dominated by the neighbours (Venus), who were themselves horrible (in detriment). The querent later told me hair-raising stories about the neighbours terrorizing the village. 如果问卜者正在考虑购买一处房产，可以看看邻居情况。我们关注的是待购房屋 的邻居，而非问卜者当前的邻居，因此邻居由 6 宫代表，即 4 宫的 3 宫：房屋的 邻居。曾有一位问卜者询问是否应永久迁居至她的度假屋。4 宫主是太阳在天秤 座，因此房屋状况不佳（处于弱势）。它被金星所定位或主导，而金星本身处于 落陷状态。金星掌管 6 宫。房屋状况不佳（在天秤座弱势）是因为它被邻居（金 星）所主导，而邻居本身很糟糕（处于落陷）。问卜者后来告诉我一些关于邻居

恐吓村民的骇人听闻的故事。

### ✸When considering the condition of the property, do remember the reality of the

situation: people rarely buy the house they want, but the least bad they can afford. Don’t drag in issues about the condition of the property if the querent doesn’t ask. If the question is ‘Will the deal go through?’ the querent does not need to be told ‘Oh, but the place really doesn’t look so good!’ Unless very wealthy, the querent probably knows this already.

### ✸评估房产状况时，务必牢记现实情况：人们很少能买到理想的房子，往往只

能负担得起最不差的那个。如果问卜者没有询问，就不要主动提及房产状况的问 题。如果问题是“交易能成吗？”，问卜者不需要被告知“哦，但这地方看起来 真的不怎么样！”除非非常富有，否则问卜者很可能已经知道了。

If wishing to negotiate the price, remember that the price does not make up its own mind about things. Lord 10 can give us some clues, as above, but much more important is Lord 7: the seller. Lord 7 in a fixed sign is a stronger testimony that the price will not change than Lord 10 being in one. 如果想就价格进行谈判，请记住价格本身不会做决定。10 宫主能给我们一些线 索，如上所述，但更重要的是 7 宫主：卖方。7 宫主在固定星座比 10 宫主在固 定星座更能有力地证明价格不会变动。

Although the texts use the 10th house for the price, in many questions it is more appropriate to use the 5th: the profit from the property. If the querent is the buyer, the price will be Lord 10 (‘Can I get the price reduced?’). If the querent is the seller, asking ‘Can I make some decent money from this sale?’ use Lord 5. The question here is about the profit from the house. 尽管典籍中使用 10 宫代表价格，但在许多问题中，使用 5 宫（房产的利润）更 为合适。如果问卜者是买方，价格将由 10 宫主代表（“我能把价格降下来吗？”）。 如果问卜者是卖方，询问“我能从这次出售中获得不错的收益吗？”，则使用 5 宫主。这里的问题是关于房产的利润。

While the 3rd from the 4th can be the new house’s neighbours, be careful in how you read this. In the example above, Lord 6 was the neighbours. But without further knowledge to confirm this it could have been, for example, the new house’s local transport links (its 3rd house: routine journeys) which were so bad that life there would be difficult. Or many other things. Always remember that less is more. It is better to say ‘There is a heavy affliction here, but I can’t be sure what that shows’ than to hope to be lucky by pinning it on one particular idea. It is easy to start writing novels from a few clues in the chart. Don’t! ✷ 虽然 4 宫的 3 宫可以代表新房子的邻居，但解读时需谨慎。在上面的例子中，6 宫主代表邻居。但如果没有进一步的知识来确认，它也可能代表，例如，新房子 的当地交通连接（它的 3 宫：日常出行）非常糟糕，导致生活在那里会很困难。

或者是许多其他可能性。永远记住，少即是多。最好说“这里存在严重的刑克， 但我不确定它代表什么”，而不是寄希望于运气，将其归结为某个特定的想法。 很容易根据星盘中的几个线索就开始编故事。不要这样做！✷

### ✸A common question is ‘Should I buy this one or that one?’ If the querent favours

one option, use Lord 4 for that one and another planet, chosen by description, for the alternative. Then compare their condition. If the querent has no clear favourite, choose all significators by description. To do this, ask the querent what is particular about each house. Keep the replies brief! If you keep the querents on a short lead, they will give the few important words of description that are relevant to the chart in question. For instance, if it’s a choice between a very old house and the house by the river, Saturn could signify the old one and a planet within a degree or two of a water sign the one by the river. The big flat or the penthouse: Jupiter for the big one, a planet in an air sign or near the MC (top of the chart) for the penthouse. Different people would describe the same houses in different ways. One might say ‘This one is new-build, that one is old’, while another would say ‘This one is near the river, that one is near my work’ or ‘This one is big and the other is small’. The chart is the querent’s creation, so you can trust that the querent’s choice of descriptive criteria will be pertinent to that chart. It is not unusual for this request for description to make the horary investigation redundant: ‘This one’s near the beach, that one’s next to the factory… oh, decision made!’

### ✸一个常见问题是“我应该买这套还是那套？”。如果问卜者偏爱其中一个选

项，用 4 宫主代表那一套，再用另一颗依据描述选择的星体代表另一套。然后比 较它们的状况。如果问卜者没有明确的偏爱，则全部通过描述来选择征象星。为 此，请询问问卜者每套房子的特别之处。让回答保持简短！如果你能引导问卜者 简短回答，他们会给出与当前星盘相关的几个重要描述性词语。例如，如果是在 一栋很老的房子和河边房子之间选择，土星可以代表老房子，而位于水象星座一 两度内的星体可以代表河边的房子。大公寓还是顶层公寓：木星代表大的，位于 风象星座或靠近中天（星盘顶部）的星体代表顶层公寓。不同的人会用不同的方 式描述相同的房子。一个人可能说“这套是新建的，那套是旧的”，而另一个人 可能说“这套靠近河边，那套靠近我工作的地方”或“这套很大，另一套很小”。 星盘是问卜者创造的，因此你可以相信问卜者选择的描述标准与该星盘是相关的。 这种要求描述的做法使卜卦调查变得多余的情况并不少见：“这套靠近海滩，那 套在工厂旁边……哦，决定了！”

Don’t be afraid to make the querent do some work. Don’t accept a list of a dozen potential properties: make the querent narrow it down to two or, at most, three. ✷ 不要害怕让问卜者做一些工作。不要接受一份十几处潜在房产的列表：让问卜者 将其缩小到两处，最多三处。✷

Letting property

房产出租

Questions about letting or renting property should be judged in the same way as questions about buying or selling it. It is the same question: ‘Can I do the deal?’ These questions are judged from the 1st and 7th house. Modern writers follow Lilly in assigning tenants to the 6th house, but this is wrong. In Lilly’s day, your tenant was subservient to you: he would probably have worked on your hand; he would certainly, if he had a vote, have cast it as you instructed him. This is no longer the case: a tenancy agreement is made between two parties on equal footing. Note that it is not the astrology that has changed; it is the meaning of the word. 关于房产出租或租赁的问题，应以与买卖房产问题相同的方式判断。这是同一个 问题：“我能达成交易吗？”这类问题通过 1 宫和 7 宫来判断。现代作者遵循 Lilly 的做法，将租户分配给 6 宫，但这是错误的。在 Lilly 的时代，你的租户是 从属于你的：他很可能在你的土地上劳作；如果他有投票权，他肯定会按照你的 指示投票。如今情况已非如此：租赁协议是在地位平等的双方之间签订的。请注 意，改变的并非占星学原理；而是这个词的含义。

### ✸I find considerable resistance to my statement that tenants are no longer 6th-house

people. The situation today is not as it was when Lilly was writing. This is not a matter of opinion; it is a matter of historical fact. If I rent a flat today, I can be sure that my landlord will not send his wife to tend me when I am ill, not will he be exhorted from the pulpit to feast me at Christmas if I have fallen on hard times. Treating tenants as 6th-house is akin to feeding your car on hay. ✷

### ✷我发现，关于“租户不再是 6 宫之人”的观点遇到了相当大的阻力。今天的

状况已不同于 Lilly 写作的时代。这不是观点问题；这是历史事实问题。如果我 今天租了一套公寓，我可以确定，当我生病时，我的房东不会派他的妻子来照顾 我，如果我陷入困境，他也不会被布道坛劝诫在圣诞节款待我。若将租客视作 6 宫之人，无异于用干草喂养汽车——荒诞不经。✷

The only difference between a selling and a letting question comes if Lords 1 and 7 join by opposition. While this is acceptable with a selling/buying question, it promises regret in the long-term relationship that will exist between tenant and landlord. 出售问题与出租问题之间的唯一区别在于，如果 1 宫主和 7 宫主通过对冲相位会 合。在买卖问题中这可以接受，但它预示着在租户与房东将存在的长期关系中会 出现悔意。

‘Should I let to these people?’ Consider the nature and condition of Lord 7: the better its condition, the more they can be trusted. Suppose Lord 7 is Jupiter in fall: a debilitated benefic. They look OK, but are rotten within. Be careful that Lord 7 is not afflicting Lord 4 or 5 (tenants harm the property or the profit from it). "我应该把房子租给这些人吗？"考虑 7 宫主的属性和状况：其状况越好，他们越 值得信赖。假设 7 宫主是处于弱势的木星：一颗虚弱的吉星。他们看起来不错，

但内里腐败。需注意 7 宫主是否刑克 4 宫主或 5 宫主（租户损害房产或从中获得 的利润）。

If the question is ‘Should I sell my house, or rent it out?’ finding Lord 7 in a cardinal or fixed sign would suggest selling; the duality implicit in a double-bodied sign would suggest renting. If Lord 7 shows renting, and that this will be harmful, advise the querent to sell, and vice versa. Perhaps Lord 10 (the price) in a sale question is weak now, but will soon gain in strength: we might advise the querent to let the property for a while, then sell when the market rises. 如果问题是“我应该卖掉我的房子，还是把它租出去？”，发现 7 宫主在基本或 固定星座会建议出售；双体星座中隐含的双重性则建议出租。如果 7 宫主显示出 租，且这将是有害的，则建议问卜者出售，反之亦然。或许在出售问题中，10 宫主（价格）目前弱势，但很快会获得力量：我们可能建议问卜者先将房产出租 一段时间，等市场上涨时再出售。

### ✸As with my revision above, in judging whether to sell or to let it is the 5th house

that is important, not the 10th. The concern is with the profit from the property: 2nd from 4th. ✷

### ✸与上文我的修订一致，在判断是出售还是出租时，重要的是 5 宫，而非 10

宫。关注点在于房产的利润：4 宫的 2 宫。✷

Should I take the farm, or the business? 我该接手农场还是商铺？

### ✸In the whole of this section I followed Lilly much too closely. Mea culpa. In such

a question the 4th is the place in question; the 7th is the person you are buying or renting it from. The question is about the money to be made from the place, so that money to be made from the property. The 10th will be only the price at which you are buying or renting, so may give some clues as to whether that too high or low. But the important part is the profit: 5th house. The idea that the 4th is ‘the end of the matter’ is quite wrong: it is the place in question.

### ✷在本节全部内容中，我过于紧密地追随了 Lilly 的观点。这是我的疏忽。在此

类问题中，4 宫代表相关场所；7 宫代表你正从其处购买或租赁该场所的人。问 题关乎从该场所可获得的金钱，即从该房产可获得的利润。10 宫仅代表你购买 或租赁的价格，因此可能提供一些线索，暗示该价格是过高还是过低。但重要的 是利润：5 宫。认为 4 宫是“事情的终结”的观点是完全错误的：它代表的是相 关场所。

The house position of Lord 1 is in itself of no significance, except in that being just

inside the 7th house shows the querent in a weak position for negotiation. This, though, is not by any means necessarily a ‘No’. Much better that the 4th or, especially, the 5th is favoured by the presence of a fortunate planet than tha the 1st is. 1 宫主的宫位位置本身没有意义，除非其刚进入 7 宫内部，这表明问卜者在谈判 中处于弱势地位。然而，这绝不必然意味着“否定答案”。4 宫，尤其是 5 宫， 得到一颗幸运星体的垂青，远比 1 宫得到垂青要好得多。

NB: this question is not about the success or otherwise of a particular career, but about the profitability of a particular property. So this is not ‘Can I make a living as a hairdresser?’ (see chapter 23) but ‘Is it worth renting this particular salon?’ ✷ 注意：此问题并非关于特定职业的成功与否，而是关于特定房产的盈利能力。因 此，这不是“我能以美发师为生吗？”（见第 23 章），而是“租下这个特定的 沙龙值得吗？”✷

If the querent is thinking of buying or renting a place to work on or in, treat the chart slightly differently from an ordinary house purchase. These questions assume that the property is available if the querent decides to take it, so we are not looking for an aspect between Lords 1 and 7. They also assume that the place will be put to work in some way: ‘Should I buy this farm?’ ‘Should I rent this recording-studio?’ ‘Should I buy this shop?’ 如果问卜者正在考虑购买或租赁一处用于在其中或在其上工作的场所，其星盘的 解读方式应与普通购房略有不同。此类问题假设，如果问卜者决定接受，该房产 是可获得的，因此我们不是寻找 1 宫主和 7 宫主之间的相位。它们还假设该场所 将以某种方式投入使用：“我应该买下这个农场吗？”“我应该租下这个录音室 吗？”“我应该买下这家店铺吗？”

The querent is 1st house; the seller or lessor is 7th. The 10th shows the profit that the querent will make from taking the place. The 4th shows the final outcome. 问卜者是 1 宫；卖方或出租方是 7 宫。10 宫显示问卜者接受该场所后将获得的 利润。4 宫显示最终结果。

Finding Lord 1 in the first, or in a sign that aspects the sign on the Ascendant by trine or sextile is a good indication that the querent is making a beneficial deal. The closer Lord 1 is to the Ascendant or its aspect, and the more essential dignity it has, the better. Similarly, a fortune (once again: this is any planet with good essential dignity) in the 1st house is a positive sign. Any debilitated planet is a bad sign, unless this debilitated planet is Lord 7. If Lord 7 is in the sign on the Ascedant, it will always be in its detriment. If Lord 7 is sitting on the Ascedant, it shows that the other party is pushing to get the deal done; if Lord 7 is just inside the Ascedant, it shows that the querent has the other party in his power, and so has considerable strength from which to dictate terms. 发现 1 宫主在 1 宫内，或在一个与上升点星座形成拱或六合相位的星座内，是问 卜者正在达成有利交易的良好征象。1 宫主越靠近上升点或其相位点，且其拥有 的先天尊贵越多，情况就越好。同样，1 宫内有吉星（再次强调：这是指任何具

有良好先天尊贵的星体）是积极的征象。任何受克星体都是不良征象，除非这颗 受克星体是 7 宫主。如果 7 宫主在上升点星座上，则它将总是处于落陷状态。如 果 7 宫主坐落在上升点上，表明对方正推动交易完成；如果 7 宫主刚进入上升点 内部，表明问卜者已将对方掌控在手中，因此拥有相当大的力量来制定条款。

Consider the trustworthiness of the seller. If Lord 7 is in its detriment and in the 12th house, caveat emptor! Lord 7 badly debilitated or the 7th house afflicted by the presence of a debilitated planet warns the querent to check the small-print in the contract: the terms could be disadvantageous. 考虑卖方的可信度。如果 7 宫主处于落陷状态且在 12 宫内，买家自慎！7 宫主 严重受克，或 7 宫因有受克星体存在而受克，都警告问卜者仔细检查合同细则： 条款可能不利。

Judge the condition of the 10th house and its Lord in the usual way. The 4th shows ‘the end of the matter’: will the querent look back on this as a good deal done, or look back with regret? Judge from the usual consideration, e.g. Lord 4 is dignified Jupiter, it is a good deal; debilitated Saturn, it is a bad one; strong Venus in the 4th house, it is a good deal; debilitated Mars, it is a bad one. 以通常方式判断 10 宫及其宫主星的状况。4 宫代表“事情的终结”：问卜者未 来回顾此事时，会认为是一笔好交易，还是心怀悔意？根据通常的考量因素判断， 例如，4 宫主是尊贵的木星，则是好交易；是受克的土星，则是坏交易；4 宫内 有强旺的金星，则是好交易；有受克的火星，则是坏交易。

OTHER SALE QUESTIONS 其他出售类问题

If the question is whether or not the deal will be done, these can be judged exactly as house purchase questions above: we want an applying aspect between Lord 1 and 7. For non-property sales, this aspect being an opposition would tell us that the deal will bring regret. If the other party has a specific house in the chart (‘Will my uncle sell me his car?’), use that instead of the 7th. 如果问题是交易是否会达成，可完全依照上述房产购买问题来判断：我们需要 1 宫主与 7 宫主形成入相位。对于非房产类销售，此相位若为对冲相位，则告诉我 们这笔交易将带来悔意。如果对方在星盘中有特定宫位（“我的叔叔会把他的车 卖给我吗？”），则使用该宫位而非 7 宫。

More often the question is not whether the deal can be done, but whether it should be done: ‘Should I buy this car/boat/antique?’ The object is shown by the 2nd house. Although it is not yet the querent’s possession, it is the querent’s potential possession, so we can judge from the 2nd in the same way that we can judge the querent’s romantic prospects with a potential partner by giving the potential partner the 7th. The question is all about the querent’s movable possessions (2nd house); it boils down to

‘Should I exchange some of my 2nd-house stuff (money) for this other 2nd-house thing (object desired)?’ What the chart shows us is the quality of the object desired. 更常见的问题并非交易能否达成，而是是否应该进行这笔交易：“我应该买这辆 车/船/古董吗？”交易对象由 2 宫代表。虽然它尚未成为问卜者的所有物，但它 是问卜者的潜在所有物，因此我们可以从 2 宫判断，就像我们可以通过将潜在伴 侣赋予 7 宫来判断问卜者的恋爱前景一样。这个问题完全是关于问卜者的动产（2 宫）；归根结底是“我是否应该用我的一些 2 宫财物（钱）来交换这另一件 2 宫事物（想要的物品）？”星盘向我们展示的是所购物品的质量。

What is its condition? Suppose the second-hand car I am thinking of buying is shown by Venus at 28 Pisces. It is currently in its exaltation (nice, but overrated) and is about to enter its detriment. Don’t buy it! As always, if the testimony can be read as descriptive, debilities can usually be ignored. If I plan to soup up this car and take it racing, its significator’s entry into cardinal fire Aries would be entirely appropriate. 它的状况如何？假设我正在考虑购买的二手车由双鱼座 28 度的金星代表。它目 前处于旺势（不错，但评价过高）并且即将进入落陷状态。别买！一如既往，如 果征象可解读为描述性的，则衰弱通常可以忽略。如果我计划改装这辆车并带它 去参赛，其征象星进入基本火象的白羊座将完全合适！

If the seller’s trustworthiness is in doubt, look at Lord 7. The more essential dignity, the more the seller can be trusted. 如果对卖方的可信度有疑问，则查看 7 宫主。其先天尊贵越多，卖方越值得信赖。

### ✸ Trustworthiness is not always so straightforward an issue. See the addition on

pages 190-191.✷

### ✸可信度并非总是如此直接的问题。参见第 308 页的增补内容。✷

# Fifth House Questions

# 5 宫的问题

PREGNANCY 怀孕

Am I pregnant? 我怀孕了吗？

With pregnancy testing so readily available across the chemist’s counter, this question is asked more rarely than once it was. More common is ‘Is my dog pregnant?’ The method is the same, turning the chart if the enquiry is about the dog. 如今药房柜台随处可购得验孕试剂，此问题已比往昔更为少见。更常见的是“我 的狗怀孕了吗？”若询问对象是狗，方法相同——转宫即可。

### ✸Much of this section leans too heavily on Lilly and should be ignored. This is

especially true of all comments about malefic and benefics, and planets aspecting the Ascendant or a planet in an angular house. 本节内容大多过于依赖 Lilly 的论述，应予以忽略。尤其是所有关于吉星与凶星、 以及四轴点或角宫内行星相位的评论。

Strong positive testimony is a separating aspect between Lord 1 or Moon and Lord 5: Mum has come into contact with Baby. But remember that prohibitions work retrospectively too (see page 109): if either planet has made another aspect since the aspect that showed conception, the aspect showing conception is prohibited: so far as we are concerned, it didn’t happen. An applying aspect between Mum and Baby is a definite No. If their contact is in the future, she cannot be pregnant now. Note that this does not mean ‘Not now, but you will be soon’. The querent is not asking about the future; she is asking only about the situation right now. 有力的积极征兆是 1 宫主或月亮与 5 宫主之间形成出相位：母亲已与婴儿发生接 触。但请记住，阻碍同样具有追溯效力（参见第 184 - 186 页）：若任一行星在 显示受孕的相位之后又形成了其他相位，则显示受孕的相位即被阻碍——就我们 判断而言，它并未发生。母亲与婴儿之间形成入相位则明确答案为“否”。若它 们的接触在未来，则她现在不可能怀孕。请注意，这并非意味着“现在没有，但 很快会有”。问卜者并非询问未来；她只询问当前状况。

Lord 5 just inside Mum’s house – the baby inside Mum – will almost always give a Yes. It can, however, be overruled by compelling testimony otherwise, such as an applying aspect between Mum and Baby. 5 宫主刚进入母亲的宫位（婴儿在母体内）几乎总是给出“是”的答案。然而， 若有其他强有力的相反征兆（例如母亲与婴儿之间形成入相位），则可推翻此判 断。

Lord 5 exactly in station is a strong negative. A planet in station isn’t moving. If it isn’t moving, it isn’t alive. I do mean ‘exactly’. 5 宫主恰好处于停滞是强烈的否定征兆。一颗停滞的行星没有移动。若不移动， 则无生命。此处的“精准”需严格考量。

In such questions there is no significance in Lord 5 being essentially debilitated or retrograde.✷ 在此类问题中，5 宫主处于衰弱或逆行并无特殊意义。✷

The clearest and strongest testimony is finding Lord 5 in the 1st house, close to the Ascendant. This gives a clear picture of the baby (Lord 5) inside the mother, and is a definite Yes. With so clear a picture of the situation, we do not need an aspect linking mother and baby. Lord 1 or the Moon in the 5th shows only that the querent is thinking about pregnancy; this needs supporting testimony to allow a Yes. Its being closely aspected by a strong benefic, or there being a strong benefic close to the 5th cusp, would be sufficient. 最清晰、最强烈的征兆是发现 5 宫主在 1 宫，靠近上升点。这清晰地描绘了婴儿 （5 宫主）在母亲体内的画面，明确答案为“是”。既然星盘已如此清晰地呈现 状况，我们便不需要连接母亲与婴儿的相位。1 宫主或月亮在 5 宫仅显示问卜者 正在思考怀孕之事；这需要其他支持性征兆才能判断为“是”。若有强有力的吉 星与之紧密成相，或是有强有力的吉星靠近 5 宫头，便已足够。

Lord 1, Lord 5 or the Moon aspecting and in strong mutual reception with a planet in an angular house is testimony for Yes. Lord 1 in close trine or sextile to the Ascendant is helpful. 1 宫主、5 宫主或月亮与角宫内行星成相且处于强互溶关系，是判断“是”的征 兆。1 宫主与上升点形成紧密的拱或六合相位亦有助益。

A malefic close to the 5th cusp or the Ascedant is testimony for No, unless the malefic in question is Lord 1 or 5. Lord 5 combust is a strong No. 凶星靠近 5 宫头或上升点是判断“否”的征兆，除非该凶星恰好是 1 宫主或 5 宫主。5 宫主被燃烧是强烈的“否”。

### ✸With the rider that if Sun is Lord 1 and the aspect is separating, Lord 5 combust

would be a strong Yes: Mum and Baby have been in contact and, as always, we can

ignore combustion if the aspect with the Sun is what we want (p. 70 above). ✷

### ✸但需补充：若太阳是 1 宫主且相位为出相位，则 5 宫主被燃烧反而是强烈的

“是”：母亲与婴儿已有过接触，并且，一如既往，若我们所需的正是与太阳的 相位（参见上文第 127 页），则可忽略燃烧。✷

Pregnancy and death are the places where antiscia will not do the job of a bodily aspect: do not judge Yes to any question on pregnancy on the strength of an antiscion alone. 怀孕与死亡是映点无法替代实体相位的领域：切勿仅凭映点就对任何怀孕问题判 断为“是”。

NB: while these testimonies being in fertile signs is encouraging, their being in barren signs does not preclude a positive result. The barren signs are more significant in general questions of the ‘will I ever…..?’ variety (see below). 注意：虽然这些征象星位于肥沃星座令人鼓舞，但位于贫瘠星座并不排除肯定结 果。贫瘠星座在“我是否会……”这类一般性问题中更为重要（见下文）。

### ✸The matter of barren or fertile signs can be ignored. If there is contact between

Mum and Baby, showing conception, she obviously isn’t barren. If there is no such contact, she may well be fertile, but yet not pregnant. The barren/fertile is relevant only to the general ‘Will I have children?’

### ✸贫瘠或肥沃星座的问题可以忽略。如果母亲与婴儿之间有接触（显示受孕），

她显然并非不育。若无此接触，她可能生育能力正常，但只是尚未怀孕。贫瘠/ 肥沃仅与“我会有孩子吗？”这类一般性问题相关。

The point about antiscia, above, is sound. ✷ 上文关于映点的论点是正确的。✷

N even more B: finding Lord 5 in the 8th is not a problem. It does not mean that the querent is carrying a dead baby! But the ruler of the 5th entering the 8th can be testimony that the querent is pregnant and will miscarry. 更需注意：发现 5 宫主在 8 宫不是问题。这并不意味着问卜者怀的是死胎！但 5 宫主进入 8 宫可以是问卜者怀孕并将流产的征兆。

### ✸A significator entering the 8th house is never testimony that that person will die.

Not, then, is Lord 5 entering the 8th house testimony of miscarriage. ✷

### ✸征象星进入 8 宫绝不表示该人会死亡。同样，5 宫主进入 8 宫也非流产的征

兆。✷

In any question on pregnancy, if other testimonies show that the woman is pregnant, finding the South Node or a debilitated malefic in her 5th house gives the potential for miscarriage. This potential needs supporting testimony if it is to be realised: do not judge on that alone. Miscarriage is an event, not a potential, and as such needs action in the chart to show it happening. 在任何关于怀孕的问题中，若其他征兆显示该女子已怀孕，发现南交点或一颗衰 弱的凶星在其 5 宫，则显示有流产的可能。此可能性需要其他支持性征兆才会实 现：切勿仅凭此一点判断。流产是一个事件，而非可能性，因此需要星盘中显示 正在发生的行动。

### ✸MOST IMPORTANT: I cannot imagine a situation in which ‘You will miscarry’ is

a judgement that can be given, even if clearly shown in the chart. What we can see does not always need to be said. Being human is far more important than being right. ✷

### ✷最重要的一点：即便星盘清晰显示流产迹象，“你会流产”也绝非应给出的

判断。眼见未必皆需言明。秉持人文关怀远比追求占卜精准更重要。✷

Is she pregnant? 她怀孕了吗？

This is judged much as above, except that Lord 5 in the 1st will not, of course, give a Yes: it is not the querent’s pregnancy that concerns us. This question is usually asked by a man of a woman with whom he has slept at least once, which makes her (in this context) a 7th-house person. So Lord 5 in the 7th would show a Yes, as would also Lord 11 (5th from the 7th, so her baby) in the 7th. In one such chart, Lord 5 and 11 were conjunct in the 7th: this did underline the Yes; it did not promise twins. Had they been in a double-bodied sign, it might have. 此问题的判断方法与上述大致相同，不同之处在于：5 宫主在 1 宫当然不会给出 “是”的答案——因为这与问卜者本人的怀孕无关。此问题通常由男性提出，对 象是与他至少发生过一次关系的女性，在此语境下她属于 7 宫所代表之人。因此， 5 宫主在 7 宫会显示“是”，11 宫主（即 7 宫的 5 宫，代表她的孩子）在 7 宫亦 然。在一张此类星盘中，5 宫主与 11 宫主在 7 宫内合相：这确实强调了“是” 的判断；但并非预示双胞胎。若它们位于双重性质星座，则有可能。

If the question is not about a 7th-house person, but, for instance, the querent’s sister or mother, we would look to that house and the 5th from there. The only circumstance in which we can have two houses showing the baby is when a male querent is asking if a woman is carrying his child: the radical 5th is ‘my baby’, the turned 5th is ‘her baby’ (with no suggestion of this meaning it was not fathered by querent). Do not involve the turned 11th house in questions asked by someone other than the father. 若问题涉及的不是 7 宫所代表之人，而是例如问卜者的姐妹或母亲，我们则应关

注对应宫位及其 5 宫。唯一可能同时有两个宫位显示婴儿信息的情况是：当男性 问卜者询问一名女子是否怀有他的孩子时——基准盘的 5 宫代表“我的孩子”， 转宫后的 5 宫代表“她的孩子”（这并不暗示孩子非问卜者所生）。若非父亲本 人提问，则不应涉及转宫后的 11 宫。

When considering those testimonies that involve angularity, it is the radical angular houses that matter: houses do not become angular by being turned (e.g. the 4th from the 3rd is not angular in a chart about my sister). 在考虑涉及角宫的征兆时，重要的是基准盘中的角宫：宫位不会因转宫而变为角 宫（例如，在关于我姐妹的星盘中，3 宫的 4 宫并非角宫）。

### ✸As noted in the addition on p. 202, there is no significance in a planet being in an

angular house in these questions. ✷

### ✸如第 325 - 326 页补充说明所述，在这些问题中，行星位于角宫并无特殊意义。

✷

Will I conceive? 我会怀孕吗？

My experience is that this question is usually asked by those contemplating fertility treatment, occasionally as ‘Will I conceive on this holiday?’ or similar. 我的经验是，提出此问题的人通常正考虑接受生育治疗，偶尔也会以“我这次假 期会受孕吗？”或类似形式出现。

In principle, nothing is simpler: we look for an aspect linking mother (Lord 1 and the Moon) and baby (Lord 5) in the usual way. Lord 5 and one or both of the querent’s significators being in a fertile sign (Cancer, Scorpio, Pisces) makes the judegment more confident. Even if all three of these significators are in barren signs (Gemini, Leo, Virgo), a clear aspect between strong planets will still give conception. As supporting testimonies, a benefic planet in the 5th house, especially Jupiter in Cancer or Pisces, in helpful. So is the North Node. 原则上，没有比这更简单的了：我们按照常规方式寻找连接母亲（1 宫主与月亮） 和婴儿（5 宫主）的相位。5 宫主以及问卜者的一颗或两颗征象星位于肥沃星座 （巨蟹座、天蝎座、双鱼座）会使判断更具信心。即使这三颗征象星皆位于贫瘠 星座（双子座、狮子座、处女座），强旺行星间清晰的相位仍会显示受孕。作为 辅助征兆，吉星位于 5 宫——尤其是木星在巨蟹座或双鱼座——是有利的。北交 点亦然。

Watch for afflictions to the significators or the 5th house, especially from Saturn. Satrun in the 5th, especially if close to the cusp, is a strong negative testimony (unless it is Lord 1, when this placement would reflect the querent’s interest in the subject).

Lord 5 combust is a definite No, unless the Sun is Lord 1. 需注意征象星或 5 宫所受的侵害，尤其是来自土星的。土星在 5 宫（特别是靠近 宫头时）是强烈的否定征兆（除非它是 1 宫主，此时此位置仅反映问卜者对此事 的关注）。5 宫主被燃烧明确为“否”，除非太阳是 1 宫主。

Do remember the basic point that Juptier and Venus are not necessarily helpful. How benefic they can be depends on their condition. A client asked about her inability to conceive. Jupiter was just inside the 7th house, in Gemini. Being in its detriment, it afflicts the house it is in: the husband. Jupiter is natural ruler of sperm. In its detriment and in a barren sign: the husband has a low sperm count. Or Venus in Virgo: dignity by triplictiy, debility by fall, in a barren sign; fun, but no conception. It is well to remind the querent that, even the best of astrologers being fallible, prediction is not a reliable form of contraception. 务必记住一个基本点：木星和金星未必总是有益的。它们的吉性程度取决于其状 态。曾有一位客户询问她为何难以受孕。木星刚好在 7 宫内，位于双子座。因其 处于落陷状态，会侵害其所在宫位：即丈夫。木星是精子的先天守护星。处于落 陷且位于贫瘠星座：表明丈夫精子数量少。又如金星在处女座：处于三分尊贵的 位置，但因弱势而衰弱，且位于贫瘠星座；愉悦，但无法受孕。最好提醒问卜者， 即使最优秀的占星师也可能出错，预测并非可靠的避孕方式。

### ✸If the man asks ‘Will we have a child?’ an aspect from Lord 5 to either Lord 1 or

Lord 7 (the woman) will give a Yes. If the woman asks, an aspect between Lord 5 and Lord 7 will not do. ✷

### ✸若男性询问“我们会有孩子吗？”，5 宫主与 1 宫主或 7 宫主（代表女方）

成相会给出“是”的答案。若女性询问，5 宫主与 7 宫主成相则无效。✷

Charts for questions about fertility treatment are often finely balanced, and tact is required in dealing with the querent. The charts are finely balanced because the situation is finely balanced: if the couple was brimming over with fertility, the question would not be asked. Often the judgement is either, ‘It really doesn’t look like it; but do remember that the astrologer is fallible’, or ‘I can’t give a definite Yes, but there is sufficient potential here that you may think it worth proceeding’. 关于生育治疗问题的星盘常常处于微妙的平衡状态，需要技巧来应对问卜者。星 盘之所以微妙平衡，是因为现实情况本就如此：若夫妇双方生育能力充沛，便不 会提出此问题。判断往往要么是“看起来确实不太可能；但请记住占星师也可能 出错”，要么是“我无法给出明确的‘是’，但这里有足够的潜力，您或许认为 值得尝试”。

First look for potential fertility: check Lord 1, 5, 7 and 11, the Moon, the Moon’s dispositor. We consider Lords 5 and 11 as significators of the husband and his baby-potential (though for straight ‘Will I conceive?’ questions joining Lord 11 to Lord 1 will not give conception).

首先寻找潜在的生育能力：检查 1 宫主、5 宫主、7 宫主、11 宫主、月亮以及月 亮的定位星。我们将 5 宫主和 11 宫主视为丈夫及其生育潜力的征象星（但对于 直接的“我会受孕吗？”问题，连接 11 宫主与 1 宫主不会显示受孕）。

### ✸There is no need to involve the Moon’s dispositor. There is much superfluity in

the old texts, based on the idea that the more testimonies we can throw at a question, the greater our chance of being able to scrape up a pleasing answer. This regardless of whether there is any relevance in those testimonies. This is an example of such. ✷

### ✸无需涉及月亮的定位星。古典文献中有大量冗余内容，其理念是：我们能为

一个问题堆砌的征兆越多，就越有可能凑出一个令人满意的答案。这完全不顾那 些征兆是否相关。此即一例。✷

Are they in fertile or barren signs? The other signs are neutral. Fertile signs are positive, but the absence of barren signs is enough to give hope. Do not consider the signs on the cusps of these houses: with so many houses in play, we are most likely to find a scattering of fertile and barren there, but the house rulers can be anywhere. 它们位于肥沃星座还是贫瘠星座？其他星座为中性。肥沃星座是积极的，但没有 贫瘠星座就足以带来希望。无需考虑这些宫头的星座：由于涉及多个宫位，我们 很可能会在那里发现肥沃与贫瘠星座混杂出现，但宫主星可能位于任何地方。

Then consider benefits or afflictions to houses 1,5,7,11 and their rulers. By now you may have a clear No, in which case you can stop. As long as testimony of barrenness is not overwhelming, carry on to look for an aspect to show that what potential there is will be realised. Do not look to the 10th house for the fertility treatment: the 10th is the treatment in sickness charts, but is not relevant here. If conception is to be by fertility treatment, a connection between mother and baby by either collection or translation of light is typical. It doesn’t matter which planet is making this connection, or which house it rules: it still gives conception. The involvement of a third planet in translation and collection of light mirrors the third-party involvement in fertility treatment. 接着考虑对 1 宫、5 宫、7 宫、11 宫及其宫主星的助益或侵害。至此，你可能已 得出明确的“否”，若是如此便可停止。只要不育的征兆并非压倒性的，就继续 寻找显示现有潜力将实现的相位。勿将 10 宫视为生育治疗：在疾病盘中 10 宫代 表治疗，但于此不相关。若受孕需通过生育治疗实现，通过光线聚集或光线传递 连接母亲与婴儿是典型情况。由哪颗行星建立此连接、或它掌管哪个宫位并不重 要：它依然显示受孕。光线聚集与光线传递中涉及第三颗行星，正反映了生育治 疗中第三方的参与。

Once you have a planet connecting Mum and baby, consider its nature (nice planet or nasty planet?), its receptions with Lords 1 and 5 (is it in Mum’s sign, so wanting to help her, or is it in her fall, harming her?), and whatever other testimonies there may be around the 5th house. The aspect is enough to show conception; these other factors

will tell what happens next – particularly whether the baby will be carried full term. 一旦有行星连接了母亲与婴儿，需考虑其属性（是吉星还是凶星？）、它与 1 宫主和 5 宫主的接纳关系（它位于母亲的星座因而想帮助她，还是位于她的弱势 星座从而伤害她？），以及 5 宫周围可能存在的其他征兆。相位足以显示受孕； 这些其他因素将告知后续发展——尤其是胎儿能否足月。

Then the most important step: engage your brain and, more important still, your heart before speaking to the querent. You cannot lie; but all that is seen does not need to be told. 然后是最重要的一步：在与问卜者交谈前，启动你的头脑，更重要的是，启动你 的心。你不能说谎；但所见并非皆需言明。

Will I ever conceive? 我未来能否受孕？

As with ‘Will I ever marry?’ we must consider the default option here. If the querent is 20, we must judge Yes unless the chart shows a clear No. If the querent is 50, we must judge No unless there is a very clear Yes. 与“我会结婚吗？”类似，此处我们必须考虑默认情况。若问卜者 20 岁，我们 必须判断为“是”，除非星盘清晰显示“否”。若问卜者 50 岁，我们必须判断 为“否”，除非有非常明确的“是”的征兆。

For the ‘will I ever’ part we need only to consider the potential, as above: check Lord 1,5,7 and 11, the Moon, the Moon’s dispositor. 对于“未来能否”部分，我们仅需如上所述考虑潜在可能性：检查 1 宫主、5 宫 主、7 宫主、11 宫主、月亮及月亮的定位星。

### ✸As noted in the addition above, there is no reason to bring the Moon’s dispositor

into judgement.✷

### ✸正如前文补充说明所述，没有理由将月亮的定位星纳入判断。✷

Are they in fertile or barren signs? The other signs are neutral. Fertile signs are positive, but just the absence of barren signs gives hope. Do not consider the signs on the cusps of these houses: it is the signs the house rulers are in that concern us. If there is an aspect between Lords 1 and 5, so much the better, but for a querent of 20, some sign of fertility and the absence of major afflictions to the 5th house or its ruler is sufficient to judge Yes. 它们是否位于肥沃星座或贫瘠星座？其他星座为中性。肥沃星座是积极的，但仅 无贫瘠星座便足以带来希望。勿考虑这些宫头的星座：我们关注的是宫主星所在 的星座。若 1 宫主与 5 宫主之间有相位，则更佳；但对于 20 岁的问卜者，只要 有一些生育能力的迹象，且 5 宫或其宫主星无重大侵害，便足以判断为“是”。

If our querent is 50, we would need to see all or most of our key planets in fertile signs and a strong aspect linking Lords 1 and 5, with no serious afflictions. 若我们的问卜者为 50 岁，则需要看到所有或大多数关键行星位于肥沃星座，且 有强相位连接 1 宫主与 5 宫主，且无严重侵害。

This question is often accompanied by a ‘when’, or indeed is phrased as ‘when’ with the ‘will I’ assumed. In the latter case, unless the Yes leaps out of the chart in the form of an aspect, we must determine the ‘if’ before tackling the ‘when’. Once we have decided that the querent will conceive, we know that the timing must be in the chart somewhere. Well-behaved charts give us a clear aspect to work from; but not all charts are so well-behaved. This can demand a stretch of the astrological muscles. But with a long-term issue like this we can push planets through the usual prohibitions, such as other aspects or changes of sign. The only pass-nots are station and conjunction with the Sun. With this freedom, you will find a way of linking querent and Lord 5. NB: you can do this only because you have already found that the main answer to the question is ‘Yes’. Once you have connected Mum and baby, calculate the timing in the usual way. 此问题常伴随“何时”的询问，或实际上以“何时”的形式提出，而“是否”是 隐含前提。在后一种情况下，除非星盘中以相位形式明确跳出“是”的答案，否 则我们必须先确定“是否”，再处理“何时”。一旦我们断定问卜者将会受孕， 便知时机必然隐藏在星盘某处。规整的星盘会给出清晰的相位供我们推算；但并 非所有星盘都如此规整。这可能需要对占星技巧稍作延伸运用。但对于此类长期 性问题，我们可以推动行星超越通常的阻碍，例如其他相位或换星座。唯一的不 可逾越条件是停滞和与太阳合相。凭借此自由度，你将找到连接问卜者与 5 宫主 的方法。注意：你之所以能这样做，仅因你已确定问题的主要答案为“是”。一 旦连接了母亲与婴儿，便按常规方式计算时间。

### ✸Do not be tempted to bring in the Sun as natural ruler of Man and Venus as natural

ruler of Woman in questions like this. Their use is only to help pick apart the psychological web that binds two people together ✷ chapter 21). They are not relevant here. ✷

### ✸切勿在此类问题中引入太阳作为男性的先天守护星或金星作为女性的先天守

护星。它们的用途仅在于帮助剖析将两个人绑定在一起的心理网络（第 21 章）， 与此处无关。✷

Number and gender 数量和性别

Do not strive for precision in predicting the number of children the querent will have. This is, as Lilly would say, ‘too scrupulous a querent’. Our choices are: 1, 1or 2, a few,

lots. This is quite accurate enough. 切勿强求精确预测问卜者将有多少子女。正如 Lilly 所言，这是“过于苛求的问 卜者”。我们的选择范围是：1 个、1 或 2 个、数个、许多。这已足够准确。

Consider Lords 1,5,7 and 11, the Moon, the Moon’s dispositor. 考虑 1 宫主、5 宫主、7 宫主、11 宫主、月亮及月亮的定位星。

### ✸Again, as explained in the addition on p. 206, don’t involve the Moon’s dispositor

in this.✷

### ✸再次说明，如第 331 页补充解释所述，不要在此涉及月亮的定位星。✷

Once you have decided that there will be at least one child, how strong are the testimonies of fertility? All these planets in fertile signs would be testimony for ‘lots’; only one fertile would suggest only one child. The planets showing fertility being accidentally strong (seriously strong – there is no need to quibble here) increases the number they are likely to give. Angularity is particularly important here; but vary your idea of ‘accidentally strong’ to fit the question. For example, suppose Lord 1 is Juptier in Cancer – about as fertile an indication as can be – and is close to the 5th cusp: this would be a powerful testimony for many children, even though it is not angular. 一旦你判定至少会有一个孩子，生育能力的征兆有多强？所有这些行星皆位于肥 沃星座将是“许多”的征兆；仅有一颗位于肥沃星座则可能暗示只有一个孩子。 显示生育能力的行星若偶然强旺（显著强旺——此处无需纠结）会提升其可能带 来的数量。角宫在此尤为重要；但需根据问题调整你对“偶然强旺”的理解。例 如，假设 1 宫主是位于巨蟹座的木星——这已是生育能力最旺盛的指示——且靠 近 5 宫头：这将是多子女的有力征兆，即便它不位于角宫。

Note that although Gemini and Virgo are barren signs, they are also double-bodied. If the overall judgement is that the querent will have children, they can give more than one. 请注意，虽然双子座和处女座是贫瘠星座，但它们也属双重性质星座。若整体判 断为问卜者将会有孩子，它们可能预示不止一个。

For gender, consider the same planets: are they masculine or feminine? Are the signs they are in masculine or feminine? Although it is tempting to ignore the fact that the Moon is feminine, because the Moon is present in every such assessment, I suggest that including this – giving feminine a head start – helps reduce the imbalance in favour of masculine. Give added weight to any these planets with good accidental strength. 关于性别，考虑同样的行星：它们是阳性还是阴性？它们所在的星座是阳性还是 阴性？尽管很容易忽略月亮属阴性这一事实（因为月亮存在于每一项此类评估 中），但我建议纳入此点——让阴性占些先机——有助于减少偏向阳性的不平衡。 对于任何具有良好偶然强度的行星，可给予额外权重。

The majority verdict gives the sex of the first child. If there is a significant dissenting opinion, this can be taken to show the sex of the second – if you have judged that there will be a second. Further than that we need not go. 多数意见决定第一个孩子的性别。若有显著不同意见，可视为第二个孩子性别的 显示——前提是你已判定会有第二个孩子。更进一步的预测则无需进行。

### ✸This method of determining the sex of the child or children does not work. By

which I don’t mean that it works no better than tossing a coin: it works far worse. The proportion of male and female births is roughly 50/50. But with only two female planets, this method gives a huge imbalance in favour of male. The reason for this is simple. Throughout most of astrology’s history, the way the astrologer put a smile on the client’s face was by announcing ‘It’s a boy!’ This is one of the crassest examples of the fairground astrology with which the old texts are littered.

### ✸这种判定孩子性别的方法并不奏效。我并非指其准确率与抛硬币无异：而是

远比抛硬币更差。男女出生比例大致为 50/50。但由于只有两颗阴性行星，此方 法会严重偏向男性。原因很简单：在占星学历史的大部分时期，占星师让客户面 露笑容的方式就是宣布“是个男孩！”。这是市集占星学最粗陋的例子之一，古 典文献中充斥着此类内容。

I don’t know a method that does work. What would seem the obvious solution – looking only at whether Lord 5 is in a male or female sign – does not. But I am more than happy to have no answer to this one. If we remember that giving the answer that does not match the querent’s whim is likely to result in there being no child at all, a discreet silence would seem by far the better option. While, as with pregnancy testing, such answer are increasingly available elsewhere. 我不知道有何方法真正有效。看似显而易见的解决方案——仅看 5 宫主位于阳性 还是阴性星座——也行不通。但我非常乐意对此没有答案。如果我们记得，给出 不符合问卜者期待的答案很可能导致孩子根本不会降生，那么谨慎的沉默似乎是 好得多的选择。何况，正如验孕一样，此类答案如今越来越多地可通过其他途径 获得。

On which subject, there are other questions that clients will try to ask: ‘Is the baby my wife’s carrying really mine?’ ‘Is the guy who’s raised me this last 30 years really my father?’ ‘Is she really a virgin?’ Some of my students have heatedly disagreed with me on this, but so far as I can see the answer to such questions is ‘Yes’, and this does not demand the casting of a chart. Such questions are beneath human dignity. ✷ 关于此话题，客户可能试图提出其他问题：“我妻子怀的孩子真的是我的吗？” “过去 30 年抚养我的人真的是我父亲吗？”“她真的是处女吗？”我的一些学 生对此与我激烈争论，但在我看来，此类问题的答案是“是的”，且无需起盘。 这类问题有损人格尊严。✷

### ✸When will the baby be born?

### ✸孩子何时出生？

With this question we are looking for some change in the condition of Lord 5, happening within a realistic time-frame. The first thing to look for is a change of sign, showing the baby’s situation changing – almost as if the baby is moving house. Well-behaved charts provide such a testimony. With less well-behaved charts, the best I can suggest is scratching the head and looking around for some plausible indication of significant change. We must be open to whatever the chart offers. The common assumption is that birth will be shown by an applying aspect between Mum and Baby. This makes no sense. An aspect brings things into contact, but Mum and Baby are already in closer contact than they will ever have again. ✷ 对于此问题，我们寻找 5 宫主状况的某种变化，且发生在合理的时间范围内。首 先要看的是换星座，显示婴儿处境的变化——几乎如同婴儿在搬家。规整的星盘 会提供此类征兆。对于不那么规整的星盘，我最好的建议是挠头环顾，寻找某种 合理的重大变化迹象。我们必须对星盘呈现的任何信息保持开放。常见的假设是， 出生将通过母亲与婴儿之间的入相位显示。这并不合理。相位使事物产生联系， 但母亲与婴儿已经处于比未来任何时候都更紧密的联系中。✷

ADOPTION 领养

The child that the querent is hoping to adopt is 11th house: 5th from the 7th – someone else’s child (unless it is the child of someone specific: e.g. the sister’s child would be 5th from the 3rd). The usual question is ‘Will I get this child?’ for which we hope to find an aspect between the querent’s significators and Lord 11. 问卜者希望领养的孩子对应 11 宫：即 7 宫的 5 宫——他人的孩子（除非是特定 某人的孩子：例如姐妹的孩子则为 3 宫的 5 宫）。通常的问题是“我能得到这个 孩子吗？”，对此我们希望找到问卜者的征象星与 11 宫主之间的相位。

Once the child has been adopted, it is the querent’s. All question about it should be judged from the 5th house, exactly as if it were a natural child. 一旦孩子被领养，它便是问卜者的。所有关于它的问题都应从 5 宫判断，完全如 同亲生子女一般。

# Sixth and Eighth House

# Questions

# 6 和 8 宫的问题

MEDICAL QUESTIONS 医学问题

The judgement of medical questions is a huge subject, to deal with which in full would demand in itself a book longer than this one. I can do no more here than give an overview of the method, which will suffice for many simple enquiries, and to point the reader requiring a more exhaustive treatment of this topic in the right direction. 判断医学问题是一个庞大的主题，若要充分探讨，其本身所需篇幅就远超过本书。 在此，我只能概述其方法，这对许多简单的咨询来说已经足够，并为需要更详尽 研究此主题的读者指明正确的方向。

The vital first point is that although the 6th is the house of illness, it does not signify the illness in a medical question. Suppose the question were ‘Will I win the gold medal?’ and Lord 1 was applying to aspect with Lord 10 (success, victory: the medal), when the aspect was prohibited by Lord 6. Judgement would be, ‘You would; but you’re going to get ill’. A question such as this has illness as one issue among many. In the chart for a medical question, however, the whole chart is concerned with this sick person suffering from this illness: the subject of illness is not confined to one house. Do not, then, leap to Lord 6 as significator of the illness. 至关重要的第一点是：尽管 6 宫是疾病宫，但在医学问题中，它并不象征疾病本 身。假设问题是“我会赢得金牌吗？”，而 1 宫主正与 10 宫主（成功、胜利： 即金牌）形成相位，但该相位受到 6 宫主的阻碍。判断将是：“你本可以；但你 会生病”。像这样的问题中，疾病只是众多议题之一。然而，在一张针对医学问 题的星盘中，整张盘都关乎这位病人及其所患的疾病：疾病的主题并不仅限于一 个宫位。因此，不要急于将 6 宫主当作疾病的征象星。

Prognosis or diagnosis? 预后还是诊断？

Medical questions fall into two groups: ‘What is wrong?’ and ‘What will happen?’ It is the diagnosis question that is too complex to be handled here; but I can give the

method. Following this will enable you to identify the planet that signifies the illness. You can then refer to Richard Saunders’ Astrological Judgemnet and Practice of Physic for the diagnosis. 医学问题分为两类：“问题出在哪里？”和“将会发生什么？”其中诊断问题过 于复杂，无法在此详述；但我可以给出方法。遵循此法将使你能够识别象征疾病 的星体。然后，你可以查阅理 Richard Saunders（理查德·桑德斯）的《Astrological Judgemnet and Practice of Physic》以进行诊断。

38. London, 1677. There is a good modern edition in the Astrology Classics series from The Astrology Center of America.
38. 伦敦，1677 年。美国占星中心出版的占星经典系列中有很好的现代版本。

Saunders was a contemporary of Lilly, who held him in high esteem. His book contains a breakdown of each planet in each part of each sign, describing the ailments that his placement shows, their immediate cause (the bodily imbalance of which the symptoms are a manifestation), and what can be done to treat them. He also gives a method of approaching the horary question on illness, but ignore this: follow it and you will be consistently wrong. Use the method I give here, then go to Saunders for the diagnosis. Saunders 是 Lilly 的同时代人，Lilly 对他评价甚高。他的书详细分解了每一颗星 体在每一个星座的每一部分，描述了其所落位置显示的疾病、其直接原因（症状 所体现的身体失衡）以及可以采取的治疗方法。他也提供了一种处理疾病卜卦问 题的方法，但请忽略它：如果遵循它，你将会出错。使用我这里给出的方法，然 后再参考 Saunders 进行诊断。

Warning: Saunders, as is usual in traditional medicine, divides ailments into four categories, from those of the first degree, which are the mildest, to those of the fourth degree, which are ‘beyond nature’ and often fatal. You will no doubt remember the films where the cops give someone ‘the third degree’: a serious beating, but not fatal. These degrees must be taken within the context given by the illness itself: if the querent’s cold is described as being ‘in the fourth degree’, this means that it is a bad cold; it does not mean the querent will die from it. 警告：Saunders 如同传统医学中常见的那样，将疾病分为四个等级，从最轻微的 一级疾病，到“超乎自然”且常常致命的四级疾病。你肯定记得电影里警察给某 人“第三级”待遇：一顿痛打，但不致命。这些等级必须放在疾病本身所提供的 语境中来理解：如果问卜者的感冒被描述为“处于四级”，这只意味着这是一场 重感冒；并不意味着问卜者会因此而死。

The methods given in the texts, including Saunders’ Astrological Judgement, are confused and often faulty, largely because the authors mix horary method with the method of judging a decumbiture chart, with no distinction between the two. A decumbiture is the chart set for the moment at which the patient takes to his bed, or when a sample of his urine is delivered to the astrologer/physician. Decumbiture is far more cumbersome than horary, and is to be used only if you are the treating physician

and if you will be visiting the patient every couple of days to revise your treatment. 包括 Saunders《Astrological Judgement》在内的传统文献中给出的方法混乱且 常常有误，很大程度上是因为作者们混用了卜卦方法和判断卧病盘的方法，而没 有区分二者。卧病盘是为病人卧床不起之时，或将其尿液样本送达占星师/医师 之时所起的星盘。卧病盘比卜卦盘繁琐得多，仅在你本人是主治医师且每隔几天 就会探视病人以调整治疗方案时才使用。

### ✸ I would urge humility in these questions. I am appalled at the readiness with

which some ‘medical astrologers’ offer prescription despite having no knowledge of medicine beyond that gained by reading two books or attending a weekend workshop. The astrologer-physicians of the past understood medicine as well as astrology. Astrology alone is not enough. ✷

### ✷我敦促在处理此类问题时保持谦逊。一些“医学占星师”仅仅读过两本书或

参加过一个周末研讨会，对医学知识知之甚少，却动辄开出处方，这令我感到震 惊。过去的占星师兼医师们既通晓占星学也精通医学。仅有占星学是不够的。✷

【Enough, already! - Posted on February 25th, 2014 【够了，到此为止！- 发布于 2014 年 2 月 25 日

With medical matters perhaps more than with questions on any other topic it ’ s important to remember the general rule: answer the question, then stop! We have no reason to assume that the stars will answer questions that have not been asked, so if I’ m asking about my headaches I will not also find a diagnosis for my indigestion. Fail to do this and you’ll find that every querent is suffering from every illness known to man.】 在医疗问题上，也许比其他任何主题的问题都更需要牢记这条通用规则：回答完 问题，然后就此打住！我们没有理由假设星辰会回答那些没有被问及的问题，所 以如果我问我头痛的事，我不会同时找到我消化不良的病因。不这样做的话，你 会发现每个问卦者都遭受着人类已知的所有疾病的折磨。】

The starting-point: am I ill? 起点：我病了吗？

This is occasionally the question asked: ‘Are these snuffles going to turn into a cold that will ruin my holiday?’ ‘Should I call off my world record attempt?’ More often, this question is redundant: if the person were not ill, the question would not have been asked. Either way, this is our point of entry to the medical horary. 这种情况偶尔会被问到：“这些鼻塞会发展成毁掉我假期的感冒吗？”“我应该 取消我的世界纪录尝试吗？”更常见的情况是，这个问题是多余的：如果这个人 没有生病，就不会问出这个问题。无论是哪种情况，这都是我们进入医学卜卦的 切入点。

Look at Lord 1, if the querent is asking about himself, or the ruler of whichever house signifies the person. I shall call it Lord 1 throughout this section; adjust as necessary if the querent is asking about someone else. What is its nature: hot/dry, cold/dry, hot/moist or cold/moist? Then look at the sign it is in: what is its nature? If the planet is in a sign that does not exactly match its nature, this is an indication that the person is indeed unwell. So also if the planet is debilitated, retrograde, combust or otherwise afflicted. Note that a planet can be in a sign of contrary nature and yet rule that sign, e.g. hot/dry Mars in cold/moist Scorpio. 观察 1 宫主（如果是问卜者在询问自己），或象征此人的那个宫位的守护星。在 本节中，我将统称其为 1 宫主；如果问卜者是在询问他人，请根据需要调整。它 的属性是什么：热/燥、冷/燥、热/湿还是冷/湿？然后观察它所落的星座：这个 星座的属性是什么？如果行星所处的星座与其自身属性不完全匹配，这表明此人 的确身体不适。同样，如果行星处于衰弱、逆行、燃烧或其他受克状态也是如此。 请注意，行星可能落在一个与自身属性相反的星座，却同时守护那个星座，例如 热/燥的火星落在冷/湿的天蝎座。

The significator of the illness will be whichever planet is harming Lord 1. If Lord 1 is in a sign of different nature to its own, this will be the ruler of that sign. So also if Lord 1 is in its detriment or fall. If Lord 1 is combust, take the Sun, which is the afflicting planet; it is also worth having a look at the ruler of whichever sign the two planets are in. If Lord 1 is suffering from an adverse aspect, take the aspecting planet. Look also at planets in tight aspect to the Ascendant, especially if the problem is located in the head or face. 疾病的征象星将是那个正在伤害 1 宫主的行星。如果 1 宫主位于一个与其自身属 性不同的星座，那么该星座的守护星就是疾病的征象星。如果 1 宫主处于其落陷 或弱势，同样如此。如果 1 宫主被燃烧，则取太阳作为克害行星；同时值得看看 这两颗行星所在星座的守护星。如果 1 宫主正受到一个不利相位的影响，则取那 颗与之成相位的行星。也要观察与上升点紧密成相位的行星，尤其是当问题位于 头部或面部时。

Lord 1 can itself signify the illness, most commonly if it is in a sign that it rules but which is of contrary nature, or if it is retrograde. If retrograde, look also at the ruler of the sign it is in. 1 宫主本身也可以象征疾病，最常见的情况是它落在由其守护但属性相反的星座 中，或者当它逆行时。如果逆行，也要查看其所在星座的守护星。

There can be more than one significator for the illness. Sometimes this shows different levels of causation (‘You are suffering from palpitations of the heart, but this is exacerbated by your financial worries’); sometimes there is more than one problem. Note that any planet in any condition can be a significator of illness: it’s not only the bad guys. When Jupiter was passing through Cancer, I saw many charts where he was significator and the illness was marked by an excess of moisture. 疾病的征象星可能不止一个。有时这表明不同层次的病因（“你患有心悸，但这

因你的财务忧虑而加剧”）；有时则表示存在不止一个问题。请注意，任何状态 下的任何行星都可能成为疾病的征象星：不只是“坏家伙们”。当木星行经巨蟹 座时，我看到许多星盘中木星是征象星，而疾病的特点是湿气过重。

Now that you have the significator(s) of the illness, refer to Saunders for the diagnosis. Writing in the Seventeenth century, Saunders does not use the same medical model as a modern doctor, but his diagnostic is none the less accurate for that. 既然你已找到了疾病的征象星，便可查阅 Saunders 以进行诊断。Saunders 写于十 七世纪，所用的医学模型与现代医生不同，但他的诊断准确度并未因此降低。

### ✸This checking if planet and sign are compatible is only for the significator of the

sick person. In almost all cases, we are not trying to determine if the person is indeed ill (‘Get back to work!’) but following Lilly’s terminology to show us the significator of the illness. There is no point in checking whether the significator of the illness, the significator of the body-part affected, or anything else is in a compatible sign. Only the significator of the person.

### ✸这种检查行星与星座是否相合的方法，仅适用于生病之人的征象星。在几乎

所有情况下，我们并非试图确定此人是否真的生病（“回去工作！”），而是遵 循 Lilly 的术语来找到疾病的征象星。检查疾病的征象星、受影响身体部位的征 象星或其他任何事物是否处于相合的星座，是毫无意义的。只检查人的征象星。

There is no significance in whether the sign the planet is in is total incompatible or only partly so. If the sign is totally incompatible (for instance, a cold/dry planet in a hot/moist sign) this does not mean the illness is more severe than if only partly incompatible (e.g. a cold/dry planet in a cold/moist sign). This incompatibility tells us nothing about the nature of the illness. All it does is point us towards the planet that signifies that illness. 行星所在的星座是完全不兼容还是部分不兼容，这一点没有特殊意义。如果星座 完全不相容（例如，一颗冷/燥的行星位于热/湿的星座），这并不意味着疾病比 部分不相容（例如，一颗冷/燥的行星位于冷/湿的星座）时更严重。这种不相容 性并不能告诉我们关于疾病属性的任何信息。它的作用仅仅是指向我们象征该疾 病的那颗行星。

Do not use the Moon as cosignificator of the querent in medical questions. One planet is quite enough! Use two and you will be inflicting everyone with far more than their fair share of illnesses. 在医学问题中，不要使用月亮作为问卜者的共同征象星。一颗行星已经足够了！ 使用两颗，你会给每个人强加远超其份内的疾病。

When considering body-parts, use only the accidental rulers (i.e. the ruler of the relevant house), not the natural rulers. For instance, for the person’s heart, look to the Lord of the 5th, not the Sun. ✷

当考虑身体部位时，只使用偶然的守护星（即相关宫位的宫主星），而不是先天 守护星。例如，对于人的心脏，看 5 宫主，而不是太阳。✷

What will happen? 将会发生什么？

If the significator of the illness is in a fixed sign, the illness will be long-lasting; if in a cardinal sign, it will be short; if in a mutable sign it will come and go, or give better days and worse days. Qualify this by the sign that the person’s own significator is in, according to the same criteria. 如果疾病的征象星位于固定星座，则疾病将会持久；若位于基本星座，则病程较 短；若位于变动星座，则病情会反复，时好时坏。请根据同样的标准，参考问卜 者自身征象星所在的星座来进一步判断。

### ✸The amount of essential dignity or debility the significator of the illness has is of

no importance. Illness is of its nature unpleasant. If the illness is signified by Jupiter in Pisces it is not the best fun you’ve ever had. Not it is especially nasty if signified by debilitated Saturn. ✷

### ✸疾病的征象星拥有多少先天尊贵或衰弱并不重要。疾病就其属性而言就是不

愉快的。如果疾病由位于双鱼座的木星象征，那也绝不是你有过的最有趣的体验。 同样，如果由衰弱的土星象征，也并非就意味着格外凶险。✷

Look at whatever it is that is afflicting the person’s significator. Is the significator moving away from it or moving towards it? For example, if illness is shown by the significator being in an incompatible sign, has it recently entered that sign, or is it about to leave it? If it leaves, will its condition get better or worse? If the affliction is an aspect, is the aspect applying (getting worse) or separating (getting better)? 观察任何正在伤害问卜者征象星的事物。征象星是正在远离它，还是正在靠近 它？例如，如果疾病通过征象星位于不相容的星座来显示，那么它是刚刚进入该 星座，还是即将离开？如果它离开，其状况会变好还是变坏？如果伤害来自一个 相位，那么该相位是正在入相位（恶化）还是出相位（好转）？

Is the significator changing direction? A planet in first station (turning retrograde) is likened to a man taking to his sickbed: he is ill and will get worse. A planet in second station is likened to a man rising from his sickbed: he feels shaky now, but is recovering. 征象星是否正在改变方向？一颗处于第一停滞期（即将逆行）的行星，好比一个 人卧病在床：他病了并且会恶化。一颗处于第二停滞期（即将恢复顺行）的行星， 则好比一个人正从病床上起身：他现在感觉虚弱，但正在康复。

### ✸If the question is ‘When will I get better?’ remember than in most cases recovery

is a gradual process, not something of an instant, like turning on a light. Suppose recovery is shown by the significator changing sign in 10 degrees. The judgement would be ‘10 days (or weeks, or months) and then some’. The patient will be more or less back to normal, but the reality of the situation is that the final symptoms usually linger a while, like guests who have outstayed their welcome. ✷

### ✸如果问题是“我什么时候会好转？”，请记住在大多数情况下，康复是一个

渐进的过程，而非像开灯那样瞬间完成。假设康复是通过征象星在 10 度后换座 来显示的。那么判断将是“10 天（或周，或月）之后，然后还有些时日”。病 人将大致恢复正常，但实际情况是最后的症状通常还会逗留一阵，就像过了欢迎 期的客人一样。✷

Mars afflictions are usually acute, Saturn afflictions long-lasting. But do factor in the nature of the problem: the breaking of a leg is a quick, Mars-type action, but recovery is slow. 火星造成的伤害通常是急性的，土星造成的伤害则较为长久。但务必结合问题的 属性来考量：腿部骨折是一个快速、火星类型的行动，但恢复却很缓慢。

These general indications apply to run-of-the-mill, non-threatening illnesses. My experience is that people with run-of-the-mill, non-threatening illnesses are less likely to consult a horary astrologer than those with illnesses that may prove fatal. With the majority of medical enquiries we must begin by working out if the patient will live or die. So: 这些普遍征象适用于常规的、不具威胁性的疾病。根据我的经验，与那些可能致 命的疾病患者相比，患有常规、不具威胁性疾病的人咨询卜卦占星师的可能性更 小。对于大多数医学咨询，我们必须首先判断病人是生是死。因此：

QUESTIONS ON DEATH 关于死亡的问题

I will consider here all questions about death, those that involve illness and those that do not. 我将在此探讨所有关于死亡的问题，包括涉及疾病的和不涉及疾病的。

You may well decide that you do not wish to handle questions on death, but it is as well that you should know how they are judged. Questions do not have to be overtly about death for it to be involved: in many circumstances we need to look at testimonies of death to assure ourselves that it is not going to happen (e.g. a political exile asking ‘Is it safe for me to go home?’). Although the idea of predicting death may seem off-putting, there are many reasons for people sincerely wanting to know.

The most common are when the querent has to make financial provision for the care of an elderly relative (‘Do I extend the overdraft, or do I need to remortgage the house?’) and when the patient is receiving treatment for a potentially fatal illness. 你很可能会决定不希望处理关于死亡的问题，但最好还是了解如何判断这类问题。 有些问题并不一定直接关于死亡，但死亡可能牵涉其中：在许多情况下，我们需 要审视死亡的征象，以确保它不会发生（例如，一位政治流亡者询问“我回家安 全吗？”）。尽管预测死亡的想法可能令人不快，但人们真诚希望知道的原因有 很多。最常见的情况是，当问卜者需要为照顾年长亲属做财务安排时（“我是该 延长透支额度，还是需要重新抵押房子？”），以及当病人正在接受可能致命的 疾病治疗时。

Although the techniques of predicting death from a horary are reliable, do remember that you are not. Except in cases of serious illness, I most strongly advise that you do not predict death unless, if at all possible, you have checked with the birthchart. This is not a fail-safe, but it does mean you must get it wrong twice to be in error with your judgement. “So why bother with the horary if I’m going to refer to the nativity anyway?” Because it will give you a valuable short-cut: instead of searching through years of progressions, it will take you straight to a likely date. 尽管根据卜卦预测死亡的技术是可靠的，但请务必记住，你本人并不可靠。除非 是重病情况，我最强烈建议你不要预测死亡，除非——如果有可能——你已经核 对过本命盘。这并非万全之策，但这意味着你必须犯两次错误，你的判断才会出 错。“那么，如果我反正都要参考本命盘，为什么还要费心进行卜卦呢？”因为 它能给你提供一个宝贵的捷径：与其搜索多年的推运，它会直接带你锁定一个可 能的日期。

As always, be realistic with the precision you provide. If death will occur next week, it is reasonable that you should give the day, or at least whether it will be early or late in the week. If the death will occur in twenty years’ time, giving the year is accuracy enough. Achieving greater precision is very clever, but our purpose is not to demonstrate how clever we are. 一如既往，对于你提供的精确度要现实一些。如果死亡将在下周发生，你有理由 给出具体哪一天，或者至少是这周早些还是晚些时候。如果死亡将在二十年后发 生，给出年份就足够精确了。达到更高的精度非常聪明，但我们的目的不是为了 展示我们有多聪明。

There are two main enquiries on this subject: the general ‘When will I die?’ and the more particular ‘Will I die’ referring to death from this illness that the querent has now. 关于这个主题主要有两类询问：笼统的“我什么时候会死？”和更具体的“我会 死吗？”（特指问卜者目前所患的此病是否会致死）。

When will I die? 我什么时候会死？

The great thing with this question is that the event is certain, so we know that there must be a timing in the chart somewhere. This means we can set aside many of the usual rules. We can ignore prohibitions: they can be taken to show events along the way. We can push our significators as far as we need through sign after sign. There are only two barriers that we cannot allow our significators to pass: 这个问题最大的好处在于事件是确定的，所以我们知道星盘中必定在某个地方存 在时间指示。这意味着我们可以抛开许多通常的规则。我们可以忽略阻碍：它们 可以被视为沿途发生的事件。我们可以根据需要，将我们的征象星一个星座接一 个星座地向前推进。只有两个障碍是我们不能允许我们的征象星越过的：

* conjunction with the Sun
* 与太阳的合相

* station.
* 停滞

Conjunction with the Sun is a pass-not. At station a planet’s speed shows to nothing. As, when timing, we must adjust the time if the planet is significantly faster or slower than usual, a planet at zero speed would give us infinite time. This might please the querent, but is unlikely to prove accurate. 与太阳的合相是一个无法越过的障碍。在停滞时，行星的速度显示为零。由于在 确定时间时，如果行星速度明显快于或慢于平常，我们必须调整时间，那么一颗 速度为零的行星会给我们无限的时间。这可能会让问卜者高兴，但不太可能准确。

Well-behaved charts have an applying aspect between Lords 1 and 8. As ever, it does not matter which applies to which. Any aspect can kill: there is no difference between trines and oppositions. Any planet can kill: even if Lord 8 is a strongly dignified benefic, the person will still die. I would be most reluctant to judge death from an antiscion. Death cannot have the sense of the covert or hidden that antiscia carry: even if the death is unknown to others, it is clear enough to the person who dies. 表现良好的星盘中，1 宫主和 8 宫主之间会有一个入相位。一如既往，谁向谁形 成相位并不重要。任何相位都可能致死：拱相位和对冲相位没有区别。任何行星 都可能致死：即使 8 宫主是一颗先天尊贵很强的吉星，这个人仍然会死。我会非 常不愿意根据一个映点来判断死亡。死亡不可能带有映点所携带的隐蔽或隐藏的 含义：即使死亡不为他人所知，对死者本人来说也是足够清晰的。

Lord 1 on the 8th cusp is not a testimony in this question: it shows only that the querent is thinking about death. Similarly with Lord 8 applying to conjunct the Ascendant: it shows the idea of death weighing down on the querent, but it does not show Death himself paying a call. But these can be taken as testimony of death, and as such give us the timing, in questions where death within a short period of time is regarded as certain (‘I’ve been told I have only weeks to live; when will the end com?’). But while in such circumstances Lord 1 entering the 8th can show death, Lord

1 already in the 8th does not: the querent is not already dead. 1 宫主位于 8 宫头在这个问题中不是一种征象：它只表明问卜者正在思考死亡。 同样，8 宫主即将与上升点形成合相也是如此：它表明死亡的想法正压在问卜者 心头，但并不代表死神本人即将造访。但是，这些在死亡被视为短期内必然发生 的问题中（例如：“我被告知只有几周可活了；结局何时到来？”），可以被视 为死亡的征象，并据此给我们时间指示。然而，在这种情况下，1 宫主进入 8 宫 可以表示死亡，但 1 宫主已经在 8 宫内则不表示：问卜者并非已经死亡。

### ✸I stress this point. The significator applying to the 8th cusp is never testimony in

the ‘if ’ question: ‘will the person die?’ It can be testimony of timing in the ‘when’ question. But this is only when death is certain.✷

### ✸我强调这一点。征象星正接近 8 宫头在“是否”类问题（“这个人会死吗？”）

中从来不是一种征象。它可以在“何时”类问题中作为时间指示的征象。但这仅 适用于死亡确定无疑的情况。✷

In those charts where there is no applying aspect between Lord 1 and 8 (remember: the aspect must perfect) we must find another significator for one or the other. As there can be only two reasons for the lack of aspect – as above – find a replacement significator for whichever planet is either conjuncting the Sun or passing through station. This is the significator that is being uncooperative, so change this one and keep the other. So if Lord 1 turns retrograde before aspecting Lord 8, keep Lord 8 as significator of death and find an alternative for Lord 1. 在那些 1 宫主和 8 宫主之间没有入相位的星盘中（记住：相位必须成相），我们 必须为其中一方找到另一个征象星。由于缺乏相位只可能有两个原因——如上所 述——为那颗要么正与太阳合相、要么正经历停滞的行星找一个替代征象星。这 是那个不合作的行星，所以更换这个，保留另一个。因此，如果 1 宫主在与 8 宫主成相位前转为逆行，则保留 8 宫主作为死亡的征象星，并为 1 宫主找一个替 代。

If the Moon, as is usual, is cosignificator of the querent, it can be used instead. If that too is ruled out, the Sun is a good alternative, in its role as Lord of Life. If it is Lord 8 that is ruled out, use either Saturn, as natural ruler of death, or the dispositor of the Part of Death. 如果月亮像通常那样作为问卜者的共同征象星，则可以代替使用。如果它也因故 被排除，太阳作为生命主星，是一个很好的替代。如果是 8 宫主被排除，则可以 使用土星（作为死亡的先天守护星），或者死亡点的定位星。

There are several versions of the Part of Death. I use Asc + 8th cusp – Moon and 8th cusp + Saturn – Moon. Neither reverses by night. Don’t get carried away with the Parts, though! They are useful in emergencies, when the planets are not cooperating and we know there must be a death. In any question where death is not certain, do not take the Parts as providing it: if death is not shown by the planets, the person is most

unlikely to die. 有几种不同版本的死亡点。我使用上升点+8 宫头–月亮，以及 8 宫头+土星–月 亮。两者在夜间都不反向计算。不过，不要过度沉迷于这些点！它们只在紧急情 况下有用，即当行星不合作而我们又知道死亡必然发生时。在任何死亡并不确定 的问题中，不要认为点能提供死亡征象：如果死亡未由行星显示，那么此人极不 可能死亡。

### ✸The Part of Death should be used only as an absolute last resort, when death is

certain and there is nothing else at all on which we can hang a timing. Use it at other times and you’ll be killing your querents far too readily.✷

### ✸死亡点应仅作为绝对的最后手段使用，即当死亡确定无疑且我们完全没有任

何其他可以确定时间的依据时。在其他时候使用它，你会过于轻易地“宣判”你 的问卜者死亡。✷

If you are turning the chart, because the querent is asking about someone else’s death, you must consider the ruler of both the radical and the turned 8th house. You will usually find that one or other of them is in play; sometimes both. 如果你在进行转宫（因为问卜者在询问他人的死亡），你必须同时考虑基准盘和 转宫后的 8 宫的守护星。你通常会发现其中一方或另一方在起作用；有时两者皆 是。

When you have found the aspect showing death, time it in the usual way, bearing in mind the querent’s age. This is a time when the astrologer crosses his fingers and hopes for the best result: predicting early death is not pleasant. If, however, you are not prepared to do it, you should not be judging such questions. 当你找到了显示死亡的相位时，以通常的方式判断时间，同时要考虑问卜者的年 龄。这时占星师会祈求好运，希望得到最好的结果：预测早逝并不令人愉快。然 而，如果你没有准备好这样做，你就不应该判断这类问题。

Will I die? 我会死吗？

Odd though some horaries are, I have yet to be asked ‘Will I die?’ as a general, long-term question. I deal here with death from a particular illness or a particular situation (‘Is it safe for me to go back to my country?’). I will treat this as if the querent is asking about himself and refer to Lord 1; if the querent is asking about somebody else, use the ruler of the appropriate house instead. Remember that the Moon does not become cosignificator of the person the querent is asking about. 虽然有些卜卦问题很奇怪，但我还没遇到过将“我会死吗？”作为一个笼统的、 长期的问题来询问的情况。我在这里处理的是由特定疾病或特定情况导致的死亡 （例如：“我回自己的国家安全吗？”）。我将按问卜者询问自己来处理，并指

代 1 宫主；如果问卜者是询问他人，则使用相应宫位的守护星代替。请记住，月 亮并不成为问卜者所询问之人的共同征象星。

### ✸Don’t use it as cosignificator of the querent either, unless, as in the section above,

death is certain.✷

### ✸也不要将它作为问卜者的共同征象星使用，除非如上节所述，死亡是确定无

疑的。✷

An applying aspect between Lords 1 and 8 is the prime testimony of death. Time it in the usual way. A separating aspect must be judged according to the situation. Death has presumably not already happened, or the question should not be asked, so it is usually a positive testimony: the person has come into contact with death; he is still alive; he will survive. Unless there is other killing testimony coming up. If, however, the person is in a coma this separating aspect usually means that death, in any meaningful sense of the word, has already occurred: see the chart below for an example. 1 宫主和 8 宫主之间的入相位是死亡的首要征象。按通常方式判断时间。一个出 相位必须根据具体情况来判断。死亡推测尚未发生，否则问题就不该被提出，因 此这通常是一个积极的征象：此人已与死亡接触过；他仍然活着；他将幸存。除 非还有其他致命的征象即将出现。然而，如果此人正处于昏迷状态，这个出相位 通常意味着，在“死亡”这个词的任何有意义层面，死亡已经发生：参见下文的 星盘示例。

Keep your eyes open for translations or collections of light. 时刻留意传递或光线聚集。

Remember that if the querent is asking about someone else, you must consider the Lords of both the radical and the turned 8th houses: either can kill. 记住，如果问卜者是在询问他人，你必须同时考虑基准盘和转宫后的 8 宫的守护 星：两者皆可致死。

Entering combustion or being combust and still applying to the Sun is testimony of death. 正在进入燃烧状态，或已处于燃烧状态但仍与太阳形成入相位，是死亡的征象。

### ✸ I would not take entering combustion as testimony of death. Being combust

already cannot be testimony, because there is no gradation in death: you are either dead or you are not. You can’t be a bit dead, so you can’t get more dead.✷

### ✸我不认为正在进入燃烧状态是死亡的征象。已经处于燃烧状态则不能作为征

象，因为死亡没有程度之分：你要么死了，要么没死。你不可能“有点死”，所

以你不可能“更死”。✷

Being combust and separating from the Sun is testimony that the worst has passed. With the usual rider of ‘all things being equal’ this can be taken as testimony of survival. 处于燃烧状态但正在与太阳形成出相位，表明最坏的情况已经过去。在通常的“其 他条件不变”的前提下，这可以视为存活的征象。

If the situation is serious enough, any major deterioration in the condition of the main significator can be taken as fatal. In one chart, the person asked about was in a coma, his significator the Moon in Cancer. All might seem fine: lots of essential dignity and a cold/moist planet in a cold/moist sign. But the testimonies must be judged within the context of the question. The Moon was in the 30th degree of Cancer, on the point of leaving the sign, on which it would enter hot/dry Leo and lose all its dignity. The person’s condition was about to deteriorate dramatically. He was in a coma: how much worse could he get? This was testimony of death. 如果情况足够严重，主要征象星状态的任何重大恶化都可以被视为是致命的。在 一张星盘中，被询问的人处于昏迷状态，其征象星月亮在巨蟹座。表面看来一切 似乎都还好：很多先天尊贵，一颗冷/湿的行星落在冷/湿的星座。但征象必须在 问题的语境中进行判断。月亮位于巨蟹座最后一度，即将离开这个星座，届时它 将进入热/燥的狮子座并失去所有尊贵。此人的状况即将急剧恶化。他处于昏迷 状态：还能恶化到什么程度？这就是死亡的征象。

Most important: mutual reception between the significator of the person and the significator of death saves. As Lilly says, ‘after desperation, there will be recovery’. Yes, this works, even with a clear applying aspect between Lords 1 and 8 – although it works only with reception by major dignity. Be aware of what is happening by Jupiter in Cancer. With the person’s significator being the Moon in Cancer, there was powerful mutual reception between person and death. But with the person’s significator changing sign and losing that mutual reception, death was certain. 最重要的是：代表人的征象星与代表死亡的征象星之间的互溶可以拯救生命。正 如 Lilly 所说：“在绝望之后，会有康复。”是的，这确实有效，即使 1 宫主 和 8 宫主之间存在明显的入相位——尽管它只在主要尊贵的接纳关系下才有效。 要注意木星在巨蟹座时发生的情况。如果人的征象星是位于巨蟹座的月亮，那么 人与死亡之间就存在强有力的互溶。但随着人的征象星改变星座并失去那种互溶， 死亡就确定了。

39. Lilly p.254

“Surely if Death and person love each other (mutual reception) they will want to be together, so the person will die?” No. The idea here is that Death and the person are friends, so Death leaves the keys on the table and turns his back, letting the person escape from his clutches. “当然，如果死亡和人彼此相爱（互溶），他们就会想在一起，所以人会死，对

吗？”不对。这里的理念是，死亡和此人是朋友，所以死亡把钥匙留在桌上并转 过身去，让此人从他的掌控中逃脱。

### ✸Mutual reception between person and Death saves only if the question is ‘Will I or

won’t I?’ Where death is certain (‘When will I?’), it does not.✷

### ✸只有当问题是“我会死还是不会死？”时，人与死亡之间的互溶才能拯救生

命。如果死亡已经确定（“我何时会死？”），则无效。✷

Death is an event of some significance: you will not find it shown by a minor testimony in some dark corner of the chart. If there is no clear testimony for death, the person will live. 死亡是一个具有重大意义的事件：你不会在星盘某个阴暗角落的次要征象中找到 它的显示。如果没有明确的死亡征象，此人将会存活。

A close aspect, especially conjunction, between Lord 1 and either Venus or Jupiter in major dignity is a positive sign – unless this helpful planet rules the 8th house or is significator of the illness. 1 宫主与处于主要尊贵状态的金星或木星之间的紧密相位（尤其是合相）是一个 积极的信号——除非这颗有益的行星守护着 8 宫或是疾病的征象星。

The person’s significator close to the 7th cusp is testimony of death. Although being angular is strengthening, by primary motion (the apparent movement of the planets around the Earth) a planet on the Descendant is setting, which is an obvious indication of dying. This is all the more true if this significator is the Sun. 此人的征象星接近 7 宫头是死亡的征象。虽然位于角宫会增强力量，但由于恒星 周日运动（行星围绕地球的视运动），位于下降点的行星正在西入，这显然是逝 去的象征。如果这个征象星是太阳，则更是如此。

The person’s cusp or significator falling on Antares, with its sense of the ending of cycles, is a bad sign. 此人的宫头或征象星落在具有周期终结意味的心宿二上，是一个不好的迹象。

### ✸ Those last three points are very minor. Death being an absolute, we need an

absolute verdict. A majority opinion based on the balance of minor testimonies will not do.

### ✸最后这三点是非常次要的。死亡是绝对的，我们需要一个绝对的判断。基于

次要征象平衡得出的多数意见是行不通的。

Because death is an absolute, not capable of qualification, there is no significance in the amount of essential dignity Lord 8 has. You are either dead or you are not. You

will not be any the more dead if Lord 8 is in detriment, nor any the less if it has dignity. 因为死亡是绝对的，无法被量化，所以 8 宫主拥有多少先天尊贵没有意义。你要 么死了，要么没死。如果 8 宫主处于落陷，你不会“更死”；如果它拥有尊贵， 你也不会“死得少一些”。

In many charts the timing of death is clear (and remember: if you aren’t asked for a timing, don’t feel the need to give one!). In others it is not specific, but sufficient for the circumstances. For instance, when the querent needs to book a plane ticket to visit a dying relative the chart may not give an exact timing, but say something like, ‘Very soon: go visit her now!’ or ‘Not for a while, there’s no great urgency here’. But sometimes the timing of death, as with the timing of birth can remain hidden, even with hindsight. Our knowledge is always only partial, but for those charts that seem to offer not even the hint of a whisper of a plausible clue, my best explanation is that there seem to be certain cards that God likes to hold close to His chest – particularly the coming into and the going out of life. I have no better answer to this.✷ 在许多星盘中，死亡的时间是清晰的（记住：如果没有人问你时间，不要觉得有 必要给出一个！）。在其他星盘中，时间并不具体，但对于当时的情境来说已经 足够。例如，当问卜者需要预订机票去探望一位垂危的亲属时，星盘可能不会给 出确切的时间，但会说类似这样的话：“很快：现在就去看她吧！”或者“暂时 不会，这里没有太大的紧迫性”。但有时，死亡的时间，就像出生时间一样，可 能始终是隐藏的，即使事后回顾也是如此。我们的知识永远只是片面的，但对于 那些似乎连一丝一毫合理线索都未提供的星盘，我最好的解释是：似乎有些牌， 上帝喜欢紧握在胸前——尤其是生命的来与去。对此，我没有更好的答案。✷

Will my friend live? 我的朋友能活下来吗？

The querent said, ‘My friend has been taken to hospital. She is in a coma. The doctors don’t know what’s wrong with her, but think she my have had a brain haemorrhage. What is the problem? What is going to happen?’ 问卜者说：“我的朋友被送进了医院。她处于昏迷状态。医生不清楚具体病因， 怀疑可能是脑出血。问题究竟出在哪里？接下来会怎样发展？”

The querent is not involved in this question, so we go straight to the 11th, the house of friends. Its ruler, Mercury, signifies the friend. Seeing Mercury in Gemini, we might think that the friend is doing fine. But no: although Mercury is in a sign that it rules, in a medical question it is in a very bad condition. Mercury is a cold/dry planet. It is in a hot/moist sign, a sign contrary to its nature. It is dis-eased. The friend is not well. This much we know, of course: the woman is in a coma. 问卜者与此问题无关，所以我们直接看 11 宫，即朋友宫。其守护星水星象征这 位朋友。看到水星在双子座，我们可能会认为朋友情况良好。但并非如此：尽管 水星落在其守护的星座，但在医学问题中，它处于非常糟糕的状态。水星是一颗 冷/燥的行星。它位于一个热/湿的星座，一个与其属性相反的星座。它处于“失 衡”状态。朋友身体不佳。这我们当然知道：这位女士处于昏迷中。

Which planet is causing Mercury problem? We can look to the ruler of the sign Mercury is in. This brings us back to Mercury. There is no reason that the significator of the illness should not be the same as that of the patient. But here we have a more likely culprit, especially considering the sudden onset of the illness. Mercury is just separating from opposition to Mars. Mars is peregrine and retrograde, so it is a nasty

sort of Mars. 哪颗行星正在给水星造成问题？我们可以查看水星所在星座的守护星。这又把我 们带回到水星本身。疾病的征象星与病人的征象星相同，这并无不可。但这里我 们有一个更可能的“罪魁祸首”，尤其是考虑到疾病的突然发作。水星刚刚与火 星形成出相位的对冲。火星处于游离且逆行状态，所以是一种恶劣的火星。

The Moon’s most recent aspect can also be taken into account. Its last aspect was to this nasty Mars. Mars is confirmed as significator of the illness. 月亮最近的相位也可以考虑进来。它最后一个相位就是与这颗恶劣的火星形成的。 火星被确认为疾病的征象星。

### ✸There is no reason to bring in the Moon’s last aspect. This is something Lilly has

taken from the method for judging decumbitures.✷

### ✸这里没有理由引入月亮的最后相位。这是 Lilly 从判断卧病盘的方法中借鉴来

的。✷

Mars in this part of Sagittarius, Saunders says,‘is hot and dry above nature, consuming and drying up the radical moisture and humidity of the body, and utterly extinguishing the life of man’. It does this by infecting ‘the body and blood with much thick, red choler that is hot and very dry’. Choler is the fiery humour, the fiery part of the human constitution. The doctors suspected a brain haemorrhage; had this fatal Mars been in the friend’s 1st house (the 1st being the house of the head), it could well have shown this: a kind of fiery explosion in the brain. It isn’t; it is in her 5th (the 5th house from the 11th), which is the house of the heart. She has had a heart attack. This was confirmed at the post mortem. Saunders 说，火星在射手座的这个位置，“其热与燥超乎自然，消耗并耗尽了 身体的根本湿气与水分，彻底熄灭人的生命”。它通过“以大量粘稠、红色的胆 汁质感染身体和血液来实现这一点，这种胆汁质是热的且非常燥的”。胆汁质是 火性的体液，是人体质中的火性部分。医生怀疑是脑出血；如果这颗致命的火星 位于朋友的 1 宫（1 宫是头部之宫），它很可能就显示了这一点：大脑中的一种 火性爆发。但它不在；它在她的 5 宫（从 11 宫算起的第 5 宫），即心脏之宫。 她心脏病发作了。这在尸检中得到了证实。

40. Saunders, op. cit., p.152.

What will happen to her? She is in a coma, so our first question must be, ‘Will she live or will she die?’ Looking into the death of somebody other than the querent, we must consider both the turned and the radical 8th house. Here, the turned 8th house (8th from the 11th: the radical 6th) is ruled by Mars. Mercury (the friend) is separating from opposition to it. If the sick person is sitting up in bed and chatting, this is a most positive sign: she has come into contact with death; she is still alive; she is going to survive. In the context of someone in a coma it can be taken that death, in

the real sense, has already happened. 她将会发生什么？她处于昏迷中，所以我们的首要问题必须是：“她会活还是会 死？”研究问卜者以外的人的死亡，我们必须同时考虑转宫后的和基准盘的 8 宫。这里，转宫后的 8 宫（从 11 宫算起的第 8 宫：即基准盘的 6 宫）由火星守 护。水星（朋友）刚刚与它形成出相位的对冲。如果病人正坐在床上聊天，这是 一个非常积极的迹象：她已与死亡接触过；她还活着；她将会幸存。但在一个人 昏迷的语境下，可以认为死亡，在真正意义上，已经发生。

The Moon separates from Mars and applies to Mercury, translating light between them and so remaking the aspect: the friend will die. The number of degrees the Moon must travel to perfect the opposition gives the timing: she will be pronounced dead at the end of that afternoon. In the blessedly small number of horaries I have been asked to judge on death in comas, this remaking of a separated aspect by translation of light is typical for showing the doctors’s recognition that hope has gone. 月亮与火星形成出相位，并与水星形成入相位，在它们之间传递光线，从而重建 了相位：朋友将会死亡。月亮必须移动的度数以达到成相给出了时间：她将在那 天下午晚些时候被宣布死亡。在我有幸被请求判断的为数不多的关于昏迷死亡的 卜卦中，这种通过光线传递重建已出相位的相位，通常对应医生确认无望的时刻。

### ✸The Moon’s translation of light is valid. This does not contradict my added point

about ignoring the Moon’s last aspect, above. That was Lilly’s advice to have a look at the last aspect the Moon made, because it is the Moon. Here, we aren’t looking at the Moon because it is the Moon, but because it is the planet translating the light from Mars to Mercury.✷

### ✸月亮的光线传递是有效的。这与我在前面补充的关于忽略月亮最后相位的观

点并不矛盾。那是 Lilly 的建议，要看一下月亮形成的最后一个相位，因为它是 月亮。而在这里，我们关注月亮并非因为它是月亮，而是因为它是那颗在火星与 水星之间传递光线的行星。✷

DOCTORS, MEDICINE AND SURGERY 医生、药物和外科手术

‘Is this doctor any good?’ ‘Is this treatment working?’ ‘Should I have this operation?’ When judging such questions, do be cautious. The astrology may be eloquent, but unless you have a sound knowledge of medicine you are unlikely to fully understand what it says. But we can, even without such a knowledge, make the suggestion that ‘These pills seem to be doing you more harm than good; maybe there’s an alternative’, or ‘This doctor seems to be out of his depth; can you insist on seeing a specialist?’ “这位医生好吗？”“这种治疗有效吗？”“我应该做这个手术吗？”在判断此 类问题时，务必谨慎。占星征象可能很有说服力，但除非你具备扎实的医学知识，

否则不太可能完全理解其含义。不过，即使没有这样的知识，我们也可以提出建 议，例如：“这些药片似乎对你弊大于利；也许有替代方案”，或者“这位医生 似乎力不从心；你能坚持要求看专家吗？”

Doctors in general, seen as learned people, are 9th house (‘Was that the doctor’s cat who chased mine down the street?’), but the doctor that is dealing with this illness, or who is potentially dealing with it, is 7th house. If the querent is asking about someone else’s illness, the doctor will be that person’s 7th house. People often ask about their spouse’s treatment: spouse is 7th, so the spouse’s doctor will be 7th from the 7th, which is the 1st. That’s fine: we don’t need to have the querent in the chart, so we can give Lord 1 to doctor. 一般而言，医生被视为有学识的人，用 9 宫表示（“是那位医生的猫在街上追我 的猫吗？”），但正在处理或可能处理此病的医生，则用 7 宫表示。如果问卜者 是询问他人的疾病，医生将是那个人的 7 宫。人们经常询问配偶的治疗情况：配 偶是 7 宫，因此配偶的医生将是配偶的 7 宫，即 1 宫。这没问题：我们不一定需 要在星盘中体现问卜者，所以我们可以将 1 宫主赋予医生。

### ✸The doctor is the 7th house, seen as the querent’s partner in recovering health. The

vet is also 7th house: the querent’s partner in healing the cat. Not the cat’s 7th house. ✷

### ✸医生是 7 宫，被视为问卜者恢复健康的伙伴。兽医也是 7 宫：问卜者治疗猫

的伙伴。而不是猫的 7 宫。✷

In this context, take the treatment as Lord 10. This is only in this context: the 10th is the treatment that is being given, not the treatment that should be given. In some cases, surgery will be seen as part of the range of treatment prescribed and so can be taken as 10th house. In itself, however, surgery is a 6th-house matter. There is an idea that it is 8th-house, but this is wrong: the aim of surgery is to keep us out of the 8th house. In practice, we can usually go straight to Mars, natural ruler of surgery. If you need to distinguish between doctor and surgeon (‘My doctor says this but my surgeon says that.’) keep the 7th house for the doctor and use the dispositor of the planet signifying the surgery (usually Mars) for the surgeon. There is no problem with this planet dispositing itself: read the same indications for the surgeon and the surgery. 在此语境下，将治疗视为 10 宫。仅在此语境下如此：10 宫代表正在进行的治疗， 而非应该进行的治疗。在某些情况下，手术可能被视为处方治疗方案的一部分， 因此也可视为 10 宫。然而，手术本身属于 6 宫范畴。有人认为它属于 8 宫，但 这是错误的：手术的目的是使我们免于进入 8 宫。在实践中，我们通常可以直接 看火星，它是手术的先天守护星。如果你需要区分医生和外科医生（“我的医生 这么说，但我的外科医生那么说。”），保留 7 宫给医生，而用代表手术（通常 是火星）的行星的定位星来指代外科医生。这颗行星定位自身没有问题：对外科 医生和手术解读相同的征象即可。

Once you have identified the relevant planet, consider its strength and its receptions with the patient and the illness. Essential debility is not necessarily a problem, if it is descriptive. Example: if Mars is the surgery, Mars in a Venus sign would well describe gynaecological or cosmetic surgery. If that were the nature of the operation, the essential debility could be ignored. More important than dignity – though strength is of course helpful – is reception. We would hope to see the significator of the illness in strong dignities of either the doctor, the treatment or the surgery. If the illness is disposited by the doctor, he has power over it. Finding doctor, treatment or surgery in strong dignity of the illness is negative testimony: the illness is boss. Doctor, treatment or surgery in dignity of the patient’s significator is helpful, although less so than testimony showing power over the illness; but it is most important that doctor, treatment or surgery is not in detriment or fall of the patient’s significator. 一旦确定了相关的行星，就考虑其力量以及它与病人及疾病之间的接纳关系。如 果是描述性的，先天衰弱不一定是个问题。例如：如果火星代表手术，火星落在 金星星座可以很好地描述妇科或美容手术。如果手术的性质就是如此，那么先天 衰弱可以忽略不计。比尊贵更重要的是接纳关系——尽管力量当然也有帮助。我 们希望看到疾病的征象星处于医生、治疗或手术的强烈尊贵位置。如果疾病被医 生的征象星定位，则医生对其有控制力。发现医生、治疗或手术处于疾病的强烈 尊贵位置，则是负面征象：疾病是老大。医生、治疗或手术处于病人征象星的尊 贵位置是有益的，尽管不如显示对疾病有控制力的征象；但最重要的是，医生、 治疗或手术不处于病人征象星的落陷或弱势位置。

Examples: suppose the patient is Jupiter, the illness is Mars and the treatment Saturn. Mars is in Aquarius: good – the treatment has power over the illness. Saturn is in Sagittarius: good – the treatment loves the patient, and so will want to help him. But Saturn in Capricorn would be bad news: despite its essential strength, it exalts Mars, showing that the illness has power over the treatment, and is in the fall of Jupiter, showing it harming the patient. 举例：假设病人是木星，疾病是火星，治疗是土星。火星在水瓶座：很好——治 疗对疾病有控制力。土星在射手座：很好——治疗“喜爱”病人，因此愿意帮助 他。但如果土星在摩羯座，那就是坏消息了：尽管它先天力量强大，但它旺势火 星，表明疾病对治疗有控制力，并且处于木星的弱势，表明它会伤害病人。

Certain fixed stars can be important in questions about eye surgery. See page 131. 某些恒星在关于眼科手术的问题中可能很重要。参见第 220 页。

Don’t expect charts for questions on surgery to look pretty. No matter how beneficial the surgery might be, it remains a drastic intervention. 不要指望关于手术问题的星盘看起来很“漂亮”。无论手术多么有益，它仍然是 一种剧烈的干预。

You will sometimes be asked to compare two doctors. They cannot both be shown by the patient’s 7th house. Asking for a brief description of the two will enable you to identify them in the chart. For instance, a querent thought her son would need an

operation, and asked if this should go private. Her son was receiving NHS treatment, and his 7th house (the doctor treating him) was ruled by the Moon (the people). The ruler of the querent’s 7th (which we could read as the doctor the mother was considering) was Jupiter, natural ruler of rich folks.
