The Moon, at 29 Scorpio, was immediately leaving Mars dignities: the NHS surgeon decided that he did not need the operation after all. 有时你会被要求比较两位医生。他们不可能都用病人的 7 宫来表示。要求对两位 医生做一个简要描述，可以使你在星盘中识别他们。例如，一位问卜者认为她的 儿子需要手术，并询问是否应该选择私立医院。她的儿子正在接受国民医疗服务 体系（NHS）的治疗，他的 7 宫（治疗他的医生）由月亮（代表民众）守护。问 卜者的 7 宫主（我们可以解读为母亲正在考虑的医生）是木星，富人的先天守护 星。月亮在天蝎座 29 度，即将离开火星的尊贵范围：NHS 的外科医生最终判定 他并不需要手术。

### ✸Remember the reality of the situation. Perhaps Lord 7 is in detriment: a bad doctor.

But a bad doctor can stumble upon the right treatment, while even the best doctor will be unable to cure various ills.✷

### ✸记住实际情况。也许 7 宫主处于落陷：一位糟糕的医生。但糟糕的医生也可

能碰巧用对了治疗方法，而即使是最好的医生也无法治愈各种疾病。✷

HIRING STAFF 雇佣员工

If you are hiring someone at work, taking on a new downstairs maid or calling a plumber, the prospective employee is shown by the 6th house. Ideally, Lord 6 will be essentially strong (the person is honest and has the necessary skills), accidentally unafflicted (no impediment to using those skills) and in dignities of Lord 1. The latter is important because the servant must accept orders. Too often the chart shows the reverse: Lord 1 is in major dignities of Lord 6, showing that the querent likes the prospective servant. This is not the best reason for hiring someone. Lord 6 in the detriment or fall of Lord 1 would be a definite No. 如果你在工作中雇佣某人，雇佣一位新的楼下女佣，或呼叫一位水管工，这位潜 在的雇员由 6 宫表示。理想情况下，6 宫主应该先天有力（此人诚实且具备必要 技能），偶然不受克（使用这些技能没有障碍），并且处于 1 宫主的尊贵位置。 后者很重要，因为仆人必须接受命令。但星盘常常显示相反的情况：1 宫主处于 6 宫主的主要尊贵位置，这表明问卜者喜欢这位潜在的仆人。这并非雇佣某人的 最佳理由。6 宫主处于 1 宫主的落陷或弱势位置，则绝对是“不行”。

Watch out for afflictions to the 6th house. The South Node, for instance, in the 6th would be a definite No. Always be cautious with Mercury and the signs that it rules:

even at its best, its concept of honesty can be flexible. A client phoned to ask if she could trust her cleaner, who was shown by Jupiter in Gemini. Debilitated planet in a Mercury sign: definitely not! She called back a few minutes later to say she had gone upstairs to find the cleaner packing her best clothes into a suitcase. 要警惕 6 宫受到的伤害。例如，南交点在 6 宫绝对是“不行”。对于水星及其守 护的星座要始终保持谨慎：即使是在其最佳状态，它对“诚实”的概念也可能是 灵活的。一位客户打电话问她是否可以信任她的清洁工，清洁工由位于双子座的 木星代表。衰弱的行星在水星星座：绝对不行！几分钟后她回电话说，她上楼发 现清洁工正把她最好的衣服装进手提箱。

If you are asked ‘Should I employ A, B, or C?’ give the 6th house to the favoured candidate and find other significators for the rivals. Keep it to A, B or C: the querent who can’t come up with a shortlist is not treating the matter seriously, so why should you? Ask the querent for a brief description of each candidate. As long as it is kept brief, the description will contain whatever clues you need to pin the candidate to a planet. ‘One of them is a redhead (Mars) and the other is really solemn (Saturn).’ You can trust that each querent will give the appropriate identifying words, because the chart is a picture of that querent’s reality. Once you found a planet for each candidate, compare them by the criteria above. 如果被问到“我应该雇佣 A、B 还是 C？”，将 6 宫赋予最受青睐的候选人，并 为竞争对手寻找其他征象星。仅限于 A、B 或 C：如果一个问卜者连一个简短名 单都列不出来，说明他没有认真对待这件事，那你又何必认真呢？请问卜者简要 描述每位候选人。只要描述简短，其中就会包含你所需的一切线索，以便将候选 人与某颗行星对应起来。“其中一个红头发（火星），另一个非常严肃（土星）。” 你可以相信每位问卜者都会给出恰当的识别性词语，因为星盘正是该问卜者现实 的写照。一旦为每位候选人找到对应的行星，就根据上述标准进行比较。

We are not looking for aspects in this question, as it assumes that the querent can hire that person if they decide to do so. But querent and candidate applying by opposition is a strong warning that employing that one will lead to regret. 在这个问题中，我们并不寻找相位，因为它假定问卜者如果决定就可以雇佣那个 人。但是，如果问卜者与候选人的征象星正形成对冲相位，则强烈警告雇佣此人 将导致后悔。

When will the plumber arrive? 水管工何时会到？

Casting such a chart, I would expect to find Lord 6 applying to conjunct the Ascendant (coming to the querent’s house). Failing that, an aspect between Lords 1 and 6 or, at a pinch, Lord 6 applying to the 4th cusp will do. Take the timing in the usual way. No aspect, no arrival. 设置这类星盘时，我预期会发现 6 宫主正与上升点形成合相（来到问卜者家）。 如果没有，1 宫主和 6 宫主之间的相位，或者在不得已时，6 宫主正接近 4 宫头

也可以。按通常方式判断时间。没有相位，就不会到来。

# Seventh House Questions

# 7 宫的问题

LOVE AND MARRIAGE 爱情与婚姻

When I first started in horary practice, I expected questions on relationship to make up the greater proportion of my trade. This did not prove so – I could never have imagined the range of questions that do get asked – but there have been substantially more questions on relationships than on any other single issue. These fall broadly into two groups: ‘Will it start?’ and ‘Will it end?’ Lest you wonder why I pay such attention here to marital disharmony, remember that people in happy relationships are rarely impelled to consult astrologers about them. 当我最初开始卜卦占星实践时，曾预计有关关系的问题将构成我业务的主要部分。 实际情况并非如此——我从未想象过人们会提出如此广泛的问题——但关于关 系的问题确实远多于任何其他单一议题。这些问题大致可分为两类：“会开始吗？” 和“会结束吗？”。为避免您疑惑我为何在此如此关注婚姻不和谐，请记住，身 处幸福关系中的人很少会因此去咨询占星师。

### ✸Remember Tolstoy’s words: ‘Happy families are alike; every unhappy family is

unhappy in its own way’. As the happy ones aren’t asking the questions, what we are left with is the myriad variety of unhappiness. There are recurrent themes, of course, but as you pick apart the web of feelings that each chart contains – for these are not the simple black or white of ‘Yes, you’ll get the job’ or ‘No, you won’t’ – do strive most strenuously to see the truth that is shown in the chart you are judging. This will not be the same as that in the chart you judged a few days ago, nor as the television drama you were watching last night, nor as what happened in your own love-life when you were 25. In judging these questions, more than those on any other subject, it is easy to import our own scripts. Be careful not to do so. To avoid so doing, check each step of your judgement against the evidence of the chart, making sure that it does not contradict the testimonies you find there. If a step does not fit the astrological evidence, that step is wrong and must be rethought. ✷

### ✸请记住 Tolstoy（托尔斯泰）的话：“幸福的家庭都是相似的；不幸的家庭各

有各的不幸。”既然幸福的人不问问题，我们面对的就是各式各样的不幸。当然， 其中存在反复出现的主题，但当你剖析每张星盘中蕴含的情感网络时——因为这

些远非“是的，你会得到那份工作”或“不，你不会”那样简单的非黑即白—— 请务必尽最大努力看清你正在判断的星盘所显示的真相。这不会与你几天前判断 的星盘相同，不会与你昨晚看的电视剧相同，也不会与你 25 岁时自己的爱情经 历相同。在判断这些问题时，比判断任何其他主题的问题都更容易带入我们自己 的剧本。注意不要这样做。为避免如此，请依据星盘的证据检查你判断的每一步， 确保其不与你在此发现的征象相矛盾。如果某一步与占星学证据不符，那一步就 是错的，必须重新思考。✷

The significators 征象星

In questions about love and marriage, the querent is signified, as ever, by Lord 1 and the Moon (unless the Moon is ruler of the house enquired about, in this case the 7th) and the questied, the person asked about, is shown by Lord 7. The quesited is shown by Lord 7 even if the relationship exists as yet only as a desire or a possibility. For instance, if the question is ‘When will I meet the man I will marry?’ we look to the 7th even if there is no candidate on the horizon at the moment. If the querent is thinking of promoting a friend to 7th-house duties, we would look to the 7th, not the 11th: the question is really ‘Is so-and-so a suitable partner?’ That so-and-so happens to be a friend now is irrelevant. If the question is about some specific person’s feelings for the querent, however, we may need to look at a different house. For example, to judge ‘Has my neighbour got a crush on me?’ we would look at Lord 3. 在关于爱情和婚姻的问题中，问卜者一如既往地由 1 宫主和月亮象征（除非月亮 是所询问宫位的守护星，在此情况下是 7 宫），而所占之事，即被询问的人，则 由 7 宫主显示。即使关系目前仅存在于欲望或可能性中，所占之事仍由 7 宫主显 示。例如，如果问题是“我何时会遇到我将要结婚的人？”，我们关注 7 宫，即 使此刻视野中尚无候选人。如果问卜者正考虑将一位朋友提升到 7 宫的职责，我 们应看 7 宫，而非 11 宫：问题实质是“某某是否是合适的伴侣？”该某某目前 恰好是朋友这一事实并不相关。然而，如果问题是关于某个特定的人对问卜者的 感受，我们可能需要查看不同的宫位。例如，判断“我的邻居是否迷恋我？”我 们会看 3 宫主。

The man, whether querent or quesited, will be given the Sun as cosignificator and the woman, Venus. This is only in relationship questions. If the Sun or Venus rules the 1st or 7th house, it cannot be assigned in this way: the person shown by that house has first claim on its services. Do not use Mars instead of the Sun, even if the Sun is already in use. If the question concerns a man/man or woman/woman relationship, the Sun and Venus cannot be used in this way, because we have no reason for assigning them to one person rather than to the other. 男性，无论是问卜者还是所占之事，将额外赋予太阳作为共同征象星；女性则赋 予金星。这仅适用于关系问题。如果太阳或金星守护 1 宫或 7 宫，则不能以此方 式分配：由该宫位象征的人对其服务拥有首要索取权。即使太阳已被使用，也不 要用火星替代太阳。如果问题涉及男/男或女/女关系，则不能以这种方式使用太

阳和金星，因为我们没有理由将其分配给其中一人而非另一人。

So: 因此：

1. Querent gets Lord 1 and the Moon.
1. 问卜者获得 1 宫主和月亮。

2. Person asked about gets Lord 7.
2. 被询问的人获得 7 宫主。

3. Whether they are querent or quesited, the man gets the Sun and the woman gets Venus – UNLESS they have already been claimed under points 1 and 2.
3. 无论他们是问卜者还是所占之事，男性获得太阳，女性获得金星——除非他 们已在第 1 和第 2 点下被认领。

In many relationship questions there is more than one 7th-house person involved: ‘I’m married, but do I have a future with my lover?’ Always give Lord 7 to the person specifically asked about, which in this example is the lover. We can, if necessary, then find another planet to signify the other one. It is usually safe to take Saturn as significator of the unwanted spouse. If in doubt, the receptions will make the choice of planet clear, or confirm that we have chosen correctly: see below for more detail on this. 在许多关系问题中，涉及不止一个 7 宫相关的人：“我已婚，但我和我的情人有 未来吗？”总是将 7 宫主赋予被具体询问的人，在此例中是情人。如有必要，我 们可以找到另一颗行星来象征另一个人。通常可以安全地将土星视为不想要的配 偶的征象星。如有疑问，接纳关系将使行星的选择变得清晰，或确认我们选择正 确：更多细节见下文。

### ✸If no third person is involved in the situation, the person querent asks about will

always be signified by Lord 7. If there is a third person, the person asked about will usually be signified by Lord 7. Check this option first, to see if it fits the evidence of the chart. But sometimes the person asked about is not the focus of the querent’s attention. For instance, ‘Have I got a future with my lover?’ may translate as ‘Can I save my marriage?’ or vice versa.

### ✸如果情境中没有涉及第三方，问卜者询问的人将始终由 7 宫主象征。如果存

在第三方，被询问的人通常仍以 7 宫主象征。但需优先核验是否符合星盘证据。 但有时被询问的人并非问卜者关注的焦点。例如，“我和我的情人有未来吗？” 可能转化为“我能挽救我的婚姻吗？”反之亦然。

Saturn may well show the unwanted spouse, but, as always, check this with the evidence: the case for another planet may be more compelling. If one of the querent’s

planets has just entered Saturn’s sign and the other has recently started to exalt Saturn, Saturn is not significator of the person querent wants to be rid of! 土星很可能显示不想要的配偶，但一如既往，需用证据核实：另一颗行星的情况 可能更有说服力。如果问卜者的一颗行星刚进入土星的星座，而另一颗最近开始 对土星呈旺势，那么土星就不是问卜者想要摆脱的人的征象星！

Querents can be opaque in their questions. One memorable case was ‘Will we separate?’ When I told the querent that the chart made no sense she replied that they had separated a fortnight before. So the question was not ‘Will we separate?’ but ‘Will we get back together?’ and the default option no that if he didn’t leave the querent nothing would happen, but that if he didn’t leave the other woman nothing would happen. ✷ 问卜者的问题可能含糊不清。一个令人难忘的案例是“我们会分开吗？”当我告 诉问卜者星盘显示不合理时，她回答说他们两周前已经分开了。所以问题不是“我 们会分开吗？”而是“我们会复合吗？”而默认选项是，如果他不离开问卜者， 什么事也不会发生，但如果他不离开另一个女人，什么事也不会发生。✷

Some questions with more than one 7th-house person do not involve cheated spouses: ‘I’ve been dating Tom for a few weeks, but, Wow! there's this new guy?’ so, as the person directly asked about, he would be given the 7th. In others, the situation is more ambivalent. Be open to what the chart is showing you. For example, a planet recently aspected by one of the querent’s significators could show the new guy; so could a planet recently arrived in the 10th house (just come into the workplace). 一些涉及不止一个 7 宫相关者的问题不涉及被欺骗的配偶：“我和 Tom（汤姆） 约会了几周，但是，哇！现在有个新家伙？”那么，作为被直接询问的人，新家 伙会被赋予 7 宫。在其他情况下，情境更为矛盾。要对星盘向你展示的信息保持 开放。例如，一颗最近与问卜者的一颗征象星形成相位的行星可能显示新家伙； 一颗最近进入 10 宫（刚来到工作场所）的行星也可能显示。

Receptions will often guide us to the correct significator in those charts where someone other than Lord 7 is involved. If this person is in some way an issue there will be receptions confirming this. For example: a woman asks ‘Is my marriage going to survive?’ Venus is Lord 1 and Mars is Lord 7. The querent has the Moon as her cosignificator, and would also have Venus, because she is a woman, were it not that she already has Venus as Lord 1. Her husband has the Sun as his cosignificator, because he is a man. Suppose Mars and the Sun are both in Cancer while the Moon is in Pisces: one of our querent’s significators and both of her husband’s are in strong Jupiter dignities. Whatever Jupiter signifies must be important to them both. The husband exalts Jupiter, with all that this dignity tell us of exaggerated regard, while the Moon is ruled by it. Jupiter, then, may well signify the husband’s mistress: he is crazy about her, while she, by virtue of the role she has assumed in her life, has power over the querent. 在那些涉及 7 宫主以外他人的星盘中，接纳关系常常指引我们找到正确的征象星。 如果此人在某种程度上是个问题，将会有接纳关系证实这一点。例如：一位女士

问“我的婚姻能维持下去吗？”金星是 1 宫主，火星是 7 宫主。问卜者有月亮作 为她的共同征象星，并且本应还有金星，因为她是女性，但金星已是她的 1 宫主。 她的丈夫有太阳作为他的共同征象星，因为他是男性。假设火星和太阳都在巨蟹 座，而月亮在双鱼座：我们问卜者的一颗征象星和她丈夫的两颗征象星都处于强 大的木星尊贵状态。无论木星象征什么，必定对他们双方都很重要。丈夫对木星 呈旺势，这揭示了过度的关注；而月亮被木星守护。那么，木星很可能象征丈夫 的情妇：他对她非常着迷，而她，凭借她在生活中扮演的角色，对问卜者拥有影 响力。

Lilly tells us to take the planet from which the Moon has most recently separated as another significator for the querent, and that to which it next applies as another significator for the quesited. Don’t! These extra significators do nothing but clutter the picture to no purpose. Lilly 告诉我们，取月亮最近刚出相位的行星作为问卜者的另一征象星，取月亮 接下来入相位的行星作为所占之事的另一征象星。不要这样做！这些额外的征象 星除了毫无意义地使图像混乱外，别无他用。

### ✸ This is one more idea that exists only in order to facilitate the giving of the

pleasing judgement. The Moon will usually signify the querent, so if the planet to which the Moon applies automatically signifies Prince Charming, ‘Oh look, your planet applies to his: your dreams will come true!’ ✷

### ✸这又是一个仅仅为了便于给出令人愉悦的判断而存在的想法。月亮通常象征

问卜者，所以如果月亮入相的行星自动象征白马王子，“哦看，你的行星与他的 行星入相：你的梦想将会成真！”✷

Another significator which is often of the greatest importance is the dispositor of the Part of Marriage. If our main significators share a strong interest, as shown by reception, in a planet which as yet has no role in the chart, four times out of five you will find that this planet is the dispositor of the Part of Marriage. Refer back to pages 138-142 for a discussion of this and related Parts. 另一个常常至关重要的征象星是婚姻点的定位星。如果我们主要的征象星通过接 纳关系显示出对一颗尚未在星盘中扮演角色的行星有强烈的共同兴趣，十有八九 你会发现这颗行星是婚姻点的定位星。关于此点及相关点的讨论，请回看第 231
- 236 页。

In some questions the Part of Divorce is useful (see page 141). Mars itself can also be a significator of divorce, if it’s not already in use signifying one of the people involved. If, and only if, it is very close to the action, Uranus too can show divorce or separation. For instance, if the question is ‘Will this relationship last?’ finding Uranus on the 7th cusp is testimony that it will not. Finding it on the Ascendant, however, may show only that the idea of divorce is weighing on the querent. 在某些问题中，离婚点是有用的（见第 235 页）。火星本身也可以是离婚的征象

星，如果它尚未被用作象征所涉及的人之一。如果，且仅如果，天王星非常接近 事件核心，它也可以显示离婚或分离。例如，如果问题是“这段关系会持久吗？” 发现天王星在 7 宫头就是它不会持久的征象。然而，发现它在上升点，可能只表 明离婚的想法正压在问卜者心头。

Receptions 接纳关系

Look back at chapter 8, on receptions. 请回顾第 8 章关于接纳关系的内容。

We now have up to three significators (Lord 1, Moon and either Sun or Venus) for our querent and either one or two (Lord 7 and either Sun or Venus) for the quesited. Each of the different significators shows a different facet of that person: 现在，我们为问卜者配备了最多三个征象星（1 宫主、月亮以及太阳或金星）， 为所占之事配备了一到两个（7 宫主以及太阳或金星）。每个不同的征象星都显 示了该人的不同面向：

* Lord 1 and Lord 7 show that person as thinking being, as personality, as ‘head’
* 1 宫主和 7 宫主显示该人作为思考者、作为个性、作为”头脑"的一面

* the Moon shows the querent, but specifically the querent’s emotions: the heart
* 月亮显示问卜者，但特指问卜者的情感：内心

* the Sun and Venus, if in use as natural significator of man or woman, show the animal.
* 太阳和金星，如果被用作男或女的自然征象星，则显示其动物性本能。

This has much to do with sexual attraction, and you will rarely go far wrong by using this to give a simple division of the person into head, heart and lust. There is, though, more to it than that. It shows the biological imperative to unite with someone of the opposite sex. Forget all about political correctness when considering this: it is pure Tarzan and Jane – ‘You good woman. Come back to my cave and bear me strong children’. It is the man in his Man-stuff; the woman in her Woman-stuff. My experience is that the problem behind many questions asked on relationships revolve around a failure to recognise how great a role this side of the nature plays in the formation of attitude. 这与性吸引力有很大关系，通过将其简单地划分为头脑、内心和欲望来理解一个 人，通常不会错得太远。然而，其内涵不止于此。它显示了与异性结合的生物性 本能驱力。在思考这一点时，请抛开所有政治正确性：这是纯粹的 Tarzan（泰山） 和 Jane（简）——“你是个好女人。回到我的洞穴，为我生育强壮的孩子。”它 显示男人作为男人的特质；女人作为女人的特质。根据我的经验，许多感情问题 背后的症结，往往源于未能认识到这天性的一面在态度形成中扮演了多重要的角

色。

### ✸This last is an important point not sufficiently emphasized here. Especially once

the relationship is established and the blaze of passion a little quieter, problematic issues involving the Sun (when significator of the man in his Man-stuff) often have less to do with virtuosity between the sheets than with the willingness or capacity for earning a living. Similarly with Venus when significator of the woman in her Woman-stuff. What Tarzan and Jane expect of themselves and of each other. ✷

### ✷最后这一点很重要，但此处强调不足。特别是在关系确立、激情火焰稍息之

后，涉及太阳（当作为象征男人特质的征象星时）的问题，往往与床笫之欢的技 巧关系不大，而更与谋生的意愿或能力相关。金星作为象征女人特质的征象星时 亦然。Tarzan 和 Jane 对自己以及对彼此的期望是什么。✷

Receptions show the motives and values of the people involved. In many relationship questions an analysis of this is all that is required: ‘Does he really love me?’ or ‘What is going on in our relationship?’ Even in those questions that are oriented towards an event (‘Will she marry me?’) the receptions are of the utmost importance: the other person will not marry (or date, or continue a relationship) without a motive for doing so. This motive does not need to be love. Example: the querent’s significators are not in any dignity of the quesited’s, but they do exalt Lord 8. ‘You don’t love this guy: you’re after his money (8th house is 2nd from 7th: the partner’s money). Unfortunately, (Lord 8 in its detriment) he hasn’t got any.’ 接纳关系显示了相关人员的动机和价值观。在许多关系问题中，对此进行分析就 足够了：“他真的爱我吗？”或“我们的关系到底怎么了？”即使是在那些以事 件为导向的问题中（“她会嫁给我吗？”），接纳关系也至关重要：没有动机， 对方是不会结婚（或约会，或继续关系）的。这种动机不一定是爱。例如：问卜 者的征象星不在所占之事的任何尊贵状态中，但它们确实对 8 宫主呈旺势。“你 并不爱这个人：你是图他的钱（8 宫是 7 宫的 2 宫：伴侣的钱）。不幸的是，（8 宫主处于落陷）他根本没钱。”

As that example suggests, in these questions we are often clarifying the querent’s own feelings as much as analyzing the other person’s. Suppose the question is ‘Does my relationship with X have a future?’ and the querent’s significators show little interest in X’s significators, but are all disposited by the ruler of the Part of Marriage: ‘You don’t have any real feeling for this guy; you just want a relationship and her happened along’. This is not the full answer to such a question, but it will have a great bearing on it. Often the answer to ‘Is there a future with him?’ is not Yes or No, but ‘Are you quite sure you want a future with him?’ 正如那个例子所暗示的，在这类问题中，我们常常既要分析对方的感受，也要澄 清问卜者自身的感受。假设问题是“我和 X 的关系有未来吗？”而问卜者的征 象星对 X 的征象星几乎不感兴趣，但它们全部被婚姻点的定位星定位：“你对 这个人并没有真正的感情；你只是想要一段关系，而他恰好出现了。”这并非此

类问题的完整答案，但将对其有重大影响。通常，“和他有未来吗？”的答案不 是“是”或“否”，而是“你确定你想和他有未来吗？”

That we are given different significators to show different parts of the person’s being is important. It is a rare chart in which the querent’s significators all agree with each other. People probably don’t ask horary questions if they are completely unified in their view of the other person, but only when they feel an uncomfortable ambivalence. 星盘赋予我们不同的征象星来显示一个人存在的不同部分，这一点很重要。问卜 者的所有征象星彼此完全一致的星盘是罕见的。如果人们在对另一个人的看法上 完全统一，他们可能不会来问卜卦问题，只有当他们对对方感到一种令人不安的 矛盾心理时才会如此。

Example: the querent is a man and: 示例：问卜者为男性，且：

Lord Asc (querent as head) is in the fall of Lord 7; 上升点主星（问卜者作为头脑）位于 7 宫主弱势的位置；

the Moon (querent’s heart) is in Leo 月亮（问卜者的内心）在狮子座

The Sun (querent as Man) is in the exaltation of Lord 7. 太阳（问卜者作为男人）位于 7 宫主旺势的位置。

‘You are very attracted to her (Sun exalts Lord 7); this extreme (exaltation) attraction is dominating your feelings and no doubt making you think that you love her (Moon is ruled by the Sun, which is querent as Man, but has itself no interest in Lord 7); but you can’t stand her personality (Lord Asc in fall of Lord 7).’ “你非常被她吸引（太阳对 7 宫主呈旺势）；这种极端的（旺势）吸引力主导着 你的感受，无疑让你以为你爱她（月亮被太阳守护，而太阳是作为男人的问卜者， 但其本身对 7 宫主并无兴趣）；但你无法忍受她的个性（上升点主星在 7 宫主的 弱势中）。”

Miscellaneous notes 补充说明

Reception by exaltation is very powerful, but is not built to last. Remember that exaltation, like all receptions, doesn’t tell us anything about the other person’s feelings: we must look at the receptions of the other person’s significators to find out about that. It is not uncommon for ‘Is there a future in our relationship?’ to show one of the querent’s significators nearing the end of the sign in which it exalts Lord 7. If other testimonies agree, this shows ‘No, your relationship is coming to an end – because soon you will not want it to continue’. As the querent is still in the thrall of

this exaltation, such a judgement is invariably met with disbelief. 旺势接纳关系非常强大，但往往难以持久。请记住，旺势接纳如同所有接纳关系 一样，并未告诉我们对方的感受：我们必须查看对方征象星的接纳关系来了解这 一点。在“我们的关系有未来吗？”这样的问题中，常可见问卜者的一颗征象星 正接近 7 宫主旺势的星座的末尾。若其他征象也一致，这便显示“不，你们的关 系即将结束——因为你很快将不再希望它继续”。由于问卜者此时仍受此旺势关 系支配，这样的判断往往招致怀疑。

A woman’s significator is combust in a chart where the Sun signifies the man as Man: she is overwhelmed by his masculine attraction. This can happen even if receptions are negative. Combustion too doesn’t last. 在一个以太阳象征男性特质的星盘中，若一位女性的征象星处于燃烧状态：她完 全被他的男性魅力所压倒。即使接纳关系为负面，这种情况也可能发生。燃烧状 态同样不会持久。

A female querent’s significators are weak, show little interest in the man she’s asking about, and are ruled by Venus, Venus signifying her as Woman. She feels that she as Woman is in need of some attention. Similarly with a man whose significators are weak and in major Sun dignities. 一位女性问卜者的征象星虚弱，对她所询问的男性兴趣寥寥，且被金星定位，而 金星正是象征她女性特质的行星。这表明她感觉自己作为女性，需要获得一些关 注。同样，一位男性若其征象星虚弱且处于太阳的主要尊贵状态（如入庙），也 显示类似感受。

Don’t be unrealistic in what you expect to find! People do manage to have satisfactory relationships without all their significators being strong and in powerful mutual reception. 不要对期待发现的情况抱有不切实际的幻想！人们确实能够在并非所有征象星都 强大且处于强力互溶关系的情况下，维持令人满意的关系。

Lord 1 in the sign on the 7th cusp will automatically be in its detriment. This shows that querent loves the person asked about, and, because of that love, is vulnerable. In this case the detriment can be disregarded. If Lord 1 is in the other sign ruled by Lord 7, it will still be in its detriment and, again, the reception shows that the querent loves that person. But this shows a quite different dynamic: the querent is miserable, and therefore loves that person (‘Oh wonderful person, who will stop me being unhappy’). With the obvious implication that if the querent stops being miserable, the love too will stop. The same distinction is true of Lord 7 in the sign on the Ascendant or in the other sign ruled by Lord 1. 1 宫主若位于 7 宫头所在的星座，将自动处于落陷状态。这表明问卜者爱着被询 问的人，并且因为这份爱而变得脆弱。在这种情况下，可以忽略落陷的含义。若 1 宫主位于 7 宫主守护的另一个星座，它仍将处于落陷状态，并且，接纳关系再 次显示问卜者爱着那个人。但这显示了一种完全不同的动力：问卜者因痛苦而滋 生爱意（“哦，了不起的人啊，谁能让我不再痛苦”）。其明显含义是，如果问

卜者停止了痛苦，这份爱也将随之停止。同样，7 宫主位于上升点所在星座或 1 宫主守护的另一个星座时，也存在类似的区别。

Conjunction: in a question about relationships, if one of the main significators in conjunct a planet that is not one of the main significators, it is a certain sign that the person signified is with someone else. Remember that Lilly and his contemporaries used ‘copulation’ as a synonym for conjunction – which it is: that is what conjunction means. A woman asked ‘When will I meet a man?’ and the chart showed her main significator conjunct two other planets. ‘What do you mean? You’re with two men now.’ ‘Yes. But they don’t count.’ 合相：在关于关系的问题中，若主要征象星之一与一颗非主要征象星形成合相， 这明确象征该征象星所代表的人正与他人在一起。请记住，Lilly 及其同时代的 人曾用“交合”作为合相的同义词——事实就是如此：这就是合相的含义。一位 女性问“我何时会遇到一个男人？”，星盘显示她的主要征象星与另外两颗行星 合相。“你是什么意思？你现在正和两个男人在一起。”“是的。但他们不算数。”

### ✸ A little overstated, in that conjunction with an unidentified planet will usually

show that person is busy with somebody else. But it can mean other things if there is compelling evidence otherwise. Example: a woman was asking if her boyfriend would marry her. Receptions showed she had little interest in him, and one of her significators was conjunct another planet, in which she showed great interest. A puzzling picture, explained by the planet she was conjunct being Lord 5: she was pregnant.✷

### ✸略有夸张的是，与一颗未明确定位的行星合相，通常显示此人正与他人纠缠。

但若有强有力的相反证据，也可能意味着其他情况。例如：一位女性询问她的男 朋友是否会娶她。接纳关系显示她对他兴趣不大，而她的一颗征象星与另一颗行 星合相，她对那颗行星却表现出极大兴趣。这一令人困惑的画面得以解释，是因 为与她合相的行星是 5 宫主：她怀孕了。✷

Mars: if receptions show Mars as important in the situation, but it is not significator of either person or dispositor of the Part of Marriage, it may well be acting as natural ruler of either lust or divorce. Or, as with any unassigned planet, it may signify ‘some other person’. 火星：如果接纳关系显示火星在情境中很重要，但它既不是任何人的征象星，也 不是婚姻点的定位星，那么它很可能在作为欲望或离婚的自然征象星。或者，如 同任何未被分配的行星一样，它可能象征“某个其他人”。

Do not introduce extra characters without good evidence for doing so. You are not writing soap opera! 若无充分证据，不要引入额外角色。你可不是在写肥皂剧！

When will I? 我何时会？

Identify the significators, then look for an aspect between any of querent’s and any of the quesited’s, timing it in the usual way. Application to the 7th cusp will not do. Nor will application to the Part of Marriage or its dispositor. Consider the receptions: without some suitable reception the aspect will not produce the event. 首先确定征象星，然后寻找问卜者的任一征象星与所占之事的任一征象星之间的 相位，并按照常规方式推演时间。入相 7 宫头是不够的。入相婚姻点或其定位星 也是不够的。必须考量接纳关系：若缺乏某种恰当的接纳关系，相位将不会促成 事件。

If the question is ‘When will I marry?’ the timing shown is for the decision: the timing of the event itself – when the church is booked and when the caterers are available – is up to the people involved. I know of no way to distinguish between marriage and commitment without marriage, although if the relationship already exists an applying aspect can be taken to show its formalisation in marriage. 如果问题是“我何时会结婚？”，所显示的时间指向的是“决定”的时刻：事件 本身的时间（预定教堂、确定餐饮供应时间等）则取决于当事人。据我所知，无 法通过星盘区分结婚与无婚姻的承诺关系，但如果关系已经存在，一个入相可以 视作其通过婚姻正式化的标志。

The chart will usually show the next significant relationship rather than the ‘soul mate’ that is sometimes requested. 星盘通常显示的是下一段重要的关系，而非有时问卜者所寻求的“灵魂伴侣”。

“What if there is no aspect?” Querents commonly ignore the preliminary question of ‘Will I?’ and jump straight to ‘When?’ If the chart shows an aspect, we can do the same; if it does not, we may need to investigate if there will ever be such a relationship: see below. Usually, however, in such cases the querent’s significators are weak and there is more reception between the querent’s own significators than there is between them and the significators of the prospective mate. You will usually find that the querent’s significators are heading towards places where they are less weak. Often the next sign they enter will be their own. In such cases we don’t need to address the ‘Will I ever?’ but can suggest that the querent is unhappy at the moment, and is too busy licking past wounds to be ready for a relationship, but after whatever length of time (timing the gain of strength as usual) will be once again – so let’s take another look at the situation then. Such charts often show the break-up of a recent relationship by separating aspects, especially oppositions. “如果没有相位怎么办？” 问卜者常常忽略“我会吗？”这个前置问题，直接 跳到“何时？”。如果星盘显示有相位，我们可以照常推时；如果没有，我们可 能需要探究是否终究会有这样一段关系（见下文）。然而，通常情况下，此类星 盘中问卜者的征象星虚弱，并且问卜者自身征象星之间的接纳关系，比它们与潜 在伴侣征象星之间的接纳关系更为显著。通常你会发现问卜者的征象星正移向它

们不那么虚弱的位置。通常它们下一个进入的星座会是它们自己守护的星座。在 这种情况下，我们不需要处理“我终究会吗？”这个问题，而是可以指出问卜者 此刻不快乐，正忙于舔舐过去的伤口而无暇准备开始新关系，但在经过一段时间 （按照常规方法推算获得力量的时间）后将会再次准备好——因此，我们可以建 议彼时再审视情况。这类星盘常通过出相位，特别是对冲相位，来显示近期关系 的破裂。

If a description of the quesited is required, take it from Lord 7, not from any cosignificator. Qualify the indications of Lord 7 by its dispositor, other major dignities and tight aspects to it. Judge the quesited’s wealth from the 8th house (2nd from the 7th) and job from the 4th (10th from the 7th). 如果需要描述所占之事的特征，应从 7 宫主获取，而非从任何共同征象星。需根 据其定位星、其他主要尊贵状态以及与它的紧密相位，来界定 7 宫主所指示的特 征。判断所占之事的财富看 8 宫（7 宫的 2 宫），工作看 4 宫（7 宫的 10 宫）。

To decide where they will meet, we need to decide who is going to whom. This is not shown by which significator applies to which. Whose significators have more accidental strength? It will be that person who goes to where the other one is. BUT: although being in an angular house gives accidental strength, if the quesited’s significator is close to the 7th cusp and in the same sign as that cusp, this is powerful testimony that this person is not coming out to play, no matter what aspect there might be. Similarly, if the querent’s planets are in the 1st house the querent will not stir much to make things happen. It might seem odd that the querent has asked this question with such an attitude, but it is by no means rare. Other testimonies usually show that the querent feels she ought to be in a relationship, even though she does not really want one – or doesn’t want one that involves another person. 要判断他们将在何处相遇，我们需要确定谁会去往谁所在之处。这并非由哪颗征 象星入相另一颗所显示。谁的征象星拥有更强的偶然尊贵？那么将是这个人前往 另一个人所在的地方。但是：尽管位于角宫能带来偶然尊贵，但如果所占之事的 征象星接近 7 宫头且与该宫头位于同一星座，这便是强有力的征象，表明此人不 会主动行动，无论存在何种相位。类似地，如果问卜者的行星位于 1 宫，问卜者 也不会太积极地去促成事情发生。问卜者以这样的态度提出这个问题可能显得奇 怪，但这绝非罕见。其他征象通常表明，问卜者觉得自己“应该”有一段关系， 即使她并非真正想要——或者不想要一段涉及他人的关系。

Having decided which person is going to which – person A is going to person B – take the house occupied by person B’s aspected significator to show where the meeting happens. This will usually be the 10th (at work), 11th (through friends) or 9th house. The 9th covers most of the other usual meeting-places: evening-class, church, holidays. For a querent from a culture where an arranged or introduced match is anticipated, it will show the marriage bureau. This fills the role once taken by the local wise man (9th) in arranging a match, and so is itself shown by the 9th house. 确定了谁将去往谁那里（A 去往 B 所在处）之后，取 B 那颗被入相的征象星所 落入的宫位，来显示相遇发生的地点。这通常是 10 宫（工作中）、11 宫（通过

朋友）或 9 宫。9 宫涵盖了其他大多数常见的相遇地点：夜校、教堂、度假地。 对于来自预期包办婚姻或介绍相亲文化的问卜者，这可以显示婚姻介绍所。这相 当于过去由当地智者（9 宫所象征）安排配对所扮演的角色，因此其本身由 9 宫 象征。

Will I ever? 我终究会吗？

This is one of the questions with which we must be aware of the default option. If the querent is 20, we must judge Yes unless the chart shouts No; if the querent is 80, we must judge No unless the chart shouts Yes. 这是我们必须意识到存在“默认选项”的问题之一。如果问卜者 20 岁，我们必 须判断“会”，除非星盘强烈显示“不会”；如果问卜者 80 岁，我们必须判断 “不会”，除非星盘强烈显示“会”。

Testimonies for marriage: 支持婚姻的征象：

* Lord 1, Moon or Venus/Sun (depending on querent’s sex) in a fertile sign
* 1 宫主、月亮或金星/太阳（根据问卜者性别而定）位于肥沃星座

* Lord 1 in the 7th, or Lord 7 in the 1st
* 1 宫主在 7 宫内，或 7 宫主在 1 宫内

* Moon beholding Sun or Venus (regardless of querent’s sex). See page 113 for a definition of ‘beholding’.
* 月亮注视太阳或金星（无论问卜者性别）。“注视”的定义见第 192 - 193 页。

### ✸Lord 1 in the 7th shows that the querent is keen. Marriage is then, of course, more

likely than if querent is not keen; but this shows us no more than that.✷

### ✸1 宫主在 7 宫显示问卜者非常渴望。当然，这比问卜者不渴望时更有可能结

婚；但此征象仅此而已。✷

If the qurerent is 80, I would be reluctant to judge Yes without a direct aspect between main significators. 如果问卜者 80 岁，除非主要征象星之间有直接相位，否则我不愿判断“会”。

Major negative testimonies would be: 主要的负面征象包括：

* debilitated Saturn on the 7th cusp – unless Saturn is Lord 1

* 衰弱的土星在 7 宫头——除非土星是 1 宫主

* debilitated Saturn on Ascendant – unless Saturn is Lord 7
* 衰弱的土星在上升点——除非土星是 7 宫主

* Lord 7 combust and applying to the Sun – unless the querent is male or the Sun is Lord 1.
* 7 宫主处于燃烧状态且正入相太阳——除非问卜者为男性或太阳是 1 宫主。

If the question is, ‘Will I ever, and when?’ and these testimonies and the default option are enough to allow a Yes, you can be very flexible with the usual rules when finding the timing. Once you know that the event will happen, you know that the timing must be in the chart somewhere – and sometimes this timing is not so obvious. With the usual limitations of not taking a planet through either its station or conjunction with the Sun, you can ignore the other prohibitions, which can instead be read as events along the way. Prohibiting aspects will not prohibit and you can take a planet into its next sign. But do use your common sense: if you have to take the significator forward by three signs to find an aspect, you have probably missed another option. 如果问题是“我终究会吗？如果会，何时？”，并且这些征象和默认选项足以允 许判断“会”，那么在推时上你可以非常灵活地运用常规规则。一旦你确定事件 将会发生，你就知道时间信息必定隐藏在星盘的某个地方——有时这个时间点并 不那么明显。在遵循常规限制（不考虑行星停滞或与太阳合相）的前提下，你可 以忽略其他的阻碍相位，它们反而可以被解读为过程中的事件。阻碍相位将不再 阻碍，你也可以考虑行星进入下一个星座的情况。但务必运用你的常识：如果你 必须将征象星向前推进三个星座才能找到一个相位，那你很可能错过了另一种选 项。

Regardless of what signifies whom, an applying Sun/Moon conjunction is an excellent indicator of marriage. 无论行星各自象征谁，一个正在形成的太阳/月亮合相是婚姻的极佳征象。

Will it last? 会持久吗？

If the question is about a marriage, or about the starting of a relationship, the nature of the aspect showing the event does not tell us anything about how the marriage will proceed. Whether the aspect is, for example, a sextile or a square shows how easily the couple gets to the altar; it shows nothing about what happens afterwards. A square aspect could bring the happiest of marriage, but it will show that there are some snags on the way to the wedding. Maybe he has to ask her more than once. Maybe the wedding has to wait until her mother can attend. The only aspect that affects what happens afterwards is the opposition. This brings the two parties together with regret,

which, in our society, usually results in divorce. 如果问题是关于一段婚姻，或一段关系的开始，那么显示事件的相位性质本身， 并不告诉我们婚姻将如何发展。例如，相位是六合还是刑相位，只显示双方结合 （走到婚姻殿堂）的顺利程度；完全不预示之后会发生什么。刑相位可能带来最 幸福的婚姻，但它表明在通往婚礼的路上存在一些阻碍。也许他不得不向她求婚 不止一次。也许婚礼必须等到她母亲能出席。唯一会影响后续发展的相位是对冲 相位。这会使双方带着遗憾结合，而在我们的社会中，这通常会导致离婚。

To judge ‘Will we be happy?’ look at the receptions between the two people’s significators. Don’t expect too much, and don’t be put off by some major negatives amid positives: we are dealing with real life, not fairy tale. Do be wary of strong receptions which a change of sign is about to end. Look also at the Part of Marriage and, especially, its dispositor. Consider its essential strength (showing happiness) and the nature of the sign it is in. Fixed shows permanence, cardinal a quick flame that burns and dies, mutable a coming and going. But read this, as always, in the light of other testimonies. 要判断“我们会幸福吗？”，需看两人征象星之间的接纳关系。不要期望过高， 也不要因为积极征象中出现一些重大负面因素而却步：我们处理的是现实生活， 而非童话故事。务必要警惕那些即将因星座改变而结束的强烈接纳关系。同时也 要看婚姻点，尤其是它的定位星。考量其先天强弱（显示幸福程度）及其所在星 座的属性。固定星座显示持久，基本星座显示快速燃起又熄灭的火焰，变动星座 显示来来回回。但要一如既往，结合其他征象来解读。

### ✸Receptions show attitudes, and two people neither of whom knows the other exists

cannot have attitudes towards each other. So in a question such as ‘When will I meet the man I will marry?’ the receptions can tell us only about attitudes right now, not how the couple will get along once married. The Part of Marriage, however, tells us about the relationship between the querent and the 7th-house person. This relationship doesn’t exist until they have met, so in questions like this the Part of Marriage can tell us only about the future, and the matter of future happiness must be judged from that. ✷

### ✸接纳关系显示态度，而两个互不相识的人不可能对彼此有态度。因此，在诸

如“我何时会遇到我将要结婚的人？”这样的问题中，接纳关系只能告诉我们当 下的态度，而非两人婚后将如何相处。然而，婚姻点告诉我们问卜者与 7 宫相关 者之间的关系。这种关系在他们相遇之前并不存在，所以在此类问题中，婚姻点 只能告诉我们未来，未来的幸福与否必须据此判断。✷

You will often be asked ‘Is there a future in this relationship?’ when the couple has barely met. Some charts show a clear No; the occasional one shows a strong long-term bond; most show sufficient to keep the relationship alive for a while, but not beyond that. Unless a decision must be made on whether to commit in some way – perhaps by taking a joint mortgage – or if the other person is a serial killer, the

purpose of asking such a question quite escapes me. If the querent were to drop every man when the astrologer says No, she would never acquire the emotional education needed to embark on that relationship for which the astrologer might say Yes. 你常会在双方刚认识不久时被问到“这段关系有未来吗？”。有些星盘明确显示 “没有”；偶尔有些显示强烈的长期纽带；大多数显示有足够的维系因素让关系 存活一阵子，但仅此而已。除非必须就是否以某种方式（例如共同抵押贷款）做 出承诺而决定，或者对方是连环杀手，否则我实在无法理解问这种问题的目的。 如果占星师一说“没有”，问卜者就放弃每一个男人，那她将永远无法获得情感 上的成长，而这种成长正是开启占星师可能说“有”的那段关系所必需的。

You will also often be asked the same question at moments of crisis in an established relationship. It is always wise to enquire if there is anyone else involved when the question is first asked; if you do so when delivering your judgement later the querent may assume that you have seen this in the chart, when in fact you are only seeking to clarify a planet’s role that you’re not sure about. Judgement on such questions will be largely by receptions, and as such can identify stresses and potentials – which is surely more useful than making a flat prediction. Even if there is little positive reception between the spouses, remember that the status quo will continue unless someone decides to end it. Even if they loathe each other, is anyone going to act? Look for oppositions and for planets changing house or sign. Such changes may be positive, especially if they involve an increase in reception, or they may show nothing of significance; but, for instance, Lord 7 leaving the 1st house can show ‘Your wife’s about to leave you’, or Lord 1 leaving a sign ruled by the dispositor of the Part of Marriage can show ‘It looks as if you are on the point of walking out’. 你也常会在既定关系出现危机时被问到同样的问题。在问题提出之初，询问是否 有他人介入总是明智的；如果你在稍后给出判断时才问，问卜者可能会以为你是 从星盘中看出来的，而实际上你只是试图澄清一颗你不确定的行星所扮演的角色。 对此类问题的判断主要依据接纳关系，从而可以识别出压力和潜力——这肯定比 做出一个断然的预测更有用。即使配偶之间的积极接纳关系很少，也要记住，现 状将持续下去，除非有人决定结束它。即使他们互相憎恨，会有人采取行动吗？ 寻找对冲相位以及行星换宫或换座的迹象。这种变化可能是积极的（特别是如果 它涉及接纳关系的增强），也可能显示并无重大意义；但是，例如，7 宫主离开 1 宫可能显示“你的妻子即将离开你”，或者 1 宫主离开婚姻点定位星所守护的 星座可能显示“看起来你好像正要出走”。

Such charts will often suggest possibilities for improving the relationship, or spotlight behaviours that exacerbate the situation, so the judgement is often ‘If you carry on doing xyz, he’ll leave’ or ‘Unless you do abc she’ll divorce you’. Examples: suppose with a male querent Lord 1 is keen on Lord 7, but the Sun hates her, and Lord 7 and Venus show major interest in the Sun: ‘Unless you show her some physical attention…’ Or if the Moon loves Lord 7, but is in a mute sign, ‘Unless you tell her you love her…’ 这类星盘通常会提出改善关系的可能性，或突显加剧局势的行为，因此判断往往 是“如果你继续做 xyz，他就会离开”或“除非你做 abc，否则她会和你离婚”。

例如：假设一位男性问卜者，其 1 宫主对 7 宫主很感兴趣，但太阳（作为其男性 特质的征象）却厌恶她，而 7 宫主和金星（作为对方女性特质的征象）却对太阳 表现出极大的兴趣：“除非你对她表现出一些身体上的关注……”或者，如果月 亮（问卜者的情感）爱着 7 宫主，但却在一个沉默的星座：“除非你告诉她你爱 她……”

Be wary of announcing affairs on any evidence other than that of conjunction. And even then, be wary of announcing affairs: you may be able to see it; this does not necessarily mean that the querent needs to hear it. Mutual reception, no matter how strong, may show a high mutual regard between two people, but is not in itself evidence of infidelity. Although if the receptions show all the spouse’s attention directed towards someone else? Perhaps there is powerful mutual reception between Lord 7 and another planet – but maybe that planet rules the turned 10th, showing hubby wrapped up in his work. If you have a conjunction, there need not be any reception at all between the two planets: the people may be happily conjuncting without their emotions being involved. Do not underestimate the power of flattery: if the suspect planet is in the sign or exaltation of Lord 7, Lord 7 may have his head turned without reciprocating the feelings. Especially if the suspect planet is just inside the 7th house. Similarly if a woman is asking and an unidentified planet is combust (Sun being husband as animal man): he has someone throwing herself at him. But without close conjunction, there is no firm evidence that he is responding. The more essential dignity the suspected spouse’s planets have (showing him/her honourable) and the more reception they have with the querent’s planets (showing love for the querent), the less likely he/she will be to stray. 要警惕仅凭合相以外的任何证据就宣布有婚外情。即使是合相证据，也要警惕宣 布有婚外情：你或许能看到；但这未必意味着问卜者需要听到它。互溶关系，无 论多么强烈，可能只表明两人之间有高度的相互尊重，但本身并非不忠的证据。 不过，如果接纳关系显示配偶所有的注意力都指向了别人呢？也许 7 宫主与另一 颗行星之间有强大的互溶关系——但那颗行星可能是转宫 10 宫（事业）的主星， 显示丈夫埋头于工作。如果有合相，两颗行星之间甚至可能完全没有任何接纳关 系：人们可能愉快地结合，但并未投入感情。不要低估奉承的力量：如果可疑行 星在 7 宫主的入庙或旺势位置，7 宫主可能会被迷惑，但未必回报以感情。尤其 是如果可疑行星刚好在 7 宫内。同样，如果是一位女性问卜者，且一颗未明确定 位的行星处于燃烧状态（太阳是丈夫作为动物性男人的征象）：说明有女人向他 投怀送抱。但若没有紧密的合相，就没有确凿证据表明他有回应。可疑配偶的行 星拥有的先天尊贵越多（显示他/她品行端正），并且与问卜者行星之间的接纳 关系越多（显示对问卜者的爱），他/她出轨的可能性就越小。

Querents sometimes ask if the partner is homosexual. If the suspicion is of an affair with some particular person, treat this exactly as affair questions above. More often, it is a general enquiry. If the partner is male, look for his significators in strong Sun dignities, or in the detriment or fall of Venus, showing a liking for men or a hatred of women. Yes, if the Sun is in strong Sun dignities it could show that he is full of the usual sexual feelings, but the question is presumably not asked if the querent is

receiving these. Remember that the question asked determines the reality of the chart. The Sun in the turned 12th house (the radical 6th) gives cause for suspicion: he seems to be hiding something about his sexuality, though this may not be that he is homosexual. The Sun in the radical 12th could show that he is up to something he would prefer the querent not to know about, but this too may be unconnected to homosexuality. If the querent is a man asking about his female partner, look for her significators in strong Venus dignities or in the detriment or fall of the Sun, or Venus in the turned 12th. Important: do not import these testimonies into questions where this is not the issue addressed! If you find, for instance, the Sun in Scorpio in the chart for any other relationship question, this does not mean that the man is homosexual. 问卜者有时会询问伴侣是否是同性恋。如果怀疑是与某个特定的人有染，则完全 按照上述婚外情问题处理。更常见的情况是笼统的询问。如果伴侣是男性，寻找 其征象星是否处于太阳的强尊贵状态（如入庙），或在金星的弱势或落陷位置， 这显示喜欢男性或厌恶女性。是的，如果太阳处于其自身的强尊贵状态，也可能 显示他充满通常的性感觉，但如果问卜者正在接收这些感觉，问题大概就不会被 提出了。记住，所问的问题决定了星盘所呈现的现实。太阳在转宫 12 宫（基准 盘的 6 宫）会引起怀疑：他似乎隐藏了一些关于他性取向的事情，尽管这可能并 不意味着他是同性恋。太阳在基准盘 12 宫可能显示他正在做一些宁愿问卜者不 知道的事情，但这也可能与同性恋无关。如果问卜者是男性，询问他的女性伴侣， 则寻找她的征象星是否在金星的强尊贵状态，或在太阳的弱势或落陷位置，或金 星在转宫 12 宫。重要提示：在问题不涉及此议题时，不要引入这些征象！例如， 在任何其他关系问题的星盘中发现太阳在天蝎座，这并不意味着该男性是同性恋。

Will he take me back? 他会让我回去吗？

We have here an aberration. If a woman has been thrown out of her husband’s home and asks if he will forgive her, Lilly gives the woman the 7th house, even though she is the querent.At first I thought this was a historical oddity, but from the tiny number of charts I have judged on this matter, at least one seems to make better sense judged like this. I can see no sound reason for departing from usual practice here, and so suggest that you approach such questions in the usual way, but you should be aware of this point. If there is clear evidence in the chart encouraging you to take Lord 7 as the querent (perhaps the querent admits to having had an affair, and Lord 7 is separating from conjunction with a planet that is not Lord 1), you may, with all due caution, decide to follow Lilly. 我们在此遇到一个特例。如果一位女性被丈夫赶出家门，并询问他是否会原谅她， Lilly 将 7 宫赋予该女性，即使她是问卜者。起初我以为这只是历史奇谈，但 根据我判断过的极少数此类案例，至少有一个星盘似乎按此方式判断更能说得通。 我找不到充分的理由在此处背离常规做法，因此建议你以通常方式处理此类问题， 但你应该知晓这一点。如果星盘中有明确证据鼓励你将 7 宫主视为问卜者（例如 问卜者承认曾有婚外情，而 7 宫主正与一颗非 1 宫主的行星结束合相），你可以 在充分谨慎的前提下，决定遵循 Lilly 的方法。

41. Lilly, p. 318.

Writing in the Seventeenth century, he would have regarded the idea of a woman throwing her husband out of the house as ludicrous, and so gave no instructions for that. 作为十七世纪的作者，他可能会认为女人把丈夫赶出家门这一想法是荒谬的，因 此没有给出相关指示。

### ✸Too much deference to Lilly again. He’s tripped over the prejudices of his age. In

horary, the querent is given the 1st house. There is no reason to make an exception for questions on this one topic.✷

### ✸又是对 Lilly 过分遵从了。他被他那个时代的偏见绊倒了。在卜卦占星中，问

卜者被赋予 1 宫。没有理由仅针对这一个主题问题就破例。✷

Example charts on relationship questions 关于关系问题的示例星盘

See the charts on pages 92 and 122. 参见第 160 页和第 207 页的星盘.

BUSINESS PARTNERSHIPS 商业伙伴

See chapter 23, page 271. 见第 23 章，第 433 页。

SHOULD I STAY OR SHOULD I GO？ 我应该留下还是离开？

‘Am I better off in London, or should I move away?’ ‘Maybe I should go home?’ ‘Should I move to France?’ ‘Should I stay at work, or go back to college?’ Althoug these questions are usually phrased as ‘Should I do X or Y?’ they are rarely such an even choice, i.e. which of two roads to take. The question is usually ‘Should I make this change or should I leave things as they are?’ What the chart shows us is the view forward, as if the querent were standing at the top of a hill, looking at the road stretching into the distance, and thinking either ‘Oo-er, I don’t like the look of that’, or ‘Wow, that looks inviting!’

“我是留在伦敦更好，还是应该搬走？”“也许我应该回家？”“我应该搬到法 国去吗？”“我应该继续工作，还是回大学读书？”虽然这些问题通常以“我应 该做 X 还是 Y？”的形式提出，但它们很少是这种势均力敌的选择，即两条路 选哪一条。问题通常是“我应该做出这个改变，还是应该保持现状？”星盘向我 们展示的是向前看的图景，如同问卜者站在山顶，眺望延伸至远方的道路，心里 想着要么“呃，我不喜欢那个样子”，要么“哇，那看起来很吸引人！”

As such, the 1st house and Lord 1 show things as they are; the 7th house and Lord 7 show things as they will become if the change is made. So: 因此，1 宫和 1 宫主代表现状；7 宫和 7 宫主代表如果做出改变后事物将呈现的 状态。所以：

* 7th house better than 1st: go. If not, stay.
* 7 宫比 1 宫好：离开。若非如此：留下。

* Lord 7 stronger than Lord 1: go. If not, stay.
* 7 宫主比 1 宫主强：离开。若非如此：留下。

* Moon or Lord 1 separating (by any aspect) from a benefic and going to a malefic: stay.
* 月亮或 1 宫主正出相位（任何相位）离开一颗吉星并前往一颗凶星：留下。

* Moon or Lord 1 separating from a malefic and going to a benefic: go.
* 月亮或 1 宫主正出相位离开一颗凶星并前往一颗吉星：离开。

NB: when considering the planet to and from which the Moon and Lord 1 are moving, do remember that ANY planet in strong essential dignity is good, and ANY planet in essential debility is bad. NB:当考量月亮和 1 宫主正在移向和移离的行星时，务必记住：任何处于强先天 尊贵状态的行星都是好的，任何处于先天衰弱状态的行星都是坏的。

Examples: 示例：

* Planet in detriment in 7th house, Lord 1 in its exaltation: stay put.
* 7 宫有行星处于弱势，而 1 宫主处于其旺势：留在原地。

* Dignified planet in 1st house, Moon separates from dignified planet and applies to one that is peregrine: stay put.
* 1 宫有拥有尊贵的行星，月亮出相位离开一颗有尊贵的行星，并正入相一颗游 离的行星：留在原地。

* South Node in 1st house, North Node in 7th: go.
* 南交点在 1 宫，北交点在 7 宫：离开。

“But what if there is conflicting testimony?” There often will be: few such situations are clear-cut. Weigh the number and strength of the various testimonies. In many such charts staying and going are equally good, equally bad: if that is what the chart shows, that is the judgement. Don’t feel that you must produce an unequivocal answer. The answer is often, ‘It doesn’t make much difference’. “但如果征象相互矛盾怎么办？”这种情况常常发生：很少有此类情况是泾渭分 明的。权衡各种征象的数量和强度。在许多这类星盘中，留下和离开同样好或同 样坏：如果星盘显示了这一点，那就是判断结果。不要觉得你必须给出一个明确 的答案。答案常常是：“差别不大”。

Such questions are about change, so the prospective change is often shown in the chart by an imminent change of sign. Lord 1 and/or the Moon will be at the end of a sign, about to enter a new one. Do we let them make this change, or do we keep things as they are? Perhaps they both gain in dignity as they make the change: go! Or perhaps they conjunct debilitated Saturn or enter combustion as soon as they change sign: stay! Or perhaps the change makes no significant difference: stay or go as you please. In such cases the chart is saying ‘This is your prospective future. Do you want to accept this, by moving your planets forward into it, or do you want to stay as you are?’ 这类问题是关于变化的，所以预期的变化常常在星盘中通过即将发生的换座来显 示。1 宫主和/或月亮会处在一个星座的末尾，即将进入一个新的星座。我们是让 它们完成这个变化，还是保持现状？也许它们在变化中获得了更强的尊贵：离开！ 或者也许它们一换座就与衰弱的土星形成合相或进入燃烧状态：留下！又或者这 个变化没有显著影响：请随意，留或走都可以。在这种情况下，星盘是在说：“这 是你预期的未来。你想通过推动你的行星进入这个未来来接受它，还是想保持现 状？”

If the question gives a specific place for ‘there’, you can pick up the querent’s planets and drop them into that house. So if the querent asks, ‘Should I get a job or go to university?’ imagine that you can pick up Lord 1 and place it just inside the 10th cusp. How is it there, by essential and accidental dignity? Then imagine it just inside the 9th cusp. How is it there? This will give a comparison of work and university. If the querent is especially concerned about emotional happiness, do this with the Moon as well as or instead of Lord 1. NB: if you are ‘sending the querent to work’ like this, you cannot, of course, think ‘Lord 1 is in the 10th, therefore it is strong’, because this would always be the case, whatever the work. You can think, ‘If I put Lord 1 in the 10th it is conjunct the South Node and in its detriment. Yuk!’ 如果问题中为“那里”指定了一个具体地点，你可以“拿起”问卜者的行星，“放 置”到那个宫位中。例如，如果问卜者问：“我应该找工作还是去上大学？”想 象一下，你可以拿起 1 宫主，将其刚好放在 10 宫头内侧。它在那里情况如何， 依据先天和偶然尊贵判断？然后想象它刚好在 9 宫头内侧。它在那里情况又如 何？这将提供一个工作与大学的比较。如果问卜者特别关注情感幸福，对月亮也 进行此操作，或以其代替 1 宫主。注意：如果你像这样“把问卜者送到工作场所”，

你当然不能想“1 宫主在 10 宫，所以它很强”，因为无论是什么工作，情况都 会如此。你可以想：“如果我把 1 宫主放在 10 宫，它与南交点合相且处于弱势。 糟糕！”

You CANNOT do this with the general ‘Stay or go?’ 1st versus 7th house question, because putting Lord 1 just inside the 7th cusp will automatically put it in its detriment. 对于笼统的“留下还是离开？”这种 1 宫与 7 宫比较的问题，你不能这样做，因 为把 1 宫主刚好放在 7 宫头内侧会自动使其处于弱势。

Be aware of changes. Suppose the question is ‘How will I get on at college?’ and putting Lord 1 just inside the 9th cusp puts it into its detriment. But the 9th cusp at 27 degrees of its sign, and putting Lord 1 into that next sign gives it strong essential dignity, or brings it conjunct a strongly dignified Jupiter: ‘You’ll get off to a slow start, but once you’ve found your feet you’ll do wonderfully’. 注意变化。假设问题是“我在大学会过得怎么样？”，把 1 宫主刚好放在 9 宫头 内侧使其处于弱势。但 9 宫头在某个星座的 27 度，把 1 宫主放入下一个星座使 其获得强先天尊贵，或使其与一颗拥有强尊贵的木星形成合相：“你起步会比较 慢，但一旦站稳脚跟，你会做得非常出色。”

You can do this if the querent is an immigrant and is asking, ‘Should I go back to X?’ The 1st house will show where he is now, the 4th will show ‘home’ (even if this is an ancestral homeland where the querent has never set foot) and the 9th will show a foreign country. You need to ask the querent, ‘Which do you call home: the country where you live now or the land of your roots?’ This will tell you if the proposed destination is 4th house (my homeland) or 9th (a foreign country). 如果问卜者是移民，并且问：“我应该回 X 国吗？”你可以这样做。1 宫代表他 现在所在的地方，4 宫代表“家”（即使这是问卜者从未踏足的祖籍地），9 宫 代表外国。你需要问问卜者：“你把哪里称为家：是你现在居住的国家，还是你 根源的土地？”这会告诉你提议的目的地是 4 宫（我的祖国）还是 9 宫（外国）。

In general ‘stay or go’ questions, be careful with Lord 4: sometimes it shows the present house, sometimes the potential one. It is best to leave it out of judgement unless you can see which. For instance, if Lord 1 is applying to Lord 4, Lord 4 must be the potential house. 在一般的“留或走”问题中，要小心对待 4 宫主：有时它显示现在的住所，有时 显示潜在的住所。除非你能分清，否则最好不将其纳入判断。例如，如果 1 宫主 正入相 4 宫主，那么 4 宫主必定是潜在的住所。

### ✸I must clarify here. This method of comparing 1st and 7th houses is only for when

the querent is considering long-term physical relocation: ‘Should I stay here or go there?’ It is not to be used for short-term changes, like going on holiday, nor other proposed changes such as of job or house. The job I’m thinking of taking might be on

the other side of the world, but if it’s a matter of whether I want the job it is not a 1st/7th question. It becomes such only if the focus is on the relocation and job is simply a way of making that happen. Similarly with house: ‘Should I stay at work or move to France’ is not about buying this or that property, but the overall picture of whether I will be better off in France.

### ✸我必须在此澄清。这种比较 1 宫和 7 宫的方法，仅适用于问卜者考虑长期实

际搬迁的情况：“我应该留在这里还是去那里？”它不适用于短期变化，如去度 假，也不适用于其他提议的变化，如换工作或换房子。我正在考虑的工作可能在 世界另一端，但如果这是一个我是否想要这份工作的问题，那就不是 1/7 宫的问 题。只有当焦点在搬迁本身，而工作只是实现搬迁的一种方式时，才成为此类问 题。房子问题同理：“我应该继续工作还是搬到法国”不是关于购买这处或那处 房产，而是关于我在法国是否会过得更好的整体图景。

A question such as ‘Should I stay at work or go back to college?’ is not a 1st/7th matter. To judge that, compare the 9th and 10th houses, part of which comparison will be dropping Lord 1 into each of them. We are concerned here with things placed in those houses, for better or for worse; the condition of the houser-rulers: their receptions with Lord 1 and the Moon. Be aware of imminent changes. For instance, suppose Lord 10 is Jupiter at 28 Gemini. The job is in poor condition. But it’s about to have a huge increase in dignity: ‘Stick with the career. It won’t be long before it gets much better’.✷ 诸如“我应该继续工作还是回大学？”这样的问题，不是 1/7 宫范畴的事情。判 断这种问题，需要比较 9 宫和 10 宫，部分比较方法就是将 1 宫主分别“放置” 到这两个宫位中。我们关心的是这些宫位内行星的好坏；宫主星的状态：它们与 1 宫主和月亮的接纳关系。注意即将发生的变化。例如，假设 10 宫主是木星， 在双子座 28 度。工作状况不佳。但它即将获得巨大的尊贵提升：“坚持这份职 业。用不了多久情况就会好很多。”✷

SPORTS AND CONTESTS 体育与竞赛

### ✸This subject is treated in much more depth than space in a general textbook allows,

with many example charts, in my Sports Astrology. ✷

### ✷此主题在拙著《Sports Astrology》中结合众多示例星盘进行了远比一本通用

教科书篇幅所允许的更为深入的探讨。✷

Will we win? 我们会赢吗？

Whether this question is asked by a supporter or by someone who is taking part in the match, it is Us against Them. The team the querent supports is given the 1st house, as an extension of the self, in the same way that the querent would say ‘We won’, despite not himself playing. The unspeakable ruffians his team is competing against are the open enemies: 7th house. 无论此问题是由支持者还是参赛者提出，都是“我方”对阵“敌方”。问卜者支 持的团队被赋予 1 宫，作为自我的延伸，正如问卜者会说“我们赢了”，尽管他 自己并未上场。与他所支持的团队竞争的那些不可言喻的对手，则是公开的敌人： 7 宫。

Be careful: if the querent’s main concern is with betting on the match, treat this as question of profit (chapter 16). 需注意：如果问卜者主要关注的是比赛投注，应将其视为利润问题处理（参见第 16 章）。

For us to be able to judge this question, the querent must have some interest in the outcome of the match for its own sake. His support for the good guys may be only lukewarm, but he must have some preference for one of the teams over the other. If his own team is not playing, it is possible that he might have a hearty dislike of one of the teams involved – perhaps it is his favourite’s local rival. In that case the question is really, ‘Will my enemy be defeated?’ so the enemy is given the 7th house and its opponents – the enemy’s enemy – the 1st. If the querent is indifferent to both teams, we have no criterion for deciding which gets the 1st house and which the 7th, so we cannot judge the chart. Do not be tempted to give the 1st house to the home team, or to the team the querent names first: whatever that might be, it is not horary. Nor can we give it the 7th, as ‘any old person’, because the querent’s indifference makes both teams ‘any old person’. 要让我们能够判断此问题，问卜者必须对比赛结果本身抱有某种兴趣。他对“好 人队”的支持可能并不热烈，但他必须对其中一方比对另一方有所偏好。如果他 自己的主队未参赛，他可能对参赛的其中一队深恶痛绝——也许那是他主队的地 域对手。在这种情况下，问题实质是“我的敌人会失败吗？”，因此将敌人赋予 7 宫，而敌人的对手（即敌之敌）赋予 1 宫。如果问卜者对两队都漠不关心，我 们便没有标准来决定谁得 1 宫、谁得 7 宫，因此无法判断该星盘。切勿因诱惑而 将 1 宫赋予主场队伍，或赋予问卜者首先提及的队伍：无论那是什么，那都不是 卜卦占星。我们也不能将其赋予 7 宫作为“任何人”，因为问卜者的漠不关心使 得双方队伍都成了“任何人”。

This method can be used for questions on individual sports, provided the querent supports or dislikes one or other of the players. It is still Us against Them, as in ‘Will the heroic Brit win this tennis-match?’ The answer to which is ‘No’. 此方法可用于个人运动项目的问题，前提是问卜者支持或厌恶其中一位选手。这 仍然是“我方对阵敌方”，如“那位英勇的英国人会赢得这场网球赛吗？”其答 案是“不会”。

### ✸It is rare to be able to ask such questions of individual sports, because it is rare for

the querent to regard the individual sportsman as ‘us’ as might be done with a team. If the favoured tennis-player wins the querent will probably say ‘He won’ or ‘She won’, not ‘We won’. The usual exception is when the player is seen as representing the country. Thinking the player is good-looking is not enough!✷

### ✸能够就个人运动项目提出此类问题的情况较为罕见，因为问卜者很少会像看

待团队那样将个人运动员视为“我们”。如果受青睐的网球选手获胜，问卜者很 可能会说“他赢了”或“她赢了”，而不是“我们赢了”。通常的例外是当选手 被视为代表国家时。仅仅觉得选手长得好看是不够的！✷

Although we are regarding the team favoured as an extension of the querent, the Moon does not have its usual role as the querent’s cosignificator. At least, it does only in moments of dire emergency when nothing else is happening in the chart. Its role in these questions is usually a minor one, occasionally having a function as ‘the flow of events’. 尽管我们将受支持的团队视为问卜者的延伸，但月亮并不具有其通常作为问卜者 共同征象星的角色。至少，只有在星盘中无其他情况发生、且处于极度紧急的时 刻，它才扮演此角色。在这些问题中，月亮的角色通常是次要的，偶尔作为“事 件流程”发挥作用。

Neither should you concern yourself with houses other than the 1st and the 7th. Too many sports horaries disappear in a fog of confusion as the astrologer seeks to locate the team’s fans, its players and its bank balance in the chart. Keep It Simple! All that concerns us is who will win. This will be shown by the first and seventh houses. While the manager of every losing team may blame defeat on the referee, the horary chart is far more sporting and has no role for Lord 10. 你也不必关注 1 宫和 7 宫以外的宫位。当占星师试图在星盘中定位球队的球迷、 球员及其银行账户时，太多体育卜卦盘会陷入混乱的迷雾中。保持简单！我们关 心的只是谁会赢。这将由 1 宫和 7 宫显示。尽管每支输掉比赛的队伍的经理都可 能将失败归咎于裁判，但卜卦星盘要公平得多，其中没有 10 宫主（裁判的象征） 的角色。

【Sports issues - Posted on June 21st, 2014 【体育赛事问题 - 发布于 2014 年 6 月 21 日

There are two problems with sports predictions that come up again and again. One is with using the method of predicting matches from the time of the event, as I described in chapter 2 of Sports Astrology. I wrote there that the method works better the more singular is the game. For the finals of competitions it works excellently; for routine league fixtures it works no better than random. If you insist on using the method where I’ve said it doesn’t work, please don’t be surprised when you find it doesn’t

work. Note also that a league match is a league match is a league match. It is no more singular because it is the last game of the season, or between Barca and Real, or between the two teams vying for the championship. 体育预测中有两个反复出现的问题。其一是使用我从事件时间预测比赛的方法， 正如我在《Sports Astrology》第二章中描述的那样。我在那本书中写道，比赛越 独特，该方法效果越好。对于决赛，它效果极佳；对于常规联赛，它的效果与随 机猜测无异。如果你坚持在我已经指明无效的地方使用该方法，当你发现它确实 不灵验时，请别感到惊讶。另请注意，联赛比赛就是联赛比赛，不会因为它是一 场赛季收官战，或是巴萨对阵皇马，又或是两支争冠球队之间的较量，就变得独 特起来。

The second common problem is with horaries, especially on tennis matches. If the querent strongly identifies with one team in a match, that team can be given the 1st house and its enemies the 7th. It’s simple: if you support the team you would say ‘We won’ or ‘We lost’. Hence 1st house. Students are reluctant to accept how rare it is for someone to have that level of identification with e.g. a tennis player. You would not say ‘We won’ or ‘We lost’ after a tennis match. Consider the difference. You could have been following your team since you were 5. When you were 5 your favourite tennis player was probably not born. You follow the team regardless of players and managers coming and going. The team is ‘we’ when it wins the championship; it is still ‘we’ 10 years later, when it has been relegated to the minor leagues. Your tennis-player will not be ‘we’ in 10 years’ time, when she is playing for fun in her local park. Yes, you can give the player of an individual sport the 1st house, as ‘we’, but don’t expect to get the judgements right if you do.】 第二个常见问题与卜卦占星有关，尤其是在网球比赛中。如果问卦者强烈认同比 赛中的某一方，该方可以被赋予 1 宫，而其对手则归 7 宫。道理很简单：如果你 支持某支队伍，你会说“我们赢了”或“我们输了”。因此是 1 宫。学生们往往 难以接受，一个人对某事物（例如一位网球运动员）有如此强烈的认同感是多么 罕见。你不会在网球比赛后说“我们赢了”或“我们输了”。考虑一下其中的区 别。你可能从 5 岁起就支持一支队伍。当你 5 岁时，你最喜欢的网球运动员可能 还没出生。无论球员和教练如何来来去去，你都会支持这支队伍。当队伍赢得冠 军时，它是“我们”；十年后，当它降级到低级别联赛时，它仍然是“我们”。 而你的网球运动员，十年后当她在家附近的公园里打着玩的时候，就不会是“我 们”了。是的，你可以将个人项目的运动员作为“我们”赋予 1 宫，但如果你这 样做，就别指望能得到准确的判断。】

Lilly tells us to take the planet from which the Moon has most recently separated as another significator for the querent in a contest horary, and that to which it next applies as another significator for the enemy. Don’t! These extra significators do nothing but clutter the picture. Lilly 告诉我们，在竞赛卜卦盘中，取月亮最近刚出相位的行星作为问卜者的另 一征象星，取月亮接下来入相位的行星作为敌方的另一征象星。不要这样做！这 些额外的征象星除了使图像混乱外，别无他用。

Begin by assessing the condition of the houses themselves. What, if anything, is in them? If there is something there, does it strengthen the house or afflict it? Remember that the closer a planet is to the house cusp, the greater its effect on that house. The effect of a planet that is in the house, but in a different sign to the house cusp, will be much diminished. This is so no matter how close the planet might be to the cusp (e.g. cusp at 29 Aries; planet at 0 Taurus: effect still much reduced). Example: suppose the Ascendant is at 15 Pisces, with Saturn in the 1st at 2 Aries. The presence of this debilitated Saturn (in its fall) is a serious affliction to the good guys. Jupiter is at 17 Pisces, so the presence of this strongly dignified Jupiter is highly beneficial to the good guys. Jupiter being much closer to the Ascendant and, most importantly, being in the same sign as the Ascendant, the benefic influence of Jupiter is much stronger than the malign influence of Saturn. 首先评估宫位自身的状况。宫位内是否有行星？如果有，它是加强了该宫位还是 对其造成损害？记住，行星越靠近宫头，对该宫位的影响越大。如果行星虽然在 该宫内，但与宫头星座不同，其影响力将大大减弱。无论行星多么接近宫头都是 如此（例如，宫头在白羊座 29 度；行星在金牛座 0 度：影响力仍然大幅降低）。 示例：假设上升点在双鱼座 15 度，土星在 1 宫内白羊座 2 度。这颗衰弱的土星 （处于落陷状态）的存在对“好人队”是严重的损害。木星在双鱼座 17 度，因 此这颗拥有强尊贵的木星的存在对“好人队”极为有利。木星更接近上升点，并 且最关键的是与上升点处于同一星座，因此木星的吉性影响力远强于土星的凶性 影响力。

The houses that concern us oppose each other, so ignore planets casting aspects to them. If a planet aspects one house, it will also aspect the house opposite with an aspect of similar quality. 由于我们关注的两个宫位彼此相对，因此可以忽略对它们形成相位的行星。如果 一颗行星与其中一个宫位形成相位，它也必将与对宫形成性质相似的相位。

The Moon’s Nodes can be treated very simply in these charts: North good, South bad. They come as a pair, so if one is in the good guys’ house, the other will be in the bad guys’. This means that we must consider only one of them – it doesn’t matter which. If the North Node is in the 1st, we can judge that house to be strengthened, or we can judge the 7th house to be weakened by the presence of the South Node. Don’t count these as two separate testimonies. In all astrological judgement we must be wary of anything that follows automatically. 在这些星盘中，月交点可以非常简单地处理：北交点吉，南交点凶。它们成对出 现，因此如果一个在“好人队”的宫位，另一个就会在“坏人队”的宫位。这意 味着我们只需考虑其中之一——哪一个都可以。如果北交点在 1 宫，我们可以判 断该宫位被加强，或者可以判断 7 宫因南交点的存在而被削弱。不要将其算作两 个独立的征象。在所有占星判断中，我们必须警惕任何自动随之出现的事物。

Now consider Lords 1 and 7. Which is the stronger? The major accidental dignities are much more important than essential dignity in these questions. Essential dignity might tell us who deserves to win; accidental dignity will tell us who does win. But if

all other testimonies are more or less equal, a strong discrepancy in essential dignity can be crucial. The exception to this general downplaying of essential dignity is the exaltation. The team whose significator is in its own exaltation will take the field believing it is a team of gods playing mere mortals. Such an attitude makes it more likely to win. In contest horaries, exaltation is stronger than sign rulership. 现在考虑 1 宫主和 7 宫主。谁更强？在这些问题中，主要的偶然尊贵远比先天尊 贵更重要。先天尊贵可能告诉我们谁配赢；偶然尊贵则会告诉我们谁会赢。但如 果所有其他征象大致相当，先天尊贵的巨大差异可能至关重要。这种普遍弱化先 天尊重要性的情况有一个例外，那就是旺势。征象星处于自身旺势的球队将带着 “我们是众神对战凡夫”的信念上场。这种态度使其更可能获胜。在竞赛卜卦盘 中，旺势强于入庙。

Receptions between Lords 1 and 7 are important. Not, of course, for showing who likes whom, but for showing who is in whose power. Again, exaltation is stronger than sign-rulership: if Lord 1 is ruled by Lord 7 and Lord 7 is in the exaltation of Lord 1, it is Lord 1 who benefits. The enemy is overawed by our team. Mutual reception with other planets is not strengthening. Mutual reception is like friendship. No matter what good friends the querent or his team might have, they are not going to run onto the pitch to score the winning goal. 1 宫主和 7 宫主之间的接纳关系很重要。当然，这并非为了显示谁喜欢谁，而是 为了显示谁在谁的掌控之中。同样，旺势强于入庙守护：如果 1 宫主被 7 宫主守 护，而 7 宫主处于 1 宫主的旺势，那么是 1 宫主受益。敌人被我方球队震慑住了。 与其他行星的互溶关系没有加强作用。互溶如同友谊。无论问卜者或其球队有多 么好的朋友，他们不会跑进球场去踢进制胜一球。

House placement and combustion are the most important accidental dignities in these charts. A planet in an angular house has a great advantage over one in a succedent or cadent house. The closer to the cusp, the greater the advantage. A planet in a house but not in the sign of the cusp is strengthened, but much less. A significator in its own house is especially strengthened; a significator in its opponent’s house is usually a conclusive sign of defeat: it is in the hands of the enemy. A significator on the cusp of, rather than inside, the enemy’s house, however, is in an exceptionally powerful position. Planet in a house is controlled by that house; planet on a house controls that house. 在这些星盘中，宫位位置和燃烧是最重要的偶然尊贵。位于角宫的行星比位于续 宫或果宫的行星有巨大优势。越靠近宫头，优势越大。位于某宫但不在该宫头星 座内的行星会被加强，但程度轻得多。位于自己宫位的征象星尤其得到加强；位 于对手宫位的征象星通常是失败的明确标志：它已落入敌人手中。然而，征象星 若在敌人宫位的宫头（而非宫内），则处于异常强大的位置。行星在宫内受该宫 控制；行星在宫头则控制该宫。

Combustion being the most grievous of all afflictions, a significator combust shows that team will lose. It would be a rare combination of horrors that could outweigh that. 燃烧是所有损害中最严重的，征象星燃烧显示该队将输。需要极其罕见的恐怖组

合才能压倒这一征象。

Close aspect with a benefic will help that planet; close aspect with a malefic will harm it, remembering, as always, that any essentially strong planet will be helpful, any essentially debilitated planet malign. Five degrees of separation is the absolute maximum with which we need concern ourselves; the closer the stronger. 与吉星的紧密相位将有助于该行星；与凶星的紧密相位将损害它，请始终牢记， 任何先天强劲的行星都是有益的，任何先天衰弱的行星都是有害的。我们需要关 注的最大容许度是 5 度；越紧密则影响越强。

In a chart cast to find the outcome of a match, disregard sign changes. A significator might be about to enter its own sign, bringing a massive increase in essential strength, but however close to that change it might be, this will not be relevant to the result of a single game. If the question were on a longer-term issue, such as ‘Will my team do better than team X this season?’ such a change would be most relevant: ‘You’ll start off badly, but will soon hit your stride’. 在预测比赛结果的星盘中，忽略换座。一颗征象星可能即将进入其自己守护的星 座，带来先天力量的巨大提升，但无论它多么接近这个变化，这与单场比赛的结 果无关。如果问题是关于更长远的议题，例如“我的球队这个赛季会比 X 队表 现更好吗？”这样的变化就非常相关了：“你们开局会很糟，但很快会找到节奏”。

As the Moon shows the flow of events, its application to one or other of the significators will be a minor testimony in favour of that team. It can swing an even balance, but will not outweigh any strong indications. 由于月亮显示事件的流程，它与任一征象星的入相将是支持该队的一个次要征象。 它可以打破均势，但无法压倒任何强烈的指示。

I have found little use for the Arabian Parts in these charts. Even Fortuna and the Part of Victory disdain to get involved. 我发现在这些星盘中阿拉伯点的用处不大。就连福点和胜利点也不屑于参与其中。

If we want reliable judgements, we must be thorough, but there is no virtue in splitting hairs. In most charts, the balance of power will be clear-cut. If arguments for each team are equally persuasive, we are unlikely to choose the victor by microscopic analysis of testimony. In some sports, this even balance will be a judgement in itself: the match will be drawn. In games that must produce a winner, check that you haven’t missed something – antiscia, for instance. Then follow William Lilly’s advice, ‘When the testimonies of Fortunes and Infortunes are equal, defer judgement, it’s not possible to know which way the balance will turn’.Regard for the limitations of knowledge, whether individual or collective, is no failure. 如果我们想要可靠的判断，就必须全面，但没有必要吹毛求疵。在大多数星盘中， 力量对比会是清晰的。如果双方的论据同样有说服力，我们不太可能通过对征象 的微观分析来选择胜者。在某些体育项目中，这种势均力敌本身就是一个判断： 比赛将打平。在必须产生胜者的比赛中，检查你是否遗漏了什么——例如映点。

然后遵循 William Lilly 的建议：“当吉星与凶星的征象相等时，推迟判断，无法 预知天平将偏向何方”。认识到知识的局限性，无论是个人还是集体的，并非 失败。

42. Lilly, p. 123

### ✸The speed of a significator may or may not be important, depending upon the

sport. Use your common sense. If the question is about the 100 metres, the athlete signified by a planet in station will definitely not win. But in a football match, the team that runs around fast does not necessarily have an advantage: its stationary opponents, who have parked the proverbial bus across their goal, may well come out on top.✷

### ✸征象星的运行速度是否重要取决于体育项目。运用你的常识。如果问题是关

于 100 米赛跑，由一颗停滞行星象征的运动员肯定赢不了。但在足球比赛中，跑 得快的队伍不一定有优势：其静止不动的对手（即俗称在球门前“摆大巴”的球 队）很可能会胜出。✷

The exception to the 1st house versus 7th house rule is in contests where kingship is significant, such as boxing title fights. Here the question is ‘Will the king retain his crown?’ This approach must not be taken in other sports: that team A happened to win the championship last season does not make any difference to today’s match, for at the beginning of each new season all teams begin as equals. In a boxing title fight, the sole reason for the contest is that the challenger has the opportunity to depose the champion. 1 宫对 7 宫规则的一个例外是王权有重要意义的比赛，例如拳王争霸赛。这里的 问题是“国王能保住他的王冠吗？”其他体育项目不得采用此方法：A 队上个赛 季碰巧赢得了冠军，这对今天的比赛没有影响，因为每个新赛季开始时所有队伍 都是平等的。在拳王争霸赛中，比赛的唯一原因是挑战者有机会推翻冠军。

Give the champion the 10th house, the chanllenger the 4th (7th from the 10th). If they do not rule either of these houses, the Sun can also stand for the champion, as natural ruler of kings, and the Moon – natural ruler of the common people – for the challenger. Judgement is much as above, with three variations: 赋予卫冕冠军 10 宫，挑战者 4 宫（10 宫的 7 宫）。如果它们不守护这些宫位中 的任何一个，太阳也可代表冠军（作为王者的自然守护星），月亮——平民的自 然守护星——可代表挑战者。判断方法与上述大致相同，但有三个变化：

* The Arabian Part of Resignation and Dismissal (Saturn + Jupiter - Sun) is worth noting.
* 阿拉伯点中的辞职与解雇点（土星+木星-太阳）值得关注。

* Changes of dignity can show the outcome on their own. If the significator of the

champion is about to enter the sign of its fall, or that of the challenger its exaltation, we have a clear testimony of victory for one or the other.
* 尊贵状态的变化本身就能显示结果。如果冠军的征象星即将进入其弱势或落陷 的星座，或者挑战者的征象星即将进入其旺势的星座，我们就有了支持其中一方 的明确胜利征象。

* A void of course Moon, which can be ignored in most contest charts, because we know that something will happen – there will be a match, which will have some outcome – is a strong testimony that the status quo will be preserved. Nothing will happen, so the champion will retain his crown.
* 月亮空亡在大多数竞赛盘中可以忽略，因为我们知道会有事情发生——会有比 赛，会有结果——但它是一个强有力的征象，表明现状将得以维持。不会有变化 发生，因此冠军将保住他的王冠。

The long-term forecast 长期预测

‘How will my team do this season?’, ‘Will my team win the championship?’, ‘Will it be relegated?’ “我的球队这个赛季会表现如何？”、“我的球队会赢得冠军吗？”、“它会降 级吗？”

In distinction to the one-against-one contest horaries above, this can be asked about a team or individual player to which the querent is indifferent: ‘How will team X do this season?’ ‘Will Venus William win this tournament?’ This is possible because the enquiry concerns only one team, so we do not encounter the problem of deciding which team should be assigned to which house. If the querent is indifferent to it, the team or player named is ‘any old person’ and so is given the 7th. 与前述一对一的对决卜卦不同，这类问题可以针对问卜者漠不关心的某个球队或 个人运动员提问：“X 队这个赛季会怎么样？”“Venus William（维纳斯·威廉 姆斯）会赢得这次锦标赛吗？”这是可能的，因为询问只涉及一支队伍，所以我 们不会遇到决定哪支队伍该分配给哪个宫位的问题。如果问卜者对其漠不关心， 那么提及的球队或运动员就是“任何人”，因此赋予 7 宫。

Judgement is usually simple, as long as we shun the temptation to force the spectacular answer. Ego tells us it is a far better thing to predict the unlikely. It is not: it is a far better thing to predict what will happen. Most of the time, the unlikely does not happen. ‘How will my team do this season?’ – in most cases the answer to this will be ‘Indifferently’. Few teams win things; few are relegated. While ‘Will my team win the championship?’ ‘No’, is not the most satisfying of client/consultant exchanges, if that is what will happen, that is what will happen. 判断通常很简单，只要我们抵制住强行给出惊人答案的诱惑。自我意识告诉我们， 预测出人意料的结果才更显本事。其实不然：预测出即将发生的实际情况才是更

重要的。大多数时候，小概率事件并不会发生。“我的球队这个赛季会表现如何？” ——在大多数情况下，答案是“不怎么样”。很少有球队能赢得什么；也很少有 球队会降级。虽然“我的球队会赢得冠军吗？”“不会”这种客户与咨询师之间 的交流并不令人满意，但如果事实如此，那结果就是如此。

The querent’s team will be signified by the ruler of the 1st. Do not take the Moon as cosignificator. Look for significant changes in essential dignity and connections to appropriate houses. In practice, anything that will merit an answer other than ‘Indifferently’ is usually fairly obvious. A planet entering the sign of its exaltation is. 问卜者的球队将由 1 宫主象征。不要将月亮视为共同征象星。寻找先天尊贵的显 著变化以及与相关宫位的联系。实际上，任何值得给出“不怎么样”以外答案的 情况通常都相当明显。例如，一颗行星进入其旺势的星座。

Examples: ‘How will my team do?’ Significator enters its own sign or exaltation: it will win promotion. Significator enters its fall: it will – literally enough – go down. Significator conjuncts 10th cusp or Lord 10: it will win the championship. It enters the 12th or 8th house, or conjuncts one of their rulers: the team will be relegated. ‘Will we win the championship?’ with querent’s planet applying to conjunct Lord 10: Yes. If this conjunction happens in the next sign: ‘Not this season, but you will next’. 示例：“我的球队会表现如何？”征象星进入其自己守护的星座或旺势星座：它 将赢得升级。征象星进入其落陷星座：它将——字面意思足够明确——降级。征 象星与 10 宫头或 10 宫主形成合相：它将赢得冠军。它进入 12 宫或 8 宫，或与 这些宫的宫主星之一形成合相：球队将降级。“我们会赢得冠军吗？”如果问卜 者的行星正入相合 10 宫主：会。如果这个合相发生在下一个星座：“不是这个 赛季，但下个赛季你们会”。

A querent asked if her team would win anything that season; the chart showed a conjunction with Lord 10, but not until the next sign. That conjunction was in a double-bodied sign: her team won both major competitions the next season. 一位问卜者问她的球队那个赛季是否会赢得任何奖项；星盘显示将有一个与 10 宫主的合相，但要到下一个星座才会发生。那个合相发生在一个双体星座：她的 球队在下个赛季赢得了两项主要赛事的冠军。

The 8th, the house of death, can show the extinction of the club; but we must be cautious. It is more likely that its meaning will be found within the assumptions of the question, which will usually relate only to on-field matters. Even in a context where the club’s survival could not be taken for granted, there would need to be serious 2nd-house (financial) problems apparent in the chart before we predicted so dire a fate. 8 宫，死亡之宫，可以显示俱乐部的消亡；但我们必须谨慎。其含义更可能是在 问题本身的假设范围内找到，而这些问题通常只与场上事务相关。即使在俱乐部 生存不能被视为理所当然的背景下，星盘中也需要有明显的 2 宫（财务）问题， 我们才会预测如此可怕的命运。

Combustion and cazimi are important. ‘Will Venus William win Wimbledon?’ Her planet combust: no chance. Her planet cazimi: no one else has a chance. Contacts with planets other than the Sun or the rulers of the relevant houses are usually insignificant. No matter how fortunate that trine from a benefic might be, it will not bring the championship; no matter how hard that Saturn opposition, it will not bring relegation. Such testimonies can add precision to a judgement. Suppose the significator is very weak, but favoured by a trine from strong Jupiter: ‘Your team will struggle all season, but will not go down’. But this is just decoration. 燃烧和日核很重要。“Venus William 会赢得温网吗？”她的行星燃烧：没机会。 她的行星处于日核状态：其他人没机会。与太阳或相关宫主星以外的行星的接触 通常不重要。无论来自吉星的拱相位多么幸运，它不会带来冠军；无论土星的对 冲相位多么困难，它不会带来降级。这类征象可以为判断增添精确性。假设征象 星非常虚弱，但得到一颗强劲木星拱相位的支持：“你的球队整个赛季都会很挣 扎，但不会降级。”但这只是点缀。

Answering the general enquiry, ‘Who will win the league?’ would be easy – if the team in that league were called Jupiter, Mars and Venus. I have not found any method of linking planets to a full field of teams. At least, no method that works. But if the chart shows a void of course Moon, this question can still be answered. Void of course Moon: nothing changes. The team that won last year will win again. 回答“谁将赢得联赛？”这个普遍询问会很容易——如果该联赛中的球队名叫木 星、火星和金星的话。我还没有找到任何将行星与一整组球队联系起来的方法。 至少，没有有效的方法。但如果星盘显示月亮空亡，这个问题仍然可以回答。月 亮空亡：没有变化。去年获胜的球队将再次获胜。

### ✸When there is one person or team against the field, there is usually a prize at stake.

The significator of whomever the querent is asking about will be chosen as usual; Lord 10 will show victory; any planet other than these will show a member of the field. For instance, ‘Will my daughter’s team win the school tournament?’ Lord 5 showed the daughter’s team. Lord 10 was separating from aspect to Lord 5. They hadn’t won already, so this separation was in itself a chear No. This was confirmed by Lord 10 applying to another planet: someone else will win. There is no need to try to identify who that someone else might be.

### ✸当有一个个人或团队对阵整个赛场时，通常会有悬而未决的奖品。问卜者所

询问对象的征象星将按常规选择；10 宫主将显示胜利；除这些以外的任何行星 将显示赛场中的一员。例如，“我女儿的球队会赢得学校锦标赛吗？”5 宫主显 示女儿的球队。10 宫主正结束与 5 宫主的相位。他们还没有赢过，所以这个出 相本身就是一个清晰的“否”。这一点被 10 宫主正入相另一颗行星所证实：别 人会赢。不需要试图确定那个“别人”可能是谁。

Victory will be shown by the Lord of the radical 10th, not the turned 10th: if victory already belonged to the person asked about the question would not need to be asked.

The exception is if I am asking ‘Will Mum win?’ Radical Lord 10 is already busy, signifying my mother, so we would have to turn the chart to find a significator for victory. ✷ 胜利将由基准盘 10 宫主显示，而非转宫 10 宫主：如果胜利已经属于被询问的对 象，那就不需要问这个问题了。例外情况是，如果我问“妈妈会赢吗？”基准盘 10 宫主已经有任务了，象征着我的母亲，所以我们将不得不转宫以找到胜利的 征象星。✷

### ✸Questions about events such as ice-dancing or talent-shows, decided on a vote, not

by achievement of some objective criterion, should be treated as elections, not contests. See pages 251-253, below.✷ 关于通过投票而非达成某种客观标准来决定结果的事件（如冰舞或选秀节目）的 问题，应视为选举而非竞赛。见下文第 401 - 404 页。✷

【Cazimi in competitions - Posted on July 14th, 2014 【竞赛中的日核 - 发布于 2014 年 7 月 14 日

A student asked the horary ‘Will Argentina win the World Cup?’ He did not identify with Argentina - the question was not ‘Will we win?’ - so they are shown by Lord 7: any old person. Lord 7 was cazimi. 一位学生问了卜卦问题“阿根廷会赢得世界杯吗？”他本人并不代表阿根廷—— 问题不是“我们会赢吗？”——因此阿根廷由 7 宫主代表：任何第三方。7 宫主 正处于日核。

In most questions on competition, such as ‘Will A beat B?’, a significator cazimi would be a clear ‘Yes’ for that player or team. It would take a remarkable accumulation of contrary testimonies to out-gun that. 在大多数竞争性问题中，例如“A 会打败 B 吗？”，如果某一方或其征象星处 于日核，对该选手或球队而言就是一个明确的“是”。需要极其大量的反面征象 积累才能压倒这一优势。

But in a question about open competition, one team against everybody else, this is not so. A planet cazimi is likened to a man raised up to sit beside the king. But if this is so, that man is by definition not the king. So in this case what the cazimi gives us is a clear astrological picture of ‘close but no cigar’.】 但在一个关于开放式竞争（一队对抗所有其他队）的问题中，情况则不同。处于 日核的行星，被比作一个被提升到与君王同坐的人。但若如此，按定义此人就不 是君王本身。所以在这种情况下，日核给我们的清晰占星学图景是“接近胜利， 但终未如愿”。】

TRIALS 审判

I deal here with civil trials, which are the subject of questions more often than criminal cases. Criminal trials are discussed in chapter 25. 我在此讨论民事诉讼，这是比刑事案件更常成为问卜主题的领域。刑事审判在第 25 章讨论。

The difference between a trial and a contest is that the outcome of a contest is decided by clear external criteria: you score more points, you get me in checkmate, you force my arm down onto the table. In a trial the decision is given by a judge, based on what he thinks best. Yes, in our society the decision is usually made by a jury, but I find it simpler to follow Lilly in referring to the decisionmaker as ‘the judge’. This clarifies the thought process when we approach the chart: ‘Good judge? Bad judge?’ Keep it simple! But remember that when we refer to ‘the judge’ we mean ‘the legal process’. It is not necessary to distinguish between judge and jury: we are concerned with the outcome, not with giving a running commentary on the events of the trial. 审判与竞赛的区别在于，竞赛结果由明确的外部标准决定：你得分更高，你将我 军，你把我的手臂压到桌面上。而在审判中，判决由法官根据他认为的最佳判断 作出。是的，在我们的社会中，判决通常由陪审团作出，但我发现遵循 Lilly 的 做法，将决策者称为“法官”更为简便。这在我们解读星盘时能澄清思路过程： “好法官？坏法官？”保持简单！但请记住，当我们提到“法官”时，我们指的 是“法律程序”。没有必要区分法官和陪审团：我们关心的是结果，而不是对审 判过程进行实时评论。

There are four key players in a trial chart: the querent (Lord 1); the enemy (Lord 7); the judge, or the ‘the legal process’ if you wish to be long-winded (Lord 10); the verdict, which, as ‘the end of the matter’, is Lord 4. The Moon is, as usual, cosignificator of the querent, although with three other houses in play she will often be the ruler of one of those instead. 在审判星盘中有四个关键角色：问卜者（1 宫主）；敌人（7 宫主）；法官，或 者如果你想啰嗦点，可称为“法律程序”（10 宫主）；判决，作为“事件的终 结”，是 4 宫主。月亮照例是问卜者的共同征象星，不过由于有其他三个宫位参 与其中，月亮常常是其中某一宫的守护星。

### ✸ No, don’t use the Moon as cosignificator of the querent in trial questions.

Consider: the main testimony of victory is an aspect between one or other party and Lord 4. Giving the querent two planets and the enemy only one gives the querent twice as much chance of winning. This might be pleasing but is unlikely to reflect reality.✷

### ✸不，在审判问题中不要将月亮用作问卜者的共同征象星。考虑一下：胜利的

主要征象是一方或另一方与 4 宫主之间的相位。给问卜者两颗行星而敌人只有一 颗，这给了问卜者双倍的获胜机会。这可能令人愉快，但不太可能反映现实。✷

The 2nd house of the querent and that of the enemy show their money and/or their lawyer and witnesses. If the lawyer is asking the question, treat it as Us against Them, giving the 1st house to both the lawyer and the lawyer’s client, and the 7th to both the enemy and the enemy’s lawyer. Even if the lawyer is the querent, priority will always be with the person directly involved in the action: it is as if the lawyer were asking as that person’s mouthpiece. 问卜者和敌人的 2 宫显示他们的金钱和/或他们的律师与证人。如果是律师提问， 应将其视为“我方对阵敌方”，将 1 宫赋予律师及其当事人双方，将 7 宫赋予敌 人及其律师双方。即使律师是问卜者，优先级始终在直接参与诉讼的人身上：就 好像律师是作为那个人的代言人提问一样。

First consider the condition of Lords 1 and 7. Essential dignity tends to show the justice of the case, and has lamentably little to do with the matter of who wins. Reception can be important, though, especially if aspects show the possibility of settling out of court. Suppose Lord 7 is in the exaltation of Lord 1: great new! Our querent is in a fine position to push for a settlement.
