Suppose Lord 1 exalts Lord 7, but further examination shows that our querent will win in court: we must caution him to resist his feelings that he cannot win, refuse any proffered settlement and let justice take its course. 首先考虑 1 宫主和 7 宫主的状况。先天尊贵往往显示案件的正义性，但与谁赢关 系不大，这很可悲。然而，接纳关系可能很重要，特别是如果相位显示庭外和解 的可能性。假设 7 宫主在 1 宫主旺势的位置：好消息！我们的问卜者处于有利地 位，可以推动和解。假设 1 宫主位于 7 宫主旺势的位置，但进一步检查显示我们 的问卜者将在法庭上获胜：我们必须告诫他，要抵制认为自己赢不了的情绪，拒 绝任何提出的和解，让正义自行其道。

Accidental dignity says more about who will win or loss than essential dignity. The accidentally stronger protagonist will win – if contact with the judge or the verdict does not determine otherwise. Contacts with the judge or verdict usually do determine otherwise. 在显示谁输谁赢方面，偶然尊贵比先天尊贵更能说明问题。偶然尊贵更强的一方 将获胜——除非与法官或判决的联系另有决定。而与法官或判决的联系通常确实 会改变结果。

Consider the condition of Lord 10. Lots of essential dignity: good judge. In detriment or fall: bad judge. But remember that the judge could sleep through the whole trial and decide the verdict by tossing a coin, yet still arrive at a just outcome. PLEASE do not say ‘Lord 10 is accidentally strong, so the judge has a major say in the outcome’. Of course he does: he’s the judge. 考虑 10 宫主的状况。先天尊贵多：好法官。弱势或落陷：坏法官。但要记住， 法官可能在整个审判过程中都在睡觉，通过抛硬币来决定判决，但仍可能得出公 正的结果。请注意不要说“10 宫主偶然尊贵强，所以法官对结果有重大发言权”。 他当然有：他是法官。

Consider the receptions between the judge and Lords 1 and 7. Does the judge like one party and dislike the other? This can be crucial, especially with an applying aspect between the judge and either the liked or the disliked party. Such a contact will override any balance of strength between Lords 1 and 7, giving the verdict to whichever the judge prefers. Again, do not say ‘Lord 7 is ruled by Lord 10: the judge has power over him’. Of course the judge has power over him: he is in court. 考虑法官与 1 宫主和 7 宫主之间的接纳关系。法官喜欢一方而不喜欢另一方吗？ 这可能至关重要，特别是当法官与被喜欢或被不喜欢的一方有入相时。这样的联 系将压倒 1 宫主和 7 宫主之间的任何力量平衡，将判决给予法官偏好的那一方。 再次强调，不要说“7 宫主被 10 宫主守护：法官对他有控制权”。法官当然对 他有控制权：他正在法庭上。

Lord 10, then, is of great importance. But even more important than Lord 10 is Lord 4: the verdict. In life both parties get the verdict: one likes it; one doesn’t. In the horary chart Lord 4 is like a prize: who gets there first wins. So look for an applying aspect between Lord 1 or Lord 7 and Lord 4. 因此，10 宫主极为重要。但比 10 宫主更重要的是 4 宫主：判决。在现实中，双 方都会得到判决：一方喜欢；一方不喜欢。在卜卦星盘中，4 宫主就像一个奖品： 谁先得到它谁就赢。所以要寻找 1 宫主或 7 宫主与 4 宫主之间的入相。

### ✸To clarify: an aspect with Lord 10 can show victory or defeat, depending upon

Lord 10’s receptions. If Lord 10 likes me and aspects me, I win; if it dislikes me and aspects me, I lose. An aspect with Lord 4 shows victory, regardless of Lord 4’s receptions. This is because of the reality of the situation: the verdict is not an autonomous thing. It cannot make up its own mind: it does what it is told. So an aspect with Lord 4, which is in my detriment, does not mean ‘The verdict doesn’t like me, so I’ll lose’, but ‘I’ll win, but the verdict won’t favour me much’. See the example chart below.✷

### ✸需要澄清的是：与 10 宫主的相位可能显示胜利或失败，这取决于 10 宫主的

接纳关系。如果 10 宫主喜欢我并与我成相，我赢；如果它不喜欢我并与我成相， 我输。而与 4 宫主的相位则显示胜利，无论 4 宫主的接纳关系如何。这是因为实 际情况：判决并非自主之物。它不能自己做决定：它按指令行事。所以，与处于 我弱势位置的 4 宫主成相，并不意味着“判决不喜欢我，所以我会输”，而是“我 会赢，但判决不会对我很有利”。参见下面的示例星盘。✷

Are Lords 1 and 7 themselves applying to aspect? If to conjunction, the parties will reach an agreement before the case comes to court. To any other aspect, they will agree after the case opens, but before the verdict is handed down. This is an occasion for the astrologer to offer useful advice: should the querent accept a settlement, or is he better to fight it out? Should he take a paltry settlement, because if he doesn’t he will lose everything? Remember the qualities of the signs: if the enemy is in a fixed sign, he will not budge; if cardinal, he will soon give up; if mutable, he will be

flexible. 1 宫主与 7 宫主自身是否正在形成入相位？如果是合相，双方将在案件开庭前达 成协议。若是其他任何相位，他们将在案件审理开始后、但在判决下达前达成一 致。这是占星师提供有用建议的时机：问卜者应该接受和解，还是最好抗争到底？ 他是否应该接受微不足道的和解，因为如果不这样做，他将失去一切？请记住星 座的属性：如果敌人处于固定星座，他将寸步不让；如果是基本星座，他将很快 放弃；如果是变动星座，他将灵活变通。

### ✸A cardinal sign shows that the enemy doesn’t want a long fight, but this doesn’t

necessarily mean they will surrender. I may not want to run a marathon, but this doesn’t mean I won’t strive my utmost to win the 100 metres. All things being equal, though, this distaste for a long fight will make the possibility of a settlement more likely.

### ✸基本星座显示敌人不想进行持久战，但这并不一定意味着他们会投降。我可

能不想跑马拉松，但这并不意味着我不会竭尽全力去赢 100 米短跑。然而，在条 件相同的情况下，这种对持久战的厌恶将使和解的可能性更大。

A settlement may involve an apology or admission of fault. The common error is to think such an admission will be made from an upsurge of tender conscience, and so to look for testimony showing such. It is a court of law, not a confessional: any such admission will be made because it is seen as the least bad option. 和解可能涉及道歉或承认过错。常见的错误是认为这种承认会出于良心上的突然 不安，从而寻找显示此类情况的征象。但这是法庭，不是忏悔室：任何此类承认 都将是因为它被视为最不坏的选择而作出的。

Once again, the reality of the matter: we do not need to see an aspect between the victor and the other party’s money. We don’t need to demonstrate that the victor gets some money, because this is what happens in court, even if only the contemptuous 1 penny damages. Though if there is such an aspect, its nature can be informative. I once accompanied a friend to court. In a settlement, she was awarded ￡ 35,000 in damages. On which her lawyers presented her with a bill for ￡ 36,000. Had there been a horary on the matter, this outcome could well have been shown by an opposition between querent and Lord 8: the outcome was not worth it. 再次强调，实际情况是：我们不需要看到胜利者与对方金钱（8 宫）之间的相位。 我们不需要证明胜利者能得到一些钱，因为这在法庭上是会发生的事情，即使只 是象征性的 1 便士赔偿金。不过，如果存在这样的相位，其性质可以提供信息。 我曾陪一位朋友上法庭。在和解中，她被判获得 35，000 英镑的损害赔偿金。随 后她的律师向她提交了一张 36,000 英镑的账单。如果当时对此事有一张卜卦盘， 这个结果很可能通过问卜者与 8 宫主之间的对冲相位显示出来：得不偿失。

If the chart shows that I will win, Lord 8 does not show how much money my enemy has, but how much of it I will get. This because the question is about the outcome of a

court-case, not about my enemy’s financial viability. If I am suing MegaCorp, Lord 8 in detriment doesn’t show they have no money, but that very little of it will be coming to me.✷ 如果星盘显示我会赢，那么 8 宫主显示的并非我的敌人有多少钱，而是我能得到 其中的多少。这是因为问题关乎法庭案件的结果，而非我敌人的财务偿付能力。 如果我正在起诉巨无霸公司，8 宫主处于弱势并不显示他们没有钱，而是表明我 能得到的钱非常少。✷

Will we win? （See chart on next page) 我们会赢吗？

This question was asked by the lawyer, so Lord 1 shows Us and Lord 7 Them. 此问题由律师提出，因此 1 宫主代表我方，7 宫主代表敌方。

How are the good guys? Lord 1 is in its own term, suggesting that she has a certain amount of right on her side; but is in the 9th, so not so strong. “But the 9th is the house of law.” No: the 9th house covers law only as an abstract subject – higher learning. It has nothing whatever to do with law in action, as in a court case. 好人方情况如何？1 宫主处于其得界，表明她某种程度上站在道理一边；但位于 9 宫，所以并不强势。“但 9 宫不是法律之宫吗？”不：9 宫仅涵盖作为抽象学 科的法律——即高等学问。它与实际法律行动（如法庭案件）毫无关系。

How are the bad guys? Lord 7 is in its fall: boo!! I find it helpful to think in such pantomime terms, as it keeps the main lines of the argument so clear. He’s in his fall: yes, he really is a baddie. But he is also in his triplicity and term. And he is powerfully placed on the MC. This accords with what the querent said about him: that he was a well known villain who was adept at twisting the law in his favour. If there were no other significant testimony, this placement would be enough to give him the victory. 坏人方情况如何？7 宫主处于其落陷：太棒了！！我发现用这种戏剧化表达来思 考很有帮助，因为它能保持论证主线如此清晰。他处于落陷：是的，他确实是个 坏家伙。但他同时也处于其三分和得界。而且他强有力地定位在中天。这与问卜 者对他的描述相符：他是一个知名的恶棍，擅长曲解法律使之对自己有利。如果 没有其他重要征象，仅此定位就足以让他获胜。

How is the judge? Lord 10 is in its detriment: bad judge. There is a powerful mutual reception between Lords 7 and 10. Lord 7 is ruled by the Moon, the judge. Big deal: we know that, as he is in court. But the judge exalts him: this is not good. 法官情况如何？10 宫主处于其弱势：坏法官。7 宫主与 10 宫主之间存在强力的 互溶关系。7 宫主被月亮（法官）守护。这有什么了不起的：我们知道，因为他 正在法庭上。但法官对其呈旺势：这可不是好事。

Lord 10 separates from its aspect to Lord 7. This is a puzzle. What are we to make of this? Yes, it could show past contact between baddie and judge. Lilly gives a long list of testimonies that show the judge has been bribed:follow this list and you will find it so comprehensive that you will never see a legitimate court case. I strongly suggest that you disregard such possibilities unless the querent raises them in the question, in which case such past contact, especially with so heavy a mutual reception and Lord 10 so debilitated, would be evidence. 10 宫主正结束与 7 宫主的相位。这令人困惑。我们该如何理解这一点？是的， 这可能显示坏家伙与法官过去有过接触。Lilly 列出了一长串显示法官被贿赂的 征象列表：遵循这个列表，你会发现它如此全面，以至于你永远不会看到一个 合法的法庭案件。我强烈建议你忽略这种可能性，除非问卜者在问题中提出，如 果是这样的话，这种过去的接触，尤其是对于如此重要的互溶，并且 10 宫主如 此的虚弱，将成为证据。

43. Lilly, pp. 374-5

This separating contact with such mutual reception could show that the judge’s mind is already made up. Perhaps the case has already opened, the verdict has been decided and all that awaits now is an announcement of the decision. But that was not the situation here: the trial had not yet started. So what does this separating aspect mean?

这种带有如此互溶关系的分离接触可能表明法官心意已决。也许案件已经开庭， 判决已经决定，现在等待的只是宣布决定。但这里的情况并非如此：审判尚未开 始。那么这个出相意味着什么？

Look at what Lord 10 is doing. 看看 10 宫主正在做什么。

It separates from aspect to Lord 7 and applies to aspect with Saturn. What is Saturn? Lord 4: the verdict. 它正结束与 7 宫主的相位，并正入相与土星形成相位。土星是什么？是 4 宫主： 判决。

This is a translation of light. The Moon picks up Lord 7 and carries its light to Lord 4, effectively connecting Lord 7 with Lord 4, so taking the bad guy to the verdict. Because the verdict is seen as a prize, the first one there gets it: this means that the bad guy wins. The translation shows this perfectly: the (bad) judge carries the (evil) enemy to the verdict. 这是一种光线传递。月亮“拾起”7 宫主，并将其光线“携带”给 4 宫主，有效 地将 7 宫主与 4 宫主连接起来，从而将坏家伙带向判决。因为判决被视为一个奖 品，先到者先得：这意味着坏家伙赢了。光线传递完美地显示了这一点：（坏的） 法官将（邪恶的）敌人带向了判决。

He wins. But let’s look further. There is a weak malefic afflicting the 8th house (enemy’s money) by its presence. What is this weak malefic? It is Lord 4: the verdict. Even though he wins, the verdict harms his pocket. Look at the reception between verdict and baddie. Mars is in the detriment of Saturn: the baddie hates the verdict. Saturn is in the detriment of Mars: the verdict hates or harms the baddie. 他赢了。但让我们进一步看看。有一颗虚弱的凶星因其存在而损害了 8 宫（敌人 的金钱）。这颗虚弱的凶星是什么？是 4 宫主：判决。即使他赢了，判决也会损 害他的钱袋。看看判决与坏家伙之间的接纳关系。火星在土星的弱势位置：坏家 伙憎恨判决。土星在火星的弱势位置：判决憎恨或损害坏家伙。

How come? Look at Lord 10. The judge exalts the bad guy. But, in this case, he can do that only by being in his detriment (Moon, which is Lord 10, can exalt Mars, which is Lord 7, only by being in Capricorn, which is its detriment). The judge can exalt this bad guy only by being a bad judge. Lord 10 is also in the triplicity and term of Venus, Lord 1. The judge likes our querent; but this liking is weaker than the exaggerated infatuation that is exaltation. We have seen that the enemy really is a baddie, but has points of law on his side. 怎么会这样？看看 10 宫主。法官位于坏家伙旺势的位置。但是，在这种情况下， 法官只能通过处于自身的弱势来做到这一点（月亮，即 10 宫主，位于火星，即 7 宫主，的旺势位置，即擢升火星，只能通过在摩羯座，而摩羯座是月亮的弱势）。 法官只有通过成为一个坏法官才能位于这个坏家伙旺势的位置。10 宫主也处于 1 宫主（金星）的三分和得界。法官喜欢我们的问卜者；但这种喜欢弱于旺势所代

表的夸张迷恋。我们已经看到敌人确实是个坏家伙，但法律条款对其有利。

So what do we have? The judge (= the court system) has to rule in favour of the enemy on point of law. But (Lord 10 in significant dignities of Lord 1) he can still see the virtues of our querent’s case. So although the law demands that judgement is given in favour of the baddie, the verdict (Lord 4 afflicts baddie’s 2nd) is framed in such a way that it still harms his pocket. 那么我们得到了什么？法官（= 法庭系统）必须在法律论点上做出对敌人有利的 裁决。但是（10 宫主在 1 宫主的重要尊贵状态中）他仍然能看到我们问卜者案 件的优点。因此，尽管法律要求判决对坏家伙有利，但判决（4 宫主损害了坏家 伙的 2 宫）的措辞方式仍将损害他的钱袋。

### ✸Regarding my comments on the ‘weak malefic’: see the added note on page 52.

The verdict is not any the nastier because it is Saturn. Saturn is the actor, not the role. There is a peregrine planet afflicting the 8th house. This planet signifies the verdict. There is mutual reception by detriment between verdict and the baddie. It is this that shows that the baddie will not be happy with the verdict.✷

### ✸关于我对“虚弱的凶星”的评论：参见第 99 页的附加说明。判决并不因为它

是土星而更恶劣。土星是扮演者，不是角色。有一颗游离行星损害了 8 宫。这颗 行星象征判决。判决与坏家伙之间存在基于弱势的互溶关系。正是这点表明恶徒 不会对判决结果感到满意。✷

POLITICS 政治

I deal here with elections, but these principles will enable you to judge any other common political question. 我在此讨论选举，但这些原则将使你能够判断任何其他常见的政治问题。

In a horary about an election, which candidate is given which house depend on who is asking the question. As I write this, George Bush has recently been re-elected, defeating John Kerry. Consider the various questions that might have been asked before the election: 在关于选举的卜卦盘中，哪位候选人被赋予哪个宫位，取决于谁在提问。在我写 下此文时，George Bush（乔治·布什）刚刚击败（约翰·克里）获得连任。考 虑一下在选举前可能提出的各种问题：

* Bush asks ‘Will I win?’ He is 1st; his opponent 7th.
* Bush 问：“我会赢吗？”他是 1 宫；他的对手是 7 宫。

* Mrs Bush asks ‘Will George win?’ Technically, this should give George the 7th house, because she is asking about her husband. The question could probably be read as ‘Will we win?’ however, giving Bush the 1st, his opponent the 7th.
* Bush 夫人问：“George 会赢吗？”严格来说，这应该给 George7 宫，因为她 是在询问她的丈夫。但这个问题或许可以理解为“我们会赢吗？”，从而赋予 Bush1 宫，其对手 7 宫。

* A Republican asks, ‘Will we win?’ Us against Them: 1st versus 7th.
* 一名共和党人问：“我们会赢吗？”我方对阵敌方：1 宫对 7 宫。

* John Kerry asks ‘Will I win?’ Read this as ‘Can I beat the king?’ giving Kerry the 1st and Bush the 10th. Similarly if a Democrat asks, ‘Will we win?’
* John Kerry（约翰·克里）问：“我会赢吗？”这可解读为“我能击败国王吗？”， 赋予 Kerry1 宫，Bush10 宫。同理，如果一名民主党人问：“我们会赢吗？”也 如此处理。

* If Bush were not already in power and Kerry asked ‘Will I win?’ there would be no king involved. Kerry would be 1st; Bush 7th.
* 如果 Bush 当时尚未执政，而 Kerry 问“我会赢吗？”，则不涉及国王。Kerry 将是 1 宫；Bush 是 7 宫。

* A impartial American asks, ‘Who will win?’ Give Bush the 10th, because he is king, Kerry the 4th, because he is the king’s enemy.
* 一位持中立立场的美国人问：“谁会赢？”赋予 Bush10 宫（因为他是国王）， Kerry4 宫（因为他是国王的敌人）。

* I ask, ‘Who will win?’ Bush is the king of a foreign country: 10th from the 9th = 6th. His enemy is the 7th from the 6th = 12th.
* 我问：“谁会赢？”Bush 是一个外国的国王：9 宫的 10 宫 = 6 宫。他的敌人 是 6 宫的 7 宫 = 12 宫。

The exact situation will vary depending on the constitution of the country, but following the basic rules of house meaning will enable you to select the correct houses. Ignore the fact that in most countries the theory is that no one is in power when the election is held: most elections can be seen as the king against someone, whether the ‘king’ is an individual or a party. In an open election, with various candidates running for a vacant office, ‘Will Cedric win?’ will give Cedric the 1st house (I think he’s wonderful), the 7th house (either I think he’s dreadful or I couldn’t care less) or the 3rd house (he’s my brother). 具体情境会因国家政体而异，但遵循宫位含义的基本规则将使你能够选择正确的 宫位。忽略大多数国家在选举时理论上是“无人执政”这一事实：大多数选举都 可以被看作是国王与某人的对决，无论这个“国王”是个人还是一个政党。在一 个开放选举中，多位候选人竞选一个空缺职位，“Cedric（塞德里克）会赢吗？” 这个问题，可能将 Cedric 赋予 1 宫（我认为他很棒）、7 宫（要么我认为他很糟

糕，要么我根本不在乎）或 3 宫（他是我兄弟）。

The Moon is of extreme importance in horaries about elections. It is natural ruler of the people, and so signifies the electorate. If the Moon goes to aspect the significator of one of the candidates, that candidate will win. This is so despite its receptions. Even if the Moon is in the fall of Cedric’s significator, if it applies to aspect that significator Cedric will win. The Moon’s receptions become important if it makes no aspect to either significator: look to see which candidate the Moon favours. The receptions, however, may not be decisive. A void of course Moon is testimony of the status quo being preserved. 在关于选举的卜卦盘中，月亮极为重要。它是人民的自然守护星，因此象征选民。 如果月亮去形成与某位候选人征象星的相位，那位候选人将获胜。即使存在负面 的接纳关系也是如此。即使月亮处于 Cedric 征象星的落陷位置，如果它正入相 该征象星，Cedric 也会赢。如果月亮与任何一方的征象星都未形成相位，那么月 亮的接纳关系就变得重要了：观察月亮青睐哪一位候选人。然而，接纳关系可能 并非决定性的。月亮空亡是维持现状的征象。

If the Moon is not making the electorate’s feelings clear, consider the condition of the main significators. Essential dignity is not so important: being a bad guy will not stop a candidate being elected. Imminent changes of dignity, however, for better or for worse, can be crucial. Look especially at house placement (significator entering the 10th is positive; significator in the opponent’s house is strongly negative), sign placement (the king in the middle of a fixed sign is likely to stay in power; leaving a fixed sign, his reign may be over) and the major accidental qualities, especially combustion. Be more cautious than usual with cazimi: the candidate wants to be the king, so being ‘in the bosom of the king’ will not be enough; but if other testimonies are lacking cazimi can still prevail. 如果月亮未能清晰显示选民的情绪，则需考虑主要征象星的状况。先天尊贵不那 么重要：作为坏蛋并不会阻止候选人当选。然而，即将发生的尊贵状态变化（无 论是变好还是变坏）可能至关重要。要特别注意宫位位置（征象星进入 10 宫是 积极的；征象星在对手的宫位是非常消极的）、星座位置（国王处于固定星座的 中间，则很可能继续掌权；若离开固定星座，他的统治可能结束）以及主要的偶 然属性，尤其是燃烧。对于日核要比通常更加谨慎：候选人想要成为国王，所以 仅仅“处于国王的怀抱”是不够的；但如果缺少其他征象，日核仍然可以胜出。

Be cautious too when a significator is entering its own house, whether this is its mundane house (= house) or its celestial house (= the sign that it rules). While this makes the planet stronger, it can often be taken literally, showing the candidate going home. In many situations this will be testimony of defeat. 当一颗征象星即将进入其“自己的宫位”时（无论是其世俗宫位=宫位，还是其 天宫宫位=其守护的星座），也要谨慎。虽然这会使行星变得更强，但通常可以 按其字面意思理解，显示候选人“回家”。在许多情况下，这是失败的征象。

If neither candidate is king, leaving the 10th house unengaged, a significator applying

to aspect Lord 10 will be strong testimony that that candidate will become king. 如果双方候选人都不是现任国王，使得 10 宫未被占用，那么一颗征象星正入相 10 宫主将是该候选人将成为国王的有力征象。

If one candidate is king, it is worth casting the Part of Resignation & Dismissal. Contact (mainly conjunction or opposition; other aspect only as minor testimony) with that or its dispositor will help unseat him. 如果其中一位候选人是国王，则值得绘制辞职与解雇点。与该点或其定位星形成 相位（主要是合相或对冲；其他相位仅作为次要征象）将有助于罢黜他。

### ✸ Questions on non-political matters decided by voting, such as ice-dancing and

television talent-shows, should be judged by the Moon, as above. The Moon’s first aspect shows victory, either to the person asked about or to some other person. This will answer most questions. If the Moon makes no aspect, judge by its receptions, showing the voters’ preferences.✷

### ✸关于通过投票决定的非政治事务的问题（例如冰舞和电视选秀节目），应如

上所述，通过月亮来判断。月亮的第一个相位显示胜利，要么属于被询问的人， 要么属于其他人。这将回答大多数问题。如果月亮未形成任何相位，则根据其接 纳关系来判断，这显示了投票者的偏好。✷

When will she fall? 她什么时候会失势？ The querent, who was well placed to know, expected Benazir Bhutto to lose power at any moment. He asked, ‘When will she fall?’ 问卜者身处能获悉内情的位置，预期 Benazir Bhutto（贝娜齐尔·布托）随时可 能失势。他问道：“她何时会倒台？”

The querent is Pakistani, so she is his ‘king’: 10th house. Lord 10, Venus, is sitting most comfortably in the middle of its own, fixed sign, just inside the 10th house. Whatever expectations the querent might have, Mrs Bhutto’s position is secure. 问卜者是巴基斯坦人，因此她是他的“国王”：10 宫。10 宫主金星正安然位于 其自己守护的固定星座的中心，且刚好在 10 宫之内。无论问卜者有何种预期， Bhutto 夫人的地位是稳固的。

The Moon losing what little light it has, however, is indication that the situation is coming to an end. Venus must travel 17 degrees to leave its sign. It is fixed and angular, giving long + long for the timing. With the event anticipated within days and the Moon so late in its cycle, confirming that the event would happen, months seemed to be the longest reasonable time-unit. Allowing a few days grace for action to follow astrology, the prediction was for the next November. 然而，月亮正失去其本就微弱的光芒，这预示着局势即将终结。金星需运行 17 度才能离开其星座。它处于固定星座且位于角宫，推运时间上意味着很长+很长。 由于预期事件会在几天内发生，且月亮处于其周期的末期，这证实了事件将会发

生，因此“月”似乎是最长的合理时间单位。考虑到占星征象显现后行动可能稍 有延迟，预测是下一个十一月。

The querent assured me that this was impossible, as she could not hold onto power for so long. The event followed as predicted. 问卜者向我坚称这不可能，因为她无法掌权那么久。但事件正如预测的那样发生 了。

【Wars and rumours of wars. - Posted on April 6th, 2014 【战争与战争的传闻 - 发布于 2014 年 4 月 6 日

That truth is indeed the first casualty of war makes any astrological investigation of these events, whether through horary or mundane astrology, particularly difficult. We rarely have any solid ground of understanding on which to build our judgement. Hundreds of years after a war historians still argue their radically different interpretations of what went on and why, so it’s no surprise that what the media tell us about what is happening now rarely has much connection with the truth. Discussing such a situation with one of the biggest names in front-line journalism, I was surprised less by his lack of knowledge of what was happening than by his sublime lack of interest in what was happening, caring only for whatever snippets of information could be turned to support his Walt Disney view of events. We might expect that the astrologer who is close to the seat of power would have a clearer picture, but this is not so either, for the one who is nominally in that driving-seat is often quite as much the baffled passenger as are the rest of us, carried blindly along by the tide. 真相确实是战争的第一个牺牲品，这使得任何针对这些事件的占星学研究，无论 是通过卜卦占星还是世运占星，都变得尤为困难。我们几乎没有任何坚实的理解 基础来构建我们的判断。一场战争结束数百年后，历史学家们仍在争论其过程和 原因的各种截然不同的解释，因此，媒体告诉我们的关于当下正在发生的事情， 很少与真相有多少关联，也就不足为奇了。与一位前线新闻界的知名人士讨论这 种情况时，令我惊讶的与其说是他对正在发生的事情缺乏了解，不如说是他对正 在发生的事情极度缺乏兴趣，他只关心那些能支持他那 Walt Disney（沃尔特·迪 斯尼）式事件观的一丁点儿信息碎片。我们可能会期望接近权力中心的占星师能 有更清晰的图景，但事实也并非如此，因为名义上坐在驾驶座上的人，往往也和 我们其他人一样，是一个困惑的乘客，被时代的潮流盲目地裹挟前行。

This makes the choice of significators difficult. If my country is going to war and I am asking a question about it, my country will be shown by the 1st house, as ‘us’. This regardless of my views on the matter. But although my country is ‘us’ the guys we’re shooting at are not necessarily our enemy. We may have no concern with them at all, but be shooting at them in order to exert pressure on whomever really is our enemy. A student asked if the outbreak of war would be shown by an aspect between the two significators. In itself, no: an aspect could just as well show a negotiated settlement. 这使得征象星的选择变得困难。如果我的国家要卷入战争，而我正就此提问，我

的国家将由第一宫代表，作为“我们”。这与我个人对此事的看法无关。但是， 尽管我的国家是“我们”，我们射击的对象却未必是我们的敌人。我们可能与他 们毫无瓜葛，射击他们只是为了对真正的敌人施加压力。一位学生问道，战争的 爆发是否由两个征象星之间的相位来显示。就其本身而言，并非如此：一个相位 同样可以显示通过谈判达成的解决方案。

The question of who will win is not as straightforward as judging a contest horary. If I score 3 goals and you score 2, I have won: simple. War is often not so simple, because it is rarely war a l’outrance. My student was asking about Ukraine. This is less a matter of ‘Will Russia win?’ than of ‘Will Russia get what it wants?’ But what does it want? Mr Putin does not wear his intentions on his sleeve – if, indeed, he knows them himself. It is, for instance, not uncommon for states to engineer a foreign war in order to quell discontent at home. Or following Machiavelli’s advice that the state, like the human body, needs to let blood from time to time to keep itself in health. 谁会赢的问题，并不像判断一场竞赛卜卦那样直接。如果我进了 3 个球，你进了 2 个，我就赢了：这很简单。战争往往不那么简单，因为它很少是决死之战。我 的学生问的是乌克兰问题。这与其说是“俄罗斯会赢吗？”，不如说是“俄罗斯 能得到它想要的吗？”。但它想要什么呢？Putin（普京）先生并不把自己的意 图写在袖子上——如果他本人真的知道的话。例如，国家为了平息国内不满而策 划一场对外战争，这种情况并不少见。或者遵循 Machiavelli（马基雅维利）的建 议，即国家如同人体，需要不时放血以保持健康。

We must be particularly careful to avoid prejudging the question by our choice of significators: see the discussion on questions about alcoholism in The Horary Textbook, Revised Edition for more on this trap. My student, who is Russian, was asking if the south-east of Ukraine would join Russia. But what is the south-east of Ukraine? Is it part of a neighbouring country? Something that belongs to the enemy? A part of his own country presently controlled by his country’s neighbours? or by his country’s enemy? Or is it simply a pawn in a much larger game?】 我们必须特别小心，避免通过选择征象星来预先判断问题：关于这个陷阱的更多 讨论，请参见《The Horary Textbook, Revised Edition》中关于酗酒问题的讨论。 我的学生是俄罗斯人，他问乌克兰东南部是否会加入俄罗斯。但乌克兰东南部是 什么？它是一个邻国的一部分吗？是属于敌人的东西？是他自己国家目前被邻 国控制的一部分？还是被自己国家的敌人控制的一部分？或者它只是一场更大 博弈中的一枚棋子？】

# Nineth House Questions

# 9 宫的问题

KNOWLEDGE, JOURNEYS AND DREAMS 知识、旅行与梦想

Will I profit from my knowledge? 我能从我的知识中获利吗？

This is the method for those frequent questions on ‘Can I earn a living as an astrologer/taror–reader/psychic?’ as well as queries on less arcane forms of knowledge, all usually occasioned by urgent need to turn a penny. The knowledge itself is shown by the 9th house. Potential profit from it is seen as the knowledge’s money: 2nd from the 9th, which is the 10th house. 这是针对那些常见问题（例如“我能以占星师/塔罗占卜师/灵媒为生吗？”）， 也适用于其他非神秘学领域的知识求问，这些问题通常都源于赚取收入的迫切需 求。知识本身由 9 宫表示。从中获利的潜力被视为知识的财帛：9 宫的 2 宫，即 10 宫。

Although in the abstract the distinction between this and certain 10th-house questions on career might seem blurred, in practice it is always clear enough. Even though the knowledge involved is astrological, my question ‘Will I get paid well if I go to work for Astrologers Inc.?’ is not a 9th-house matter: that would be 10th for the position and 11th for the wages. There is a distinction between a job (10th house) and the utilization of my knowledge (9th house). 尽管抽象来看，这与某些关于事业的 10 宫问题之间的区别可能显得模糊，但在 实践中总是足够清晰的。即使所涉及的知识是占星学的，我的问题“如果我去为 占星公司工作，我会获得丰厚报酬吗？”也不是 9 宫事务：那会是 10 宫代表职 位，11 宫代表薪酬。工作（10 宫）与我知识的运用（9 宫）之间存在区别。

It is, I suppose, feasible that someone might ask ‘Will I profit from my ability to read and write?’ in which case the knowledge, being elementary, would be 3rd house and the profit from it 4th. 我想，有人可能会问“我能从我的读写能力中获利吗？”，在这种情况下，知识 是基础性的，属于 3 宫，而从中获利则为 4 宫。

First, consider the condition of the querent’s knowledge. There is no direct connection – as the earnings of so many astrologers so clearly show – between the soundness of the knowledge and the profits that can be made from it. It is nonetheless helpful to see if the querent has any knowledge or not. Look at Lord 9 and the 9th house itself. 首先，考虑问卜者知识的状况。知识的健全性与从中可获得的利润之间并无直接 联系——正如许多占星师的收入状况所清楚表明的那样。尽管如此，但考察问卜 者是否具备知识仍有助益。观察 9 宫主和 9 宫本身。

The more essential dignity Lord 9 has, the better the knowledge. Generally, accidental strength or weakness will strengthen or weaken the knowledge, but, as ever, we must read the testimonies within the context. For example, finding Lord 9 in an angular house would strengthen the knowledge, in a cadent would weaken it. Yet if the knowledge is connected with large animals, finding Lord 9 in the 12th would be only appropriate and could not be taken as a debility. Or: being in an angular house would be an indication that the knowledge can be expressed easily, can manifest in the world. Yet if Lord 9 is in the 1st, especially if in a fixed sign, the knowledge could be stuck inside the querent, incapable of expression. 9 宫主的先天尊贵越多，知识越好。通常，偶然的强或弱会增强或削弱知识，但 一如既往，我们必须在具体语境中解读征象。例如，发现 9 宫主位于角宫会增强 知识，位于果宫则会削弱它。然而，如果知识与大型动物相关，发现 9 宫主在 12 宫反而是合适的，不应视为衰弱。再比如：位于角宫可能表示知识易于表达， 能在世间显现。但如果 9 宫主在 1 宫，尤其是在固定星座，知识可能困在问卜者 内心，无法表达。

Note other accidental features, such as the nature of the sign Lord 9 is in. A mute sign, for instance, does not bode well for any expression of this knowledge. Maybe Lord 9 has recently increased in dignity by entering a sign which is fixed: there has been a recent improvement in the querent’s knowledge, but (fixed signs moving slowly) it won’t improve further for a long time. Again, be aware of what the points you are considering might mean in context. Lord 9 retrograde, for example, which would usually be a debility, can be taken as a fitting description of the knowledge, and hence as no debility, if the knowledge involves looking back to the past. 注意其他偶然特征，例如 9 宫主所在星座的属性。例如，一个无声的星座对任何 此类知识的表达都不是好兆头。或许 9 宫主最近因进入一个固定星座而增强了尊 贵：问卜者的知识最近有所提高，但由于固定星座变动缓慢，很长时间内不会再 有进步。再次提醒，要意识到你正在考虑的要点在特定语境中可能意味着什么。 例如，9 宫主逆行通常是衰弱，但如果知识涉及回溯过去，则可视为对该知识的 恰当描述，从而不算是衰弱。

Consider any aspects to Lord 9: do these show help or hindrance? As ever, you must consider the receptions to fully understand the effect of the aspect. Example: Lord 9 is squared by Lord 5. With a positive mutual reception between them, perhaps the querent’s children, although their demands apparently hinder the querent’s knowledge,

in fact further it by what he learns in his interactions with them. With Lord 5 receiving Lord 9 into its detriment, the same square might show the querent’s love of alehouses and taverns harming his knowledge. 考虑任何与 9 宫主形成的相位：这些相位显示的是帮助还是阻碍？一如既往，你 必须考虑接纳关系以充分理解相位的影响。例子：9 宫主与 5 宫主相刑。如果它 们之间有积极的互溶接纳，也许问卜者的孩子，尽管他们的需求表面上阻碍了问 卜者的知识，实际上却通过问卜者在与他们的互动中所学而促进了知识。如果是 5 宫主接纳了 9 宫主至其落陷位置，同样的刑相位可能显示问卜者对酒馆的爱好 损害了他的知识。

Planets in the 9th house will help or hinder the knowledge according to their nature: essentially dignified planets will help it; essentially debilitated ones will hinder it. The nearer the cusp, the more powerful the effect. 9 宫内的行星会根据其属性帮助或阻碍知识：具有先天尊贵的行星会帮助它；先 天衰弱的行星会阻碍它。越靠近宫头，影响越强。

We do not need to find an aspect between Lord 9 and Lord 1, but if there is an aspect we must consider its nature. Suppose Lord 1 is conjunct Lord 9, which is in its fall: the querent is afflicted by his lack of knowledge. 我们不需要找到 9 宫主和 1 宫主之间的相位，但如果存在相位，我们必须考虑其 性质。假设 1 宫主与 9 宫主合相，而 9 宫主处于落陷：问卜者因其知识的匮乏而 受困扰。

The profit from the knowledge is judged by considering the 10th house and its ruler, in the same way as we have assessed the state of the querent’s knowledge by looking at the 9th and its ruler. 通过考虑 10 宫及其宫主星来判断从知识中获得的利润，方式与我们通过观察 9 宫及其宫主星来评估问卜者知识状况相同。

NB: we do not need to find an aspect between Lord 10 and either Lord 1 (querent) or Lord 9 (querent’s knowledge) to show the profit coming to the querent. That it is profit from the knowledge assumes that it is coming to the querent: it would not be profit otherwise. But if there is an aspect, we must consider its nature. Example: 注意：我们不需要找到 10 宫主与 1 宫主（问卜者）或 9 宫主（问卜者的知识） 之间的相位来显示利润归于问卜者。既然是“来自知识的利润”，就假定它是归 于问卜者的：否则就不是利润了。但如果存在相位，我们必须考虑其性质。例如：

* Lord 10 in its detriment, applying to Lord 1 by trine. There is very little profit, but what there is comes easily.
* 10 宫主处于落陷位置，以拱相位向 1 宫主行进。利润很少，但现有的部分来得 容易。

* Lord 10 in its exaltation, squaring Lord 1. Big profit, but you’ll have to struggle for it.

* 10 宫主处于旺势位置，与 1 宫主相刑。利润丰厚，但你必须为之奋斗。

* Lord 10 opposing Lord 1. No matter how much profit there might be, it will not be worth the effort expended to gain it.
* 10 宫主与 1 宫主对冲。无论可能有多少利润，都不值得为获得它而付出的努力。

Being adjacent houses, the 9th and 10th often have the same planet as ruler. This is not a problem, because we do not need to find an aspect between their rulers. It tells us that the knowledge and its rewards are of the same quality (as long as nothing is happening to the houses themselves to show otherwise). 由于是相邻的宫位，9 宫和 10 宫常常有相同的行星作为宫主星。这不是问题， 因为我们不需要找到它们宫主星之间的相位。这告诉我们知识和其回报具有相同 的性质（除非宫位本身发生其他情况显示相反）。

We must also consider the 8th house. Being 2nd from the 7th it is ‘other people’s money’, the other people in this context being the customers. Restrictions in the amount of money the customers have will limit the potential profits. 我们还必须考虑 8 宫。作为 7 宫的 2 宫，它是“他人的钱财”，此处的“他人” 指顾客。顾客拥有的金钱数量限制将制约潜在的利润。

Consider this as with the 9th and 10th houses above, with one exception: if Lord 8 is in its own sign it shows that the customers have plenty of money; if it is also in the 8th house, even though they have plenty of money, it is staying in their pockets. This is no good to our querent! If Lord 8 is also in a fixed sign, the money is staying all the more resolutely in their pockets. 参照上述对 9 宫和 10 宫的分析来考虑这一点，但有一个例外：如果 8 宫主在其 入庙星座，表明顾客有很多钱；如果它也位于 8 宫内，那么即使他们有很多钱， 钱也留在他们口袋里。这对我们的问卜者毫无益处！如果 8 宫主还位于固定星座， 钱就更加坚决地留在他们口袋里了。

Once the 9th, 10th and 8th house have been judged, take a look at the querent. If the judgement so far has shown difficulties, is the querent capable of taking action to overcome them? If, on the other hand, Lord 1 is badly debilitated, the querent might be unable to stir himself to take advantage of even the most glowing financial prospects. 判断完 9 宫、10 宫和 8 宫后，看一看问卜者自身。如果迄今为止的判断显示有 困难，问卜者是否有能力采取行动克服它们？另一方面，如果 1 宫主严重衰弱， 问卜者可能连最光明的财务前景都无法激励自己去利用。

### ✸The customers’ money is very much a secondary consideration in a question like

this. If the profit is good, we needn’t bother with Lord 8, because if the customer’s money were not flowing in, the profit would not be good. But if the profit is not good, looking at Lord 8 might reveal the problem: perhaps the customers haven’t got any

money, or don’t wish to part with what they have. It may be possible for the querent to do something about this, by aiming at different customers or finding some more persuasive marketing.

### ✸在这样的问题中，顾客的钱财是非常次要的考虑因素。如果利润看好，我们

无需费心看 8 宫主，因为如果顾客的钱财没有流入，利润就不会好。但如果利润 不好，查看 8 宫主可能会揭示问题：也许顾客没有钱，或者不愿拿出他们拥有的 钱。问卜者或许有可能对此采取行动，例如瞄准不同的顾客或找到更具说服力的 营销方式。

Be realistic. Lord 10 may show there is light at the end of the financial tunnel, but if the tunnel is too long and too dark, the querent is unlikely to reach it. Realistic too in how you read the receptions of Lord 7, the customers. For instance, Lord 7 exalting Lord 1 could show that the customers think the querent is wonderful. More likely is that they have unrealistic expectations of what the querent might offer. If they expect the querent’s astrological knowledge to turn life to spun sugar or the querent’s massage skills to raise the dead, they will be disappointed and their money will not be forthcoming. Such expectations can be unrealistic no matter how great the querent’s knowledge.✷ 务必务实。10 宫主可能显示财务困境的尽头有光，但如果隧道太长太暗，问卜 者未必能坚持抵达。在解读 7 宫主（顾客）的接纳关系时也要务实。例如，7 宫 主位于 1 宫主旺势的位置可能表示顾客认为问卜者非常出色。更可能的是他们对 问卜者能提供的东西抱有不切实际的期望。如果他们期望问卜者的占星知识能将 生活变得如棉花糖般甜蜜，或期望问卜者的按摩技能能起死回生，他们将会失望， 他们的钱也不会到来。无论问卜者的知识多么渊博，这样的期望都可能是不切实 际的。✷

Examinations 考试

‘Will I pass the exam?’ is a specific form of profit from knowledge question. The exam is the profit, so is shown by the 10th house. An aspect between querent and exam is helpful, but given enough reception we can manage without. A square will give a pass, unless the receptions are bad; an opposition will fail, unless the receptions are especially good, when it can show a pass at a disappointing grade. “我会通过考试吗？”是知识获利问题的一种特定形式。考试即是利润，因此由 10 宫表示。问卜者与考试之间的相位是有帮助的，但如果有充分的接纳关系， 没有相位也能判断。刑相位会带来通过，除非接纳关系不佳；对冲相位会导致失 败，除非接纳关系特别好，此时可能表示以令人失望的成绩通过。。

Do remind the querent that however positive your prediction might be, it is still necessary to do some work. 务必提醒问卜者，无论你的预测多么积极，仍然有必要做一些准备工作。

### ✸To pass an examination, we need not only to have sufficient knowledge, but also

to demonstrate that we have it: to make that knowledge visible. So while we can look at Lord 10 to show success in the exam, I would prioritise Lord 9 itself. It must be in good enough condition – depending on how demanding the exam is – and visible. Being near the top of the chart (i.e. being high in the sky, where it can be seen) is a major positive. Being hidden away at the bottom of a chart, a strong negative. A planet that is combust cannot be seen, so combustion is a No, even if the planet is above the Earth. Remember that if the planet is combust in its own sign or exaltation, the sense of being hidden remains, even though it is not otherwise afflicted. How much testimony is needed depends upon how demanding the exam is. Is it like a driving-test, where everyone who reaches a certain basic standard passes, or is it a competitive exam where only the very best candidates can pass?

### ✸要通过考试，我们不仅需要拥有足够的知识，还需要展示我们拥有它：使知

识可见。因此，虽然我们可以观察 10 宫主来显示考试成功，但我更优先关注 9 宫主本身。它必须处于足够良好的状态——取决于考试的要求有多高——并且是 可见的。位于星盘顶部附近（即在天上较高的位置，可以被看到）是一个主要的 积极因素。隐藏在星盘底部则是强烈的负面因素。一颗燃烧的行星是不可见的， 因此燃烧意味着“不通过”，即使该行星在地平线上方。记住，如果行星在其入 庙星座或旺势位置燃烧，被隐藏的感觉依然存在，即使它没有其他方面的损害。 需要多少征象支持取决于考试的要求有多高。它是像驾驶考试那样，所有达到某 个基本标准的人都能通过，还是竞争性考试，只有最优秀的考生才能通过？

Most exams concern 9th-house type knowledge, but a driving-test, which is about negotiating the daily routine of life, is 3rd house. Similarly with a test on basic literacy in the person’s native language, or simple arithmetic. Anything above the level is 9th-house. 大多数考试涉及 9 宫类型的知识，但驾驶考试是关于处理日常生活的常规事务， 属于 3 宫。母语的基本读写能力测试或简单算术测试也是如此。任何高于此水平 的考试都属于 9 宫。

If the exam is directly linked to getting a job, the exam itself often becomes irrelevant. If the exam forms a large part of the selection procedure, the question is usually not so much ‘Will I pass the exam?’ as ‘Will I get the job?’ (for which, see the next chapter). If, for instance, the aspect between Lord 1 and Lord 10 that would show the querent getting the job were prohibited by a debilitated Lord 9, we might judge that the reason for failure is a poor showing in the exam; if an exalted Lord 9 translated light between Lord 1 and Lord 10, that excelling in the exam would bring querent the job.✷ 如果考试与获得工作直接相关，考试本身往往变得无关紧要。如果考试构成选拔 程序的大部分，问题通常不是“我会通过考试吗？”，而是“我会得到这份工作 吗？”（关于此点，请参见下一章）。例如，如果显示问卜者得到工作的 1 宫主 与 10 宫主之间的相位被一个衰弱的 9 宫主所阻碍，我们可能会判断失败的原因

是考试表现不佳；如果一个旺势的 9 宫主在 1 宫主和 10 宫主之间传递光线，那 么在考试中表现出色将为问卜者带来工作。✷

Will I profit from the voyage? 我会从这次航行中获利吗？

This is judged in the same way as the knowledge questions above: the 9th house shows the voyage and the 10th its profit. So if Saturn squares Lord 9 there are delays to the voyage; if it squares Lord 10, there are restrictions to the profit. Venus trines Lord 9 but opposes Lord 10: the voyage is lots of fun, but doesn’t pay for itself. 此问题的判断方式与上述知识问题相同：9 宫代表航行，10 宫代表其利润。因此， 如果土星刑 9 宫主，则航行会有延误；如果土星刑 10 宫主，则利润会受到限制。 如果金星拱 9 宫主但对冲 10 宫主：航行乐趣颇多，但不足以抵偿其成本。

This also covers questions such as: 此类问题也涵盖诸如：

* Will this course boost my earning power?
* 这门课程会提升我的赚钱能力吗？

* Is going to this trade-show a good idea?
* 参加这次贸易展览会是个好主意吗？

‘Spiritual’ matters “灵性”事务

### ✸ From time to time I’ve been asked about answering questions such as ‘Will I

achieve enlightenment in this lifetime?’ or ‘Is xyz in this life the result of abc in a former life?’ I’m sure many astrologers would happily attempt such questions. I wouldn’t, because the concept of ‘enlightenment’ in this sense, or of a former life, is something outside my understanding. As such, I would have no idea of how to make such a judgement. This is something quite different from not knowing much about the subject: I know little about how stock markets work, but I am aware that they exist.✷

### ✸偶尔有人问我如何回答诸如“我此生会证悟吗？”或“今生的 XYZ 是否是前

世 ABC 的结果？”这类问题。我相信很多占星师会很乐意尝试解答这类问题。 我不会，因为“证悟”或“前世”这类概念超出了我的理解范围。因此，我完全 不知道该如何做出此类判断。这与对某个主题知之甚少截然不同：我对股票市场 如何运作了解不多，但我知道它们存在。✷

Dream analysis 解梦

If the dream is prophetic and the question is about its veracity, use the method for determining truth or falsehood described in chapter 17. If the question is ‘What was that all about?’ set the chart as usual for the time this question is asked. Don’t try to establish the time of the dream. Find the significators for the characters in the dream from their usual houses: the querent, dreaming the dream, will be the 1st, even if he’s dreamed he’s Elvis; his farm will be the 4th; his dog the 6th. In essence, treat the dream exactly as if it were an event in daily life. The aspects and receptions between the significators will enable you to tease out the meaning of the dream. 如果梦境具有预示性，而问题是关于其真实性，请使用第 17 章中所述的判断真 伪的方法。如果问题是“那到底是什么意思？”，则按通常方式以提出此问题的 时间起盘。无需试图确定梦境发生的时间。根据常规宫位找出梦中角色的征象星： 问卜者，作为做梦的人，将是 1 宫，即使他梦见自己是猫王；他的农场将是 4 宫；他的狗将是 6 宫。本质上，完全将梦境当作日常生活中的事件来处理。征象 星之间的相位和接纳关系将使你能够梳理出梦境的含义。

You do not need to pay any special attention to the 9th house when doing this. The whole chart is about the dream, not only the 9th house. The 9th would be used if the dream featured, for instance, a priest or teacher or voyage, or there were a dream within the dream. The situation is the same as in a medical horary: there, the whole chart is about the illness, so the illness is not confined to the 6th house. 当解梦的时候，无需特别关注 9 宫。整个星盘都与梦境相关，而不仅仅是 9 宫。 只有当梦境中出现例如神职人员、教师或航行，或者梦中有梦时，才会用到 9 宫。这种情况与医疗卜卦类似：在医疗卜卦中，整个星盘都与疾病相关，因此疾 病并不局限于 6 宫。

Choosing a school 选择学校

Parents ask about their children’s schools. Elementary school is 3rd house; anything above that level is 9th. If there is a distinction between higher and lower levels of education, the lower can always be given to the 3rd, the higher to the 9th (‘Will she enjoy university better than high school?). Even though the child is not usually the querent in these questions, do not turn the chart to locate the school: use the radical 9th or 3rd houses, not the 9th or 3rd from the 5th. Although we speak of ‘my school’, the school does not belong to the child. 家长会询问关于孩子学校的问题。小学属于 3 宫；高于此级别的任何教育都属于 9 宫。如果需要在不同教育层级之间进行区分，较低层级的总是可以归为 3 宫， 较高层级的归为 9 宫（例如“她会更喜欢大学而不是高中吗？”）。即使在这些 问题中孩子通常不是问卜者，也不要通过转宫来定位学校：使用基准盘的 9 宫或 3 宫，而不是 5 宫的 9 宫或 3 宫。尽管我们常说“我的学校”，但学校并不属于

孩子。

‘How will she do at her new school?’ is straightforward: look at the receptions and any applying aspects between Lord 5 (the child) and Lord 9 (the school). In a question like this we do not need to have an aspect, because we are not asking if something will happen; we are enquiring about a state of affairs. But if there is an aspect, we must take notice of it. “她在新学校会表现如何？”这个问题是直接的：观察 5 宫主（孩子）和 9 宫主 （学校）之间的接纳关系以及任何正在形成的相位。在此类问题中，我们并不一 定需要相位，因为我们不是在询问某事是否会发生；我们是在探究一种状况。但 如果存在相位，我们必须注意到它。

Look at the condition of Lord 9 to see how good a school it is. No matter how good the school might be, however, it does not necessarily suit this particular child, hence the importance of the receptions. Lord 9 in the exaltation of Lord 5: the school thinks the child is wonderful and will favour her. Lord 9 in the fall of Lord 5: the school thinks she is dreadful and will harm her. 观察 9 宫主的状况以判断学校的优劣。然而，无论学校本身多么优秀，它不一定 适合这个特定的孩子，因此接纳关系至关重要。9 宫主位于 5 宫主的旺势位置： 学校认为孩子很棒，将会优待她。9 宫主位于 5 宫主的落陷位置：学校认为她很 糟糕，将会对她不利。

Mentally pick up the child’s significator and drop it just inside the 9th house. How is it there? Consider both essential and accidental testimony. Lord 5 finds itself in its exaltation: she’ll do well. In combustion: she’ll do badly. Perhaps the sign changes a few degrees into the 9th house. Dropping Lord 5 just inside the house leaves it weak, but in that next sign it will be strong: she’ll get off to a shaky start, but will quickly find her feet. 在脑海中想象将孩子的征象星拿起，轻轻放入 9 宫内。它在里面状况如何？同时 考虑先天和偶然征象。5 宫主发现自己位于其旺势位置：她会表现良好。处于燃 烧状态：她会表现糟糕。也许在进入 9 宫几度后星座会改变。将 5 宫主刚放入宫 位内时它可能较弱，但在下一个星座它会变强：她起步会有些摇晃，但很快就能 站稳脚跟。

As always, benefics or malefics in the 9th house will affect the quality of that house, with direct reference to the context of the question – which in this case is how the child will fare. Jupiter in Pisces in the 9th is most fortunate. Saturn in Aries is to be avoided. As always, it is the amount of essential dignity a planet has that makes it benefic. Saturn in its own sign or exaltation in the 9th would be strongly fortunate. Not as much fun as Jupiter or Venus in dignity, but fortunate nonetheless. 一如既往，9 宫内的吉星或凶星会影响该宫位的质量，需直接参照问题的背景— —在本例中即是孩子的境况如何。木星在双鱼座位于 9 宫是非常幸运的。土星在 白羊座则应避免。同样，决定一颗行星是否为吉星的关键在于其拥有的先天尊贵 数量。土星在其入庙星座或旺势位置位于 9 宫将非常幸运。虽然不如木星或金星

处于尊贵位置那样有趣，但仍然是幸运的。

If the question is about the choice of this school or that school, the querent’s favoured option is given the 9th (or 3rd) house. We must then find a significator for the alternative or alternatives. Do make the querent do some of the work: you have every right to demand that they narrow the options to a short-list. If you are presented with half-a-dozen or more alternatives, send the querent away to think about it some more. 如果问题是关于选择这所学校或那所学校，问卜者偏好的选项被赋予 9 宫（或 3 宫）。然后我们必须为其他一个或多个备选学校找到征象星。务必让问卜者也做 一些工作：你完全有权要求他们将选项缩减到一个短名单。如果给你六七个甚至 更多的备选学校，请让问卜者回去再考虑一下。

There are various theories on how to find significators for the other schools. A popular one suggests taking the 3rd from the 9th. Don’t! This is a false extrapolation from the technique of using the 3rd from the 3rd to show my brother’s brother (i.e. my younger brother). The alternative school is not the first school’s brother. 关于如何为其他学校寻找征象星有各种理论。一种流行的观点建议取 9 宫的 3 宫。不要这样做！ 这是从“用 3 宫的 3 宫来表示我兄弟的兄弟（即我的弟弟）” 这一技巧错误推导出来的。备选学校并不是首选学校的兄弟。

Holding slightly more water is the idea of taking the 7th from the 9th (he 3rd) to show the rival school. But the alternative schools are not really rivals, in the sense that candidates for a job or contestants in a game are. While if there is more than one alternative, this still leaves the problem of locating the others. 另一种稍微合理点的想法是取 9 宫（或 3 宫）的 7 宫来表示竞争对手学校。但备 选学校并非真正的竞争对手，不像求职者或比赛选手之间那样。而且，如果不止 一个备选，这仍然无法解决如何定位其他学校的问题。

I recommend that you ask the querent to describe the different schools. Stress that this description should be brief: no more than a few words. If the descriptions are kept short, the querent will concentrate on the salient distinguishing features. You can then choose significators by planetary nature. ‘That school is very arty; the other is much more old-fashioned’: the first is Venus, the second Saturn. 我建议你让问卜者描述一下不同的学校。强调描述应简短：不超过几个词。如果 描述保持简短，问卜者就会专注于突出的区别性特征。然后你可以根据行星属性 来选择征象星。“那所学校很有艺术气息；另一所则传统得多”：第一所是金星， 第二所是土星。

Once you have chosen the significators, compare their strength and consider their receptions with Lord 5. Again, remember that the best school (most dignity) may not be the one best suited to this individual, so weight the receptions when making judgement. 一旦你选择了征象星，就比较它们的强弱，并考虑它们与 5 宫主之间的接纳关系。 再次记住，最好的学校（拥有最多尊贵）可能并非最适合这个个体的学校，因此

在做出判断时要权衡接纳关系。

# Tenth House Question

# 10 宫的问题

JOB QUESTIONS 求职问题

Will I get the job? 我能得到这份工作吗？

The querent is Lord 1 and the Moon; the job is Lord 10. If there is an applying aspect between them, all things being equal, the querent will get the job. The nature of the aspect must be judged in the usual way: if it is a trine, he gets the job easily; if an opposition, he gets it, but wishes he hadn’t, or doesn’t keep it for long. As always, look out for collections or translations of light, especially if an intermediary, such as an agent or head-hunter, is involved. 问卜者的征象星是 1 宫主和月亮；工作的征象星是 10 宫主。如果它们之间形成 入相位，在其他条件同等的情况下，问卜者将得到这份工作。必须按通常方式判 断相位的性质：如果是拱相位，他能轻松得到工作；如果是对冲相位，他能得到， 但会希望自己没得到，或者无法长期保有。一如既往，要留意光线聚集或光线传 递，特别是当涉及中介（如代理或猎头）时。

Lilly says that an aspect to the Sun will work instead of one to Lord 10, but this is on the assumption that the querent is seeking a royal appointment. Lilly 说，与太阳形成相位可以代替与 10 宫主形成相位，但这建立在问卜者谋求 的是皇家任命的假设之上。

Finding the querent’s significator in the 10th house is only a minor testimony of success. It shows that the querent wants the job (or, if not in the same sign as the 10th cusp, that he wants a job), and the querent who wants it is more likely to get it than the one who does not. But it shows no more than that. If other testimony confirms that the job will be given, application of the querent’s significator to the 10th cusp can show the timing. 发现问卜者的征象星在 10 宫，仅是成功的次要征象。它只表明问卜者想要这份 工作（或者，如果不在与 10 宫头相同的星座，则表明他想要一份工作），而想 要工作的问卜者比不想要的人更有可能得到它。但它仅此而已。如果其他征象确

认工作将被给予，问卜者的征象星与 10 宫头形成入相位可以显示时间。

Finding Lord 10 in the 1st house is much more positive: the job is in the querent’s pocket. The closer Lord 10 is to the cusp, the stronger is the testimony. But if Lord 10 is on the cusp rather than inside the house it usually shows nothing more than that the idea of getting a job is weighing on the querent. 发现 10 宫主在 1 宫则积极得多：工作已在问卜者囊中。10 宫主越靠近宫头，这 个征象就越强。但如果 10 宫主在宫头而非宫内，通常只表明得到工作的想法正 压在问卜者心上。

Even if there is an aspect, pay attention to the strength of the querent’s significator: would you employ Saturn retrograde in its detriment? Chances are, no one else will either. The more strength the querent’s planet has, the more sought-after the querent is likely to be. In certain cases, especially if the querent is making a speculative application rather than one for a known vacancy, the job (which can be taken as synonymous with the company: Lord 10) may be too weak to offer employment, even if reception shows that it would like to do so. 即使存在相位，也要注意问卜者征象星的力量：你会雇佣一颗逆行且落陷的土星 吗？很可能，别人也不会。问卜者的行星力量越强，问卜者本人就可能越抢手。 在某些情况下，特别是当问卜者是在投递投机性申请，而非针对已知空缺职位时， 工作（可视为公司的同义词：10 宫主）可能过于衰弱而无法提供职位，即使接 纳关系显示它愿意这样做。

If the querent’s planets are in dignities of Lord 10, the querent wants the job to whatever extent the dignities suggest: if in the sign of Lord 10, he wants it a lot; if in the face, he has a small interest in it; if in the exaltation of Lord 10, he exaggerates its qualities. Exaltation does not tell us anything about the job itself, but it does show that the querent overrates it, so no matter how good the job might be it is unlikely to live up to expectations. 如果问卜者的行星位于 10 宫主的尊贵位置，则问卜者想要这份工作的程度取决 于尊贵的含义：若在 10 宫主的入庙星座，他非常想要；若在得面位置，他兴趣 不大；若在 10 宫主的旺势位置，他夸大了工作的品质。旺势并不告诉我们工作 本身的情况，但它确实表明问卜者高估了它，因此无论工作本身多好，都难以达 到预期。

Of course, people who apply for jobs are not always driven by enthusiasm for the job itself. You will often find the querent’s planets showing a strong interest in Lord 2, the querent’s bank balance. In such cases, Lord 2 is usually weak: ‘I’m broke – I need a job!’ Sometimes they will show a strong interest in Lord 11, the 2nd from the 10th: the job’s money. Check the condition of Lord 11 to see if the pay will be good. Suppose Lord 11 applies to the querent by trine, is itself strong, and is in the sign of the querent’s exaltation: he’ll be paid well and without delays, and (exalts him) can expect bonuses. Suppose Lord 11 is in fall and applies to the querent by square: the pay is dreadful, less than expected, and he will have to fight for it. It is also worth

checking the relationship between Lord 11 and Lord 2: the querent’s bank balance and the wages loving each other (mutual reception) is a positive sign. An aspect between querent and wages in not testimony of getting the job. 当然，申请工作的人并非总是由对工作本身的热情驱动。你常会发现问卜者的行 星对 2 宫主（问卜者的银行余额）表现出强烈兴趣。这种情况下，2 宫主通常是 衰弱的：“我破产了——我需要一份工作！”有时，他们会表现出对 11 宫主（10 宫的 2 宫，即工作的钱财）的强烈兴趣。检查 11 宫主的状况以判断薪资是否优 厚。假设 11 宫主通过拱相位与问卜者形成入相位，自身有力，且位于问卜者的 旺势星座：他将得到优厚且无延迟的报酬，并且（提升他）可以期待奖金。假设 11 宫主处于弱势，并通过刑相位与问卜者形成入相位：薪资极差，低于预期， 并且他必须为之奋斗。检查 11 宫主与 2 宫主之间的关系也值得一做：问卜者的 银行余额与工资彼此相爱（互溶关系）是积极的迹象。问卜者与工资之间的相位 并非得到工作的征象。

### ✸Although the 11th house, as the 2nd from the 10th, is the job’s money, it does not

show how much money the company has in the bank; it shows how much of that money the company will give to me. Only if the focus of the question is different, such as ‘Will the company I work for go bust?’ does the 11th show the company’s bank balance.✷

### ✸尽管 11 宫作为 10 宫之 2 宫，是工作的钱财，但它并不显示公司银行里有多

少钱；它显示的是公司将把那笔钱中的多少给我。只有当问题的焦点不同时，例 如“我工作的公司会破产吗？”，11 宫才显示公司的银行余额。✷

With all but a few jobs we cannot expect to see Lord 10 in any dignity of our querent. With all but a few jobs, it is a matter of indifference to the job whether it is done by Tom, Dick or Harry. It is only with jobs requiring rare skills or having a high profile, the type of job for which one might be headhunted, that we would expect to see Lord 10 showing a strong interest in the querent. So with most charts on this subject, finding Lord 10 in even the term or face of Lord 1 is a positive testimony: the job likes the querent. We still need an aspect, though. Lord 10 in the detriment or fall of Lord 1 shows a strong dislike, so the querent would be unlikely to get the job. If the querent were particularly strong the job might overlook its dislike in view of his qualifications. 对于绝大多数工作，我们不能指望看到 10 宫主处于问卜者的任何尊贵位置。对 于绝大多数工作来说，由 Tom、Dick 还是 Harry 来做这份工作，对工作本身而言 无关紧要。只有在那些需要罕见技能或引人注目、可能通过猎头招聘的工作类型 中，我们才会期望看到 10 宫主对问卜者表现出强烈的兴趣。因此，对于大多数 涉及此主题的星盘，发现 10 宫主即使仅仅位于 1 宫主的得界或得面位置，也是 一个积极的征象：工作喜欢问卜者。不过，我们仍然需要一个相位。10 宫主位 于 1 宫主的落陷或弱势位置，则显示出强烈的厌恶，因此问卜者不太可能得到工 作。如果问卜者特别有力，鉴于其资历，工作可能会忽略这种厌恶。

### ✸The strength of Lord 10 is occasionally of importance. As noted above, if Lord 1

is in poor condition the querent is not a prime candidate, so even with an aspect may not be given the job. But if Lord 10 is also in poor condition,, the company may be so desperate that it will employ anybody. Bear in mind, too, the reality of the situation. If the querent is applying to stack shelves in the supermarket, a job for which the company probably will employ just about anybody, the weakness of Lord 1 will not be important.✷

### ✸10 宫主的力量偶尔也很重要。如上所述，如果 1 宫主状况不佳，问卜者就不

是首选候选人，因此即使有相位也可能得不到工作。但如果 10 宫主状况也同样 不佳，公司可能绝望到愿意雇用任何人。同时，也要牢记现实情况。如果问卜者 申请的是超市理货员这样的职位，公司很可能雇用几乎任何人，那么 1 宫主的衰 弱就不那么重要了。✷

The North Node or a strongly dignified planet in the 10th, especially if close to the cusp, shows fortune in 10th house matters; the South Node or a debilitated planet there shows loss. These do not necessarily relate directly to the Yes or No of ‘Will I get the job?’ For example, with the South Node in the 10th other testimonies may show that the querent gets the job, but it’s a horrible job. 北交点或一颗强而有力的行星在 10 宫，尤其是靠近宫头时，显示 10 宫事务方面 的好运；南交点或一颗衰弱的行星在那里则显示损失。这些不一定直接关系到“我 能得到工作吗？”的是与否。例如，南交点在 10 宫，其他征象可能显示问卜者 得到了工作，但这是一份糟糕的工作。

As in any question where change is required, a void of course Moon is a strong negative indicator, suggesting that the issue is going nowhere. As always, it can be overruled by more compelling testimony. 如同任何需要改变的问题一样，空亡月亮是一个强烈的负面指标，表明事情将毫 无进展。一如既往，它可能被更有力的征象所推翻。

Lord 7 shows the querent’s open enemies: the rivals for the position. If Lord 10 aspects Lord 7 before it reaches Lord 1, the other applicant gets the job. If Lord 12 were involved in the action, this could show a secret enemy: the one who writes the anonymous letter that rubbishes the querent’s application. 7 宫主代表问卜者的公开敌人：该职位的竞争者。如果 10 宫主在到达 1 宫主之 前先与 7 宫主形成相位，那么其他申请者将得到这份工作。如果 12 宫主介入其 中，这可能显示一个隐秘的敌人：例如写匿名信中伤问卜者申请的人。

If the querent is asking about someone else – usually a spouse or a child – applying for a job, use the radical 10th for the job. The job is something external to the person, so we take the radical 10th in the same way that ‘Will my daughter get into university?’ would be shown by the radical 9th. Use the turned 10th to judge a question about that person’s career, boss or a job they already have. If the question is

about a 10th-house person (‘Will Mum get the job?’) we have to use the turned 10th for the job. 如果问卜者是在询问他人（通常是配偶或子女）申请工作的情况，使用基准 10 宫来代表工作。工作是外在于该人的事物，因此我们采用基准 10 宫，就像“我 女儿能上大学吗？”会用基准 9 宫来显示一样。使用转宫 10 宫来判断关于该人 职业、老板或已有工作的问题。如果问题涉及 10 宫相关的人（“妈妈能得到那 份工作吗？”），我们必须使用转宫 10 宫来代表工作。

### ✸With jobs in the public sector, be alert to separating asepcts between Lord 10 and

Lord 7. It is common for the employers to be legally obliged to advertise the position, even though the decision on who will fill it has already been made. So this separating aspect would show that the job has already gone to someone else.

### ✸对于公职求职，要警惕 10 宫主与 7 宫主之间的出相位。用人单位常因法规要

求公示已内定岗位，此时出相显示职位已花落别家。

As always, be clear about what is asked. For instance, a question such as ‘Will my book be published?’ is not ‘Will I get the job?’ and the publishers are not shown by the 10th house. They would be seen as employers only if the querent were applying for a job as staff writer. The publishers would be people with whom the querent does a deal: 7th house. The subject of the deal is the querent’s creation: 5th house. The question is, in effect, ‘Will they buy my baby?’ A Yes would be shown by an applying aspect between Lord 1 or the Moon and Lord 7, or between Lord 5 and Lord 7.✷ 一如既往，要明确问题的内容。例如，“我的书会被出版吗？”这个问题并非“我 能得到工作吗？”，出版商不由 10 宫代表。只有当问卜者申请的是驻店作家的 职位时，他们才会被视为雇主。出版商是问卜者与之达成交易的人：第 7 宫。交 易的对象是问卜者的创作：5 宫。这个问题实质上是“他们会买我的‘孩子’吗？” 肯定的答案会通过 1 宫主或月亮与 7 宫主之间，或 5 宫主与 7 宫主之间形成入相 位来显示。✷

People at work 工作中的人际关系

In a question directly about the boss (‘Will I get along with my new boss?’) the boss is shown by the tenth house and Lord 10. Any of my superiors, even the most minor of them, will be 10th house if that person is the subject of the question. If we need to distinguish between different levels of authority over me, we can take the rulers of the various dignities my significator is in. Example: suppose the question is ‘To which level of management should I take my complaint?’ and my significator is Saturn at 12 Sagittarius in a daytime chart. It is disposited by Jupiter, in the triplicity of the Sun, the term of Venus and the face of the Moon. Jupiter is in Leo, the detriment of Saturn, so I won’t get any sympathy from the big boss. The Sun is in Taurus, so the next level

of management will be indifferent. The Moon, my face-ruler, is in Cancer, so my immediate superior doesn’t like me either. But Venus is in Capricorn: if I go to the next level up, I will receive a sympathetic hearing. If Venus were accidentally strong, so much the better: this superior can do something about my problem. 在直接关于老板的问题中（“我能与新老板相处融洽吗？”），老板由第 10 宫 和 10 宫主代表。我的任何上级，即使是最低级别的，如果此人是问题的焦点， 都将由 10 宫代表。如果我们需要区分对我有不同级别的权威，可以采用我的征 象星所在的各种尊贵位置的守护星来区分。例如：假设问题是“我应该向哪一级 管理层投诉？”，我的征象星是土星，位于射手座 12 度，在一个日生盘中。它 的定位星是木星，位于太阳的三分位置、金星的得界位置和月亮的得面位置。木 星在狮子座，是土星的落陷位置，所以我不会从大老板那里得到任何同情。太阳 在金牛座，所以再下一级的管理层会漠不关心。月亮，我的面主星，在巨蟹座， 所以我的直接上级也不喜欢我。但金星在摩羯座：如果我找再上一级，我会得到 富有同情心的倾听。如果金星偶然有力，那就更好了：这位上级能为我的问题做 点什么。

If we need to identify the boss in a question about the job (‘Will I get this job and how will I get along with the boss?’), we cannot give the boss the 10th because that is already being used to show the job. Sometimes we can turn the chart, taking the 10th from the 10th (radical 7th) as ‘the boss of the job’. But in many questions the 7th is already busy, signifying either the rivals for the position or the co-workers. In that case, we can use the dispositor of Lord 10, which is literally the ruler of the job. 如果我们需要在一个关于工作的问题中识别老板（“我能得到这份工作吗？与老 板相处会如何？”），我们不能将老板分配给 10 宫，因为 10 宫已被用来代表工 作。有时我们可以转宫，取 10 宫之 10 宫（基准 7 宫）作为“工作的老板”。但 在许多问题中，7 宫已被占用，要么代表职位的竞争者，要么代表同事。在这种 情况下，我们可以使用 10 宫主的定位星，顾名思义，它就是工作的统治者。

If the question were ‘Will I get along with my new boss?’ the prime consideration would be the receptions between the significators. We do not need to find an aspect, because we are analyzing a situation, not looking for an event; but if there is an aspect between the significators, we must take notice of what it is. Look also at which planets have influence over the boss by disposition. Example: suppose my significator is Saturn and the boss’s is Venus. Venus is in Capricorn: so far, so good – the boss likes me a lot. But in Capricorn it aslo exalts Mars, and when I look at Mars I find it is in Leo, the sign where Saturn (me) is in detriment. This is not so good: although he likes me, the boss has an inflated regard (exaltation) for someone else (Mars), who hates me (in the sign where my planet is in detriment). 如果问题是“我能与新老板相处融洽吗？”，首要考虑的是征象星之间的接纳关 系。我们不需要寻找一个相位，因为我们是在分析一种状况，而不是寻找一个事 件；但如果征象星之间存在相位，我们必须注意它是什么。同时也要查看哪些行 星通过定位对老板有影响。例如：假设我的征象星是土星，老板的征象星是金星。 金星在摩羯座：到目前为止，还不错——老板非常喜欢我。但在摩羯座，它也旺 势火星，而当我查看火星时，发现它在狮子座，这是土星（我）落陷的星座。这

就不太妙了：尽管老板喜欢我，但他过分看重（旺势）另一个人（火星），而那 个人讨厌我（在我的行星落陷的星座）。

My co-workers are 7th house. They are my equals, people on the same level as me. My colleagues are not 11th house: they are colleagues, not friends. If I happen to befriend one among them, that person would become 11th house, although remaining 7th in the context of most questions I might ask about my job. It is as if we were members of a troupe of actors. That I enjoy the company of this actor when we are off-stage is irrelevant to the roles we play in the drama. 我的同事是 7 宫。他们是我的平级，与我处于同一水平的人。我的同事不是 11 宫：他们是同事，不是朋友。如果我恰好与其中一人成为朋友，那个人会成为 11 宫，尽管在我可能问及工作的多数问题情境中，他仍然保持 7 宫属性。这就 像我们是一个剧团的成员。在台下我享受与这位演员的陪伴，这与我们在戏剧中 扮演的角色无关。

My subordinates, those below me in the pecking-order, are 6th house: my servants. 我的下属，那些在等级秩序中在我之下的人，是 6 宫：我的仆人。

Will I keep the job? 我能保住工作吗？

The first thing to look for here is fixity. The angles, Lord 1 or Lord 10 in a fixed sign is a strong argument for the situation staying as it is, so the querent keeps the job. The Moon void of course says the same. 这里首先要看的是固定性。四轴点、1 宫主或 10 宫主落在固定星座，是现状将 持续的有力论据，因此问卜者能保住工作。空亡月亮也说明同样的情况。

### ✸Here, as always, there is no significance whatever in the nature of the sign on any

angle or any house cusp. Ignore this point about the angles being fixed. A void of course Moon is not a strong testimony and is easily overruled – unless it is either Lord 1 or Lord 10, in which case its going nowhere would be a clear Yes. ✷

### ✸在此，一如既往，任何四轴点或任何宫头星座的属性本身没有任何意义。忽

略关于四轴点落入固定星座这一点。空亡月亮并非有力征象，很容易被推翻—— 除非它恰好是 1 宫主或 10 宫主，在这种情况下，它停滞不前会是一个明确的肯 定答案。✷

Lord 1 or Lord 10 about to leave a sign is a strong argument that there will be change, so the job will not be kept. This is so even if the sign it is leaving is fixed. If it also loses dignity or enters debility as it moves, this is an even stronger testimony. I would not put much significance on the Moon, if it is the querent’s cosignificator, leaving its sign: this is more likely to show the worry that has precipitated the question.

1 宫主或 10 宫主即将离开一个星座，是情况将发生变化的强有力论据，因此工 作将无法保住。即使它所离开的星座是固定的，也是如此。如果它在移动过程中 还失去了尊贵地位或进入了衰弱状态，这就是一个更强的征象。如果月亮是问卜 者的共同征象星，我不会过于看重它离开其星座这一点：这更可能显示促使问卜 者提出问题的担忧。

We do not need an aspect to see either the querent keeping the job or losing it. If there is an aspect, it may well be significant. Look too at any past aspect between Lords 1 and 10: if they came together by opposition, the querent will not stay in the job. This does not tell us that the querent is leaving now, though: we would need to find another indicator to show us when. Example: perhaps Lords 1 and 10 came together by opposition with mutual reception by sign. The opposition says that the job will not last. Lord 1 or Lord 10 changing sign, and hence breaking the mutual reception, would be a likely indicator of the timing. 我们不需要一个相位来判断问卜者是保住还是失去工作。如果存在一个相位，它 很可能是有意义的。同时也要查看 1 宫主和 10 宫主之间过去的任何相位：如果 它们是通过对冲相位结合的，问卜者将不会留在工作中。但这并没有告诉我们问 卜者现在就离开：我们需要找到另一个指示器来告诉我们时间。例如：也许 1 宫主和 10 宫主通过对冲相位结合，并且有星座互溶关系。对冲相位表明工作不 会长久。1 宫主或 10 宫主改变星座，从而打破互溶关系，可能会是一个时间指 示。

Receptions between the job and the querent can be significant testimony: if the job likes the querent, it is more likely to keep him on. But this can be overruled by the considerations above. If it is a ‘me or him’ situation, the other candidate for dismissal will be Lord 7, and no matter how bad the querent’s position, if Lord 7 is in a worse it is the querent who will survive. But be alive to the possibility that the company may change its mind, laying off neither or both. 工作与问卜者之间的接纳关系可能是有力的征象：如果工作喜欢问卜者，就更可 能留住他。但这可能被上述考虑因素推翻。如果是一个“不是我走就是他走”的 局面，另一个可能被解雇的候选人将是 7 宫主，无论问卜者的处境多么糟糕，如 果 7 宫主的情况更糟，那么将是问卜者留下来。但要意识到公司可能改变主意， 两者都不解雇或两者都解雇的可能性。

It is worth casting the Part of Resignation & Dismissal, to see if that has anything to contribute. Lord 1 applying immediately to conjunct or oppose it would be strong testimony of losing the job. The Ascedant, 10th cusp or Lords 1 or 10 on Antares, star of cycles ending, suggests the same. 值得排出辞职与解雇点，看看它是否有所提示。1 宫主马上与之形成合相或对冲 的入相位，将是失去工作的有力征象。上升点、10 宫头或 1 宫主/10 宫主落在周 期终结之星——心宿二上，也暗示同样结果。

Do not regard what the company has told the querent as truth! The truth is in the chart.

切勿将公司告诉问卜者的话视为真相！真相在星盘中！

Will I get my job back? 我能找回原来的工作吗？

A common testimony here is Lord 1 or Lord 10 either retrograde or moving forward having recently been retrograde. Either way, it is travelling in the opposite direction to its recent direction, so if that recent direction has taken it out of the job, the return will bring it back in. Lord 1 re-entering either the 10th house, the sign on the 10th cusp or the other sign ruled by Lord 10 would be a conclusive testimony of recovery. Note that in ‘Will I get the job?’ Lord 1 entering the 10th house will not give a Yes; in ‘Will I get the job back?’ its re-entry will, because in this case there is a concrete context for its having been in the 10th: it was in the job (10th house), left in (moved out) and now is going to be in it again (re-entry). 这里一个常见的征象是 1 宫主或 10 宫主正在逆行，或是刚刚结束逆行开始顺行。 无论是哪种情况，它都在与其近期的运行方向相反的方向行进，因此，如果那个 近期的方向曾使它离开了工作，那么返回的方向将把它带回来。1 宫主重新进入 10 宫、10 宫头所在的星座、或 10 宫主守护的另一个星座，将是恢复工作的决定 性征象。请注意，在“我能得到这份工作吗？”的问题中，1 宫主进入 10 宫并 不会给出肯定的答案；而在“我能找回原来的工作吗？”的问题中，它的重新进 入则会，因为在此情况下，它“曾经在 10 宫”有一个具体的背景：它曾经在工 作（10 宫）中，离开了（移出），现在即将再次进入（重新进入）。

Lord 10 in the 1st is a strong positive testimony, as is an applying aspect between Lords 1 and 10. 10 宫主在 1 宫是一个强烈的积极征象，1 宫主与 10 宫主之间的入相位也是。

What will the job be like? 这份工作会是什么样的？

‘Should I take the job?’ and ‘Will I get the job?’ are not the same question. The first assumes that the job is, at least potentially, gettable. We do not need to look for an aspect, although if there is an aspect between job and querent its nature must be considered. If it is an opposition, for instance, the querent will regret taking the job or will not hold it for long. “我应该接受这份工作吗？”和“我能得到这份工作吗？”不是同一个问题。前 者假设这份工作至少是可能得到的。我们不需要寻找相位，尽管如果工作与问卜 者之间存在相位，必须考虑其性质。例如，如果是对冲相位，问卜者会后悔接受 了这份工作，或者无法长期保有。

Look at Lord 10, considering its strength, both essentially and accidentally. An essentially strong Lord 10 that is accidentally afflicted may show what is in essence a

good job being less able to be the nice number that it truly is because of external constraints. The nature of any affliction can often help us identify what the problem is. Perhaps Lord 10 is in 1st station: business is about to decline. Lords 7 and 10 are each in the other’s detriment: there is strife between the company and the querent’s putative co-workers. Applying opposition between Lord 10 and Lord 5 (which is the 8th from the 10th): the company is about to go bust (meet its death). Consider also the effects of any planets in the 10th house, especially those close to the cusp: the South Node or a malefic are warnings of trouble; a strong Jupiter would promise benefit. 审视 10 宫主，考虑其力量，包括先天品质和偶然品质。一个先天有力但偶然受 困的 10 宫主，可能显示本质上是一份好工作，但由于外部限制，无法完全展现 其真正美好的面貌。任何困阻的性质通常能帮助我们识别问题所在。也许 10 宫 主处于停滞：业务即将衰退。7 宫主和 10 宫主彼此位于对方的落陷位置：公司 与问卜者未来的同事之间存在冲突。10 宫主与 5 宫主（即 10 宫之 8 宫）形成入 相位对冲：公司即将破产（面临死亡）。同时也要考虑 10 宫内任何行星的影响， 尤其是靠近宫头的行星：南交点或一颗凶星是麻烦的警告；一颗强有力的木星则 预示利益。

Do not be unrealistic in what you expect to find: it can still be a nice job without the company being a market leader, and ‘good enough’ is the answer here more often than ‘wonderful’. Neither should you expect to find Lord 10 showing any liking for the querent by reception (see above). If it does, this is a bonus. 不要对你期望发现的东西抱有不切实际的想法：即使公司不是市场领导者，工作 依然可能不错，而且答案往往是“足够好”，而不是“棒极了”。你也不应期望 发现 10 宫主通过接纳关系显示出对问卜者的任何喜欢（见上文）。如果确实有， 那是一个额外的好处。

Pay special attention to the condition of Lord 11, the pay. Try to identify any afflictions to Lord 1 from the list of office-staff above, e.g. opposition from Lord 7: ‘You won’t get along with your workmates’. 要特别关注 11 宫主（薪资）的状况。尝试从上述“办公室人员”列表中识别出 对 1 宫主的任何困阻，例如来自 7 宫主的对冲：“你将与同事相处不融洽”。

You can mentally pick up the querent’s significator and place it just inside the 10th cusp, thus sending it to work. How is it there? If in strong essential dignity, it is happy; if debilitated, it is not. Accidental dignity or debility may be important too. Perhaps it is cazimi there: ‘You’ll be the boss’s blue-eyed boy’ (cazimi: ‘like a man raised up to sit beside the king’). Perhaps it is conjunct a weak Saturn: there will be problems, which looking at what Saturn signifies in that chart may enable you to identify. As ‘Should I take the job?’ is often as much an emotional as a rational decision, it is often more important to drop the Moon into the 10th, sending the querent’s emotions to work. Be careful: if you are doing this you cannot say, ‘It’s in the 10th, so it’s strong’. That would be the case with any job. 你可以在想象中拿起问卜者的征象星，将它正好放入 10 宫头内侧，从而送它去 工作。它在那边感觉如何？如果处于强力的先天尊贵位置，它是快乐的；如果处

于衰弱状态，则不然。偶然尊贵或衰弱也可能很重要。也许它在那里处于日核位 置：“你会成为老板的宠儿”（日核：“如同被提拔起来坐在国王身边的人”）。 也许它与一颗衰弱的土星合相：将会出现问题，通过查看土星在那个星盘中的征 象，你或许能够识别出问题所在。由于“我应该接受这份工作吗？”常常既是情 感决定也是理性决定，因此更重要的往往是把月亮放入 10 宫，送问卜者的情感 去工作。小心：如果你这样做，你不能说“它在 10 宫，所以它有力”。这对于 任何工作来说都是成立的。

### ✸As always, be careful with assumptions. We might assume that the low wages

shown by a debilitated Lord 11 would be off-putting, but the money might not be important: perhaps the querent is more interested in polishing up the cv or likes the idea of working in the wildlife park. Ask the querent and check the evidence in the chart. For instance, if Lord 1 exalts Lord 2, money is an important issue, so the querent will not be happy working in a job that doesn’t pay.✷

### ✸一如既往，要小心假设。我们可能假设，一颗衰弱的 11 宫主所显示的低薪会

令人望而却步，但金钱可能并不重要：也许问卜者更感兴趣的是完善简历，或者 喜欢在野生动物公园工作的想法。询问问卜者，并核对星盘中的证据。例如，如 果 1 宫主位于 2 宫主的旺势位置，那么金钱就是一个重要问题，因此问卜者不会 乐于从事一份报酬不高的工作。✷

The next job 下一份工作

‘Should I pack this job in and go to work for so-and-so?’ With this and similar questions we need to distinguish between the present and the possible future job. In most cases we can take the sign on the 10th cusp and its ruler to show the present job and the next sign round in the order of the zodiac (anticlockwise) and its ruler to show the next job. Consider them as in ‘What will the job be like?’ above. “我应该辞掉现在这份工作，去为某某人工作吗？”对于这个问题以及类似问题， 我们需要区分当前工作和未来可能的工作。在大多数情况下，我们可以用 10 宫 头所在的星座及其守护星代表当前工作，用沿黄道顺序（逆时针方向）的下一个 星座及其守护星代表下一份工作。按照上文“这份工作会是什么样的？”中的方 法来考虑它们。

Be flexible! Suppose the MC is at 2 Gemini and the querent has held the present job for years. The long time spent in that job does not fit with only 2 degrees of that sign having passed the MC. In this case it would make sense to regard Taurus as the present job and Gemini as the next one, as if the querent were mentally already in it. Always be open to what the chart is trying to tell you. 要灵活！假设中天在双子座 2 度，而问卜者从事当前工作已多年。在该星座仅 2 度经过中天的情况下，却已工作了很长时间，这与星象不符。在这种情况下，将

金牛座视为当前工作、双子座视为下一份工作是有意义的，就好像问卜者在心理 上已经进入了下一份工作。永远对星盘试图传达给你的信息保持开放态度。

If Lord 1 is about to change sign this will show the proposed change of job, even if neither its present not its next sign has any connection with the 10th house. The chart is showing change; the change under discussion is a change of job: this must be the change shown by the chart. Is the planet stronger in the next sign, or weaker? This will usually be judged by essential dignity, but sometimes accidentals are in play. Suppose that as soon as the significator enters the new sign it becomes combust: ‘Stay where you are!’ 如果 1 宫主即将改变星座，这将显示所提议的工作变动，即使它当前和下一个所 在的星座与 10 宫都无关。星盘显示的是变化；所讨论的变化是工作变动：这必 定是星盘所显示的变化。该行星在下一个星座是更强了，还是更弱了？这通常通 过先天尊贵来判断，但有时偶然品质也起作用。假设征象星一进入新星座就变得 燃烧：“待在原地别动！”

Is the company I work for going bust? 我工作的公司会倒闭吗？

This translates as ‘Is the company going to die?’ and should be judged accordingly. Treat it exactly as if the company were a person, following the method described in chapter 20. 这等同于“公司会‘死亡’吗？”，并应据此进行判断。将公司完全视为一个人 来对待，遵循第 20 章描述的方法。

Vocational questions 职业的问题

I strongly advise that you do not accept such questions without requiring the querent to come up with some options. So great is the variety of jobs that unless you do this whatever answer you produce will say more about the limits of your imagination than about the querent’s vocational aptitude. Sometimes the question will be phrased as ‘I want to be a movie-star, but maybe I should stick to accountancy’; even if it is not, provided that the querent gives us some clues, we can feed possibilities into the chart to see which holds the best prospects. 我强烈建议，除非问卜者能提出一些选项，否则不要接受此类问题。工作种类如 此繁多，除非你这样做，否则你给出的任何答案都更多地反映了你想象力的局限， 而不是问卜者的职业倾向。有时问题会表述为“我想成为电影明星，但也许我应 该坚持做会计”；即使不是这样，只要问卜者提供一些线索，我们就可以将可能 性代入星盘，看看哪个前景最好。

Once you have some options, look at the chart and find the planets that signify them,

working from house rulerships and the planets’ natural rulerships. For example, the acting career would be shown by Lord 5 and accountancy by Mercury. “But what if Lord 5 is Mercury?” The chart is tailored to the question, so Lord 5 will probably not be Mercury. If it is, the chart will provide another obvious indicator. Trust; it works. 一旦你有了几个选项，就查看星盘，根据宫位主宰关系和行星的自然主宰属性， 找出代表它们的行星。例如，演艺事业由 5 宫主代表，会计由水星代表。“但如 果 5 宫主就是水星呢？”星盘是为问题量身定制的，所以 5 宫主很可能不是水星。 如果是，星盘也会提供另一个明显的指示。相信它；这方法有效。

Once you have the significators, compare them, considering their own dignities (essential and accidental) and their receptions with Lord 1 and the Moon (taking the Moon as cosignificator of the querent, with particular reference to the querent’s emotions). Be careful when considering dignities: if a testimony is descriptive, treat it as such and do not regard it as debilitating. Suppose the querent wants to be a blacksmith: Saturn in Aries would be an ideal astrological job description, so we would ignore Saturn’s being in fall there. But Saturn being retrograde would be a problem – unless the querent were intent on reviving lost smithing skills, or had some other aim (resurrecting an ancestral business, perhaps) that rendered the retrogradation entirely suitable. 一旦你确定了征象星，就比较它们，考虑其自身的尊贵（先天和偶然）以及它们 与 1 宫主和月亮（将月亮作为问卜者的共同征象星，特别指向问卜者的情感）的 接纳关系。考虑尊贵时要小心：如果一个征象是描述性的，就按描述性对待，不 要视为衰弱。假设问卜者想成为一名铁匠：土星在白羊座将是一个理想的占星学 职业描述，因此我们会忽略土星在那里处于弱势。但土星逆行会是个问题——除 非问卜者一心想要复兴失传的打铁技艺，或有其他目标（或许是复兴祖传生意）， 使得逆行变得完全合适。

Pay great attention to the receptions between the significator of the job and those of the querent. If the question is about earning a wage with no concern for how congenial the job might be, we do not need to concern ourselves with querent/job compatibility. This question is usually about job suitability, so the greater the level of mutual reception between querent and job, the better. 要非常关注工作征象星与问卜者征象星之间的接纳关系。如果问题只关心赚取工 资，不关心工作是否合意，我们就不需要考虑问卜者/工作的兼容性。而此类问 题通常关乎工作是否适合，因此问卜者与工作之间的互溶程度越高越好。

“Where’s the money in this?” If you are choosing a planet for the job because it is the appropriate house ruler (e.g. Lord 5 for acting), use the 2nd house from that house to show the wages. If you are choosing a planet for its own indications (Mercury for accountancy, Saturn for grave-digging) take the 2nd sign from the sign that planet is in. So if the querent wants to be a couturier (Venus) and Venus is in Sagittarius, you would take the 2nd sign from there (1st from Sagittarius is Sagittarius; 2nd is Capricorn) and its ruler to show the wages. “这行的钱景如何？”如果你因为某个行星是恰当的宫主星而选择它代表工作

（例如，5 宫主代表演艺事业），则使用该宫之 2 宫来代表薪资。如果你根据行 星自身的指示选择它（水星代表会计，土星代表掘墓人），则取该行星所在星座 之后的第二个星座。因此，如果问卜者想成为一名女装设计师（金星），而金星 在射手座，你就取射手座之后的第二个星座（射手座之后第 1 个星座是射手座本 身；第 2 个是摩羯座）及其守护星来代表薪资。

For a general question with no possible vocations suggested by the querent, consider Mercury, Venus and Mars, taking the strongest of them to signify the vocation. Broadly, Mercury shows brainwork, Mars works with muscle, Venus works by charm or aesthetics. Take further description from sign, house and close aspects. Accidental debilities often show description rather than disadvantage. For example, strong Mars in the 7th (open enemies): go and be a soldier. In the 6th (illness): be a surgeon. In the 12th (large animals): join the cavalry. Mars opposing Saturn (buildings): be a demolition worker. 对于问卜者没有提出任何具体职业可能性的笼统问题，可以考虑水星、金星和火 星，取其中最强的行星来象征职业。大致而言，水星代表脑力工作，火星代表体 力工作，金星代表依靠魅力或美学的工作。进一步的描述则来自星座、宫位和紧 密相位。偶然衰弱常常是描述性的而非不利的。例如，有力的火星在 7 宫（公开 敌人）：去当兵。在 6 宫（疾病）：当外科医生。在 12 宫（大型动物）：加入 骑兵。火星对冲土星（建筑）：当拆迁工人。

Especially if you have no clear answer from the above, it can be worth casting the Part of Vocation. Consider the Part itself and, especially, its dispositor. 特别是如果从上述方法得不到明确答案时，排出职业点是值得的。考虑该点本身， 尤其是它的定位星。

Do bear in mind the obvious: many careers that are open at 20 are not open at 50. Read the chart in that light. 一定要记住显而易见的一点：许多 20 岁时开放的职业道路，在 50 岁时并不开放。 要基于此来解读星盘。

We are sometimes asked about someone else’s career. This is usually as a subsidiary question to ‘When will I meet the man I will marry?’ In this case, take the turned 10th house and its ruler. 我们有时会被问到关于他人的职业。这通常是“我什么时候会遇到我将要嫁的 人？”的一个附带问题。在这种情况下，取转宫 10 宫及其守护星。

We cannot use that person’s main significator to describe the job, because the main significator will describe that person. This would imply that, for instance, everyone who’s built like a soldier becomes a soldier. Nor can we take the strongest of Mercury, Venus and Mars, because this would be the same for both the other person and the querent. Note that we did not consider Lord 10 when finding the querent’s vocation. This is because the 10th house shows what the person does do, rather than what they should do. With ‘What will my future husband do for a living?’ it is what he does do

that concerns us. 我们不能用那个人的主要征象星来描述工作，因为主要征象星描述的是那个人本 身。这将意味着，例如，每个体格像军人的人都会成为军人。我们也不能取水星、 金星和火星中最强的那颗，因为这颗星对他人和问卜者会是相同的。注意，在寻 找问卜者的职业时，我们没有考虑 10 宫主。这是因为 10 宫显示的是一个人实际 从事的工作，而不是他们应该从事的工作。对于“我未来的丈夫将以什么为生？” 这样的问题，我们关心的是他实际做什么。

Follow the usual clues for linking planet to job. Keep your judgements broad: precision has its place in horary, but that place is not here. ‘Something artistic’ is a better answer to this question than ‘Second viola in the London Symphony Orchestra’. 遵循通常的线索来将行星与工作联系起来。判断要保持宽泛：精确性在卜卦占星 中有其位置，但这里不是。“某种艺术类工作”是对此问题比“伦敦交响乐团第 二中提琴手”更好的答案。

Although we cannot take the profession from the person’s main significator, the main significator can rule out possibilities. If we have decided, from Lord 7, that the future husband is a skinny little guy, he will not be working as a black-smith. If his Lord 10 suggests that he is, we will have to think of another job that it might describe. 虽然我们不能从一个人的主要征象星推断职业，但主要征象星可以排除某些可能 性。如果我们根据 7 宫主已判定未来的丈夫是个瘦小的人，他就不会当铁匠。如 果他的 10 宫主暗示他是，我们就得想想它可能描述的另一种工作。

### ✸When the querent is deciding between specific job-offers, it can sometimes be as

simple as is described above: ‘Should I take the job as bank-clerk or as window-dresser?’ gives us the choice of Mercury or Venus. More often the querent is choosing between different companies offering similar jobs. By asking the querent what distinguishes the jobs, you will find which planets signify each of them. The choice between the big company and the high-tech company would be a choice between Jupiter and Mercury, for instance. This is just as with distinguishing between different properties (page 198, above).✷

### ✸当问卜者在特定的工作机会之间做决定时，有时可以像上面描述的那样简单：

“我应该接受银行职员的工作还是橱窗装饰师的工作？”这给了我们水星或金星 的选择。更多时候，问卜者是在提供类似工作的不同公司之间选择。通过询问问 卜者这些工作的区别，你将发现哪些行星分别代表它们。例如，在大公司和高科 技公司之间的选择，就是在木星和水星之间的选择。这与区分不同房产的方法相 同（见上文第 319 页）。✷

Business partnerships 商业合伙关系

### ✸For the question ‘Should I take this person as a partner in my business?’ Use Lord

1 and the Moon for the querent, Lord 7 for the prospective partner, Lord 10 for the business and Lord 11 for the business’s profit. The question is about whether it’s a good idea, not whether it will happen, so no aspect is necessary. But if there is an aspect between querent and Lord 7, its nature must be considered. No matter how promising other testimonies might be, an opposition would not augur well.

### ✸对于“我应该和这个人成为生意伙伴吗？”的问题，用 1 宫主和月亮代表问

卜者，7 宫主代表潜在合伙人，10 宫主代表生意，11 宫主代表生意的利润。这 个问题是关于这是否是个好主意，而不是它是否会发生，因此不需要相位。但如 果问卜者的象征星与 7 宫主之间存在相位，必须考虑其性质。无论其他征象多么 有希望，对冲相位都不是好兆头。

Though I have yet to see a chart on this subject where other testimonies show even the smallest promise. It seems almost compulsory for the querent to exalt the partner, and for the condition of Lord 7 to show that the partner cannot even begin to meet these elevated expectations. In itself, this exaltation is not necessarily a problem. The querent may think the partner has super-powers, but if the business does not demand super-powers the lack of them may not become apparent. Nonetheless, this unrealistic assessment of the other person, perfectly normal at the start of a romantic relationship, is not a sound basis for a working partnership. 不过我尚未见过关于此主题的星盘中有其他征象显示出哪怕一丝的希望。问卜者 旺势合伙人似乎几乎是必然的，而 7 宫主的状况则显示合伙人甚至无法开始满足 这些被抬高的期望。就其本身而言，这种旺势不一定是个问题。问卜者可能认为 合伙人拥有超能力，但如果生意不需要超能力，那么缺乏超能力可能不会显现出 来。然而，这种对他人不切实际的评估，虽然在浪漫关系开始时完全正常，却不 是工作伙伴关系的可靠基础。

Pay attention to the balance of power, not only as shown by the receptions between querent and Lord 7, but by the receptions and placement of Lord 10. Suppose Lord 10 is tucked just inside the 7th house, completely under the partner’s control. Possibly this could be acceptable if the querent intended to step back and let the partner run things, but not otherwise. Then check the receptions between Lord 7 and both Lord 10 and Lord 11. We would hope to find indications of the partner favouring them: being in good dignity of theirs, while also having sufficient strength to be able to help. I have yet to see this, though. ✷ 要注意权力的平衡，不仅要看问卜者与 7 宫主之间的接纳关系，还要看 10 宫主 的接纳关系和位置。假设 10 宫主正好紧贴 7 宫头内侧，完全在合伙人的控制之 下。如果问卜者打算退居幕后让合伙人经营，这可能可以接受，否则就不行。然 后检查 7 宫主与 10 宫主及 11 宫主之间的接纳关系。我们希望能找到合伙人有利 于它们的迹象：处于它们的良好尊贵位置，同时自身也有足够的力量来提供帮助。 不过，我至今还没见过这种情况。✷

# Eleventh House Questions

# 11 宫的问题

WILL I GET MY WISH? 我会如愿吗？

Our forebears devoted much ink to the problem of what we should do when the querent refuses to specify the question, insisting instead on ‘Will I get this thing that I’m not going to tell you about?’ I strongly suggest that the response must be ‘If you won’t tell me the question, I’ll do the chart, but won’t tell you the answer’.
