Always remember that it’s easier for you to find another client than it is for the client to find another good astrologer. 我们的前辈们曾花费大量笔墨探讨一个问题：当问卜者拒绝明确说明问题，只是 坚持问“我会得到那个我不想告诉你的事情吗？”时，我们该如何应对。我强烈 建议，回答必须是“如果你不告诉我问题，我会排盘，但不会告诉你答案”。永 远记住，对你而言，找到另一个客户比客户找到另一个好的占星师要容易得多。

Once you have a certain number of horaries under your belt, you will begin to recognise what charts on certain subjects look like. Most notably, you will be able to spot the love question that masquerades as something else. It is not unusual for questions about moving home or job advancement to have their real theme as, in simple terms, ‘Does he love me?’ If the querent doesn’t ask, my opinion is that we should not answer; but we can gently nudge the querent to see if she wishes to open this issue. 一旦你手头有了一定数量的卜卦案例，你就会开始认识到特定主题的星盘是什么 样子的。最明显的是，你将能够识别出那些伪装成其他问题的爱情疑问。关于搬 家或工作晋升的问题，其真实主题简单地说是“他爱我吗？”，这并不罕见。如 果问卜者没有问，我的意见是我们不应回答；但我们可以温和地引导问卜者，看 她是否愿意公开这个问题。

HOW MUCH IS MY TAX BILL？ 我的税金会有多少？

The government is 10th house, its coffers are 11th. These charts will usually show an

applying aspect between Lord 2 (querent’s money) and either Lord 10 or Lord 11. Consider the receptions, checking to see what Lords 10 and 11 – with special emphasis on whichever of them is making the aspect to Lord 2 – think of the querent’s money. The more the taxman loves it, the more of it he will want. If he exalts Lord 2, it is a sign that he overestimates how much the querent has, or, at least, how much is owed. 政府是 10 宫，其金库是 11 宫。这类星盘通常会显示 2 宫主（问卜者的钱财）与 10 宫主或 11 宫主之间形成入相位。要考量接纳关系，特别检查 10 宫主和 11 宫 主——尤其是其中正与 2 宫主形成相位的那一颗——如何看待问卜者的钱财。征 税者越喜爱它，他想拿走的就越多。如果他对 2 宫主呈旺势接纳，这是一个迹象， 表明他高估了问卜者拥有的金额，或者至少是高估了所欠的税款。

If finding the government or its coffers love the querent’s money (in the sign of Lord
2) is bad news, finding this love is reciprocated is encouraging. A strong mutual reception between them will reduce the bill. It is like the movies where the hero loves her, but gallantly sends her back to someone else: the mutual reception shows that even though the taxman wants the money, he will reduce his demands. 如果发现政府或其金库喜爱问卜者的钱财（在 2 宫主入庙的星座）是个坏消息， 那么发现这种爱意得到回应则令人鼓舞。它们之间强烈的互溶关系会减少账单金 额。这就像电影里英雄爱她，却大度地将她送回别人身边：互溶关系表明，即使 征税者想要钱，他也会降低要求。

Consider also any other forthcoming afflictions to Lord 2, and Lord 2’s strength, which will show how capable the querent’s purse is of surviving the taxman’s predations (such questions are usually asked in extremis!). 还要考虑任何其他即将对 2 宫主造成的刑克，以及 2 宫主的力量，这将显示问卜 者的钱包在征税者的掠夺下存活的能力如何（这类问题通常是在万不得已之时提 出的！）。

VISAS AND PERMITS 签证和许可证

### ✸The 11th, being the 2nd from the 10th, shows the king’s possessions, and so ‘the

gift of the king’: that treasure we would like to be granted. As such, it is the house for questions about entry visas and residence permits.

### ✸11 宫，作为 10 宫的 2 宫，代表国王的财产，因此是“国王的礼物”：即我

们希望被赐予的财富。因此，它是关于入境签证和居留许可问题的宫位。

“Whose king?” If the querent is already in the country, the king is the king of that country, and so is 10th house. This regardless of the querent’s nationality, citizenship

or status. If the querent is not in that country, the king in question is that of a foreign country. The foreign country is 9th, so its king is the radical 6th (10th from 9th = 6th). In that case, the king’s gift would be the 2nd from there, which is the radical 7th. If the querent is applying for entry to a country that shares a border with his own, one could argue that that country is 3rd house, as his neighbour. That is, I think, a little fanciful; stick with the 9th. “谁的国王？” 如果问卜者已经在目标国家，那么国王就是该国的国王，因此 是 10 宫。这与问卜者的国籍、公民身份或地位无关。如果问卜者不在那个国家， 那么相关的国王就是外国的国王。外国是 9 宫，所以其国王就是基准盘的 6 宫（9 宫的 10 宫 = 6 宫）。在这种情况下，国王的礼物就是那里的 2 宫，也就是基准 盘的 7 宫。如果问卜者申请进入一个与他自己国家接壤的国家，有人可能会争辩 说那个国家是 3 宫，作为他的邻居。我认为这有点异想天开；坚持用 9 宫。

What we hope to see is an applying aspect between Lord 1 or the Moon and the significator of the gift. An aspect with the king himself is less convincing, but will usually work, as long as it isn’t an opposition. The reality of the situation means that the receptions of the king’s significator are unlikely to be of importance. Unless there are strong and known issues – the querent is a notorious gangster or has recently kicked the king’s cat – he will be just one more unknown name towards which the king will have no attitude. Reality, too, will tell us if the application is a formality, to which rejection would be an exception, or a grail that few achieve. If a formality, the absence of a negative (such as an applying, but prohibited, aspect between querent and gift) would be sufficient to judge Yes. If the grail, we would need not only the aspect but some reception to show why our querent has been selected above all others. 我们希望看到的是 1 宫主或月亮与礼物的征象星之间形成入相位。与国王本身的 相位说服力较弱，但通常也有效，只要不是对冲相位。实际情况意味着国王的征 象星的接纳关系不太可能重要。除非存在强烈且已知的问题——例如问卜者是个 臭名昭著的匪徒或最近踢了国王的猫——否则他只是又一个陌生的名字，国王对 其不会有任何态度。现实情况也会告诉我们，这份申请是走个形式（拒绝属于例 外），还是少数人才能获得的圣杯。如果是走形式，只要没有负面因素（例如问 卜者与礼物之间虽有入相位但被阻碍），就足以判断为“是”。如果是圣杯，我 们不仅需要相位，还需要一些接纳关系来显示为何我们的问卜者能在所有人中脱 颖而出。

In many such charts, though, the aspect to the gift itself is not needed. If we can show that the querent makes the journey (aspect with Lord 9) this will usually imply that the entry visa has been granted. If we can show that the querent is staying put in the country where he seeks to reside, this will usually imply that residence has been granted. ‘Usually’, because other options are available. But if the qurent were considering those options it is unlikely the question would have been asked.✷ 然而，在许多此类星盘中，并不需要与礼物本身有相位。如果我们能显示问卜者 会踏上旅程（与 9 宫主有相位），这通常意味着入境签证已被批准。如果我们能 显示问卜者会留在他寻求居住的国家，这通常意味着居留许可已被批准。说“通 常”，是因为还有其他可能。但如果问卜者当时在考虑那些其他可能，问题就不

太可能会被提出。✷

# Twelfth House Questions

# 12 宫的问题

WITCHCRAFT AND IMPRISONMENT 巫术与监禁

Am I bewitched? 我被下咒了吗？

For all that this might seem a question occurring only in dusty texts from days long past, it is asked, and not infrequently. Sometimes by querents whose culture has a different view of witchcraft than our own; sometimes by those who have dabbled beyond their depth; most often in modern guise: ‘Am I under psychic attack?’ or ‘Is he controlling my thoughts?’ being the usual contemporary framing of what is essentially the same question. 尽管这问题看上去只属于尘封已久的过往文献，但它确实被提出，且并非罕见。 有时是来自文化中对巫术看法与我们不同的问卜者；有时是那些涉足过深、不自 量力之人；而现代最常见的表述则是：“我正遭受精神攻击吗？”或“他是否在 控制我的思想？”，这实质上是同一问题的当代版本。

We must always be open to the querent’s world-view, no matter how bizarre it might seem to us. While the astrologer who does not recognize that ‘there are more things in Heaven and Earth’ than his preconceptions allow will be a poor astrologer, there is yet a dividing line between those of different views and those who are crazy, looking only for someone to latch on to. It is well to develop a nose for these, as once admitted into your working life it can take a disproportionate amount of time and effort to usher them through the exit. 我们必须始终对问卜者的世界观保持开放态度，无论它在我们看来多么怪异。虽 然那些不认同“天地间存在远超其预想之事”的占星师不会是好的占星师，但在 不同观点者与纯粹疯狂、只想找人依附者之间，仍有一条界线。最好能培养出对 后者的嗅觉，因为一旦让其进入你的工作生活，可能需要花费不成比例的时间和 精力才能将其请出。

It is the nature of the assault that makes this a 12th house issue, not whether the querent knows the supposed assailant’s name. If the question is ‘Is Albert psychically

attacking me?’ it is a 12th-house matter. Remember: in the past when querents would ask ‘Am I bewitched?’ they would usually know the identity of the village witch who was supposedly hexing their cattle. In certain specific circumstances, if the accused has a particular relationship to the querent, you will need to check that house (‘Has my ex-lover put a spell on me?’). Usually, however, we can go straight to the 12th. 问题的性质使之成为 12 宫议题，与问卜者是否知道所谓攻击者的姓名无关。如 果问题是“Albert（阿尔伯特）是否在精神上攻击我？”，这便是一个 12 宫事务。 请记住：在过去，当问卜者问“我是否被施了巫术？”时，他们通常知道所谓对 其牲畜下咒的村中巫婆的身份。在某些特定情况下，如果被指控者与问卜者有特 殊关系，你需要查看相关宫位（“我的前任是否对我下了咒？”）。然而，通常 我们可以直接查看 12 宫。

The major testimonies of bewitchment are: 被下咒的主要征象包括：

* the same planet rules both 1st and 12th houses
* 同一颗行星同时守护 1 宫和 12 宫

* close contact between Lords 1 and 12.
* 1 宫主与 12 宫主之间存在紧密联系。

Look at the receptions: as ever, these will hold the key. If Lord 12 is ruled by Lord 1, the querent is not bewitched: the querent has power over the supposed witch. If Lord 1 is ruled by Lord 12, remember that the supposition of witchcraft can be enough to give that person power over the native, without the suspect having done anything. A contact with Lord 12 is much more convincing. An applying aspect between Lords 1 and 12 is not evidence. An applying aspect shows something in the future, and the question is not ‘Will I be bewitched?’ 查看接纳关系：一如以往，这些关系是关键所在。如果 12 宫主被 1 宫主定位， 则问卜者未被施术：问卜者对所谓的巫师拥有力量。如果 1 宫主被 12 宫主定位， 请记住，仅仅是巫术的臆想便足以让那个人对盘主产生影响力，而无须嫌疑人实 际采取任何行动。若与 12 宫主形成相位则更具说服力。1 宫主与 12 宫主之间的 入相位并非证据。入相位显示未来之事，而问题并非“我将会被施巫术吗？”

### ✸Ignore the point about the same planet ruling both 1st and 12th houses. With no

other type of question is there any significance in finding the same planet ruling both relevant houses; nor is there any significance in it here. This idea has been created by astrologers trying to scratch up some testimony in charts for questions which, by their nature, are unusually opaque. The astrologer who agrees with the querent that witchcraft is a likely explanation for the cow having died will, of course, be inclined to hunt for testimony that might support that explanation.✷

### ✸请忽略关于同一颗行星守护 1 宫和 12 宫的说法。在其他任何类型的问题中，

发现同一颗行星守护两个相关宫位都没有特殊意义；在此处也同样没有意义。这 个观点是由一些占星师创造的，他们试图在那些本质上异常晦涩的问题的星盘中， 勉强寻找一些征象。当然，那些赞同问卜者认为巫术是奶牛死亡的可能解释的占 星师，自然会倾向于寻找可能支持该解释的征象。✷

【Bewitchment is not necessarily a 12th-house matter. - Posted on March 7th, 2014 【蛊惑未必是 12 宫的事 - 发布于 2014 年 3 月 7 日

So don’t be in a hurry to run to the 12th when the querent speaks of such. For example, as Shakespeare tells us, ‘what a hell of witchcraft lies/ In the small orb of one particular tear!’ (Lover’s Complaint, 288-9). That I may feel myself bewitched does not mean that somebody has deliberately put a spell upon me.】 所以，当问卦者提到此类事情时，不要急于跑到 12 宫去。例如，正如 Shakespeare （莎士比亚）告诉我们的，“那小小一滴眼泪的晶莹球体/蕴含着多么地狱般的 蛊惑力量！”（《情女怨》，第 288-9 行）。我可能感觉自己被蛊惑了，这并不 意味着有人故意对我施了咒。】

Am I harming myself? 我是否在伤害自己？

The 12th is the house of self-undoing, and so is the relevant house in questions about addictions and other harmful practices. If the querent asks, for example, ‘Is my drinking harming me, and how?’ it is a 12th-house matter. Any idea that it might be 5th-house (pleasure) is dispelled by the nature of the question. Look to Lord 12: is it nice or nasty? Remember that even benefic planets in detriment or fall are nasty. What is its relationship to Lord 1? A weak planet with power over Lord 1 (e.g. Lord 1 in sign of Lord 12) is testimony that the vice has power over the querent. The stronger the reception, the more the power (e.g. Lord 1 in a face ruled by Lord 12: the power is small). 12 宫是自我毁灭之宫，因此也是涉及成瘾及其他有害行为问题的相关宫位。例 如，若问卜者问：“我的饮酒习惯是否正在伤害我，以及如何伤害？”，这便是 12 宫事务。任何认为这可能属于 5 宫（愉悦）的想法，都会被问题的性质所否 定。查看 12 宫主：它是吉还是凶？记住，即使是落入落陷或弱势的吉星也是凶 恶的。它与 1 宫主的关系如何？一颗虚弱但对 1 宫主有掌控力的行星（例如，1 宫主位于 12 宫主掌管的星座），便是此恶习掌控问卜者的征象。接纳关系越强， 掌控力越大（例如，1 宫主位于 12 宫主掌管的得面：掌控力微小）。

The mode of the sign will show how stubborn will be the problem: a fixed sign shows it is a long-term issue; mutable, that it will come and go; cardinal, that it may be a problem now, but won’t be for long. Where is Lord 1 going? Leaving a fixed sign where it is ruled by Lord 12 for a mutable where it is not: the querent is finding a way out of this problem. Leaving a cardinal sign where it is under minor rulership of Lord 12 (term or face, maybe) for a fixed sign where it is in major dignity of Lord 12: the

querent thinks the problem is under control, but is falling more seriously into its grasp. 星座的模式将显示问题的顽固程度：固定星座表明这是长期问题；变动星座表明 它会时有时无；基本星座表明现在可能是个问题，但不会持久。1 宫主正去往何 处？从它被 12 宫主定位的固定星座，移动到一个不被其定位的变动星座：问卜 者正在寻找摆脱此问题的方法。从一个受 12 宫主次要定位（可能是得界或得面） 的基本星座，移动到一个受 12 宫主主要尊贵定位的固定星座：问卜者认为问题 已受控制，但实际上正更深地陷入其掌控。

### ✸I would urge caution with such questions, especially when the querent is asking

about somebody else. Do not assume that it is a 12th-house matter. Consider: a querent asked ‘Is my husband an alcoholic?’ The phrasing is unhelpful, because the use of a label rather than of a description points us straight to the 12th house. If the matter were so clear-cut, it is unlikely the question would have been asked, at least as it is phrased here.

### ✷对于此类问题，我建议保持谨慎，尤其是当问卜者在询问他人情况时。不要

假定它一定是 12 宫事务。试想：一位问卜者问“我丈夫是个酒鬼吗？”这种措 辞并无帮助，因为使用标签而非描述性语言，直接指向了 12 宫。如果事情如此 明确，问题就不太可能被提出，至少不会以这里的措辞方式提出。

Suppose the querent thought hubby was eating more than was good for him. It’s unlikely she would have used a labelling-type word in her question, but would have asked ‘Is he eating too much?’ In which case we would not have looked at the 12th, but at the 2nd (the throat and what goes into it). If hubby has been to AA for the past three years and she now suspects he has fallen off the wagon, there is a known issue, so the question might reasonably be phrased as asked. Just as if he were stuffing himself with cake then making himself vomit, she might ask ‘Is he bulimic?’ That would be a 12th-house matter. More often, the question is better approached as ‘Is what he is putting down his throat harming him?’ which is 2nd house (turned 2nd, of course, when asked about someone else). Of particular importance would be the receptions of Lord 2. Lord 7 is ruled by Lord 8, which is in the detriment of Lord 7:‘Yes, what your husband’s drinking certainly is harming him’. 假设问卜者认为丈夫吃得太多，不利于健康。她不太可能在问题中使用标签式的 词语，而会问“他是不是吃得太多了？”那样的话，我们就不会看 12 宫，而是 看 2 宫（喉咙及摄入之物）。如果丈夫过去三年一直参加匿名戒酒会，而她现在 怀疑他再次酗酒，这是一个已知的问题，那么问题以所问的方式提出或许是合理 的。同样，如果他暴食蛋糕然后催吐，她可能会问“他患有贪食症吗？”那将是 12 宫事务。但更多时候，将问题视为“他摄入喉咙的东西是否正在伤害他？” 来处理更好，这属于 2 宫事务（当询问他人时，当然是转宫 2 宫）。2 宫主的接 纳关系将尤为重要。如果 7 宫主被 8 宫主定位，而 8 宫主处于 7 宫主的落陷位置： “是的，你丈夫的饮酒无疑正在伤害他”。

The question is not necessarily about excess, so don’t be too ready to assume such. If the querent has been warned off alcohol for medical reasons, for instance, he might be wondering if a glass of wine with his Sunday dinner will really do him so much harm. 问题不一定关乎过量，因此不要轻易做此假设。例如，如果问卜者因医疗原因被 警告戒酒，他可能想知道周日晚餐时喝一杯葡萄酒是否真的对他有如此大的危害。

The problem of choosing the right house here reveals the limitation of the methaphor of chart as theatre. In the chart, Lord 12 will always be there, regardless of whether it is involved in the drama. If we are watching Romeo and Juliet, we don’t see Macbeth hanging around at the back of the stage in case he gets the opportunity to join in. We run the risk here of assuming the answer in our approach to the question.✷ 在此选择正确宫位的问题，揭示了将星盘比喻为剧场的局限性。在星盘中，12 宫主总是存在，无论它是否参与剧情。如果我们在看《罗密欧与朱丽叶》，并不 会看到 Macbeth（麦克白）在舞台后方徘徊，等待机会加入。在此，我们面临的 风险是，在分析问题时就已假定了答案。✷

Imprisonment 监禁

Questions of whether someone will be sent to get out of prison are usually straightforward. Remember that if the querent is asking about someone else, we must consider both the turned and radical 12th houses. It is important that you know whether the person is already in prison or not. 关于某人是否会被送入或离开监狱的问题通常比较直接。记住，如果问卜者询问 的是他人，我们必须同时考虑转宫 12 宫和基准盘的 12 宫。了解此人是否已在狱 中至关重要。

Imprisonment is often shown simply: the person’s significator on the cusp of the 12th (or turned 12th) house. The planet about to enter the house of imprisonment is a compelling testimony that the person will follow suit. If the planet turns retrograde before entering the house, it shows that no matter how certain imprisonment might seem the person will go free. 监禁通常有简单的显示：当事人的征象星位于 12 宫（或转宫 12 宫）宫头。一颗 即将进入监禁宫位的行星，是此人将步此后尘的有力征象。如果该行星在进入宫 位前转为逆行，则表明无论入狱看起来多么确定，此人终将获释。

When the person is on remand, it is usual to find his significator already in the 12th: he is already in prison. If its condition is about to worsen, perhaps by aspecting a malefic planet or by losing essential dignity, he will be committed. The chart is showing that the person’s condition is worsening, in a way fitting the context of the question. We might judge the same if the significator, in the 12th, were moving from a cardinal to a fixed sign. 当某人被还押候审时，通常会发现其征象星已在 12 宫内：他已在狱中。如果其

状态即将恶化，例如与凶星形成相位或失去先天尊贵，他将被定罪收监。星盘显 示此人的状况正在恶化，其方式符合问题的背景。如果征象星在 12 宫内从基本 星座移入固定星座，我们也可以做出同样判断。

An applying aspect with Lord 12 or Lord of the turned 12th would show the same. Another common indicator is the significator entering the sign of its fall: it is, literally, going down. 与 12 宫主或转宫 12 宫主形成入相位，也会显示同样的情况。另一个常见的征象 是征象星进入其弱势星座：这字面上意味着“走下坡路”。

The greater the essential dignity the planet has, the more likely the person is to be innocent. 行星的先天尊贵程度越高，此人无罪的可能性越大。

If the question is about to somebody being released, the desired testimonies will be the reverse of the above. 如果问题是关于某人获释，所需的征象将与上述情况相反。

Will Deirdre be sent down? Deirdre（迪尔德丽）会被判入狱吗？

To while away long evenings, William Lilly would ‘in merriment’ ask a servant to hide something and then cast a chart to find it. I have never developed his affection

for lost object questions; my preferred horary merriment comes in predicting the story line in soap operas. 为消磨漫漫长夜，William Lilly 会“以娱乐的方式”让仆人藏起某物，然后起卦 寻找。我从未培养出他对失物问题的钟爱；我偏爱的卜卦娱乐在于预测肥皂剧的 剧情线。

In Coronation Street, Deirdre was in the dock, facing charges of fraud after falling for a charming but unscrupulous con-man. As the foreman of the jury stood up to give the verdict, the credits began to roll. Rather than wait three days to find out, I set the chart. 在《加冕街》中，Deirdre 因被一个迷人但无耻的骗子所惑而面临欺诈指控，站 在被告席上。当陪审团团长起身宣布裁决时，片尾字幕开始滚动。我不愿等上三 天去查明结果，于是起了星盘。

I had no particular interest in Deirdre, so she is ‘any old person’: 7th house. Had I strongly identified with her, perhaps having experienced something similar myself, she would be given the 1st house, as if the question were ‘Will we be sent down?’ If I were strongly smitten with her, she would still be 7th, this time as the object of my affections. 我对 Deirdre 并无特殊兴趣，所以她属于“任何人”：7 宫。如果我强烈认同她， 或许因为自己有过类似经历，她会被赋予 1 宫，就像问题是“我们会被判入狱吗？” 一样。如果我深深地迷恋她，她仍然是 7 宫，但这次是作为我情感的对象。

Deirdre was already in prison, as she had been refused bail. Lord 7, Mars, shows this: it is in the turned 12th house (12 from 7th = radical 6th). It is in its own sign: lots of essential dignity, so Deirdre is innocent. But it is about to conjunct Saturn, which is in its fall and so is very nasty. It is also the natural ruler of imprisonment. Something horrible is going to happen to her: she will be convicted and sentenced to jail. Deirdre 已被拒绝保释，所以她已在狱中。7 宫主火星显示了这一点：它位于转宫 12 宫（7 宫之 12 宫 = 基准盘 6 宫）。火星位于其入庙星座：具有很多先天尊贵， 所以 Deirdre 是无辜的。但它即将与土星合相，而土星位于其弱势位置，因此非 常凶恶。土星也是监禁的先天守护星。可怕的事情即将发生在她身上：她将被定 罪并判刑入狱。

This is all happening in a cardinal sign, however, suggesting things that are quickly over. Once past Saturn, Mars hasn’t far to travel before it enters Deirdre’s 1st. She is entering her own house. This, as so often in horary, can be taken literally: she will soon be coming home. Before Mars gets home it meets Mercury, which is retrograde: what has been said (Mercury) will change (retrograde). Someone’s story will change, as a result of which Deirdre will be freed. 然而，这一切都发生在一个基本星座内，暗示事情会很快结束。一旦经过土星， 火星在进入 Deirdre 的 1 宫前无需运行太远。她正在进入自己的宫位。正如卜卦 中常见的那样，这可以按字面理解：她很快就会回家。在火星到家之前，它会遇 到逆行的水星：已经说过的话（水星）将会改变（逆行）。某个人的说辞将会改

变，结果 Deirdre 将获释。

The South Node close to the cusp of the turned 11th (11 from 7th = radical 5th) shows where Deirdre will be hurt: through her friends. Although there is a moderately strong mutual reception between Mars and Jupiter, ruler of this house (each in the other’s triplicity), they oppose each other by antiscion. It was the testimony of a friend that was crucial to her conviction. But the friends (Jupiter is in a double-bodied sign, so there is more than one) are honest (strong essential dignity), so the false testimony must have been given in error. Juptier being a strongly dignified benefic, they will want to act for the best, and the mutual reception shows them helping. 南交点靠近转宫 11 宫宫头（7 宫之 11 宫 = 基准盘 5 宫），显示了 Deirdre 将在 何处受到伤害：通过她的朋友。尽管火星和此宫主星木星之间存在中等强度的互 溶关系（各自位于对方的三分星座），但它们通过映点形成对冲。一位朋友的证 词对她的定罪至关重要。但朋友们（木星位于双体星座，所以不止一个）是诚实 的（强大的先天尊贵），所以伪证必定是出于错误而提供的。木星作为一颗尊贵 有力的吉星，意味着他们会希望做出最好的行动，互溶关系也显示了他们在提供 帮助。

Note here an example of that important point about mutual reception: it can work only to the extent that both planets are strong. Here both planets are strong, so the friends are capable of helping and Deirdre is capable of being helped. 这里请注意关于互溶关系的一个重要例证：它只有在两颗行星都强旺的情况下才 能发挥作用。这里两颗行星都强旺，所以朋友们有能力帮助，Deirdre 也有能力 接受帮助。

To smooth the feathers of those horrified at the asking of so ‘trivial’ a question – merriment being forbidden in some outposts of contemporary horary – I should add that Deirdre’s imprisonment brought front-page headlines in the national press and questions in parliament. Not, perhaps, quite so trivial! The story unfolded as the chart shows. 为了让那些对提出如此“琐碎”问题感到震惊的人平复情绪——在某些当代卜卦 占星的前哨站，娱乐是被禁止的——我应当补充说明，Deirdre 的入狱事件登上 了全国性报纸的头版头条，并在议会引发了质询。这或许，并非那么微不足道！ 故事的发展正如星盘所示。

# The Weather

# 天时（天气）

Questions about the weather are among the simplest of horaries. Judgement is made using some of the fundamental building-blocks of astrology: hot, cold, moist and dry. Given these and some wind, we have all that we need for accurate weather-forecasting. So don’t complicate it! 关于天气的卜卦问题是最简单的类型之一。判断时运用占星学的一些基本构建要 素：热、冷、湿与燥。有了这些要素和一些风，我们就能进行精确的天气预报。 所以，别把它复杂化！

If it is a general question about the weather in this area, use the 1st house: ‘Will we have a hot summer this year?’ ‘When will this rainy spell end?’ If the question relates to a specific event, use the house that shows that event: ‘I’m playing golf tomorrow: what will the weather be like?’ (5th house); ‘I’m going to stay with my friend; do I need to take warm clothes?’ (11th house: ‘What is the weather at my friend’s house?’). Such questions are often asked about sailing trips: if it is a long voyage, look to the 9th house; if it is ‘messing about in boats’, or sailing around without a destination, look to the 5th; if it is the ferry that you catch to go to work each day, it is a routine journey and so 3rd. 如果是一般性的、关于本地区天气的问题，使用 1 宫：“今年夏天会热吗？”“这 段雨天什么时候结束？”如果问题与特定事件相关，则使用代表该事件的宫位： “我明天要打高尔夫：天气会怎样？”（5 宫）；“我要去朋友家住；需要带厚 衣服吗？”（11 宫：“我朋友那里的天气如何？”）。这类问题常针对航海旅 行提出：如果是长途航行，看 9 宫；如果是“随便玩玩船”，或无目的地的航行， 看 5 宫；如果是每天上班乘坐的渡轮，那是常规行程，因此看 3 宫。

### ✸ See the added discussion at the end of this chapter for more on the choice of

houses.✷

### ✸关于宫位选择的更多探讨，请参见本章末尾的补充论述。✷

Although you can ask general questions about the weather in the place where you are, you cannot ask them routinely with the expectation of getting an accurate answer. You cannot mechanically repeat ‘What’s the weather going to be today?’ when you wake

each morning. 虽然你可以询问你所在地的天气概况，但你不能将其当作例行公事并期望得到准 确答案。你不能每天早上醒来就机械地重复问“今天天气会怎样？”。

Once you have chosen the appropriate house, the ruler of that house shows the event in question (the party, the voyage), even if it is a 1st house matter and the event is only the vague ‘here’. The house ruler itself is the event: it is not the weather at that event. If the house is ruled by Saturn, this does not mean that the weather will be cold and dry; we have to look at what is happening to Saturn. 一旦选定了恰当的宫位，该宫的守护星即代表所问事件（聚会、航行），即使这 是一个 1 宫事务且事件仅仅是模糊的“这里”。宫主星本身就是事件，并非该事 件发生地的天气。如果该宫由土星守护，这并不意味着天气会又冷又燥；我们必 须观察土星的状态。

Planets are things; signs describe them. Planets are nouns; signs are adjectives. The sign will describe the planet within the context determined by the question; in a weather question, the sign will describe the house ruler in terms of the weather: it will be hot, cold, moist or dry. If the house-ruler is in an earth sign, which is cold and dry, the weather at that event will be cold and dry; if in an air sign (hot and moist), it will be hot and moist. Yes, it is this simple. 行星是实体；星座描述它们。行星是名词；星座是形容词。星座将在问题设定的 语境下描述行星；在天气问题中，星座将以天气的术语来描述宫主星：它是热、 冷、湿还是燥。如果宫主星在一个冷且燥的土象星座，那么该事件发生时的天气 将是冷且燥的；如果在热且湿的风象星座，天气将是热且湿的。是的，就是这么 简单。

For more detail on exactly how cold and dry this earth sign shows it will be, look to the ruler of that sign. The example chart below will make this clearer. Then note any close aspects to the significator. An aspect from a moist planet in a moist sign will bring rain; a sextile might show a light shower; an opposition, a destructive downpour. Qualify your judgement by the season: ‘hot’ in the middle of winter is not going to be the same as ‘hot’ in the middle of summer. Cold moisture in winter may be snow, depending on where you are. 要更详细地了解这个土象星座所显示的冷燥程度究竟如何，可查看该星座的守护 星。下面的示例星盘会让这一点更清晰。然后注意征象星的任何紧密相位。来自 湿性行星在湿性星座的相位会带来降雨；一个六合相位可能预示着小阵雨；一个 对冲相位则可能是一场破坏性暴雨。根据季节来限定你的判断：仲冬时节的“热” 与仲夏时节的“热”含义不同。冬季的冷湿可能是雪，具体取决于你所在的地点。

Jupiter, the Great Benefic, is natural ruler of rain. Astrology shares the farmer’s rather than the holiday-maker’s idea of what is good weather. Mercury rules wind, so aspects from Mercury will show whether the wind is helpful or a hindrance for your voyage. The condition of Mercury will show how strong the wind will be. On a grander scale, Mercury is also natural ruler of earthquakes, which are seen as wind

within the earth. 木星作为大吉星，是雨水的先天守护星。占星学对好天气的定义更接近农民而非 度假者的观念。水星掌管风，因此来自水星的相位将显示风对你的航行是有助益 还是阻碍。水星的状态将显示风的强度。在更大的尺度上，水星也是地震的先天 守护星，被视为地壳内部的“风”。

### ✸Remember that there is no such thing as good or bad weather. We may call it such,

but this is only our opinion of it. Weather just is. A hurricane, for instance, is not in any sense misbehaving or defective weather, nor is it any more weather-ish than is a gentle breeze: it is weather doing what weather does. As such, essential dignity can be ignored in these judgements. The Moon in Cancer is a cold/moist planet in a cold/moist sign. So is the Moon in Scorpio. Either will show cold/moist weather. That the one is essentially dignified and the other essentially debilitated does not mean one will conform more than the other to our idea of what is pleasant.✷

### ✸记住，天气本身并无好坏之分。我们或许会这样称呼它，但这只是我们的看

法。天气就是天气。例如，飓风在任何意义上都不是行为不当或有缺陷的天气， 它也并非比微风“更像”天气：它只是天气在做天气该做的事。因此，在这些判 断中可以忽略先天尊贵。月亮在巨蟹座是一颗冷/湿的行星位于冷/湿的星座。月 亮在天蝎座也是如此。两者都显示冷/湿的天气。一个入庙而另一个落陷，并不 意味着其中一个比另一个更符合我们对于宜人天气的期望。✷

What will the weather be at my party? 我的派对天气会如何？

The querent held an annual barbecue party with a huge crowd of guests, so the weather on the chosen day was of some importance. 问卜者举办一年一度的烧烤派对，宾客众多，因此选定日期的天气相当重要。

It is a party, so look to the 5th house. The sign on the cusp of the 5th well describes the party: it is a hot and dry sort of party – a barbecue. This describes the party; it does not describe the weather. Nor does Mars, ruling this house, have any effect upon the weather. Mars is the party; we are looking at what affects Mars. 这是派对，所以看 5 宫。5 宫头的星座很好地描述了派对：这是一个热且燥的派 对——烧烤。这描述的是派对本身；它并非描述天气。火星作为此宫的守护星， 也对天气没有任何影响。火星是派对；我们要观察的是影响火星的因素。

Mars signifies the barbecue. What sort of barbecue? It is in a cold/moist sign: a wet sort of barbecue. 火星代表烧烤。什么样的烧烤？它在一个冷/湿的星座：一场湿漉漉的烧烤。

What sort of wet? The Moon (ruler of the sign that told us it was wet) signifies the wet. It is in Pisces, another water sign: it will be a wet sort of wet. It is conjunct Jupiter: a big wet sort of wet. Conjunct Juptier in Pisces: a very big wet sort of wet. 什么样的湿？月亮（告诉我们“湿”的那个星座的守护星）代表湿。它在双鱼座， 另一个水象星座：这是一种湿透了的湿。它与木星合相：一场大雨般的湿。与木 星合相于双鱼座：一场倾盆大雨般的湿。

It rained torrentially from morning till night. 那天从早到晚下着倾盆大雨。

### ✸Although this judgement worked, I would not now approach the chart in this way.

The party was to be held in the querent’s own garden, her ‘here’. As such, it should, I think, be judged from the 1st house, not the 5th. The party isn’t relevant: the weather ‘here’ would have been the same whether she were throwing a party or digging the garden. Look at the chart: working from the 1st house gives exactly the same judgement. Lord 1 is again Mars, which now signifies ‘here’. In a water sign, so it is a wet sort of here, etc. Similarly, if I were to ask, ‘Will the weather be good enough for me to take my computer to the garden to work?’ it would not become a 10th-house matter because I am thinking of working. Nor would the weather change if I felt lazy and decided to snooze on a deck chair instead. It is still the basic ‘here’ of where I live: 1st house.

### ✸尽管这个判断奏效，但我现在不会用这种方式来看这张星盘。派对是在问卜

者自家的花园里举行，那是她的“这里”。因此，我认为这应该从 1 宫而非 5 宫来判断。派对本身并不相关：无论她是在办派对还是挖花园，这里的天气都是 一样的。再看这张星盘：从 1 宫着手会得出完全相同的判断。1 宫主同样是火星， 此时它代表“这里”。在水象星座，所以这是湿漉漉的“这里”，等等。类似地， 如果我问：“天气是否好到我可以把电脑拿到花园里工作？”这并不会因为我想 工作就变成 10 宫事务。同样，如果我懒懒地决定躺在躺椅上打盹，天气也不会 改变。它始终是我居住地的基本“这里”：1 宫。

With other places, use your common sense. If the friend you are visiting lives in the next street, the weather will be as it is in your own ‘here’: 1st house. If your friend lives in another country, look at the 11th. If the golf-course where you will be playing is near your home, it will be ‘here’; if 100 miles away, look at the 5th house.✷ 至于其他地方，运用常识判断。如果你拜访的朋友住在邻街，天气就和你自己的 “这里”一样：1 宫。如果你的朋友住在另一个国家，看 11 宫。如果你要打高 尔夫的高尔夫球场在你家附近，那它就是“这里”；如果在一百英里外，则看 5 宫。✷

# Electing with Horary

# 用卜卦占星择日

Electional astrology is choosing the optimum moment at which to act. It is a time-consuming business, and so if done by a professional is expensive. It cannot be done without the study of the birthchart. For those querents who, whether for lack of known birth-data or financial reasons, a full election is not possible, or for those who do not need precision of time in their election, we can choose the time to act with horary. 择日占星学是选择一个行动的最佳时刻。这是一项耗时的工作，因此若由专业人 士操作，费用不菲。若不研究本命盘，就无法进行择日。对于那些或因缺乏出生 数据、或因经济原因而无法进行完整择日的问卜者，或是那些在择时上无需精确 到分秒的人，我们可以用卜卦占星来选择行动的时间。

This will not give us a timing to the minute, as can be done with a full election, but it does provide what is for many purposes all the accuracy that is needed. 这无法像完整择日那样给出精确到分钟的时机，但它确实能提供在许多情况下所 需的全部准确度。

Once again, this is very simple. Don’t complicate it! All you need do is to identify the relevant planet, which will be the ruler of the house in question. ‘When is the best day to have my party?’: Lord 5. ‘When is the best day to launch this work project?’: Lord
10. In many cases the question boils down to ‘When is the best day for me?’: take Lord 1. 再次强调，这非常简单。别把它复杂化！你需要做的只是识别出相关的行星，也 就是所问宫位的守护星。“举办派对的最佳日子是哪天？”：取 5 宫主。“启动 这个工作项目的最佳日子是哪天？”：取 10 宫主。在许多情况下，问题归结为 “哪一天对我来说最好？”：取 1 宫主。

Having identified the planet, look at its movement. What is it going to do? What is going to happen to it? No matter how dire its position now might be, sooner or later it will be in a stronger position. Ask yourself, ‘What is the best situation for this planet in the near future?’ Once you have identified this, take the distance from where the planet is now to where it will be when it gets there and judge the timing in the usual way. 识别出行星后，观察它的运动。它将要做什么？它会发生什么？无论它现在的位

置多么糟糕，迟早它会处于更强的位置。问问自己：“在不远的将来，这颗行星 的最佳状态是什么？”一旦你确定了这一点，测量这颗行星从当前位置到抵达该 状态位置的距离，并像往常一样判断时间。

In many questions of this kind there are severe time restraints: ‘Should I do the deal on Monday or Thursday?’ 在这类问题中，往往会有严格的时间限制：“我应该周一还是周四做这笔交易？”

In such cases the transits to the horary chart on the specified days can be eloquent. Suppose, for example, the question is, ‘I have a choice of June 20th or June 30th for my interview to get into college; which is best?’ and the ephemeris shows that on the 20th Lord 1 (the querent) conjuncts the 9th cusp of the horary chart (the college), where it is exalted. ‘Go on the 20th: they’ll think the world of you!’ Or maybe between the 20th and 30th the ruler of the 9th (the college) changes sign and enters some dignity of Lord 1 (the querent): ‘Go on the 30th, because they will like you more then’. 在这种情况下，特定日期的行运对卜卦盘的相位可能很有说服力。例如，假设问 题是：“我有两个选择，6 月 20 日或 6 月 30 日参加大学入学面试，哪天更好？” 星历表显示，20 日那天，1 宫主（问卜者）合相卜卦盘的 9 宫头（大学），并且 在该位置入旺。“选 20 号：他们会对你评价极高！”或者，也许在 20 日到 30 日之间，9 宫主（大学）转换星座，进入了 1 宫主（问卜者）的某种尊贵位置： “选 30 号吧，因为他们那天会更喜欢你。”

Usually, however, we can concentrate on the task of getting our one significator as strong as possible. Example: suppose the question is ‘When is the best day to submit my masterpiece to a publisher?’ Your masterpiece is your baby: 5th house. Suppose Mars rules the 5th and will conjunct the North Node in 3 degrees. This will make it stronger, which is what we want, and the 3 degrees will give us the timing: 3 days, weeks or months, depending on the sign and house it is in. These questions usually carry their own time-limits, which makes the choice of time-unit easy (‘When within the next fortnight should I do this?’). Or it is exalted. So the answer might be, ‘Wait four days, then do it any time you like’. 然而，通常情况下，我们可以专注于让我们的一个征象星尽可能强大。例如：假 设问题是“哪天是把我的杰作提交给出版商的吉日？”你的杰作是你的宝贝：5 宫。假设火星守护 5 宫，并且将在 3 度内合相北交点。这会让它更强大，这正是 我们想要的，这 3 度会给出时间指示：3 天、3 周或 3 个月，取决于它所在的星 座和宫位。这类问题通常自带时间限制，这使得时间单位的选择变得容易（“未 来两周内我该哪天做这件事？”）。或者，这颗行星入旺了。所以答案可能是： “等四天，然后你想哪天做都行”。

Most important: do not do anything that implies the setting of a new chart for the elected time. To do this is to begin to do a full election, and this cannot be done without the study of the birthchart. With a horary, you do not have the necessary information – so don’t try to do it. Example of this would be, ‘Mars gets strong in 4

days, and on that day the Moon is in the 10th,’ or ‘And on that day Venus trines Saturn.’ Neither should you aim for precision with a horary election. It is rare for the answer to be more specific than, at most, a particular day. You cannot get a time from an election like this, so don’t try. Often the answer will be ‘After such a date’ or ‘As soon as possible’. 最重要的一点：不要做任何暗示要为择定时刻另起新盘的事情。这么做就相当于 开始做一个完整的择日盘，而这若不研究本命盘是无法进行的。在卜卦占星中， 你并没有必要的信息——所以不要试图这样做。例如，以下这类做法就属于此列： “火星 4 天后会变强，那天月亮在 10 宫，”或者“那天金星拱土星。”你也不 应该试图在用卜卦择时时追求精确度。答案极少能具体到某一特定日子（至多如 此）。你无法通过这种择时获得具体时刻，所以别白费力气。通常，答案会是“在 某日期之后”或“越快越好”。

### ✸I can no longer see any validity in electional astrology as is usually done. It is no

more than a means to facilitate the transfer of money from client to astrologer by indulging the client’s wishful thinking. The idea that I will succeed in this or that by acting when Mars or Venus is in a certain place in the sky is quite as groundless as the idea that I will succeed by wearing the right aftershave or chewing the right gum. Electing with horary is something quite different. It does not have the idea of succeeding because a certain planet is in a certain place. The discussion of the two approaches, and why the one is valid while the other is not, is too long for inclusion in a general textbook. It can be found on my website, www.johnfrawley.com.✷

### ✸我已无法再看到传统择日占星学有任何有效性。它不过是通过迎合客户的痴

心妄想，来促进金钱从客户流向占星师的一种手段。认为当火星或金星在天空中 处于某个特定位置时行动，我就会在这事或那事上成功——这种想法，和我用对 了须后水或嚼对了口香糖就会成功一样，毫无根据。而用卜卦占星择时则完全不 同。它并不持有“因为某颗行星处于某位置所以会成功”的观念。这两种方法的 对比，以及为什么一种有效而另一种无效，讨论起来篇幅太长，不适合纳入一本 通用教科书。相关内容可在我网站 www.johnfrawley.com 上找到。✷

# Astrologer and Client

# 占星师与顾客

Working in the Seventeenth century, William Lilly did the occasional postal consultation, but most of his clients were sitting in front of him while he judged the charts for their questions. Many would have been in a distressed state, whether about their medical problems, their marital prospects or the lost cow on whose recovery their financial future depended. The modern horary astrologer will probably do most consultations by phone, post or email. With such a distance between astrologer and clinet, it is easy to forget that these charts are not abstract mental exercises, but people’s lives. We are dealing with flesh, blood and tender hearts, not a collection of symbols on a page. 在 17 世纪执业时，William Lilly 偶尔会进行邮政咨询，但大多数问卜者都是坐 在他面前，由他为其问题判断星盘。许多人可能正处于焦虑状态，无论是关于他 们的医疗问题、婚姻前景，还是那只丢失的母牛——其能否找回关乎他们未来的 财务状况。现代卜卦占星师可能会通过电话、邮寄或电邮进行大多数咨询。由于 占星师与问卜者之间存在这样的距离，很容易忘记这些星盘并非抽象的思维练习， 而是关乎人们的生活。我们处理的是有血有肉、有脆弱心灵的人，而不是纸上一 堆符号的集合。

There are advantages and disadvantages to the querent being present while the chart is judged. The main advantage, other than reminding us that we are dealing with a human being, is that we can easily ask for information about points that puzzle us in the chart. But in practice this is necessary more rarely than might be expected. If it is needed, we can contact the querent. 问卜者在判断星盘时在场既有优点也有缺点。主要的优点，除了提醒我们面对的 是人之外，我们还可以轻松询问星盘中令我们困惑之处的信息。但实际上，这种 情况出现的频率比预期的要少。如果需要，我们可以联系问卜者。

The main disadvantage is that the querent’s presence is distracting. I prefer to have my total attention on the astrology while I judge the chart, then have my total attention on the client while giving the judgement. Lilly’s contemporaries would customarily accuse each other of twisting judgements to get the client’s cash. The awareness of the client’s emotional state. There is a natural human desire to please, in which even horary astrologers share; having the client’s hopes and fears hanging over you as you judge can lead you astray. It is far more likely to do so if the client is sitting in front of you at the time. I suspect that this caused more distortion of

judgement in Lilly’s day than deliberate financial chicanery. 主要的缺点是问卜者在场会分散注意力。我更喜欢在判断星盘时将全部注意力集 中在占星学上，然后在给出判断时将全部注意力集中在问卜者身上。与 Lilly 同 时代的人通常会互相指责对方为了获取问卜者的钱财而扭曲判断。对客户情绪状 态的察觉，以及人类天生取悦他人的欲望，即使是卜卦占星师也不例外；在判断 时，问卜者的希望和恐惧悬于你心头，可能会让你误入歧途。如果当时问卜者就 坐在你面前，这种情况更有可能发生。我怀疑在 Lilly 那个时代，这种情况导致 的判断失真比蓄意的金钱欺诈更为普遍。

Assuming that the astrologer has made the financial arrangement with the client clear, so that there is no ‘Cross my palm with silver and I’ll tell you more’, the money problem arises only with such question as ‘Should I invest in…?’ and ‘Should I emloy…?’ There, the astrologer will be aware that the answer ‘No’ may bring another question about the next prospective investment or employee, and therefore another fee. And the astrologer will be aware that the client knows this too. This can start a game of ‘I think that he thinks that I think…’ There is no answer to this other than striving to give each judgement with a clear conscience, and pointing out whatever errors in attitude the chart might suggest: ‘You’re seeking to change your investments because you feel that you ought to be acting, but they’re fine where they are’; ‘Try choosing an employee because she knows her job, not because you fancy her’. 假设占星师已经与问卜者明确了财务安排，这样就不会出现“给我银币，我告诉 你更多”的情况，那么金钱问题只会在诸如“我应该投资于……吗？”和“我应 该雇用……吗？”这类问题中出现。在这种情况下，占星师会意识到，回答“不” 可能会引发关于下一个潜在投资或雇员的另一个问题，从而带来另一笔费用。而 且占星师也会意识到问卜者也知道这一点。这可能会引发一场“我认为他认为我 认为……”的游戏。对此，除了努力以清白的良心给出每一个判断，并指出星盘 可能暗示的态度上的任何错误之外，别无他法：“你想改变投资，是因为你觉得 应该有所行动，但它们目前的位置很好”；“选择雇员应看重其业务能力，而非 你对她有好感。”

Even if you prefer to deal with clients in person, modern reality will usually not allow it. No matter how good at horary you may become, you are unlikely to find querents queuing at your door. Many horary questions have one word answer; this is fully satisfactory in a telephone call, less so if the client has travelled for some hours to reach you – no matter how valuable that one word might be. 即使你更喜欢亲自接待问卜者，现代的现实情况通常也不允许。无论你的卜卦占 星多么精湛，你也不太可能发现问卜者在你门口排队。许多卜卦问题的答案只需 一个字；这在电话咨询中完全可以接受，但如果问卜者花了几个小时的路程来找 你，这种情况就不那么理想了——无论那个字多么有价值。

A one word answer is often all that is needed. If that is all, that is all; do not turn it into a counseling session because you feel you need to fill up some time. You have done your work. 一个字的答案往往就足够了。如果这就是全部，那就是全部；不要因为觉得需要

填补时间而把它变成一场咨询会谈。你已经完成了你的工作。

Resist the temptation to turn every judgement into a choice of black or white. In many situations, mediocrity is all that is on offer, so if mediocrity is what the chart shows, that is the answer. Questions are often phrased in the hope of the marvellous – the prefer mate, the ideal job – but the judgement to such questions is often ‘You could do a lot worse’, ‘It’s OK’, or ‘It doesn’t much matter which you choose’. This is a valid answer. 抵制住将每个判断都变成非黑即白的选择的诱惑。在许多情况下，所能提供的只 是平庸的结果，所以如果星盘显示的是平庸，那就是答案。问题通常被表述得充 满对奇迹的期待——理想的伴侣、完美的工作——但对这类问题的判断通常是 “这算不错了”、“还行”或“你选哪个都差不多”。这是一个有效的答案。

Sometimes you will feel confident in your judgement; sometimes you will not. There is no need to pretend otherwise. It is acceptable to say, ‘This chart’s really clear. I am fallible, but I’m pretty confident that xyz will happen’, or ‘This chart’s really a puzzle. I think I’m reading it right, in which case…’ 有时你会对自己的判断感到自信；有时则不会。无需假装。可以说，“这个星盘 非常清晰。我虽然会犯错，但我相当有信心 xyz 会发生”，或者“这个星盘确实 是个谜。我想我理解对了，如果这样的话……”

You will get questions wrong, and you will continue to do so no matter how much knowledge and experience you gain. Some questions allow you a second shot: if, for instance, the lost object isn’t where you judged it to be, you can go back to the chart to find another interpretation of the testimonies. Some questions do not allow a second shot, because the time for it has passed. This is unfortunate, and hearing ‘You told me such-and-such, but…’ hurts to the same extent that ‘I told you your prediction was impossible, but…’ please. It does not mean you need to don sackcloth and ashes. Study the chart so you learn from your mistakes, but do not demean yourself before the client: your being perfect is not part of the contract. 你会把问题判断错，而且无论你获得多少知识和经验，这种情况都会继续发生。 有些问题允许你有第二次机会：例如，如果丢失的物品不在你判断的位置，你可 以回到星盘，为这些征象寻找另一种解读。有些问题不允许有第二次机会，因为 时机已经过去了。这很不幸，听到“你告诉我会如何如何，但是……”和“我告 诉过你，你的预测不可能，但是……”一样令人难受但这并不意味着你需要为此 披麻蒙灰。研究星盘，从错误中学习，但不要在问卜者面前贬低自己：你并非完 人，这本来就不是合同的一部分。

You will become familiar with the words ‘What if?’ You have just answered your client’s question by telling her that the object of her affection does not love her. ‘But what if I were Julia Roberts?’ she asks, ‘You might have given me a differen answer’. 你会熟悉“如果……会怎样？”这句话。你刚刚回答了问卜者的问题，告诉她心 仪的对象不爱她。“但如果我是 Julia Roberts（朱莉娅·罗伯茨）呢？”她问道， “你可能会给我不同的答案。”。

‘But you’re not Julia Roberts.’ “但你不是 Julia Roberts。”

‘But what if I were?’ “但如果我是呢？”

I have never had that conversation with a client, but I have often had the conversation that begins, ‘But what if I’d asked you the question at a different time? You might have given a different answer.’ 我从未与客户有过这样的对话，但经常遇到以这样的话开头的讨论：“但要是我 在另一个时间问你这个问题呢？你可能会给出不同的答案。”

‘But you didn’t.’ “但你没有。”

‘But what if I had?’ “但如果我那样做了呢？”

Perhaps the greatest lesson of horary is that there is no such things as ‘What if?’ What is, is; what is not, is not. The assumption of horary is that the question is a product of that person in the reality of that person’s life. It is asked when it is asked because the querent is who the querent is. Only when the querent can become someone else can the question be asked at a different time. 卜卦占星学或许最大的教训在于：根本没有“如果……会怎样？”这回事。存在 的就是存在，不存在的就是不存在。卜卦占星学的前提假设是，问题是那个人在 其现实生活的真实境遇下的产物。问题在某个时刻被提出，是因为问卜者就是问 卜者本人。只有当问卜者能变成另一个人时，问题才有可能在另一个时刻被提出。

In dealing with querents, there are many pits into which the unwary may fall. It is well be aware of the more common ones, as avoiding them is a lot easier than clambering out of them. You will need to decide a policy on various issues with which querents will confront you. Don’t worry: this policy need not be set in stone. If situations show you’ve got it wrong, you’ll change it, while you’ll find there are exceptions to most of the rules you may make. You may, for example, decide to accept a certain question from a friend or long-standing client that you would not take from a first-time querent. Remember: once you have accepted give, the querent will usually assume that you have looked at the chart and seen something so horrible that you cannot bear to tell it. So it is worth deciding what you will do in difficult situations before these situations arise. 在处理问卜者时，许多陷阱可能会让粗心者栽跟头。最好能了解那些较常见的陷 阱，因为避开它们比掉进去再爬出来要容易得多。你需要就问卜者会向你提出的 各种问题决定应对策略。别担心：这个策略并非一成不变。如果实际情况表明你 之前的做法有误，你会做出调整，同时你也会发现，你制定的多数规则都存在例

外情况。例如，你可能会决定接受某个朋友或老客户的特定问题，而这类问题你 不会接受首次来访的问卜者。请记住：一旦你接受了咨询费，问卜者通常会认为 你已经看了星盘，并且看到了某些可怕到你不忍告知的事情。因此，值得在这些 情况发生前就决定好你在困境中将如何应对。

Most questions involve someone other than the querent, so where will you set the barrier between legitimate enquiry and unwarranted intrusion? 大多数问题都涉及到问卜者之外的其他人，你该如何划分合理询问与越界窥探的 界限？

Will you accept questions on death? Or serious illness? Fear not, if you have a sensitive spot, your querents will find it! What about questions that touch on your deeply held beliefs? Perhaps you are a Catholic, for instance, and are asked ‘Should I have an abortion?’ It may be tempting to side-step these issues by not accepting questions of such import. But even what appear the most innocuous of questions can carry a huge emotional cargo: avoid questions of import and you will avoid all questions. 你会接受关于死亡或重病的问题吗？如果你有敏感之处，不用怕，你的问卜者总 能找到它！对于那些触及你深层信仰的问题呢？比如，你是个天主教徒，却被问 到“我应该堕胎吗？”通过不接受此类重要问题来回避它们或许很诱人。但即便 是看起来最无害的问题，也可能承载着巨大的情感包袱：回避重要问题，就等于 回避了所有问题。

I strongly suggest that the basis for any consultation must be that we are adults dealing with adults. Many of the reservations commonly voiced to answering certain questions are patronising in the extreme, their basic theme being ‘I can’t say that in case I upset the poor little clinet’. Unless you intend hanging a sign outside your booth, ‘Horary Astrologer: pleasing answers only’, we must play by grown-ups’ rules: you ask the question, you get the answer. But you have the right to refuse questions, and you have the right to refuse clients. 我强烈建议，任何咨询的基础都必须是：我们是成年人，在与成年人打交道。许 多对回答某些问题常见的保留意见都极端地带有居高临下的意味，其基本主旨是 “我不能那么说，免得让那可怜的小客户难过”。除非你打算在你的咨询亭外挂 个牌子，写着“卜卦占星师：只提供令人满意的答案”，否则我们必须遵守成年 人的规则：你提问，就得接受答案。但你有权拒绝问题，也有权拒绝客户。

For all that we play by grown-ups’ rules, there are judgements that are not easy to give. Here follows my reply to a student who asked how to handle these, and William Lilly’s own letter to the Student in Astrology: 尽管我们遵守成年人的规则，但有些判断确实不易给出。以下是我对一个学生询 问如何处理这些情况时的回复，以及 William Lilly 本人在《致占星学徒的一封信》 中的话：

I can’t say it better than Lilly, where he advises us to ‘afflict not the querent with

harsh judgement’. We must tell the truth, and if they have asked the question they must get the answer to it, no matter how unpleasant: the biggest danger is that we put so much sugar on it that the answer itself gets lost. But we can be judicious with what we say: we don’t need to tell all that we see, just because we can see it – that makes us feel clever, but doesn’t benefit the client. 我无法说得比 Lilly 更好，他建议我们“不要用严厉的判断折磨问卜者”。我们 必须说出真相，既然他们问了问题，就必须得到答案，无论多么令人不快：最大 的危险是我们加了太多糖，以至于答案本身被掩盖了。但我们可以审慎地选择言 辞：我们无需只因能看到就说出我们看到的一切——那会让我们觉得自己很聪明， 但对客户并无益处。

We must make it clear that we are not infallible: this leaves room for hope, which must never be destroyed. Especially when predicting death, reminding the client that all is in the hands of God is important. Prayer is always helpful. Or when saying that there is no future with Prince Charming, ‘by all means prove me wrong, but I really can’t see it’. 我们必须明确，我们并非不会犯错：这为希望留出了空间，而希望绝不能破灭。 特别是在预测死亡时，提醒客户一切皆掌握在上帝手中很重要。祈祷总是有益的。 或者在断言与白马王子没有未来时说，“务必请证明我错了，但我真的看不出来”。

Strive to find a positive – but only if there is one. A common scenario is ‘No, there is no future with X, but it seems that you’re only in this relationship because you’re at such a low spot. By the autumn you should be feeling more confident in yourself and will be ready for the quality of relationship that you deserve’. Or things about no being ready at the moment, as if your capacity for finding a loving relationship isn’t quite ripe yet. These may sound anodyne, but such things are often shown in the chart. 努力找到积极的一面——但前提是确实存在。一个常见的情景是：“不，和 X 没有未来，但看来你陷入这段关系只是因为你正处于人生的低谷。到了秋天，你 应该会对自己更有信心，并准备好迎接你应得的那份高质量的感情。”或者关于 目前尚未准备好的事情，比如你寻找真爱关系的能力尚未完全成熟。这些听起来 可能无关痛痒，但星盘中常常显示出这类信息。

You will be surprised how easily people take what you might think to be the worst possible news: it often comes as a relief, or as a confirmation of what they sensed would happen. Just say what you have to say quickly, simply and clearly. There is an Arab saying that we must always be kind – but sometimes being kind means chopping the limb off with one stroke. Sawing away at it only prolongs the pain. 你会惊讶地发现，人们多么容易接受那些你可能认为是天大的坏消息：它往往带 来一种解脱，或是印证了他们预感会发生的事。只需迅速、简洁、清晰地陈述你 必须说的话。有句阿拉伯谚语说，我们必须始终仁慈——但有时仁慈恰在于快刀 斩乱麻。迟疑不决只会延长痛苦。

And as Polonius said: to thine own self be true. Say things as you would say them: if you try to adopt a style that isn’t you, the falsehood in that will grate. The judgements

I regret are not the ones I’ve got wrong – which is always allowable – but those where the tone in which I’ve delivered the judgement has been inappropriate. That is not allowable! 正如 Polonius（波洛尼厄斯）所说：最重要的是忠于你自己。用你习惯的方式去 说：如果你试图采用一种不属于你的风格，其中的虚假会让人感到不适。我所后 悔的判断，并非那些我弄错了的——这总是可以被允许的——而是那些我传递判 断时的语气不当。那是不允许的！

### To The Student In Astrology.

### 致占星学徒

44. Lilly, introductory pages. Punctuation modernized.
44. Lilly，引言部分。标点已按现代用法修订。

My Friend, whoever thou art, that with so much ease shall receive the benefit of my hard studies, and dost intend to proceed in this heavenly knowledge of the stars, wherein the great and admirable works of the invisible and all-glorious God are so manifestly apparent. In the firstplace, consider and admire thy Creator, and be thankful unto him. Be thou humble, and let no natural knowledge, how profound and transcendent soever it be, elate thy mind to neglect that divine Providence, by whose all-seeing order and appointment all things heavenly and earthly have their constant motion; butthe more thy knowledge is enlarged, the more do thou magnify the power andwisdom of Almighty God, and strive to preserve thyself in his favour, being confident, the more holy thou art, and more near to God, the purer Judgment thou shalt give. Beware of pride and self-conceit, and remember how that longago no irrational creature durst offend man, the microcosm, but did faithfully serve and obey him, so long as he was master of his own reason and passions, or until he subjected his will to the unrea-sonable part. But alas! when iniquity abounded, and man gave the reins to his own affection, and deferred reason, then every beast, creature and outward harmful thing became rebellious and tinserviceable to his command. Stand fast, oh man! to thy God, and assured principles. Then consider thy own nobleness, how all created things, both present and to come, were for thy sake created; nay, for thy sake God became man. Thou artthat creature, who being conversant with Christ, livest and reignest above the heavens, and sits above all power and author-ity. How many preeminences, privileges, advantages hath God bestowed on thee? Thou rangest above the heavens by contemplation, conceivest the morion and magnitude of the stars; thou talkest with angels, yea with God himself; thou hast all creatures within thy dominion, andkeepest the devils in subjection. Do not then, for shame, deface thy Nature, or make thyself unworthy of such gifts, or deprive thyself of that great power, gloryand blessedness God hath allotted thee, by casting from thee his fear, for

possession of a few imperfect pleasures. 我的朋友，无论你是谁，若能轻松获益于我艰辛的研究成果，并决心继续探究这 门揭示无形而荣耀之上帝伟大奇迹的天体学问——首先，当心怀敬畏感念造物主， 谦卑自持。纵有渊博学识，亦不可骄矜到漠视神圣天意。万物皆依其慧眼所定的 秩序运转，你愈是学识广博，愈当颂扬全能上帝的威能与智慧，力求蒙其恩宠。 要深信：心灵愈是圣洁，愈能接近上帝，所作判断便愈显澄明。谨防傲慢自负！ 须知远古之时，只要人类仍能主宰理性与情感，未将意志屈从于兽性，万物皆忠 顺服务于尘世之灵长。可悲啊！当罪恶横行，人若放纵情欲而背离理性，众生便 皆叛逆不服管束。世人啊！当坚守对上帝的信仰与确凿准则。且思量自身尊贵： 万物皆为汝而造，上帝更为汝道成肉身。汝这能与基督对话、统御诸天、超脱权 柄的存在——上帝赐予了多少殊荣？汝以沉思巡游天际，测算星轨；与天使甚至 上帝对话；统辖万物，制伏恶魔。切莫自贬天性，辜负恩赐，为须臾欢愉而背弃 敬畏，丧失上帝所赐的权能与福泽。

Having considered thy God, and what thyself art, during thy being God’s servant, now receive instruction howin thy practice I would have thee carry thyself. As thou daily conversest with the heavens, so instruct and form thy mind according to the image of Divinity. Learn all the ornaments of virtue; be suffi-ciently instructed therein. Be humane, courteous, familiar to all, easy of access. Afflict not the miserable with terror ofa harsh judgment. In such cases, let them know their hard fate by degrees; directthem to call on God to divert his judge-ments impending over them. Be modest; conversant with the learned, civil, sober man; covet not an estate; give freely tothe poor, both money and judgment. Let no worldly wealth procure an erroneous judgment from thee, or such as may dishonour the Art, or this divine Science. Love good men; cherish those honest men that cordially study this Art. Be sparing in delivering judgment against the Commonwealth thou livest in. Give notjudgment of the death of thy Prince; yet I know experimentally, that Reges subjacent legibus stellarum.Marry a wife of thy own; rejoice in the number of thyfriends; avoid law and controversy. In thy Study, be totus in illisthat thou mayestbe singulus in arte. Be not extravagant or desirous to learn every science; be not aliquid in omnibus.Be faithful, tenacious, betray no one’s secrets; no, no, I charge thee - never divulge either friend or enemy’s trust committed to thyfaith. Instruct all men to live well; be a good example thyself; avoid the fashion of the times; love thy own native country; exprobrate no man, no not anenemy; be not dismayed if ill spoken of, Conscientia mille testes;God suffersno sin unpunished, no lie unrevenged. 既明上帝与己身之位份，今授汝实践之则：日日观天象，当使心性契合神性。广 习美德，待人以仁，亲和有礼。莫以严苛判词折磨困顿之人，当循循善诱使其知 命，劝其祈求上帝消灾解难。持身谦逊，结交博学文雅之士；淡泊财物，慷慨济 贫。勿容俗利玷污判断，辱没此神圣技艺。亲善贤德，扶持诚研此道者。慎对国 事之判，绝不可妄断君主生死——虽实证显明“君王亦受星律制约”。宜娶妻 成家，珍视良友，避讼事争端。治学当“专心致志，方能卓然成家”。勿贪多 求全沦为“杂而不精”。守口如瓶，重诺守信——纵对仇敌亦不泄其托付。劝 人向善，以身作则；不趋时流，热爱故土；不责难人，包括仇敌。遭谤不惊—— “清白良心胜于千证”，上帝必惩恶罚谎。

William Lilly

45 Kings are subject to the law of the stars. 45 君王亦受星律制约。

46 Be dedicated, that thou mayest be without peer. 46 专心致志，方能卓然成家。

47 A jack of all trades. 47 杂而不精 。

48 A good conscience is a thousand witnesses. 48 清白良心胜于千证。

APPENDIX 1 附录 1

# Chart Calculation

# 绘制星盘

You need: the time of the question; latitude and longitude of the place. An ephemeris. A Table of Houses. 你需要：提问的时间；所在地点的经纬度；一本星历表；一本宫位表。

Tables for Regiomontanus houses are, as far as I know, unavailable, so use Placidus houses. Although I recommend Regiomontanus, if you use another valid system with sincerity, you will find it will work: you will be asked the right questions at the right times to fit with the house system you are using. 据我所知，Regiomontanus（雷吉蒙塔努斯）宫位制的表格现在已经找不到了， 所以请使用（普拉西度）宫位制。尽管我推荐 Regiomontanus 宫位制，但如果你 带着诚意使用其他有效的宫位系统，你会发现它同样可行：你会在恰当的时间被 问到恰当的问题，以适应你所使用的宫位系统。

There is a table of Placidus houses in Raphael’s Ephemeris. If you are using an ephemeris that does not contain such a table, buy a copy of Raphael’s. You will only need one annual edition, because the table remains the same year after year. 在《Raphael（拉斐尔）星历表》中附有 Placidus 宫位表。如果你使用的星历表 不包含此表，请购买一本《Raphael星历表》的副本。你只需要一个年度的版本， 因为这张表格年复一年保持不变。

Reduce local time to GMT. 将当地时间转换为 GMT（格林尼治时间）。

A: Work out how many hours & minutes since previous noon GMT. A：计算出距离上一次 GMT 正午已经过去了多少小时和分钟。

B: Add 4 minutes per degree east of Greenwich; subtract 4 minutes/degree west. B：每东经 1 度增加 4 分钟；每西经 1 度减去 4 分钟。

C: Add 10 seconds per hour of GMT since previous noon. C：距离上一次 GMT 正午的 GMT 标准时间，每小时增加 10 秒。

D: Add A+B+C D：将 A、B、C 的结果相加

Look in ephemeris for Sidereal Time for previous noon. 在星历表中查找上一次 GMT 正午的恒星时。

Add your total at D to this. 将你在 D 步得到的总数加到这个恒星时上。

You now have local sidereal time. (You may need to subtract 24 hours to get a number less than 24) 你现在就得到了当地恒星时。（你可能需要减去 24 小时，以确保数值小于 24。）

Look at the Table of Houses for your latitude. 根据你的纬度查找宫位表。

Locate the local sidereal time you have calculated in this table. 在表中找到你刚刚计算出的当地恒星时。

Read off the house-cusps. Six are given: the other six are their opposities. 读出宫头位置。表格中会列出六个宫头：另外六个宫头就是它们的对宫。

You now have located the signs in your chart. 至此，你已经确定了星盘中的星座位置。

Look in the ephemeris to locate the planets at that time on that day. 在星历表中查找当天当时行星的位置。

The ephemeris will give you the positions of the planets each noon: you will need to work out their exact positions by proportion. Don’t be too fussy about this! 星历表会给出每个正午的行星位置：你需要通过比例计算出它们的确切位置。不 必对此过于苛求！

Whatever other books might claim, you do not need logarithms. Logarithms are a comparatively recent discovery: throughout most of astrology’s long history astrologers happily managed without them. So can you. 无论其他书籍如何宣称，你都不需要用到对数。对数是相对近代的发现：在占星 学漫长历史的大部分时间里，占星家们没有对数也照样轻松地演算。你同样可以 做到。

You will not usually need to calculate the planets’ positions precisely. The only times you need exactitude are: 你通常不需要精确计算行星的位置。只有在以下情况才需要精确性：

* when you need to know if this aspect happens before that aspect
* 当你需要知道这个相位是发生在那个相位之前还是之后

* when you need to know if this aspect happens before or after the planets change sign.
* 当你需要知道这个相位是发生在行星换座之前还是之后。

If you are using Raphael’s, you will find this information in the back of the ephemeris, so you don’t need to work it out yourself. 如果你使用的是《Raphael星历表》，这些信息可以在星历表的末尾找到，所以 你无需自己计算。

Practice this by calculating the charts given in this book. Remember that you are using a different house system, so the house cusps may be a few dgrees out. As long as they roughly agree, your calculation is probably right. 通过计算本书中给出的星盘来练习。请记住，你使用的是不同的宫位系统，因此 宫头可能会有几度的出入。只要大致吻合，你的计算很可能就是正确的。

APPENDIX 2 附录 2

# House Meanings

# 宫位的意义

### Your son’s pet rabbit

### 你儿子的宠物兔

Your son is 5th; rabbits are animals smaller than goats, so 6th. 6th from the 5th is the 10th. Count this round on the chart to make sure that when you count 6th from the 5th you get the 10th, not the 11th. Always count the house you start with as the 1st, so the 1st from the 5th is the 5th, 2nd from the 5th is the 6th, etc. 你儿子对应 5 宫；兔子属于小于山羊的动物，因此对应 6 宫。从 5 宫数起的第 6 宫是 10 宫。在星盘上按顺序数一遍以确保正确：从 5 宫开始作为第 1 宫计算， 那么从 5 宫数的第 1 宫是 5 宫本身，第 2 宫是 6 宫，依此类推，最终得到 10 宫。

### Your father’s house

### 你父亲的房子

Your father is 4th; houses are 4th: 4th from 4th, which is the 7th. BUT: although this is true in theory, in practice someone else’s house is usually shown by their 1st. This is literally ‘their house’. Exactly as in the cat chart on page 4: the cat is in the cat’s 1st: he is in the cat’s house. 你父亲对应 4 宫；房子本身也对应 4 宫：因此需要看从 4 宫数起的第 4 宫，即 7 宫。但是：尽管理论上如此，实际应用中，他人的房产通常由其 1 宫代表——字 面意思就是“他的家”。正如第 19 页关于猫的星盘案例：猫位于猫自己的 1 宫， 即它在自己的“房子”里。

We need take the person’s 4th (in this example, the 4th from the 4th) only if we need to distinguish between person and property, as in ‘Will my father sell his house this year?’ 只有在需要区分人与财产时才使用该人的 4 宫（本例即从 4 宫数起的第 4 宫）， 例如“我父亲今年会卖掉他的房子吗？”

### Your pregnant sister

### 你怀孕的姐妹

Your sister is 3rd. Pregnant or not pregnant, she is still your sister; she is still 3rd. 你姐妹对应 3 宫。无论是否怀孕，她仍然是你的姐妹，因此仍以 3 宫代表。

### Your new car

### 你的新车

Your movable possession: 2nd house. 你的动产：2 宫。

### Your journey to work

### 你的通勤路线

Routine journey: 3rd house. Even if you make this journey in your car, the car is not the journey, so the car is never your 3rd house. 常规出行路线：3 宫。即使开车通勤，汽车本身不等于出行路线，因此汽车从不 归入你的 3 宫。

### Your boss

### 你的上司

10th house. 10 宫。

### The guy who shares your office

### 与你共享办公室的人

A colleague: 7th house. 同事：7 宫。

### The dream your friend is telling you about

### 你朋友正在讲述的梦境

Your friend is 11th; dreams are 9th. His dream is 9th from the 11th, which is the radical 7th. 你朋友对应 11 宫；梦境对应 9 宫。他的梦境需看从 11 宫数起的第 9 宫，即基准 盘的 7 宫。

### Your brothers

### 你的兄弟

3rd house. 3 宫。

### Your younger brother, in contrast to your elder brother

### 你的弟弟，相对于你的哥哥

All your brothers and any of your brothers may be signified by the 3rd. If you need to distinguish between different brothers, you can turn the chart. The elder brother would be shown by the 3rd; a younger would be regarded as his brother, hence 3rd from the 3rd, which is the radical 5th. 所有你的兄弟以及任何一位兄弟都可能由 3 宫代表。如果需要区分不同的兄弟， 你可以使用转宫。哥哥将由 3 宫代表；弟弟则被视为哥哥的兄弟，因此需要看从 3 宫数起的第 3 宫，即基准盘的 5 宫。

If you specifically asked the question about your younger brother, he would be given the 3rd. If you then needed to include your elder brother in the judgement, he would be shown by the 3rd from the 3rd. 如果你具体问及关于弟弟的问题，那么弟弟将由 3 宫代表。如果此时需要在判断 中纳入哥哥，那么哥哥将由从 3 宫数起的第 3 宫代表。

This taking of 3rd from the 3rd to show another brother has given birth to a brood of errors. Your first wife may be 7th, but your second wife is not 3rd from the 7th, unless you intend marrying your first wife’s sister. Nor is your next job 3rd from the 10th (your job’s brother). The 3rd house from something does not show ‘another thing of that kind’. It shows that thing’s sibling. 这种用从 3 宫数起的第 3 宫来代表另一个兄弟的做法引发了一连串的错误。你的 第一任妻子可能由 7 宫代表，但你的第二任妻子并非从 7 宫数起的第 3 宫，除非 你打算娶你第一任妻子的妹妹。你的下一份工作也不是从 10 宫数起的第 3 宫（你 工作的兄弟）。从某事物数起的第 3 宫并不代表“另一件同类事物”，而是代表 该事物的兄弟姐妹。

That the 3rd from the 3rd shows my brother’s brother has led many to find other representatives of a house by repeating the number of that house, claiming for instance that if your present job is 10th your next job will be 10th from the 10th, or that your job’s job, or your job’s boss (this is one way of locating the boss in a question about a job). 7th from the 7th would be your spouse’s spouse (you). Unless you marry yourself, it is not your second spouse. 由于从 3 宫数起的第 3 宫代表我兄弟的兄弟，这导致许多人通过重复该宫位的数 字来寻找其他同类宫位的代表，例如声称如果你当前的工作是 10 宫，那么你的 下一份工作将是 10 宫的第 10 宫，或者你工作的“工作”，或者你工作的老板（这 是在关于工作的问题中定位老板的一种方式）。从 7 宫数起的第 7 宫将是你的配 偶的配偶（也就是你自己）。除非你与自己结婚，否则这并非你的第二任配偶。

### Your children

### 你的孩子

5th house. 5 宫。

### Your younger child, in contrast to your elder child

### 你年幼的孩子，相对于你年长的孩子

In this case, taking the 3rd house is valid: your younger child is seen as the elder’s sibling. 3rd from the 5th = 7th. The same would be true if you asked specifically about your younger child: the elder would be seen as the younger’s sibling. 3rd from the 5th again. 在这种情况下，使用 3 宫是有效的：你年幼的孩子被视为年长孩子的兄弟姐妹。 从 5 宫数起的第 3 宫 = 7 宫。如果你 具体询问你年幼的孩子，情况也是如此： 年长的孩子将被视为年幼孩子的兄弟姐妹。同样是从 5 宫数起的第 3 宫。

It is not 5th from the 5th. That is your child’s child, your grandchild. 这不是从第 5 宫数起的第 5 宫。那是你孩子的孩子，也就是你的孙子/孙女。

### Your ex-spouse

### 你的前任配偶

If you are asking specifically about this person (‘Will my ex turn up at the party?’), use the 7th. If you are asking about your present spouse, the present spouse is 7th and you can find another significator for the ex. See chapter 21 for details of how to do this. 如果你具体询问的是这个人（例如“我的前任会出现在派对上吗？”），使用 7 宫。如果你问的是你现任配偶，现任配偶是第 7 宫，你需要为前任找到另一个征 象星。具体操作方法详见第 21 章。

### The local priest

### 当地的牧师

9th. Whether you follow his faith or not, even if he bought his ordination on the internet, he is still 9th house. 9 宫。无论你是否信仰他的宗教，甚至即使他的圣职是从网上买来的，他仍然属 于 9 宫。

### The priest’s brother

### 牧师的兄弟

3rd from the 9th = 11th. 9 宫的 3 宫 = 11 宫。

### The priest’s sister-in-law

### 牧师的嫂子/弟媳

The priest’s brother is 11th. His wife is 7th from 11th = 5th. 牧师的兄弟是 11 宫。他的妻子是从 11 宫数起的第 7 宫 = 5 宫。

### The king of Spain

### 西班牙国王

If you live in Spain, he is your king: 10th. If you don’t, he is the king of a foreign country: 10th from the 9th = 6th. With expatriates, use your common sense to decide which to use, depending on the context of the question. 如果你住在西班牙，他是你的国王：10 宫。如果你不住在西班牙，他是外国的 国王：从 9 宫数起的第 10 宫 = 6 宫。对于侨居国外的情况，请根据问题的上 下文运用常识来决定使用哪一个。

### Your father’s liver

### 你父亲的肝脏

The liver is 5th house. 5th from the 4th = 8th. 肝脏属于 5 宫。4 宫的第 5 宫 = 8 宫。

### That packet of rice you bought this morning

### 早上你购买的那袋大米

Your movable possession: 2nd. 你的动产：2 宫。

### That wrap of cocaine you bought this morning

### 早上你买的那包可卡因

Your movable possession: 2nd. It is not 12th house: the cocaine is not your self-undoing; your taking it is your self-undoing. It is that vital distinction between function and object again. 你的动产：2 宫。它不是 12 宫：可卡因本身并不是你的自我毁灭；你吸食它才 是你的自我毁灭。这再次体现了功能与物件之间的重要区别。

### The book you borrowed from the library

### 你从图书馆借的图书

2nd house. It is, albeit temporarily, yours. In the same way, the money you have lent to other people is not your 2nd house, but theirs. 2 宫。它（尽管是暂时的）是你的。同样地，你借给别人的钱不属于你的 2 宫， 而是属于他们的。

### The book you have written

### 你写的书

Your baby: 5th house. 你的“孩子”：5 宫。

### The person who told the cops about your secret life as a

### criminal mastermind

### 那个告诉警察你作为犯罪主谋的秘密生活的人

Informer: 12th house. Whether you are a criminal mastermind or not, he still informed against you, so is still 12th house. 告密者：12 宫。无论你是不是犯罪主谋，他确实告发了你，所以仍然属于 12 宫。

### Your butler

### 你的男管家

6th. Jeeves’ relationship to Wooster is 2nd house: he is less a servant than an advisor; but this is unusual. My butler’s duties are limited to supervising other staff and decanting the port: he is my servant, so 6th house. 6 宫。Jeeves（吉夫斯）与 Wooster（伍斯特）的关系属于 2 宫：他与其说是仆人， 不如说是顾问；但这并不常见。我的管家的职责仅限于监督其他员工和斟波特酒： 他是我的仆人，所以是 6 宫

### Your job as a butler

### 你作为男管家的工作

10th. As your job always is. If we didn’t serve somebody, somehow, while we worked, we would never get paid. 10 宫。你的工作总是如此。如果我们在工作时不以某种方式为某人服务，我们 就永远不会得到报酬。

### Mines

### 矿井

4th house. Bottom of the chart. 4 宫。星盘的底部。

### The man who’s come to repair your plumbing

### 那个来给你修水管的人

Your servant: 6th house. 你的仆人：6 宫。

### The man who’s just whispered a hot tip for the next race

### into your ear

### 那个刚刚在你耳边低语下一场比赛劲爆内幕的人

Your advisor: 2nd house. Or, if he knows you’ve been attending Gamblers Anonymous and is seeking to lead you astray, 12th house (your secret enemy). 你的顾问：2 宫。或者，如果他知道你一直在参加匿名戒赌会，并试图引诱你误 入歧途，那么他就是 12 宫（你的秘密敌人）。

### Your university

### 你的大学

9th house. 9 宫。

### Your daughter’s university

### 你女儿的大学

9th house. Although we say it is here, it isn’t: she just goes there. Unless we need to distinguish, as in ‘Is my university better than hers?’ in which case we would give hers the 9th from the 5th = 1st. 9 宫。虽然我们这么说，但实际上并非如此：她只是去那里上学。除非我们需要 加以区分，比如在“我的大学比她的好吗？”这样的问题中，在这种情况下，我 们会把她的大学定为从 5 宫数起的第 9 宫 = 1 宫。

### Your teacher’s university

### 你老师的大学

Now we must distinguish, because the teacher himself is 9th, so we cannot take the 9th for his university. 9th from the 9th = 5th. 现在我们必须加以区分，因为老师本身是 9 宫，所以我们不能再用 9 宫来代表他 的大学。从 9 宫数起的第 9 宫 = 第 5 宫。

### Astrology

### 占星学

Higher knowledge: 9th house. 高等知识：9 宫。

### Particle physics

### 量子物理学

Higher knowledge: 9th house. 高等知识：9 宫。

### Your mistress’s brother’s Great Dane

### 你情妇兄弟的大丹狗

Your mistress is 7th house. Her brother is 3rd from 7th = 9th. Great Danes may be larger than most goats, but dogs are generically smaller than goats, so he is 6th house. 6th from 9th = 2nd. 你的情妇是 7 宫。她的兄弟是从 7 宫数起的第 3 宫 = 9 宫。大丹犬可能比大多

数山羊大，但狗通常比山羊小，所以它属于 6 宫。从 9 宫数起的第 6 宫 = 2 宫。

### The cruise you’re thinking of taking

### 你正在考虑的巡航旅行

Special journey: 9th house. 特殊的旅行：9 宫。

### The ship on which you’ll be taking it

### 你将乘坐的游轮

The ship you sail in: 1st house. 你乘坐的船：1 宫。

### Your dog’s ball

### 你养的狗的球

Her possession: 2nd from 6th = 7th. It is not her 5th. The game she plays with it might be her 5th, but not the ball itself. Function and object again. 它的财产：从 6 宫数起的第 2 宫 = 7 宫。这不是它的 5 宫。它玩球的游戏可能是 它的 5 宫，但球本身不是。又是功能与物件的区别。

### Your mother’s friend’s child

### 你母亲朋友的孩子

Your mother is 10th, so her friend is 11th from 10th = 8th. Her child is 5th from 8th = 12th. 你的母亲是 10 宫，所以她的朋友是从 10 宫数起的第 11 宫 = 8 宫。她的孩子是

从 8 宫数起的第 5 宫 = 12 宫。 APPENDIX 3 附录 3

# How to Spot an Aspect

# 如何识别相位

Yes, the whole celestial system is in motion! What we see before us in the chart is a freeze-frame of a continually moving thing, exactly as if we had pressed the pause button on a DVD. The chart as it stands no more tells us how the story will turn out than does that one frozen frame from a film. The villain has a gun in his hand; is he going to fire it? Mars is somewhere near Saturn; will they meet? From that freeze-frame alone, we cannot tell. 没错，整个天体系统都在运动！我们在星盘中所看到的，其实是持续运动中的天 体被定格的一瞬间，就像我们在 DVD 上按下了暂停键。这张静态的星盘并不能 告诉我们故事的结局，正如电影中的一个定格画面无法揭示剧情走向一样。坏人 手里拿着枪，他会开枪吗？火星在土星附近，它们会相遇吗？仅凭那个定格画面， 我们无从得知。

You need to be able to work out if a certain aspect will happen and, often, when that aspect will happen. First rule: faster planets catch up with slower planets. So you need to learn the usual order of speed. From fastest to slowest it is: 你需要能够判断某个相位是否会形成以及，通常，该相位将在何时形成。首要法 则：运行速度快的行星会追上运行速度慢的行星。因此，你需要了解行星通常的 速度顺序。从最快到最慢依次是：

Moon Mercury Venus Sun Mars Jupiter Saturn 月亮 水星 金星 太阳 火星 木星 土星

But, as discussed in the main text, the planets don’t always move at the same speed. My Ferrari may be faster than his tractor, but if I’m pulling into a petrol station he may at that moment be travelling faster than me. The Moon is always very much the fastest. Apart from the Sun, whose speed never significantly varies, the others can all slow to zero and then click into reverse. 但是，正如正文中所讨论的，行星并不总是以相同的速度运行。我的法拉利可能 比他的拖拉机快，但如果我正在驶入加油站，那一刻他可能比我跑得还快。月亮 始终是最快的。除了太阳的速度不会有显著变化外，其他行星的速度都可能减慢 到零，然后转为逆行。

Finding aspects from the ephemeris

从星历表中找出相位

This is easy. Open your ephemeris to any month. You will see the planets marked along the top, with their daily position is columns extending downward. The sign each planet is in is marked at the top of its column and elsewhere in that column whenever the planet changes sign. 这很简单。将星历表打开到任意月份。你会看到行星符号排列在表格顶部，它们 的每日位置则向下排列在对应的列中。每颗行星所在的星座标注在其所在列的顶 部，以及在该列中该行星换座的位置。

You will see that in most columns the numbers larger as you read downwards. If the numbers in a column get smaller, that planet must be retrograde. Except when the numbers jump from 29 to 0, which is when the planet is moving into a new sign. 你会发现，在大多数列中，随着你向下阅读，数字会变大。如果某一列中的数字 变小了，说明那颗行星正在逆行。除非数字从 29 跳到了 0，那是行星正在进入 新星座的标记。

Pick any two planets. You want to know if they make an aspect during this month. Run your eye down each of their columns to see if the numbers reach a point where they coincide. Example: maybe you see Saturn’s daily position marked 9.02, 9.07, 9.12, 9.17. Mercury’s position on those same days reads 7.13, 8.41, 10.09, 11.35. Mercury’s number started out smaller than Saturn’s; it then became larger. There must have been a poin at which they coincided – when Mercury was at 9 degrees and something. 任意挑选两颗行星。你想知道它们在这个月内是否形成相位。用眼睛扫视它们各 自所在的列，看看数字是否达到重合的点。例如：也许你看到土星的每日位置标 记为 9.02、9.07、9.12、9.17。而同一天水星的位置则是 7.13、8.41、10.09、11.35。 水星的数字开始小于土星，然后变得比土星大。这中间必定有一个点它们重合了 ——也就是当水星运行到 9 度多的时候。

This point of coincidence may be an aspect. If there is no point of coincidence, there cannot be an aspect. But not all such coincidences are aspects. It depends which signs the planets are in. Now check their signs: 这个重合点可能就是一个相位。如果没有重合点，就不可能形成相位。但并非所 有这样的重合都是相位。这取决于这两颗行星所在的星座。现在检查它们的星座：

same sign: conjunction 同一星座： 合相

adjacent signs: no aspect 相邻星座： 无相位

next to adjacent: sextile 再相邻（相隔两个星座）： 六合相位

next to that: square 再相隔（相隔三个星座）： 刑相位

next to that: trine 再相隔（相隔四个星座）： 拱相位

opposite signs: opposition 相对星座： 对冲相位

adjacent to the opposite sign: no aspect 与对宫相邻的星座： 无相位

NB: this is SIGNS, not HOUSES. 注意：这里指的是星座，不是宫位。

Done that? Good. You now know how to spot an aspect in the ephemeris. But checking these columns for every possible planetary pairing would be tedious. You do need to know how to do this, but you can cut out most of the work by looking for aspects in the chart itself. 明白了吗？很好。你现在知道如何在星历表中识别相位了。但是，为每一对可能 的行星组合检查这些列会很繁琐。你确实需要知道怎么做，但你可以通过在星盘 本身上寻找相位来省去大部分工作。

Finding aspects from the chart 从星盘上找出相位

Believe it or not, after a while you will glance at a chart and notice all the aspects without even thinking about it. Much in the same way that a mechanic will listen to a car for a moment and know exactly what is wrong with it, not by running through a list of possibilities in his head, but because he can hear it and knows. 信不信由你，过一段时间后，你只需瞥一眼星盘，甚至想都不用想就能注意到所 有相位。这很像一位机械师听一会儿汽车的声音就能准确知道哪里出了毛病，他 并不是在脑海里快速过一遍各种可能性，而是因为他听到了声音，所以知道。

When judging a horary, you will usually be concerned with only a few planets and their possible aspects. But let’s look at this chart and check all its aspects, as an example. 在判断卜卦盘时，你通常只需要关注几颗行星及其可能形成的相位。但让我们以 这张星盘为例，来检查一下它所有的相位。

Start with the faster planet, the Moon. 从运行较快的行星，月亮，开始。

What degree is in now? 12.53. 它现在位于多少度？12.53 度。

As it moves forwards, it will move into degrees of gradually higher number. 随着它向前运行，它会逐渐进入度数更高的位置。

Which planet is at the lowest number of degrees that is higher than 12.53? 哪颗行星的度数是最接近且高于 12.53 度的？

Mercury, at 15.10. 是水星，位于 15.10 度。

The Moon moves so fast it will soon reach 15 degrees of its own sign, by which time Mercury will scarcely have moved. 月亮移动得非常快，很快就会到达它所在星座的 15 度，而此时水星几乎没怎么 动。

The Moon, then, will reach the same number of degrees as Mercury. ASPECT ALERT! We have a coincidence of degrees. Is it an aspect? 那么，月亮将与水星达到相同的度数。相位警报！我们发现了度数的重合。这是

相位吗？

Mercury is not in an adjacent sign to the Moon, but in the next sign but one. 水星并不在与月亮相邻的星座，而是相隔一个星座（即再相邻的星座）。

Yes, it is an aspect: a sextile. 是的，这是一个相位：六合相位。

What next for the Moon? 月亮接下来会如何？

The planet with the next lowest number of degrees is Jupiter, at 18.10. 下一个度数最低的行星是木星，位于 18.10 度。

This gives a another coincidence. But the Moon is in Libra; its opposite sign is Aries. Jupiter is in Pisces, a sign adjacent to Aries. There cannot be an aspect. 这又是一个度数重合。但月亮在天秤座；它的对宫是白羊座。木星在双鱼座，是 与白羊座相邻的星座。不可能形成相位。

Now what? 现在呢？

The Sun, Mars and Venus are all at degrees which the Moon will reach. But all of them are in signs adjacent to Libra, where the Moon is. The Moon cannot make an aspect to them. 太阳、火星和金星所在的度数都是月亮将要达到的。但它们都在与月亮所在的天 秤座相邻的星座里。月亮无法与它们形成相位。

Anything else? 还有别的吗？

Saturn is at 28.26 of its sign. The Moon moves so fast that it must catch Saturn before it changes sign. 土星位于它所在星座的 28.26 度。月亮移动得非常快，它会在土星换座之前追上 土星。

Is Satrun in an aspectable sign? 土星在可以形成相位的星座吗？

Yes: it is in Aries, the opposite sign to the Moon’s. There is an opposition. 是的：它在白羊座，是月亮所在星座的对宫。会形成一个对冲相位。

That’s it for the Moon. Now for the next fastest planet, Mercury. Mercury is at 15.10 of its sign.

月亮的部分就到这里。现在来看下一个最快的行星，水星。水星位于它所在星座 的 15.10 度。

Where’s it going? 它的运行方向是什么？

Mercury moves fast. It must catch Jupiter at 18 degrees. 水星移动很快。它必然会追上位于 18 度的木星。

Good – there is an aspect here. But only in potential. When looking at the Moon, we knew that it wasn’t going to change course, but keep steaming forwards through the zodiac. The Sun, too, keeps plodding on its way. But all the other planets can change direction. 好的——这里有一个相位。但这仅仅是潜在的。在观察月亮时，我们知道它不会 改变路线，只会持续在黄道带上向前推进。太阳也会一直稳步前行。但所有其他 行星都可能改变方向。

Yes, it looks as if Mercury will make an aspect with Jupiter, and then with Mars and then Saturn. But it won’t. It is about to turn retrograde. Even though the 3 degrees it has to travel to aspect Jupiter at 18 Pisces is not a great distance, it fails to make it. There is no aspect here. 是的，看起来水星似乎会与木星形成相位，然后与火星，再与土星形成相位。但 它不会。它即将转为逆行。尽管它距离与位于双鱼座 18 度的木星成相只需要再 走 3 度，这个距离并不大，但它最终没能形成相位。这里没有相位。

Venus is at 27 degrees of its sign, and will soon reach 28 dgrees, bringing it to the same degree as Saturn. But Saturn is in a sign adjacent to Venus’ opposition, so there is no aspect. 金星位于它所在星座的 27 度，很快将达到 28 度，从而与土星达到相同度数。但 土星所在的位置与金星的对宫星座相邻，所以没有相位。

The Sun is at 22 degrees. Mars is at 23. The Sun never turns retrograde or appreciably slows down, so will soon catch Mars. Mars is in the next sign but one to the Sun, so there is an aspect: a sextile. 太阳位于 22 度。火星位于 23 度。太阳从不逆行，速度也不会明显减慢，所以它 会很快追上火星。火星与太阳相隔一个星座（即再相邻的星座），所以存在一个 相位：六合相位。

Mars is at 23 degrees of its sign. Venus is at 27. But Venus moves faster than Mars, so there will be no aspect. But it is worth checking the ephemeris to make sure that Venus is not moving retrograde or moving so slowly that Mars might catch her. With Venus so close to the Sun, though, this will not happen. 火星位于它所在星座的 23 度。金星位于 27 度。但金星比火星移动得快，所以不 会形成相位。不过还是值得查看一下星历表，确认金星没有逆行或移动得极慢，

以至于火星可能追上她。不过，由于金星离太阳如此之近，这种情况不会发生。

Jupiter is at 18 degrees, Saturn at 28. They are in adjacent signs, so there is no possibility of an aspect. 木星位于 18 度，土星位于 28 度。它们位于相邻的星座，所以不可能形成相位。

APPENDIX 4 附录 4

# How to Read the Square Chart

# 如何解读方形星盘

Modern books on astrology, including this one, customarily print charts in a circular format. Older books usually print them as a square. I hope this book will inspire you to study some of the old texts, especially Lilly’s Christian Astrology. Finding your way around in the square chart is not difficult. 现代占星著作（包括本书）通常将星盘印刷为圆形，但古籍多采用方形排版。本 书希望引导读者研读古典文献，尤其是 Lilly 的《Christian Astrology》。掌握方 形星盘的解读方法并不困。

This example is a chart Lilly cast to answer his own question about the recovery of some fish he had ordered, but which had been stolen from the warehouse before reaching him. 以下示例是 Lilly 为解答自身问题而绘制的星盘，问题关于他订购但尚未送达便 被从仓库盗走的一些鱼。

49. Lilly, p. 397.（45~48 在 LILLY 给学生写的信中，我没有录入并翻译。）

Start with the box in the middle of the chart. The Saturn glyph in the top lefthand

corner of the central box shows the day of the week: Saturday. Sometimes this is labeled dies, Latin for day. Often there is another glyph labeled hor, short for hora, Latin for hour. These are the planets that rule that day and that hour of that day. I have omitted all mention of them in this book, as after years of wasted time I have realised they serve absolutely no purpose in horary. 从星盘中央的方框开始。中央方框左上角的土星符号表示星期：星期六。有时此 处会标注“dies”，拉丁语意为“日”。通常还有另一处标注“hor”的符号，是 拉丁语“hora”（小时）的缩写。这些是掌管该日及该日该时辰的行星。我在本 书中省略了所有关于它们的论述，因为在浪费了多年时间后，我意识到它们在卜 卦占星中完全没有用处。

Then comes the time for which the chart is cast, in this case February 10th, 1638. If you want to recreate the chart on your computer you will need to adjust both time and date. 接着是星盘绘制的时间，本例中为 1638 年 2 月 10 日。如果您想在电脑上重新生 成此星盘，则需要调整日期和时间。

Lilly’s England was still using the Julian calendar; his dates are known as Old Style. To convert them to the New Style that we use today you must add 10 days to them. Most software will not do this for you, so you need to do it yourself. Lilly’s date of February 10th becomes February 20th New Style. The adjustment varies from century to century: 10 days is correct for the 1600s. Check the positions of the Sun and Moon to make sure you have got the right day. 当时的 Lilly 所处的英格兰仍在使用儒略历；他的日期被称为“旧历”。要将其 转换为我们今天使用的“新历”，您必须加上 10 天。大多数软件不会为您做此 转换，因此您需要自行操作。Lilly 的 2 月 10 日（旧历）对应新历的 2 月 20 日。 调整的天数因世纪而异：对于 17 世纪，加上 10 天是正确的。请通过太阳和月 亮的位置来确认您得到的日期是正确的。

The year was sometimes taken as starting on March 1st, so what Lilly calls February 1638 could be February 1639 by our reckoning (i.e. he could be regarding February as the last month of 1638, not the second month of 1639). Usage was never consistent, so be careful: for dates in January or February, check the position of the outer planets to make sure you have the right year. In this case, Lilly’s 1638 is our 1638. 当时，年份有时被认为是从 3 月 1 日开始，因此 Lilly 所称的 1638 年 2 月，按我 们的算法可能相当于 1639 年 2 月（也就是说，他可能将 2 月视为 1638 年的最后 一个月，而不是 1639 年的第二个月）。用法从未统一过，所以要小心：对于 1 月或 2 月的日期，请检查外行星的位置以确认年份正确。在本例中，Lilly 的 1638 年就是我们的 1638 年。

The day was often taken as starting at noon, not midnight. This results in times in the morning being given as ‘p.m.’ Again, usage was not consistent: Lilly uses sometimes one style, sometimes the other. Look at the position of the Sun, remembering that it is on the Ascendant at dawn, near the MC at noon and on the Descendant at sunset. In

this chart, the Sun has recently risen and is heading towards the MC: it must be morning. On another day Lilly could just as well have called this 8.45 pm. 一天通常被认为从正午开始，而不是子夜。这导致上午的时间会被标注为“下午”。 同样，用法并不统一：Lilly 有时使用一种方式，有时使用另一种。观察太阳的 位置，记住太阳在黎明时分位于上升点，正午前后靠近中天，日落时分位于下降 点。在此星盘中，太阳刚刚升起并向中天移动：这一定是早晨。换作另一天， Lilly 完全可能将这个时间称为晚上 8 点 45 分。

He was not using any time zone recognized by your computer. He had obsession with accuracy of timing, and used an approximation to local time. This is not the same as Local Mean Time. Start by entering the time he gives as LMT, then jiggle the time about about to find the closest fit with the chart Lilly gives. Do not expect to arrive at an exact match. 他并未使用您的电脑所识别的任何时区。他极度注重时间的准确性，并使用近似 的地方时。这与地方平均时不同。开始时，将他给出的时间作为地方平均时输入， 然后微调时间，以找到与 Lilly 给出的星盘最接近的匹配。不要期望能完全精确 吻合。

Below the time, Lilly has noted the Moon’s most recent aspect and its next aspect. It is separating (a is Latin for ‘from’) from opposition of Jupiter and applying (ad is Latin for ‘to’) to sextile Mercury. 在时间下方，Lilly 记录了月亮最近的相位及其下一个相位。它正（a 是拉丁语， 意为“来自”）离开与木星的对冲相位，（ad 是拉丁语，意为“趋向于”）进 入与水星的六合相位。

The four triangles sharing a side with this central box are the angular houses, in their usual arrangement: 1st house on the reader’s left, 10th house at the top. The Ascendant is the uppermost side of the 1st house, so the Ascendant here is at 4.27 Taurus. The 2nd cusp is 13.28 Gemini, the 3rd 1.02 Cancer, the 4th 14 Cancer, and so on. 与中央方框共享边的四个三角形是角宫，按通常的排列方式：1 宫位于读者左侧， 第十宫位于顶部。上升点是 1 宫最上方的边，因此这里的上升点位于金牛座 4 度 27 分。2 宫头位于双子座 13 度 28 分，3 宫头位于巨蟹座 1 度 2 分，4 宫头位 于巨蟹座 14 度，依此类推。

The glyph for the sign a planet is in is not usually given, the sign being shown by way the planet is placed within that house. The Moon lies paralled to the Ascendant, so is at 15.03 Taurus. Had it been in the early degrees of Gemini, it would have been placed parallel to the 2nd cusp, which is in Gemini. In the 12th house, the Sun and Mercury are both in Pisces, as shown by their being parallel to the cusp that is in Pisces. 行星所在的星座符号通常不单独标出，而是通过行星在该宫内的放置方式来显示 星座。月亮平行于上升点放置，因此位于金牛座 15 度 3 分。如果它位于双子座 早几度，它就会被放置得平行于 2 宫头，而 2 宫头位于双子座。在 12 宫，太阳 和水星都位于双鱼座，这通过它们平行于位于双鱼座的宫头线来显示。

Incepted planets, such as Saturn and Venus in this chart, are printed parallel to neither cusp, and usually carry the glyph of their sign. “内嵌”行星，如本命盘中的土星和金星，被标记为既不平行于任何一个宫头线， 通常带有其所在星座的符号。
